GEN 1:1 Šurut maze Allaye asman edde zobin sirišṭi goijje.
GEN 1:2 Duniyai akarsara edde hali aššil, hiyanor uwore aššil andare guijja goin fani. Ar Allar Ruh fanir uwottu sola fira gorat aššil.
GEN 1:3 Toi Allaye hodde, "Fohor ok," henot fohor oiye.
GEN 1:4 Allaye sadde fohor bala oiye, toi Allaye fohorottu andarore zuda goijje.
GEN 1:5 Allaye fohorore nam diye "din," ar andarore hibaye nam diye "rait." Toi heṛe hazinna oiye edde binna oiye, ar hiyan aššilde foila din.
GEN 1:6 Allaye hodde, "Fanit maze ekkan gũitor ḍoil fák zaga ok, ar fani dui bag oi aleda ok."
GEN 1:7 Ei bafe Allaye fanit maze ekkan fák zaga goijje, nisor fani edde uworor fani aleda goijje. Ar henot hen oiye.
GEN 1:8 Bade Allaye he gũitor ḍoil fák zagaganor nam diye asman. Toi heṛe hazinna oiye edde binna oiye, ar hiyan aššilde dusora din.
GEN 1:9 Bade Allaye hodde, "Asmanor nisor hár fani ek zagat zoma ok, ar deha zok fuwana zaga." Ar henot hen oiye.
GEN 1:10 Allaye he fuwana zagar nam diye zobin, ar he fani zoma oiyede hiyanor nam diye doriya. Ar Allaye sadde hin bala oiye.
GEN 1:11 Allaye hodde, "Zobine háil ker, biz fodai gorede lota-fata, edde šobzi zar zar zat mozin dana loi gula dorade gula gas okkol, zobinor uwore fuṛaok." Ar henot hen oiye.
GEN 1:12 Toi zobine háil ker, biz fodai gorede lota-fata, edde šobzi zar zar zat mozin dana loi gula dorade gula gas okkol, fuṛaiye. Ar Allaye sadde hin bala oiye.
GEN 1:13 Toi heṛe hazinna oiye edde binna oiye, ar hiyan aššilde tisera din.
GEN 1:14 Bade Allaye hodde, "Raitottu dinore aleda goribolla asmanot gũitor ḍoil fák zagat fohor okkol ok, ar hin okkol sinno ok, boro din okkololla, din okkololla edde bosorolla,
GEN 1:15 ar hin okkole duniyait fohor dibolla asmanot gũitor ḍoil fák zagat takok." Ar henot hen oiye.
GEN 1:16 Toi Allaye dinor uwore razagiri goribolla ekkan beši ḍõr fohor, ar raitor uwore razagiri goribolla hiyanottuwaro ekka šoṛo fohor, ei beši ḍõr fohor duniyan edde tara banaiye.
GEN 1:17 Ar Allaye hinore asmanot gũitor ḍoil fák zagat buwaiye,
GEN 1:18 din edde raitor uwore razagiri goribolla, edde andarottu fohorore aleda goribolla. Ar Allaye sadde hin bala oiye.
GEN 1:19 Ar heṛe hazinna oiye edde binna oiye, ar hiyan aššilde sair lomboror din.
GEN 1:20 Bade Allaye hodde, "Fani nanan ḍoilla zandaror zãke bori uṛok, edde duniyair uwore asmanot maze faik okkol urok."
GEN 1:21 Toi Allaye doriyar he ḍõr ḍõr zanuwar okkol edde fanit zãk bandi solede nanan zator ze hár zandar okkol ase, hin okkolore, edde nanan zator faik okkol sirišti goijje. Ar Allaye sadde hin bala oiye.
GEN 1:22 Allaye hin okkolore duwa goijje, edde hodde, "Fólwala o edde beši o, ar doriyar fanire furon goro, duniyait faik okkol o beša beši ok."
GEN 1:23 Ar heṛe hazinna oiye edde binna oiye, ar hiyan aššilde faš lomboror din.
GEN 1:24 Tarfore Allaye hodde, "Zobinottu hár ḍoilla zandar zanuwar okkol niyoli aiyok: górot falede edde buke aṛede zandar, abanaiya fahari hár ḍoilla zandar okkol." Ar henot hen oiye.
GEN 1:25 Allaye zar zar zat mozin fahari zanuwar edde zar zar zat mozin górot falede zanuwar edde zar zar zat mozin zobinot hár ḍoilla buke aṛede zandar okkol banaiye. Ar Allaye sadde hin bala oiye.
GEN 1:26 Tarfore Allaye hodde, "Ãra ãrar súrot loi, ãrar ḍoilla manuš banai. Hitara doriyar mas, asmanor faik, górot falede edde fahari zanuwar, ar duniyair hár ḍoilla buke aṛede zandar okkolor uwore šašon goribo."
GEN 1:27 Toi Allaye manušore nizor súrote sirišti goijje, Allar súrote hibare sirišti goijje; maya edde morod gori hibaye hitarare sirišti goijje.
GEN 1:28 Allaye hitarare duwa goijje edde hitarare hodde, "Fólwala o edde zono šoinkaye beši o edde duniyai furon goro, ar duniyaire nizor šašonor tole ano. Ar doriyar mas okkol, asmanor tole faikor okkol, edde duniyair hár ḍoilla buke aṛede zandar okkolor uwore razagiri goro."
GEN 1:29 Tarfore Allaye hodde, "So, ãi duniyait asede hár ḍoilla biz fodai gorede lota-fata edde hár ḍoilla dana loi gula dorade gas okkol tũwarare dilam, hin okkol tũwarar haiddo oibo.
GEN 1:30 Ar duniyair hár zandar okkolore, asmanor uworor hár ḍoilla faik edde buke aṛede zandar okkolore, mani zeduggun zandar šiz ase hinolla adar hisabe hail fata gas gusola dilam." Ar henot hen oiye.
GEN 1:31 Toi Allaye hibar foida goijja hár kiššur uzu saiye, ar so, hin beši bala oiye. Toi hazinna oiye edde binna oiye, ar hiyan aššilde so lomboror din.
GEN 2:1 Endilla gori asman edde zobin ar hinor butore hár kissu tiyar gora šeš oiye.
GEN 2:2 Ar Allaye hãt dinor din hibaye gorat aššilde hamore šeš goijje; he hãt dinor din hibar hár hamottu ziraiye.
GEN 2:3 Toi ei hãt dinor dinware Allaye duwa goriyore fobitro din goijje, kiyollahoile he dinot hibar sirišti edde goijjilde hár hamottu ziraiye.
GEN 2:4 In oiyede asman edde zobinor sirišṭi kahani zẽtte hinore sirišṭi gora oil, zẽtte Mabud Allaye asman edde zobin banaiye.
GEN 2:5 Hẽtte duniyair zobinot hono zõl, gas gusola nu aššil, ar maṛot hono lota-fata no fuṛe, kiyollahoile Mabud Allaye hẽtte o duniyait hono zór no defeṛa edde zobinot saš goribolla o hono manuš nu aššil.
GEN 2:6 Kintu meṛir tolottu fani uṛiyore zobinor uworor muk agagura bizito.
GEN 2:7 Toi Mabud Allaye meṛir dúil loi manuššuwar forma banaiye edde hibar nak sai fu diyore butore zibon niyaš golai diye edde manušwa ek ziyãta zandar oiye.
GEN 2:8 Ar Mabud Allaye fuke Edenot ekkan bagan lagaiye; edde hibar tiyari manušware hibaye heṛe raikke.
GEN 2:9 Mabud Allaye meṛittu hár zator gas okkol fuṛi uṛabaiye, zin saite o šundor, edde háite o bala, ar baganor maze zibon gas edde neki bodi aholor gas.
GEN 2:10 Ar baganot fani dibolla Edenottu ekkan hal niyolle; edde hiyanottu sairgan muk oiye.
GEN 2:11 Foilaganor nam oilde Fišon; iyan oilde hiyan ziyan fura Havilah deš guriyore giye, heṛe zeṛe šuna fa za.
GEN 2:12 (Ar he dešor šuna bala, ar heṛe bedullium edde šoham fattor o ase.)
GEN 2:13 Dusora halor nam oilde Gihon; iyan oilde hiyan ziyan fura Kuš deš guriyore giye.
GEN 2:14 Tisera halor nam oilde Hiddekol; iyan oilde hiyan ziyan Asšur dešor fukottu di giye. Ar sair lombor hal oilde Efurat.
GEN 2:15 Bade Mabud Allaye manušware loi Eden baganot saš goribolla edde hiyanor dehafuna goribolla heṛe raikke.
GEN 2:16 Toi Mabud Allaye manušware endilla hokum diye, "Tui ei baganor hár gasor gula issa mozin hái faribi;
GEN 2:17 kintu neki bodi ahol gasottu no há foribo, kiyollahoile ze din tui hibattu háibi, he din tui moribi moribi."
GEN 2:18 Bade Mabud Allaye hodde, "Manušwalla ekela takonan iyan bala no, ãi hitalla hitar laikka ekzon modot goroya zuri banaiyum."
GEN 2:19 Toi Mabud Allaye meṛittu hár fahari zanuwar edde asmanor faik okkolore tiyar goijje; bade manušwaye hinore ki ki name ḍake, hiyan saibolla hin okkolore hibar hãse ainne, henot manušwaye ze zandar zanuwarore ze name ḍaikke, hibar he nam oiye.
GEN 2:20 Manušwaye hár górot falede zanuwar edde asmanor hár faik okkol edde fahari zanuwar okkolor nam raikke. Kintu he manušwalla hibar laikka ekzon modot goroya zuri fa no za.
GEN 2:21 Toi Mabud Allaye manušwar uwore bári gum forefan goijje; toi hiba gumot maze Allaye hibar šaiṭṭanar ãḍḍittu ekkan loiye edde hiyanot bodole gusto loi borai diye.
GEN 2:22 Mabud Allaye manušwattu kuli loilde aḍḍigan loi ek mayafuwa goijje, edde hibare manušwar hãse ainne.
GEN 2:23 Hetunot manušwaye hodde, "Ebar oiye! Iba ãr aḍḍir aḍḍi, ãr gustor gusto; hibare 'mayafuwa' ḍaka oibo, kiyollahoile ibare manušwar butottu lowa oiye."
GEN 2:24 Hetolla manuše hitar bab mare erizagoi edde hitar bou loi ek o, ar hitara duizon ek ga o.
GEN 2:25 Hẽtte manušwa edde hibar bou hitara dunizon lenḍa aššil, ar hiyanot hitarattu hono šorom nu aššil.
GEN 3:1 Mabud Allaye banaiyede zobinor hár fahari zandar zanuwar okkolottuwaro beši salak aššilde oilde haf, toi hite mayafuwaware hodde, "Allaye ki hãsa hoiye, 'Tũwara baganor hono gasor gula no háiyo'?"
GEN 3:2 Mayafuwawaye hafware hodde, "Ãra baganor gas okkol beggunor gula hái fari;
GEN 3:3 kintu baganor maze ze gas ase, hibar gular babute Allaye hoiye, 'Tũwara hibattu no háiyo, hin no suiyo, hen gorile moriba.'"
GEN 3:4 Toi hafe mayafuwaware hodde, "No, tũwara no moriba,
GEN 3:5 kiyollahoile Allaye zane ze, ze din tũwara hibattu háiba, hedin tũwarar suk kuli zaiboide edde neki bodi aholor giyan fai tũwara Allar ḍoil oizaibagoi."
GEN 3:6 Toi mayafuwawaye dekedde, he gasor gulawa háite bala oibo, ar hiba suke saite o šundor, hin bade giyan faibolla hoi oile o hon sa. Toi hibaye ho uggwa gula fari loi háiye, ar fũwati aššilde hibar zamai, hibare o diye, hibaye o háiye.
GEN 3:7 Henot hitara dunizonor suk kuli giyeoi, ar hitara ulongode hiyan buzi faijje; toi hitara ḍũir fata gãtiyore ga guijje.
GEN 3:8 Bade hazinnar ṭanḍa hawar ṭaimot Mabude bagonot gurafira goredde abaz hitara fuinne, toi manušwa edde hibar bou Mabud Allar sarmottu baganor gas okkolor butore lukai taikke.
GEN 3:9 Kintu Mabud Allaye manušware ḍaki hodde, "Tui hoṛe?"
GEN 3:10 Manušwaye hodde, "Ãi baganot tũwar abas fuinni, edde ãi ḍoraiyi; kiyollahoile ãi ulongo, ar ãi lukaiyi."
GEN 3:11 Toi Mabud Allaye hodde, "Tui ze ulongo iyan tore hone hoiye? Ze gasottu no háibolla mana goijjilam, tui ki hibattu gula háiyos?"
GEN 3:12 Henot manušwaye hodde, "Ze mayafuware tũi eṛe ãr fũwati diyo, hibaye ãre gasottu diye, ar ãi háiyi."
GEN 3:13 Toi Mabud Allaye he mayafuware hodde, "Tui in ki goijjos?" Mayafuwawaye hodde, "Hafe ãre dúha diye, edde ãi háiyi."
GEN 3:14 Bade Mabud Allaye hafore hodde, "Tui ei ham goijjosde hetolla, "Hár górowa zanuwar, edde fahari zandar zanuwar okkolor butore bodduwa tore! feṭ loi tor sola fira, ar háibi tui dúil tor zibonor hár din okkolot.
GEN 3:15 Ãi tui edde mayafuwar maze, tor bonšo edde hibar bongšor maze, dušmonai golai diyum; hite tor mata fiši dibo, ar tui hitar formurit kuṭ maribi."
GEN 3:16 Hibaye mayafuwaware hodde, "Ãi tui hamilor ṭaimot mosibot baraidiyum. tui beši zontrona loi fuwa biyaibi. Ar tor zamair uzu tottu issa oibo Ar hite tor uwore šašon solaibo."
GEN 3:17 Ar hibaye manušware hodde, "Tui tor bouwor hota doijjos, edde ze gasor babute ãi tore hokum dilam, 'Tui hibattu no háis,' hibattu gula háiyos, "Tor zoriya zobinore bodduwa; beši duk hošto gori, hiyanottu há foribo. tor zibonor hár din okkolot.
GEN 3:18 ar hiyane keṛa edde agasa okkol tolla fuṛaibo, ar maṛot zin baribo hin tui háibi.
GEN 3:19 mukottu gam zóraiyore, haiddo háibi meṛit firi nu aiyos foijjonto, tore to hentu lowa oiye, Kiyollahoile tui oilde dúil, ar dúilot tui firizaibi."
GEN 3:20 Bade manušwaye hibar bouwor nam diye Hawa, kiyollahoile hiba hár zinda okkolor ma oiye.
GEN 3:21 Mabud Allaye Adom edde hibar bouwolla samrar hor banaiye edde hitarare findai diye.
GEN 3:22 Tarfore Mabud Allaye hodde, "So, neki bodi aholor giyan fai manuš ãrar ekzonor ḍoil oiye, bala edde horaf zaner. Ebar hite zene hat barai diyore zibon gasor gula háiyore azibon basi tai no fare."
GEN 3:23 Toi Mabud Allaye manušware zentu lowa oil, Eden baganottu he meṛit saš goribolla niyolai diye.
GEN 3:24 Endilla gori hibaye manušware hentu niyolai diye, edde zibon gasor heṛe zaibar fõtot fahara dibolla Eden baganor fuk ḍakottu Karubi firista okkolore raikke, ar he fũwati heṛe ekkan zolonto toluwar raikke ziyan azibon guri guri taikke.
GEN 4:1 Adome hibar bou Hawa loi mille, toi hiba hamil oiye edde Kabilore zormo diye. Hibaye hodde, "Mabudor modote ãi ekzon manuš zormo di faijji."
GEN 4:2 Tarfore hibaye Kabilor bái Habilore zormo diye. Habil sool soroya, ar Kabil zobin saš goroya oiye.
GEN 4:3 Bade ek šome Kabile Mabudor hãse hodun zobinor fošol aniyore kurbani goijje.
GEN 4:4 Ar Habile o hitar nizor zanuwaror zákottu hougguwa foila zormor soolor sore ani hinor sorofwala gustore loi Mabudor hãse kurbani goijje. Mabude Habilore edde hitar kurbanire goisse,
GEN 4:5 kintu Kabil edde hitar kurbanire no gose. Henot Kabil kub beši gušša oiye ar hite nak muk hala gori roiye.
GEN 4:6 Toi Mabud Allaye Kabilore hodde, "Tui gušša kiyolla oiyos, ar nak muk kiyolla hala goijjos?
GEN 4:7 Tui o soiyigan goitti boli torgan o gosa no oito ne? Ar zodi soiyigan no goros, henoile to gunaye tore faibolla dorozat ai boi roiye, kintu tottu hiyanor uwore šašon sola foribo."
GEN 4:8 Tarfore ekdin Kabile Habilore hodde, "Aio, ãra bilot zai." Bade hitara bilot aššilde šomot, Kabile Habilore hamela goijje edde mari felaiye.
GEN 4:9 Hetunot Mabude Kabilore hodde, "Tor bái Habil hoṛe?" Kabile hodde, "Ãi hoi no fari, ãi ki ãr bái soroya ne hono?"
GEN 4:10 Mabude hodde, "Sa, tui in ki goijjios! Tor báiyor lou zobinottu tai ãr hãse hander.
GEN 4:11 Tor uwore gozob foijje. Tor báiyor lou tor hatottu ze zobine suišše he zobinor bodduwa ehon tor uwore foijje.
GEN 4:12 Tui zẽtte alsaš goribi hẽtte hine tore heto fól no dibo. Tui duniyait ziransara edde musafer oibi."
GEN 4:13 Toi Kabile Mabud Allare hodde, "Ei šaza ãlla bordašor bare oibo.
GEN 4:14 So, aijja tũi ãre enttu lorai dila, ziyanor zoriya ãi tũwar sukor arguwale oi zaiyumboi. Ãi zẽtte ziransara musafer oi duniyait gúriyum hẽtte zar sarme foriyum hite ãre kun gori faribo."
GEN 4:15 Kintu Mabude Kabilore hodde, "Etolla tore ze maribo, hitar uwore hãt gun daiya lowa oibo." Ar Mabude ekkan nišana diye, toi zene ze honokiye hitare faile no mare.
GEN 4:16 Bade Kabile Mabudor sarmottu zaigoi Eden baganor fuk ḍakottu Nod dešot taka šuru goijje.
GEN 4:17 Bade Kabile hitar bouwor hãse giye, toi hiba hamil oiye edde Honnukore zormo diye. Bade Kabile ekkan šohor bainde edde hitar futor nam mozin hiyanor nam Honnuk raikke.
GEN 4:18 Honnuke fut Iradore faiye, ar Irad Mehuyaelor baf oiye, Mehuyael Metúšayaelor baf oiye, ar Metúšayael Lemekor baf oiye.
GEN 4:19 Lemeke dui bou loiye, ekzonor nam Adah, oinno ar ekzonor nam Šilla.
GEN 4:20 Adaye Jabalore biyaiye. Hite aššilde ṭambu mari zanuwar faloya okkolor bongšor foila manuš.
GEN 4:21 Hitar báiyor nam oilde Jubal. Hite hanai edde baši bazoya bongšor foila manuš.
GEN 4:22 Ar Šillar feṛot Tubal-Kabil zormo oiye. Hite fitol edde lowar bout ḍoilla zontro okkol banaito. Tubal Kabilor boinor nam oilde Naamah.
GEN 4:23 Toi Lemeke hitar bouwainde hodde, "Oh Adah edde Šilla, tũwara ãr hota funo; Lemekor bouwain, ãr hota funo. Ãre ze ek manuše zohom diye, ze zuwane ãr gat hat tuille, hitare ãi marifelaiyi.
GEN 4:24 Zodi Kabilor kunor bodola hãtgun o, toile Lemekolla hoitor hãtgun."
GEN 4:25 Bade adome abar hibar bouwor hãse giye, ar hibaye ar ek futore zormo diye edde hitar nam raikke Set, "kiyollahoile Kabile Habilore kun goijje boli Allaye hitar zagat ãre ar ugguwa fuwa diye."
GEN 4:26 Setottu o ek fut zormo oiye, ar hite hitar nam raikke Enuš. Hẽtte manuš okkole Mabud Allar nam ḍaka šuru goijje.
GEN 5:1 Adomor bongšo nama oilde endilla. Allaye manušware banailde šomot, hibaye hibare nizor ḍoilla gori sirišti goijje.
GEN 5:2 Maya edde morod goriyore hibaye hitarare širišti goijje, ar sirišti gora oiyede hedin hibaye hitarare duwa goijje edde "Adom" nam diye.
GEN 5:3 Bade Adom ekšo tiriš bosor boyošot, hibar nizor ḍoilla edde hibar nizor súrotor ḍoilla ek fut oiye, ar hibar nam raikke Set.
GEN 5:4 Set zormo oi bade, adom aro aštošot bosor duniyait basi aššil edde aro bout futziyain okkol oil.
GEN 5:5 Adom muṭ nošo tiriš bosor baisse, toi bade hibar moron oiye.
GEN 5:6 Set ekšo fãs bosor boyošot, hiba Enušor baf oiye.
GEN 5:7 Enuš zormo oi bade, Set aro aštošo hãt bosor basi aššil edde aro futziyain okkol oiye.
GEN 5:8 Set muṭ nošo baro bosor baisse, toi bade hibar moron oiye.
GEN 5:9 Enuš nobboi bosor boyošot, hiba Kenanor baf oiye.
GEN 5:10 Kenan zormo oi bade, Enuš aro aštošo fundro bosor basi aššil edde aro futziyain okkol oiye.
GEN 5:11 Beggun mili nošo fãs bosor baisse, toi bade hibar moron oiye.
GEN 5:12 Kenane hoittor bosor boyošot, hiba Mahalalelor baf oiye.
GEN 5:13 Mahalalel zormo oi bade, Kenan aro aštošo sališ bosor basi aššil edde aro futziyain okkol oiye.
GEN 5:14 Beggun mili nošo doš bosor baisse, toi bade hibar moron oiye.
GEN 5:15 Mahalalel haiṭ fãs bosor boyošot, hiba Yaredor baf oiye.
GEN 5:16 Yared zomo oi bade, Mahalalel aro aštošo tiriš bosor basi aššil edde aro futziyain okkol oiye.
GEN 5:17 Beggun mili Mahalalel aštošo nobboi fãs bosor baisse, toi bade hibar moron oiye.
GEN 5:18 Yared ekšo haiṭ dui bosor boyošot, hibaye Honnukor baf oiye.
GEN 5:19 Honnuk zormo oi bade, Yared aro ašṭo šot bosor basi aššil edde aro futziyain okkol oiye.
GEN 5:20 Beggune mili Yared nošo haiṭ dui bosor baisse, toi bade hibar moron oiye.
GEN 5:21 Honnuk haiṭ fãs bosor boyošot, hibaye Metúšalar baf oiye.
GEN 5:22 Metúšalah zormo oi bade, Honnuk Allah loi tin šot bosor aza goijje edde aro futziyain okkol oiye.
GEN 5:23 Beggun mili Honnukor boyoš tinšo haiṭ fãs bosor oiye.
GEN 5:24 Honnuk Allah loi solito; tarfore hiba ar no takil, kiyollahoile Allaye hibare hibar hãse loigiyegoi.
GEN 5:25 Metúšalah ekšo aši hãt bosor boyošot, hibaye Lemekor baf oiye.
GEN 5:26 Lemek zormo oi bade, Metúšalah aro hãtšo aši dui bosor basi aššil edde aro futziyain okkol oiye.
GEN 5:27 Beggun mili Metúšalah nošo haiṭ no bosor baisse, toi bade hibar moron oiye.
GEN 5:28 Lemek ekšo aši dui bosor boyošot, hibattu ek fut oiye.
GEN 5:29 Ar hibaye hibar nam raikke Nuh, edde hodde, "Mabude bodduwa goijjede he meṛit ãrar ham edde hator koṭin haṛonit ite ãrare šantona dibo."
GEN 5:30 Nuh zormo oi bade, Lemeke aro fãs šo nobboi fãs bosor basi aššil edde aro bout futziyain okkol oiye.
GEN 5:31 Beggune Lemek hãt šo hoittor hãt bosor baisse, toi bade hibar moron oiye.
GEN 5:32 Tarfore Nuh fãs šot bosor oi bade, hibaye Šem, Ham, edde Yafetor baf oiye.
GEN 6:1 Ei bafe zehon duniyait manušor šoinkka beši owa šuru goijje edde bout mayafuwain okkol zormo oiye,
GEN 6:2 toi Allar futain okkole mainšor ziyain okkolore šundor dekiyore, zattu zare issa, hite hibare biya goijje.
GEN 6:3 Henot Mabude hodde, "Ãr Ruh insanor butore hamiša taki no zaibogoi, kiyollahoile hitara lou edde gustor; hitarar aiyu oibo ekšo kuri bosor."
GEN 6:4 Hẽtte, edde hiyar bade o duniyait folowan okkol aššil, Allar futain okkole mainšor ziyain okkol loi zehon mille, hitarattu fuwain okkol oiye, hitara zara aššil he furan hailla nam gora beši ḍõr ḍõr bir okkol.
GEN 6:5 Mabud Allaye sadde, duniyait manušor naformani beši ḍõr, edde hitarar dilor hár sinta bafona hár šomot bolke horafir uzu.
GEN 6:6 Hetolla, Mabude duniyait manuš banaiyede hiyan loi bezar oiye, edde dile duk faiye.
GEN 6:7 Toi Mabude hodde, "Ãi ze manuš zati sirišti goijji, hinore duniyaittu fũsi felaiyum; manušottu loti zandar zanuwar foijjonto, buke aṛede zandar edde asmanor tole faik okkolore o; kiyollahoile ãi hitarare sirišti goriyore ãr dile duk far."
GEN 6:8 Kintu Nuhuye Allar torfottu doya faiye.
GEN 6:9 In oilde Nuhur bongšor kahani. Nuh ekzon forhesgar manuš aššil. He šomot manuš okkolor butore hiba aššilde ekzon haṭi manuš. Nuhuttu Allar loi aza zugazug aššil.
GEN 6:10 Nuhuttu Šem, Ham edde Yafet name tin fut aššil.
GEN 6:11 Hẽtte Allar nozorot duniyaigan horaf oigiyegoi edde zai-zulume boriuiṭṭe.
GEN 6:12 Allaye duniyair mikka saiye, ar so, hiyan horaf oigiyegoi, haron duniyair hár mainše hitarar kufõt giyegoi.
GEN 6:13 Toi Allaye Nuhure hodde, "Hár zandaror šeš hal ãr sarme aišše, kiyollahoile hitarar duwara duniyai zulume boriuiṭṭe; ar sa, ãi duniyair fũwati hitarare dongšo gorifelaiyum.
GEN 6:14 Tui gupér gas diyore ekkan zahaz tiyar gor; hiyanor butore kamera okkol goribi, edde hiyanor butore baire kuldar ḍoli dibi.
GEN 6:15 Endilla gori hiyan tiyar gora foribo: Zahazsan lamba tin šot hat, fatari šoṛa fõnzaš hat, ar hiyan usol oibo tiriš hat.
GEN 6:16 Ar zahazor sanir ek hat tolottu zanala tiyar goribi edde zahazor ḍakottu doroza rakibi; hiyanor foila, dusora, edde tisera ṭala gori tiyar gora foribo.
GEN 6:17 Ar sa, asmanor tole zeto ḍoilla zandar niyaš foran loi basi ase, hitara beggun dongšo oibolla ãi duniyait ek fanir tuwan aniyum, Duniyair hár zandar mori zaiboi.
GEN 6:18 Kintu tor loi ãi ãr wadar sukti buwaiyum. Tui zai zahazot gólibi. Ar tor fũwati tor futain okkol edde tor bou edde tor futaindor bouwain okkol takibo.
GEN 6:19 Ar lou gustowala zandar miyala modda zura zura tor fũwati zinda takibolla zahazot loibi.
GEN 6:20 Hár zator faik okkolottu, hár zator zandar zanuwar okkolottu edde hár zator buke aṛede zandar okkolottu foran basaibolla ek ek zura tor hãse aibo.
GEN 6:21 Tui háibar hár ḍoilla ziniš okkol loi dola gori rakibi. Hin oibode tor edde hitarar haiddo."
GEN 6:22 Nuhuye hendilla goijje, Allaye hokum dilde mozin hibaye hár kissu goijje.
GEN 7:1 Toi Mabude Nuhure hodde, "Tui edde tor fura gór ṭiya beggune zahazot golo, kiyollahoile ei halor manuš okkolor butore ãr sarme šude tore forhesgar lot faiyi.
GEN 7:2 Tottu fotti zator paki zanuwar okkolottu, zur milai, hãt zura gori, ar fotti zator napaki zanuwar okkolottu, zur milai, ek zura gori lowa foribo.
GEN 7:3 Ar asmanor faik okkolottu o hendilla gori, zur milai, hãt zura gori tor fũwati lowa foribo. Duniyait hitarar bongšo basai rakibolla hendilla goribi.
GEN 7:4 Kiyollahoile ar hãt din bade ãi duniyait sališ din sališ rait zór diyat rakium. Henot ãr sirištir hár zandar okkolore duniyaittu fũsi felaiyum."
GEN 7:5 Toi Mabude Nuhure hokum dilde mozin hibaye hár kissu goijje.
GEN 7:6 Duniyait fanir tuwan šuru oilde šomot Nuhur boyoš so šot bosor.
GEN 7:7 Fanir bottuwanottu uddar faibolla Nuhuye hibar bou, futain ar futaindor bouwain okkol loi zahazot góille.
GEN 7:8 Ar paki zanuwar okkolottu, napaki zanuwar okkolottu, faik okkolottu edde meṛit buke aṛede hár kissu,
GEN 7:9 zur zur Nuhur hãse aiyore zahazot góille, Allaye Nuhure hokum dilde mozin.
GEN 7:10 Ar he hãt din farai zaigoi bade duniyait tuwanor fani aišše.
GEN 7:11 Nuhur boyoš sošot bosor furaiyede he bosoror dui maš hõtoro dinor din, atikka meṛir tolottu beša beši fani uṛa šuru goijje, ar zóror fani zen asmanot faṛon doijje.
GEN 7:12 Sališ din sališ rait dori duniyair uwore zór forat roiye.
GEN 7:13 He din Nuh, Šem, Ham, Yafet name Nuhur futain okkol, edde hitarar fũwati Nuhur bou edde futor bouwain okkol zahazot góille.
GEN 7:14 Ar hitarar fũwati fotti zator ek ek zura gori fahari edde górwali zanuwar edde buke aṛede zandar, ar hár ḍoilla faik okkol o aššil.
GEN 7:15 Zibon niyaš loi basi roiyede hár zandar okkol zura zura Nuhur hãse zai zahazot goillil.
GEN 7:16 Hár zanuwar okkol, zandar ziniš okkol miyala edde morod mili zahazot uiṭṭe, ode ode Allaye Nuhure hokum dilde mozin. Toi Mabude zahazor dorozagan bon gori diye.
GEN 7:17 Bade sališ din mula duniyait maze tuwanor fani bariuṛat roiye. Tuwanor fani barizaiyore zahazsan meṛir uwottu fanit baši uiṭṭe.
GEN 7:18 Toi fani uiṭṭe edde duniyait beša beši fani bari giyegoi ar zahazsan fanir uwore baša šuru goijje.
GEN 7:19 Duiniyair uwore tuwanor fani eto beši uiṭṭe, hinor duwara asmanor nisor ḍõr ḍõr fahar okkolore beggunore ḍufaifelaiye.
GEN 7:20 Fahar okkol ḍufi bade o fani aro fundro hat uworor mikka uiṭṭe.
GEN 7:21 Henor zoriya duniyait solafira gorede hár zandar, faik, górot falede edde fahari zanuwar okkol, duniyait zãk bandi sorede šoṛo zandar okkol, ar hár manuš okkol mori giyegoi.
GEN 7:22 Fuwana zobinor uwore zibon niyaš loi basi aššilde zandar okkol beggun mori giyegoi.
GEN 7:23 Endilla gori hibaye zobinor bukor hár zandar fũsifelaiye, manuš, zanuwar, buke aṛede zandar okkol edde asmanor faik duniyaittu saf oigiyegoi. Šude Nuh edde hibare fũwati zara zahazot aššil hitara basi roiye.
GEN 7:24 Tuwanor faniye duniyai ek šo fõnzaš din ḍufi aššil.
GEN 8:1 Kintu Allaye Nuh edde hibar fũwati zahazot aššilde hár zandar okkolore monot raikke, Allaye duniyait bataš ba baiye, henot fani homa šuru goijje.
GEN 8:2 Ar meṛir tolottu fani uṛa edde asmanor faṛa okkol bondo oi giyegoi, asmanottu zór diya o tamigilgoi.
GEN 8:3 Ar fani meṛir uwottu lami zat taikke; ekšo fõnzaš din šeše fani bout homigiyegoi,
GEN 8:4 edde hãt maš hõtoro dinor din zahassan Ararot faharor uwore bazigiyegoi.
GEN 8:5 Bade doš maš foijjonto fani homat roiye; he doš mašor foila dinot faharor tuli okkol dehagiye.
GEN 8:6 Ar sališ din faraizaigoi bade, Nuhuye zahazot ze zanala goijjil, hiyan hibaye kuille,
GEN 8:7 edde uggwa hawa baire defeṛaiye, henot hiba meṛir uwottu fani fuwai no zagoi foijjonto aiya zat gorat roiye.
GEN 8:8 Bade meṛir uwottu fani homigiyegoi ne, hiyan saibolla, hibaye uggwa hoitor baire defeṛaiye.
GEN 8:9 Kintu hẽtte o šara duniyair uwore fani aššil boli hoitorguwaye hono mikka ṭeng rakibar zaga no fa, hetolla hibar hãse zahazot uwafes firi aišše. Ar hibaye hat niyolaidiyore hibare doijje edde zahazor butore nizor hãse raikke.
GEN 8:10 Toi hibaye aro hãt din entezar goijje, bade he hoitorguware zahazottu abar baire defeṛaiye.
GEN 8:11 Hazinna hoitorguwa hibar hãse firi aišše; ar so, hibar ṭuṛot ugguwa tottoza zaitun fata aššil; iyanot Nuhuye buzi faijje, ze meṛir uwottu fani homi giyegoi.
GEN 8:12 Toi hibaye aro hãt din entezar goijje, he hoitorguware abar baire defeṛaiye, edde hiba hibar hãse ar uwafes firi nu aiye.
GEN 8:13 Nuhor boyoš sošo ek bosoror foila mašor foila dinor din meṛir uwottu fani fuwaigiyegoi; Toi Nuhuye zahazor sáni kulifelaiye edde baire saiye, ar so, meṛir tola fuwaigiyegoi.
GEN 8:14 Bade dusora mašor ek kuri hãt dinor din meṛi fuwaigiyegoi.
GEN 8:15 Toi Allaye Nuhure hodde,
GEN 8:16 "Tui tor bou ar tor futain edde hitarar bouwain okkolore loi zahazottu niyoli zagoi.
GEN 8:17 Ar tor fũwati asede hár faik, zanuwar edde buke aṛede zandar, zeto zandar zanuwar ase, hin beggunore tor fũwati niyolai loiai, hitara duniyaire bori tulok, edde fólwala ok edde beši ok."
GEN 8:18 Toi Nuhuye hibar bou ar futain edde hitarar bouwain okkol beggunore loi zahazottu niyoli aišše.
GEN 8:19 Ar zar zar zat mozin hár fahari zanuwar edde hár gorwali zanuwar, hár faik, ar meṛir uwore buke solafira gorede hár kissu, zahazottu niyoli aišše.
GEN 8:20 Tarfore Nuhuye Mabudolla ekkan kurbangah tiyar goijje edde fotti zator paki zanuwar edde faik okkolottu hougguwa loi hiyanor uwore fura-kurbani okkol kurbani goijje.
GEN 8:21 Mabud he kurbanir kušbot kuši oiye edde mone mone hodde: "Manušolla ãi ar hono din meṛire bodduwa no diyum, zodi o manušor dil zuwan hale loti horaf. Ar zendilla ãi ehon goijji, hendilla ãi ar hár zandarore dongšo no goriyum.
GEN 8:22 "Zetodin duniyai takibo, niyom mozin biz owa edde fošol haṛa, ṭanḍa edde gorom, šit hal edde gorom hal, din edde rait, owa honodin no tamibo."
GEN 9:1 Allaye Nuh edde hibar futaindore duwa goriyore hodde, "Fólwala o, edde beši o edde duniyai furon goro.
GEN 9:2 Duniyair hár zandar zanuwar okkol, edde asmanor hár faik okkol, ar zobinot buke aṛede zandar okkol, ar doriyar hár mas okkol tũwarar ḍor edde bóiye sola fira goribo; ar hin okkolore tũwarar hatot diya oiye.
GEN 9:3 Hár kissu ziyãta edde lorasora gorede zanuwar okkol tũwaralla haiddo oibo. Ãi age zendilla tũwarare hak šobzi haiddo hisabe diyilam hendilla ehon in okkol o dilam.
GEN 9:4 "Kintu foranwala gusto mani lou šoho gusto no há foribo.
GEN 9:5 Honokiye zodi tũwarare kun gore toile ãi hameka tũwarar louwor bodole hitar lou mani hitar foranor dabi goriyum. Hiba fokšu ok ba manuš ok. Ar manušor foran ze manuše lo, hitar foran o lowa oibo, iyan ãr dabi.
GEN 9:6 "Manušor lou ze bair gore, manuše o hitar lou bair goribo, kiyollahoile Allaye, manušore nizor súrot loi banaiye.
GEN 9:7 Ar tũwara fólwala o, edde beši o, duniyair sairo mikka šiṛi foro edde heṛe o aro beši o."
GEN 9:8 Bade Allaye Nuh edde hibar futaindore hodde:
GEN 9:9 "So, tũwara edde tũwarar bongšo okkol loi edde tũwarar fũwati asede hár zandar zanuwar okkol,
GEN 9:10 faik fokšu, górwali zanuwar edde fahari zanuwar, duniyait zeto ḍoilla zandar zanuwar okkol zahazottu niyoli aišše, hitara loi ãi ãr wadar sukti buwaiyum.
GEN 9:11 Ãi tũwarar loi ãr wadar sukti buwair: Ar honodin endilla no oibo; fanir bottuwanor duwara hár foranwala zandar okkolore dongšo gora no oibo. Ar duniyaire dongšo gorifelaibolla ar hono din fanir bottuwan no oibo."
GEN 9:12 Allaye aro hodde, "Tũwara edde tũwarar fũwati asede hár zandar zanuwar okkol edde ãr maze ze wadar sukti buwair, hiyanor sinno oilde iyan, ziyan bongšor bade bongšo dori solat takibo,
GEN 9:13 he bebostar sinno hisabe miyulat, ãi ãr donu dehaiyum. Hiyan oibo duniyai loi, ãr he wadar suktir sinno.
GEN 9:14 Ãi zẽtte duniyair uwore miyula dola goriyum, hẽtte donugan miyulat deha dibo,
GEN 9:15 henot tũwara edde hár zandar zanuwar loi, ãr ei wadar hota ãi monot goriyum. Ar hono din hár zandar dongšo oibolla fanir tuwan no oibo.
GEN 9:16 Miyulat zehon donugan deha zaibo, henot ãi hiyanor mikka saiyum, henot duniyair hár zandar okkol loi, ãr azibonor wadare monot goriyum."
GEN 9:17 Tarfore Allaye Nuhure hodde, "Duniyait hár zandar okkol loi ãi buwaiyide wadar suktir sinno oilde iyan."
GEN 9:18 Nuhur ze futain okkol zahazottu niyoli aišše, hitara oilde Šem, Ham edde Yafet. (Ham aššilde Kenanor baf.)
GEN 9:19 Itara oilde Nuhur futain okkol; itarar bongšo šara duniyai sorai gilgoi.
GEN 9:20 Bade Nuhuye al saš gora šuru goijje edde ekkan ãngur keti goijje.
GEN 9:21 Hibaye ekdin šoraf fiyore matal oiye edde nizor ṭambur butore lenḍa oi fori roiye.
GEN 9:22 Kenanor baf Hame hitar bafor ei abosta deikke edde baire zai hitar dui báiyore hin zanaiye.
GEN 9:23 Kintu Šem edde Yafete ekkan hor handot felai loiyore fissa aṛi zaiyore hitarar bafor lenḍa gare guridiye. Hitarar muk fissa firaiya aššilde hetolla hitara bafor lenḍa gare no deke.
GEN 9:24 Bade Nuh šorafor gúmottu uṛiyore hibar šoṛo fute hiba loi goijjede he befare zani faijje,
GEN 9:25 hibaye hodde, "Kenanore bodduwa! Hite hitar báiyaindor hãse gulamor gulam ok!"
GEN 9:26 Hibaye aro hodde, "Šemor Allah Mabudor tarif ok! Kenan Šemor gulam ok!
GEN 9:27 Allaye gorok, Yafetor eleha barok; Hite Šemor ṭambur tole takok, Ar Kenan hitar gulam bonok."
GEN 9:28 Bor tuwan bade Nuhuye aro tin šo fõnzaš bosor baisse.
GEN 9:29 Beggun mili Nuh šaro no šot bosor baisse, toi bade hibar moron oiye.
GEN 10:1 In oilde Nuhur futain, Šem, Ham edde Yafetor bongšor kahani, bor tuwan bade hitara zarattu futain okkol oil.
GEN 10:2 Yafetor futain okkol oilde: Gumer, Magog, Madai, Javan, Tubal, Mešek edde Tiraš.
GEN 10:3 Gumeror futain okkol oilde: Aškenaz, Ripát edde Togarmah.
GEN 10:4 Javanor futain okkol oilde: Elišah, Toršiš, Kittim edde Dodanim.
GEN 10:5 (doriyar ḍiyat takoya ei bongšo okkolottu zar zar zuban, gór edde zati okkol mozin bout deš okkolot šiṛi giyegoi.)
GEN 10:6 Hamor futain okkol oilde: Kuš, Mišor, Puṭ edde Kenan.
GEN 10:7 Kušor futain okkol oilde: Seba, Havilah, Sabta, Raamah edde Sabteka. Raamar futain okkol oilde: Seba edde Dedan.
GEN 10:8 Kuš Nimrudor baf oiye, ze duniyait foila folowan oil.
GEN 10:9 Hite aššilde Mabudor sarme ek folowan šiyari; hetolla iyan endilla ho, "Nimrudor ḍoil Mabudor sarme ekzon folowan šiyari"
GEN 10:10 Sinearor Babel, Erek, Akkad edde Kalneh, ei zaga okkol oilde foila hitar raijjor ongšo.
GEN 10:11 He dešottu hite Asšurot zaiyore Nineveh, Rehobot-Ir, Kalah
GEN 10:12 edde Resen bainde, ziyan Nineveh edde Kalar maza mazi, ziyan oilde ekkan ḍõr šohor.
GEN 10:13 Mišoror bafe Ludiyo, Anamiyo, Lehabiyo, Noftuhiyo,
GEN 10:14 Patrušiyo, Kasluhiyo, (hitara zarattu Filistini okkol niyoli aišše.) edde Kaptíyo okkol,
GEN 10:15 Kenan oiyede hibar foila fut Sidonor baf, tarfore Hetor,
GEN 10:16 Zebušiyo, Amorittiyo, edde Girgašiyo,
GEN 10:17 Hibbiyo, Arkiyo, edde Siniyo,
GEN 10:18 Arvadiyo, Zemariyo, edde Hamatiyo. Aro bade zaiyore Kenaniyo zatir bongšo okkol sorai foijjil.
GEN 10:19 Sidon šohorottu Gerar gẽši giyede rastat Gaza foijjonto edde Gaza šohorottu Súdum, Gumarrah, Admah edde Zeboyim zaibar fõt Laša foijjonto Kenaniyo okkolor dešor šima aššil.
GEN 10:20 Itara oilde nizor nizor gušti, baša edde zati mozin Hamor bongšor manuš.
GEN 10:21 Yafetor bor bái Šemottu o futziyain oiye. Šem aššilde Eberor futain okkolor fordada.
GEN 10:22 Šemor futain oilde: Elam, Asšur, Arpákšad, Lud edde Aram.
GEN 10:23 Aramor futain okkol oilde: Uz, Hul, Getér edde Maš.
GEN 10:24 Arpákšad Šelar baf oiye, Šelah Eberor baf oiye.
GEN 10:25 Eberottu dui fut: Ekzonor nam aššil Feleg, kiyollahoile hitar ṭaimot duniyai bag oil; hitar báiyor nam aššil Joktan.
GEN 10:26 Joktan aššilde itarar baf Almodad, Šelef, Hasarmaveth, Jerah,
GEN 10:27 Hadoram, Uzal, Diklah,
GEN 10:28 Obal, Abimael, Šeba,
GEN 10:29 Ofir, Havilah edde Jobab. Itara beggun aššilde Joktanor futain okkol.
GEN 10:30 (Mešattu fuk mikka Sefar fahari eleha okkolot hitara bošobaš goitto.)
GEN 10:31 Foribar, baša, deš edde zati hisabe itara oilde Šemor bongšor manuš.
GEN 10:32 Ar bongšo edde zati mozin itara oilde Nuhur futaindor bongšodor. Bor tuwan bade itararar butottu bout zati okkol duniyait sorai gilgoi.
GEN 11:1 Hẽttiyaror din okkolot šara duniyair mainše šude ek zubanot hota hoito edde hitarar baša aššilde o ek ḍoilla.
GEN 11:2 Bade hitara fuk mikka agguwai zaite zaite Sinear dešot ekkan fuwainna zaga faiye edde heṛe hitara bošoti loiye.
GEN 11:3 Hitara ekzone ar ekzonore hodde, "Aiyo, ãra iṭ banai edde hinore furaidi doro gori!" Hen hoi hitara fattoror bodole iṭ edde mosollar bodole duna bebar goijje.
GEN 11:4 Hitara aro hodde, "Aiyo, ãra ekkan ãralla šohor banai ar en ekkan usol gór banai ziyanor tuliye asman suibo, toi zene ãrar nam mošuhor o, edde ãrattu šara duniyait šiṛašitta oizagoi no fore!"
GEN 11:5 Tarfore manuš okkole ze šohor edde usol gór bainde, hiyan saibolla Mabud nise laimme,
GEN 11:6 edde hodde, "So, itara beggun ek zati edde ek zubanot hota hoiya okkol, itara ei ham gora šuru goijje, bade zaiyore itara ze kissu goribolla ereda loibo, ošombob kissu no oibo.
GEN 11:7 Hetolla aiyo, ãra nise zai hitarar zubanore gulmal goridigoi toi zene hitara ekzone ar oinno zonor hota buzi no fare."
GEN 11:8 Tarfore Mabude he zagattu hitarare duniyair hár mikka šiṛašitta gori diye. Henot hitarar šohor banaibar ham bondo oi giyegoi.
GEN 11:9 Etolla he zagar nam oiyede Babel, ziyanor mani gulmal, haron Mabude šomosto duniyair zubanot gulmal bazaidiye. Mabude manuš okkolore hentu duniyair hár mikka šiṛašitta gori diye.
GEN 11:10 In oilde Šemor bongšo okkolor kahani. Tuwan zai dui bosor bade, Šemor boyoš ekšot bosor zẽtte oiye, hiba Arpákšador baf oiye.
GEN 11:11 Ar Šem Arpákšador baf oi bade, hiba aro fãs šot bosor basi aššil edde aro bout futziyain okkol oiye.
GEN 11:12 Arpákšad tiriš fãs bosor boyošot, hiba Šelar baf oiye.
GEN 11:13 Šelar baf oi bade, Arpákšad aro sair šo tin bosor basi aššil edde aro bout futziyain okkol oiye.
GEN 11:14 Šelah tiriš bosor boyošot, hiba Eberor baf oiye.
GEN 11:15 Ar Eberor baf oi bade, Šelah aro sair šo tin bosor basi aššil edde aro bout futziyain okkol oiye.
GEN 11:16 Eber tiriš sair bosor boyošot, hiba Felegor baf oiye.
GEN 11:17 Ar Felegor baf oi bade, Eber aro sair šo tiriš bosor basi aššil edde aro bout futziyain okkol oiye.
GEN 11:18 Feleg tiriš bosor boyošot, hiba Reuror baf oiye.
GEN 11:19 Reuror baf oi bade, Feleg dui šo no bosor basi aššil edde aro bout futziyain okkol oiye.
GEN 11:20 Reu tiriš dui bosor boyošot, Serugor baf oiye.
GEN 11:21 Serugor baf oi bade, Reu aro dui šo hãt bosor basi aššil edde aro bout futziyain okkol oiye.
GEN 11:22 Serug tiriš bosor boyošot, hiba Nahuror baf oiye.
GEN 11:23 Nahuror baf oi bade, Serug aro dui šo bosor basi aššil edde aro bout futziyain okkol oiye.
GEN 11:24 Nahur ek kuri no bosor boyošot, hiba Ṭerar baf oiye.
GEN 11:25 Ṭerar baf oi bade, Nahur aro ekšo unnuš bosor basi aššil edde aro bout futziyain okkol oiye.
GEN 11:26 Ṭerah hoittor bosor boyošot, hiba Ibraim, Nahur edde Haranor baf oiye.
GEN 11:27 In oilde Ṭerar bongšor kahani. Ṭerah aššilde Ibraim, Nahur edde Haranor baf. Ar Haran Lutor baf oiye.
GEN 11:28 Kintu Haran hibar baf Ṭerar sarme hibar zormostan, Kaldiyar Ur šohorot moron oiye.
GEN 11:29 Ibraim edde Nahur dunizone biya goijjil; Ibraimor bouwor nam aššil Sarai, ar Nahuror bou aššilde Haranor zi Milka, ar Haran aššilde Milka edde Jiskar baf.
GEN 11:30 Sarai bázá aššil, hibattu hono futziyain no o.
GEN 11:31 Ṭeraye hibar fut Ibraim edde hibar nati mani Haranor fut Lut edde hibar futor bou mani Ibraimor bou Saraire fũwati loiye edde itara beggune Kenan dešot zaibolla Kaldiyar Ur šohorottu ruwana diye. Ar hitara Harran foijjonto aiyore heṛe bošoti loiye.
GEN 11:32 Ṭerah dui šo fãs bosor baisse, edde Harranot Ṭerar moron oiye.
GEN 12:1 Mabude Ibraimore hodde, "Tui tor nizor deš, tor egena gušti edde tor bafor gór sari, ãi ze dešot tore dehaiyum tui heṛe za.
GEN 12:2 "Ãi tore ek ḍõr zati goriyum, edde ãi tore duwa goriyum; Ãi tor namore ḍõr goriyum, edde tui oinno zonolla rahamot oibi.
GEN 12:3 Zara tore duwa goribo, ãi hitarare duwa goriyum, ar zara tore bodduwa dibo, ãi hitarare bodduwa diyum. duniyair fotti zatiye tor duwara duwa faibo."
GEN 12:4 Toi Mabude hoiyede mozin Ibraime baisa diye, ar Lut o hibar fũwati giye. Harranottu niyoli zargoide šomot Ibraimor boyoš oilde hoittor fãs bosor.
GEN 12:5 Ibraime hibar bou Saraire edde báiyor fut Lutore, ar hitara Harranot ze dón šombotti hamail, ze gulam okkol fail, hin beggun loiyore Kenan dešot zaibolla baisa diye, toi hitara Kenanot fõisse.
GEN 12:6 Ar Ibraime deš bai zaite Šekimot he Paki zaga Mure-elun gas foijjonto giye. Hẽtte Kenaniyo okkol he dešot aššil.
GEN 12:7 Tarfore Mabude Ibraimore deha diye edde hibare hodde, "Ei dešgan ãi tor bongšore diyum." Toi Ibraime hibare deha diyede he Mabudor mutallek heṛe ekkan kurbangah tiyar goijje.
GEN 12:8 Bade hibaye hentu Betelor fuke fahari elehat agguwai zaiyore fosimottu Betel ar fukottu Ai šohoror maza mazi ek zagat hibar ṭambu gãijje. Heṛe hibaye Mabudor mutallek ekkan kurbangah tiyar goijje edde Mabudor name ḍaikke.
GEN 12:9 Tarfore Ibraime hentu baisa diyore doine Negevor mikka zat roiye.
GEN 12:10 Bade dešot ek raṭ oiye, toi Ibraime lamat Mišorot forbaš goribolla baisa diye; kiyollahoile Kenan dešot koṭin raṭ oil.
GEN 12:11 Ar Ibraim zehon Mišoror hãsa haši aišše, hibaye hibar bou Saraire hodde, "Sa, ãi zani, tui kub šundori.
GEN 12:12 Tore zẽtte Mišoriyo okkole dekibo, hitara hoibo, 'Iba itar bou.' Toi hitara tore zinda rakibo kintu ãre mari felaibo.
GEN 12:13 Hetolla hitarare endilla hois ze, tui ãr boin, toi zene tor hatire hitara ãr loi bala bebohar gore, ar tor zoriya ãr foran basi zagoi."
GEN 12:14 Ibraim zehon Mišorot góille Mišoriyo okkole deikke ze Sarai kub šundori.
GEN 12:15 Feruwanor ofisar okkole hibare dekiyore hitara Feruwanor hãse hibar tarif goijje; toi hibare raz moholot loi za oiye.
GEN 12:16 Ar hibar hatire hite Ibraim loi bala bebohar goijje, ar henot hibaye bout sool, goru, gada, gadi, uṭ edde gulam edde bandi okkol faiye.
GEN 12:17 Kintu Ibraimor bou, Sarailla boli Mabude Feruwan edde hitar foribaror uwore koṭin bola okkol goṭaiye.
GEN 12:18 Toi Feruwane Ibraimore ḍaki ainne edde hodde, "Tũi ãr loi endilla ka goijjio? Hiba tũwar boude hiyan tũi ãre kiyolla no ho?
GEN 12:19 Tũi 'Iba ãr boin' kiyolla hoiyo, toi ãi hibare biya goribolla loi annilam? So, doro tũwar bou, hibare lo edde zogoi!"
GEN 12:20 Bade Feruwane hitar manuš okkolore Ibraimor babute hokum diye, ar hitara Ibraimor šombotti šoho, hibare edde hibar bouwore bidai diye.
GEN 13:1 Toi Ibraime hibar bou edde hibar hár kissu loiyore Mišorottu niyoli zai Negevot giye, ar Lut o hibar fũwati aššil.
GEN 13:2 Ibraim goru, soole edde šuna rufaye kub beši tuwangor aššil.
GEN 13:3 Bade hibaye doine Negevottu ek zagattu ar ek zagat zaite zaite Betel foijjonto aišše, Betel edde Aior maza mazi ze zagat age hibar ṭambu aššil,
GEN 13:4 edde zeṛe hibaye foila kurbangah tiyar goijjil. Heṛe Ibraime Mabudor nam ḍaikke.
GEN 13:5 Ar Ibraimor fũwati giyede, Lutottu o, goru sool edde ṭambu okkol aššil.
GEN 13:6 Kintu zagaganot hitara dunizon ekotro bošoti gora šombob no o, kiyollahoile hitarar šombotti eto oṭṭalika aššil ze hitara ekku fũwati taki no fare.
GEN 13:7 Ar Ibraimor zanuwar soroya edde Lutor zanuwar soroya okkolor maze hoijja uiṭṭe. Ar he šomot Kenaniyo edde Perišiyo okkol o he dešot bošoti gorito.
GEN 13:8 Toi Ibraime Lutore hodde, "Sa, tui edde ãr maze, tor zanuwar soroya edde ãr zanuwar soroya okkolor maze hono hoijja no ok, kiyollahoile ãra to egena.
GEN 13:9 Tor sarme fura deš udda fori no take ne? Meherbani gori tui ãttu alok oizagoi! Tui zodi ban ḍaikka zos ãi den ḍaikka zaiyum, ar zodi tui den ḍaikka zos ãi ban ḍaikka zaiyum."
GEN 13:10 Lute suk tuli sadde Zordanor fura niso zaga, Soar foijjonto hár zaga zola edde saite Mabudor baganor ḍoilla otóba Mišoror ḍoilla. (Iyan aššilde Mabude Súdum edde Gumorrare dongšo goribare age.)
GEN 13:11 Hetolla Lute Zordanor hár elehare nizolla basi loiyore fuk mikka giyegoi. Ei bafe hitara ekzon loi arekzon alok oiye.
GEN 13:12 Ibraim Kenan dešot ar Lute he elehar niso zagar šohorgunot edde Súdum foijjonto ṭambu maijje.
GEN 13:13 Súdum šohoror manuš okkol aššilde beši horaf edde Mabudor berudde beša beši guna gorat aššil.
GEN 13:14 Lut Ibraim loi alok oizaigoi bade Mabude Ibraimore hodde, "Tui ze zagat asos hentu suk tuli uttor doin fuk fosim beggulla sa,
GEN 13:15 haron tui ze zaga okkol dehor hin ãi tore edde tor bongšore azibonolla diyum.
GEN 13:16 Ar duniyair dúilor ḍoilla tor bongšo baraiyum; honokiye zodi duniyair dúilore goni fare, toile tor bongšore o gona zaibo.
GEN 13:17 Uṭ, ei dešganor lamba edde fatari gurisa, kiyollahoile ãi tore iyan diyum."
GEN 13:18 Toi Ibraime ṭambu hãri loiyore Hebronot asede Mamre elun gas bonor ḍake zaiyore bošoti goijje, edde heṛe Mabudor mutallek ekkan kurbangah tiyar goijje.
GEN 14:1 He hár din okkolot zẽtte Sinearor badša Amrapél, Ellasaror badša Aryok, Elamor badša Kedor-Laomer edde Goyimor badša Tidal,
GEN 14:2 itara Súdumor badša Bera, Gumorrar badša Birša, Admaror badša Šinab, Zeboyimor badša Šemebor edde Belar (mani Soaror) badšar berudde larai goijje.
GEN 14:3 Ei fãszon badšaye hitarar šoinno okkol beggunore ekkui fũwati gori Siddimor ḍeilot giye, (ziyanore mora doriya o ho.)
GEN 14:4 Itara baro bosor foijjonto Kedor-Laomeror hokumotor tole aššil, kintu tero bosorot aiyore hitara beruddota goijje.
GEN 14:5 Bade soiddo bosoror ṭaimot Kedor-Laomor edde hitar fũwajja badša okkole zaiyore Ašterot-Karnayimot Refaitiyo okkolore, Hamot Zuziyo okkolore, Šaveh Kiryatayimot Emittiyo okkolore,
GEN 14:6 enki moidanor ḍake asede El-Paran foijjonto zaiyore Seir fahari Horittiyo okkolore, hamela goijje.
GEN 14:7 Bade hitara hentu firi aiyore En-Mišpáṭ (ziyanore ehon Kadeš) heṛe aišše, edde hitara Amalekiyo okkolor fura dešore edde Hasseson-Tamarot takitode Amorittiyo okkolore hõṛai felaiye.
GEN 14:8 Ar Súdumor badša, Gumorrar badša, Admar badša, Zeboyimor badša, edde Belar (ziyan ehon Soar) badša, itara niyoli giye edde zuddolla hitarar šoinno okkolore Siddim ḍeilot tiya goraiye,
GEN 14:9 Elamor Kedor-Laomor badša, Goyimor Tidal badša, Sinearot Amrapél badša edde Ellasarot Aryok badša, fãszon sair zon badša loi zuddo goribolla.
GEN 14:10 Siddimor ḍeilot beša beši dúnar gãra okkol aiššil; ar Súdum edde Gumorrar badša okkol dárgoide šomot, hitara heṛe fori giyegoi, ar bakigun faharor uzu dáigiyegoi.
GEN 14:11 Toi ei sair badšaye Súdum edde Gumorrar hár šombotti edde hitarar haiddo luṭ gori loi hentu giyegoi.
GEN 14:12 Ar hitara Ibraimor bái fut Lut edde hibar dón šombotti loigiyegoi, kiyollahoile hiba Súdumot bošoti gorat aššil.
GEN 14:13 Toi dáizaigoi fajjilde ekzone aiyore Ibroni Ibraimore hóborgan hoiye. He šomot hiba Amorittiyo Mamrer elun gas bonor ḍake bošobaš gorat goijjil, Mamre aššilde Iškol edde Aneror bái, hitara Ibraim loi ekdol aššil.
GEN 14:14 Ibraime zehon fuinne ze hibar báiyor futore bondi gori loi giyegoi, hetunot hibaye górot zormo oiyede tin šo aṛaro zon domaya gulamore loi Dan šohor foijjonto fisottu lorai loigiye.
GEN 14:15 Bade raitta hiba edde hibar manuš okkol, hitara bag oiye. Hitara hitarare hamela goijje, edde Damaskusor uttorottu asede Hoba foijjonto fisottu lorai loigiye.
GEN 14:16 Toi hibaye hár zinišfati uwafes firai ainne, ar hibaye aro firai ainne, hibar egena Lut edde hibar dón šombotti, ar mayafuwain edde manuš okkolore.
GEN 14:17 Kedor-Laomor edde oinno badša okkolore hõṛai felai zẽtte Ibrahim uwafes firi aišše, Súdumor badšaye hibar loi deha goribolla Šaveh (ziyanore Badšar Ḍeil o ḍaka o) he ḍeilot aišše.
GEN 14:18 Ar Šalemor badša Melkisedeke ruṭi edde šoraf ainne. Hiba aššilde šorbo šoktiwala Allar ekzon imam,
GEN 14:19 toi hibaye Ibraimore duwa goijje, hodde, "Šorbo šoktiwala Allah, asman edde zobin sirišṭi goroyaye Ibraimore rahamot gorok.
GEN 14:20 Ar šorbo šoktiwala Allar tarif ok, ze tor dušmon okkolore tor hatot diye." Tarfore Ibraime hár kissur doš bag hibare diye.
GEN 14:21 Ar Súdumor badšaye Ibraimore hodde, "Mal samanagun tũi lo, ar manuššunore ãre do."
GEN 14:22 Kintu Ibraime Súdumor badšare hodde, "Ãi asman zobin sirišti goroya šorbo šoktiwala Mabud Allar mikka hat tuli wada gori hoir ze,
GEN 14:23 ãi tũwar hono kissu no loiyum, ekgas fũta otóba ṭengor senḍalor fita o no, fore zene tũi en hoi no faro, 'Ãi Ibraimore tuwangor banaiyi.'
GEN 14:24 Bolke ãr zuwan okkole háiyede hin bade ãi hono kissu no gosiyum. Aner, Iškol edde Mamre, zara ãr fũwati gil, hitarar fawana bag hitara fok."
GEN 15:1 In okkol bade, Mabudor kalam Ibraimor hãse ek dehar duwara aišše: "Ibraim, no ḍorais! Ãi tor ḍal oiyum, tor enam beši ḍõr."
GEN 15:2 Kintu Ibraime hodde, "Oh Mabud, ãr Malik, tũi ãre ki di fariba, ãide fuwain sara oi roiyi edde ãr šombottir mirazdar oibode oilde Damaskusor Eliyas?"
GEN 15:3 Ar Ibraime hodde, "Tũi ãre hono futziyain no do; hetolla so, ãr góror ekzon gulam ãr šombottir mirazdar oibo."
GEN 15:4 Hetunot Mabudor kalam hibar hãse aišše, "Ite tor mirazdar no oibo, kintu tor nizor kun tor šombottir mirazdar oibo."
GEN 15:5 Toi hibaye Ibraimore baire loigiye edde hodde, "Ãsmanor mikka sa edde zodi faros he tara okkolore goni šeš gor." Toi Allaye hodde, "Tor bongšo o hendilla ogona oibo."
GEN 15:6 Ibraime Mabudore biššaš goijje, ar hetolla hibare hibaye forhesgar hisabe goisse.
GEN 15:7 Ar hibaye Ibraimore hodde, "Ãi he Mabud, tore ei dešore miraz dibolla, ze tore Kaldiyar Ur šohorottu niyolai ainne."
GEN 15:8 Toi Ibraime hodde, "Oh Mabud, ãr Malik, iyan ãr oibode ãi kengori zaniyum?"
GEN 15:9 Toi Mabude hodde, "Tui tin bosojja uggwa gorur so, tin bosojja uggwa sool, tin bosojja uggwa faṛa berasool, edde uggwa hoitoror so, uggwa hoitor, ãr hãse angoi."
GEN 15:10 Bade Ibraime hin beggun hibar hãse ainne edde hinore mazottu siri dui falda gori ek faldar ulda ḍake ar ek faldare raikke, kintu faikgunore dui falda no gore.
GEN 15:11 Toi šiyari faik okkol he mora zanuwar okkolor uwore zafi forerbar Ibraime hinore lorai diye.
GEN 15:12 Bade beil dufedde šomot Ibraim beši hora gumot foijje, ar so, beši ḍor edde boiyanok ekkan andar hibar uwore foijjede masus gorer.
GEN 15:13 Hetunot Mabude Ibraimore hodde, "Iyan tui hameka zani lo, tor bongšodor okkol ofor dešot musaferi goribo edde bideši mainšor gulami goribo, mainše hitarare sair šot bosor foijjonto duk dibo.
GEN 15:14 Kintu hitara ze zatir gulam bonibo, ãi hitarar bisar goriyum, toi tarfore hitara beša beši dón šombotti okkol loi he dešottu niyoli zaiboi.
GEN 15:15 Ar tui šantiye tor bafdada okkolor hãse zaibi edde beši bura boyošot hoborot zaibi.
GEN 15:16 Tor bongšor sair gurur manuš okkole eṛe firi aibo, kiyollahoile Amorittiyo okkolor guna ehono šaza diya forede hettor no o."
GEN 15:17 Bade beil ḍufizaigoi zehon ekkubare andar oi giyegoi, hetunot dũwaye boraiya uggwa sula edde ekkan zalaiya uzal deha gilo edde oi dui bag goijja gustor mazottu di giyegoi.
GEN 15:18 Hedin Mabude Ibraim loi ek wadar sukti buwaiye edde hodde, "Ãi Mišor dešor Nil halottu loti ḍor hal, Fúrat foijjonto ei zagagan tor bongšore dilam.
GEN 15:19 Kenan dešitta okkol, Kenišittiya edde Kodomoniyo,
GEN 15:20 Hetittiyo, Perišiyo edde Refaitiyo
GEN 15:21 Amorittiyo, Kenaniyo, Girgašiyo edde Zebušiyo manuš okkolor zaga okkolore tore dilam."
GEN 16:1 Ibraimor bou, Saraiye, hiballa hono fuwain no biya. Kintu hibattu Hazera name ek Mišoriyo bandi aššil;
GEN 16:2 toi Saraiye Ibraimore hodde, "So Mabude ãre fuwain feṛot lowattu dure raikke, foriyad gorir, tũi ãr bandir hãse zo; oitfare ãi hibar duwara ek fut faiyum." Ar Ibraime Sarair hotat razi oiye.
GEN 16:3 Toi Ibraime Kenanot doš bosor taki bade, Saraiye, hibar Mišoriyo bandi Hazerare loi, hibar nizor zamai, Ibraimore diye.
GEN 16:4 Bade hiba Hazerar hãse giye, edde hiba hamil oiye. Ar hibaye zehon hamil oiyede buzi faijje, hibaye hibar malik sahebare hela gora šuru goijje.
GEN 16:5 Henot Saraiye Ibraimore hodde, "Ãr uwore ei dukkor daiyi tũi. Ãi ãr bandire tũwar bukot dilam, kintu hiba hamilde buzi fariyore hibaye ãre hela gorer. Mabude tũwar edde ãr bisar gorok!"
GEN 16:6 Ibraime Saraire hodde, "Sa, tor bandi tor hatot, tottu ziyan bala lage gor." Henot Saraiye Hazerare en duk diya šuru goijje, hiba hentu dáigiyegoi.
GEN 16:7 Bade Mabudor firistaye bošoti sara elehat, Soar zade fõtor kinare nol kuwa asede he nol kuwar fanir ḍake Hazerare faiye.
GEN 16:8 Hibaye hodde, "Sarair bandi, Hazera, tui hontu aiyor edde hoṛe zor?" Hibaye zuwabe hodde, "Ãi ãr saheba Sarair hãsottu dáizairgoide."
GEN 16:9 Toi Mabudor firistaye hodde, "Tui tor saheba Sarair hãse uwafes firi zaigoi edde hibar gulami manilogoi."
GEN 16:10 Mabudor Firistaye hodde, "Ãi tor bongšore eto baraidiyum, hitarare goni šeš gora no zaibo."
GEN 16:11 Mabudor firistaye hibare aro hodde: "Sa, tui hamil, ar tui ek fut biyaibi. Ar tui hitar nam rakibi Ismail, kiyollahoile Mabude tor dukkore fuinne.
GEN 16:12 Ar hite ekzon murailla gadar ḍoilla manuš oibo; hite beggunor berudde hat tulibo, ar beggune hitar berudde hat tulibo. ar hite hitar egena okkol loi, bezur takibo."
GEN 16:13 Bade hiba loi ze hota hoiye he Mabudore ei namman diye: "Tũi he Allah ze ãr uzu sor," haron hibaye hodde, "Ze ãr uzu sar ãi hibare dekilam neki?"
GEN 16:14 Hetolla he kuwar nam aššil Beer-Lahai-Roi, hiba Kadeš edde Beredor maza mazi zagat ase.
GEN 16:15 Bade Hazeraye Ibraimolla ek futore biyaiye, ar Ibraime Hazeraye biyaiyede he futor nam diye Ismail.
GEN 16:16 Hazeraye Ibraimolla Ismailore biyaiyede hẽtte Ibraimor boyoš aši so bosor.
GEN 17:1 Ibraimor boyoš zehon nobboi no bosor oiye, hẽtte Mabude hibare deha diye edde hodde, "Ãi he Šorbo-Šoktiwala Allah, ãr issa mozin sol edde hosuri sara o.
GEN 17:2 Ar ãi tui edde ãr maze ãr wadar sukti buwaiyum edde tor bongšore beši baraidiyum."
GEN 17:3 Henot Ibraime soida foijje, toi Allaye hibare hodde,
GEN 17:4 "Sa, iyan ãr wadar sukti tor loi: Tui bout zatir baf oibi.
GEN 17:5 Tore ar Ibraim hoi ḍaka no oibo, kintu tor nam oibo Ibrahim, kiyollahoile ãi tore bout zatir baf goijji.
GEN 17:6 Ãi tore fólwala goriyum, ar tor butottu bout zati goriyum, edde tor butottu badša okkol niyoli aibo.
GEN 17:7 Ãi tui edde ãr maze azibonor wadar sukti buwaiyum, ze wadar sukti tui edde tor bongšor bade bongšo dori sirohal solat takibo. Ãi tor edde tor bongšor manuš okkolor Allah oiyum.
GEN 17:8 Ze Kenan dešot tui ehon bidešitta oi zibon haṛaor, hiyanore ãi tui edde tor bongšore sirohalolla šombotti hisabe diyum, edde hitarar Allah oiyum."
GEN 17:9 Toi Allaye Ibrahimore hodde, "Tottu o ãr wadar sukti falon gora foribo, tui bade tor bongšodor okkole o.
GEN 17:10 Iyan oilde ãr wadar sukti ziyan tui edde ãre maze, tui bade tor bongšodor okkolor maze: Tũwarar fotti furušore azomi gora foribo.
GEN 17:11 Tũwara fottizonor bodar baror sam haṛa foribo, ar iyan oibode ãr edde tũwarar maze wadar suktir sinno.
GEN 17:12 Bongšor bade bongšo dori tũwarar furuš fuwain okkol zormo oi ašṭo dinor din azomi gora foribo, enki zara bongšodor no, kintu tor górot zormo oiye ba hono bidešittattu kinna gulam okkolore udda.
GEN 17:13 Tor górot zormo oiye ba tor kinna gulam, hitarare o azomi gora foribo. Ar iyan oilde tũwarar gat sirohalolla ãr wadar sukti asede sinno.
GEN 17:14 Kintu ze hono azomi agoraiya, zarare bodar sam haṛa no o, hitare hitar nizor zatir butottu fũsifela oibo, kiyollahoile hite ãr wadar sukti bainge."
GEN 17:15 Allaye Ibrahimore aro hodde, "Tor bou Saraire tui Sarai name no ḍakis; hibar nam oibo Sarah.
GEN 17:16 Ãi hibare duwa goriyum, ar hibattu o ãi tore ek fut diyum. Ãi hibare duwa goriyum toi hiba bout zati okkolor ma oibo; Hibar butottu badša okkol aibo."
GEN 17:17 Hetunot Ibrahime uite fori hãšše edde mone mone hodde, "Ek šot bosor oiyede ekzonottu ki fut zormo oibo? Ar nobboi bosojja Saraye ki fuwa biyaibo?"
GEN 17:18 Bade Ibrahime Allare hodde, "Ismail tũwar rahamote basi takok!"
GEN 17:19 Toi Allaye hodde, "Tor bou Saraye hameka tolla ek morod fuwa biyaibo, ar tui hitar nam Isak rakibi. Ãi hitar loi ãr wadar sukti buwaiyum, ek sirohalolla zari takibode wadar sukti, hite bade hitar bongšo okkololla.
GEN 17:20 Ar Ismailor babute tor foriyad ãi funni: Sa, ãi hitare o duwa goriyum, ar hitare fólwala goijjum edde hitar bongšo beši baraidiyum. Hitar butottu baro sordar okkol uṛibo, ar ãi hitare ek ḍõr zati banaiyum.
GEN 17:21 Agami bosor en šomot Saraye tolla zare biyaibo, he Isak loi kintu ãi ãr wadar sukti buwaiyum."
GEN 17:22 Ibrahim loi hota howa šeš gori bade Allah hibar hentu uṛi giyegoi.
GEN 17:23 Allaye hoilde mozin, he ekkui dinot Ibrahime hibar fut Ismailore edde hibar górot zormo oiyede edde hibar kinna gulam, hitara beggunore, hibar góror hár furuš okkolore loi azomi goraiye.
GEN 17:24 Ibrahimor boyoš nobboi no bosor zẽtte hibare azomi gora oiye,
GEN 17:25 ar hibar fut Ismailor boyoš tero;
GEN 17:26 Ibrahim edde Ismail dunizonore ekkui dinot azomi gora oiye.
GEN 17:27 Ar hibar fũwati Ibrahimor góror hár furuš okkol, górot zormo oiyede edde bidešittattu kinna gulam, hitara beggunore azomi gora oiye.
GEN 18:1 Bade Mabude Mamrer elun gas bonor hãse Ibrahimore deha diye. Ar hẽtte hiba dinor goromor ṭaimot ṭambur duwaror mukot boiṛa aššil.
GEN 18:2 Hen šomot suk tuli sadde tinzon furuš manuš Ibrahimor sarme hoddur dure tiyai roiye. Deki mottor hibaye ṭambur duwaror mukottu hitarar hãse dũri zai meṛit uite foijje.
GEN 18:3 Ibrahime hodde, "Oh Malik, aroz gorir, ãi zodi tũwar nozorot doya faiyiede o, toile õne ei gulamor hãsottu no zaiyogoi.
GEN 18:4 Ãi ekkena fani anigoi, toi zene õnora beggune ṭeng dui foro edde ei gastalat aram gori faro,
GEN 18:5 edde kissu hána anidi, toi zene hin haiyore ga doro gori faro, bade õnora zeṛe zor heṛe zaiyo, zehon ei gulamor sarmottu rasta bai zor." Hetunot hitara hodde, "Tui zen hor hen gor."
GEN 18:6 Toi Ibrahim toratori ṭambut Sarar hãse zai hodde, "Toratori gori ek bosta bala moida lo edde hinore maki hodun ruṭi banao."
GEN 18:7 Bade Ibrahim nize dũri zai zanuwaror zakottu uggwa barik, šundor gorur so aniyore hibare gulamor hatot diye edde hite toratori randito loigiye.
GEN 18:8 Tarfore Ibrahime doi, dud edde rainda gusto loi hitarar sarme diye. Ar hitara hana háiye edde hiba hitarar ḍake ek gasor tole tiyai taikke.
GEN 18:9 Toi hitara hibare fusar goredde, "Tor bou Sarah hoṛe?" Hibaye hodde, "Uṛe, hiba ṭambur butore ase."
GEN 18:10 Hitarar butottu ekzone hodde, "Agami bosor ei ṭaimot ãi abar hameka tor hãse aiššum, ar sa, hẽtte tor bou Sarattu ek fut takibo." Ei hota Saraye ṭambur dorozat hibar fisottu takiyore funniye.
GEN 18:11 Hẽtte Ibrahim edde Sarah dunizonor boyoš beši oiye edde Sarar fuwa biyaibar boyoš o farai giyegoi.
GEN 18:12 Hetolla Saraye mone mone hãšiyore hodde, "Ãr roš-hoš golizai ei bura hale ãttu abar ei kuši firi aibo neki? Ar ãr malik o bura."
GEN 18:13 Bade Mabude Ibrahimore hodde, "'Ãi ki hãsa ei bura hale fuwa biyaiyum' hoiyore kiyolla Saraye hãšer?
GEN 18:14 Mabudolla hono kissu koṭin ase neki? Agami bosor en šomot ãi abar tor hãse aiššum edde Sarattu ek fut takibo."
GEN 18:15 Hetunot Saraye ḍoraiyore hodde, "Hou no! Ãi no hãši." Kintu hibaye hodde, "Oi, tui hãššos."
GEN 18:16 Bade he manuššune hentu zaiboilla uiṭṭe edde hitara Súdumor mikka saiye, ar hitarare bidai dibolla hitarar fũwati Ibrahim o aṛer.
GEN 18:17 Toi Mabude hodde, "Ãi ziyan goitto zair hiyan ki ãi Ibrahimottu lukaium ne?
GEN 18:18 Ibrahim ek beši dõr edde šoktiwala zati oibo, ar duniyair hár zati okkolore hibar duwara rahamot gora oibo.
GEN 18:19 Kiyollahoile ãi hitare basi loiyi, toi zene hite hitar fuwain edde hitar bongšo okkolore Mabudor rasta mozin soiyi edde niyai ham goribolla hokum de, zene Mabude Ibrahimor hãse ze wada dil hin Ibrahimor uwore furon gori fare."
GEN 18:20 Toi Mabude hodde, "Súdum edde Gumorrar berudde guzorani beši ḍõr, ar hitarar guna beši boiyanok,
GEN 18:21 ze ãi ehon nise zaiyum edde hin saiyum ze guzorani ãr hãse fõisse iyan ki hendilla horaf ne naki no. Ar hen no oile, ãi zanifariyum."
GEN 18:22 Toi he manuššune hentu firi Súdumor mikka giye, kintu Ibrahim ehono Mabudor sarme tiyat roiye.
GEN 18:23 Bade Ibrahime ḍake zaiyore hibare hodde: "Õne ki horaf okkolor fũwati forhesgar okkolore o fũsifelaiba?
GEN 18:24 He šohoror butore zodi fõnzaš zon forhesgar take, ar heṛiyar fõnzaš zon forhesgar okkolore o ki õne he zagar mutallek rahamot no goriyore ki hiyan dongšo gorifelaiba?
GEN 18:25 Horaf okkolor fũwati forhesgar okkolore o dongšo gora, õnottu dure takok. Forhesgar okkolore horafor sarme ana, õnottu dure takok. Fura duniyair bisarhare ki niyai bisar no goribo ne?"
GEN 18:26 Hetunot Mabude hodde, "Súdumor butore zodi fõnzaš forhesgar manuš fai, toile hitarar zoriya ãi he gũṛa zaga hiyanore basai rakiyum."
GEN 18:27 Toi Ibrahime hodde, "So, ãi tũwar šanot dúil edde sai, ar ãi šahoš gori ãr Malik loi hota hoir,
GEN 18:28 zodi fõnzaš forhesgarottu fãszon hom o, toile ki ei fãszonor zoriya fura šohor dongšo gorifelaiba?" Hibaye hodde, "Ãi heṛe sališ fãszon faile hiyan dongšo no goriyum."
GEN 18:29 Hibaye hibare abar hodde, "Heṛe zodi sališzonore fa gile ka?" Hibaye hodde, "He sališzonor zoriya, ãi hen no goriyum."
GEN 18:30 Tarfore hibaye hodde, "Malik ãr hotat naraz no oiyo, kintu ãre hoito do. Heṛe zodi tirišzonore fa gile ka?" Toi hibaye hodde, "Heṛe zodi ãi tirišzonore faile o ãi hen no goriyum."
GEN 18:31 Ibrahime hodde, "So, šahoš gori ãi ãr Malik loi hota hoir, doro, heṛe zodi kurizonore fa gile ka?" Hibaye hodde, "Ei kurizonor zoriya, ãi hiyan dongšo no goriyum."
GEN 18:32 Toi Ibrahime hodde, "Malik ãr hotat naraz no oiyo, edde ãre šude ar ekbar hoito do. Heṛe zodi došzon fa gile ka?" Hibaye hodde, "Ei došzonor zoriya, ãi hiyan dongšo no goriyum."
GEN 18:33 Toi Mabude Ibrahim loi hota howa šeš gori bade hiba hentu giyegoi, ar Ibrahim hibar nizor górot firi aišše.
GEN 19:1 Bade he firista dunizon hãzinna Súdum šohorot fõisse, ar he šomot Lut šohoror geiṛor hãsat boiṛa aššil. Hibaye zehon hitarare deikke, hibaye uṛiyore hitara loi deha goitto giye, edde meṛit uite fori šorman zanaiye,
GEN 19:2 edde hodde, "Ãr malik okkol, meherbani gori õnora ei gulamor górot aiyore rait haṛao, ṭeng duwo. Bade binna sori uṛi õnorar baisar uzu zaigoi faribo." Hitara hodde, "No, ãra šohoror butore rait haṛaiyum."
GEN 19:3 Kintu Lute zehon beši doddali loi zúr goijje, hitara hibar fũwati giye edde hibar górot góille. Bade Lute iš adiya ruṭi seki hitaralla hánar entezam goijje, toi hitara háiye.
GEN 19:4 Hitara neiṭṭo zaibar agottu Súdum šohoror zuwan edde bura, hár manuš okkole sairo ḍakottu ai Lutor gór girifelaiye.
GEN 19:5 Hitara Lutore ḍak mari hodde, "Aijja raitta tor heṛe aiššede manušgun hoṛe? Hitarare bair goriyore ãrar hãse niyolai an, toi zene ãra hitarare ãrar issa mozin gori fari."
GEN 19:6 Toi Lute dorozar baire niyoliyore hitarar hãse giye edde hibar fisottu dorozagan bon gori diye.
GEN 19:7 Ar hodde, "Oh ãr báiyain okkol, meherbani gori tũwara endilla horaf ham no goijjo.
GEN 19:8 So, ãttu ziyain duizon ase, zitarare hono furuš mainše no suye, ãi tũwaralla hitarare anigoi edde tũwarattu hitara loi zen issa tũwara gorogoi. Šude ei manuššunore kissu no goijjo, kiyollahoile hitara ehon ãr góror salor tole assoro loiye."
GEN 19:9 Kintu hitara hodde, "Ator o, fõtottu lori tiya. Ei manušwa eṛe ãrar hãse aiššede bideši hisabe, tarbade oite ite ãrar uwore matabbori gorer. Ehon utarattuwaro tor loi ãra aro beši horaf bebar goriyum." En hoi hitara mummikka zai góror doroza bangifelaibolla Lut loi beša beši ṭelaṭeli gora šuru goijje.
GEN 19:10 Kintu butottu manuš dunizone hat barai di Lutore góror butore ṭani golai felaiye edde dorozagan bongorifelaiye.
GEN 19:11 Ar hitara dorozar baire tiyat aššilde zuwan edde bura manuš okkolore anda gori felaiye, hiyanor zoriya hitara doroza tuwaite tuwaite oran oigiyegoi.
GEN 19:12 Toi bade manuš dunizone Lutore hodde, "Tottu ei šohorot tor zi zamaiyain, futain edde ziyain otóba ar hono kiye ase ne? Tui hitara beggunore loi ei zagattu bair oizagoi,
GEN 19:13 kiyollahoile ãra iyan dongšo gorifelaiyum. Iyanor manuš okkolor berudde Mabudor hãse guzorani eto beši ḍõr, hibaye ei šohor dongšo gorifelaibolla ãrare faṭaiye."
GEN 19:14 Hetunot Lute baire giye edde hitara zara hibar zi zamai oibo hitarar loi hota hoiye. Hibaye hodde, "Tũwara toratori ei zaga sari zogoi, kiyollahoile Mabude ei šohorgan dongšo gorifelaibolla tiyar ase!" Kintu hitara mone goijje Lute fašai gorer buli.
GEN 19:15 Binna dol fohor oiyede šomot firista okkole Lutore hodde, "Toratori goro! Tor bou edde tor dui zi, zara eṛe ase, hitarare loi entu niyoli zagoi, ar no oile ze gozob ei šohoror uwore lami aiyer tui o hinot maze fori dongšo oizaibigoi."
GEN 19:16 Lute zaite deri goijje, kintu Mabudor rahamot Lutor uwore aššil buli he dui zone Lut edde hibar bou edde ziyaindore hatot dori ṭani šohoror baire loi ainne.
GEN 19:17 Endilla gori hitarare bair gori ani bade, hitarar ekzone hodde, "Basito mone hoile dái zogoi! Fissa firi no saiyo ar ei fuwainna zagar hono mikka no tiyaiyo! Faharot dáizogoi, ar no oile tũwara o dongšo oiba!"
GEN 19:18 Kintu Lute hitarare hodde, "Oh malik okkol, hendilla no ok!
GEN 19:19 So, õnor ei gulame õnor nozorot doya faiye, ar ãr zibonore basaiyore ãr uwore dõr doya dehaiyo. Tarfore o ãi faharot dáizaigoi no faijjum; ei bifodde ãr uwore zafi foribo edde ãi mori zaiyumboi.
GEN 19:20 So, eṛe ḍake ekkan šohor ase, ziyanot dũri dáiza šombob, ar hiyan šoṛo o no ne? Ãre heṛe dáizaibolla ejazot do, toi ãr zibon basi zaiboi."
GEN 19:21 Toi hibaye hibare hodde, "Bala, ãi ei babute o tor foriyad rakilam edde tui ze zagar hota hoiyos hiyan dongšo no goriyum.
GEN 19:22 Kintu toratori heṛe dáizagoi, kiyollahoile tui heṛe no fõsosgoi foijjonto ãi kissu gori no farir." (Hetolla he šohoror nam oiye Soar.)
GEN 19:23 Lut Soarot fõissegoide šomot beil uiṭṭe.
GEN 19:24 Tarfore Mabude asmanottu, Mabudor torfottu Súdum edde Gumorrar uwore baros edde oini šil zór felaiye.
GEN 19:25 Hibaye he šohor okkol edde hár fuwainna zaga šoho he šohor okkolot takitode hár manuš okkol edde zobinot zin barito, hár kissure dongšo gorifelaiye.
GEN 19:26 Kintu Lutor bouye hibar fissa firi saiye, ar henot hiba nunor kúṛa oigiyegoi.
GEN 19:27 Tarfordin binna sore Ibrahime uṛi he zagat hiyanot giye zeṛe hibaye Allar sarme tiyai aššil.
GEN 19:28 Hibaye tiyai nisor Súdum edde Gumorrar hár fuwainna zagar uzu saiye, ar dekedde iṭ baṛar bambuttu dũwa uṛerfan, he elehattu dũwa uṛer.
GEN 19:29 Ebafe Lut zeṛe takito he fuwainna zagar šohorgun dongšo goribar šomot Allaye Ibrahimor hota bafi Lutore heṛiyar mosibotor butottu lari loi ainne.
GEN 19:30 Bade Lut edde hibar dui ziyore loi Soarottu ek faharot zai heṛe bošoti loiye, kiyollahoile Lute Soarot takare ḍoraiye. Ar heṛe ek faharor gãtot hitara taka šuru goijje.
GEN 19:31 Bade ekdin ḍõr ziye šoṛo ziyore hodde, "Baba to bura oi zargoi. Ei elehat en hono furuš manuš o nai ze aiyore ãrare duniyair niyom mozin biya gori faribo.
GEN 19:32 Aio! Ãra ãrar bafore šoraf habai fol gori hibar hãse zai. Henot babar duwara ãra ãrar bonšo rokka gori fariyum."
GEN 19:33 Henot hitara he raitta nizor bafore šoraf habaiye, bade Lutor ḍõr ziye baf loi gum zaito giye. Kintu hibar neṛa edde uṛa Lute ṭer no fa.
GEN 19:34 Tarfor din ḍõr ziye šoṛo ziyore hodde, "Sa, gelde raitta ãi babar loi gum gilam, ai, ãra aijja raitta o babare abar šoraf habai. Bade tui zai babar loi gum zaibi, endilla gori ãra ãrar bafor bongšo rokka gori fariyum."
GEN 19:35 Ei bafe hitara he raitta o hitarar bafore šoraf habai fol goijje edde šoṛo ziye o bafor loi gum zaito giye. Kintu hibar neṛa edde uṛa Lute ṭer no fa.
GEN 19:36 Endilla gori Lutor dui ziye hitarar bafor duwara hamil oiye.
GEN 19:37 Bade ḍõr ziyottu ek morod fuwa oiye, edde nam diye Muwab. Hite oilde ehonor Muwabiyo okkolor fordada.
GEN 19:38 Ar šoṛo ziyottu ek morod fuwa oiye, edde hitar nam raikke Ben-Ammi. Hite oilde ehonor Ammoniyo okkolor fordada.
GEN 20:1 Toi Ibrahim hentu Negevot giye edde Kadeš edde Šuror maze hale ekkan zagat bošoti loiye. Ar kissu dinolla hibaye Gerarot zai taikke.
GEN 20:2 Ar heṛe o Ibrahime hibar bou Sarar babute hodde, "Iba ãr boin." Henot Geraror badša Abimaleke manuš defeṛaiyore Sarare hitar hãse ainne.
GEN 20:3 Kintu raitta Allaye Abimalekore kuwafot aiyore hodde, "Sa, tui morar mukot, kiyollahoile ze maya fuwa tui loi ainnos hiba ar ekzonor bou."
GEN 20:4 Abimaleke kintu ehono hibar ḍake no za, ar hite hodde, "Malik, õne niduši zati oile o ki dongšo goriba?
GEN 20:5 Hite nize ki 'ibar ãr boin,' ar hibaye nize ki 'iba ãr bái' no ho ne? Ãi šorol mone edde niduši hate ei ham goijji."
GEN 20:6 Bade Allaye hitare kuwafot hodde, "Oi, ãi zani tui šorol mone ei ham goijjos, ar hetolla ãr berudde guna gorattu tore dure raikki, ar hetolla ãi tore hibare suito no di de.
GEN 20:7 Ehon tui he manušwar bouwore hitar hãse firaidifela, kiyollahoile hite ekzon nobi, ar hite tolla duwa goribo, henot tui basibi. Ar zodi firai no dos, toile iyan zani rak, tui edde tũwara beggune hameka moriba."
GEN 20:8 Tarfordin binna sore Abimaleke uṛi hitar gulam okkol beggunore ḍaikke, edde ei hota okkol zehon hitarare funaiye, hitara kub beši ḍoraiye.
GEN 20:9 Bade Abimaleke Ibrahimore ḍaki ainne edde hibare hodde, "Tũi ãra loi endilla kiyolla gorila? Ãi tũwar ki hosuri goijji, ze tũi ãi edde ãr raijjor uwore ettor ḍõr guna ainno? Endilla hono kiye no gorede ham tũi ãr loi gorila."
GEN 20:10 Toi Abimaleke Ibrahimore aro hodde, "Tũi ki saiyore endilla ham goijjilade?"
GEN 20:11 Ibrahime zuwabe hodde, "Ãi mone goijjilam, 'ei zagat hameka hono Allar ḍor nai, ãr bouwolla boli oitefare hitara ãre mari felaibo.'
GEN 20:12 Ar hiba ãr boinde hiyan o soiyi, ãr bafor zi zodi o hibar ãr mar boitta zi no; ar hiba ãr bou oiye.
GEN 20:13 Ar zẽtte Allaye ãre ãr bafor górottu bair gori ainne, hẽtte ãi hibare hoilam, 'Tui ãre endilla goriyore ador dehai faribi, Ãra zeṛe zaiyum zaiyum, tottu howa foribo "Iba ãr bái."'"
GEN 20:14 Toi Abimaleke hodun goru sool edde gulam edde bandi Ibrahimore diye, ar hinor fũwati hibar bou Sarare o hibar hãse firai diye.
GEN 20:15 Toi Abimaleke hodde, "So, ãr deš gũṛa tũwar sarme ase, tũwattu ziyot foson lage hiyot tako."
GEN 20:16 Ar hite Sarare hodde, "So, ãi tũwar hár mainšor sarme tũi nidušide hiyan zanefan ãi tũwar báiyore ek hazar rufar foiša dir. Henot beggunor sarme forman oibo ze tũi hono hosuri no goro."
GEN 20:17 Tarfore Ibrahime Allar hãse duwa goijje ar henot Allaye Abimalek, hitar bou edde hitar bandi okolore aram goijje zene hitara abar fuwain owaifare,
GEN 20:18 kiyollahoile Ibrahimor bou Sarar zoriya Mabude Abimalekor góror hár mayafuwaindor fuwain owattu bad gori raikkil.
GEN 21:1 Mabude hibar kalam mozin Sarar mikka nozor diye edde hibaye ziyan goribo wada dil Saralla Mabude hiyan goijje.
GEN 21:2 Sarah hamil oiye edde hibaye Allaye ze ṭaimor hota hoil, he ekkui ṭaimot Ibrahimor bura boyošot, hiballa ek futore biyaiye.
GEN 21:3 Ar Ibrahime he fut, zare Saraye hiballa biyaiye, hitara nam diye Isak,
GEN 21:4 Allaye hokum dilde mozin hibar fut Isak zehon ašṭo din oiye, Ibrahime hitare azomi goraiye.
GEN 21:5 Ibrahim ekšot bosor boyošot hibar fut Isak zormo oiye.
GEN 21:6 Saraye hodde, "Allaye ãr mukot hãši ainne, ar hár kiye ze ei babute funibo hitara o ãr fũwati hãšibo."
GEN 21:7 Hibaye aro hodde, "Saraye fuwaindore bukor dud habai faribo, hen Ibrahimore hone hoi farito? Otoso hibar ei bura boyošot ãi hiballa ek futore zormo diyi."
GEN 21:8 Bade fuwawa bari uiṭṭe edde ze din dud saraiye, ar Isakore dud saraiyede he din Ibrahime ek ḍõr mela goijje.
GEN 21:9 Ar Saraye dekedde Mišoror Hazeraye Ibrahimolla ze futore biyaiye, hite ṭaṭṭa gorer,
GEN 21:10 Toi hibaye Ibrahimore hodde, "Ei bandi edde hibar futore dur goro, kiyollahoile ei bandir fute ãr fut Isakor fũwati honodin dón šombottir mirazdar oi no faribo."
GEN 21:11 Ei ziniš iyan Ibrahimor nozorot beši horaf oiye, kiyollahoile hiyan hibar futor babute.
GEN 21:12 Kintu Allaye Ibrahimore hodde, "Tor fut edde tor bandir babute mon horaf no goris. Saraye tore zen hor tui hibar hota fun, kiyollahoile iyan Isakor duwara zin tor bongšo dora oibo.
GEN 21:13 Ãi he bandir futore o ek zati banaiyum, kiyollahoile hite o tor fuwa."
GEN 21:14 Ibrahime binna sore uṛi kissu hána edde fani boraiya uggwa samrar hoilla Hazerar handot tulidiyore hibar fut šoho bidai gori diye. Hiba hentu niyoli zai Beer-Šebar bošoti sara elehat gura fira goijje.
GEN 21:15 Hoillar fani zehon šeš oi giyegoi, hibaye fuwaware ek zõlor zafor tole neṛai raikke.
GEN 21:16 Tarfore uggwa tir mela marile zeddur za heddur dure zai hiba boi taikke, "Fuwawar moron zen ãttu deha no fore" mone mone hen hoi hiba heṛe boi guzori handa šuru goijje.
GEN 21:17 Fuwawar handani Allaye funniye edde Allar firistaye behostottu Hazerare ḍak diye edde hodde, "Hazera, tottu ki oiye? No ḍorais, kiyollahoile fuwawa zeṛe ase hentu hitar handani Allaye funniye.
GEN 21:18 Tui fuwaware tul edde hitare tor hatot doro gori dor, kiyollahoile ãi hitare ek ḍõr zati banaiyum."
GEN 21:19 Tarfore Allaye Hazerar suk kuli diye, henot hibaye uggwa fanir kuwa deikke. Toi hibaye zaiyore samrar hoillat fani boijje edde fuware fani fito diye.
GEN 21:20 Allah he fuwar fũwati aššil ar hite bari uiṭṭe. Hite bošoti sara elehat takito, edde tir maroya ustad boinne.
GEN 21:21 Hite Faronor bošoti sara elehat bošoti goijje, ar hitar maye Mišorottu ek mayafuware loi hitare biya goraidiye.
GEN 21:22 He šomot Abimalek edde hitar foila komonḍar Fikole Ibrahimore hodde, "Tũi ze kissu goro hinot Allah tũwar fũwati ase.
GEN 21:23 Hetolla tũi eṛe Allar sarme ãre hosom gori ho, ze tũi hono din ãi otóba ãr fuwain ba ãr bongšo loi beimani no goriba. Ar ãi zendilla tũware doya dehaiyi, tũi ãre edde ze dešot tũi bidešitta hisabe takor, ei dešor loi hendilla doya dehaiba."
GEN 21:24 Ibrahime hodde, "Oi, ãi hosom gorilam."
GEN 21:25 Abimalekor gulam okkole zurgori uggwa fanir kuwa dokol goijjilde babute Ibrahime Abimalekor hãse nališ goijje.
GEN 21:26 Kintu Abimaleke hodde, "Iyan hone goijje ãi hoi no fari. Tũi ãre iyan age o no ho."
GEN 21:27 Tarfore Ibrahime hodun sool edde goru ainne edde hin Abimalekore diye, ar hitara dunizone ekkan sukti goijje.
GEN 21:28 Ibrahime zakottu hãttuwa fãṛi bera soolor so aleda gori raikke.
GEN 21:29 Toi Abimaleke hibare fusar goredde, "Tũi ei fãṛi bera soolor so hãttuware aleda gori raikkode iyanor mani ki?"
GEN 21:30 Hibaye hodde, "Ei bera soolor so hãttuwa in tũi ãr hatottu goso, toi zene tũi ãlla goba oi faro ze ei kuwa ze ãi kujji."
GEN 21:31 Etolla he zagar nam oilde Beer-šeba, kiyollahoile he zagat hitara dunizone ek wadar hosom háil.
GEN 21:32 Hitara Beer-šebat ei sukti šeš gori bade, Abimalek edde hitar foila komonḍar Fikole Filistini okkolor dešot firigiyegoi.
GEN 21:33 Bade Ibrahime Beer-šebat maze uggwa zaugas lagaiye, edde heṛe he Mabud Ošeš Allar nam ḍaikke.
GEN 21:34 Ar Ibrahim Filistini okkolor dešot bidešitta hisabe bout din forbaš goijje.
GEN 22:1 Ei goṭonar bade Allaye Ibrahimore forikka goijje. Allaye hibare hodde, "Ibrahim!" Ibrahime hodde, "Oto ãi eṛe."
GEN 22:2 Toi Allaye hodde, "Tũi tor fut, šude lehar fut, tor adoijja fut Isakore loi Muriah elehat za, edde heṛiyar fahar zibar hota ãi tore hoiyum, hibar uwore fura kurbani hisabe hitare kurbani gor."
GEN 22:3 Ibrahime binna sore uṛiyore hibar gadar fiṛot godi buwaye, ar hibar gulam okkolor butottu duizon gulamore edde hibat fut Isakore fũwati loi, fura kurbanilla darguwa haṛi loiyore Allaye hoilde he zagar mikka baisa diye.
GEN 22:4 Tin dinor din Ibrahime suk tuli saiye edde durottu tai he zaga deikke.
GEN 22:5 Toi hibaye hibar gulam okkolore hodde, "Tũwara gadawa loi eṛe tako, ar ãi edde ãr fut uṛe zai dórmo gorigoi, abar tũwarar hãse firi aiššum."
GEN 22:6 Toi Ibrahime fura kurbanir darguwar fuzá loi hibar fut Isakor handot diye edde hibar hator oinor dešši edde suri loi hitara dunizon ekku fũwati giye.
GEN 22:7 Toi Isake hibar baf Ibrahimore hodde, "Oh baba!" "Ki hodde o fut?" hoi Ibrahime zuwab diye. Isake hodde, "Oin edde darguwa dekir, kintu fura kurbanilla bera soolor so hoṛe?"
GEN 22:8 Ibrahime zuwabe hodde, "Fura kurbanilla bera soolor so Allaye nize zuhai dibo, o fut!" Toi hitara dunizon fũwati giye.
GEN 22:9 Allaye hibare hoilde he zagat hitara fõsiyore Ibrahime heṛe ekkan kurbangah tiyar gori hiyanor uwore darguwa loi hãzaidiye, bade hibar fut Isakore kurbangar uwore, darguwar uwore raikke.
GEN 22:10 Ar Ibrahime futore zorgoraibolla suri hatot loiyore tuille.
GEN 22:11 Kintu Mabudor firistaye behostottu ḍak diye edde hodde, "Ibrahim, Ibrahim!" Hibaye zuwab diye, "Oto ãi eṛe!"
GEN 22:12 Hibaye hodde, "Fuwawar uwore tor hat no dis, hitare hono kissu no goris, kiyollahoile ãi ehon buzi faijji, tui Allare ḍoros, ãlla tor šude lehar futore kurbani dite o fisfa no goros."
GEN 22:13 Hetunot Ibrahime hibar suk tuli saiye, ar so, hibar fisottu uggwa faṛa sool, šingot zõl berai ãṭkiroiye; bade Ibrahime zai he faṛa soolguwa aniyore futor bodole hibare fura kurbani kurbani diye.
GEN 22:14 Ibrahime he zagar nam raikke "YHWH-Jireh" (Mabud ze zuhaide.) Etolla ehono endilla ho, "Mabudor faharot zuhaide."
GEN 22:15 Toi Mabudor firistaye behostottu dusora bar Ibrahimore ḍak maijje
GEN 22:16 edde hodde, "Tui tor futore kurbani dite fisfa no goros, hetolla ãi Mabud nize hosom hái hoir ze,
GEN 22:17 ãi hameka tore beši duwa goriyum, ar asmanor tara ḍoilla edde doriyar soror balur reni zedun tor bongšo hedun beši gori diyum. Tor bongšo okkole hitarar dušmon okkolor šohor okkolore dokol goribo.
GEN 22:18 Tor bongšor duwara duniyair hár zatiye duwa faibo, kiyollahoile tui ãr hokum mainnos."
GEN 22:19 Toi bade Ibrahime hibar gulam okkolor hãse firi giye, edde hitara beggune ekku fũwati hentu Beer-Šebat firi zaiboilla baisa diye. Ar Ibrahim Beer-Šebat bošoti goijje.
GEN 22:20 Ei goṭona goṭi bade Ibrahimore howa oiye, "So, tũwar bái Nahurolla Melkaye o futain okkol biyaiye:
GEN 22:21 Foila zormo Uz, hitar bái Buz, Aramor baf, Kamuel,
GEN 22:22 Kesed, Hazo, Fildaš, Jidlap edde Betuel."
GEN 22:23 Betuel Rebekar baf oiye. Ibrahimor bái Nahuror bou Melkaye ei ašṭo futore biyaiye.
GEN 22:24 Nahuror bandi bou zar nam Reuma, hibaye o: Ṭebah, Gaham, Tahaš edde Maakah, itarare biyaiye.
GEN 23:1 Sarar boyoš ek šo hãtaiš bosor oil; hiba hetodin basi aššil.
GEN 23:2 Ar Kenan dešot Kiryat-Arbat (hiyan oilde, Hebronot) hibar moron oiye, ar Ibrahime Saralla handibolla edde šuk falon goribolla giye.
GEN 23:3 Bade Ibrahime hibar mora bouwor ḍakottu uiṭṭe edde Hetittiyo okkolor hãse zai hodde,
GEN 23:4 "Ãi tũwarar butore ekzon osin bidešitta; hoborstan banaibolla ãre tũwarar butore ekkan zaga beso, toi zene ãr sarme ãr mora bouwore dohon gorai fari."
GEN 23:5 Hetittiyo okkole Ibrahimore zuwabe hodde,
GEN 23:6 "Malik, ãrar hota funo, tũi ãrar butore ekzon Allar šoktišali neta. Ãrar hoborgunor butore he barik hoboror butore tũwar morare dohon gorogoi. Tũwar mora gãraibolla ãrar honokiye hitar hobor zaga sari dite ošikar no goribo."
GEN 23:7 Toi Ibrahime uṛiyore he dešor manuš mani Hetittiyo okkolor sarme mata niyuraiyore ijjot goijje.
GEN 23:8 Bade hibaye hitarare hodde, "Ãr morare ãr sarme dohon goraito diba iyan zodi tũwarar issa o, toile ãr hota funo, Soharor fut Efron loi ãlla ottor o,
GEN 23:9 toi zene hitar maṛor šeš šimat, Mokfelar gãt, ziba hitattu ase, hiba hite ãre de. Hite zene tũwarar sarme hiyanor fura dam loiyore hoborstan banaibolla ãr hãse besifele."
GEN 23:10 Ar Hetittiyo okkolor fũwati Efron o heṛe boiṛa aššil, ar Hetittiyo Efrone Ibrahimore zuwab dedde hiyan hitar šohor geiṛot góillede beggune funniye.
GEN 23:11 Hite hodde, "No, ãr malik, õne ãr hota funo, ãi ãr zatir manušor sarme he maṭ edde hiyanot ze gãt ase, hiba šoho ãi tũware dilam. Tũwar morare dohon gorogoi."
GEN 23:12 Hetunot Ibrahime abar dešor mainšor sarme mata niyuraiyore ijjot goijje.
GEN 23:13 Ar he dešor manuš beggunor sarme hibaye Efronore hodde, "Zodi mone ho foriyad gorir, tũi ãr hota funo, ãi maṛor dam di, meherbani gori tũi ãttu hingun goso, toi zene ãi ãr mora bouwore heṛe dohon goraifari."
GEN 23:14 Efrone Ibrahimore zuwabe hodde,
GEN 23:15 "Malik, ãr hota funo, he zagar dam oiyede sair šot rufar ṭĩya, kintu hin ãlla edde tũwalla hono kissu no, tũwar bouwore heṛe dohon gorogoi."
GEN 23:16 Ibrahime Efronor hota buzi faijje edde hite Hetittiyo okkolor sarme rufar ṭĩyar hota hoilde mozin, sair šot rufar ṭĩya šodor okkolor maf mozin mafiyore hitare diye.
GEN 23:17 Ei bafe Mamrer ḍake Mokfelat asede Efronor maṭ edde gãt, ar he maṛor sairo mikkar hár gas šoho,
GEN 23:18 hár Hetittiyo okkol hitar šohor geiṭor sarme goillilde hitarar sarme Ibrahimor šombotti šabbišṭo oiye.
GEN 23:19 Tarfore Ibrahime Kenan dešor Mamrer ḍake (ziyan Hebronot) Mokfelar maṛot asede gãtot hibar bou Sarare gãraiye.
GEN 23:20 Endilla gori he maṭ edde heṛe asede gãt hoborstan hisabe Hetittiyo okkolor hatottu Ibrahimor hãtot aišše.
GEN 24:1 Hẽtte Ibrahim bura edde boyoš beši oiye, ar Mabude hibare hár kissut duwa goijjil.
GEN 24:2 Ibrahime hibar góror šobsaite furan gulam, zar uwore hibattu aššilde hin beggunor hár bár aššil, hitare hodde, "Tor hattan ãr ranor tole rak.
GEN 24:3 Ãi tore behosto edde duniyair Allah, Mabudor sarme hosom gorai, ze Kenaniyo okkolor butore ãi bošobaš gorir, itarar butottu ãr futolla bou no anibi,
GEN 24:4 kintu ãr dešot ãr nizor egena okkolor hãse zai ãr fut Isakolla bou anibi."
GEN 24:5 He gulame hibare hodde, "Zodi he maya fuwa ãr fũwati ei dešot aite razi no o, henoile ze deš sari tũi eṛe aigiyogoi he dešot ki abar tũwar futore loizaiyum?"
GEN 24:6 Ibrahime hodde, "Kiyal rakis, ãr futore tui hono mote heṛe no loizais.
GEN 24:7 Mabud ze Behostor Allah, ze ãre ãr bafor gór edde ãr zormostanottu niyolai ainne, ze ãr loi hota hoiye edde hosom hái hoiye, 'Ei dešgan ãi tor bongšore diyum' hibaye tor age hibar firistare defeṛaibo, zene tui ãr futolla hentu ek bou ani faros.
GEN 24:8 He maya fuwa zodi tor fũwati aite razi no o, toile tui ãr hosomottu hedin azad; kintu hono mote ãr futore heṛe no loizais."
GEN 24:9 Toi he gulame hitar giros Ibrahimor ranor tole hat raki ei befare hibar loi hosom háiye.
GEN 24:10 Tarfore he gulame hitar girosor ũṭ okkolottu došwa ũṭ loi, hitar girose diyede hár ḍoilla dami zinišfati okkol loi baisa diye. Hite Aram Nahuriyamor mikka ruwana diyore Nahuror šohorot giye.
GEN 24:11 Hite heṛe šohoror baire uṭgunore ek fanir kuwar ḍake luṛai ejje; ar hiyan aššilde hazinna ṭaimot, zẽtte mayafuwainde fani tulito za.
GEN 24:12 Tarfore hite duwa gorer, "Oh Mabud, ãr giros Ibrahimor Allah, aijja ãre kamiyaf goro, edde ãr giros Ibrahimore doya dehao.
GEN 24:13 So, ãi ei fanir kuwar hãsat tiyai roiyi, ar ei šohoror mainšor ziyain okkole fani tulibolla niyoli aiyer.
GEN 24:14 Iyan endilla ok zẽtte ãi ek zuwan mayafuware hoi, 'Tor górawa lama, zene ãi fani fiyi fari,' ar hibaye ho, 'fiyo, ai tũwar uṭgunore o ãi fani diyum' henoile hiba tũwar gulam Isakolla tũwar basai gora ok. Ar iyanot ãi zaniyum ze tũi ãr girosore doya dehaiyo."
GEN 24:15 Ar so, ei duwa goijja no oite, Rebekah góra handot loi niyoli aiyer. Hiba aššilde Ibrahimor bái Nahuror bou Melkar fut Betuelor zi.
GEN 24:16 He zuwan maya fuwawa aššil beši šundori, ek kumari, zibare hono manuše no sue. Hiba kuwat laimme edde góra furai loi abar uwafes uṛi aišše.
GEN 24:17 Hen šomot gulammuwaye dũri hibar sarme zaiyore hodde, "Meherbani gori, tor górattu ãre ekka fani fito de."
GEN 24:18 Hibaye hodde, "Malik, fani fiyo," ar toratori górawa hibar handottu hibar hatot lamaiye edde hitare fani fito diye.
GEN 24:19 Ar hibaye hitare fani fito di bade hodde, "Ãi tũwar uṭgunolla o fani tuliyum, zetun hitara fani fiya šeš no gore."
GEN 24:20 Tarfore hibaye toratori hibar górar fanigun zanuwarore fani habade nor kulot ḍali diyore dũri abar kuwar ḍake fani tulibolla giye, edde hitar hár uṭ okkololla fani tuille.
GEN 24:21 Ar manušwaye nizamot hibar uzu saiye, Mabude hitar baisa kamiyaf goijje ne na ki no gore zanibolla.
GEN 24:22 Uṭgune fani fiya šeš oi bade, manušwaye adá šekel uzonor ugguwa šunar nakful, edde dui hatolla doš šekel uzonor duiyan šunar haru hibar sarme bair goijje.
GEN 24:23 Toi hite hodde, "Tui haro zi, meherbani gori ãre ho, tor bafor górot ãra rait haṛaibolla hono ekkan zaga ase ne?"
