GEN 24:24 Hibaye zuwabe hodde, "Ãi Melkar fut Betuelor zi, zare Melkaye Nahurolla biyaiye."
GEN 24:25 Hibaye aro hodde, "Ãrar górot beša beši ker edde buši ase edde takibar zaga o ase."
GEN 24:26 Hetunot he manušwaye Mabudor soida foriyore šukuriya zanaiye,
GEN 24:27 ar hodde, "Hár tarif ãr giros Ibrahimor Allah Mabudore, zibaye ãr girosor mutallek hibar doya edde imandari dehare forai no fele. Ãre o fõtot, he Mabude rasta dehaiyore ãr girosor egena báiyor górot ainne."
GEN 24:28 Bade he zuwan mayafuwawaye dũri zaiyore hibar mar górot ei hota okkolore hoiye.
GEN 24:29 Ar Rebekkattu Labon name ek bái aššil, hite oi kuwar ḍake manušwar hãse dũri giye,
GEN 24:30 Hite zehon nakful edde hitar boinor hatot haru deikke, ar manušwaye hoilde hin hitar boine hodde funniye, hite niyoliyore he manušwar hãse giye, edde hite kuwar hãsat ũṛor ḍake tiyat lotfaiye.
GEN 24:31 Toi hite hodde, "Oh Mabudor rahamotwala manuš, aiyo! Baire kiyolla tiyai taikko? Ãi õnolla gór edde uṭgunolla zaga ṭik goijji."
GEN 24:32 Toi manušware górot ainne edde uṭgunottu fũza lamai loiye. Ar uṭgunore ker edde buši diye, ar manušwa edde hitar sãti mainšore ṭeng dúibolla fani diye.
GEN 24:33 Tarfore zehon hána ainne, hetunot manušwaye hodde, "Ãi ãr hota hoiya no o foijjonto ãi hána no háiyum." Toi Labone hodde, "Toile ho!"
GEN 24:34 Toi hite hor, "Ãi Ibrahimor gulam.

GEN 24:36 Ãr girosor bou, Saraye hibar ei bura boyošot ãr girosolla ek futore biyaiye. Hitare hibar nizor hár kissu difelaiye.
GEN 24:37 Ar ãr girose ãre endilla hoi hosom goraiye, 'Ãi zarar dešot bošobaš gorir, he Kenaniyo okkolor ziyain okkolottu ãr futolla bou no anibi,
GEN 24:38 kintu tui ãr bafor górot zaibi edde ãr nizor egenar butottu ãr futolla ugguwa bou anibi.'
GEN 24:39 "Tarfore ãi ãr girosore fusar goijjilam, 'Kintu mayafuwa zodi ãr fũwati aito no sa ka?'
GEN 24:40 "Hibaye ãre hoil, 'Ãi zar sarme sola fira gori he Mabude firistare tor fũwati defeṛaibo edde tor baisare kamiyaf goraibo, toi zene ãr bafor gór edde egena okkolor butottu ãr futolla bou ani faros.
GEN 24:41 Tui ãr egenar górot zai bade zodi hitara hibare no de toile tui ãr ei hosomottu azad.'
GEN 24:42 "Aijja ãi zẽtte kuwar ḍake aišši, ãi hoiyide, 'Oh Mabud, ãr giros Ibrahimor Allah, meherbani gori tũi ãr ei baisare kamiyaf goro.
GEN 24:43 Ar so, ãi ei kuwar ḍake tiyai roiyi. Hono zuwan maya fuwa zodi fani tulito aiye, ãi hibare hoiyum, "Meherbani gori, tũwar górattu ãre ekka fani fiyabo,"
GEN 24:44 ar hibaye zodi ãre ho, "Fani fiyo, Ãi tũwar uṭgunolla o fani tuliyum," henoile hiba he maya fuwa ok, zibare Mabude ãr girosor futolla basona goijje.'
GEN 24:45 "Ãr dilot ei hota howa šeš no oite, Rebekah góra handot loi, niyoli aišše. Hiba kuwat laimme edde fani tuille, ar ãi hibare hoidde, 'Meherbani gori ãre ekka fani do.'
GEN 24:46 "Hibaye toratori hibar górawa handottu lamaiye edde hodde, 'Fani fiyo, ar ãi tũwar uṭgunore o fani diyum.' Toi ãi fani filam, edde hibaye uṭgunore o fani diye.
GEN 24:47 "Bade ãi hibare fusar goijji, 'Tui haro zi?' "Hibaye hodde, 'Ãi Melkar fut Betuelor zi, zare Melkaye Nahurolla biyaiye.' "Toi ãi hibare nakot nakful, ar hatot haru findai dilam.
GEN 24:48 Tarfore ãi Mabudore sojida goriyore šukuriya zanaiyi. Ãi ãr giros Ibrahimor Allah Mabudore šukurana adai goijji, kiyollahoile hibaye ãre soiyi rastat loi ainne zene ãi ãr girosor báifutor ziyore hibar futolla loi zai fari.
GEN 24:49 Ehon õnora zodi ãr giros loi doya edde soiyi bebar goribolla razi aso, toile ho. Ar zodi no tako, hiyan o ho, henot ãi zene ar oinno hono mikka zai fari."
GEN 24:50 Toi Labon edde Betuele zuwab diye, "Iyan zehon Mabudor torfottu oiye; ãra tũware bala edde bura kissu hoi no farir.
GEN 24:51 So, otiya Rebekah, hibare loi zo, Mabude hoilde mozin hiba tũwar girosor futor bou ok."
GEN 24:52 Ibrahimor gulame zehon hitarar ei hota fuinne, hite meṛit fori Mabudor sarme soida foijje.
GEN 24:53 Tarfore he gulame šuna rufa guwana fati hor sour bair gori hinore Rebekare diye; ar bout dami ziniš okkol o hite hibar bái edde mare diye.
GEN 24:54 Toi hite edde hitar fũwati aššilde manuš okkol, hitara beggune há fiya goijje edde heṛe rait haṛaiye. Bade hitara binna sore uiṭṭe, hite hodde, "Ãi ãr girosor heṛe zaiboilla bidai do."
GEN 24:55 Kintu hibar bái edde maye hodde, "Zuwan mayafuware aro ašṭo, doš din antaz ãrar fũwati takok; tarfore hiba zaibo."
GEN 24:56 Ar hite hitarare hodde, "Ãre ar eṛe raki no diyo, Mabude zehon ãr sofor kamiyaf goijjede dekir; ãre bidai do, ãi ãr girosor heṛe zaigoi."
GEN 24:57 Tarfore hitara hodde, "Toi zuwan mayafuwaware ḍaki, hibar mukottu ekka funi sai."
GEN 24:58 Toi hitara Rebekare ḍaikke edde fusar goijje, "Tui ei manušwar fũwati zaibi ne?" Hibaye hodde, "Ãi zaiyum."
GEN 24:59 Toi hitara hitar boin Rebekah edde hibar dáimare Ibrahimor gulam edde hitar manuš okkolor fũwati defeṛaiye.
GEN 24:60 Hitara Rebekare duwa gorer edde hibare hor, "Oh ãrar boin, tui hazar hazar futziyaindor ma o; tor bongšo okkole odihar adai gorok hitarar dušmon okkolor šohor okkolot."
GEN 24:61 Bade Rebekah edde hibar bandi okkol tiyar oiye edde uṭ okkolor uwore sori manušwar fise fise giye; ar he gulame Rebekare loi giyegoi.
GEN 24:62 Ehon Isak Beer Lahai Roi kuwar hentu bai gil, kiyollahoile hiba Negevot takito.
GEN 24:63 Hazinna odde ṭaimot Isake ãṛat maze maṛot giye, ar hibaye uwor mikka sadde šomot dekedde hodun uṭ aiyer.
GEN 24:64 Ar Rebekaye o uwor mikka saiye edde Isakore deikke. Toi hiba uṛottu nise laimme
GEN 24:65 edde gulamware hodde, "Maṛottu ãṛi ãrar uzu aiyedde hiba honnuwa?" Toi gulammuwaye hodde, "Hiba ãrar giros." Toi hibaye gũwaṛa loiye edde nizore guijje.
GEN 24:66 Tarfore he gulame hite goijjilde hár kissu beggun Isakore zanaiye.
GEN 24:67 Isake hibare hibar ma Sarar ṭambut ainne, edde Isake hibare loiye, toi hiba bou oiye edde hibare Isake ador goijje; hibar ma mori bade, Rebekar adore Isakore šantona dil.
GEN 25:1 Ibrahime ar ugguwa bou loiye, zar nam Keturah.
GEN 25:2 Hibaye hiballa Simron, Jokšan, Medan edde Midiyan, Išbak edde Šuah, itarare biyaiye.
GEN 25:3 Jokšane Šeba edde Dedan, itarare faiye; ar Dedanor bongšo okkol aššilde Asšuriyo, Letušiyo edde Leummiyo.
GEN 25:4 Ar Midiyanor futain okkol aššilde Efah, Efer, Hanok, Abida edde Eldaah. Itara beggun aššilde Keturar bongšo okkol.
GEN 25:5 Ibrahime hibar nizor hár kissu Isakore di giye.
GEN 25:6 Kintu Ibrahim basi taite, hibar bandi bouwaindor boitta hibar futain okkolore hadiya okkol diye, edde hibar fut Isakor hentu hitarare fuk mikka fuk dešot faṭai diye.
GEN 25:7 Ibrahimor zibonor bosoror din okkol oilde in: Hiba ekšo hoittor fãs bosor basi aššil.
GEN 25:8 Tarfore hibar boyoš oiyore edde beši bura boyošot šeš niyaš felaiye, edde hibar nizor manuš loi dola oiyegoi.
GEN 25:9 Hibar futain Isake edde Ismaile Mamrer sarme Hetittiyo Soharor fut Efronor maṭor Mokfelar gãtot hibare dohon diye,
GEN 25:10 ziyan Ibrahime Hetittiyo okkolottu kini loil, heṛe hibar bou Sarar fũwati Ibrahimore o dohon gora oiye.
GEN 25:11 Ibrahimor moron oi bade, hibar fut Isakore Allaye rahamot goijje. Ar Isak Beer Lahai Roir hãse bošobaš goijje.
GEN 25:12 Iyan oilde Ibrahimor fut Ismailor bongšo kahani, zare Sarar Mišoriyo bandi Hazeraye Ibrahimolla biyail.
GEN 25:13 In okkol oilde Ismailor futaindor nam okkol, hitarar zormonamat nam okkol asede mozin: Ismailor foila zormo Nebayot, Kedar, Adbeel edde Mibsam,
GEN 25:14 Mišma, Dumah, Massa,
GEN 25:15 Hadad, Tema, Jetur, Nafiš edde Kedmah.
GEN 25:16 In okkol aššide Ismailor futain okkol, edde hitarar fara okkol edde ṭambu okkol mozin itara oilde baro guštir sordar okkolor nam okkol.
GEN 25:17 Ismailor zibonor bosoror din okkol oilde in: Hiba ekšo tiriš hãt bosor basi aššil. Bade hibaye šeš niyaš felaiye edde mori giyegoi, ar hibar nizor manuš loi dola oiyegoi.
GEN 25:18 Ar Ismaili okkol Havilattu Šur foijjonto, ziyan Mišorottu Asšuror mikka, ei zaga okkolot bošobaš goijje, edde hitara hitarar hár sordar okkole ekku fũwati taki no fare.
GEN 25:19 In okkol oilde Ibrahimor fut Isakor bongšor kahani. Ibrahim Isakor baf oiye,
GEN 25:20 ar sališ bosor boyošot Isake Paddanor Aramiyo Betuelor zi edde Aramiyo Labonor boin Rebekare biya goijje.
GEN 25:21 Ar Isake hibar bouwolla Mabudor hãse duwa goijje, kiyollahoile hiba bázá aššil. Mabude hibar duware goisse, edde Rebekah hamil oiye.
GEN 25:22 Bade hibar gorbor butore fuwainde dora dori diye edde hibaye hodde, "Ãttu endilla ka or?" Toi hibaye Mabudottu fusar goitto giye.
GEN 25:23 Mabude hibare hodde, "Tor gorbot dui zati ase, Tor udorottu loti dui zati alok oiya oibo; Ek zati ar ek zatittuwaro beši šoktiwala oibo, ḍõrguwa oibo šoṛowar gulam."
GEN 25:24 Bade zehon hibaye biyaibar ṭaim aišše, ar so, hibar górbot zoikka morod fuwain.
GEN 25:25 Ar foila niyoli aiššede hite lal, hitar hara ga kẽšša bazu ḍoilla, hetolla hitara hitar nam raikke Iš.
GEN 25:26 Tarfore hitar bái niyoli aišše hitar hate Išor formurit dori, hetolla hitar nam raka oiye Yakub. Isakor boyoš haiṭ bosor zẽtte Rebekaye itarare biyaiye.
GEN 25:27 Ei fuwain ḍõr oiye edde Iš ekzon maṛot takoya, ekzon beši bala šiyari goroya oiye, ar Yakub aššilde ekzon nizam manuš, ze ṭambut takito.
GEN 25:28 Isak šiyari gusto hána moza faito, hetolla Išore ador goijje, kintu Rebekaye Yakubore ador goijje.
GEN 25:29 Ekbar Yakube zul rãder, Iš horan ferešan oi maṛottu firi aišše.
GEN 25:30 Hite Yakubore hodde, "Toratori gor, oi lal zulottu ãre kissu haito de, kiyollahoile ãi horan oiyi." (Hetolla Išore Edom zar mani Lal o ḍakito.)
GEN 25:31 Kintu Yakube hodde, "Age tui ãre tor foila zormor odihargan besifela."
GEN 25:32 Išye hodde, "Sa, ãi mori zairgoi, foila zormor odihar loi ãi ki goijjium?"
GEN 25:33 Yakube hodde, "Tui aijja ãr loi hosom há." Henot hite hitar hãse hosom háiye, edde hitar foila zormor odihargan Yakubore besifelaiye.
GEN 25:34 Toi Yakube Išore ruṭi edde rainda mošorir ḍailor zul diye. Ar hite há fiya gori bade hentu giyegoi. Endilla gori Išye hitar foila zormor odiharganore muillo sara goijje.
GEN 26:1 Ibrahimor ṭaimot ṛat oilde he foilawa bade ar ugguwa raṭ oiye. Toi Isak Gerarot Filistini okkolor badša Abimelekor hãse giye.
GEN 26:2 Mabude Isakore deha diye edde hodde, "Tui entu Mišorot lami no zaisgoi, ãi tore ze zagar babute hoiyum tui he zagat bošoti gor.
GEN 26:3 Tui hotokkalolla ei zagat tak, edde ãi tor fũwati takiyore tore rahamot goriyum, kiyollahoile ãi tore edde tor bongšore ei zaga okkol diyum, edde tor baf Ibrahimor hãse ze hosom háiyi hiyan ãi furon goijjium.
GEN 26:4 Ãi tor bongšore asmanor tara zedun hedun goriyum edde ei zaga okkol hitarare diyum, ar tor bongšor duwara duniyair hár zatiye duwa faibo,
GEN 26:5 kiyollahoile Ibrahime ãr hota fuinne edde ãr hár dabi, ãr hokum okkol, ãr ain edde kanon okkol falon goijje."
GEN 26:6 Toi Isak Gerarot taigiyegoi.
GEN 26:7 Ar he zagar mainše hibar bouwore boute fusar goijje, hibaye hodde, "Hiba ãr boin." Hibaye "Hiba ãr bou" hoite ḍoraiye, kiyollahoile hibaye ḍoraiye ze "Rebekkalla boli hitara hibare mari felaibo, kiyollahoile hiba beši šundor."
GEN 26:8 Isake bout hal heṛe bošobaš gori bade, Filistini badša Abimaleke zanala bai dekedde, Isake hibar nizor bou Rebekah loi šuhag gorer.
GEN 26:9 Toi Abimaleke Isakore ḍaikke edde hodde, "Sa, hiba hameka tor bou! Tui kengori hiba 'Ãr boin' hoi faijjos?" Isake hitare zuwabe hodde, "Kiyollahoile ãi mone goijjilam ãi hiballa boli foran haraiyum."
GEN 26:10 Abimaleke hodde, "Tui ãrar loi endilla kiyolla goijjos? Ze hono mainše to tor bou loi gum zai farito, ar tui ãrare hosurbon banaifelaiti."
GEN 26:11 Toi Abimaleke hár manuš okkolore endilla hoi hokum zari goijje: "Ze honokiye ei manušwar berudde otóba hitar bouwor berudde za, hitare hameka marifela oibo."
GEN 26:12 Isake he dešot saš goijje edde he bosor hinot ek šot gun fošol faiye. Mabude hibare rahamot goijje.
GEN 26:13 Toi hiba ḍor owa šuru goijje, ar ekattu ekka bariuṛat takiyore beši ḍõr manuš boinne.
GEN 26:14 Ar hibattu goru sool edde beša beši gulam okkol oiye, ar Filistini okkole hibar loi riš goijje.
GEN 26:15 Henot hibar baf Ibrahim zinda taite hibar gulam okkole kujjilde hár kuwa okkolore Filistini okkole meṛi felaiyore búzaifeliye.
GEN 26:16 Bade Abimaleke Isakore hodde, "Tui ãrar hentu zagoi, kiyollahoile tui ãrattuwaro beši šoktiwala oiyos."
GEN 26:17 Toi Isak hentu giyegoi edde Geraror ḍeilot zai ṭambu gãijje edde heṛe taikke.
GEN 26:18 Toi hibar baf Ibrahim zinda taite kujjilde kuwa hinore Isake abar kuijje, zinore Ibrahim mori bade Filistini okkole búzaifelail, ar bafe hinore ze nam okkol dil hibaye hinore he ekkui nam okkol diye.
GEN 26:19 Isakor gulam okkole ḍeilot kuriyore heṛe ugguwa fanir nal faiye.
GEN 26:20 Kintu Geraror soolsoroya okkole Isakor soolsoroya okkol loi hoijja diye edde hodde, "Ei fani ãrar!" hetolla Isake he kuwar nam diye Ešek, kiyollahoile hitara hibar loi hoijja goijjil.
GEN 26:21 Bade hitara ar uggwa kuwa kuijje, kintu hiba loi o hitara hoijja goijje; hetolla hibaye hibar nam diye Sitnah.
GEN 26:22 Toi hiba hentu giyegoi edde ar uggwa kuwa kuijje, ar hiballa hitara hoijja no gore, ar hibaye hibar nam diye Rehobot edde hodde, "Šeš foijjonto Mabude ãrare farot zaga diye, ar ãra ei zagat fólwala oi faijjum."
GEN 26:23 Ar hentu hiba Beer-Šebat giye.
GEN 26:24 He raitta Mabude hibare deha diyore hodde, "Ãi tor baf Ibrahimor Allah, tũi no ḍorais; ãi tor fũwati asi, ãi tore rahamot goriyum; ar Ibrahimor hatire ãi tor bongšore baraidiyum."
GEN 26:25 Toi Isake heṛe ekkan kurbangah tiyar goijje edde Mabudor nam ḍaikke. Heṛe hibaye hibar ṭambu o maijje, edde hibar gulam okkole heṛe uggwa kuwa kuijje.
GEN 26:26 Bade Abimaleke hitar dusto Ahussat edde hitar foila šenafoti Fikolore loi Gerarottu Isakor hãse aišše.
GEN 26:27 Isake hitarare hodde, "Tũwara ãr hãse kiyolla aiššo, tũwara to hingša gori ãre hentu dũrai dila?"
GEN 26:28 Hitara hodde, "Ãra foriškar gori dekir ze Mabud tor fũwati ase; hetolla ãra baffilam ze 'tui edde ãrar maze uggwa wada sukti takon zoruri.' Aio, ãra tor loi hosom hái,
GEN 26:29 ãra zendilla šude tor balai bade hono hoti no gori edde tore šanti gori bidai dilam, hendilla tui o ãrar hono hoti no goribi. Ar ehon tore Mabude rahamot goijje."
GEN 26:30 Toi Isake hitaralla hánar entezam goijje, edde hitara há fiye goijje.
GEN 26:31 Tarfordin binna sore uṛi ekzon loi ekzone hosom háiye. Bade Isake hitarare bidai diye, ar hitara šanti gori hentu baisa diye.
GEN 26:32 He din Isakor gulam okkol aiyore hitarar kuijja uggwa kuwar babute Isakore hoiye. Hitara hodde, "Ãra fani faiyi!"
GEN 26:33 Hibaye hibare nam diye Šeba. Hetolla he šohoror nam aijo foijjonto Beer-Šeba.
GEN 26:34 Ar Išor boyoš sališ bosor oiyede šomot, Hetittiyo Beerir zi Yudit, edde Hetittiyo Elonor zi Bašmathore o, biya goijje.
GEN 26:35 Ar hitara Isak edde Rebekar zibonore tita gori tuillil.
GEN 27:1 Isak zẽtte bura oiye edde sukor zuti eto homi giyegoi hiba ar suke deki no farito, hibaye hibar ḍõr fut Išore ḍaikke edde hodde, "Ãr fut." Hite hodde, "Oto ãi eṛe."
GEN 27:2 Toi Isake hodde, "Sa, ãi bura oiyi ar hon din ãr moron o ãi no zani.
GEN 27:3 Tor zontrofati, tir edde hanḍa loi maṛot za edde ãlla kissu šiyar gori an.
GEN 27:4 Ãi foson goride hendilla kissu bana, edde ãlla an, ãi haiyum, toi zene ãi moribar age tore ãi duwa gori fari."
GEN 27:5 Isake hibar fut Iš loi hota hodde Rebekaye fuinne. Toi zehon Iše maṛottu šiyar gori anibolla giye,
GEN 27:6 Rebekaye hibar fut Yakubore hodde, "Sa, ãi tor bafe tor bái Išore endilla hodde funni,
GEN 27:7 'Ãlla kissu šiyar gori an edde ai foson goride hendilla kissu háibolla bana, toi zene ãi moribar age Mabudor sarme tore duwa di fari.'
GEN 27:8 Hetolla oh fut, ãi tore ehon zen goitto hoir hũšiyare fun:
GEN 27:9 Tui zai zakottu barik duwa soolor so ãre ani de, toi zene ãi tor bafe zendilla foson gore hendilla mozar kissu hána tiyar gori fari.
GEN 27:10 Tarfore tui hinore tor bafe háibolla hibar hãse loizabi, zene hiba moribar age tore hibar duwa di fare."
GEN 27:11 Yakube hibar ma Rebekare hodde, "So, ãr bái Iš ekzon kẽšša manuš, ar ãi kẽš sara.
GEN 27:12 Ãr bafe zodi ãre sue edde tuwai fa ze ãi hibare dúha dir, henoile ãi nizor uwore duwattuwaro bodduwa ḍaki aniyum."
GEN 27:13 Hibar maye hodde, "Oh fut, tor he bodduwa ãr uwore forok, bolke tui ãi ziyan hoir hiyan gor, zaiyore hingun ãlla ani de."
GEN 27:14 Tarfore Yakube zai hin loi mar hãse loigiye. Toi Yakubor bafe zendilla foson goitto, maye hendilla mozar hána tiyar goijje.
GEN 27:15 Ar górot hibar ḍõr fut Išor ze šundor horsuwor aššil, Rebekaye hin loi hibar šoṛo fut Yakubore findai diye.
GEN 27:16 Yakubor hatot edde golat zeṛe kẽš nuwaššil, heṛe hibaye soolor sam berai diye.
GEN 27:17 Tarfore nize banaiyede mozar hána edde ruṭi Yakubor hatot tulidiye.
GEN 27:18 Bade Yakube hibar bafor hãse zai hodde, "Baba!" Isake zuwabe hodde, "Oto ãi, oh fut, tui honnuwa?"
GEN 27:19 Yakube hibar bafore hodde, "Ãi tũwar foila zormo Iš. Tũi ãre hoilade hendilla goijji. Meherbani gori uṛi boiyo, ãr šiyari gusto ho, toi zene tũi ãre tũwar duwa di faro."
GEN 27:20 Zuwabe Isake hibar futore hodde, "Tui in eto toratori kengori faili, oh fut?" Zuwabe Yakube hodde, "Tũwar Mabud Allaye milai diye."
GEN 27:21 Isake Yakubore hodde, "Ãi tore sui farifan ãr ḍake ai, tui soyi ãr fut Iš oi ne no zani sai!"
GEN 27:22 Yakube hitar bafor ḍake aišše, toi hibaye suiye edde hodde, "Abaz to Yakubor abaz, ar hat to Išor hat."
GEN 27:23 Hibaye hitare sini no fare, kiyollahoile báiyor hator ḍoilla Yakubor hat o kẽšwala aššil; toi hibaye duwa diye,
GEN 27:24 edde hodde, "Tui ki soiyi ãr fut Iš oi?" Yakube hodde, "Oi baba."
GEN 27:25 Toi hibaye hodde, "Toile hin ãr hãse an, ãi ãr futor šiyaror gusto hái, toi zene ãi tore duwa di fari." Toi Yakube hin hibar hãse loigiye edde hibaye háiye; ar Yakube hibare kissu šoraf ani diye edde hibaye fiye.
GEN 27:26 Tarfore hibar baf Isake hodde, "Oh fut, ikka ai, ãre suma de."
GEN 27:27 Toi Yakub hibar ḍake giye edde suma diye. Ar Isake hitar fušak fũiye edde endilla hoi duwa diye edde hodde, "Ãr futor šugondi, oilde en ek maṭor ḍoilla, ziyanore Mabude rahamot goijje.
GEN 27:28 Allaye zen tore asmanottu kúwa de, ar tor zobinot bol de, ar beša beši gĩyu edde noya šoraf de.
GEN 27:29 Zati okkole tor gulam ok, ar hokkol mainše tor sarme mata zuhauk. Tor báiyaindor uwore tui malik o, ar tor mar futainde tore mata zuhauk. Tore zara bodduwa dibo, hitarar uwore bodduwa! Tore zara duwa goribo, hitarar uwore rahamot."
GEN 27:30 Isake Yakubore duwa diya šeš gori bade Yakube hibar baf Isakor sarmottu zaigoi mottor hibar bái Iš šiyar gori aišše.
GEN 27:31 Hibaye o mozar ziniš okkol tiyar goijje edde bafor hãse ainne, toi bafore hodde, "Baba, uṛo, tũwar futor šiyaror gusto ho, toi zene tũi ãre duwa di faro."
GEN 27:32 Hibar baf Isake hibare hodde, "Tui honnuwa?" Hibaye hodde, "Ãi tũwar foila zormo, Iš."
GEN 27:33 Ei hota funi Isak beša beši hafa šuru goijje edde hodde, "Toile šiyar gori ãlla šiyaror gusto annilde hiba honnuwa? Ãi tui aibar age hin háiyi edde hitare duwa difelaiyi, ar ehon hite rahamot faigiyegoi!"
GEN 27:34 Išye zehon hitar bafor hota fuinne, hite õraguzori hainde edde hitar bafore hodde, "Baba, ãre o duwa goro!"
GEN 27:35 Kintu hibaye hodde, "Tor báiye dúha bazi gori aiyore tor duwa hite loi giyegoi."
GEN 27:36 Iše hodde, "Etolla no ne hitar nam Yakub? Ehon foijjonto hite ãre dui bar dúha diye: Hite ãr foila zormor odihar loiye, ar ehon hite ãr duwa loifelaye." Tarfore hibaye fusar goredde, "Tũi ãlla ki hono duwa no rako ne ki?"
GEN 27:37 Isake zuwabe Išore hodde, "Sa, ãi hitare tor uwore malik goijji edde hitar guštir beggunore hitar gulam goijji. Ãi hitalla gĩyu edde noya šorafolla bondobos goijji, ehon ãi tolla ar ki gori fariyum?"
GEN 27:38 Iše hitar bafore hodde, "Baba, tũwattu ki šude ekkan duwa aššilde ne ki? Baba, ãre o duwa goro!" Toi Iše guzori hainde.
GEN 27:39 Toi hitar baf Isake hitare zuwabe hodde, "Sa, tor bošoti oibo bol sara zobinot, zeṛe no foribo asmanottu kúwa.
GEN 27:40 Ar tui toluwar loi basibi, ar tui tor báiyor gulami goribi. Kintu tui zẽtte odoizzo oi uṛos, tui hitar zũwal, tor handottu felaidibi."
GEN 27:41 Ar Yakubore hibar bafe duwa dil boli Iše hibare hingša goijje. Ar Iše mone mone hodde, "Ãr bafolla šuk goribar ṭaim hãsaiyegai; tarfore ãi ar bái Yakubore marifelaiyum."
GEN 27:42 Toi Rebekaye zehon hibar ḍõr fut Išor hota zani faijje, hibaye hibar šoṛo fut Yakubor hãse hóbor defeṛaiye, hodde, "Fun, tor bái Iše tore marifelaibar ereda loi nizore šantona der.
GEN 27:43 Hetolla oh fut, tũi ãr hota fun: Uṭ, tui ehon Haranot ãr bái Labonor heṛe dái zagoi.
GEN 27:44 Hoto din tui heṛe takgoi, tor báiyor rag homi no zagoi foijjonto,
GEN 27:45 ar hitar rag gilegoi edde tui ziyan goijjos hiyan hite foraifelaile, ãi hóbor defeṛaiyum edde hentu tore loi aniyum. Ãi ekkui dinot tũwara dunizonore kiyolla haraitam?"
GEN 27:46 Bade Rebekaye Isakore hodde, "Ei Hetittiyo mayafuwaingunolla buli ãttu ar basi taito mone no hor. Heṛe uwore zodi Yakube o ei dešor hono Hetittiyo mayafuware biya gore toile ãi basi taki ki lab oibo?"
GEN 28:1 Toi Isake Yakubore ḍaikke edde duwa goijje, ar hibaye endilla hokum diye: "Tui Kenaniyo hono mayafuware biya no goribi.
GEN 28:2 Tui Paddan Aramot tor mar baf Betuelor górot za, heṛe tor mar bái Labonor hono ziyaindor butottu tolla ugguwa bou lo.
GEN 28:3 Šorbo-Šoktiwala Allaye tore rahamot gorok edde fólwala gorok edde barai tulok, toi zene tui ugguwa bout zatir šomaz os.
GEN 28:4 Ar hibaye Ibrahimor duwa tui edde tor fũwati tor bongšore dok, toi zene ze zagat tui ehon ekzon bidešitta hisabe takor, ziyanore Allaye Ibrahimore dil, hiyan tor šombotti oi fare."
GEN 28:5 Toi Isake Yakubore bidai diye, edde Yakube Paddan Aramot, Aramiyo Betuelor fut, Rebekar bái Labonor hãse giye, ze aššil Yakub edde Išor ma.
GEN 28:6 Iše zehon zanifaijje ze Isake Yakubore duwa goijje edde Paddan Aramottu hono ek maya fuwa biya goribolla heṛe defeṛaiye, edde hitare duwa goribar šomot hokum dil, "Tui Kenaniyo hono mayafuware biya no goribi."
GEN 28:7 Ar Yakube hitar baf edde mar hota mainne edde Paddan Aramot giyegoi.
GEN 28:8 Toi Išye buzi faijje ze Kenaniyo mayafuwain okkol hitar baf sukot hondilla horaf de hiyan.
GEN 28:9 Hetolla hite Ismailor heṛe giye, edde dui bou bade hite Ibrahimor fut Ismailor zi, Nebayotor boin, Mahalathore biya goijje.
GEN 28:10 Ar Yakub Beer-Šebattu niyoliyore Haranor mikka giye.
GEN 28:11 Ar hono ek zagat fõsi bade heṛe rait haṛaiye, kiyollahoile beil góillegoi. Toi hibaye hentu ugguwa fattor loiye, edde matar tole diyore gum zaibolla neiṭṭe.
GEN 28:12 Toi Yakube šopponot dekedde, duniyair uwore ekkan hãṭṭa uwa oi roiye, ar hiyanor uworor mata asman suiye, ar so, hiyan bai Allar firista okkol uṛa lama gorer.
GEN 28:13 Ar Mabude hiyanor uwore tiyaiye edde hodde: "Ãi Mabud, tor baf Ibrahimor edde Isakor Allah. Tui zeṛe neṛi roiyos he zaga hiyanore ãi tore edde tor bongšore diyum.
GEN 28:14 Tor bongšo okkol duniyair dúilor ḍoilla oibo edde fuk fosim edde uttor doine tor bongšo šiṛi zaiboi, edde tui edde tor bongšor duwara duniyair hár zatire duwa gora oibo.
GEN 28:15 Ar sa, ãi tor fũwati asi, tui zeṛe zaibi za, ãi tore rokka goriyum, edde ãi tore ei zagat loi aniyum; kiyollahoile ãi tore wada diyide hin goijja no oite ãi tore eri no zaiyumboi."
GEN 28:16 Bade Yakubor gum bainge edde hiba hodde, "Ei zagat hameka Mabud ase, ar ãi to iyan no zanitam."
GEN 28:17 Ar hibaye ḍoraiye edde hodde, "Ken ḍor lagede zaga iyan! Iyan ar kissu no, hameka Allar gór oibo, iyan oilde behostor geiṭ."
GEN 28:18 Tarfore Yakube binna sore uiṭṭe edde ze fattor hibaye matar tole dil hiba loi faiya ḍoilla gori buwaiye edde hibar uwore tel ḍaille.
GEN 28:19 Ar he zagar nam diye Betel, zodi o he šohorganor nam age Luz aššil.
GEN 28:20 Toi Yakube ek manoš goijje edde hodde, "Zodi Allah ãr fũwati take edde zeṛe zair he fõtot ãre rokka gore, edde ãre háibolla hána ar findibolla hoor de,
GEN 28:21 ar zodi šušondane ãi bafor górot firi aifari, toile ei Mabud ãr Allah oibo.
GEN 28:22 Ar ze fattor ãi eṛe faiyar ḍoilla tiya gorai raikki, hiyan Allar gór oibo, ar tũi za kissu ãre diba hinor doš bag ai tũware diyum."
GEN 29:1 Bade Yakube zat roiye edde fuk mullukka okkolor dešot aišše.
GEN 29:2 Heṛe hibaye maṛot maze uggwa kuwa deikke, ar so, hibar ḍake tinnuwa berasoolor zãk luṛiroiye, kiyollahoile he kuwattu hinore fani fiyaito. Ar kuwawar mukot ekkan beši ḍõr fattor.
GEN 29:3 Ar heṛe zãk okkol beggun zẽtte dola oito, hitara kuwar mukor fattorguware algaiyore zãkore fani fiyaito. Tarfore hitara fattorguware abar uwafes loi kuwar mukot buwai dito.
GEN 29:4 Yakube soolsoroya okkolore fusar goredde, "Ãr báiyain okkol, tũwara hoṛiyar?" "Ãra Harranottu" hoi hitara zuwab diye.
GEN 29:5 Yakube hitarare hodde, "Tũwara Nahuror nati, Labonore sino ne?" "Oi, ãra sini," hoi zuwab diye.
GEN 29:6 Tarfore Yakube hitarare hodde, "Hiba bala asede no ne?" Toi hitara hodde, "Oi, bala ase, ar so, hibar zi Rahela berasoolor zãk loi aiyerwa."
GEN 29:7 Yakube hodde, "So, beil foitte ar bout deri ase, zanuwaror zãk okkolore ekottro goribar ṭaim aizo no o. Tũwara bolke tũwarar soolgunore fani fiyaiyore hinore abar soraito loizo."
GEN 29:8 Hitara zuwabe hodde, "Ãra hen gori no faijjum, zãk beggun ekottro no o foijjonto, toi kuwar mukottu fattorgan algaiyore ãra zãkore fani fiyai faijjumde."
GEN 29:9 Yakube ehono hitara loi hota hor, hen šomot Rahela hibar bafor berasoolor zãk loi heṛe aišše, kiyollahoile hiba aššilde soolsoroni.
GEN 29:10 Toi Yakube zehon hibar mamu Labonor zi Rahelare edde Labonor soolor zãkore deikke, hibaye ḍake zai kuwar mukottu fattorgan algaiye edde hibar mamu Labonor zãkore fani fiyaiye.
GEN 29:11 Bade Rahelare suma diye edde õraguzori handa šuru goijje.
GEN 29:12 Toi Yakube Rahelare hoil ze hiba hibar bafor egena edde Rebekar fut. Toi hibaye dũri giye edde hiyan bafore hoiye.
GEN 29:13 Ar Labone hitar boinor fut Yakubor babute funiyore, dũri hibar loi deha goitto giye, edde hibar loi ãzaãzi goijje, edde hibare suma diye, edde hibare hitar górot loi ainne, ar heṛe Yakube hitare in okkol beggun hoiye.
GEN 29:14 Bade Labone hibare hodde, "Soiyi tui ãr nizor ãḍḍi edde gusto." Toi Yakub hitar górot ek maš taikke,
GEN 29:15 bade Labone Yakubore hodde, "Tui ãr egena buli ki bina muzoriye ãr ham goribi ne? Tore beton ki diya foribo ãre ho."
GEN 29:16 Labonottu duizon zi ase; ḍõrguwar nam Leah, ar šoṛowar nam Rahela.
GEN 29:17 Leattu aššilde šude duwa šundor suk, kintu Rahelar hara ga edde siyara, hár kissu šundor aššil.
GEN 29:18 Yakube Rahelare muhabbot goitto. Yakube hodde, "Tũwar šoṛo zi Rahelalla ãi hãt bosor tũwar gulami goijjium."
GEN 29:19 Labone hodde, "Ãi hibare oinno honokiyore diyattuwaro tor diya iyan ãlla aro bala oibo. Tui ãr hãse tak!"
GEN 29:20 Toi Yakube Rahelalla hãt bosor gulami goijje, ar hibattu hibar uwore muhabbotor zoriya hinore hibattu šude kissu dinor ḍoil laigge.
GEN 29:21 Tarfore Yakube Labonore hodde, "Ãr din šeš oiye, ehon ãr bou ãre do, ãi zene hiba loi taki fari."
GEN 29:22 Toi Labone heṛiyar manuš okkol beggunore ekkui fũwati goijje, edde ek hánar entezam goijje.
GEN 29:23 Ar hazinna zehon oiye, hite hitar zi Leare loi Yakubor hãse ani diye, toi Yakube hibar loi taikke.
GEN 29:24 Labone hitar bandi Zilpare hitar zi Lealla daima hisabe hibare diye.
GEN 29:25 Toi binna zehon oiye dekedde, hiba Leah! Toi Yakube Labonore hodde, "Tũi in ãr loi goijjode in ki? Ãi Rahelalla tũwar gulami goijjide, no ne? Tũi ãre dúha kene dila?"
GEN 29:26 Labone hodde, "Foila zormor age šoṛoware biya diya iyan ãrar ei zagar niyom no.
GEN 29:27 Tui ei biyar hãt dinna furon gor; bade aro hãt bosor gulamir bodole ãra tore šoṛoware o diyum."
GEN 29:28 Henot Yakube hendilla goijje, hãt dinna furon goijje, ar Labone hitar zi Rahelare o Yakubor bou oibolla diye.
GEN 29:29 Labone hitar bandi Bilhare Rahelalla daima hisabe hibare diye.
GEN 29:30 Yakube Rahela loi o taikke, ar hibaye Leattuwaro Rahelare beši ador goijje. Ar Yakube Labonor hãse aro hãt bosor gulami goijje.
GEN 29:31 Bade Mabude zehon deikke ze Leare ador no gore, hibaye hibare hamil oi farefan gori diye, kintu Rahela baz oi roiye.
GEN 29:32 Leah hamil oiye edde ek futore biyaiye. Hibaye hitar nam raikke Ruben, kiyollahoile hibaye hodde, "Mabude ãr dukkore deikke; ebar ãr šuwamiye ãre hameka ador goribo."
GEN 29:33 Hiba abar hamil oiye, edde ek futore biyaiye, toi hibaye hodde, "Ãre ador no gorede hiyan Mabude funniye, hetolla hibaye ãre iba o diyede." Toi hibaye hitar nam raikke Simeon.
GEN 29:34 Hiba abar hamil oiye edde ek futore biyaiye, toi hibaye hodde, "Ebar ãr šuwami ãlloi bazi takibo, kiyollahoile ãi hiballa tin futore zormo diyi." Toi hibaye hitar nam raikke Levi.
GEN 29:35 Hiba abar hamil oiye edde ek futore biyaiye, toi hibaye hodde, "Ebar ãi Mabudore tarif goriyum." Toi hibaye hitar nam raikke Ehudah. Tarfore hibar fuwa biya bon oigiyegoi.
GEN 30:1 Rahelaye zehon deikke ze hibaye Yakubolla hono fuwain no biya, hibar boinor uwore hibattu hingša oiye. Hibaye Yakubore hodde, "Ãre fuwain do, ar no oile ãi moriyum."
GEN 30:2 Henot Yakubor gušša Rahelar uwore zoli uiṭṭe edde hodde, "Ãi ki Allar zagat ne, zibaye tor udorot fól diyare ošikar goijje?"
GEN 30:3 Toi hibaye hodde, "So, otiya, ãr bandi Bilhah hibar hãse zo, zene hibaye fuwa biyai ãr kulot de, toi zene ãi hibar duwara oile ãi o ma oi fari."
GEN 30:4 Toi hibaye hibar bandi Bilhare Yakubore ek bou hisabe diye. Yakube hibar hãse giye,
GEN 30:5 edde hiba hamil oiye, ar Yakubolla ek fut biyaiye.
GEN 30:6 Toi Rahelaye hodde, "Allaye ãr bisar goijje; hibaye ãr foriyad fuinne edde ãre ek fut diye." Hiyanor zoriya hibaye hitar nam raikke Ḍan.
GEN 30:7 Bade Rahelar bandi Bilhah abar hamil oiye edde Yakubolla dusora ek futore biyaiye.
GEN 30:8 Toi Rahelaye hodde, "Allar kutsi loi ãr boin loi kutsi doriyore ãi zitti." Hetolla hibaye hitar nam raikke Naftali.
GEN 30:9 Bade Leaye dekedde hibar fuwa owa bon oigiyegoi, hibaye hibar bandi Zilpare loi Yakubore ek bou hisabe diye.
GEN 30:10 Toi Lear bandi Zilpaye Yakubolla ek futore biyaiye.
GEN 30:11 Toi Leaye hodde, "Ki baggitta!" Toi hibaye hitar nam raikke Gad.
GEN 30:12 Bade Lear bandi Zilpaye Yakubolla dusora ek futore biyaiye.
GEN 30:13 Toi Leaye hodde, "Ãi hoto šuki! kiyollahoile zobuti okkole ãre šuki hoibo." Toi hibaye hitar nam raikke Ašer.
GEN 30:14 Ar gĩyu dade ṭaimot Rubene maṛot giye edde hodun dudim-sara faiye, zinore hite hitar ma Leare ani diye. Rahelaye Leare hodde, "Tor futor dudim-sarattu ãre olfo desena!"
GEN 30:15 Kintu Leaye hodde, "Tui ãr zamai hari loiyosde hiyane ki no o, ne? Ãr futor dudim-saragun o loifelaibi ne ki?" Zuwabe Rahelaye hodde, "Bala, tor futor dudim-sarar bodole Yakub aijja raitta tor loi takibo."
GEN 30:16 Toi Yakub zehon hazinna maṛottu górot aišše, Leaye bare niyoli hibar hãse zai hodde, "Tũi ãr hãse aiyo, kiyollahoile ãr futor dudim-sara loi tũware bara goijji." Toi he raitta Yakube hibar loi taikke.
GEN 30:17 Ar Allaye Lear foriyad fuinne, hibaye hamil oiye edde Yakubolla fãs lombor futore biyaiye.
GEN 30:18 Toi Leaye hodde, "Ãr šuwamire ãi bandi diyide hiyanor enam Allaye ãre diye." Toi hibaye hitar nam raikke Issakar.
GEN 30:19 Bade Leah abar hamil oiye, edde Yakubolla so lombor futore biyaiye.
GEN 30:20 Toi Leaye hodde, "Allaye ãre barik hadiya diye. Ehon ãr šuwamiye ãre šorman dibo, kiyollahoile ãi hiballa so futore zormo diyi." Toi hibaye hitar nam raikke Sebulun.
GEN 30:21 Bade hibaye ek zerfuwa biyaiye edde hibar nam raikke Dina.
GEN 30:22 Allaye Rahelar mikka kiyal raikke; hibaye hibar foriyad fuinne edde hamil oi farefan gori diye.
GEN 30:23 Henot hiba hamil oiye edde hibaye ek futore biyaiye edde hodde, "Allaye ãr šorom loifelaye."
GEN 30:24 Hibaye hitar nam raikke Yusuf, ar hodde, "Mabude ãre aro ek fut dok."
GEN 30:25 Ar Rahelattu Yusuf zormo oi bade Yakube Labonore hodde, "Ãre bidai do, toi zene ãi ãr nizor dešor górot firizai fari.
GEN 30:26 Ar ãr bouwain edde fuwain zaralla ãi tũwar gulami goijji, hitarare ãre do, toi zene ãi zai fari; kiyollahoile tũi to zano ãi tũwalla hondilla haṛoni goijji."
GEN 30:27 Toi Labone hodde, "Ãi zodi tottu doyar nozor fai taki toile meherbani gori tak, kiyollahoile ãi goni sai zani faijji ze Mabude tor zoriya ãre rahamot goijje."
GEN 30:28 Hite aro hodde, "Tore beton hodun diya foribo tui ho, ãi tore diyum."
GEN 30:29 Kintu Yakube hitare hodde, "Tũi to nize zano ãi tũwalla hondilla ham goijji, ar ãr hatot tũwar zanuwaror zãkor abosta hondilla oiye.
GEN 30:30 Kiyollahoile ãi aibar age tũwattu ze hom šombotti aššil hin beša beši barigiyegoi, edde ãr zoriya Mabude tũware rahamot goijje, kintu ãr nizor gór okkololla hõtte hamai goriyum?"
GEN 30:31 Toi Labone fusar goredde, "Ãi tore ki diyum?" Yakube hodde, "Tũi ãre kissu no diyo; ãlla zodi ekkan ham goro, toile ãi tũwar zanuwaror zãk okkolore soraiyum edde hinore saiyum:
GEN 30:32 Aijja ãi tũwar hár zanuwar okkolor mazottu di zaiyum edde hinor butottu šoṛo ḍõr fuṛawala dag asede berasool edde sool, ar hala berasoolor so okkolore aleda gorito sai. Hin oibode ãr beton.
GEN 30:33 Tarfore zẽtte tũi ãre beton saibolla hazir oiba, hẽtte ãr soyiye ãr goba dibo. Toi šoṛo ḍõr fuṛawala dag naide hendilla hono berasoolor so zodi ãr zanuwaror zãkor butore fa gile, toile hin ãi suri goijji dora oibo."
GEN 30:34 Labone hodde, "Sa, toile tor hota mozin hendilla ok!"
GEN 30:35 Toi Labone hedin sitara faṛa soolgun edde dag asede faṛi sool okkol zedunor uwore dola aššil hin edde hala rongor berasool okkolore aleda goijje edde hinore hitar futaindor hãse zimma diye.
GEN 30:36 Ar Labone hite edde Yakubor maze tin dinor fõtor baisa foijjonto bebedan raikke, ar Labonor baki zãk okkolore Yakube lagar sorat roiye.
GEN 30:37 Bade Yakube liboni, luš edde armon gasor tottoza kẽsa ḍeila haṛi loiye edde hinor uwore sál tuliyore dag goijje, gasor ḍeila okkolor butoror dola deha zafan goriyore.
GEN 30:38 Toi hibaye he sál tuilla ḍeilagunore zanuwaror zãke fani fiyede zaga okkolot raikke, toi zene zãk okkol fani fito aile hin okkol šuza sarme fore. Zanuwar okkole fani fito aitode šomot zur zaito.
GEN 30:39 Ar hine ḍeilagunor sarme zur zaito, edde hine ze so okkol biyaito, hin sitara, ar no oile ḍõr otóba šoṛo dagwala oito.
GEN 30:40 Yakube soolor so edde berasoolor so okkolore aleda gori rakito, kintu faṛi sool okkolore Labonor boitta sitara edde hala sool okkolor mikka muk firabaito. Ebafe Yakube hiba nizolla ek soolor zãk gori felaiye, edde hinore Labonor zanuwaror zãk loi no miyaito.
GEN 30:41 Ar beši šoktiwala zanuwargune zene ḍeilar ḍake zur za, hiyanolla buli fani fiyede zagat maze zanuwar okkolor sarme he ḍeila okkol rakito,
GEN 30:42 kintu leṛa zanuwar okkol oile sarme no rakito. Henot leṛa zanuwar okkol Labonor, ar šoktiwala zanuwar okkol Yakubor oito.
GEN 30:43 Ar ei bafe Yakub kub beši tuwangor oiye edde hibattu zanuwar edde gulam bandi edde ũṭ gada beši oiye.
GEN 31:1 Bade Labonor futainde endilla hodde Yakube fuinne, "Ãrar bafor hár kissu Yakube loifelaiye, ãrar baforgunottu hite ei šombotti okkol goijje."
GEN 31:2 Yakube Labonor siyarar mikka kiyal goijje, ar so, Labon Yakub loi agor ḍoilla nai.
GEN 31:3 Hetunot Mabude Yakubore hodde, "Tui tor bafor dešot tor egena okkolor hãse uwafes firizagoi, ar ãi tor fũwati takiyum."
GEN 31:4 Toi Yakube hóbor defeṛaiye edde Rahelare edde Leare maṛot hibar zanuwaror zãk asede heṛe ḍaikke.
GEN 31:5 Hitarare hodde, "Ãi tũwarar bafor siyarar sai buzi faijji ze ãr loi tũwarar baf agor ḍoilla nai, kintu ãr bafor Allah ãr fũwati ase.
GEN 31:6 Ar tũwara nize o zanode hota, ãi ãr hár bol šokti diyore tũwarar bafolla gulami goijji.
GEN 31:7 Tarfore o tũwarar bafe ãre ṭokaiye edde ehon foijjonto doš bar ãr beton bodol goijje, kintu Allaye hibare ãre hoti goitto no de.
GEN 31:8 Hibaye zodi hoito, 'dagwalagun oibo tor beton,' henot hár zãke dagwala so biyaito; ar zodi hoito, 'sitaragun tor beton oibo,' henot zãke sitara so biyaito.
GEN 31:9 Ei bafe Allaye tũwarar bafor zanuwaror zãkgun loifelaiye edde ãre diye.
GEN 31:10 "Zanuwaror zãk okkole zurzade musumot ãi ekbar šopponot suk tuli sailam ze sai sool okkolor uwore ze faṛa sool okkol uiṭṭe hin beggun sitara edde ḍõr šoṛo dagwala.
GEN 31:11 Tarfore Allar firistaye ãre šopponot hodde, 'Yakub.' Ar ãi hoidde, 'Oto, ãi eṛe asi.'
GEN 31:12 Toi hibaye hodde, 'Tor suk tuli sa, faṛa sool okkol zin zanuwaror zãkor uwore uṛer hin sitara, šoro ḍõr dagwala, kiyollahoile Labone tor loi goredde hin beggun ãi dekki.
GEN 31:13 Ãi he Betelor Allah, zeṛe tui ek kúṛar uwore tel ḍali diyore ãr hãse manoš goijjili. Uṭ, tui ehon ei deššanottu niyoli zagoi edde tui zormo oiyosde dešot uwafes firizagoi.'"
GEN 31:14 Toi Rahela edde Leaye hodde, "Ãrattu ki ãrar bafor góttu ehono mirazor bag ase ne?
GEN 31:15 Hibaye ki ãrare bidešitta hisabe no goner ne? Hibaye ãrare besifelaiye edde ãralla ze ṭiya diya oil hin hibaye háifelaiye.
GEN 31:16 Ei šombotti Allaye ãrar bafottu ãra edde ãrar futziyaindolla hari loiyede. Ar hetolla ehon Allaye tũware za kissu hoiye tũi hen goro."
GEN 31:17 Toi Yakube hibar fuwain edde bouwaindore ũṛor fiṛot tuli diye,
GEN 31:18 edde hibaye hibar hár zanuwar zãk šoho aro dusora dón šombotti zin Paddan Aramot hamail hin beggun o fũwati loiye, Kenanot hibar baf Isakor hãse zaiboilla.
GEN 31:19 Ar zẽtte Labone hitar berasoolor kẽš ãsaibolla gil, Rahelaye hibar bafor góror muttigunore suri goijje.
GEN 31:20 Ar Yakube Aramiyo Labonore dúha diye, kiyollahoile Yakube dái zargoide he babute o hoi no za.
GEN 31:21 Ar ebafe Yakubor za kissu aššil hin loi hiba hentu dái giyegoi, Fúrat hal farai giye edde Giliyad faharor mikka giye.
GEN 31:22 Ar tin din bade Labonore howa oiye ze Yakub dái giyegoi.
GEN 31:23 Toi hite hitar egena okkolore fũwati loiyore hãt dinor fõt foijjonto Yakubore lorai loigiye edde Giliyad faharot hibare lot faiye.
GEN 31:24 Kintu Allah raitta šopponot Aramiyo Labonor hãse ai hodde, "Hũšiyar, Yakubore bala horaf kissu no hois."
GEN 31:25 Ar zẽtte Labone Yakub loi dola oiye, hẽtte Yakube Giliyad faharor uwore ṭambu gãijjil, ar Labon edde hitar egena okkole o heṛe ṭambu gãijje.
GEN 31:26 Bade Labone Yakubore hodde, "Tui in ki goijjos? Tui ãre dúha diyos, ar ãr ziyaingunore larair bondir ḍoilla gori kiyolla loi aiššos?
GEN 31:27 Tui nizamot kiyolla dáiyos edde ãre dúha diyos? Tui ãre no hos kiyolla? Toi zene ãi tore kušir sãte gan, tobla edde bina bazaiyore bidai goritam.
GEN 31:28 Tui kene ãr nati edde ziyaindore suma dito foijjonto no dili? Tui endilla ham goriyore bekufai goijjos.
GEN 31:29 Tũwarar hoti goribar šokti ãr hatot ase, kintu gelde raitta tũwarar bafor Allaye ãre hodde, 'Hũšiyar, Yakubore bala horaf kissu no hois.'
GEN 31:30 Ar ehon tor bafor górot zaibolla oitofare tottu foran handedde hetolla tui ai giyosgoide, kintu ãr góror muttigun kiyolla sur goijjos?"
GEN 31:31 Yakube zuwabe hodde, "Ãi ḍorailam, kiyollahoile ãi baffilam, tũi zodi zurgori ãttu tũwar ziyaindore hari loi rakido.
GEN 31:32 Tũi zar hãse tũwar muttigun faiba, hitare marifela oibo. Ãr hár zinišfatir butore tũwar hono kissu takile tũwar egena okkolor sarme hin talaš gori loifelo." Asole Yakube no zanito ze, Rahelaye hin suri goijje.
GEN 31:33 Toi Labone Yakubor ṭambur butore edde Lear ṭambur butore ar dui bandir ṭambur butore góille, kintu kissu no fa. Bade hite Lear ṭambuttu niyoli aiyore Rahelar ṭambur butore góille.
GEN 31:34 Rahelaye kintu he muttigun loi zai ũṛor godir butore golai eriyore hibar uwore boi aššil. Labone hibar ṭambur hár zagat ataiye, kintu kissu no fa.
GEN 31:35 Rahelaye hibar bafore hodde, "Malik ãi tũwar sarme uṛi tiyai no farir boli tũi gušša no oiyo, kiyollahoile ãttu ehon mašik oiye." Hetolla Labone talaši gori bade o he muttigun tuwai no fa.
GEN 31:36 Iyanot Yakub naraz oiyore Labonore hosuri diyore hodde, "Ãr hosuri ki? Ar ãr oinnai o ba ki ze tũi ãre fise fise lorai aiššo?
GEN 31:37 Ar ãr hár zinišfati sai tũwar góror hono ziniš faiyo ne? Fai takile tũwar egena okkolor sarme rako, edde hitara ãra duni fokkor bisar gorok.
GEN 31:38 "Ei kuri bosor ãi tũwar hãse roiyi, eṛe butore bera sool ba soole hono so nošto no gore. Ar ãi tũwar soolor zakottu hono faṛa sool o no hái.
GEN 31:39 Enki fahari zanuware marifelaiyede hendilla hono zanuwarore o ãi tũwar hãse hono din no ani; edde he hoti ãi nize boššiyi. Ar hono zanuwar suri oigilegoi o hin din ok ba rait ok tũwara ãr hãsottu hotifuron loiyo.
GEN 31:40 Ãi dine fuijji ar raitta ṭanḍa faiyi, edde ãr sukottu gum zaitogoi.
GEN 31:41 Ei kuri bosor ãi tũwar górot roiyi, tũwar dui ziyolla soiddo bosor, ar so bosor tũwar zanuwarolla gulami goijji. Heṛe butore tũi doš bar foijjonto ãr beton bodolaiyo.
GEN 31:42 Ãr bafor Allah, ze Ibrahimor Allah edde Isakor Ḍor zodi ãr fokkiya no oito, toile tui ãre ehon hameka hali hate bidai goitta. Kintu Allaye ãr duk edde ãr hator mehennot deikke, ar hetolla hibaye gelde raitta tũware dõk diyede."
GEN 31:43 Toi Labone zuwabe Yakubore hodde, "Ei mayafuwain okkol ãr ziyain, ei fuwain okkol ãr fuwain, ei zanuwaror zãk oilde ãr zãk. Tui zin dehor in beggun ãr. Ehon ãr ei mayafuwain edde hitarattu oiyede fuwaindore ki goriyum?
GEN 31:44 Ai, tui loi ãi loi duni zone ekkan wadar sukti gori, ziyan tui edde ãr maze goba oi takibo."
GEN 31:45 Toi Yakube ugguwa fattor loiyore faiya ḍoilla gori tiya goraiye.
GEN 31:46 Toi Yakube egena okkolore hodde, "Tũwara o kissu fattor dola goro." Toi hitara fattor ani ugguwa ṭal banaiye, edde beggune hiyanor ḍake há fiya goijje.
GEN 31:47 Labone he fattoror ṭalguware nam diye Jegar-Šahaduta, ar Yakube hiyanor nam diye Gal-Ed.
GEN 31:48 Toi Labone hodde, "Ei ṭal oilde aijja tui edde ãr maze goba." Hetolla hiyanore Gal-Ed,
GEN 31:49 ar Mišfa nam raka oil, kiyollahoile hite hodde, "Ãra ekzon ar ekzonottu dure oiyumde hẽtte Mabude tor edde ãr uwore kiyal rake.
GEN 31:50 Zodi tui ãr ziyaindor loi horaf bebar goros otóba ãr ziyain takite oinno bou biya goros, zodi o hono manuš ãrar fũwati nai, kintu sais, ãi edde tui, ãrar maze Allah oilde goba."
GEN 31:51 Labone Yakubore aro hodde, "Ei ṭalguwa edde ei faiyawa, sa, ei tiya goraiya faiya, ziba ãi edde tor maze ãi buwailam.
GEN 31:52 Ei ṭal oilde ek goba edde faiya oilde ek goba, ze ãi ei ṭal farai tor hoti goitto no zaiyum, ar tui o ei ṭal edde faiya farai ãr hoti goitto no aibi.
GEN 31:53 Ibrahimor Allah edde Nahuror Allah edde hitarar bafor Allaye ãrar bisar gorok." Toi Yakube hibar baf Isakor Ḍor loi ek hosom háiye.
GEN 31:54 Bade Yakube he faharot ek kurbani diye edde hibar egena okkolore ek hánar dawat diye. Toi hitara hána háiye edde hitara heṛe rait haṛaiye.
GEN 31:55 Bade Labone binna sore uṛi nizor nati edde ziyaindore suma diye edde duwa goijje. Tarfore hite hentu giyegoi edde górot firi giyegoi.
GEN 32:1 Ar Yakube o nizor baisar uzu giye, edde Allar firista okkole hibar loi aiyore deha oiye.
GEN 32:2 Hitarare dekiyore Yakube hodde, "Itara Allar fouz okkol!" Hetolla he zagar nam diye Mahanaim.
GEN 32:3 Ar Yakube hibar ãgottu hóborguwa okkolore Seir elehat Edom maṛot Išor hãse defeṛaiye.
GEN 32:4 Yakube hitarare šikai diye, "Tũwara ãr malik Išore hoiye boli hoiba: 'Tũwar gulam Yakube hoiye: ãi Labonor hãse forbaš haiṭṭi edde etodin foijjonto heṛe aiššilam.
GEN 32:5 Ãttu goru gada sool berasool edde gulam edde bandi ase. Ar ãi ãr malike bala nozore saibo ei aša loi ãi ei hóborgan tũware hãse defeṛair.'"
GEN 32:6 Ar hóborguwa okkol Yakubor hãse firi aišše, hitara hodde, "Ãra tũwar bái Išor hãse gilam, ar hibaye o tũware fũwati sair šot manuš loi saito aiyer."
GEN 32:7 Toi Yakube beši ḍoraye edde dilot ouskus oiye, ar hibar fũwati aššilde hitarare edde hibar goru edde berasoolor zãk okkol, ũṭ okkolore dui grup goijje.
GEN 32:8 Toi hibaye hodde, "Iše zodi aiyore ek dolore hamela gore, ar ek dol ziba basi takibo hiba dái zaigoi faribo."
GEN 32:9 Toi Yakube hodde, "Oh Mabud, ãr fordada Ibrahimor Allah, ãr baf Isakor Allah, tũi zibaye ãre hoila, 'Tor dešot tor egena okkolor hãse tui firizagoi, ãi tor balai goijjium.'
GEN 32:10 Tũwar ei gulamor mikka ze hár rahamot edde imandari dehayo, hin hono kissur laikka ãi no, kiyollahoile uggwa hator laṛi loi ei Zordan farailam, kintu ehon ãttu dui dol oiye.
GEN 32:11 Aroz gori, ãr bái Išor hatottu ãre uddar goro, kiyollahoile ãi hitare ḍorai, ar zodi hite aiyore ãre edde ma-fuwaindore marifele.
GEN 32:12 Ar tũi to hoila, 'ãi tore balai goriyum edde tor bongšore doriyar balur renir ḍoilla beši goriyum, zin goni šeš gora no zaibo.'"
GEN 32:13 Toi Yakub he raitta heṛe rait haṛaiye, ar hibattu aššilde hinottu ek hadiya hisabe hibar bái Išolla loiye:
GEN 32:14 Dui šot sai sool edde kuriwa faṛa sool, dui šot miyala berasool edde kuriwa modda berasool,
GEN 32:15 so šoho dud dede hendilla tirišwa ũṭ, sališwa gai goru edde došwa bolod goru, ar kuriwa gadi edde došwa modda gada.
GEN 32:16 Bade hibaye hinore ek ekzon gulam okkolor hatot diye, toi hibar gulam okkolore hodde, "Tũwara ãr agottu farai zogoi, ar zãkor maze maze hoddur dur zaga farot raikko."
GEN 32:17 Bade hibaye foila zãkor hitare hokum diye: "Ãr bái Iš zodi tui loi deha o, edde fusar gore, 'Tui har gulam, hoṛe zodde, edde tor sarme asede in har?'
GEN 32:18 Toi tui hoibi, 'In tũwar gulam Yakubor, inore ek hadiya hisabe ãr malik Išor hãse faṭa oiye, so, hiba o ãrar fisottu ase.'"
GEN 32:19 Hibaye, dusora, tisera, edde aro oinno zara zãk loi zat aššil, hitara beggunore o hokum diye: "Iš loi deha oile tũwara o ekkui bafe ei hota hoiba.
GEN 32:20 Tũwara aro hoiba, 'So, tũwar gulam Yakub ãrar fisottu ase.'" Haron hibaye hodde, "Ãi ãr age ei hadiya okkol defeṛaiyore hibare šanto goijjium; toi bade ãi hibar siyara saiyum, oitofare hibaye ãre gosibo."
GEN 32:21 Toi hadiyagun hibar sarmottu fargora oil, kintu hiba nize he raitta dolor fũwati rait haṛaiye.
GEN 32:22 Bade hiba he raitta uiṭṭe edde hibar dui bou, dui bandi edde hibar egaro futore loiye edde Jabbok gáṭ bai faraiye.
GEN 32:23 Hibaye hitarare hal fargorabai bade hibaye hibattu aššilde hár kissure far gorabaiye.
GEN 32:24 Toi Yakub heṛe eka roiye, edde ek zone hiba loi binna dol fohor ofan foijjonto kutsi doijje.
GEN 32:25 Kintu Yakubore hõṛai no farede dekiyore hibaye Yakubor kiyailor sunuti sai hamela goijje, ar henot hibar loi kutsi dorat Yakubor kiyailor sunuti zurattu niyoli giyegoi.
GEN 32:26 Toi hibaye hodde, "Binna dol fohor oiye, ebar ãre eride." Kintu Yakube hodde, "Ãre rahamot no goro foijjonto ãi tũware zaito no diyum."
GEN 32:27 Toi hibaye hodde, "Tor nam ki?" Hibaye hodde "Yakub."
GEN 32:28 Toi hibaye hodde, "Tore ar Yakub ḍaka no oibo, Israil ḍaka oibo, kiyollahoile tui Allah edde manuš loi zuddo goijjos edde tui zittos."
GEN 32:29 Hetunot Yakube fusar goredde, "Meherbani gori, õnor namman ho." Kintu hibaye hodde, "Ãr nam kiyolla fusar goror?" Toi hibaye hibare rahamot goijje.
GEN 32:30 Toi Yakube he zagar nam raikke Peniel, edde hodde, "Kiyollahoile ãi Allare sarma sarmi oi dekilam, tarfore o ãr foran baisse."
GEN 32:31 Bade hiba Peniel farai giyegoide šomot beil uiṭṭe edde hibar kiyailor sunutilla buli lenga šuru goijje.
GEN 32:32 Etolla iyan ehono foijjonto endilla ze Israili okkole kiyailor sunutir uwore ze gusto ase hin no há, kiyollahoile Yakubor kiyailor sunutir gusto sai hamela gora oil.
GEN 33:1 Bade Yakube suk tuli saiye, ar so, Iš aiyer edde hibar fũwati sair šot manuš ase; hetunot hibaye fuwaingunore Leah, Rahela edde dui bandir hãse bag gori diye.
GEN 33:2 Ar hibaye age bandi edde hitarar fuwaindore agottu diye, tarfore fisottu Leah edde hibar fuwaindore, bade šešottu Rahela edde Yusufore diye.
GEN 33:3 Ar hiba nize hitarar agottu giye edde meṛit hãt bar mata niyuraiyore ijjot gori gori hibar báiyor hãse hazir oiye.
GEN 33:4 Toi Iše Yakubor loi dola oibolla dũri aišše edde Yakub loi ãzaãzi goijje, edde golat dori suma diye, ar hitara hainde.
GEN 33:5 Bade Iše suk tuli mayafuwain okkol edde fuwain okkolore deki fusar goredde, tor fũwati itara hontara? Yakube hodde, "Allar rahamote õnor gulamore ei futziyain okkol diye."
GEN 33:6 Toi bandi okkol edde hitarar fuwain okkole sarme zaiyore Išore mata niyuraiyore ijjot goijje.
GEN 33:7 Bade Leah edde hibar fuwain okkole sarme aišše edde mata niyuraiyore ijjot goijje. Ar šešottu Yusufe edde Rahela sarme giye, ar hitara o mata niyuraiyore ijjot goijje.
GEN 33:8 Toi Iše hodde, "Ãi ze dol okkol dekilam in kiyolla?" Hibaye hodde, "In ãr malikor nozorottu doya faibolla."
GEN 33:9 Kintu Iše hodde, "Ãttu beši ase, oh bái. Tottu zin ase hin tottu takok."
GEN 33:10 Yakube hodde, "No, ãi foriyad gori hoir, zodi ãi tũwar nozorottu doya faiyide o, toile tũi ãr ei hadiya goso, kiyollahoile ãi tũwar muk sa ãlla hiyan ãi Allar siyara saiyifan, ze tũi ãre kuši mone goisso.
GEN 33:11 Meherbani gori tũwar hãse ana oiyede ei hadiyagun goso, kiyollahoile Allaye ãre rahamot goijje, edde ãttu hár kissu ase." Ar Yakube beši foriyad goijje buli Iše hin goisse.
GEN 33:12 Toi Iše hodde, "Aio, ãra baisa di edde zai, ar ãi tor agottu zaiyum."
GEN 33:13 Yakube hodde, "Ãr malike to zano, ei fuwain okkol aizo gura, ar dudor sai sool edde faṛi berasool edde goru in okkololla o ãttu bafa foribo, ekdin o zodi itarare zoltigori loigile zanuwaror zãk okkol beggun morizaiboi.
GEN 33:14 Hetolla foriyad gorir, oh ãr malik, tũi tũwar gulam okkolore loi age zogoi, ar ãi ãr malikor hãse Seirot no fõsigoi foijjonto sarmor zanuwaror zãk edde fuwain okkolor ãṛar goti buzi aste aste aiššum."
GEN 33:15 Hetunot Iše hodde, "Toile ãr fũwati asede hentu manuš hodunore tor hãse raki zaito de." Yakube hodde, "Hin kiyolla? Ãr malikor hãsottu ãi doya faiyi iyan ãlla beši."
GEN 33:16 Toi Iše he din Seiror mikka hibar baisar uzu firi giyegoi.
GEN 33:17 Ar Yakube baisa di Sukkotot zai nizolla gór edde zanuwar okkololla ho ekkan ura bainde, hetolla he zagare Sukkot ḍaka oiye.
GEN 33:18 Ar Yakub Paddan Aramottu niyoli aiyore hiba aramor sãte Kenanor Šekim šohorot aišše edde šohoror barkule ṭambu maijje.
GEN 33:19 Bade hibaye ze zagat ṭambu gãijje hiyanore ekšot rufar foiša diyore Šekimor baf, Hamoror futaindottu kini loiye.
GEN 33:20 Heṛe hibaye ekkan kurbangah tuille edde hiyanore El-Elohe Israil nam diye.
GEN 34:1 Ar Lear zi Dina, zare hibaye Yakubolla biyail, hibaye dešor mayafuwain okkol loi dola oibolla baire gil.
GEN 34:2 Ar he elehar šašon goroya, Hibbi Hamoror fut Šekime hibare deikke, hite hibare loi zaiyore hiba loi neiṭṭe edde hibar ijjot hani goijje.
GEN 34:3 Ar hitar dil Yakubor zi Dinar uwore foijje; hite hibare ador goijje edde hibar loi ador muhabbotor hota okkol hoiye.
GEN 34:4 Toi Šekime hitar baf Hamorore hodde, "Ei mayafuware ãr bou hisabe ani do."
GEN 34:5 Yakube fuinne ze hite hibar zi Dinar ijjot hani goijje, ar hibar futain okkol zanuwaror zãk loi maṛot aššil; hetolla Yakube hitara górot firi no aiye foijjonto nizam mari taikke.
GEN 34:6 Bade Šekimor baf Hamor šohorottu niyoli zai Yakub loi hota hoito aišše.
GEN 34:7 Ar Yakubor futain okkole oi hóbor funi mottor hitara maṛottu firi aišše, ar hitarar dile beši duk faiye edde guššaye oin oiye, kiyollahoile Yakubor ziyor ijjot hani goriyore Šekime Israilor loi ekkan ofomanor ham goijje, ziyan hitattu muṭe o goron nuwaššil.
GEN 34:8 Kintu Hamore hitarare hodde, "Tũwar he ziyor uwore ãr fut Šekimor foran fori taikke. Meherbani gori hitalla hibare hitar bou hisabe do.
GEN 34:9 Ar ãrar loi biya dola goro, tũwarar ziyain okkolore ãrare do, ar ãrar ziyain okkolore tũwaralla lo.
GEN 34:10 Tũwara ãrar fũwati bošoti goro; deš tũwarar sarme fori roiye, tũwara eṛe šodori goro edde dón šombottir malik o."
GEN 34:11 Ar Šekime Dinar baf edde báiyaindore hodde, "Ãr mikka tũwara rahamotor nozore so, ar tũwara ãttu ziyan saiba ãi hiyan diyum.
GEN 34:12 Ei bouwor mohorana edde hadiya tũwara zedun dabi goitto so goro, tũwara hodde mozin ãi diyum, to ei zuwan mayafuwaware bou hisabe do."
GEN 34:13 Šekime hitarar boin Dinar ijjot hani goijjilde hetolla, Yakubor futainde hitare edde hitar baf Hamorore dúha loi zuwab diye.
GEN 34:14 Hitara hitarare hodde, "Ãra ei ham gori no faijjum, ekzon azomi agoraiya manušore ãrar boinore diya iyan ãralla ekkan beši šoromor ham oibo.
GEN 34:15 Bolke ei ekkan ham gorile ãra tũwarar loi razi oi fariyumde: tũwara o zodi ãrar ḍoilla, tũwarar furuš okkole azomi gorao,
GEN 34:16 toi ãra tũwarare ãrar ziyaindore diyum, ar tũwarar ziyaindore o ãralla loiyum, ãra tũwar fũwati bošoti goijjum edde ek zati oiyum.
GEN 34:17 Ar zodi ãrar hota no funo edde azomi goraiya no o, toile ãra ãrar ziyore loi zaiyumboi."
GEN 34:18 Hitarar hota Hamor edde hitar fut Šekimor nozorot bala laigge.
GEN 34:19 Toi ei zuwan ze hitar bafor góror beši ijjotwala, hite hitara hoiyede hiyan furon goitte deri no gore, kiyollahoile Yakubor ziyor uwore hitattu beši mon foijje.
GEN 34:20 Bade Hamor edde hitar fut Šekime hitarar šohor geiṛot aišše, ar hitara šohoror manuš okkol loi hota hoiye.
GEN 34:21 Hitara hodde, "Ei manušgun ãra loi šanti, itarare ei dešot bošoti goitto do edde šodori goitto do, dešot to hitaralla o bout zaga ase. Ãra hitarar ziyaindore ãralla bouwain hisabe loi, ar ãrar ziyain okkol hitarare di.
GEN 34:22 Kintu ei ekkan ham gorile manuššune ãrar fũwati bošoti goribo edde ek zati oibo. hiyan oilde zodi ãrar fotti furuše hitarar ḍoilla azomi goraiya oi.
GEN 34:23 Ar hitarar zanuwaror zãk edde hitarar dón šombotti edde hár kissu ki ãrar no oibo ne? Hetolla aiyo ãra hitarar hotat razi oi, toi hitara ãrar fũwati bošobaš goribo."
GEN 34:24 Ar he šohor geiṛot gilde hár manuš okkole Hamor edde hitar fut Šekimor hota fuinne, toi šohoror hár furuš okkolore azomi gora oiye.
GEN 34:25 Tin din bade zẽtte hitarattu biš oiye, Dinar báiyain Yakubor dui fute Simeon edde Leviye hitara zar zar toluwar loi zai baza sara šohorot hamela goijje, hár furuš okkolore marifelaiye.
GEN 34:26 Hitara Hamor edde hitar fut Šekimore toluwar loi haṛifelaiye bade hitara Dinare Šekimor górottu bair goijje edde niyoli giyegoi.
GEN 34:27 Yakubor futainde mora okkolor heṛe aišše edde šohor luṭfat goijje, kiyollahoile hitara itarar boinor ijjot hani goijjil.
GEN 34:28 Hitarar goru, sool edde gada, aro za kissu šohoror butore edde maṛot aššil hin beggun itara loiainne.
GEN 34:29 Ar hitarar hár gura fuwain edde hitarar hár bouwain okkolore bondi goriyore, hitarar hár šombotti edde góror hár kissu luṭ goijje.
GEN 34:30 Toi Yakube Simeon edde Levire hodde, "Tũwara ei dešor bašinda Kenaniyo edde Perišiyo okkolor hãse ãttu bašfuṛefan goijjo edde ãre bifodot felaiyo. Ãttu manuš hom, ar hitara zodi ãr berudde ekottro oiyore ãre hamela gore, ãi edde ãr góror gušṭi ṭiya dongšo oiyum."
GEN 34:31 Ar hitara hodde, "Ãrar boinore hite beiššar ḍoil bebar kiyolla goijje?"
GEN 35:1 Bade Allaye Yakubore hodde, "Uṭ, Betelot zaiyore heṛe bošoti gor, ar tui tor bái Išor sarmottu dáigiligoide ṭaimot ze tore deha dil, heṛe he Allalla ekkan kurbangah tiyar gor."
GEN 35:2 Toi Yakube hibar foribar okkol edde hibar fũwati zara aššil beggunore hodde, "Tũwarar hãse ze hár bezatir mutti okkol ase hinore dur goro, tũwara paksaf o edde hoor bodolo.
GEN 35:3 Ar ãra uṛi, Betelot zai, ar ze ãr mosibotor dinot ãre zuwab diye edde ze ãi zeṛe giyi ãr fũwati taikke ãi he Allalla heṛe ekkan kurbangah tiyar goriyum."
GEN 35:4 Toi hitarar hatot aššilde hár bezatir mutti okkol edde hanor guwana okkol beggun hitara Yakubore diye, edde Yakube hinore Šekimot elun gasor tolat gãraifelaiye.
GEN 35:5 Tarfore hitara hentu baisa diye, ar heṛiyar sairo mikkar šohoror okkolot Allar torfottu ḍor lami aišše, hetolla Yakubor futaindore honokiye fisottu lorai no za.
GEN 35:6 Yakub edde hibar fũwati aššilde beggune Kenan dešot Lušot (ziyan Betel) aišše.
GEN 35:7 Heṛe hibaye ekkan kurbangah tiyar goijje, edde he zagar nam diye El-Betel, kiyollahoile báiyor hãsottu dáizaibar šomot Allaye Yakubore he zagat deha dil.
GEN 35:8 Ar Rebekar daima, Deborah entehal oiye edde Betelor baire elun gasor tole dohon gora oiye, hetolla he zagar nam diya oiye Allon Bakuth (handibar-elun gas).
GEN 35:9 Yakube Paddan Aramottu aizaigoi bade Allaye hibare abar deha diye edde rahamot goijje.
GEN 35:10 Allaye hibare hodde, "Tor nam Yakub, kintu tore ar Yakub no ḍaka no oibo. Tor nam oibo Israil;" ar hibaye hibar nam raikke Israil.
GEN 35:11 Toi Allaye hibare hodde, "Ãi Allah, he Šorbo-Šoktiwala; fólwala o edde bari uṭ. Tor butottu ek zati, oi, bout zati okkol aibo, ar tor bongšottu badša okkol oibo.
GEN 35:12 Ze deš ãi Ibrahim edde Isakore dilam hiyan ãi tore o diyum, ar tui bade tor bongšore diyum."
GEN 35:13 Toi Allah hibar hentu uwor mikka uṛi giyegoi, zeṛe hibaye hiba loi hota hoil hentu.
GEN 35:14 Toi Yakube ze zagat hibaye hibar loi hota hoiye hiyanot ugguwa fattoror faiya buwaiye, toi hibar uwore šoraf edde tel ḍaille.
GEN 35:15 Allaye ze zagat hiba loi hota hoil Yakube he zagar nam raikke Betel.
GEN 35:16 Tarfore hitara Betelottu baisa diye edde Efratot gólite ehono hoddur dure ase, hen šomot Rahelaye ek fuwa biyaiye, ar hibattu fuwa halasi oite beši hošṭo oil.
GEN 35:17 Hibaye fuwa biyar biš zehon aro beši oiye, hibar daimaye hibare hodde, "No ḍorais, ebar o tottu ek fut oibo."
GEN 35:18 Kintu hiba šeš niyaš felai mori zargoide šomot, hibaye hibar futor nam raikke Ben-Oni, kintu hitar bafe nam raikke Benyamin.
GEN 35:19 Toi Rahela mori giyegoi, edde Efrator (ziyan Betlehemor) fõtor hãsat hibare dohon gora oiye.
GEN 35:20 Yakube hibar hoboror uwore ugguwa fattor faiya buwaiye, ar hiyan ehono foijjonto Rahelar hoboror faiyar sinno ase.
GEN 35:21 Tarfore Israile baisa diye edde Migdol Edaror oḍakottu ṭambu gãijje.
GEN 35:22 Israil he dešot bošobaš goredde ṭaimot, Rubene zai hitar bafor bandi bou Bilhah loi gum giye, ar Israile hiyan fuinne. Yakubottu baro fut aššil.
GEN 35:23 Lear futain okkol oilde: Yakubor foila zormo Ruben, Simeon, Levi, Ehudah, Issakar edde Sebulun.
GEN 35:24 Rahelar futain okkol oilde: Yusuf edde Benyamin.
GEN 35:25 Rahelar bandi Bilhar futain okkol oilde: Dan edde Naftali.
GEN 35:26 Lear bandi Zilpar futain okkol oilde: Gad edde Ašer.
GEN 35:27 Bade Yakube Mamre Kiryat-Arbat (hiyan oilde Hebronot) ze zagat Ibrahim edde Isak takito heṛe hibar baf Isakor hãse aišše.
GEN 35:28 Isak ekšo aši bosor basi aššil.
GEN 35:29 Tarfore hiba šeš niyaš felaiye edde morigiyegoi. Hiba furafuri zibon haṛaiyore edde bura boyošot entehal goriyore hibar fordada okkolor loi dola oiyegoi. Ar hibar futain Iš edde Yakube hibare dohon goraiye.
GEN 36:1 In oilde Išor (mani Edomor) bongšor kahani.
GEN 36:2 Iše Kenanor ziyain okkolore hibar bouwain hisabe loilde oilde: Hetittiyo Elunor zi, Adah, Hibbi Šibiyonor natini edde Anar zi, Oholibamah,
GEN 36:3 ar Ismailor zi edde Nebayotor boin Bašemat.
GEN 36:4 Ar Išolla Adaye Eliphazore, Bašmathe Reuelore,
GEN 36:5 Oholibamaye Jeušore, Jalamore edde Korare biyaiye. Itara aššilde Išor futain okkol, zarare hiballa Kenanot zormo dil.
GEN 36:6 Bade Iše hibar bouwain, futain edde hibar góror hár kiyore, ar hibar goru sool edde hibar hár zanuwar okkol edde Kenan dešot hamaiyede hár kissure loiyore hibar bái Yakubottu dure ar ekkan dešot hãr oigiyegoi.
GEN 36:7 Hitarar šo šombotti eto beši aššil, hitara ekku fũwati taki no fare; hitara bidešitta hisabe takitode he zaga hiyane hitaralla fodai gori no fare, kiyollahoile hitarattu beši zanuwar zãk okkol aššil.
GEN 36:8 Hetolla Iše (mani Edome) Seiror fahari elehat bošobaš goijje.
GEN 36:9 In oilde Seiror fahari elehat asede Edomiyo okkolor fordada Išor bongšo kahani.
GEN 36:10 In oilde Išor futaindor nam okkol: Eliphaz, Išor bou Adar fut, ar Ruyel, Išor bou Bašemator fut.
GEN 36:11 Eliphazor futain okkol: Teman, Omor, Zepho, Gatam edde Kenaz.
GEN 36:12 Ar Timnah ze Išor fut Eliphazor bandi bou, hibaye Eliphazolla Amalekore zormo dil. In okkol aššilde Išor bou Adar natiyain okkol.
GEN 36:13 In okkol oilde Reuelor futain okkol: Nahath, Serah, Šammah edde Mizzah. In okkol aššilde Išor bou Bašemator natiyain okkol.
GEN 36:14 Ar Šibiyonor natini edde Anar zi, Išor bou Oholibamar futain okkol oilde in okkol, zarare hibaye Išolla biyaiye: Zeuš, Zalam edde Korah.
GEN 36:15 In okkol aššilde Išor bongšor sordar okkol: Išor foila zormo Eliphazor futain okkol: Sordar Teman, Omor, Sefu, Kenaz,
GEN 36:16 Korah, Gatim edde Amalek. In okkol aššilde Edomor Eliphazor bongšottu; hitara oilde Aadar natiyain okkol.
GEN 36:17 Ar Išor fut Reuelor futain okkol: Sordar Nahath, Serah, Šammah edde Mizzah. In okkol aššilde Edomor Reuelor bongšottu; hitara aššilde Išor bou Bašemator natiyain okkol.
GEN 36:18 Ar itara oilde Išor bou Oholibamar futain okkol: Sordar Zeuš, Zalam edde Korah. In okkol aššilde Išor bou Anar zi Oholibamar bongšottu sordar okkol.
GEN 36:19 Itara aššilde Išor (ziba oilde Edom) futain okkol, ar Itara aššilde hitarar sordar okkol.
GEN 36:20 Itara aššilde Horittiyo Seiror futain okkol, zara he eleha okkolot aššil: Lotan, Šobal, Šibeon, Ana,
GEN 36:21 Dišon, Ezer edde Dišan. Edomot Seiror ei futain okkol oilde Horittiyo okkolor sordar okkol.
GEN 36:22 Lotanor futain okkol oilde: Hori edde Hemam, ar Lotanor ek boin oilde Timnah.
GEN 36:23 Šobalor futain okkol oilde: Alvan, Manahath, Ebal, Šefu edde Onam.
GEN 36:24 Ar Šibeonor futain okkol oilde: Aiya edde Ana. Ite oilde he Ana, ze bošoti sara elehat hitar bafor gada soradde šomot he gorom fanir nal fail.
GEN 36:25 Anar fuwain okkol oilde: Dišon edde zi Oholibamah.
GEN 36:26 Ar Dišonor futain okkol oilde: Hemdan, Ešban, Jitran edde Keran.
GEN 36:27 Ar Ezeror futain okkol oilde: Bilhan, Zavan edde Akan.
GEN 36:28 Ar Dišanor futain okkol oilde: Uz edde Aran.
GEN 36:29 In okkol oilde Horittiyo okkolor sordar okkol: Lotan, Šobal, Šibeon, Ana,
GEN 36:30 Dišon, Ezer edde Dišan.
GEN 36:31 Israili okkolore hono badšaye šašon goribar age itara oilde he badša okkol, zara Edomot šašon goijje:
GEN 36:32 Beuror fut Belaye Edomot šašon goitto, hitar šohoror nam oil Dinhabah.
GEN 36:33 Bela mori bade hitar zagat Bozrattu Serar fut Jobabe šašon goijje.
GEN 36:34 Jobab mori bade hitar zagat Temanottu Hušame šašon goijje.
GEN 36:35 Hušam mori bade hitar zagat Bedador fut Hadad, ze Muwabor maṛot Midiyaniyo okkolore hõṛaifelail, hite šašon goijje. Hitar šohoror nam oil Avith.
GEN 36:36 Hadad mori bade hitar zagat Masrekattu Samlaye šašon goijje.
GEN 36:37 Samlah mori bade hitar zagat hal hãsar Rehabotittu Šaule šašon goijje.
GEN 36:38 Šaul mori bade hitar zagat Akboror fut Baal-Hanane šašon goijje.
GEN 36:39 Ar Akboror fut Baal-Hanan mori bade hitar zagat Hadade šašon goijje. Hitar šohoror nam oil Pai, ar hitar bouwor nam aššil Matredor zi Mehetabel, ze Mesahabor natini.
GEN 36:40 In okkol aššilde Išor bongšottu sordar okkol, hitarar gušti mozin, hitara takitode zaga mozin, hitarar nam okkol oilde: Timna, Alvah, Jetheth,
GEN 36:41 Oholibamah, Elah, Pinon,
GEN 36:42 Kenaz, Teman, Mibsar,
GEN 36:43 Magdiel edde Iram.
GEN 37:1 Yakub Kenan dešot taka šuru goijje, ze dešot hibar baf bidešitta hisabe takkil.
GEN 37:2 In oilde Yakubor bongšor kahani. Yusuf, ek hõtoro bosojja zuwan, báiyaindor fũwati soolor zãk okkol soraito; hiba gura bafor bouwain Bilhah edde Zilpar futaindor fũwati takito, edde hitarar ku-asaror babute hóbor bafor hãse anito.
GEN 37:3 Israile hibar fuwain beggunottuwaro Yusufore beši ador gorito, kiyollahoile hite aššilde hibar bura halor fut; hitare ugguwa lamba kuruta banai dil.
GEN 37:4 Hitarar bafe Yusufore hitarattuwaro beši ador gorede dekiyore, hitare ingša gorito edde hitar loi hono hota šundor gori hoi no farito.
GEN 37:5 Bade Yusufe ek šoppon deikke, edde hin zehon hitar báiyaindore hoiye, hitara Yusufore aro beši ingša goijje.
GEN 37:6 Hibaye hitarare hodde, "Funo, ãi ekkan šoppon dekki:
GEN 37:7 So, ãra gĩyũ kũṛat tara bandir, ar so, ãr tarawa uṛi tiyaiye, ar tũwarar taragune ãr tarawar sairo ḍakottu tiyaiyore hibare soida goijje."
GEN 37:8 Toi hitar báiyainde hitare hodde, "Tui ki hãsa ãrar uwore razagiri goribi? Tui ki hãsa ãrar uwore šašon solaibi?" Hitar šoppon edde hotalla buli hitara hitare aro beši ingša goijje.
GEN 37:9 Bade Yusufe aro ekkan šoppon deikke, edde hiyanore hitar báiyaindore hoiye. Hite hodde, "So, ãi aro ekkan šoppon dekilam, ar so, beile, sande edde egarowa taraye ãre soida goredde dekilam."
GEN 37:10 Hite zehon hitar bafore edde báiyaindore hoiye, bafe hitare dõk diye edde hodde, "Tui in hondilla šoppon dekkili? Ãi, tor ma edde tor báiyain okkol, beggune aiyore ki hãsa tor sarme meṛit soida foijjum?"
GEN 37:11 Hitar báiyainde hitar loi riš gora šuru goijje, kintu hitar bafe he hota monot rakidiye.
GEN 37:12 Ek bar Yusufor báiyainde Šekimot hitarar bafor soolor zãk soraito giye,
GEN 37:13 toi Israile Yusufore hodde, "Tor báiyainde Šekimot soolor zãk soradde no ne? Ikka ai, ãi tore hitarar hãse defeṛai." Yusufe hodde, "Oto, ãi aišši."
GEN 37:14 Toi bafe hodde, "Tui zaiyore tor báiyain edde soolor zãkgun ken ase nai sagoi, edde aiyore ãr hãse zanais." Toi hibaye hitare Hebronor ḍeilottu defeṛaiye. Yusuf Šekimot fõsiyore,
GEN 37:15 ekzon manuše hitare lot faiye, ar so, maṛot gura fira goredde dekiyore he manušwaye fusar goredde: "Tui kiyor talaš gorodde?"
GEN 37:16 Yusufe hodde, "Ãi ãr báiyaindor talaš goridde, meherbani gori ãre ekka ho, hitara goru sool hoṛe sorar?"
GEN 37:17 Manušwaye hodde, "Hitara entu giyegoi. Ãi hitara 'Aio, ãra Dotanot zai' hen hodde funnilam." Toi Yusufe báiyaindor talašot Dotanot giye, heṛe hitarar lot faiye.
GEN 37:18 Hitara Yusuf aiyedde durottu loti deikke edde hitarar hãse no fõsibar agottu, hitara hitare marifelaibolla felain goijje.
GEN 37:19 Hitara ekzonore ekzone hodde, "Oi so, šoppon dekoya aiyer!
GEN 37:20 Aio, ãra hitare mari felai, bade hono ek faṭkuwat felai di, bade hoiyum, hitare hono fahari zanuware hái felaiye. Tarfore hitar šopponor doša ki o saiyum."
GEN 37:21 Kintu Rubene zehon ei hota funniye, hitarar hatottu Yusufore basaito saiye. Hite hodde: "No, ãra hitare zane mari no felai,
GEN 37:22 lou no bayo; hitare eṛe bošotisara elehar ei faṭkuwat maze felai do, kintu hitar uwore hat no tuillo." Rubene endilla hoiyede oilde Yusufore hitarar hatottu basaibolla edde hitare bafor hãse uwafes firai loizai faribolla.
GEN 37:23 Toi Yusuf zehon báiyaindor hãse fõisse, hitar gat finda aššilde he šundojja lamba kurutawa faṛi kuli loifelaye.
GEN 37:24 Toi hitara hibare dori faṭkuwawat felai diye. Faṭkuwawa hali aššil, ar heṛe hono fani no aššil.
GEN 37:25 Tarfore hitara hána haito boišše, hen šomot hitara suk tuli saiye, ar so, Giliyad name ek zagattu ek dol Ismaili šodori goroya aiyer. Hitara ũṛor fiṛot gori kušbo mosolla, rezom edde duf, hin okkol loi Mišor dešot zadde.
GEN 37:26 Toi Ehudaye hitar báiyaindore hodde, "Báiware marifelaiyore lukai erile ãrar ki lab oibo?
GEN 37:27 Aio, ãra hitare ei Ismaili okkolor hãse besifelai, hitar gat hat no di, kiyollahoile hite to ãrar nizor bái, ek lou-gustor." Ar hitar báiyainde he hota fuinne.
GEN 37:28 Toi Midiyaniyo šodori goroya okkol zehon hitarar ḍake aišše, hitara Yusufore faṭkuwattu tuille ṭani tuille edde kuriwa rufar ṭiyar bodole hitare he Ismaili okkolor hãse besifelaiye, ar hitara Yusufore Mišorot loiainne.
GEN 37:29 Bade Rubene faṭkuwar ḍake firi giye edde dekedde Yusuf heṛe nai, henot hite nizor hor faiṭṭe,
GEN 37:30 hitar báiyaindor hãse firi giye edde hodde: "Fuwawa to nai, ãi hoṛe zaiyum?"
GEN 37:31 Bade hitara Yusufor kurutawa loiye, ar uggwa soolor so zorgorai he kurutaware louwot buraiye.
GEN 37:32 Toi hitara he lamba kurutaware hitarar bafor hãse defeṛaiye edde hodde: "Ãra iba faiyi. Tũi bala gori so iba tũwar futor kuruta oi ne naki no?"
GEN 37:33 Hibaye kurutawa sini faijje edde hodde, "Iba to ãr futor kuruta, hitare hono fahari zanuware hái felaiye. Yusufore hameka hanhan gorifelaiye."
GEN 37:34 Toi Yakube hibar nizor hoor faiṭṭe, kĩyailot salar šoṭ berai bout din foijjonto fuwalla šuk goijje.
GEN 37:35 Hibar hár futain edde ziyainde hibare šantona dito saiye, kintu hiba hono bote šanti no o, aro hodde, "Ãi šuk goitte goitte ãr fuwar hãse fatalot zaiyumboi." Ar bafe futolla handat roiye.
GEN 37:36 Ar eṛe Midiyaniyo okkole Yusufore Mišor dešot Feruwanor ofisar okkolor butore Putifar name ekzon fahardar okkolor soddaror hãse besifelaiye.
GEN 38:1 He šomot Ehudah hitar báiyaindor hentu zaigoiyore Odullom farat Hira name ekzonor hãse taka šuru goijjil.
GEN 38:2 Heṛe Ehudaye ek Kenaniyor zi loi deha oiye, zar nam aššil Šuah. Hite hibare biya gori hibar loi milon oiye;
GEN 38:3 ar hiba hamil oiye edde ek futore zormo diye, zare nam diye Er.
GEN 38:4 Tarfore hiba abar hamil oiye edde ek futore zormo diye, hitar nam diye Onan.
GEN 38:5 Hibaye abar ek futore zormo diye edde hitar nam diye Šela. Hite zormo odde šomot Ehudah Kasibot takito.
GEN 38:6 Bade Ehudaye hitar foila fut Erolla bou ainne, ar hibar nam aššil Tamar.
GEN 38:7 Kintu Ehudar ei foila fut Mabudor nozorot en horaf aššil; Mabudehitare mari felaiye.
GEN 38:8 Toi Ehudaye Onanore hodde: "Tor bái-bou loi milon gor edde hibar loi diyoror zimma fura goriyore tor báiyolla bongšo barai tul."
GEN 38:9 Kintu Onane zainto ze, he bongšo hitar nizor no oibo; hetolla hite zetobar hitar bái-bou loi milon goijje, hetobar hite hitar birz baire felai diye.
GEN 38:10 hitar ze ham goijje hiyan Mabudor nozorot horaf, hetolla Mabude hitare o mari felaiye.
GEN 38:11 Toi Ehudaye hitar futor bou Tamarore hodde: "Ãr fut Šela zuwan no o foijjonto, tui tor bafor górot zai rari hisabe takgoi." Kiyollahoile hite baiffe, "hitar báiyaindor ḍoilla morizaiboi." Toi Tamar hibar bafor górot takibolla giyegoi goijje.
GEN 38:12 Iyar bout din bade Ehudar bou, Šuar zi, mori giyegoi. Ehudaye hiballa šuk gorattu aram oi bade, hitar Odullom farar bondu Hirar fũwati Timnah farat soolor kẽš ãsoya okkolor heṛe giye.
GEN 38:13 Hono ekzone Tamarore hoiye, "Sa, tor houre hitar soolore kẽš ãsaibolla Timnah fara zar."
GEN 38:14 Henot hibaye hibar rarir hoor kulifelaiyore mukot guwaṛa diye edde gat hoor beraiyore hiba Enaim golede rastar muk, ziyan Timnah fara za rastat, heṛe boi taikkegoi, kiyollahoile hibaye deikke ze, Šela zuwan oiye, tarfore o kintu hibare hitalla bou no bana.
GEN 38:15 Toi Ehudaye hibare deikke edde hite hiba ek beišša maya fuwa mone goijje, kiyollahoile hibar muk guijja aššil.
GEN 38:16 Toi hite rastar hãsat hibar ḍake giye edde hodde: "Ai, ãi tor hãse zai" kiyollahoile hite no zanito ze hiba hitar futor bou. Hibaye: "Ãr hãse zaito dile tũi ki diba?"
GEN 38:17 Toi hite hodde: "Ãi tolla zakottu uggwa soolor so defeṛaiyum." Hibaye, "Hiba no defeṛo foijjonto ki tũi ãr hãse hono kissu bondok hisabe diba ne?"
GEN 38:18 Hite hodde, "Ãi tor hãse bondok ki ditam?" Hibaye hodde: "Fũta šoho ei silmohor edde tũwar hator ašawa." Toi hite hin hibare diyore hibar hãse giye edde hiba hamil oiye.
GEN 38:19 Tarfore hiba uiṭṭe edde giyegoi, bade hibaye hibar gũwaṛa loifelaiye edde abar hibar rarir fušak finde.
GEN 38:20 Toi oi mayafuwar hatottu bondok surai anibolla Ehudaye hitar Odullom farar bondur di uggwa soolor so defeṛaiye, kintu hite hibare tuwai no fa.
GEN 38:21 Hite heṛiyar manuš okkolottu fusar goijje: "Enaimor fõtor hãsat ze mondir-beišša aššil, hiba hoṛe?" Hitara hodde, "Eṛe heṛiyar hono mondir-beišša nu aiye."
GEN 38:22 Toi hite Ehudar hãse uwafes firigiye edde hodde, "Ãi hibare tuwai no fai, ar heṛiyar mainše o hoiye, 'Eṛe heṛiyar hono beišša mayafuwa nu aššil.'"
GEN 38:23 Toi Ehudaye hodde: "Hibar hãse zin ase hin hibaye lok, ar no oilede ãra šormot foriyum, sa, ãi to hiballa ei soolor sowa defeṛailam, kintu tui hibare tuwai no faili."
GEN 38:24 Onumanik tin maš bade Ehudare howa oiye, "Tor futor bou Tamar beiššagiri gorer, ar so, hiyanor zoriya hiba ehon hamil" Ehudaye hodde, "Hibare baire ano edde hibare furaidifelo."
GEN 38:25 Hibare baire ana odde šomot, hibaye hibar houror hãse endilla hoi defeṛaiye, "Ei zinišgun zar, he manušwar duwara ãi hamil oiyi," hibaye aro hodde, "Fũta, silmohor edde laṛi in okkol har so."
GEN 38:26 Ehudaye hinore sini faijje edde hodde, "Hiba ãttuwaro beši forhesgar, kiyollahoile ãi hibare ãr fut Šelare no di." Ar Ehudah dusorabar honodin hibar hãse no.
GEN 38:27 Ar hibaye fuwa biyaibar šomoi zehon aišše, ar so, hibar feṛot zoikka fuwain.
GEN 38:28 Hibaye biyadde šomot hitarar butottu ekzone hitar niyolai diye; henot daimaye dori hitar hatot lal rongor fũta bandi di hodde, "Ite foila niyoli aišše."
GEN 38:29 Kintu hite hitar hat butore ṭani loifelaye, ar so, hitar bái niyoli aišše, toi hibaye hodde, "Tui kene band bangi niyoli aili!" Ar hitar nam raka oiye Perez.
GEN 38:30 Tarfore hitar bái, zar hatot lal rongor fũta banda aššil, hite zormo oiye, hitar nam raka oiye Zerah.
GEN 39:1 Ehon Yusufore Mišorot loiza oiye, ar Putifar, ekzon Mišoriyo ze aššil razar hormosarir okkolor butottu ek hormosari, faharadar okkolor boro, hite Ismaili okkol zara Yusufore heṛe ainnil, hitarattu kiniloiye.
GEN 39:2 Mabud Yusufor fũwati aššil, ar hibaye hibare kamiyaf goijje, edde hiba hibar Mišoriyo munifor górot roiye.
GEN 39:3 Ar hibar munife dekedde Mabud Yusufor fũwati ase, ar hár kissu zin gorer hinot Mabude kamiyafi der.
GEN 39:4 Yusufe hibar munifor bala nozorot foijje edde hitar hãsor šeba goroya oiye. Ar Putifare Yusufore hitar gór edde hitar hár kissur uwore dehašunar bar diye.
GEN 39:5 Ar endilla oile, zẽtte oite hite gór edde hitar hár kissur uwore dehašunar bar Yusufore diye, Yusufor zoriya he Mišoriyowar górore Mabude rahamot goijje. Ar Mabudor rahamot Putifaror górot edde ketot, hár kissur uwore oiye.
GEN 39:6 Hetolla Putifare hitar hár kissur bar Yusufor uwore diye, šude hite háitode hánagun bade ar hono kissur babute sinta no goitto. Yusuf aššilde sina ṭan edde siyara šundor zuwan,
GEN 39:7 Ar hoto din farai zai bade endilla oiye, hibar munifor bouwe Yusufor mikka kiya goijje edde hodde: "Ai, ãr bisanat ai."
GEN 39:8 Kintu hiba razi no o edde hibar munifor bouwore hodde: "So, ãr malikottu ei góror hono kissulla sinta gora no forer; hibar hár kissur bar ãr uwore saridiye.
GEN 39:9 Ei górot hiba udda ãttuwaro ḍõr no, hibaye šude tũi bade ar hono kissure mana no gore, kiyollahoile tũi hibar bou. Hen abostat maze ãi ken gori ettor ḍõr ekkan horaf ham goriyore Allar berudde guna gori faijjum?"
GEN 39:10 Hibaye Yusufore hendilla din bade din hendilla howat taikke, kintu Yusufe hibar hãse za otóba hibar fũwati owa hiyanot razi no o.
GEN 39:11 Ekdin endilla oiye, Yusuf hibar nizor hame góror butore giye, ar he šomot góror hono gulam goror butore nu aššil.
GEN 39:12 Toi hibaye Yusufor zubba sai doijje edde hodde: "Ai, ãr bisanat ai!" Kintu Yusufe hibar zubbawa hibar hatot raki dũri góror bair kule dáigiyegoi.
GEN 39:13 Ar hibaye zehon deikke ze Yusufe zubbawa hibar hatot raki dũri góror bair kule dáigiyegoi,
GEN 39:14 hibaye hibar góror gulam okkolore ḍaikke edde hodde: "So, hibaye ei Ibroni manušware ãrar loi tõša goribolla ainne! Ite ãr loi neṛibolla eṛe butore aišše, kintu ãi zure kiskisa maijji.
GEN 39:15 Ar hite ãr kiskisani funi hite hitar zubbawa ãr hãse raki dũri baire dáigiyegoi."
GEN 39:16 Toi hibaye Yusufor munif górot nu aiye foijjonto hibar zubbawa hibar hãse raki diye.
GEN 39:17 Bade hibaye hitare ei kahanigan buzaiye, hodde: "He Ibroni gulam zare tũi ãralla ainno, hite ãr hãse aišše ãr loi tõša goribolla.
GEN 39:18 Ar ãi zehon ãi zure kiskisa maijji hite hitar zubbawa ãr hãse raki dũri bair kule dáigiyegoi."
GEN 39:19 Yusufor munife hitar bouwor hota, zin hibaye hoiye, "Endilla ham tũwar gulame ãlloi goijje" funi guššaye oin oiye.
GEN 39:20 Toi Yusufor munife hibare loizaiyore ziyolot raikke, ze zagat raz bondi okkolore raka oito, heṛe, hiba he ziyolot bondi roiye. Ar Yusuf ziyolot roiyede šomot o,
GEN 39:21 Mabud hibar fũwati aššil; ar hibaye Yusufore doya dehaiye edde ziyolaror bala nozorot forefan goijje.
GEN 39:22 Toi ziyolare ziyolot asede hár hodi okkolor bar Yusufor hatot gosaidiye, edde heṛe hitara hár has harbar zin gora oito, hin goroya aššilde hiba.
GEN 39:23 ar hibar hatot zimma aššilde hinor hono kissur mikka ziyolare no saito, kiyollahoile Mabud hibar fũwati aššil, ar hibaye zin gorat aššil, hinore Mabude kamiyaf ofan goitto.
GEN 40:1 Iyar bade zai, Mišoror razar šoraf baṛidoya okkolor maziye edde ruṭibanoya okkolor maziye hitarar malik, Mišoror razar berudde hosuri goijje.
GEN 40:2 Feruwan šoraf baṛidoya okkolor mazi edde ruṭibanoya okkolor mazi, ei dui hormosarir uwore gušša oiye,
GEN 40:3 edde hitarare faharadar okkolor boror górot, zeṛe Yusufore bondi gori raka oiye, heṛe bondi gori rakkiye.
GEN 40:4 Faharadar okkolor boroye hitarare Yusufor hatot diye, ar Yusufe hitarar kermos goijje. Hitara bout din heṛe bondi taki bade,
GEN 40:5 Razar šoraf baṛidoya edde ruṭibanoya ze duizonore ziyolot raikke, hitara dunizone ekkui raitta ekzone ekkan ekkan šoppon deikke, ar hitarar ek ekkan šopponor ek ekkan mani aššil.
GEN 40:6 Tarfordin binna Yusuf hitarar hãse aiyore dekedde, ar so, hitarar nak muk beši andar.
GEN 40:7 Toi Yusufor fũwati Feruwanor ze dui hormosari hibar fũwati hibar munifor górot ziyolot bondi aššil, hitarare hibaye fusar goredde, "Õnorare saite aijja nak muk eto andar kiyolla lager?"
GEN 40:8 Hitara zuwab diye, "Ãra dunizone šoppon dekki, kintu hinor mani buzai dibolla hono kiye nai" Yusufe hitara dunizonore hodde, "Mani buzai dibar šokti Allattu no o ne? meherbani gori šoppongun ãre ho."
GEN 40:9 Toi oi mazi šoraf baṛidoyaye Yusufore hitar soppongan funaiye, hite hibare hodde, "Ãr šopponot dekidde, so, ãr muntu ekkan ãngur lota,
GEN 40:10 ar hiyanot tinnwa ḍeila aššil. Ar hinot holi ai mottor ful fuiṭṭe edde hinot tũka tũka oiyore fona ãngur oiye.
GEN 40:11 Ar Feruwanor fiyalawa ãr hatot aššil edde ãi he ãngurgun loiyi, hinore Feruwanor fiyalat roš sibi loi fiyalawa Feruwanor hatot dilam."
GEN 40:12 Yusufe hitare hodde: "Iyanor mani oilde endilla, tinnuwa ḍeila oilde tin din.
GEN 40:13 Tin dinor butore Feruwane õnore šormane entu eri dibo edde õnor agor hamot õnore uwafes dibo, ar õne age zendilla hibar šoraf baṛidoya aššila, hendilla tũi Feruwanor hatot fiyala tuli diba.
GEN 40:14 Kintu zẽtte õnor balai oibo, foriyad gorir õne ãre monot raikko edde ãr uwore doya dehaiyo; ãr babute Feruwanore hoiba edde õne ãre ei górottu niyolaiba.
GEN 40:15 Kiyollahoile ãre Ibroni okkolor dešottu sur gori ana oiye, ar eṛe o ãi en hono kissu no gori ze hitarattu ãre gãtot raka fore."
GEN 40:16 Ruṭibanoya okkolor maziye zehon dekilo ze Yusufe šopponor bala mani hoiye, toi hite Yusufore hodde, "Ãi o ekkan šoppon dekkilam: So, ãr matar uwore tin ṭuri fiṛa ase.
GEN 40:17 Uoror ṭurit Feruwanolla banaiya hãr ḍoilla hana, ar faik okkole ãr matar uwore ṭurittu hinore hát roiye."
GEN 40:18 Yusufe hodde, "Iyanor mani oilde endilla, tinnuwa ṭuri oilde tinnwa din.
GEN 40:19 Tin dinor butore Feruwane õnor holla loibo edde gagan gasot zulai rakibo, ar faik okkole gusto háibo."
GEN 40:20 Bade tin dinor din Feruwan zormo dinot, hite hitar hormosari okkololla ek mela goijje. Hite he mazi šoraf baṛidoya edde mazi ruṭibanoyare hormosari okkolor sarme hazir goijje:
GEN 40:21 Hite mazi šoraf baṛidoyaware hitar agor hamot uwafes diye, toi hite abar Feruwanor hatot fiyala tulidiya šuru goijje.
GEN 40:22 Kintu he mazi ruṭibanoyare faši diye, zendilla Yusufe hitarare mani bangidil.
GEN 40:23 He mazi šoraf baṛidoyawaye tarfore o Yusufore monot no rake, hibare foraifelail.
GEN 41:1 Dui bosor farai zai bade Feruwane ek šoppon deikke: So, hite Nil doriyar farot tiyaiye,
GEN 41:2 ar so, doriyattu hãttuwa šundor edde boli goru uṛi aišše edde hóir bonot sora šuru goijje.
GEN 41:3 Hin bade aro hãttuwa bissiri edde leṛa goru doriyattu uṛi aišše, edde hine farot oinno goru okkolor ḍake tiyaiye.
GEN 41:4 Ar bissiri edde leṛa gorugune he šundor edde boli gorugunore háifelaiye. Toi Feruwan gumottu seton oiye.
GEN 41:5 Bade hite abar gumot foijje edde dusora bar šoppon deikke: Ar so, hãttuwa fuiṭṭa edde taza gĩyur sóra ekkan narat gozaiye.
GEN 41:6 Hin bade aro hãttuwa gĩyur sóra gozaiye, hin hĩṛa edde fukali bataše fúwaigilgoi.
GEN 41:7 Ar he hiṛa gĩyur sóra okkole oi hãttuwa fuiṭṭa edde taza sóragunore gilifelaiye. Toi Feruwan gumottu seton oiye. Hite buijjede hin šude šoppon.
GEN 41:8 Kintu binna razar monot ouskus oiye. Hite manuš defeṛaiyore Mišoror hár zadugor edde giyani okkolore ḍaki ainne. Feruwane hitar šoppon okkolore hitarare buzaiye, kintu honokiye hinor mani bangidi no fare.
GEN 41:9 Hetunot mazi šoraf baṛidoyaye Feruwanore hodde: "Aijja, ãr ekkan hosurir hota ãttu monot foijje.
GEN 41:10 Feruwan ekbar hibar gulam okkolor uwore ragigilgoi, edde hibaye ãre edde mazi ruṭibanoyare faharadar okkolor boror górot bondi gori rakkil.
GEN 41:11 Ek raitta ãra ekzone ekkan ekkan šoppon dekkilam, ek ekkan šopponor ek ekkan mani aššil.
GEN 41:12 Ehon heṛe ek Ibroni zuwan, faharadar okkolor boror gulam ãrar fũwati aššil. Ãra hitare ãrar šoppongun buzailam, ar hite ãrar šoppongun ãrare bangidil, ar zar zar šoppon hitare bangi dil.
GEN 41:13 Hite ãrare zendilla mani bangi dil ṭik hendilla goṭṭil: Ãre ãr hamot uwafes diya oil, ar utare faši diya oil."
