GEN 41:14 Henot Feruwane Yusufore ḍaki anibolla defeṛaiye, ar hitara Yusufore toratori ziyolor gãtottu niyolai ainne. Hibaye sul dari hamaiye edde hoor bodoille, bade hiba Feruwanor sarme hazir oiye.
GEN 41:15 Feruwane Yusufore hodde, "Ai ekkan šoppon dekilam, honokiye hiyanor mani bangidi no farer. Kintu ãi funni, tore šoppon funaile tui hiyanor mani bangi di faros."
GEN 41:16 Toi Yusufe zuwabe hodde, "Ãi no, Allaye Feruwanore hiba šanti ode zuwab dibo."
GEN 41:17 Toi Feruwane Yusufore hodde, "Ãr šopponot maze, ãi Nil doriyar farot tiyai roiyi,
GEN 41:18 ar so, doriyattu hãttuwa šundor edde boli goru uṛi aišše edde hóir bonot sora šuru goijje.
GEN 41:19 Hin bade aro hãttuwa bissiri edde leṛa goru doriyattu uṛi aišše, ãi endilla bissiri goru okkol Mišorot ãi ar hono din no deki.
GEN 41:20 Tarfore he bissiri edde leṛa gorugune foilar boli gorur hãtoware háifelaiye.
GEN 41:21 Tarfore o hinore saite he boli gorugunore háiyefan no lage, hin agor ḍoilla bissiri taigiyegoi. Hetunot ãi gumottu seton oiyi.
GEN 41:22 "Šopponot ãi aro dekilam, hãttuwa fuiṭṭa edde taza gĩyur sóra ekkan narat gozaiye.
GEN 41:23 Hin bade aro hãttuwa gĩyur sóra gozaiye, hin hĩṛa edde fukali bataše fúwaigilgoi.
GEN 41:24 Ar he hiṛa gĩyur sóra okkole oi hãttuwa fuiṭṭa edde taza sóragunore gilifelaiye. Ãi in zadugor okkolore hoilam, kintu hitara honokiye inor mani ãre hoi no fare."
GEN 41:25 Toi Yusufe Feruwanore hodde, "Feruwanor šoppon duniyan asole ekkan, Allaye ziyan goribo hiyan Feruwanor hãse batelai diyede.
GEN 41:26 He hãttuwa šundor boli goru mani hãt bosor, ar hãttuwa fuiṭṭa edde taza gĩyur sóra mani o hãttuwa bosor; šoppon oilde ekkan.
GEN 41:27 Hin bade ze hãttuwa bissiri edde leṛa goru doriyattu uṛi aišše oilde hãttuwa bosor, ar fukali bataše fuwai gilgoide he hiṛa gĩyur sóra oilde o hãttuwa raṭor bosor.
GEN 41:28 "Ai Feruwanore iyan endilla hoilam: Allaye ziyan goribo hiyan Feruwanor hãse dehaiye.
GEN 41:29 So, Mišor agagura hãttuwa beša beši fošol oibode bosor aibo.
GEN 41:30 Ar tarbade aibo hãttuwa raṭor bosor. Toi Mišorot beša beši oilde hin forai zaiboi, edde ei raṭe dešore šeš gorifelaibo.
GEN 41:31 Ar beša beši oilde hin ar monot no takibo, kiyollahoile hiyar bade ze raṭ oibo, hiba beši boiyanok oibo.
GEN 41:32 Feruwanore dui ḍoilla gori šoppon deha oiyede haron oilde, iyan Allaye faisala gori felaiye, ar Allaye iyan hára goribo.
GEN 41:33 "Ar ehon, Feruwane ekzon manuš zuhar goro, ze buddiwala edde giyani, ar hitar uwore Mišorot bar do.
GEN 41:34 Feruwanottu dešolla aro hormosari okkol tula foribo, oi hãt bosorot beša beši oibode hẽtte hitara hinor fãs bagor ek bag tulibolla.
GEN 41:35 Hitarattu ei bala bosor okkolor aiyedde hinor hár haiddo okkole dola gora foribo, ar gĩyu okkol Feruwanor anḍare šohor okkolor haiddo hisabe dola gora foribo edde sõli raka foribo.
GEN 41:36 Ei haiddo dešolla zoma raka foribo, toi zẽtte raṛor hãt bosor Mišorot oibo, hẽtte zene raṭe dešore dongšo gori felai no fare."
GEN 41:37 Ei mošora Feruwanor edde hitar hormosari okkol nozorot beggunottu bala laigge.
GEN 41:38 Feruwane hitar hormosari okkolore hodde, "Endilla ekzon manuš ãra ar hare faiyum, zar butore ase Allar Ruh?"
GEN 41:39 Toi Feruwane Yusufore hodde, "In okkol zehon Allaye tore dehaiye, tor ḍoilla buddiwala edde giyani ar honokiye nai.
GEN 41:40 Tui ãr razbarir hár kissure solaibi, ar tor mukor hokum ãr hár manuš okkole mani solibo, šude šingašonot ãi tottuwaro ḍõr takiyum."
GEN 41:41 Toi Feruwane Yusufore hodde, "Sa, ãi šara Mišoror hár zagar uwore tore buwailam."
GEN 41:42 Bade Feruwane hitar silmohor-õṛiwa hitar hatottu kuli loi Yusufor hatot findai diye. Hite Yusufore šundor hoor findai diye edde golat ekkan šunar hãr diyai diye.
GEN 41:43 Ar hite Yusufore hitar dui lombor gũra garit buwagaraiye. Ar hitara hibar age elan goijje, "Ãṛu nise goro!" Endilla gori hite Yusufore Mišoror hár zagar uwore buwaiye.
GEN 41:44 Bade Feruwane Yusufore hodde, "Ãi Feruwan, kintu tor hokum sara fura Mišorot honokiye, no hat tulibo, otóba hãi maribo."
GEN 41:45 Feruwane Yusufore nam diye Safenat-Paneh, ar On šohoror imam, Putiferar zi Asenatore Yusufore hibar bou oibolla diye. Bade Yusuf Mišor deš guri aibolla niyoli giye.
GEN 41:46 Yusufe Mišoror Feruwanor anḍare hamot góillede he šomot hibar boyoš oilde triš bosor. Toi Yusuf Feruwanor sarmottu niyoli giyegoi edde Mišor zaga beggulla sofor goijje.
GEN 41:47 Toi foilar he hãt bosorot dešot beša beši haiddo oiye.
GEN 41:48 Mišorot ei hãt bosorot hár haiddo okkolore Yusufe dola goijje edde šohor okkolot mojud gori rakkiye. Ek ekkan šohorot hiyanor sairo ḍakor maṭ okkolor haiddore rakkiye.
GEN 41:49 Yusufe doriyar balu zedun hedun haiddo dola goijje; ar eto beši haiddo oiye hinore ar mafiyore lowa šombob no o, hetolla hibaye mafi lowa bondo gori diye.
GEN 41:50 Raṭor bosor aibar age, On šohoror imam Putiferar zi Asenator feṛottu Yusufor dui fut zormo oil.
GEN 41:51 Yusufe foila futor nam raikke Manessa, ar hodde, "Kiyollahoile Allaye ãr hár duk hošto edde ãr bafor góror hár kissure foraifelabaye."
GEN 41:52 Bade dusora futor nam raikke Efraim, ar hodde, "Allaye ãre hošṭo bugor dešot fólwala goijje."
GEN 41:53 Tarfore Mišorot beša beši haiddo oiyede he hãt bosor šeš oiye,
GEN 41:54 raṭor hãt bosor šuru oiye, ode ode Yusufe hoilde mozin. Raṭ oinno hár deš okkolot šuru oiye, kintu Mišoror hár zagat haiddo ase.
GEN 41:55 Mišorot beggulla bukkor zala šuru oiye, manuš okkole Feruwanor hãse zai haiddolla handahaṛi goijje. Feruwane hár Mišoriyo okkolore hoiye, "Yusufor hãse zo, ar hibaye tũwarare zen goitto ho hen goro."
GEN 41:56 Dešor beggulla ei raṭ sorai foijjil, toi Yusufe gudam gór okkol beggun kulidiye edde Mišoriyo okkolore gĩyu beisse; kiyollahoile Mišorot raṭ beši hora oi uṭṭil.
GEN 41:57 Ar hár dešottu Mišorot, Yusufottu gĩyu kinito aišše, kiyollahoile hár zagat raṭ beši hora oil.
GEN 42:1 Yakube Mišorot gĩyu asede zani fariyore hibaye nizor futaindore hodde, "Tũwara ekzone ar ekzonor mukor uzu kiya sai taikko?"
GEN 42:2 Hibaye aro hodde, "So, ãi Mišorot gĩyu asede fuinni, tũwara heṛe lamat zo edde henttu ãralla gĩyu kini anogoi, zene ãrar basai fari edde no mori."
GEN 42:3 Toi Yusufor doš báiye Mišorottu gĩyu kinibolla lamat giye.
GEN 42:4 Kintu Yakube Yusufor bái Benyaminore hitar báiyaindor fũwati no defeṛa, kiyollahoile hibaye hodde, "Oitfare hitar uwore hono bifod goṭibo."
GEN 42:5 Toi zara gĩyu kinito aišše hitarar fũwati Israilor futain okkol o heṛe aišše, kiyollahoile Kenanot o raṭ oil.
GEN 42:6 Ehon Yusuf oiyede dešor šašongoroya, ar iba oilde hiba ze he dešitta okkol beggunore gĩyu bessil. Toi Yusufor báiyain okkol aišše edde hitara hibar sarme meṛir uzu uite foijje.
GEN 42:7 Yusufe báiyaindore deikke edde hibaye hitarare sini faijje, kintu hibaye hitara loi osinor ḍoil goijje edde hora gori hota hoiye, hodde, "Tũwara hontu aiššode?" Hitara hodde, "Kenan dešottu, haiddo kinibolla aššide."
GEN 42:8 Yusufe báiyaindore sini faijje, kintu hitara Yusufore sini no fare.
GEN 42:9 Ar Yusufe hitarar babute ze ze šoppon okkol dekkil, hin okkol hibattu monot foijje; toi hitarare hodde, "Tũwara spai, dešot uidda zaga hoṛe ase saito aiššode."
GEN 42:10 Hitara zuwabe hodde, "No, malik, õnor gulam okkole haiddo kinto aiššede.
GEN 42:11 Ãra beggun ekzonor futain ãra šada dilla manuš, spai no."
GEN 42:12 Yusufe hitarare hodde, "No, tũwara dešot uidda zaga hoṛe ase saito aiššode."
GEN 42:13 Kintu hitara hodde, "Õnor gulam okkol baro bái aššilam, ãra oilamde Kenanor ekzonor futain okkol. Ar šoṛo bái ehon ãrar bafor fũwati ase, ar ekzon nai."
GEN 42:14 Yusufe hitarare hodde, "Iyan ãi tũwarare hoiyide hendilla, tũwara spai.
GEN 42:15 Ar tũwarare iyan loi forikka gora oibo: Ãi Feruwanor zanor hosom gori hoir, tũwarar šoṛo bái eṛe no aile, tũwara ei zagattu bair oi no fariba.
GEN 42:16 Tũwarar ekzonore defeṛao, edde tũwarar he báiyore anao, ar tũwara eṛe bondi tako, ar ei bafe tũwarar hota forikka gora oibo, tũwara hãsa hota hor ne. Zodi no oile, ãi Feruwanor zanor hosom gori hoir, tũwara spai okkol."
GEN 42:17 Toi hibaye hitarare tin din hazotot rakkiye.
GEN 42:18 Tin dinor din Yusufe hitarare hodde, "Ek ham goro, toi tũwara basi fariba, kiyollahoile ãi Allare ḍorai:
GEN 42:19 Tũwara zodi šada dilla manuš o toile tũwarar báiyaindor butottu ekzon hazotot bondi tako, ar baki beggune tũwarar bukalo góror manuš okkololla gĩyu loi zogoi.
GEN 42:20 Tarfore tũwara tũwarar šoṛo báiyore ãr hãse ano, toi tũwarar hota formanito oibo, edde tũwara no moriba." Toi hitara hendilla goijje.
GEN 42:21 Ar hitara ekzonore ekzone hodde, "Soiyi ãra ãrar báiyor babute hosurbon, kiyollahoile hite ãrar hãse minnoti goijje, edde ãra hitar foranor hošto dekiyore hin no funi; etolla ãrar uwore ei mosibot hazir oiye."
GEN 42:22 Hetunot Rubene hodde, "Ãi no ne tũwarare hoilamde, fuwawar berudde guna no goijjo? Kintu tũwara no funo, ar ehon hitar louwor hisab diya forer."
GEN 42:23 Hitara ṭer no ze Yusufe hitarar hota buzi farer, kiyollahoile hibaye hota buzaidoya bebar goijje.
GEN 42:24 Toi hiba hitarar hãsottu dure ator oi zaiyore hainde edde uwafes firi aišše. Toi hiba abar firi aišše edde hitara loi hota hoiye, Ar hitarar butottu Simeonore dori hitarar šaikkat bainde.
GEN 42:25 Bade Yusufe hitarar bosta okkolot gĩyu bori dibolla, ar hitara fotti ek ekzonor ṭiya zar zar bostat ferot dibolla, edde baisalla hána dibolla hokum diye. Toi hitaralla hendilla gora oiye.
GEN 42:26 Tarfore hitara hitarar gĩyur bosta okkol hitarar gada okkolor fiṛot loiye edde henttu giyegoi.
GEN 42:27 Ar fõtot rait haṛaibolla taimmede heṛe hitarar butottu ekzone hitar gadare adar dibolla hitar gĩyur bosta kuille. Toi hite bostar mukot hitar ṭiyagun deikke.
GEN 42:28 Henot hite báiyain okkolore hodde, "So, ãr ṭĩya firaidiye, hin ãr bostar butore." Henot ḍore hitarar foran uri giyegoi edde hafi hafi ekzonore ekzone hodde, "Allaye ãrare in ki goijje?"
GEN 42:29 Bade hitara Kenan dešot hitarar baf Yakubor hãse aišše, edde hitarar uwore zen zen goiṭṭe hin okkol beggun hibar hãse hoi funaiye. Hitara hodde,
GEN 42:30 "Ze manušwa he dešor uwore malik, hibaye ãra loi hora bafe hota hoiye, ar ãrare dešor uidda zaga tuwoya spai mone goijje.
GEN 42:31 Kintu ãra hibare hoiyi, 'Ãra šada dilla manuš, spai no.
GEN 42:32 Ãra baro bái, ek bafor futain, kintu ekzon nai, edde šoṛo bái Kenanot ehon ãrar bafor fũwati ase.'
GEN 42:33 "Henot he deš šašongoroya manušwaye ãrare hodde, 'Iyan loi ãi tũwara šada dilla manuš oi ne zani fariyum: Tũwarar ek báiyore ãr hãse raki zo, edde tũwarar bukalo góror manuš okkololla haiddo loizo.
GEN 42:34 Ar tũwarar šoṛo báiyore ãr hãse ainno, henot ãi buzifariyum ze tũwara spai no, kintu šada dilla manuš. Toi ãi tũwarar bái tũwarar hãse firai diyum, edde tũwara ei dešot besa kina gori fariba.'"
GEN 42:35 Toi hitara zẽtte bostattu haiddo ḍaille, ar so, hitara fottizonor bostar butore hitarar fottizonor ṭiyar bunda! Ei ṭiyar bunda okkol hitara edde hitarar bafe deki, beggune ḍoraiye.
GEN 42:36 Ar hitarar baf Yakube hodde, "Tũwara ãre fuwain hara goijjo. Yusuf nai, Simeon o nai, abar Benyaminore loizaito sor. In beggun ãr uwottu guzori zar!"
GEN 42:37 Hetunot Rubene hitar bafore hodde, "Ãi zodi tũwar hãse itare firai no ani, toile tũi ãr dui futore kun goijjo. Hitare ãr hatot do, ãi hitare tũwar hãse uwafes firai aniyum."
GEN 42:38 Kintu Yakube hodde, "Na, ãr fut tũwarar fũwati no zaibo; hitar bái mori giyegoi edde šude hite basi ase. Tũwara ze fõt bai zaiba, heṛe zodi hitar hono bifod o, toile hitar šukke ei fona sule ãre fatalot lamai diba."
GEN 43:1 Ehon o dešot raṭ beši hora.
GEN 43:2 Toi hitara Mišorottu ze gĩyu annil, hin beggun zehon haiya šeš oiye, hitarar bafe hitarare hodde, "Tũwara abar zo, edde ãralla aro olfo haiddo kini ano."
GEN 43:3 Toi Ehudaye hibare hodde, "Kintu he manušwaye ãrare hũšiyari diye edde hoiye, 'Tũwarar bái fũwati no takile tũwara ãr sarme no aiššo.'
GEN 43:4 Tũi zodi ãrar fũwati ãrar báiyore zaito do, ãra lamat zaiyum edde tũwalla haiddo kini aniyum.
GEN 43:5 Ar zodi no defeṛo, ãra no zaiyum, kiyollahoile he manušwaye ãrare hoiye, 'Tũwarar bái fũwati no takile tũwara ãr sarme no aiššo.'"
GEN 43:6 Toi Israile hodde, "Tũwara he manušware tũwarattu ar ek bãi ase hoiyore kiyolla tũwara ãr loi endilla bura ham gorila?"
GEN 43:7 Hitara hodde, "Manušwaye ãrar babute edde ãrar foribaror babute zora zori gori endilla hoi fusar goijje. 'Tũwarar baf ki ehono zinda ne? Tũwarattu ki aro ek bái ase?' Ar ãra hibare ei suwal okkol mozin zuwab diyi. Henot ãra ken gori zaniyum ze hite hoibo, 'Tũwarar báiyore eṛe ano?'"
GEN 43:8 Toi Ehudaye hibar baf Israilore hodde, "Fuwaware ãr fũwati defeṛo, ãra uṛi edde baisa di, toi zene ãra, tũi edde ãrar fuwain šoho, ãra forane basi edde no mori.
GEN 43:9 Ãi nize hitar zabin roilam; hitare tũi ãr hatottu gosi loiyo. Ãi zodi hitare tũwarar hãse uwafes firai no ani toile ãi hara zibon tũwar hãse hosurbon oi takiyum.
GEN 43:10 Ãra eto deri no goritam boli etone hameka ãra dui bar zaiyore uwafes ai faittam."
GEN 43:11 Toi hitarar baf Israile hodde, "Zodi hen gora fore, toile endilla goro: Manušwalla ek hadiya hisabe tũwarar bosta okkolot dešor nam gora ziniš okkolottu kissu lo, olfo duf, olfo rezom, olfo modu, kušbo mosolla, pistašo dana edde badam.
GEN 43:12 Ar tũwara fũwati ḍabol ṭĩya lo, kiyollahoile bostar mukot ze ṭĩya firi aišše, hin firai diya foribo. Oitfare hiyan ekkan hono bul oiye.
GEN 43:13 Tũwarar báiyore lo edde zolti he manušwar hãse uwafes zo.
GEN 43:14 Šorbo Šoktiwala Allaye gorok zene he manušwaye tũwarare doya gore, toi hite tũwarar dusora bái edde Benyaminore tũwarar fũwati defeṛa. Ar ãttu zodi fuwain hara owa forile o, fuwain hara oilam."
GEN 43:15 Toi manušgunore he hadiya, hatot ḍabol ṭĩya edde Benyaminore loiyore hitara uiṭṭe edde Mišorot lami giye edde Yusufor sarme hazir oiyegoi.
GEN 43:16 Yusufe hitarar fũwati Benyaminore dekiyore hibaye hibar gór sõloya ze, hitare hodde, "Ei manuššunore góror butore loiza, ar ek zanuwar zorgorao edde hanar bondobos goro; itara dũijja ãr fũwati hána háibo."
GEN 43:17 Manuššuwaye Yusufe hoilde hendilla goijje, hitarare Yusufor górot loigiye.
GEN 43:18 Kintu hitarare Yusufor górot loizarbar, hitara ḍoraiye, ar hitara hodde, "Agor baror ze ṭĩya ãrar bostat gori firigilgoi hinor befare ãrare eṛe ana oiye. Ehon itara ãrare duš dehai akromon gori faribo. Ãrar gadagun hari loifelaibo edde ãrare gulam banaifelibo."
GEN 43:19 Toi hitara Yusufor gór sõloyar hãse giye edde hitar loi goror dorozar ḍake hitar loi hota hoiye,
GEN 43:20 edde hodde, "Oh malik, ãra iyar age o ek bar haiddo kinto aiššilam.
GEN 43:21 Kintu ãra zẽtte fõtot rait haṛaibolla tiyaiyi, edde ãrar bosta kuilli, ar so, fotti ek ekzon zar zar ṭĩya bostar mukot, ãrar nizor ṭiya furafuri uzon mozin, ar ehon hin ãrar fũwati anni.
GEN 43:22 Hin bade o haiddo kinibolla fũwati ãra aro ṭĩya anni. Ãrar ei ṭiya ãrar bostat hone di rakkil hiyan ãra no zani."
GEN 43:23 Toi hite hodde, "Tũwarar balai ok, no ḍoraiyo. Tũwarar Allah edde tũwarar bafor Allaye tũwarar bostat gayebi dón diyede; tũwarar ṭĩya ãi failam." Bade hite Simeonore hitarar hãse ainne.
GEN 43:24 Bade manuššuwaye hitarare Yusufor góror butore ainne, fani diye toi hitara hitarar ṭeng duiye, ar hite hitarar gadagunore adar diye.
GEN 43:25 Yusuf dujja aibo boli hitara hadiyagunore tiyar gori raikke, kiyollahoile hitara funnil ze hitarar há fiya heṛe oibo.
GEN 43:26 Tarfore Yusuf górot aišše, toi hitara ze hadiya okkol ainne hinore góror butore loi zaiyore hibar sarme raikke edde hitara hibar sarme meṛir uite foijje.
GEN 43:27 Hibaye hitara ken ase he hóbor loi bade hibaye hodde, "Tũwarar ze burá bafor babute ãre hoila hiba bala ase ne? Hiba ki ehono basi ase?"
GEN 43:28 Hitara hodde, "Õnor gulam ãrar baf ehono basi ase, ar hiba ehono basi ase." Toi hitara meṛit uite foijje edde Yusufore ijjot dehaiye.
GEN 43:29 Ar Yusufe suk tuli saiye edde hibar nizor mar fut, afon bái Benyaminore deikke, "Ite ne tũwarar he šoṛo bái, zar hota tũwara ãre hoila?" Ar hibaye hodde, "Allaye tore rahamot gorok, oh fut!"
GEN 43:30 Toi Yusufe toratori goijje, kiyollahoile báiyore dekiyore hibar foran hainde. Yusufe ekkan handibar zaga tuwaibolla henttu niyoli giyegoi, ar hiba nizor kamerat góille edde hainde.
GEN 43:31 Bade hibaye muk dúi bade abar baire niyoli aišše, edde nizore sõli loi, ar hána bari dibolla hokum diye.
GEN 43:32 Toi hitara hiballa, edde hibar báiyain okkololla, edde hibar fũwati Mišoriyo okkol zara hána hóya, hitara beggunore aleda gori hána bari diya oiye, kiyollahoile Mišoriyo okkole Ibroni okkolor fũwati hafiya no gorito, haron hiyan aššilde hitarar hãse ekkan hingšar ham.
GEN 43:33 Yusufor sarme báiyain okkolore hitarar boyoš mozin buwaiye. Henot hitara tajjuf oi ekzone oinno zonor uzu sa šuru goijje.
GEN 43:34 Yusufe hitar nizor ṭebilottu kissu kissu hána báiyaindore dibolla bebosta goijje. Kintu oinno báiyain beggunottuwaro Benyaminore fãs gun beši diya oiye. Ar hitara Yusufor fũwati beša beši há fiya goijje edde beši kuši goijje.
GEN 44:1 Tarfore Yusufe hibar gór sõloyare endilla hokum diye: "Ei manuššune zedun boi loizai fare, hedun gĩyu hitarar bostat okkolot bori do, ar hitara fotti zonor ṭĩya hitara fotti zonor bostar mukot di diyo.
GEN 44:2 Ze beggunor šoṛo hitar bostar mukot ãr rufar fiyalawa edde hitar gĩyu kinibar ṭiya di diyo." Toi hite Yusufe hoiyede mozin goijje.
GEN 44:3 Tarfordin binna fohor zehon oiye manuššunore hitara gadagun loi hentu faṭai diya oiye.
GEN 44:4 Hitara šude šohorottu niyoli beši dure no zaite Yusufe hibar gór sõloyare hodde, "Uṭ, manuššunore fisottu lorai za, ar tui zẽtte hitare doribigoi, hitarare hoibi, 'Tũwara balair bodole burai ka goijjo?
GEN 44:5 Iba loi no ne ãr munife fiyede edde gonafora gorede? Tũwara iyan ziyan goijjo, ek horaf ham goijjo!'"
GEN 44:6 Gór sõloyaye hitarare doijjegoi edde he hota okkol hitarare hoiye.
GEN 44:7 Kintu hitara hitare hodde, "Ãr malike endilla hota okkol kiyolla hor? Õnor gulam okkole endilla ham hono din no goribo!
GEN 44:8 So, ãra bostar mukot ze ṭĩya failam hin ãra Kenan dešottu uwafes tũwar hãse firai anni, hen abostat ãra õnor munifor góror šuna rufa kiyolla sur goriyum?
GEN 44:9 Õnor ei gulam okkol zar hãse iba fazaibo, hite moribo; ar ãra o ãr malikor gulam oiyum."
GEN 44:10 Toi hite hodde, "Bala, tũwara hodde mozin oibo; zar hãse fa zaibo, hite ãr gulam oibo, ar baki tũwarar hosuri sara oiba."
GEN 44:11 Toi hitara toratori goijje edde ek ekzone hitar nizor bosta meṛit lamaiye, edde zar zar bosta te kuille.
GEN 44:12 Toi hite ḍõr báiyor bostattu loti šuru gori šoṛo báiyor bosta foijjonto tuwaiye. Ar Fiyalawa Benyaminor bostat fa giye.
GEN 44:13 Toi hitara hitarar nizor hor faiṭṭe, edde zar zar bosta gadar fiṛot bandi loi uwafes šohorot firi giye.
GEN 44:14 Ehudah edde hitar báiyain okkol Yusufor górot aišše, ar Yusuf hehono heṛe aššil; toi hitara Yusufor sarme meṛit ũite foijje.
GEN 44:15 Yusufe hitarare hodde, "Tũwara goijjode in ki goijjo? Ãr ḍoilla manuše ze goni fare, hiyan ki tũwara no zano?"
GEN 44:16 Ehudaye hodde, "Ãr malikore ãra ki hoi faijjum? Ki hota hoiyum? Ãra nidušide hiyan ken gori dehai faijjum? Õnor gulam okkolor hosuri Allaye tuwai bair goijje. So, zar hãse fiyala fa giye hite edde ãra ãr ehon malikor gulam."
GEN 44:17 Kintu Yusufe hodde, "Endilla ham ãi hono din gori no faijjum! Zar hãse he fiyala fa giye lehar te ãr gulam oibo. Ar tũwara šanti bafe tũwarar bafor heṛe firizaigoi fariba."
GEN 44:18 Tarfore Ehudaye Yusufor ḍake zai hodde: "O ãr malik, foriyad gorir, õnor ei gulamore ekkan hota hoibolla ejazot do. Õnor gulamor uwore gušša no goijjo, õne, Feruwanor fuwainna.
GEN 44:19 Ãr malike hibar gulam okkolore fusar goijjila, 'Tũwarar baf bái ase ne?'
GEN 44:20 Ar ãra malikore zuwab dilam, 'Ãrattu ek burá baf ase, ar hibattu burá halor ek fut ase; ar hitar bái mora giye, ar hite ekela ek mar ek fut, hitar bafe hitare beši ador gore.'
GEN 44:21 "Toi õne õnor gulam okkolore hoila, 'Tũwara hitare eṛe anogoi, ãi hitare niz suke saiyum.'
GEN 44:22 Ar ãra ãr malikore hoilam, 'He zuwan bafore eri ai no faribo; hite hitar bafore eri aile, hitar baf mori zaiboi.'
GEN 44:23 Kintu õne ei gulam okkolore hoila, 'Tũwarar šoṛo báiyore zodi tũwarar fũwati no ano, tũwara ãr sarme ai no fariba.'
GEN 44:24 Toi ãra õnor gulam ãr bafor górot uwafes zaiyore, ãra ãr malikor hár hota hibare zanailam.
GEN 44:25 "Toi ãrar bafe hodde, 'Tũwara abar zo, ãralla hodun haiddo kini anogoi.'
GEN 44:26 Ãra hoilam, 'Ãra lamat zai no farir; zodi ãrar šoṛo bái ãrar fũwati take, toile ãra zai faridde, kiyollahoile ãrar šoṛo bái fũwati no takile, ãra manušwar muk sai no faijjum.'
GEN 44:27 Toi õnor gulam, ãrar bafe ãrare hodde, 'Tũwara zano ze ãr bouwe ãlla dui futore biyaiye,
GEN 44:28 henttu o ekzon ãttu giyegoi, ar ãi hoilam, "hite hameka hanhan oi giyegoi" hiyattu loti ãi hitare ar no dekilam.
GEN 44:29 Ehon ãttu itare o zodi loizogoi, edde hitar hono bifod goṭe, toile tũwara hitar dukke ei burá boyošot ãre fatalot lamai diba.'
GEN 44:30 "Ar ehon, õnor gulam ãr bafor munttu ãi hazir oile, edde fuwawa ãrar fũwati no takile, (zar foranor hitar foran loi gãta),
GEN 44:31 zuwannuwa ãrar fũwati naide dekile hiba mori zaibogoi, endilla gori õnor gulam okkole õnor gulam ãrar bafore šukke ei burá boyošot fatalot lamai dibo.
GEN 44:32 Ar õnor gulam ãrar bafor hãse ãi ei zuwanor zabin oi hoilam, 'Ãi zodi hitare tũwar hãse firai no ani, toile ãi ãr bafor hãse zibonbor hosurbon takiyum!'
GEN 44:33 "Hetolla aroz gorir, ei fuwawar bodole ãre õnor gulam hisabe rako, edde ei fuwaware hitar báiyaindor fũwati firi zaito do.
GEN 44:34 Ei fuware no loi zaiyore ãi ken gori ãr bafor hãse firizai faijjum? Edde bafor ze bifod goṭibo hin o ken gori sai faijjum?"
GEN 45:1 Toi Yusuf nizor ḍake tiyat aššilde hitarar sarme nizore ar sõli raki no fare, edde guzori hodde, "Ãr sarmottu beggunore niyolai do!" Henot hibar ḍake ar kiye tiyat no aššil. Toi hetunot Yusufe báiyaindor hãse nizor foriso diye.
GEN 45:2 Ar hibaye eto ḍõr gori guzori hainde ze Mišoriyo okkole hin funniye, edde Feruwanor góror ma he babute funniye.
GEN 45:3 Bade Yusufe hibar báiyaindore hodde, "Ãi Yusuf; ãr baf ki ehono basi ase?" Kintu hibar báiyainde hibare zuwab di no fare, kiyollahoile hitara hibar sarme ḍoraye.
GEN 45:4 Yusufe hibar báiyaindore hodde, "Meherbani gori tũwara ãr ḍake aiyo." Hitara hibar ḍake giye, toi hibaye hodde, "Ãi tũwarar bái Yusuf, zare tũwara Mišorot beisso.
GEN 45:5 Ar tũwara ãre eṛe beissode hiyanolla ehon tũwarar monot duk no ainno otóba nizor uwore rag no goijjo; foran okkol basaibolla Allaye tũwarar age ãre eṛe defeṛaiye.
GEN 45:6 Kiyollahoile dešot raṭ soledde ehon dui bosor oiye, ar aro fãs bosor saš ba fošol da no oibo.
GEN 45:7 Kintu Allaye tũwarar bongšore duniyait basai rakibolla edde moha uddaror duwara tũwarare basaibolla, tũwarar age ãre defeṛaiye.
GEN 45:8 "Hetolla, ãre eṛe tũwara defeṛaiyo no, kintu Allaye. Hibaye ãre Feruwanor bafor zagat, edde hibar hár góror malik, edde šara Mišor dešor uwore šašongoroya goijje.
GEN 45:9 Tũwara toratori uwore ãr bafor hãse zo edde hibare ho: 'Tũwar fut Yusufe endilla hoiye: Allaye ãre šara Mišor dešor malik goijje; tũi eṛe lamat ãr hãse aiyo, deri no goijjo.
GEN 45:10 Tũi, tũwar futziyain edde natifuti, tũwar goru sool, ar za kissu ase beggun loi Gušen elehat takifariba; ar ãr ḍake ogai,
GEN 45:11 Ar heṛe ãi tũwarare deha funa goriyum, kiyollahoile raṭ aro fãs bosor ase. Ar no oilede tũi edde tũwarar góror guštiṭiya, zin ase beggune hošto faiba.'
GEN 45:12 "Ar so, tũwara edde ãr bái Benyamin, tũwara nizor suke dekor, ze ãi nizor muke tũwarar loi hota hoidde;
GEN 45:13 Mišorot ãr hondilla ijjot, edde zaha kissu tũwara deikko, beggun ãr bafore hoiba, ar hibare hara eṛe lamat loianogoi."
GEN 45:14 Toi hibaye hibar bái Benyaminor golat dori hainde, ar Benyamine o hibar golat dori hainde.
GEN 45:15 Ar hibaye báiyain beggunore suma diye edde hitarar golat dori hainde. Tarfore hibar báiyainde hibar loi hotabattara hoiye.
GEN 45:16 Yusufor báiyain aiššede, ei hóbor Feruwanor górot fõsiyore, Feruwan edde hitar gulam okkol beggune kuši oiye.
GEN 45:17 Feruwane Yusufore hodde, "Tui tor báiyain okkolore ho, 'Tũwara endilla goro: Tũwarar zanuwargunor fiṛot haiddo lo edde Kenanot baisa do,
GEN 45:18 ar tũwarar bafore edde tũwarar nizor nizor góror manuš okkolore loi ãr hãse aiyogoi. Ãi tũwarare Mišoror uttom zaga diyum, edde tũwara dešor barik ziniš okkol hái fariba.'
GEN 45:19 "Tui hitarare hokum dibi, 'Tũwara endilla goro: Tũwarar bou fuwaindolla Mišorottu gũra gari okkol loizo, ar hitarare edde tũwarar bafore loi aiyogoi.
GEN 45:20 Ar tũwarar malamalolla no bafiyo, kiyollahoile fura Mišoror uttom ziniš tũwarar oibo.'"
GEN 45:21 Toi Israilor futain okkole hendilla goijje. Yusufe razar hokum mozin hitarare gũra gari diye, ar hibaye hitarare fõtolla hána o diye.
GEN 45:22 Hibaye fotti zonore noya hor diye, kintu Benyaminore tin šot rufar ṭĩya edde fãs zura hor diye.
GEN 45:23 Ar bafolla hibaye in okkol defeṛaiye: došwa modda gadar fiṛot gori Mišoror barik ziniš okkol, ar došwa miyala gadar fiṛot gori gĩyũ edde ruṭi ar bafor baisalla haiddo.
GEN 45:24 Tarfore hibaye báiyaindore bidai goijje, ar hitara baisa diyar šomot hibaye hodde, "Fõtot hoijja-hanḍal no goijjo!"
GEN 45:25 Toi hitara Mišorottu niyoliyore uwore Kenanot hitarar baf Yakubor hãse aišše.
GEN 45:26 Edde hitara bafore hoiye, hodde, "Yusuf ehono zinda ase, ar šara Mišor dešor uwore hite šašongoroya oiye." Kintu bafor dil sorot taigiyegoi, kiyollahoile hitara hota hibattu biššaš no lage.
GEN 45:27 Ar Yusufe hitarare hoilde he hár hota okkol zehon hitara hibare hoiye, edde hibare boiloizaibolla Yusufe gũra gari okkol defeṛaiyede hin zehon deikke, henot hitarar baf Yakubor ruh uwafes zinda oi uiṭṭe.
GEN 45:28 Toi Israile hodde, "Iyan beši oiye! Ãr fut Yusuf ehono zinda ase; Ãi zaiyore moribar age hitare saiyum."
GEN 46:1 Tarfore Israile hibar hár kissu loi baisa diyore Beer-Šebat aišše, edde hibaye hibar baf Isakor Allar mutallek kurbani okkol diye.
GEN 46:2 Allaye raitta Israilore deha diyore hodde, "Yakub, Yakub!" hibaye hodde, So, oto ãi.
GEN 46:3 Toi hibaye hodde, "Ãi Allah, tor bafor Allah; Lamat Mišorot zaite tui no ḍorais, kiyollahoile heṛe ãi tore ek ḍõr zati goriyum.
GEN 46:4 Ãi tor fũwati lamat Mišorot zaiyum, edde hentu ãi tore abar uwafes firai o loi ainnum, ar tor sukor fata Yusufor nizor hate bandi dibo."
GEN 46:5 Toi Yakube Beer-Šebattu baisa diye. Israilor futainde hitarar baf Yakubore, edde hitara nizor nizor futziyain okkolore, edde bouwain okkolore, oi gũragari okkol, zin Feruwane hibare boiloizaibolla defeṛail, hinot gori loi giye.
GEN 46:6 Ar hitara hitarar zanuwar okkol edde Kenanot hamailde hár šombotti okkol fũwati loi, Yakub edde hibar fura bongšo ṭiya hibar fũwati, Mišorot aigiyegoi.
GEN 46:7 Yakube hibar futain, futaindor fuwain, ziyain, ziyaindor ziyain, hibar gũṛa bongšo ṭiyare hibar fũwati Mišorot loi anniye.
GEN 46:8 In okkol oilde Israilor futain okkol nam okkol (Yakub edde hibar bongšo okkol) zara Mišorot aišše: Yakubor foila zormo Ruben.
GEN 46:9 Rubenor futain okkol: Hanok, Pallu, Hešron edde Karmi.
GEN 46:10 Simeonor futain okkol: Jemuwel, Jamin, Ohad, Jakin, Sohar edde Šaul he Kenaniyo mayafuwar fut.
GEN 46:11 Levir futain okkol: Geršon, Kekat edde Merari.
GEN 46:12 Ehudar futain okkol: Er, Onan, Šela, Feroš edde Šerah. (Er edde Onan Kenan dešot entehal goijje.) Ferošor futain okkol: Hešron edde Hamul.
GEN 46:13 Issakaror futain okkol: Tola, Puvah, Job ar Šimron.
GEN 46:14 Sebulunor futain okkol: Serod, Elun ar Jahalel.
GEN 46:15 Itara oilde Lear futain okkol, zarare hibaye Paddan-Aramot Yakubolla biyail, fũwati hibar zi Dina šoho. Hitara mayafuwain edde morod fuwain beggune muṭ triš tinzon.
GEN 46:16 Gador futain okkol: Sifiyon, Haggi, Šuni, Esbon, Eri, Arodi edde Areli.
GEN 46:17 Ašeror futain okkol: Jimna, Jišba, Jišbi, Beriyah, edde hitarar boin Serah. Beriyar futain okkol: Heber edde Malhiyel.
GEN 46:18 Itara he Zilpar fuwain zare Labone nizor ziyore bandi hisabe dil, hibaye Yakubolla itarare biyaiye. Itara beggune šullo zon.
GEN 46:19 Yakubor bou Rahelar futain okkol: Yusuf edde Benyamin.
GEN 46:20 Ar Mišorot, Manessare edde Efraimore On šohoror imam Putiferar zi Asenate Yusufolla biyaiye.
GEN 46:21 Benjaminor futain okkol: Bela, Beker, Ašbel, Gera, Naman, Ehi, Ruš, Muffim, Huffim edde Ard.
GEN 46:22 Itara aššilde Rahelar futain okkol, zarare Yakubolla biyaiye. Hitara muṭ soiddo zon.
GEN 46:23 Danor fut: Hušim.
GEN 46:24 Naftalir futain okkol: Zahšiyel, Guni, Jezer edde Šillem.
GEN 46:25 Itara aššilde Bilhar futain, zare Labone nizor ziyore bandi hisabe dil. Hibaye Yakubolla itarare biyaiye. Hitara muṭ hãt zon.
GEN 46:26 Hitara zarare loi Yakube Mišorot aiyat aššil, zara hibar nizor bongšottu, Yakubor futaindor bouwain okkol sara, hitara muṭ haiṭ so zon.
GEN 46:27 Mišorot Yusufottu ze dui fut zormo oiye, edde Yakubor gušṭi zara Mišorot aišše hitara beggune muṭ hoittor zon.
GEN 46:28 Bade Yakube hibar age Ehudare Yusufor hãse defeṛaiye, zene hibaye hitare Gušenot zaibar fõt dehai de, toi hitara Gušen elehat aišše.
GEN 46:29 Toi Yusufe hibar nizor gũra garire hãzaiyore Gušenot hibar baf Israil loi deha goitto giye. Toi bafore zehon deikke, golat dori bout hotun hainde.
GEN 46:30 Hetunot Israile Yusufore hodde, "Ãi ehon moribolla tiyar! Tui zinda asos, ãi tor siyara dekilam."
GEN 46:31 Toi Yusufe hibar báiyain okkol edde hibar bafor góror manuš okkolore hodde, "Ãi Feruwanor hãse zai ei hóborgan hoigoi, hibare hoiyum, 'Ãr báiyain edde bafor góror manuš okkol zara Kenanot takito, hitara ãr hãse aišše.
GEN 46:32 Hitara soolsoroya okkol; hitara goru sool faloya okkol. Hitara hitarar goru, sool, edde hitarar nizor hár kissu fũwati loi aišše.'
GEN 46:33 Ar Feruwane tũwarare zẽtte ḍakibo edde fusar goribo, 'Tũwarar feša ki?'
GEN 46:34 Tũwara hoiba, 'Õnor ei gulam okkol edde hitarar baf dada okkole šoṛo halottu loti ehon foijjonto goru sool fali aiyer.' toi zene tũwara Gušenot takifariba, kiyollahoile soolsoroya okkol mani Mišoriyo okkolor hingšar ziniš."
GEN 47:1 Toi Yusuf giye edde Feruwanore ei hóborgan diye, hodde, "Ãr baf báiyain okkole hitarar goru sool edde hitarar nizor hár kissur loi Kenan dešottu aigiyegoi, ar ehon hitara Gušenot."
GEN 47:2 Ar hibaye hibar báiyain okkolor butottu fãs zonore loiyore hitarare Feruwanor sarme hazir goijje.
GEN 47:3 Feruwane báiyain okkolore fusar goijje, "Tũwarar feša ki?" Hitara Feruwanore hodde, "Õnor ei gulam okkol hitarar baf dada okkolor ḍoil, soolsoroya.
GEN 47:4 Ãra ei dešot forbaš goribolla aiššide, kiyollahoile õnor gulam okkole hitarar zanuwar okkol sori háibolla hono zaga no fail, kiyollahoile Kenanot raṭ beši hora oiye ar etolla aroz gorir, õnor gulam okkolore Gušenot takito do."
GEN 47:5 Toi Feruwane Yusufore hodde, "Tor baf edde tor báiyain okkol tor hãse aišše,
GEN 47:6 Mišoror deš tor sarme ase; ar dešor uttom zagat tor baf edde báiyaindore bošoti goraba; hitara Gušen elehat bošoti gorok; ar hitarar butore has laikka manuš asede tor zana takile, hitarar uwore ãr nizor zanuwar zãkor zimma de."
GEN 47:7 Bade Yusufe hibar nizor baf Yakubore ainne edde Feruwanor sarme hazir goijje; toi Yakube Feruwanore duwa goijje,
GEN 47:8 toi Feruwane Yakubore fusar goredde, "Tũwar boyoš ho bosor oiye?"
GEN 47:9 Toi Yakube Feruwanore hodde, "Ãr forbaš hal ekšo triš bosor; ãr aiur ei olfo din, hin o hoštot haiṭṭiye. Ar hin ãr baf dada okkolor forbaš halor aiuror fuwainna no o."
GEN 47:10 Bade Yakube Feruwanore duwa goijje edde hitar sarmottu bidai oiye.
GEN 47:11 Toi Feruwanor hokum mozin, Yusufe Mišor dešor uttom zagat, Rameses elehat, šombotti hisabe di, hibar baf edde hibar báiyain okkolore bošobaš goribolla buwai diye.
GEN 47:12 Yusufe hibar baf báiyain edde hibar bafor hár góror manuš okkolore, hitarar fuwain mozin haiddo zuhai diye.
GEN 47:13 Dešor hono mikka haiddo no aššil, kiyollahoile heṛe raṭ beši boiyanok oiye; Mišor edde Kenan raṭor zoriya toba oi giyegoi.
GEN 47:14 Ar Mišorot edde Kenanot zeto ṭiya aššil hin loi mainše haiddo kinat maze, Yusufe he šomosto ṭĩya dola gori loi Feruwanor górot ainne.
GEN 47:15 Mišor edde Kenan dešor manuš okkolor ṭĩya zehon šeš oi giyegoi, Mišor beggune Yusufor hãse aiyore hodde: "Ãrare haiddo do! Ãrattu ar hono ṭĩya nai boli ki ãra õnor sukor sarme moriyum ne?"
GEN 47:16 Yusufe hodde, "Tũwarattu ṭĩya šeš oigilegoi tũwarar goru sool do, toi ãi tũwarar zanuwaror bodole tũwarare haiddo diyum."
GEN 47:17 Toi hitara hitarar zanuwar okkol Yusufor hãse ainne, toi Yusufe gũra, soolor zak, gorur zak, edde gada, hin okkolor bodole tarare haiddo diye. Ebafe Yusufe hitarar hár goru sool okkolor bodole hitarare haiddo diye edde he bosor lalon falon goijje.
GEN 47:18 He bosor haṛi zaigoi bade hitara dusora bosor aiyore hodde, "Ãra ãrar malikor hãse kissu gufon no goriyum, ãrar ṭĩya beggun furaigiyegoi, ar goru sool o õnor oiye; ar ãrar ga edde zobin sara malikore sarme rakibolla ãrattu ar kissu nai.
GEN 47:19 Õnor sukor sarme ãra edde zobin šoho kiyolla moritam? Ãrare edde ãrar zobingunore haiddor bodole kini lo, ar ãra ãrar zobin šoho Feruwanor gulam oiyum. Ãrare bizor dana do, toi zene ãra zane basi fari edde no mori, ar zobingun o beabadi oi no zagoi."
GEN 47:20 Toi Yusufe Mišoror hár zobin Feruwanolla kini loiye, kiyollahoile Mišoriyo okkol fotti ekzone hitarar zaga besi felaiye, kiyollahoile hitarar uwore raṭ beši hora oil. Ei bafe Mišoror hár zaga Feruwanor oiye.
GEN 47:21 ar Yusufe Mišoror ek šimattu loti oinno šima foijjontor manuš okkol beggunore šohorot lari loi ainne.
GEN 47:22 hibaye šude šadu okkolor zobingun kini no lo, kiyollahoile hitara Feruwanottu bata faito, ar ze bata hitarare Feruwane dito hin loi hitara solito. Hetolla hitara hitarar zobin no bese.
GEN 47:23 Toi Yusufe mainšore hodde, "So, aziya ãi tũwara edde tũwarar zobin Feruwanolla kiniloilam. Ei bizor dana in lo, zobinot šiṛogoi.
GEN 47:24 Hinot folibode hinor fãs bagor ek bag Feruwanore diba, ar baki sair bagottu bizor dana edde tũwara edde tũwarar góror manuš okkol edde tũwarar fuwaindolla haiddo oibo."
GEN 47:25 Toi hitara hodde, "Õne ãrar foran rokka goilla, ãrar uwore õnor rahamotor nozor ok; ãra Feruwanor gulam oiyum."
GEN 47:26 Yusufe Mišoror zobinor babute ei ain ze goijjil hiyan aizo foijjonto zari ase. Zendilla neki, hár fošolor fãs bagor ek bag Feruwanor. Šude šadu okkolor zobin Feruwanor no o.
GEN 47:27 Toi Israili okkol Mišoror Gušen elehat bošoti goijje. Hitara heṛe šombotti fail edde hitara fólwala oiye edde manušor zono šoinka beši oi uiṭṭe.
GEN 47:28 Yakub Mišor dešot hõtoro bosor basi aššil, ar Yakubor boyoš ek šo sališ hãt bosor oiye.
GEN 47:29 Bade zehon Israil moribar ṭaim hãse aišše, hibaye hibar fut Yusufore ḍakaiyore hodde: "Ãi zodi tor doya fai taki, toile aroz gorir, tui ãr kulot hat de edde ãre hota de ze tui ãre doya dehaibi edde he mozin wada ṭik rakibi. Tũi ãre Mišorot no gãraibi,
GEN 47:30 Ãi zehon ãr baf dada okkolor hãse ziraiyum, tui ãre Mišorottu niyolai loi zaiyore hitarar hoborstanot ãre gãraibi." Yusufe hodde: "Tũi zen hor, ãi hen goijjum."
GEN 47:31 Toi hibaye hodde, "Tui ãr loi hosom gor." Toi hibaye hosom goijje, toi Israile bisanar šitanor mikka sojida foijje.
GEN 48:1 Iyar hoto din bade ekzone Yusufore hodde, "So, õnor bafottu ošuk." Henot hibaye hibar dui fut, Manessa edde Efraimore, hibar fũwati loiye.
GEN 48:2 Toi ekzone Yakubore hóbor hoiye, hodde, "So, tũwar fut Yusuf aišše." Henot Israile hibar gar hár bol diyore uiṭṭe edde bisanat uṛi boišše.
GEN 48:3 Yakube Yusufore hodde, "Kenan dešor Lušot maze Šorbo-Šoktiwala Allaye ãre deha dil edde duwa goijjil.
GEN 48:4 Hibaye ãre hoil, 'Sa, ãi tore beši fólwala goijjum edde tor bongšo barai diyum, ar ãi tore uggwa bout zatir šomaz goriyum, ar ãi tui bade tor bongšo okkolore ei dešgan sirohalolla šombotti hisabe diyum.'
GEN 48:5 "Ar ehon, tor dui fut, zara ãi eṛe Mišorot aibar age zormo oiye, hitara ãr; Ruben edde Simeonor ḍoilla Efraim edde Manessa o, hitara ãr.
GEN 48:6 Kintu itara bade zarare zonom dibi, hitara tor oibo; hitara hitarar báiyaindor name ei zagat šombottir miraz faibo.
GEN 48:7 Ar ãi Paddanottu aibar šomot Kenan dešor Efratot fõsite olfo fõt baki takite, Rahela ãr hãsottu mara giye. Henot ãi heṛe Efrator (hiyan oilde Betlehem) fõtor ḍake hibare dohon gorailam."
GEN 48:8 Toi, Israile Yusufor dui futore dekiyore hibaye fusar goredde, "Itara hontara?"
GEN 48:9 Yusufe hibar bafore hodde, "Itara ãr futain, zarare Allaye ei dešot ãre diye." Toi Israile hodde, "Hitarare ãr hãse an, ãi hitarare duwa gori."
GEN 48:10 Burá boyoše suke dekibar šokti homi zagoinor zoriya Yakube bala gori no dekito. Yusufe hibar dui futore hibar hãse ainne, ar hibar bafe hitarare suma diye edde ãzamari doijje.
GEN 48:11 Toi Israile Yusufore hodde, "Ãi baffilam, tor muk ar no dekiyum; kintu sa, Allaye ãre tor bongšo udda dehaiye."
GEN 48:12 Tarfore Yusufe hitarare Yakubor kulottu lamai diye edde meṛir uzu oi holla zuhaiore bafore salam goijje.
GEN 48:13 Bade Yusufore dunizonore loi zai, Efraimore ḍen hate dori Israilor bame edde Manessare bam hate dori Israilor ḍene, hibar ḍake ainne.
GEN 48:14 Kintu Israile hibar ḍen hattan barai di Efraimor matat rakkil, zodi o hite šoṛo fut. Ar bam hattan Manessar matat rakkil, zodi o hite foila fut.
GEN 48:15 Toi hibaye Yusufore duwa goijje edde endilla hoiye, "Ãr baf dada, Ibrahim edde Isak, Allar issa mozin solito, ãr zibonor foila loti aijja foijjonto, he Allah ze ãre soolsoroyar ḍoilla gori sõli aiyer.
GEN 48:16 he firista ze ãre hár mosibotottu uddar goijje, Hibaye ei zuwan okkolore duwa gorok. Itarar duwara ãr edde ãr baf dada, Ibrahim edde Isakor nam basi takok, ar itarar bongšo ei zobinot beša beši bari uṛok."
GEN 48:17 Hetunot Efraimor matat bafe ḍen hat raikkede deki Yusuf naraz oiye; toi hibaye Efraimor matattu bafor hattan loi Manessar matat dibolla saiye.
GEN 48:18 Yusufe bafore hodde, "Baba, hendilla no, foila zormo iteya; itar matat tũwar ḍen hat rako."
GEN 48:19 Kintu bafe na monzur oi hodde, "Ãi zani, o fut, ãi zani. Hitar butottu o uggwa zati oibo, edde hite o mohan oibo, kintu hitar šoṛo bái hitattuwaro aro beši mohan oibo. Hitar bongšor manuš okkolor butottu beši zati okkol oibo."
GEN 48:20 Toi hibaye hitarare he din duwa goijje edde hodde: "Israili zati okkole honokiyore duwa dibar šomot hitara en hok: 'Allaye tore Efraim edde Manessar ḍoilla gorok.'" Endilla hoiyore hibaye Efraimore Manessare ḍõr banaiye.
GEN 48:21 Tarfore Israile Yusufore hodde, "Sa, ãi moribar ṭaim aišše, kintu Allah tũwarar fũwati takibo edde tũwarare tũwarar baf-dadar dešot firai loizaiboi.
GEN 48:22 Ãi tore tor báiyaindottuwaro ek bag miraz beši dilam, ze beši bag ãi tore diyum, hiyan oilde he zaga ziyan ãi toluwar edde silhanḍa loi zuddo gori Amorittiyo okkolor hatottu loilam."
GEN 49:1 Bade Yakube hibar futaindore ḍaikke edde hodde, "Beggune fũwati aiyo, sarme tũwarar uwore zin goṭibo hin ãi tũwarare hoi:
GEN 49:2 "Beggune fũwati aiyo! Funo, Yakubor futain okkol, tũwarar bab Israilor hota funo.
GEN 49:3 "Ruben, tui ãr foila zormo. Tui ãr bol, ãr juwanir foila fól, tui beggunor uwore šommani edde šoktidar.
GEN 49:4 Tui fanir ḍoilla ũtari foror, tor he usol tokka ar no takibo, kiyollahoile tui tor bafor bisanat giyos; tui napak ham goijjos, hite ãr bisanat giye.
GEN 49:5 "Simeon edde Levi bái bái hitarar horafir zontro oilde toluwar.
GEN 49:6 Hitarar gufon mošorat ãr hono ongšo nai, ãi hitarar dolot no! kiyollahoile hitara guššae manuš kun gore, nizor issa mote gorur ṭengor šiṛa haṛe.
GEN 49:7 Bodduwa hitarar gušša edde gumanore, haron hin bišon edde beši zalemi. Ãi hitarare Yakubor bongšottu bag goriyum, edde Israilor butore hitarare šiṛašitta goriyum.
GEN 49:8 "Ehudah, tor báiyainde tor tarif goribo; dušmon okkolor geṛir uwore tor hat oibo; tor bafor futain okkole tor sarme mata zuhaibo.
GEN 49:9 Ãr fut Ehudah, tui šingor so; tui šiyaror gusto há šeš gori uṛi aili. Šingor ḍoilla neṛili edde uite fori roili, honokiye tor ḍake aibar šahoš no gorer.
GEN 49:10 Ekdin Ehudar bongšor butottu ekzon šašongoroya aibo, zar hokum hár zatiye manibo. Ehudattu razar aša no zaibogoi, no zaibogoi bisaror aša hibar dui ṭengor mazottu Ze foijjonto šilo no aiye ar zati okkolor baiddota hibar oibo.
GEN 49:11 He ãngur lotat hibare gadawa bandibo, ar ãngur gasor he barik ḍeilat bandibo, gadar soware, hibaye šorafot duiye hibar fušak, ãnguror louwot duiye hibar hoor.
GEN 49:12 Hibar suk oibo šorafottuwaro lal, hibar dat dudottuwaro dola.
GEN 49:13 "Sebulun doriyar farot bošot goribo, hiyan zahaz biraibar bondor oibo; Sidon foijjonto hitar dešor šima oibo.
GEN 49:14 "Issakar oilde ek boli gada ze dui soolor urar mazottu neṛer.
GEN 49:15 hite dekilo ze ziranir zagagan bala, ar deššan šundor, hetolla hite bár boibolla hand lagai dilo, ar ek bondi gulam oigiyegoi.
GEN 49:16 "Dane hitar mainšor bisar goribo, Israilor guštir ek bongšor ḍoilla gori.
GEN 49:17 Dan ek haf, fõtor ḍake ek bišdor haf, siyon rastat ze gũrar kuri sai kuṭmare, ar gũrar suwari uldi fis mikka fori zagoi.
GEN 49:18 "O Mabud ãi tũwar uddaror ofekkat asi.
GEN 49:19 "Gadore ḍahaitor dole hamela goribo, kintu te o ulda falda hamela goribo.
GEN 49:20 "Ašerottu barik haiddo fodai oibo; hite razalla mozar hana zuhaibo.
GEN 49:21 "Naftali melá horinni, hite šundojja baša ho.
GEN 49:22 "Yusuf oilde ek gulawala gas, zonnar ḍake ek gulawala gas, ze gasor ḍeila okkol ḍebal ḍiyai giye.
GEN 49:23 Tir maroya okkole hitare beši hošṭo der, hitara hitare tir marer edde hamela gorer.
GEN 49:24 Kintu hitar silhanḍa zendilla mojbut, hitar hator bayerat roiye hendilla bol, kiyollahoile Yakubor Šoktiwalar hat, ze Israilor falok edde he ḍõr fattor,
GEN 49:25 tor bafor Allah, ze tore modot gorer, he Šoktiwala, ze tore rahamot gorer, asmanor uworor rahamot loi, nisor zobinor rahamot loi, bukor dud edde gorbor rahamot loi.
GEN 49:26 Tor bafor rahamot aro barik sirohailla faharottu rahamotottuwaro, sirohailla parbotottu bala zinišottuwaro. Hin okkol Yusufor matar uwore forok, forok hitar matar širot, ze báiyain okkolor maze razfut.
GEN 49:27 "Benyamin oilde ek šiyari gendabag, binna hite šiyar háibo, ar hazinna hite luṭ baṛe."
GEN 49:28 Itara beggun oilde Israilor baro bongšo, ar in oilde zin hitarar bafe hitarare hoil zẽtte hibaye hitarare rahamot goijje. Hibaye rahamot goijje edde hitara fotti ekzon ze zar laikka mozin duwa diye.
GEN 49:29 Bade Yakube hitarare hokum diye edde hitarare hodde, "Ãi ãr baf dada okkolor hãse dola oirgoi. Hetittiyo Efronor maṛor hoboror gãtot, ãr baf dada okkolor fũwati ãre hobor diyo.
GEN 49:30 Ei gãt iba oilde Kenanot Mamrer muwamui Mokfelar maṛot, ziyan Ibrahime Hetittiyo Efronor hãsottu maṭ šoho hoborstan banaibolla kini loil.
GEN 49:31 Heṛe Ibrahim edde hibar bou Sarare o hobor diya oiye, ar Isak edde hibar bou Rebekare o heṛe hobor diya oiye, ar ãi Leare o heṛe hobor diyi.
GEN 49:32 He maṭ edde heṛe asede gãt šoho hiyan Hetittiyo okkolottu kini lowa oiye."
GEN 49:33 Yakube hibar futaindore hokum diya šeš gori bade bisanar uwore dui ṭeng ek hatar goijje, bade niyaš felaiye edde hibar baf dada okkol loi dola oiyegoi.
GEN 50:1 Hetunot Yusufe hibar bafor mukor uwore muk diyore hainde, edde hibare suma diye.
GEN 50:2 Bade Yusufe hibar bafor gat kušbo mosolla makidibolla, hibar gulam okkol edde ḍakṭor okkolore hokum diye, henot ḍakṭor okkole hibare kušbo mosolla makidiye,
GEN 50:3 Hitara he ham sališ din dori goijje, kiyollahoile kušbo mosolla maki dite sališ din lage. Ar Mišoriyo okkole hiballa hoittor din foijjonto šuk goijje.
GEN 50:4 Šukor din okkol faraizaigoi bade, Yusufe Feruwanor hormosari okkolore hodde, "Zodi ãi tũwarar nozorottu doya fai taki, toile Feruwanor hanot ei hotagun hogoi,
GEN 50:5 'Ãr bafe ãre hosom goraiye edde hoiye, "Sa, ãi morizairgoi, Kenanot ãi ãlla ze hobor kuri raikki, tui ãre hibat gãrais." Hetolla foriyad gorir, ãre heṛe uwore zaito do; ãi bafore gãrai bade abar firi aiššum.'"
GEN 50:6 Feruwane hodde, "Za, tor bafe tore zendilla hosom goraiye, tui he mozin hibar hobor degoi."
GEN 50:7 Toi Yusufe hibar bafore gãraibolla uwor mikka baisa diye, Feruwanor gulam okkol beggun, hitar góror hár murubbi okkol edde dešor hár murubbi okkol, beggune hibar fũwati uwore giye.
GEN 50:8 Ar Yusufor fura gór, edde hibar báiyain okkol, edde hibar bafor gór okkol giye; šude hitarar gura fuwain okkol edde goru soolor zãkgunore Gušenot eri giye.
GEN 50:9 ar hibar fũwati uwore gũragari edde gũrar suwari okkol o giye. Hitara beggune ḍõr ek dol oiye.
GEN 50:10 Toi hitara Zordan halor oinno faror Atador hõlat fõisse, heṛe beša beši bilag dori handa haṛi goijje. Ar Yusufe o hãt din dori bafolla šuk goijje.
GEN 50:11 Ar Kenanor bašinda okkole Atador hõlat Mišoror mainšor šuk falon šoba deki hodde, "Mišoriyo okkololla iyan ekkan beši muilliyoban šuk šoba oibo." Hetolla Zordanor oinno ḍakottu asede zaga hiyanor nam Abel-Mišraim nam oiye.
GEN 50:12 Toi hibar futaindore hokum dilde mozin hitara goijje.
GEN 50:13 Hitara hibare Kenanot loigiye, edde Mamrer muwamui Mokfelar maṛor gãtot hobor diye, ziyan Ibrahime Hetittiyo Efronor hãsottu hoborstan banaibolla kiniloil.
GEN 50:14 Bafore dohon gorai bade Yusufe báiyain okkol, aro zara hibar fũwati hibar bafore dohon goraito gil, hitara beggun šoho Mišorot firi aigiyegoi.
GEN 50:15 Yusufor báiyainde zehon deikke ze hitarar baf morigiyegoi, hitara hodde, "Otfare Yusufe ãrare hingša goribo, edde ãra hitar uwore ze burai goijjilam, hin beggunor bodola uwafes ãrattu loibo."
GEN 50:16 Hetolla hitara Yusufor hãse en hoiyore hóbor defeṛaiye, "Tor bafe moribar age ãrare endilla hokum dil:
GEN 50:17 'Tũwara Yusufore ei hota hoiyo: Tor báiyainde tor berudde oinnai goriyore ze nasoyi edde guna goijje meherbani gori tui hitarar onnaire edde gunare maf goride.' Etolla ehon ãra foriyad gorir, tor bafor Allar ei gulam okkolor onnaire edde gunare maf goride." Hitarar ei hotat Yusufe hainde.
GEN 50:18 Bade hibar Báiyain okkol o aišše edde hibar sarme meṛit ũite foijje edde hodde, "Sa, ãra tor gulam okkol."
GEN 50:19 Toi Yusufe hitarare hodde, "No ḍoraio! Ãi hon Allar zagat tiyoya?
GEN 50:20 Tũwara ãr berudde horafi goribolla baffila hiyan ṭik, kintu Allaye balar mikka baiffe. Ei bafe Allaye beši mainšor foran rokka goribar issa goijje, zendilla tũwara aziya dehor.
GEN 50:21 Hetolla no ḍoraiyo! Ãi tũwara edde tũwarar fuwaindore falizaiyum." Ei bafe hibaye hitarare dilot šanti edde buz diye.
GEN 50:22 Bade Yusuf hibar bafor gór šoho beggun loi Mišorot bošoti goijje; Hiba ekšo doš bosor zinda aššil,
GEN 50:23 ar Yusufe Efraimor fuwain edde Efraimor natiyain okkol foijjonto dekkil. Ar Manessar fut Makiror fuwain okkol o Yusufor kulot zormo oil.
GEN 50:24 Bade Yusufe báiyaindore hodde, "Ãi morizairgoi, kintu Allaye hameka tũwarar uzu nozor rakibo, edde Ibrahim, Isak edde Yakubor hãse ze deš dibar wada goijjil, tũwarare ei dešottu he dešot loizaibo."
GEN 50:25 Yusufe Israili okkolore ek hosom goraiye edde hodde, "Allaye hameka tũwarar uzu saibo, ar tũwara entu ãr ãḍḍigun tuli loizaiyogoi."
GEN 50:26 Toi Yusuf ekšo doš bosor umorot mori giyegoi. Ar mainše hibare kušbo mosolla maki diye edde hibare Mišorot ek tabutot raki diya oiye.
RUT 1:1 Još okkole šašon goribar agor ṭaimot dešot ek bar raṭ oil. Ar Ehudiyar Betlehemottu ekzon manuše, hitar bou edde dui futore fũwati loi Muab dešot hãroigilgoi.
RUT 1:2 Manušwar nam aššilde Elimelek, hitar bouwor nam aššilde Naumi, ar hitar dui futor nam aššilde Mahlon edde Kilion. Itara aššilde Ehudiyar Betlehemor Efrat-guštir manuš. Itara Muab dešot giye edde heṛe roiye.
RUT 1:3 Bade Naumir šuwami Elimelek mori gilgoi, henot hiba hibar dui futore loi roiye.
RUT 1:4 Bade hitara duizone dui Muabi hoinniare biya goijje: ekzonor nam aššil Orpa, ar ekzonor nam aššil Rut. Hitara onumanik doš bosor heṛe bošoti goijje.
RUT 1:5 Tarfore Mahlon edde Kilion, hitara dunizono mori giyegoi, ar Naumi šuwami hara, fuwain hara, duni mikkattu eka oi roiye.
RUT 1:6 Bade Naumi hibar futor bouwain dunizon fũwati loi Muab dešottu firi zaiboilla uṭṭil; haron hibaye Muab dešot fuinnil ze Mabude hibar mainšor uwore nozor diye edde ahar der.
RUT 1:7 Hiyanor zoriya hiba zeṛe takito he zagttu niyolle, ar fũwati hibar dui futor bouwain o aššil, Toi hitara Ehudiya dešot uwafes firi zaiboilla fõt bai baisa diye.
RUT 1:8 Hetunot Naumiye hibar dui futor bouwaindore hodde: "Tũwara tũwarar mar górot firizogoi. Mora okkololla edde ãlla ze raham goijjio, Mabud tũwarare o he bafe raham gorok.
RUT 1:9 Tũwara dunizone zene šuwamir górot bissram fo, Mabud tũwarare hendilla dula dok." Toi hibaye hitarare suma diye; henot hitara guzori handa šuru goijje.
RUT 1:10 Ar hibare hodde: "Na, ãra o tũwar fũwati tũwar zatir heṛe firi zaiyum."
RUT 1:11 Kintu Naumiye hodde: "Oh ãr hoinnia okkol, firizogoi, tũwara ãr fũwati kiyolla zaiba? Tũwarar šuwami oi farefan ãr feṛot ki aro morod fuwa oibar aša ase?
RUT 1:12 Oh ãr hoinnia okkol, firizogoi; haron ãr boyoš oiye, ãi abar biya gori no faijjum. Ar zodi o aša ase hoi aijja raitta biya gori, ar futain zormo di.
RUT 1:13 Toile tũwara ki hitara zuwan ofan ofekka gori tai fariba? Hitaralla ki tũwara biya no gori boi taiba? No no, Oh ãr hoinnia okkol! Iyan tũwarattuwaro ãttu aro beši titar lager, kiyollahoile Mabudor hãt ãr berudde giye!
RUT 1:14 Henot hitara abar guzori handa šuru goijje. Toi Orpaye hibar horire sumadi bidai loiye, kintu Rute hibar hórire ãzamari dori taigiyegoi.
RUT 1:15 Tehon Naumi hodde: "Sa, tor zal hibar mainšor edde hibar devotar hãse firigiyegoi, tui o tor zalor fise fise firizagoi."
RUT 1:16 Kintu Rute hodde: "Tũware felaizaite, tũwar fisa lowattu firizaibolla ãre no hoiyo: Kiyollahoile zeṛe tũi zor, ãi o zaiyum, ar zeṛe tũi takor, ãi o takiyum. Tũwar zati, ãr zati, ar tũwar Allah, ãr Allah.
RUT 1:17 Zeṛe tũi moror, ãi o morium, edde heṛe ãre hobor diya ok. Moron sara ar kissuye zodi ãre edde tũware zuda gori fare, toile Mabud ãre beši gozob dok!"
RUT 1:18 Naumi zehon dekilo hibar fũwati zaibolla Rut mon sokto gori ereda gorifelaye, tehon hibaye hibare ar kissu no hoilo.
RUT 1:19 Bade hitara dunizon zaite zaite Betlehem zehon fõssiyegoi, farar agagura hitarar babute howa hoi šuru oiye; mayafuwain okkole hodde: "Iba Naumi no?"
RUT 1:20 Hibaye hitarare hodde: "Ãre Naumi (zara mani kuši) no ḍaikkio, bolke Mara (zar mani tita) ḍako, Kiyollahoile Šorbo-šoktiwalaye ãr zibonore beši tita gori diye.
RUT 1:21 Ãi hár kissu furon gori loi baisa dilam, kintu ehon Mabude ãre hali hat loi firai ainnye. Tũwara ãre Naumi hoi ka ḍakor zehon Mabud ãr bifokkede forman diye, ar Šorbo-šoktiwalaye ãre hoštot felaiye.
RUT 1:22 Ei bafe Naumi firi aišše, hibar fũwati hibar futor bou Rut o, ze Muab dešottu firi aišše. Toi hitara Betlehem aiššede šomot gĩu da šuru oiye.
RUT 2:1 Naumir šuwami Elimelekor guštir ekzon ijjotdar tuwangor egena aššil; tãir nam Buaz.
RUT 2:2 Ek dinna Muabiya Rute Naumire hodde: Ãi ketor kuṛat zaiore ze ãre rahamotor nozore giudanar sóra feṛaito de, tar fise fise giudanar sóra feṛaigoi. Naumi hoil: Okena, za oh zi.
RUT 2:3 Bade hiba zaiore ek ketor kuṛat fošol haṛoya okkolor fise fise kuṛat foijjia giudanar sóra okkol feṛailowa šuru goijjil. Ar endilla oilo, ze kuṛat Rute giudana feṛail hiyan Elimelekor egena Buazor ket.
RUT 2:4 Ar so, Buaz Betlehemottu aišše edde fošol haṛoya okkolore hoil: Mabud tũwarar fũwati takok. Tara zuwabe hoil: Mabud õnore o duwa gorok.
RUT 2:5 Bade Buaz fošol haṛoya okkolor uwore zimmadarore fusar goijjil, Iba haro zobuti? hoi.
RUT 2:6 Tehon zimmadare hoil: Iba Muabiya zobuti, ze Naumir fũwati Muab dešottu aišše.
RUT 2:7 Hibaye ãttu fusargoijjil, meherbanigori fošol haṛoya okkolor fise fise zai kuṛattu giudanar sóra feṛai loifaijjum ne hoi. Hiba binna loti ehon foijjonto eṛe ase; bana ekkenagori góror butore aiššil edde zirail.
RUT 2:8 Toi Buaz Rutore hoil: Fun; oh ãr maya fuwa, tui giudana feṛaito oinno ketot no zais, ei ketottu no zaisgoi, ãr zobuti bandi okkolor fũwati eṛe tak.
RUT 2:9 Fošol haṛoya okkol zeṛe fošol haṛibo hikka diyan raki tui bandi okkolor fise fise zais. Tor gat hat no defan ãi zobuk okkolore hoidir. Ar fanir tirašlagile tui oi górar hãse zai, zobuk okkole ze fani tuli raikke henttu fihaisgoi.
RUT 2:10 Henot hibaye meṛit sojida fori tare salam gori hoil: Ãi boideši, õne ãre eto faṭṭa dor, õnor sarme ãi ei doya kiyottu failamde?
RUT 2:11 Buaze zuwab dil: "Tor šuwami mori bade tui tor horire zendilla goijjios edde nizor ma bab, zormostan sari ek osin zatir hãse aiššos, he šob hota beggun ãi fuinni.
RUT 2:12 Mabude tore, tui zin goijjos hinor enam dok; He Israilor Allah, Mabudor fakor nise zehon tui assoro loito aiššos, hibaye tore furafuri bafe enam dok."
RUT 2:13 Hibaye Buazore hoil: "Oh ãr malik, õne ãre rahamotor nozore so; õnor ei bandire šantona dila edde šantir hota hoila, zodi o ãi õnor bandi okkolor laikka no."
RUT 2:14 Tarfore hána háibar ṭaim zẽtte oil Buaze hibare hoil: Tui eṛe ai ruṭi hagai, tor ruṭir ṭukura rošot burai lo. Bade hibaye fošol haṛoya okkolor ḍakottu boiššil, ar Buaze hibare baijja dana dil. Toi hibaye feṭbori hána háil. bade aro hodun basitaigilgoi.
RUT 2:15 Bade hiba giudana feṛaito zehon uṛil, Buaz tar mainšore hokum dil: Hibare dolagoijjattu feṛailoito do, edde hibare hũnki no diba hoi.
RUT 2:16 Oh, tũwara hodun giudanar tarattu ṭani hiballa raki do, zene hiba feṛailoi fare, ar honokiye hibare dõk no diba.
RUT 2:17 Ar hibaye hazinna foijjonto he ketot giudana feṛail. Bade hibar feṛaiya giudana hinore baijjaiore onumanik ek ari foijjonto giudana oil.
RUT 2:18 Bade hibaye hin tuliloi šohorot uwafes firigilgoi. Horiye hibar feṛaiya giudanar bosta dekil; ar Rute basitakkilde he hánagun o hibar fũwati loiannil, ar hinore hibar horir munttu niyolaidil.
RUT 2:19 Tehon horiye hibare hoil: Tui aijjia hoṛe feṛaios? Hoṛe ham goijjos? Ze tor mikka rahamotor nozor diye, Allah tare rahamot gorok. Tehon hibaye har hãse ham goijje, hin horire zanail. Hibaye endilla hoil: Ze manušwar hãse aijjia ãi ham goijji tar nam Buaz.
RUT 2:20 Henot Naumi hibar futor boure hoil: Tare rahamot gorok he Mabude ze doya deha bondogori no fele zinda edde mora okkolor uwore. Naumi aro hoil: Hite ãrar egena, ãrare dehašuna goribar zimma asede tarar butorottu ekzon.
RUT 2:21 Ar Muabiya Rute hoil: Te ãre endilla o hoiye, ãr šomosto fošol daiya šeš no o foijjonto tui ãr mainšor fũwati fũwati takis.
RUT 2:22 Tehon Naumi hibar futor boure hoil: Mare, oinno honokiyor ketot, tore honokiye zalafura gori no farefan, tar hamor mayafuwaindor fũwati fũwati takon tolla bala oibo.
RUT 2:23 Toi fošol daiya šeš no o foijjonto, hibaye giudana feṛaibolla Buazor hamor mayafuwaindor fũwati fũwati takil edde hibar horir fũwati bošobaš goijil.
RUT 3:1 Ek din Naumiye Rutore hodde: Oh zi! Ãi tolla ki ekkan gór sešta no goijjum zene tui šuk fos?
RUT 3:2 Fun! Tui ze Buazor bandi okkolor fũwati aššili, hite ki ãrar egena no ne? Sa, hite aziya raitta hõlat giudana uraibo
RUT 3:3 Tui ga du edde kušbo tel bebargor, ar tor šundoijjia hoor findi oi hõlat za, kintu tar há fiya šeš no o foijjonto tui tare tor foriso no dis.
RUT 3:4 Te zẽtte neiṭṭo zaibo, tehon tui tar bisana otgori rakibi. Bade heṛe zaiore tui tar saddorgan ṭengor uwottu atorgorifelai heṛe neṛizaibigoi. Ar ki goraforibo hin te tore hoibo.
RUT 3:5 Hibaye zuwabe hoil: Tũi zen hor, hin beggun ãi goijjum.
RUT 3:6 Bade hiba oi hõlat lamigil edde hibar horiye zendilla hokum dil, he mozin hibaye beggun goijjil.
RUT 3:7 Buaz há fiya gorifelail edde tar mondil kuši oil, te giudana ṭalor hãsat zai neiṭṭilgoi. Ar Rut aste aste zai tar ṭengor uwottu saddorgan algaifelail edde heṛe neiṭṭil.
RUT 3:8 Bade ada raittot maze Buaz somkiuṛiṭṭil edde faš bodolil. Ar so, ekzon beṛimanuš tar ṭengor ḍake neṛitaikke.
RUT 3:9 Toi hite fusar goijjil: Tui hon? Hibaye zuwabdil: Ãi tũwar bandi Rut. Tũi tũwar saddoror tole bandire assoro do, haron tũi ãr dehašuna goroya egenar buttotu ekzon.
RUT 3:10 Te hodde: Allar rahamot ok tor uwore, oh zi! Ei foijjonto tui ze fakka dilolade hiyan dehaiyos ehon hinottu aro beši fakka dilolade hiyan dehaili. Kiyollahoile tui tuwangor otóba gorib hono ḍoilla zobukor fise no zos.
RUT 3:11 Ehon tui, oh zi, ar no ḍorais. Tui zã hoibi ãi tolla hin beggun goijjium. Haron tui ze beši bala maya fuwa hiyan ãr farar manuš beggune zane.
RUT 3:12 Ar ãi tor dehašuna goroya egenar buttotu ekzon hiyan soiyi, kintu ãttu aro hãsor ar ekzon egena ase.
RUT 3:13 Tui aijjia raittia eṛe tak. Binna zodi te tor dehašunar bar lo, toile hite hen gorok, ar zodi hite tor dehašunar bar no lo, toile zinda Mabudor hosom gori hoir, ãi tor dehašunar bar loiyum; binna no o foijjonto tui eṛe neṛitak.
RUT 3:14 Tarfore Rut binna fozor o foijjonto tar ṭengor ḍake neṛitakkil, edde ekzone ekzonore sini no farede hendilla andar takite hiba neṛattu uṛigilgoi, haron Buaze hibare hoil: Hõlat ze ekzon maya fuwa aišše hiyan honokiye no zana foribo.
RUT 3:15 Te aro hoil: Tor gar šallan loi ikka ai edde hiyanore tor munttu gori dor. Ar hibaye šallanore munttu gori doril, toi te so barang giudana mafi hibar matar uwore tulidil. Toibade hite šohoror uzu gilgoi.
RUT 3:16 Bade Rut zehon hibar horir hãse aigilgoi, hibaye fusargoijjil: Ken ken oil, oh zi? Henot hibaye beggun kulasagori hoil, Buaze hibare zen zen goijje.
RUT 3:17 Hibaye horire aro hoil: Te ãre horir hãse halihate no zais hoi ei giudana so barang in ãre diye.
RUT 3:18 Ei hota funi Naumi hoil: Tui sofor gor, oh zi, šeše hondilla o sasena! Aijjia iyanore hono šabišto no oite te no tamibo.
RUT 4:1 Bade Buaz ṭaun-geiṛot zai heṛe boiššilgoi. Ar so, ze dehašuna goroya egenar hota Buaze hoil te hehon henttu aiššil. Buaze tare, Oh, folona omuk hoi ḍakdil edde hoil: "Eṛe aio, boiyogai." Toi te fottottu ai boššilgai.
RUT 4:2 Bade Buaze došzon bura murubbi okkolore ḍaki hoil: Onora eṛe boio. Toi tara o aiyore boššilgai.
RUT 4:3 Buaze he dehašuna goroya egena hitare hodde: Naumi Muab dešottu firi aišše, hibaye ãrar egena Elimelekor zobingan besito sar.
RUT 4:4 Hetolla ãi bafilam ei befargan tũwarare zanaon dorhar. Eṛe zara aišše tarar sarme edde ãr zatir bura murubbi okkolor sarme tũi hiyan kinilo. Tũi zodi zobingan surailoito so, toile surailoifelo. Ar zodi tũi no loito so toile ãre ho, haron hiyan surailoibar odihar beggunor age tũwar, ar tũi bade ãr. Tarbade he dehašuna goroya egenaye hodde: Ṭik ase, ãi hiyan surailoium.
RUT 4:5 Henot Buaze hoil: Tũi ze din he zobingan Naumir hãsottu kiniloiba, hedin tũwattu Rut, he Muabiya rarire o gosaforibo, zene mora manušwar odihare, tar nam edde tar zobinor mirazdar take.
RUT 4:6 Ei hota funi oi dehašuna goroya egenaye hodde: Ãi henoile hiyan surailoi no faijjum, hen goillye ãr nizor fuwaindor miraz nošto gorifelayifan oibo. Ãr zagat tũi surailo, haron ãi surailoi nofarir.
RUT 4:7 Surailowa edde besa-kina in okkol age Israil dešot endilla rosom aššil ze hota fakka goribolla ekzonor ṭengor zuta ar ekzonore dito, ei bafe boni-Israil hono hamor goba goitto.
RUT 4:8 Toi oi dehašuna goroya egena hite Buazore: Hiyan tũi kinilogoi, hoi te tar ṭengor zuta kulidil.
RUT 4:9 Tehon Buaze bura murubbi edde heṛe aiššilde tara beggunore hoil: Ãi Naumir hãsottu Elimelek, Kilion edde Mahlonor šomosto šombotti kiniloilam, aijjia tũwara hinor goba oila.
RUT 4:10 Zene morar nam tar afon báiyaindor edde farattu buzi no zagoi, edde he šombottittu mirazdar okkole miraz fa, ar he mora manušwar odihare tar nam uddar goribolla ãi ãr bou hisabe Muabiya hoinnia Rut, Mahlonor boure kobul gorilam. Tũwara aijjia ei šomostor goba oila.
RUT 4:11 Toi heṛe ṭaun-geiṛor butore zara boiššil, tara šoho bura murubbi okkole hoil: Oi, ãra goba oilam. Ze maya fuwa tũwar górot aiyer hibare Mabude Rahela edde Leyar ḍoilla gora ok, zarar duwara šomosto boni-Israil lami aišše. Ar Eferatot tũwar kamiyaf ok edde Betlehemot tũwar nam mošur ok.
RUT 4:12 Mabud he zobutir feṛottu ze fuwain tũware dibo, tarar butottu di tũwar bongšo zen Tamaror feṛot Ehudar fuwa Ferošor bongšor ḍoilla o.
RUT 4:13 Bade Buaz Rutore biyagoril edde Rut tar bou oil. Buaz hibar hãse gil, toi Mabud Rutor feṛot fuwa dil edde hibattu ekzon morod fuwa oil.
RUT 4:14 Bade mayafuwain okkole Naumire hoil: Allare šukuriya, Tãi aizo tũware dehašuna goroya egenattu siri nofele. Ei fuwar nam boni-Israilor maze mošur ok.
RUT 4:15 Ite tũwar foranore abar tottoza gori tulibo edde tũwar bura boyošot tũwar deha šuna goribo, haron tũwar futor boue tũware adorgore, hibaye biyayede fuwa, ze tũwalla hãt futottu aro barik.
RUT 4:16 Bade Naumi gura morod fuwaware kulot loil edde tare lalon falon gora šuru goijjil.
RUT 4:17 Bade Naumiye ekzon morod fuwa faiye! En hoi ḍen gór bam górjjiya okkole tar nam rakil. Tara tar nam rakkil Obed. Obed aššilde Yašir bab, Yašir aššilde Daudor bab.
RUT 4:18 In oilde Ferošor hãndan okkolor nam: Ferošor fuwa Hešron,
RUT 4:19 Hešronor fuwar nam Ram, edde Ramor fuwa Omminadab,
RUT 4:20 Omminadabor fuwa Nahušon, Nahušonor fuwa Salmon,
RUT 4:21 Salmonor fuwa Buaz, Buazor fuwa Obed,
RUT 4:22 Obedor fuwa Yasir, Yasiror fuwa Daud.
JON 1:1 Mabudor kalam Amittaior fut Yunusor heṛe aišše, hodde:
JON 1:2 "Uṭ, he moha šohor, Ninivit za, ar hiyanor berudde guzori zanai degoi ze hitarar naformani ãr sarme aišše."
JON 1:3 Kintu Yunus nobi uzan Allar munttu atoroi zaibolla toiyaroil. Tãi Zaffa šohoror bondorot, Toršišot zaibo hendilla ekkan zahaz fail. Hetunot Allar munttu daizaiboilla zahazor bara di zahazor serainga okkolor fũwati Toršišot zaibolla he zahazot uṭṭil.
JON 1:4 Kintu Mabud doriyat zur bataš melamajjil edde doriyat en tuwan bail ze tuwane zahazsan bangizaibar alamot oil.
JON 1:5 Henšomot zahazor serainga okkole ḍorail, fottikiye tarar nizor nizor devotar hãse handahaṛi gora šuru goillio. Ar uzon homaibolla zahazor malfottro okkol doriyat felai dilo. Kintu Yunus nobi zahazor khulot lammilgoi edde heṛe neṛi bári gumot aššil.
JON 1:6 Tehon zahazor keptine tãir hãse ai hoil: Oh! Tũi ze gumzor, tũwattu ki oiye? Uṛo, tũwar devotare ḍako; oitfare tũwar devotaye ãrar befare sinta goribo toi ãra ar dongšo no oiyum.
JON 1:7 Tarfore zahazor serainga okkol tara ekzone ekzonore hodde: Aiyo ãra loṭari baṛi, toi zanifarium har duše ãrar kubaigio or. Bade tara loṭari baṛil, ar Yunusor name loṭari uṭṭil.
JON 1:8 Hetunot tara fusar goijjil: Tũi ãrare ho, har duše ãrattu kubaigio or? Tũwar ham ki? Tũi hontu aiššode? Tũi hon dešor manuš? Hon zatir manuš?
JON 1:9 Tãi tarare hoil: Ãi ekzon Ibroni; ãi Mabudore ḍorai, tãi behostor Allah, tãi doriyare edde fuwana zobinore banaiye.
JON 1:10 Hetunot he manuš okkole beši ḍorail edde tãire hoil: Tũi in ki goror? Yunus Allar sarmottu daizargoide hehota tara zainto, haron tãi tarare zanail.
JON 1:11 Doriya ošantir uwore ošanti oi gilgoi, hetolla tara tãire hodde: Ãra tũware ki gorile doriya ãralla šanti oibo?
JON 1:12 Tãi tarare hoil: Ãre dori doriyat felido, toi doriya tũwaralla nizam oi zaiboi; haron ãi zani, ãr duše tũwarar uwore ei bári tuwan munttu aišše.
JON 1:13 Tarfore o oi manuš okkole zahaz firaiore kulsuwaibolla darba šuru goijjil; kintu tara nofaril, haron doriya ulda taralla utaltal oi gilgoi.
JON 1:14 Ei harone tara Yunusor Mabudore ḍaka šuru goijjil, ar hoil: Oh Mabud, aroz gorir, ei manušwar foranollabuli ãrare dongšo no goijjio, ãrar uwore nidušir roktor dai no goijjio; haron, oh Mabud tũi tũwar issa mote ham goijjio.
JON 1:15 Bade tara Yunus nobire dóri doriyar fanit felaidil, tehon doriyar tuwan tamigilgoi.
JON 1:16 Henot oi manuš okkole Allare beši ḍora šuru goillio. Ar tara Mabudor mutallek kurbani gorilo edde manoš goillio.
JON 1:17 Ar Mabud Yunus nobire gilifelaibolla uggwa bor mas ṭik gori rakkil. He masor feṛot Yunus nobi tin din tin rait aššil.
JON 2:1 Tehon Yunus oi masor feṛottu tai Allah Mabudor hãse munazat goijjil, tãi hoil:
JON 2:2 Mabud, ãi tũware bifodot ḍakilam ar tũi ãr ḍak funila; ãi hoboror murottu tai tũware ḍakilam, ar tũi ãr foriyad funila.
JON 2:3 Tũi ãre mur fanit doriyar bukot felaidila, zeṛe sairo mikka fani, tũwar har goiror fanir zalazontrona ãr uwottu guzorigilgoi.
JON 2:4 Ãi hoilam, ãre tũwar nozoror tolottu dure loi za oiye, ãi ki tũwar fobitro dórmogóror uzu hono din suk tuli sai no faijjum neki?
JON 2:5 Doriyar faniye ãre giridoijje, foran foijjonto zar zar oiye, doriyaye ãre sairomikkattu giridoijje, ãr matat heṛiyar fezalota okkol beraiye.
JON 2:6 Ãi ḍufizaiore faharor gura foijjonto gilamgoi, ãr fise duniyair doroza sirohalolla ṭalamara oiye, tarfore o, oh ãr Allah Mabud, tũi ãr foranore morattu uwafes tuli anila.
JON 2:7 Ãr foran zẽtte zarzar oiye, hẽtte ãi Mabudore monot goillam, ãr munazat tũwar hãse, tũwar fobitro kaba górot fõssil.
JON 2:8 Zara misa devdevire fũze, tara tarar asol muhabbotottu durezagoi.
JON 2:9 Kintu ãi tũwar namor tarif šoho kurbani goriyum; ãi ze manoš goijji hiyan furon goriyum; ar uddar gora šudu Mabudor ham.
JON 2:10 Bade Mabud he masore hokum dil, ar he mase Yunus nobire fuwana zagar uwore hogori bairgoridil.
JON 3:1 Bade Mabudor kalam Yunus nobir uwore dusorabar naziloil.
JON 3:2 Tãi hoil; Tũi uṛo, he moha šohor, Ninivit zo, ãi tũware zin hoito hoir, hin he šohorot guzori hoidogoi.
JON 3:3 Toi Yunus nobi Mabudor hokum mozin Nineveh šohorot gil. Allar nozdikot ekkan ḍõr šohor, hiyanor ek ḍakottu ar ek ḍake zaite tin din lagito.
JON 3:4 Bade Yunus nobi šohorot za šuru gori ekdinor fot foijjonto fõsil, tehon tãi guzori hoil: Ar sališ din bade Nineveh dongšo oi zaiboi.
JON 3:5 Tehon Nineveh šohoror manuš okkole Allare biššaš goijjil. Tara ruza elan goijjil, edde tara šoṛo ḍõr beggune salaršoṭ findil.
JON 3:6 Ar he hóbor zehon Ninevir badšar hãse fõsil, te o tar šingašonottu uṛi tar razfušak kulifelail edde salaršoṭ findi saior uwore boiššil.
JON 3:7 Ar te edde tar raz hormosari okkolor hokume ei hotagun guzori elan goridil: Manuš otóba fošu, goru sool honokiyo kissu no hok, tara hána fani mukot nodok.
JON 3:8 Kintu manuš edde zanuwar tara salaršoṭ findi zoto šombob Allare ḍakok. Ar fottikiye nizor nizor kufot edde kuhamottu firi aiyok.
JON 3:9 Oitofare, Allah hantaoibo, ar monfiraibo edde tãir zolonto gušša hom goribo, ar ãra dongšo no oiyum.
JON 3:10 Hetunot Allah tarar ham, tara ze zar zar kufotottu mon firaiyede deki, Allaye tarar uwore ze dongšo ḍakianibo hoil henttu mon firail, ar hen no gore.
JON 4:1 Henot Yunus nobi moha narazoil edde guššaoil.
JON 4:2 Tãi Mabudor hãse munazat gori hoil: Ya Mabud, in no neki ãi ãr nizor dešot takite hoilamde? Hetollana ãi toratori foilabar Toršišot daizaiboilla gilamgoide; haron ãi zaintam, tũi rahamoti edde doyaban Allah, aste gušša oya edde oṭol muhabbote mohan, ar šasti mafgoridite toiyar.
JON 4:3 Hetolla ehon, o Mabud, foriyadgorir ãttu ãr foran horifelo kiyollahoile ãi zinda takattuwaro moron bala oibo.
JON 4:4 Mabude hodde: Tui gušša oiosde ki bala oil?
JON 4:5 Hẽtte Yunus nobi šohoror baire fuke ek zagat boiṛa aššil. Heṛe tãi nizolla ekkan zuguṛi baša banai heṛe tole sabat boiaššil, šohoror ki doša o hin saibar ofekkat.
JON 4:6 Mabud Allah uggwa beronggas fuṛail; ar he gasore ḍõr gori Yunus nobir uwore annil, zene tãir matar uwore gasor sába o, edde tãittu biyaram no lage. Ar Yunus nobi he beronggasswa loi beši kuši oil.
JON 4:7 Kintu tarfordin beil uṛibar age Allah uggwa log defeṛail, he loge oi beronggassware haṛifelail, he harone beronggasswa fuaigilgoi.
JON 4:8 Bade zehon beil uṛil, Allaye fukali gorom bataš defeṛail, henot Yunus nobir matat endilla ze roid lagil, tãi beši durbol oi gilgoi, edde tãi moribolla foriyadgoijjil, hoil: Ãi zinda takattu aro moron bala oibo.
JON 4:9 Tehon Allah Yunus nobire hodde: Oi beronggas šomonde rag gorilide iyan ki soiyi oil? Tãi hoil: Oy, iyanor haron ase, ãi guššaye moitto sai.
JON 4:10 Allaye hodde: Tui ei beronggasolla honokissu no goros, ibare barai o no tulos, iba ek raite fuṭṭye edde ek raite mori gilgoi, tarfore o ei beronggasolla doya lager.
JON 4:11 Toile ãi ki Ninevir ei moha šohoror uwore doya no goijjum? Heṛe endilla ek lak kuri hazarottu aro beši manuš ase, zara ḍen hat bam hat forokgori no zane; aro bout beši zanuwar okkol ase.
MAR 1:1 Allar Fut, Isa Mosir kušir hóboror babute šuru,
MAR 1:2 Esaiyah nobir kitabot iyan zendilla leka ase: "Sa, ãi tor age ãr hóborguware defeṛair, hite tor age zai tolla fõt saf goribo."
MAR 1:3 "Bošoti sara elehat ek abaze guzori zanai der, 'Tũwara Mabudor fõt ṭik goro, hibar rasta uzu goro.'"
MAR 1:4 He mozin torikotor gusol doya Yahyaye bošoti sara elehat hazir oiye edde guna maf faibolla gunattu mon firaito edde torikotor gusol loito hoiye.
MAR 1:5 Ehudiya beggullattu edde Zeruzalemor hár kiye niyoliyore hibar hãse giye. Hitara hitarar guna okkolore šikar goijje edde Zordan halot hibattu torikotor gusol loiye.
MAR 1:6 Yahyaye uṛor kẽšor hoor findito edde kĩyailot ekkan samorar duwali takito, ar hibaye firing edde fahari modu háiyore zibon haṛaiye.
MAR 1:7 Hibaye endilla hoi tobolig goijje: "Ãi bade en ekzon aiyer ze ãttũwaro šoktiwala, edde ãi niyuriyore hibar zutar fita kúlidibar laikka o ãi no.
MAR 1:8 Ãi tũwarare fani loi torikotor gusol diyi, kintu hibaye tũwarare he Pak Ruh loi torikotor gusol dibo."
MAR 1:9 He šomot Isaye Galilor Nasarat farattu aišše, edde Yahyattu Zordan halot torikotor gusol loiye.
MAR 1:10 Hibaye fanittu uṛer mottor, asman fáṛi bag oiye edde dekedde Pak Ruh hoitoror ḍoilla oi hibar uwore lami aiyer.
MAR 1:11 Ar behostottu ei hota funa giye: "Tui ãr he adoijja Fut, tor uwore ãi kub kuši."
MAR 1:12 Iyar bade he Ruhuye hibare bošoti sara elehat loigiye,
MAR 1:13 ar hiba heṛe sališ din aššil edde šoitane dúha diye. Hiba heṛe fahari zanuwar okkolor fũwati aššil, edde hibare firista okkole šeba goijje.
MAR 1:14 Yahyare ziyolot diya oi bade, Isaye Galilot aišše edde Allar kušir hóbor tobolig goijje.
MAR 1:15 Hibaye hodde: "Ṭaim oiye, Allar raijjo tũwarar hãse aišše.Tũwara mon firo edde ei kušir hóbor biššaš goro."
MAR 1:16 Ek bar hibaye Galil doriyar hãsa bai gil, hen šomot hibaye Simon edde hitar bái Anderiyaze doriyat zal feledde deikke, kiyollahoile hitara aššilde zailla.
MAR 1:17 Isaye hodde, "Aiyo, ãr fisa lo, toi ãi tũwarare manuš doribar zailla banaiyum"
MAR 1:18 Hehon hitara hitarar zal okkol felai raki Isar fisa loiye.
MAR 1:19 Toi hentu ar hoddur mummikka zaiyore Sebdeusor futain Yakub edde hitar bái Yuhannare deikke, hitara not boiyore zal baz gorer.
MAR 1:20 Toi hitarare deki mottor hibaye ḍak diye, ar hitara hitarar baf Sebdeusore muzur okkolor fũwati not diyore bade itara Isar fisa loiye.
MAR 1:21 Tarfore hitara Kofornahumot aišše, toi bade zehon dórmo din oiye, Isaye sinagogot giye edde šikka diye.
MAR 1:22 Isar šikkat beggune tajjuf oiye, kiyollahoile hibaye alem okkolor ḍoilla gori šikka no de bolke hibaye hitarare kemota loi šikka diye.
MAR 1:23 Ehon, heṛe hitarar muzolišhanar butore bod ruhuye faiya ekzon manuš aššil. Hite ḍak mari hodde,
MAR 1:24 "Oh, Nasarator Isa, õne loi ãrar loi ki talukkat? Õne ki ãrare naš goitto aiššo? Ãi zani õne honnuwa, õne to Allar he Pak zon!"
MAR 1:25 Kintu Isaye hitare dõk diyore hodde,"Nizam o, ei manušwar butottu niyoli ai."
MAR 1:26 Toi he bod ruhuye manušware doro gori musori doijje edde zure guzori hitar butottu niyoli giyegoi.
MAR 1:27 Ei hanḍo deki beggune tajjuf oiye edde hitara nizor butore howahoi goijje edde hodde, "In ki? Ek noya šikka, kemota loi! Hibaye bod ruh okkolore hokum de, ar hitara hibar hota mane."
MAR 1:28 Toi hibar babute hóbor beši toratori Galil elehar hár mikka sorai giyegoi.
MAR 1:29 Bade hitara muzolišhanattu niyoli zaigoi mottor, hitara Simon edde Anderiyazor górot giye. Yakub edde Yuhanna o hitarar fũwati aššil.
MAR 1:30 Heṛe Simonor hori zor biyaram loi bisanat fori taikke. Isa aišše mottor hitara hiyan hibare hoiye.
MAR 1:31 Toi Isa hibar ḍake zaiyore hibare hate dori tuille, henot hibattu zor sari giyegoi, ar hibaye hitarare mehemandari goijje.
MAR 1:32 Beil ḍufigiyegoi edde hazinna oiye, manušzon okkole har biyaraimma okkolore edde bod ruhuye faiya manuš okkolore Isar hãse ainne.
MAR 1:33 ar šohor ṭĩya aiyore dorozar munttu dola oiye.
MAR 1:34 Isaye hár ḍoilla biyaraimma okkolore aram goijje edde bod ruh dafaiye. Kintu hibaye bod ruh okkolore hono hota hoito no de, kiyollahoile hiba Moside hiyan hitara zainto.
MAR 1:35 Tarforor din binna sore, andar takite Isaye uiṭṭe edde niyoli ekkan nirzon zagat giye, zeṛe hibaye duwa goijje.
MAR 1:36 Kintu Simon edde hitara Isare tuwaito giye,
MAR 1:37 toi hitara hibare tuwai faiyore hodde, "Beggune õnor talaš gorer!"
MAR 1:38 Isaye hitarare hodde, "Aiyo, ãra eṛiyar ate hãsor fara okkolot zai, zene ãi heṛe o tobolig gori fari, hiyanolla to ãi aiššiyi."
MAR 1:39 Toi hibaye Galilor hár mikka giye, sinagog okkolot šikka diye, edde bod ruh okkolore dafaiye.
MAR 1:40 Ek kurus biyaraimmaye Isar hãse aiyore hibar sarme fot uite fori foriyad goijje, "Õne issa gorile ãre foriškar gori fariba."
MAR 1:41 Manušwalla Isattu doya oiye, hat barai di hitare suiyore hodde, "Ãi sai, tũi foriškar o!"
MAR 1:42 Ar hehon hitattu kurus sari giyegoi edde hite foriškar oiye.
MAR 1:43 Isaye hitare hora gori nišod goijje edde en hoiyore hehon dũrai diye:
MAR 1:44 "Ei hota honokiyore no hois. Kintu zaiyore dórmiyo alem okkolore dehagoi, ar foriškar oi faijjosde hiyanolla Musar ain mozin kurbani gorgoi. Henot hitarar hãse tui foriškar oiyosde hiyanor forman oibo."
MAR 1:45 Kintu manušwaye zaiyore hár zagat ei hóbor en bafe sorai diye, ziyanor zoriya Isaye ar hono ekkan šohorot kulasa gori goli no fare, kintu baire nirzon zagat taikke. Tarfore o hár zagattu manuš okkol hibar hãse aišše.
MAR 2:1 Hoekdin bade, Isaye zehon abar Kofornahumot aišše, edde hiba górot asede funa giye.
MAR 2:2 Toi eto manuš dola oiye, dorozar bare udda ar zaga nu aššil. Hibaye hitarare kalam tobolig goijjede šomot,
MAR 2:3 ekzon ãtur biyaraimmare loi hoekzon manuš hibar hãse aišše, manušware sairzone boi ainne,
MAR 2:4 kintu zamila buli hitara hitare Isar hãse loizai no fare, hetolla Isa zeṛe aššil he borabor hitara góror salor uwore uiṭṭe edde ekkan fõt goijje, ar ze bisanar uwore ãtur biyaraimmawa aššil, hiyanor uwore gori hitare nise lamai diye.
MAR 2:5 Hitarar biššaš dekiyore, Isaye he ãtur manušware hodde, "Fuwa, tor guna okkol maf gora oiye."
MAR 2:6 Heṛe hoekzon alem boiṛa aššil edde hitara nize nize bafa šuru goijje,
MAR 2:7 "Ei manušwaye endilla kiyolla hor? Hite kuferi gorer, šude Allah bade ar honokiye guna maf gori di no fare?"
MAR 2:8 Hitara in okkol bafedde Isaye hibar dilor butore hehon buzi faijje, edde hibaye hitarare hodde,"Tũwara dilot hendilla kiyolla sinta goror?
MAR 2:9 Ei ãtur biyaraimmare honnan howa asan oibo, 'tor guna maf gora oiye', ne naki 'tui uṭ, tor bisana lo edde aṭ'?
MAR 2:10 Kintu duniyait guna maf gori dibar kemota Adomor fuwattu ase, hiyan zene tũwara zani faro." Hen hoi Isaye he leng manušware hodde,
MAR 2:11 "Ãi tore hoir, uṭ, bisana tuli loiyore gór zagoi."
MAR 2:12 Hetunot hite uṛi hitar bisana tuli loiye edde beggunor sarmottu baire niyoli giyegoi. Henot beggune tajjuf oiye edde hitara Allar tarif goriyore hodde, "Ãra endilla ar hono oktot no deki."
MAR 2:13 Isaye abar niyoliyore doriyar farot giye, heṛe beši manuš okkol hibar hãse aišše, toi hibaye hitarare šikka diye.
MAR 2:14 Tarfore hibaye fõt bai zat maze dekedde Alfeyusor fuwa Levi hazna adai gorede zagat boiṛa, Isaye hitare hodde, "Ãr fisa lo" Toi Leviye uiṭṭe edde hibar fisa loiye.
MAR 2:15 Tarfore Isaye hitar górot gorba giye, ar heṛe bout hazna adaigoroya okkol edde gunagar manuš okkol, Isa edde hibar sahabi okkolor fũwati hánar ṭebilot boišše, kiyollahoile boute aššil zara hibar fisa loil.
MAR 2:16 Foroši dolor alem okkole zehon Isa hazna adaigoroya edde gunagar manuš okkolor fũwati hána hadde deikke, hitara sahabi okkolore hodde, "Hibaye hazna adaigoroya edde gunagar okkolor fũwati kiyolla hána hár?"
MAR 2:17 Isaye ei hota fuinne edde hitarare hodde, "Araimma mainšottu ḍakṭoror dorhar nai, kintu biyaraimma mainšottu dorhar ase. Ãi forhesgar okkolore no, kintu gunagar okkolore ḍakito aišši."
MAR 2:18 Foroši okkole edde Yahyar šagirit okkole ruza rakkil. Toi hoekzone Isar hãse aiyore fusar goijje, "Foroši edde Yahyar šagirit okkole ruza rake, kintu õnor sahabi okkole kiyolla hen no gore?"
MAR 2:19 Isaye hitarare hodde, "Dula fũwati taite kengori dular fũwajja okkole ruza raki faribo? Dula zetodin hitarar fũwati ase, hitara ruza raki no faribo.
MAR 2:20 Kintu en šomoi aiyer, zẽtte hitarar hãsottu dulare loi zaiboi, edde toi he dinot hitara ruza rakibo."
MAR 2:21 "Honokiye furan kurutat noya horor tali no sila. Kiyollahoile, he furan kurutattu noya taligan siri aibo, ar henot hanagan aro ḍõr oibo.
MAR 2:22 Ar furan samorar hoillat honokiye tottoza šoraf no ḍale, kiyollahoile ḍalile šorafgune hoillagunore o fuṛaifelaibo, henot šoraf edde hoilla dunigun borbat oi zaiboi. No, tottoza šoraf noya samorar hoillat!"
MAR 2:23 Hono ek dórmor din Isaye fõtot hono ek gĩyuketi bai gil, ar hibar sahabi okkole ãṛi zat maze giyũrdanar sora sijje.
MAR 2:24 Henot Foroši okkole hodde, "So, ain mozin dórmor din zin gora mana hitara hin kiyolla gorer?"
MAR 2:25 Hibaye hitarare hodde: "Daud edde hibar fũwajja okkolottu zehon buk laggil edde haiddor obaf aššil hẽtte hibaye ki goijje, hin tũwara honodin no foro?
MAR 2:26 Obiyator ḍõr imam aššilde ṭaimot, hibaye Allar górot goillil edde sarme rakkilde ruṭi háil, zin šude imam okkol sara ar honokiye háibar mana aššil. Hibaye aro hibar sãti okkolore o dil."
MAR 2:27 Isaye hitarare aro hodde, "Manušolla dórmodin gora oiyede, kintu dórmor dinolla manuš gora no o.
MAR 2:28 Hetolla Adomor Fut oilde dórmogóror uwore o malik."
MAR 3:1 Hiba abar sinagogot góille, ar heṛe ekzon hat mozigiyegoide manuš aššil.
MAR 3:2 Dórmor din Isaye hitare aram gore ne naki no gore hiyan saibolla hodune hibar uwore bala gori nozor raikke, toi zene hitara hibar berudde hosuri di fare.
MAR 3:3 He hat mozigiyegoide manušware Isaye hodde, "Uṛi beggunor munttu ai tiya!" Henot hite uṛi tiyaiye.
MAR 3:4 Toi hibaye hitarare fusar goredde: "Dórmor din ki gora ezajot ase? Bala ham gora ne naki horaf ham gora? Foran basa ne naki foran dongšo gora?" Kintu hitara nizam mari taikke.
MAR 3:5 Isaye hitarar sairo mikka gušša gori saiye edde hitarar dil dorode dekiyore hibar dilor beši murot ferešan oiye, edde manušware hodde, "Tor hattan mum mikka ṭan." Hite hen goijjebar hitar hattan ekkubare bala oi giyegoi.
MAR 3:6 Hetunot Foroši okkol baire giye edde Isare kene marifela za he babute Herudor dolor loi felain goijje.
MAR 3:7 Isaye sahabi okkolore fũwati loi lamat doriyar hãsat giye edde Galilottu ek ḍõr mainšor dole hibar fisa loiye.
MAR 3:8 Ar Ehudiyattu, Zeruzalemottu edde Idumiyattu, Zordanor dusora farottu edde Tiros edde Sidon elehar sairo mikkar zaga okkolottu beši manuš okkol, hibaye ze hár ham okkol goijje hin funiyore hibar hãse aišše.
MAR 3:9 Toi hibaye sahabi okkolore hiballa ekkan no ṭik gori rakito hoiye, zene mainše hibare suibolla ṭelaṭeli gori hibar uwore no foregai.
MAR 3:10 Kiyollahoile hibaye bout manuš okkolore aram goijjil, hetolla biyaraimma okkole hibare suibolla mummikka ṭelaṭeli goijje.
MAR 3:11 Napak ruh okkole zẽtte hibare dekito, hibar sarme meṛi uite fori guzori hoito, "Õne Allar Fut."
MAR 3:12 Kintu hibaye hitarare kub hora gori hokum dito, zene hiba honnuwa hiyan hitara honokiyore no ho.
MAR 3:13 Tarfore hiba faharot uiṭṭegoi edde nizor issaye kissu manušore ḍaikke. Ar hitara hibar hãse giye.
MAR 3:14 Hibaye barozonore asab basona goijje zene hitara hibar fũwati fũwati take edde hibaye hitarare toboligot defeṛai fare,
MAR 3:15 edde bod ruh dafaibolla šokti fa.
MAR 3:16 Ze barozonore basi loiye hitara oilde: Simon (Zare hibaye Fitor nam diye.)
MAR 3:17 Sebudiyusor dui fuwa Yakub edde Yuhanna, (ar ei duizonore hibaye nam diye Buwanerges, zar mani ṭaṛalor futain)
MAR 3:18 Anderiyaz, Filip, Bartolomeus, Moti, Tomas, Alfeyusor fuwa Yakub, Táddeyus, Simon Zelot,
MAR 3:19 Edde Ehudah Iskariyot, ze Isa loi beimani goijje.
MAR 3:20 Tarfore zehon hiba górot aišše, abar manuš okkol dola oiye, hetolla hiba edde hibar sahabi okkole kissu hái no fare.
MAR 3:21 Isar nizor manuš okkole ei hóbor faiyore hibare henttu niyolai loi aišše. Hitara hodde, "Iba fool oigiyegoi."
MAR 3:22 Zeruzalemottu aiššede alem okkole hodde, "Hitar butore Belsebul ase! Butor raza Belsebulor modote ite but bair gore."
MAR 3:23 Toi Isaye hitarare hibar hãse ḍaikke edde hitarare mesal kahani okkol loi hota hoiye: "Šoitane kengori Šoitanore dafai faribo?
MAR 3:24 Zodi raijjo ekkan nizor butore bag o, hiyan ṭiki tai no fare.
MAR 3:25 Abar, zodi ekkan gór nizor butore bag o, toile he górgan o ṭiki tai no fare.
MAR 3:26 Ar ehon, zodi šoitane hitar nizor berudde tiya edde hitar nizor butore bag o, toile hite ṭiki tai no faribo. Hite heddurot šeš.
