LUK 1:31 Ar fun! Tui hamil oibi edde tottu ek futore biyaibi, ar hibar nam rakibi Isa.
LUK 1:32 Hiba mohan oibo, hibare šorbo šoktiwalar fut ḍaka oibo. Allah Mabude hibar baf Daudor šingašon hibare dibo.
LUK 1:33 Yakubor bongšor uwore hibaye abadul abad razagiri goribo, ar hibar razagiri hono din šeš no oibo."
LUK 1:34 Moriyame firistare hodde, "En ken gori oi faribo? Ãi aizo kumari?"
LUK 1:35 Firistaye zuwabe hibare dedde, "Pak Ruh tor uwore aibo, edde šorbo šoktiwalar šokti tor uwore saiya oibo. Hetolla ze paki zon zormo oibo hibare Allar Fut ḍaka oibo.
LUK 1:36 Ar sa, tor egena Elizabet, hibattu o ei bura boyošot ek fut feṛot oiye. Hiba zare bázá hoito, hibattu iyan so mašor san.
LUK 1:37 Kiyollahoile Allattu ošombob kissu nai."
LUK 1:38 Moriyame hodde, "So, ãi Mabudor bandi, tũwar hota mozin ãr uwore har kissu ok." Tarfore he firista Moriyamor henttu giyegoi.
LUK 1:39 Hotodin bade Moriyame toratori gori Ehudiya elehar ek fahari farat giye,
LUK 1:40 zeṛe Zakariya take. Hiba heṛe Zakariyar górot góille edde Elizabet loi mulot oiye.
LUK 1:41 Elizabete zehon Moriyamor abaz fuinne hetunot hibar feṛor fuwaye fal mari uiṭṭe. Ar Elizabet he Pak Ruhuye furon oiye edde
LUK 1:42 zure ḍak mari hodde: "Har nari okkolor butore tore rahamot, ar rahamot ze fuwa tor gorbot ase.
LUK 1:43 Iyan ki bafe oi fare, ãr Malikor mattu ãr hãse aiya foijje?
LUK 1:44 Ãi zẽtte tor abaz funilam hẽtte ãr gorbot ãr fuwaye kušiye fal mari uiṭṭe.
LUK 1:45 Ar rahamot tore, tui biššaš goijjos, ar hetolla tor babute Mabude zen hoiye, hen furon oibo!"
LUK 1:46 Hetunot Moriyame hodde: "Ãr forane Malikor šanor tarif gorer!
LUK 1:47 ar ãr ruh ãr basailoya Allare loi kušiye ullaš,
LUK 1:48 kiyollahoile hibaye ei nihait gorib bandir uwore nozor diye. Ar so, ehonottu loti hár mainše ãre mubarak hoibo.
LUK 1:49 kiyollahoile hiba, he Šoktiwalaye ãlla beši ḍõr ham okkol goijje, paki oilde hibar nam.
LUK 1:50 hibar doya bongšor bade bongšolla, zara Hibare ḍorar.
LUK 1:51 Allaye nizor ḍũwa loi ḍõr šoktir ham goijje. Zarar nizor dilot ohonkare bora, hitarare Allaye šiṛa šitta gori felaiye.
LUK 1:52 Allaye šingašonottu raza okkolore lamai diye, kintu nisorgunore usolot goijje.
LUK 1:53 Zetarattu obaf ase, hitarare bala bala hána fani diye, kintu tuwangor okkolore hali hate bidai goijje.
LUK 1:54 Allaye ãrar fordada okkolor hãse ze wada dil, he mozin hibaye hibar gulam Israilore ufohar goijje.
LUK 1:55 Ibrahim edde hibar bongšor manuš okkolor uwore, abadul abad adorhatir goribar hota Allaye monot raikke."
LUK 1:56 Ar Moriyam maš tin maš Elizabetor górot taki bade nizor górot uwafes firi giyegoi.
LUK 1:57 Bade zehon Elizabete fuwa biyaibar din furon oiye, hibaye ek futore biyaiye.
LUK 1:58 ar hibar ḍen gór bam gójja edde egena okkole fuinne ze, Mabude hibare hoto ḍõr ador dehaiye, edde hitara hibar fũwati kuši goijje.
LUK 1:59 Ašṭo dinor din hitara fuware azomi goraito aišše, edde hibar bafor nam mozin hitara fuwar nam Zakariya rakito saiye,
LUK 1:60 kintu fuwar maye zuwabe hodde: "No, hitar nam Yahya raka oibo."
LUK 1:61 Hitara hibare hodde, "Tũwar egena okkolor butore hono kiyor nam to Yahya nai."
LUK 1:62 Bade hitara fuwar bafore išara gori hibattu zainto saiye fuwar nam ki rakito so hoi.
LUK 1:63 Zakariyaye ekkan lekibar silet maigge edde heṛe leikke: "Itar nam Yahya." Henot beggune ammuwak oiye.
LUK 1:64 Ar hehon Zakariyar muk kuligiyegoi edde zil eridiya oi giyegoi, toi hibaye Allare tarif gora šuru goijje.
LUK 1:65 Hen deki atehasor manuš okkol beggune beši ammuwak oiye. Henot ze hanḍo okkol goiṭṭe hinor babute Ehudiyar har fahari elehar manuš okkole howa hoi gora šuru goijje.
LUK 1:66 Mabudor hat ei fuwar uwore aššil buli zedune ei hota okkol fuinne hitara hin dilot raikke edde fusar goijje: "Ḍõr oile ei fuwa ki oibo?"
LUK 1:67 Hibar baf Zakariyaye he Pak Ruhuye furaiya oi nobi hisabe hota hoiye, hodde:
LUK 1:68 "Israilor Allah Mabudor tarif ok, kiyollahoile hibaye nizor mainšor uzu suk diye edde deha šunar bar loiye.
LUK 1:69 Allaye ãralla hibar gulam Daudor bongšottu ekzon šoktiwala basailoiya tuille.
LUK 1:70 (Ei wadare Allaye bout age hibar pak nobi okkolor muke howaiye.)
LUK 1:71 Dušmon okkolor edde zara ãrare hingša gore hitarar hatottu basaibo.
LUK 1:72 Allaye ãrar bafdadare doya dehaiye edde hibar paki wadare monot raikke,
LUK 1:73 he wadare hibaye ãrar baf, Ibrahimor hãse dil:
LUK 1:74 Hetolla ãra dušmon okkolor hatottu ḍor sara uddar oiyi, toi zene ãra zetodin basi, Allar sukor sarme
LUK 1:75 pak saf edde soiyi bafe Allar šeba gori fari.
LUK 1:76 Ar oh ãr fuwa, tore šorbo šoktiwalar nobi hoi ḍaka oibo, kiyollahoile tũi Malikor age age zaibi edde Malikor fõt ṭik goribi.
LUK 1:77 Edde Malikor manuš okkolore uddar sinaibi, hẽtte hitarar guna maf gora oibo,
LUK 1:78 kiyollahoile ãrar Allar doyaye boraiya. Uworwalar fohor beil uṛefan oibo ãrar uwore,
LUK 1:79 zara andarot edde morar sabat boi roiye, edde ãrare šantir fõtot solai fare."
LUK 1:80 Ar fuwawa bari uiṭṭe edde ruhuye mojbut oiye; Israili okkolor munttu aibar age foijjonto Yahya bošoti sara elehat maze zibon haṛaiye.
LUK 2:1 Hẽttiyaror din okkolot Rom dešor badša Agustusor hokum zari oiye, ze šara raijjor hár manuš okkolottu nam leka diya foribo.
LUK 2:2 Siriyar šašon goroya Kuronir ṭaimot ei foila bar manuš gona oiye.
LUK 2:3 Har mainše nam leka dibolla nizor nizor farat za šuru goijje.
LUK 2:4 Ar Yusuf aššilde badša Daudor bongšor manuš. Badša Daudor zormostan aššilde Ehudiya elehar Betlehem šohorot. Hetolla Yusuf o nam leka dibolla Galil elehar Nasarat farattu uwore Daudor šohor Betlehemot gil.
LUK 2:5 Moriyam, zar loi Yusufor biyar hotabattara ṭik oil, ar he šomot hiba hamil aššil, hibaye o Yusufor fũwati nam leka dibolla heṛe giye.
LUK 2:6 Hitara heṛe giyede šomot hibar fuwa halasi oibar ṭaim oiye.
LUK 2:7 Toi hibaye foila fuwa morod fuwa halasi goijje. Ar hibaye he fuware hoor berai di hanḍailot neṛai diye. Kiyollahoile hitaralla heṛe hiyan sara ar hono mikka takibar zaga no aššil.
LUK 2:8 Heṛe maṛot ḍakeduke hoekzon soolsoroya aššil, zara raitta soolor zãk fahara dil.
LUK 2:9 Ar Allar ek firista ai hitarar sarme hazir oiye. Toi Allar nuror tozolli sairo mikka oiye, henot soolsoroya okkole beši ḍoraiye.
LUK 2:10 Firistaye hitarare hodde, "No ḍoraiyo, kiyollahoile so, ãi tũwarare beši ḍõr kušir hóbor zanaito aišši; ei kuši hár manušolla oibo.
LUK 2:11 Kiyollahoile aziya Daudor šohorot tũwaralla ek basailoya zormo oiye; hiba oilde Mosi, Malik.
LUK 2:12 Ei hota soyide hiyanor sinno oilde, tũwara ek gura fuware hanḍailot hoor beraiya neṛaiya dekiba."
LUK 2:13 Bade atikka he firistar fũwati ek ḍõr firistar dol behostottu ai zug diye edde hitara beggune Allare ganor šure tarif gora šuru goijje:
LUK 2:14 "Uwore behostot Allar tarif ok, edde duniyait hibar manuš okkolor maze, zitarare loi Allah kuši hitarar uwore šanti ai ok!"
LUK 2:15 Firista okkol zehon hitarar henttu behostot giyegoi, soolsoroya okkole ekzone ekzonore hodde: "Aiyo, ãra Betlehem foijjonto zai, ze hota Allaye ãrare firistar duwara zanaiye hin saigoi."
LUK 2:16 Toi hitara toratori he zagat fõiššegoi, heṛe Moriyam edde Yusuf, hanḍailot neṛaiya he gura fuwar deha faiye.
LUK 2:17 Hitara he fuware deki bade he fuwar babute zin zin firistaye soolsoroya okkolore hoil hin hitara itarare zanai diye.
LUK 2:18 Ar zedun mainše soolsoroya okkolor hota fuinne, hitara beggune tajjuf oiye.
LUK 2:19 Kintu Moriyame he šob hota mone mone bafa šuru goijje edde hin nizor dilot gãti raikke.
LUK 2:20 Ar soolsoroya okkolore zendilla howa oil, hitara hendilla hár kissu deki funi Allare tarif edde šukuriya zaniye. Toi bade hitara henttu uwafes firi giyegoi.
LUK 2:21 Ašṭo din bade fuware azomi goraibar ṭaim oiye, ar hẽtte nam raka oiye Isa. Mar feṛot aibar age firistaye ei namman dil.
LUK 2:22 Bade zehon Musar šoriyotot mozin pak saf oibar ṭaim oiye. Toi Yusuf edde Moriyame gura fuwa Isare Mabudor sarme tiya goraibolla Zeruzalemot loigiye.
LUK 2:23 Zendilla Mabudor ainot leka ase, "Foila zormor har morodore Mabudor dora oibo."
LUK 2:24 Hin bade o hitara kurbani goitto giye, zendilla ainot kurbani dibar hota leka ase: "Ek zura faikor so otóba duwa hoitoror basa."
LUK 2:25 Hẽtte Zeruzalemot Simeon name ekzon dórmiyo edde allawala manuš aššil. Allaye hõtte Israil zatir dukkore dur goribo he ṭaimolla hibaye sai aššil. Pak Ruh hibar uwore aššil,
LUK 2:26 ar Pak Ruhur duwara hibare batelai diya oi ze, Malik Messiyare no dekite hibar mout no oibo.
LUK 2:27 Toi hiba Pak Ruhor išara faiyore dórmogórot aišše. Ar zehon ma bafe fuwa Isare ainor rosom mozin furon goribolla dórmogóror butore ainne.
LUK 2:28 Hetunot Simeone hibare fatarikula gori loiye edde Allar tarif gori hodde:
LUK 2:29 "Mabud, tũi tũwar kalam mozin tũwar gulamore ehon šanti gori bidai goijjo,
LUK 2:30 kiyolla buli hoile ãr dui suke tũwar uddarore dekilam,
LUK 2:31 ziyan tũi har zatilla bebosta goijjo.
LUK 2:32 Oihudi okkolor hãse forhaš oibar nur, ar tũwar zati Israilolla ijjot."
LUK 2:33 Hibar babute hoiyede hin okkolot fuwar baf edde ma tajjuf oiye.
LUK 2:34 Ar Simeone hitarare duwa goijje edde Isar mare hodde: "Sa, ei fuwaye Israilor butore boutore tole felaibo edde uwore tulibo, ar iba en ek sinno oibolla aišše zar bifokke boute matibo.
LUK 2:35 Henot hitarar monor sinta forhaš oi zaiboi. Hin bade o, Moriyam tor dilot surir agator ḍoilla duk oibo."
LUK 2:36 Ar heṛe Hanna name ekzon maya fuwa nobi aššil, hiba aššilde Ašar bongšor Panuwelor zi, hibar umor beši oil. Hiba zuwan hale hãt bosor zamair gór gori bade,
LUK 2:37 aši sair bosor umor o foijjonto rari boni takkil. Ar hiba dórmogórot ruza edde munazat loi dine raite Allar ebadotot fori takito. Hibaye dórmogór sari hono mikka no zaitogoi.
LUK 2:38 He šomot Hannaye o heṛe aiyore šukuriya adai gora šuru goijje edde zedun manuš Zeruzalem azadir entezarot aiššil, hitarare hibaye Isar babute hoiye.
LUK 2:39 Toi hitara Mabudor ain mozin hár kissu fura gori bade Galil elehat, hitarar nizor fara Nasaratot firi giyegoi.
LUK 2:40 Ar fuwawa bari uiṭṭe edde mojbut oiye, giyane furaiya oiye, edde Allar rahamot hibar uwore aššil.
LUK 2:41 Uddar idor šomot Isar ma bafe fotti bosor Zeruzalem zaito.
LUK 2:42 Toi hiba zẽtte baro bosor oiye, hẽtte hitara hitarar idor niyom mozin uwore Zeruzalem giye;
LUK 2:43 Toi idor din okkol šeš oi bade, hitara firi zargoide šomot, fuwa Isa fissa Zeruzalem tai giyegoi, ar hibar baf maye hiyan no zanito.
LUK 2:44 Isa mainšor fũwati maze ase mone gori ek dinor fõtor baisa foijjonto hitara ai giyegoi. Bade hitara hitarar egena edde sina funa manuš okkolottu Isar talaš gora šuru goijje.
LUK 2:45 Hitara zehon Isare tuwai no fa, hitara Isare tuwaibolla uwafes firi Zeruzalem giye.
LUK 2:46 Šeše, tin din bade hitara Isare dórmogórot tuwai faiye. Isaye heṛe alem okkolor maze boi hitarar hota funat aššil edde hitarare suwal fusar goijjil.
LUK 2:47 Zara Isar hota fuinne hitara Isar ahol deki edde zuwab funi beggune tajjuf oiye.
LUK 2:48 Isar baf maye Isare deki ammuwak oiye. Maye Isare hodde: "Oh fut, tũi ãrar loi en kiyolla goijjo? Tũwar baf edde ãi hoto suhara oi tũware tuwa šuru goijjilam."
LUK 2:49 Kintu Isaye hodde: "Tũwara kiyolla ãre talaš goijjila? Tũwara no zano ze ãttu ãr bafor górot taka foribo?"
LUK 2:50 Kintu Isaye hitarare ki hoiye hin hitara buzi no fare.
LUK 2:51 Tarfore Isa hitarar fũwati Nasarat uwafes firi giyegoi, edde baf mar hota mani soille. Isar maye in beggunore dilot gãti raikke.
LUK 2:52 Isa giyane edde boyoše bari uiṭṭe, Allah edde manušor adore.
LUK 3:1 Badša Ṭaiberiyar razagiri fundoro bosor soledde šommot, Ehudiya elehar govarnar aššilde Pontus Filat. Hẽtte Herud Galil elehar, ar hitar bái Filip, Ituriya edde Trakonitisor šašon goroya aššil. Ar Lusaniyas aššilde Abileniya elehar šašon goroya.
LUK 3:2 Annas edde Kaifas aššilde Ihudi okkolor ḍõr imam. Ṭik he šomot Allar kalam bošoti sara elehat maze Zakariyar fut Yahyar hãse aišše.
LUK 3:3 Ar hibaye Zordan giriyore asede hár zaga okkolot giye edde mon firaibar ek torikotor gusol tobolig goijje, ziyane guna okkolore maf diye,
LUK 3:4 Zendilla Esaiyah nobir kitabot iyan leka ase: "Bošoti sara elehat ek abaze guzori zanaider, 'Tũwara Mabudor fõt ṭik goro, hibar rasta uzu goro.
LUK 3:5 Har ḍeil okkol bora oibo, mura fahar fuwan gora oibo. Behã sura fõt fuwan gora oibo, bešoman rasta šoman gora oibo.
LUK 3:6 Ar hár mainše Allar uddar dekibo.'"
LUK 3:7 Beši manuš okkole Yahyattu torikotor gusol loibolla niyoli giye edde hibaye hitarare hodde: "Hafor dol okkol! Tũwarare Allar gozob lami aiyerde henttu dai zaibolla hũšiyar gori hone dilo?
LUK 3:8 Toile gunattu mon firaiyode hiyanor laikka gula dorai tũwarar zibonot deho. Mone mone howa šuru no goijjo ze, 'Ãrattu baf Ibrahim ase.' Kiyollahoile ãi tũwarare hoir, Allaye ei fattor okkolottu Ibrahimolla fuwain fodai gori fare.
LUK 3:9 Ar gasor gurat kuroil ehon loti lagaiya ase. Ze hono gas zibat bala gula no doribo, hiba haṛi oinot felai diya oibo."
LUK 3:10 Toi mainšor dol okkole Yahyare fusar goredde, "Toile ãrattu ki gora foribo?"
LUK 3:11 Yahyaye hitarare hodde: "Zattu duwa kuruta ase, hite zattu nai hitare uggwa dok. Ar zar hãse haiddo ase, hite o hen gorok."
LUK 3:12 Ar heṛe hazna adaigoroya o torikotor gusol loibolla aišše. Hitara Yahyare hodde, "Ustad, ãrattu ki gora foribo?"
LUK 3:13 Hibaye zuwab diye, "Ainot zen ase henor beši adai no goijjo."
LUK 3:14 Šoinno okkol hoekzone o fusar goijje, "Ãrattu ki gora foribo?" Hibaye hitarare hodde, "Hono kiyottu zurgori otóba oinnai bafe kissu adai no goijjo. Tũwara tũwarar beton loi razi tako."
LUK 3:15 Ar manuš okkole Mosilla entezar gori taikkede hisabe beggune mone mone bafa šuru goijjede,Yahya i Mosi oit fare.
LUK 3:16 Hetunot Yahyaye hitara beggunore hodde, "Ãi tũwarare fani loi torikotor gusol dir ṭik, kintu en ekzon aiyer, ze ãttuwaro šoktiwala. Ãi hibar zutar fita kuli dibar laikka o no. Hibaye tũwarare Pak Ruh edde oin loi torikotor gusol dibo.
LUK 3:17 Kula hibar hatot ase, hõlat gĩyur dana zari foriškar goribolla. Gĩyur dana hinore hibar nizor gudamot rakibo, kintu tušore hono din no nifede hendilla oin loi furaidi felaibo."
LUK 3:18 Yahyaye aro bout hota hoi manuš okkolore Allar diya kalam tobolig goijje.
LUK 3:19 Kintu Yahyaye badša Herudore jejeṛaiye, kiyollahoile hite hitar bái bou Herudiyare loi taikke edde aro bout kuham okkol goijje,
LUK 3:20 hitar oinno kuham okkolor fũwati aro ekkan noya kuham zug diye, hiyan oilde Yahyare ziyolot diye.
LUK 3:21 Ar zẽtte hár manuš okkole Yahyar hãse zaiyore torikotor gusol lor, Isaye o torikotor gusol loiye. Ar hibaye munazat goredde šomot asman kuligiyegoi,
LUK 3:22 edde he Pak Ruh ek hoitoror sonna loi Isar uwore lami aišše, ar behostottu ei abaz aišše: "Tui ãr he adoijja Fut, tor uwore ãi kub kuši."
LUK 3:23 Onumanik tiriš bosor oiyede šomot Isaye ham šuru goijje. Mainše mone goittode mozin Isa Yusufor fut, Yusuf Elir fut.
LUK 3:24 Eli Mattátor fut, Mattát Levir fut, Levi Melkir fut, Melki Zannaiyor fut, Zannaiyor fut Yusuf,
LUK 3:25 Yusuf Mottitiyar fut, Mottitiya Amošor fut, Amoš Nahumor fut, Nahum Ešalir fut, Ešali Nogir fut.
LUK 3:26 Nogi Mator fut, Mat Mottitiyar fut, Mottitiya Šimiyor fut, Šimiyo Yusekor fut, Yusek Zodar fut,
LUK 3:27 Zoda Yohananor fut, Yohanan Resar fut, Resa Serubabelor fut, Serubabel Salṭiyolor fut, Salṭiyol Nerir fut.
LUK 3:28 Neri Melkir fut, Melki Addir fut, Addi Kušomor fut, Kušom Elimadamor fut, Elimadam Eror fut,
LUK 3:29 Er Yosuvar fut, Yosuva Eliyesoror fut, Eliyesor Zorimor fut, Zorim Mattátor fut, Mottot Levir fut,
LUK 3:30 Levi Simeonor fut, Simeon Ehudar fut, Ehudah Yusufor fut, Yusuf Yonamor fut, Yonam Eliyakimor fut,
LUK 3:31 Eliyakim Meleyar fut, Meleya Minnar fut, Minna Mottotiyar fut, Mottotiya Natanor fut, Natan Daudor fut,
LUK 3:32 Daud Yasiror fut, Yasir Obedor fut, Obed Buazor fut, Buaz Salmonor fut, Salmon Nahušonor fut,
LUK 3:33 Nahušon Omminadabor fut, Omminadab Adomanor fut, Adoman Ornir fut, Orni Hešronor fut, Hešron Ferošor fut, Feroš Ehudar fut,
LUK 3:34 Ehudah Yakubor fut, Yakub Isakor fut, Isak Ibrahimor fut, Ibrahim Ṭerar fut, Tera Nahuror fut,
LUK 3:35 Nahur Šorugor fut, Serug Reuor fut, Reu Felegor fut, Feleg Eberor fut, Eber Šelar fut,
LUK 3:36 Šela Kenanor fut, Kenan Arpákšador fut, Arpákšad Šemor fut, Šem Nuhor fut, Nuh Lemekor fut,
LUK 3:37 Lemek Metúšalar fut, Metúšalah Honnukor fut, Honnuk Yaredor fut, Yared Mahalalelor fut, Mahalalel Kenanor fut,
LUK 3:38 Kenan Enošor fut, Enoš Šetor fut, Šet Adamor fut, adom Allar Fut.
LUK 4:1 Isa, Pak Ruhor šoktiye furaiya oiyore Zordanottu firi aišše edde he Pak Ruhor išaraye bošoti sara elehat sairi goijje,
LUK 4:2 zeṛe hibare sališ din foijjonto šoitane dúha diye, ar he din okkolot maze Isaye hána hono kissu no há, he din okkol šeš oi bade hibattu buk laigge.
LUK 4:3 Toi Šoitane Isare hodde, "Tui zodi Allar Fut oi, toile ei fattorguware ho ruṭi oizagoi."
LUK 4:4 Isaye hitare zuwabe hodde, "Iyan endilla leka ase: 'Manuš šude ruṭi loi no base.'"
LUK 4:5 Tarfore Šoitane Isare ek usol faharor uwore loigiye edde ek sator butore duniyair hár raijjore dehaiye.
LUK 4:6 Toi Šoitane Isare hodde, "Ãi tore ei hár odihar edde zak zomok diyum; kiyollahoile in ãre diya oiye, ar ãttu zare issa lage ãi hitare di.
LUK 4:7 Hetolla tui zodi ãre sojida goros, toile in beggun tor oibo."
LUK 4:8 Isaye zuwabe hitare diye: "Leka ase: 'Tũi tũwar Mabud Allare sojida goro, edde lehar hibare šeba goro.'"
LUK 4:9 Tarfore Šoitane Isare Zeruzalemor uwore loigiye edde dórmogóror tulir uwore tiya goraiyore hodde: "Tui zodi Allar Fut, toile enttu nise zaf mar.
LUK 4:10 Kiyollahoile kitabot leka ase: "'Hibaye hibar firista okkolore tor babute hokum dibo, tore uddar goribolla.
LUK 4:11 Hitara tore hatot gori tuli loibo, zene tor ṭengot fattoror ujaṭ no lage.'"
LUK 4:12 Kintu Isaye hitare zuwab diye, "Iyan endilla howa oiye: 'Tũi tũwar Allah Mabudore forikka no goijjo.'"
LUK 4:13 Šoitane hibare hár ḍoilla gori dúha diya šeš oi bade, toi hite olfo ṭaimolla hibar hãsottu dur oigiyegoi.
LUK 4:14 Ruhor šoktit Isa Galilot firigiye edde elehar hár zagat hibar hóbor sorai giyegoi.
LUK 4:15 Isaye hitarar bout sinagog okkolot šikka diye edde beggune Isare tarif goijje.
LUK 4:16 Isa Nasarat fara aišše, zeṛe hiba zuwan oil. Dórmor din Isaye nizor rosom mozin sinagogot giye. Heṛe hibaye pak kalam foribolla uṛi tiyaiye.
LUK 4:17 Tarfore hibar hatot nobi Esaiyar leka kitabwa diya oiye. He rol beraiya kitabwa kuli hibaye he zagagan faiye zeṛe leka ase:
LUK 4:18 "Allah Mabudor Ruh ãr uwore ase, kiyollahoile Allaye ãre ṭik goijje zene ãi gorib okkolor hãse kušir hóbor tobolig gori. Hibaye ãre bondi okkolor hãse azadir hota, anda okkolor hãse nozor danor hota gušona goribolla defeṛaiye. Zene zara zulum far hitarare ãi rehai gori fari.
LUK 4:19 edde Mabudor rahamotor bosor elan gori."
LUK 4:20 Tarfore Isaye he rol beraiya kitabware berai hademor hatot diye edde boišše. Muzolišhanar fotti mainšor suk Isar uzu oiye.
LUK 4:21 Isaye hitarare en hoi šuru goijje, "Pak kitabor ei kalam tũwara funone aziya hiyan furon oiye."
LUK 4:22 Henot beggune Isar babute goba diye edde Isar mukottu rahamoti hota funi hitara beggune tajjuf oiye. Hitara hodde, "Iba Yusufor fuwa no?"
LUK 4:23 Isaye hitarare hodde, "Tũwara ãre hameka en boson hoiba: 'Ḍakṭor, age nizore aramgor!' Aro hoiba 'Kofornahum šohorot zen zen gora oiye boli funni hendilla eṛe niz farat o hen gori deha.'"
LUK 4:24 Isaye aro hodde: "Ãi tũwarare soiyi hoir, hono nobire nizor farar mainše no gose.
LUK 4:25 Ar ãi tũwarare hoir, soiyi oilde nobi Eliyasor ṭaimot zẽtte šaro tin bosor zór noddil edde har deš okkolot raṭ oil, hẽtte Israil dešot beša beši rari mayafuwain okkol aššil.
LUK 4:26 Kintu Eliyasore hitara honokiyor hãse defeṛa no o, bolke Sidon elehar Šarifot farar ek rari mayafuwar hãse defeṛa oil.
LUK 4:27 Nobi Elišar ṭaimot Israil dešot bout kurus biyaraimma okkol aššil, kintu hitara honokiyore aram gora no o, bolke Siriya dešor Namanore aram gora oil."
LUK 4:28 Ei hota funi he muzolišhanar manuš beggun guššaye oin oiye.
LUK 4:29 Ar hitara uṛi Isare he farattu ṭeli niyolai loi za šuru goijje. Hitara ze faharot fara bainde hiyanor haindar uwore loigiye edde Isare nise feli dito saiye.
LUK 4:30 Kintu Isaye hitarar mazottu ãṛi giyegoi, honokiye Isare sui no fare.
LUK 4:31 Isaye nise Galil elehar Kofornahum šohorot giye edde dórmor din manuš okkolore šikka diya šuru goijje.
LUK 4:32 Manuš okkole Isar šikkat tajjuf oiye, kiyollahoile hibar kalam kemotawola aššil.
LUK 4:33 Heṛe sinagogot napak butor ruhuye failde ekzon manuš aššil.
LUK 4:34 He manušwaye ḍak mari hodde: "Oh, Nasarator Isa, õne loi ãrar loi ki talukkat? Õne ki ãrare binaš goitto aiššo? Ãi zani õne honnuwa, õne Allar he Pak zon!"
LUK 4:35 Kintu Isaye hibare dõk diyore hodde: "Nizam o, ei manušwar butottu niyoli ai." Toi he bod ruhuye manušware mainšor sarme meṛit asari felai raki hitar butottu niyoli giyegoi, manušwar hono hoti no o.
LUK 4:36 Manuš okkol beggune tajjuf oiyore hitara ekzonore ekzone hodde: "In ki hota! Odihar edde šokti loi napak but okkolore hokum de, ar hitara niyoli aiye!"
LUK 4:37 Toi ei hóbor he elehar hár mikka sorai giyegoi.
LUK 4:38 Bade Isa muzolišhanattu niyoli Simonor górot giye. Hẽtte Simonor hori zor biyaram loi beši hošto fat aššil. Hetolla hitara hibare aram goribolla Isar hãse foriyad goijje.
LUK 4:39 Toi Isaye Simonor horir ḍake tiyai zor biyaramore dõk diye. Ar hibattu zor sari giyegoi edde hibaye hehon uṛi hitaralla hána danar bebosta goijje.
LUK 4:40 Beil dufedde ṭaimot maze, manušzon okkole har biyaraimma zara ḍoilla boḍoilla biyaram loi hoštofar, hitarare Isar hãse ainne. Isaye hitara fottizonor uwore hat raikke, edde hitarare aram goijje.
LUK 4:41 Ar beši mainšottu bod ruh niyoli giyegoi, bod ruh okkole guzori hodde, "Tũi Allar Fut!" Kintu Isaye hitarare dõk diye edde hoito no de, kiyollahoile hiba Moside hiyan hitara zainto.
LUK 4:42 Din zehon oiye Isaye he zagattu zaigoire ekkan nirzon zagat giye. Manuš okkole Isare tuwai tuwai hibar hãse giye. Hitara Isare berai dori taikke zene hiba hitarar hãsottu no zagoi.
LUK 4:43 Kintu Isaye hitarare hodde, "Aro bout zagat zai ãttu Allar raijjor kušir hóbor tobolig goragoi foribo, kiyollahoile Allaye ãre in goribolla defeṛaiye."
LUK 4:44 Tarfore Isaye Ehudiya elehar sinagog okkolot zai zai kušir hóbor tobolig gorat taikke.
LUK 5:1 Ek šome Isa Gennesaret halor farot tiyaiye. Heṛe manuš okkole Isattu Allar kalam funibolla ṭelaṭeli goijje.
LUK 5:2 Isaye sadde halor hãsat duiyan no ase, kintu zailla okkole henttu lami zai zal duwer.
LUK 5:3 Henot oi duiyan nor butottu, Isaye Simonor not uiṭṭe. Ar hitare nogan kulottu ekkena dure loi zaibolla hoiye. Toi Isaye not boi manuš okkolore šikka diya šuru goijje.
LUK 5:4 Isaye hota howa šeš gori bade hibaye Simonore hodde, "Tui tor noganore entu maze loi za, ar mas saibolla tor zal felagoi."
LUK 5:5 Simone hodde, "Ustad, ãra šara rait mehennot gori kissu no fai, tarfore o õne zehon hor, ãi zal felaiyum."
LUK 5:6 Hitara zal felaiye bade en masor ḍõr zãk dora foijje, zenneki hitarar zal udda siri zaitoi saiye.
LUK 5:7 Henot hitarar šiyardar okkol zara oinno not ase, hitarare o hate išara gori ḍaikke, zene hitara aiyore itarare modot gori fare. Hitara aiyore duiyan no en bafe mas loi botti goijje, zene no duniyan dufi zaibar alamot oiye.
LUK 5:8 Ei hanḍo deki Simon, zare Fitor hoi o ḍake, hite Isar sarme uite fori hodde, "Malik õne ãr hãsottu zogoi, ãi gunagar."
LUK 5:9 Kiyollahoile zalot eto mas dora foijje, Simon edde hitar sãti okkol beggune tajjuf oiye,
LUK 5:10 ar hendilla ekkui bafe Simonor šiyardar, Sebudiyusor fuwain Yakub edde Yuhanna o tajjuf oiye. Hetunot Isaye Simonore hodde, "No ḍorais, ehon loti tui manuš doribi."
LUK 5:11 Tarfore hitara hitarar nogunore kulor uwore tuli felaiyore, hár kissu felai raki Isar fisa loiye.
LUK 5:12 Isaye ek bar ek šohorot giye. Heṛe ekzon kurus biyaraimma manuš aššil, zar hara ga gáye furaiya aššil. Isare deki he manušwaye meṛir uzu oi uite fori Isattu duwa sai hodde, "Malik, õne issa gorile ãre bala gori fariba."
LUK 5:13 Isaye hat ṭani hitare suiyore hodde, "Ãi sai, tũi foriškar o!" Ar hehon hitar kurus biyaram bala oi giyegoi.
LUK 5:14 Isaye hitare endilla hokum diye, "Ei hota honokiyore no hois, bolke zaiyore dórmiyo Alem okkolore dehagoi, toi bade saf oi faijjosde hiyanolla Musar ain mozin ekkan kurbani gorgoi. Henot mainšor hãse tui foriškar oiosde hiyanor forman oibo."
LUK 5:15 Tarfore o Isar hóbor aro beši sorai giyegoi. Isar hota funibolla edde biyaraimma okkol aram oibolla bout manuš okkol Isar hãse aiya šuru goijje.
LUK 5:16 Kintu Isaye hamiša nirzon zagat zai duwa gorito.
LUK 5:17 Ek din Isaye šikka der, hen šomot Foroši okkol edde dórmiyo alem okkol Isar hãse ai boiššegai. Hitara aššilde Galil edde Ehudiya elehar bout fara okkolor edde Zeruzalem šohoror manuš okkol. Biyaraimma aram goribolla Mabudor šokti Isattu aššil.
LUK 5:18 Hetunot hoekzon mainše ekzon leng biyaraimmare haiṭṭa loi bar gori ainne. Hitara hitare butore loi zaiyore Isar sarme rakito saiye.
LUK 5:19 Kintu zamila buli hitare butore loizaibar fõt no fa. Hetunot hitara góror salor uwore uiṭṭe edde salor sani hana gori bisana šo hitare manuš okkolor maze Isar sarme lamai diye.
LUK 5:20 Isaye hitarar biššaš dekiyore hodde, "Bondu, tor guna maf gora oiye!"
LUK 5:21 Henot dórmiyo alem edde Foroši okkole mone mone bafa šuru goijje, "Ite honnuwa, ze Allare ofoman gorer? Allah sara ar honokiye guna maf gori di no fare!"
LUK 5:22 Hitara mone mone ki sinta goijje Isaye buzi fariyore hodde: "Tũwara mone mone hendilla ka bafor?
LUK 5:23 Tor guna maf gora oiye howa asan oibo ne naki tui uṛi ãṛi bera howa asan oibo?
LUK 5:24 Kintu duniyait guna maf gori dibar kemota Adomor Futottu ase, hiyan zene tũwara zani faro." Hen hoi Isaye he leng manušwar mikka firi hitare hodde, "Ãi tore hoir, uṭ, tor bisanagan tuli loi górot zagoi."
LUK 5:25 Ar manušwa hehon beggunor sarme tiyaiye edde hite neṛi aššilde bisanagan tuli loiye, edde Allare šukuriya gori gori górot giyegoi.
LUK 5:26 Henot beggune kub tajjuf oiye edde Allare šukuriya zanaiye. Ar hitarattu Allar ḍor góille edde hodde, "Aijja ãra ki tajjuiffa ham dekilam!"
LUK 5:27 Tarfore Isa henttu niyoli giyegoi edde dekedde Levi name ekzon hazna adaigoroya, hite hazna tulede zagat boi taikke. Isaye Levire hodde, "Ãr fisa lo!"
LUK 5:28 Toi hite o uiṭṭe edde hitar hár kissu felai raki Isar fisa loiye.
LUK 5:29 Bade Levi manušwaye hitar górot Isalla ek ḍõr hána goijje. Heṛe aro bout hazna adaigoroya okkol edde aro bout manuš okkol šoho hitarar fũwati hána haito boišše.
LUK 5:30 Hetunot heṛe aššilde Foroši okkol edde hitarar dórmiyo alem okkole Isar sahabi okkolore nališ gori hodde, "Tũwara hazna adaigoroya edde gunagar okkol loi kiyolla há fiya goro?"
LUK 5:31 Kintu zuwabe Isaye hitarare hodde, "Araimma mainšottu ḍakṭoror dorhar nai, kintu biyaraimma mainšottu dorhar ase.
LUK 5:32 Ãi forhesgar okkolore no, kintu gunagar okkolore ḍakito aiššide, zene hitara gunattu mon fira."
LUK 5:33 Toi hitara hibare hodde, "Yahyar šagirit okkole hamiša ruza rake edde munazat gore, Foroši okkolor šagirit okkole o hen gore, kintu õnor sahabi okkole há fiya gorat take."
LUK 5:34 Isaye hitarare hodde: "Dula fũwati taite dular fũwajja okkolore ki tũwara ruza rakai fariba?
LUK 5:35 Kintu en šomoi aiyer, zẽtte hitarar hãsottu dulare loi za oibo, ar he din okkolot hitara ruza rakibo."
LUK 5:36 Hibaye hitarare ekkan mesal kahani o hoiye: "Noya kurutattu ṭura siri honokiye furan kurutat tali no laga. Kiyollahoile, hen gorile to noya kurutawa siri fela o. Ar he noya taligan o furan kurutar fũwati no mana.
LUK 5:37 Otóba honokiye no ḍale tottoza šoraf furan samorar hoillat. Kiyollahoile ḍalile he tottoza šorafgune hoillagunore fuṛai felaibo, henot šorafgun o goli zaiboi edde hoillaguno o nošto oi zaiboi.
LUK 5:38 No, tottoza šoraf noya samor hoillat raka foribo.
LUK 5:39 Furan šoraf hái bade honokiye tottoza šoraf haito no sa, kiyollahoile hite hoibo, 'Furangun bala beši.'"
LUK 6:1 Hono ek dórmor din Isaye fõtot hono ek gĩyuketi bai gil. Isar sahabi okkole giyũrdanar sora siri hatot góši góši há šuru goijje.
LUK 6:2 Hetunot hozon forošiye hodde, "Ain mozin dórmor din zin gora mana hin kiyolla goror?"
LUK 6:3 Isaye hodde: "Daud edde hibar fũwajja okkolottu zehon buk laggil hẽtte ki goijje hin ki tũwara no foro?
LUK 6:4 Hibaye to Allar górot goillil, edde sarme rakkilde ruṭi loi háil edde hibar fũwajja okkolore dil, zin šude imam okkole haibar ain ase."
LUK 6:5 Bade Isaye he Foroši okkolore hodde, "Adomor Fut oilde dórmor dinor malik."
LUK 6:6 Ar ek dórmor din Isaye sinagogot giye edde šikka diye. Heṛe en ekzon manuš aššil zar ḍen hat mozigiyegoi.
LUK 6:7 Dórmiyo alem okkol edde Foroši okkole, Isaye dórmor din he manušware aram gore ki no gore hiyan saibolla, hitara Isar uwore bala bafe nozor raikke. Toi zene hitara Isare hosuri dibar haron tuwai fa.
LUK 6:8 Kintu Isaye hitarar monor sinta zainto. Hetolla he hat mozi giyegoide manušware Isaye hodde, "Uṛi beggunor munttu ai tiya!" Henot hite uṛi tiyaiye.
LUK 6:9 Isaye dórmiyo alem okkol edde Foroši okkolore hodde,"Ãi tũwarare ekkan hota fusar gori, dórmor din ki gora ezajot ase? Bala ham gora ne naki horaf ham gora? Foran basa ne naki foran dongšo gora?"
LUK 6:10 Tarfore Isaye sairo ḍakor beggunor mikka sai manušware hodde: "Tor hattan mum mikka ṭan." Hite hen goijjebar hitar hattan ekkubare bala oi giyegoi.
LUK 6:11 Hetunot hitara guššaye heṛe uzora uzori oi giyegoi edde Isare ki gora zaibo he babute hitara hitara biyasana goijje.
LUK 6:12 He din okkolot ekdin hiba munazat goribolla ek faharor uwore uiṭṭe, edde heṛe hibaye Allar hãse munazat gorat šara rait haṛai diye.
LUK 6:13 Bade binna zehon oiye, hibaye hibar šahabi okkolore ḍaikke edde hitarar butottu barozonore basi loiye, zarare asab hoi nam diye:
LUK 6:14 Simon, zare Isaye Fitor hoi nam diye edde hitar bái Andreas, Yakub, Yuhanna, Filip, Bartolomeus,
LUK 6:15 Moti Ṭomas, Alfeusor fuwa Yakub, Simon, zare bahadur Zelot hoito,
LUK 6:16 Yakubor fut Ehudah, edde Ehudah Iskariyot, ze Isare dušmon okkolor hatot dori diye.
LUK 6:17 Hibaye hitarare fũwati loi faharottu abar lami giye edde ekkan fuwainna zagat tiyaiye. Heṛe hibar ek ḍõr sahabi okkol edde Šara Ehudiyattu, Zeruzalem edde doriyar hãsar Sidon edde Tirosottu o aro bout beši manuš okkol,
LUK 6:18 zara heṛe hibar boyan funibolla edde biyaramottu aram oibolla heṛe aišše. Ar zara napak ruh loi duk fail, hitarare o hibaye bala goijje.
LUK 6:19 Edde hár mainše hibare suibolla kušiš goijje, kiyollahoile hibar butottu ek šokti niyoli gil edde harkiyore aram goijjil.
LUK 6:20 Isaye sahabi okkolor uzu suk tuli hodde: "Allar rahamot tũwarar uwore zara gorib, Allar raijjo tũwarar.
LUK 6:21 Allar rahamot tũwarar uwore zara ehon waišša, tũwarar buk miṭa oibo. Allar rahamot tũwarar uwore zara ehon handor, tũwara hašiba.
LUK 6:22 Allar rahamot tũwarar uwore, zẽtte Adomor Futolla buli, mainše tũwarare hingša gore, tũwarare šomazottu niyolai de, ar ofoman gore, edde tũwarar nam horaf hoi tũwarare batil gore.
LUK 6:23 "He dinot anondo goro edde kušiye fal maro, kiyollahoile, so, behostot tũwaralla enam beši ḍõr. Kiyollahoile hitarar bafdada okkole o nobi okkolor loi endilla bebohar okkol gorito.
LUK 6:24 "Kintu bifod tũwarare, zara tuwangor, tũwara tũwarar šantona faifelaiyo.
LUK 6:25 Bifod tũwarare zara ehon feṭ borai faror tũwarattu buk lagibo. Bifod tũwarare zara ehon hašor, tũwara bilak goriba edde handiba.
LUK 6:26 Bifod tũwarar, zẽtte hár mainše tũwarare šunam gore. Hitarar bafdada okkole o bonḍo nobi okkolore hendilla goitto.
LUK 6:27 "Kintu tũwara zara funor ãi hitarare hoir: Tũwarar dušmonore o muhabbot goro, zara tũwarare hingša gore hitarare balai goro.
LUK 6:28 Zara tũwarare bodduwa de, hitarare duwa goro. Zara tũwarare ninda gore hitaralla munazat goro.
LUK 6:29 Ze tũwar ek galot suwar mare, hitar mikka oinno galo lagai diyo, ar ze tũwar saddor kuli lor, hitare bazu kuli loite o mana no goijjo.
LUK 6:30 Ar ze honokiye tũwattu kissu sa, hitare diyo, edde ze honokiye tũwarar hono kissu loi za, hin ar uwafes no saiyo.
LUK 6:31 "Funo, mainše tũwarare zendilla gorok aša goro, tũwara o hitarar loi hendilla bebohar goro.
LUK 6:32 "Ar zara tũwarare muhabbot gore, šudu hitarare muhabbot gorile tũwara ki gun faiba? Hendilla muhabbot to horaf mainše o gori take.
LUK 6:33 Ar zara tũwarar ufohar gore, šudu zodi hitarar ufohar goro, toile tũwara ki gun faiba? Hendilla to gunagar mainše o gore.
LUK 6:34 Ar zarar hãsottu uwafes faibar aša take, hali zodi hitarare udar do, toile tũwara ki gun faiba? Horaf mainše o horaf manuš okkolore udar de, zene hedun firaifa.
LUK 6:35 Kintu tũwara nizor dušmonore o muhabbot goro edde hitarar balai goro. Uwafes faibar aša no raki udar do. Toile tũwarar enam ḍõr oibo edde tũwara šorbo šoktiwala Allar fuwain oiba. Haron Allah našukur edde horafore o doya gore.
LUK 6:36 Tũwarar behostiyo Baf zendilla rahamoti, tũwara o hendilla rahamoti o.
LUK 6:37 "Ar tũwara bisar no goijjo, henot tũwarare o bisar gora no oibo. Duši no goijjo, henot tũwarare o duši gora no oibo. Tũwara sari do, henot tũwarare o sari diya oibo.
LUK 6:38 Dan goro, henot tũwarare o diya oibo. Beši forimane sibi sibi, zankai zankai, zaf di forefan gori tũwarar kulot diya oibo, kiyollahoile tũwara ze bafe mafi do, he bafe tũwaralla o mafa oibo."
LUK 6:39 Ar hibaye ekkan boson o hoiye: "Ekzon andaye ki ar ekzon andare fõt dehai faribo? Dunizon gorot fori no zaiboi ne?
LUK 6:40 Šagirit ustator uwore no, kintu ze furafuri šikka fa, hite hitar ustator ḍoilla o.
LUK 6:41 "Ar tũwar báiyor sukot ze hal ase hiyan kiyolla dekor, kintu tũwar nizor sukot ze gasor ḍõr seli ase hiyan kiyolla bafi no sor?
LUK 6:42 Tũwar sukot ze gasor seli ase hiyan zehon no dekor, toile tũi ken gori ar ekzonore hoi faror, 'Bái aiyo, ãi tũwar sukottu hallan loifelai, 'Oh munafek! Age nizor sukor gasor ḍõr seli hiyan loifela, toi bade tor báiyor sukot ze hal ase hiyan loi felaibolla foriškar gori dekibi.
LUK 6:43 "Bala gasot horaf gula dorede hendilla hono hota nai, ar hendilla horaf gasot o bala gula no dore.
LUK 6:44 Gula sai gas sinaza. Mainše keṛarzalittu ḍuirgula ba kẽṛagasottu ãngur no tule.
LUK 6:45 Bala manuše hitar dil boraiya balattu bala hota bair gori ane, ar horaf mainše hitar dil furaiya horafottu horaf hota bair gori ane, kiyollahoile zar dil zine furaiya, hitar gale hin ho.
LUK 6:46 "Tũwara ãre Malik, Malik hoi ka ḍako, ãi ziyan hoi hiyan zodi no goro?
LUK 6:47 Ze honokiye ãr hãse aiye, ãr hota fune edde he mozin gore, hite hár ḍoilla ãi tũwarare dehai.
LUK 6:48 Hite en ekzon manušor ḍoilla, ze gór bandibolla murgori meṛi kuijje edde fattoror uwore faiya gãijje. Bade he góror uwore boinna aišše edde ḍollor fani aišše, to górganore lari no fare, kiyollahoile hiyan mujbut gori banda oiye.
LUK 6:49 Ar ze ãr hota fune, kintu he mozin no gore, hite en ekzon manušor ḍoilla, ze faiya no gãri meṛir uwore gór bainde. Bade he górot ḍollor fani aišše, hetunot he górgan fori ekkubare dongšo oi giyegoi."
LUK 7:1 Toi Isaye manuš okkolore šikka diya šeš gori bade hiba Kofornahum šohorot giyegoi.
LUK 7:2 Heṛe ekzon Rom šenafotir gulamottu ošuk oi foran zar zar oiye. Ei gulamore he šenafotiye beši ador gorito.
LUK 7:3 Hite Isar hóbor funi hoekzon Ihudi murobbi mainšore Isar hãse aroz goribolla defeṛaiye zene Isaye zai hitar gulamore aram gori fare.
LUK 7:4 Hitara Isar hãse zai Isare beša beši aroz gori hodde, "Õne zalla ei ham goriba hite iyan faibar laikka,
LUK 7:5 kiyolla buli hoile hite ãrar mainšore ador gore edde ãrare sinagog banai diye."
LUK 7:6 Henot Isa hitarar fũwati giye. Isaye hitar góror hãsa hãsi aišše de hetunot, oi šenafotiye hitar hoekzon fũwajjare hoi defeṛaiyede: "Malik, nizore ar duk no diyo, kiyollahoile õne ãr góror salor tole aiyo, ãi he laikka no.
LUK 7:7 Ar ãre ãi o õnor hãse aibar laikka mone no gori. Kintu õnor muke ho, henot ãr gulam bala oi zaiboi.
LUK 7:8 Ãi iyan zani, kiyollahoile ãttu o oinno zonor hokum mozin sola fore, ar ãttu o šena okkol ase. Zodi ãi ekzonore 'Za,' hoi hite za. Ar ekzonore 'Ãi,' hen hoile hite aiye. Ar ãr gulamore 'Iyan gor' hen hoile hite hiyan gore."
LUK 7:9 Ei hota funi Isaye tajjuf oiye. Ze šob manuš okkol Isar fise fise aišše hitarar uzu firiyore hodde, "Ãi tũwarare hoir, Israili okkolor butore o eto ḍõr biššaš ãi ar hono šome no deki."
LUK 7:10 Šenafotiye defeṛailde hitara górot firizai sadde he šenafotir gulammuwa aram oi giyegoi.
LUK 7:11 Hotun bade Isa Nain name ek farar mikka za šuru goijje. Hibar fũwati sahabi okkol edde ek ḍõr mainšor dol o giye.
LUK 7:12 ar hiba ṭon geiṭor hãsa hãsi aišše, toi ar so heṛe ek mora lašore bargori hoborstanot gãraito loizar. He lašwa aššilde ek mar lehar ek fut, he ma aššilde ekzon rari maya fuwa. Ar hibar fũwati šohorottu bout manuš okkol aššil.
LUK 7:13 Malik Isaye he rarir mayafuwaware deki beši doya laigge edde hibare hodde, "No haindis!"
LUK 7:14 Tarfore Isaye hãse zai hãiṭṭagan suiye. Ar hãiṭṭa boi loizaoya okkole tiyaiye. Toi Isaye hodde, "He zuwan fuwa, ãi tore hoir: Uṭ!"
LUK 7:15 Hen šomot he mora lašwa uṛi boišše edde hite hota howa šuru goijje. Toi Isaye hitare hitar mar hatot tulidiye.
LUK 7:16 Hetunot beggunor dilot Allar ḍor góille edde Allar tarif gori howa šuru goijje. "Ãrar maze ekzon moha nobi uiṭṭe, ar Allaye hibar bonda okkolor uzu mon diye!"
LUK 7:17 Bade šara Ehudiya edde hiyanor sairo mikkar elehat Isar hanḍor babute sorai giyegoi.
LUK 7:18 Yahyar šagirit okkole ei šob goṭona beggun Yahyare funaiye. Ar Yahyaye duizon šagiritore ḍaikke,
LUK 7:19 edde hitarare Malik Isar hãse fusar goitto defeṛaiye, "Ze aibar hota, he zon ki õne, naki ãra oinno zonolla entezarot takiyum?"
LUK 7:20 Toi hitara Isar hãse zaiyore hodde, "Torikotor gusol doya Yahyaye ãrare õnor hãse defeṛaiye, 'Ze aibar hota he zon ki õne, naki ãra oinno zonor entezarot takiyum?'"
LUK 7:21 He šomot Isaye bout manuš okkolore biyaram, hošto edde bod ruh, in okkolottu hitarare aram goijje. Hibaye aro bout anda mainšor sukore bala gori diye.
LUK 7:22 Isaye Yahyar šagirit dunizonore endilla zuwab diye, "Tũwara zo, zin deikko edde fuinno he hóbor Yahyare hogoi: Andaye deker, lenge aṛer, kurus biyaraimma pak saf or, nafange funer, mora uṛi zargoi, edde gorib okkololla bala hóbor tobolig gora or.
LUK 7:23 Ar mubarok hite, ze ãr zoriya ujaṭ hái fori no zagoi"
LUK 7:24 Yahyar hoborguwa okkol zaigoi bade, hibaye manuš okkolore Yahyar babute howa šuru goijje: "Tũwara bošoti sara elehat ki saito gilade? Boyare lorede hóir ne?
LUK 7:25 No oile, ki saito gilade? Šundor hor findda ekzon manušore ne? So, dami hor finde edde zak zomok loi zibon haṛa, hitara mehelot take.
LUK 7:26 Toile ki saito gilade? Ki ekzon nobi re? Oi, ãi tũwarare hoir, ekzon nobittuwaro beši!
LUK 7:27 Iba oilde hiba zar babute kitabot leka ase: "'Sa, ãi tor age ãr hóborguware defeṛair, hite tor age zai tolla fõt saf goribo.'
LUK 7:28 Ãi tũwarare hoir, narittu zormo oiyede hitarar maze, Yahyattuwaro mohan kiye nai; tarfore o Allar raijjot ze šobsaite beši šoṛo, hite o hibattuwaro mohan."
LUK 7:29 (Ar šomosto manuš okkol edde hazna adaigoroya okkole ei hota funi Allah niyaiban hoi kobul goijje, kiyollahoile hitara Yahyar hãsottu torikotor gusol loiye,
LUK 7:30 kintu Foroši edde dórmiyo alem okkole Yahyar hãsottu torikotor gusol no lowat hitara nizor šommonde Allar eredare befol goijje.)
LUK 7:31 "Henoile ei zobanar manuš okkolore ãi har loi tulona goijjum? Hitara honḍoilla?
LUK 7:32 Hitara en fuwaindor ḍoilla zara bazarot boi ekzone ar ekzonore ḍakiyore hodde: "'Ãra tũwaralla baši bazailam, kintu tũwara no nasila. Ãra dukkor gan gailam, kintu tũwara no handila.'
LUK 7:33 Kiyollahoile torikotor gusoldoya Yahya aišše, edde hite ruṭi ba ãnguror roš no har, ar tũwara hor, 'Hitare bute faiye.'
LUK 7:34 Ar Adomor Fut ai há fiya gorer buli tũwara hor: 'So, ei manušwa hánar lalsi bonda edde šorafkur, ar hazna adaigoroya mainšor bondu.'
LUK 7:35 Kintu Allar giyanor butore ze za hitar zibone forman gore ze Allar giyan soiyi."
LUK 7:36 Ekzon forošiye hitar górot Isare hánar dawat diye. Hetunot Isa he forošir górot giye edde hána haito boišše.
LUK 7:37 Ehon, he šohorot ek gunagar maya fuwa aššil. Hibaye Isa he forošir górot hána hadde zani fariyore ek dola fattoror boyomot gori kušbo tel loi hiba heṛe aišše.
LUK 7:38 Bade hibaye Isar fis ḍakottu ṭengor hãse zai tiyaiye edde hainde. Tarfore sukor fani loi, Isar ṭengor fata bizai diye edde hibar matar sul loi hin fũsi loiye. Tarfore hibaye Isar ṭengor fatat suma diye edde kušbo tel maki diye.
LUK 7:39 Toi ze forošiye Isare dawat dil hite ei abosta deki mone mone hodde, "Ei manušwa zodi nobi oito toile zani farito, iba hon ḍoilla maya fuwaye suwer, kiyollahoile hiba ekzon gunagar maya fuwa."
LUK 7:40 Hetunot Isaye he forošire hodde, "Simon, ãttu tore kissu hoibar ase." Hite hodde, "Ustad, ho na."
LUK 7:41 "Ekzon ṭĩya udar doyattu duizon mainše hozzo loiye. Ekzone hozzo loiye fãs šot ṭĩya, ar ekzone fõnzaš ṭĩya.
LUK 7:42 Kintu hitarar he hozzo fuzibar ra no takone, ṭĩya udar doyaye hitara dunizonor hozzogun maf gori diye. Ehon, itarar butore hone he ṭĩya udar doyare beši muhabbot goribo?"
LUK 7:43 Simone hodde, "Zar beši hozzo maf oiye, hite boli mone gori ãi." Isaye hodde, "Tui ṭik hoiyos."
LUK 7:44 Toi Isaye he mayafuwawar uzu firiyore Simonore hodde, "Ei mayafuwaware dehor ne? Ãi tor górot golilam, tui ãre ṭeng dúibolla fani no dos, kintu ibaye sukor fani di ãr ṭeng bizaiye edde nizor sul loi hin fũsi loiye.
LUK 7:45 Tui ãre suma di solam no goros, kintu zehon loti ãi butore aišši, hibaye ãr ṭengor fatat suma diyat roiye.
LUK 7:46 Tui tel di ãr matat maki no dos, kintu hibaye kušbo tel ãr ṭengot maki diye.
LUK 7:47 Hetolla ãi tore hoir, Hibaye beši guna gorile o hibar guna maf gora oiye, ar etolla hibaye beši muhabbot dehaiye. Kintu zare olfo maf gora za, hite olfo muhabbot deha."
LUK 7:48 Bade Isaye he mayafuware hodde, "Tor guna maf gora oiye."
LUK 7:49 Zara Isar fũwati hána haito boiššil hitara hitara howa hoi gora šuru goijje, "Iba honnuwa ze guna udda maf gori de?"
LUK 7:50 Isaye hetunot he mayafuwaware hodde, "Tor imane tore uddar goijje, šanti gori zagoi."
LUK 8:1 Tarfore Isaye elan goribolla edde Allar raijjor mutallek kušir hóbor tobolig goribolla fara fara, šohore šohore gura šuru goijje. Ar fũwati he barozon sahabi,
LUK 8:2 edde zara bod ruhuttu uddar faiye, biyaramottu aram faiye hendilla hoekzon mayafuwain o fũwati aššil. Hitarar butore aššilde: Moriyam zare Mogdaleni hoi o ḍakito edde zar butottu hãttuwa bod ruh niyoli gilgoi.
LUK 8:3 Joana ze badša Herudor menezar Kusar bou. Susanna edde aro bout mayafuwain okkol. Hitarar nizor šombottittu Isa edde he barozon sahabi okkolore solaito.
LUK 8:4 Ar zẽtte beša beši manuš okkol bout šohor okkolottu aiyore Isar hãse ai birgorer. Toi Isaye hitarare šikka dibolla ei kahanigan hoiye:
LUK 8:5 "Ekzon sašaye hitar bizor dana šiṛibolla giye. Biz šiṛibar šomot hodun biz fõtor kinare foijje, hin manušor fortole oiye edde faik okkole hái felaiye.
LUK 8:6 Ar hodun biz šil meṛir uwore foijje edde hin heṛe fuiṭṭe, kintu fanir obafe saragun fuwai gilgoi.
LUK 8:7 Abar hodun biz keṛarzaliwala zagat foijje, he saragun keṛarzalir fũwati bari uiṭṭe, edde hinore keṛarzaliye sibi dori raikke.
LUK 8:8 Abar hodun biz bala zobinot foijje, hin bari uiṭṭe edde ek šot gun gula diye." Ei kahanigan hoi bade Isaye zur gola loi hodde, "Zar han ase hite funok!"
LUK 8:9 Hibar sahabi okkole ei mesal kahaniganor mani ki fusar goijje.
LUK 8:10 Isaye hodde, "Allar raijjor gufon soiyi tũwarare zainto diya oiye, kintu hitarar hãse kahanir mesale howa oiye, zene, "'Hitara deke kintu no deke, ar fune kintu no buze.'
LUK 8:11 "Ei mesal kahaniganor mani oilde endilla: Biz oilde Allar kalam.
LUK 8:12 Fõtor kinare foijjede bizor mesal hitarare diya oiye, zara kalam fune, kintu Šoitane ai hitarar dilottu hiyan tuli loi zagoi. Henot hitara ar hiyanor uwore iman ani no fare boli uddar oi no fare.
LUK 8:13 Šil meṛit foijjede bizor mesal hitarare diya oiye, ze he kalam fune edde kuširsate mani lo, kintu hitarattu hiyanor hono šiyõr nai; hitara olfo dinolla biššaš gore, ar forikkar šomot hitara fissa fori zagoi.
LUK 8:14 Keṛarzaliwala zagat foijjede bizor mesal hitarare diya oiye, zara kalam fune kintu zibon fõtot soilte soilte, šongšari sinta bafona, dón šombotti edde aram aiyešor maze hin sibot fori zagoi, hetolla zibonot hono fona fól deha no de.
LUK 8:15 Bala zobinot foijjede bizor mesal hitarare diya oiye ze soiyi šorol mone he kalam fune, edde mojbut gori kolobor butore dori rake ar hitarar sobori zibonot fona fól dore.
LUK 8:16 "Ar serag zali honokiye dešši loi guri no rake otóba haṭor tole no rake, kintu serag boiṛonir uwore rake, zene zara butore za, hitara fohor deki fare.
LUK 8:17 Henot en gufon kissu no takibo zin forhaš no oibo otóba en sufaiya kissu no takibo zin zana no zaibo ba deha no zaibo.
LUK 8:18 Hetolla tũwara hondilla gori funor he babute diyan do, kiyollahoile zattu ase hitare aro diya oibo. Ar zattu nai hite hitattu zin ase boli mone gore, hin o hitattu loifela oibo."
LUK 8:19 Ar Isar ma edde báiboinain okkole Isare saito aišše. Kintu hitara mainšor zamilalla buli Isa loi deha gori no faijjil.
LUK 8:20 Bade ekzone Isare hodde: "Õnor ma báiboinain okkole baire tiyai taikke, õne loi deha goitto sar."
LUK 8:21 Kintu hibaye hodde, "Itara zara Allar kalam fune edde he bafe falon gore, hitara oilde ãr ma edde báiboinain."
LUK 8:22 Ek din Isa edde Isar sahabi okkol ekkan not uiṭṭe. Isaye hitarare hodde, "Solo, ãra doriyar ofarot zai." Toi hitara no sajje,
LUK 8:23 edde hitara šor tulidi no solat maze Isa gumot fori giyegoi. Ar doriyat en tuwan oiye, henot hitarar nogan faniye furaiya owa šuru goijje. Henot hitara beša beši bifodot fori giyegoi.
LUK 8:24 Hitara Isar hãse zai Isare gumottu tulidi hodde, "Malik, Malik ãra ḍufizairgoi!" Hetunot Isa uṛi boyarore edde goirore dõk diye, ar boyar edde goir hanta oiye, hár kissu nirol oi giyegoi.
LUK 8:25 Tarfore Isaye sahabi okkolore hodde, "Tũwarar biššaš hoṛe?" Kintu hitara ḍore ammuwak oiye edde ekzonore ekzone hodde: "Iba honnuwa? Hibaye boyar edde doriyare hokum gore, ar hitara hibar hota mane!"
LUK 8:26 Tarfore hitara Geraseni okkolor dešot no loi fõisse, ziyan Galilor dusora faror mikka.
LUK 8:27 Ar Isa zẽtte farot laimme he šohoror ekzon bod ruhuye faiya manuš loi deha oiye. Bout dinottu loti ei manušwaye hor no finder edde górot no taker, kintu hoboror gãtot taker.
LUK 8:28 Hite Isar sarme meṛit uite fori guzori hodde: "Oh Isa, šoktiwala Allar Fut, ãlloi õnor ki tallukat? Õnor hãse ãi foriyad gorir, ãre zontrona no diyo!"
LUK 8:29 Isaye he napak ruhure manušwar butottu niyoli zaito hokum dilde hetolla hite hen goijje. Ei ruhuye bout din oite he manušware doijje. Ar hitare siyol edde beri loi bandi rakile o hite siyol siri bod ruhor kemotaye nirzon zagat zaitogoi.
LUK 8:30 Isaye hitare fusar goredde, "Tor nam ki?" Hite hodde, "Bahani" kiyollahoile hitar butore bout bod ruh okkol aššil.
LUK 8:31 Tarfore hitarare aṭai gãtot no defeṛaibolla Isare foriyad gora šuru goijje.
LUK 8:32 Heṛe faharor uwore ḍõr ek šuworor zak soredde aššil, he napak ruhugune Isare foriyad goijje šuworgunor butore hitarare goilto ezajot dibolla, ar hibaye hitarare ezajot diye.
LUK 8:33 Toi bod ruh okkole he manušwar butottu niyoli zai šuworgunor butore góillegoi. Henot he šuworor zakgun zure dũri faharor haindat giye edde henttu fori fori fanit dufi moijje.
LUK 8:34 Zara šuworor zak sorail hitara ei hanḍo deki henttu dai giyegoi. Ar ei goṭonaganore he šohorot edde farar hár zagat zai hoiyegoi.
LUK 8:35 Ki oiye hin saibolla hetunot manuš okkol niyoli aišše. Hitara Isar hãse ai dekedde, ze manušwar butottu bod ruh niyoli giyegoi, hite hor findi šuida oi Isar ṭengor ḍake boi taikke, hen deki manuš okkole ḍoraiye.
LUK 8:36 Zara he goṭonagan dekkil, hitara he bod ruye faiya manušwa ki bafe aram oil hin manuš okkolore hoiye.
LUK 8:37 Toi Geraseni elehar sairo mikkar šomosto manuš okkole Isare beši ḍoraiye hetolla hitara beggune Isare henttu zaiboilla foriyad goijje. Toi Isaye uiṭṭe edde henttu uwafes firi giyegoi.
LUK 8:38 Ze manušwattu bod ruh niyoli gilgoi, hite Isar fũwati zai faribo ne fusar goijje.
LUK 8:39 Kintu Isaye hitare en hoi bidai diye, "Tui tor górot zagoi edde tolla ze ḍõr ham Allaye goijje, hin mainšore hogoi." Henot hite farat firi giyegoi edde Isaye hitalla ze ḍõr ham goijje hin šohoror agagura hoiye.
LUK 8:40 Isa zẽtte firi aišše manuš okkole hibare kuši mone goisse, kiyollahoile hitara beggune hiballa entezar gori aššil.
LUK 8:41 Ar so, Zairus name ekzon manuš, Isar sarme aišše. Hite aššilde muzolišhanar ekzon neta. Hite Isar fot fori hitar górot zaibolla Isare foriyad gora šuru goijje.
LUK 8:42 Kiyollahoile hitattu lehar ek zi aššil, boyoš hom beši baro bosor, ar hiba morar mukot. Isa heṛe zadde šomot manuš okkole hibare har ḍakottu ṭelaṭeli goijje.
LUK 8:43 Heṛe butore ekzon beṛi maya fuwa aššil ze baro bosorfan kunzari biyaram loi duk fat ase. Ḍaktor okkolor fise har šombotti beggunore horos gori felai bade o honokiye hibare bala gori no fare.
LUK 8:44 Hibaye Isar fisottu zai Isar horor kuna suiye. Toi hehon hibar kunzari bon oi giyegoi.
LUK 8:45 Toi Isaye hodde, "Ãre hone suiye?" Kintu beggune ošikar goijje. Fitore hodde, "Huzur, mainše har ḍakottu ṭelaṭeliye zafdiforer."
LUK 8:46 Toi Isaye hodde, "Ãre hono ekzone suiye, ãi ṭer faiyi ãr butottu šokti giyede."
LUK 8:47 Mayafuwawaye dekedde hiba luwai tai no faribo, hetunot hiba hafi hafi Isar munttu aišše. Hibaye Isar sarme uite fori kiyolla Isare suiye edde kibafe hehon hibar kunzari bon oiye, in okkol har manušor sarme hibaye hoi funaiye.
LUK 8:48 Toi Isaye hodde, "Oh zi, tor biššaše tore bala goijje, arame górot firi zagoi."
LUK 8:49 Isa ehon o hota howat ase, hen šomot muzolišhanar netar górottu ekzon manuš aiyore hodde, "Tũwar zi mori giyoi. Huzurore loi ar diddari no goris."
LUK 8:50 Ei hota funiyore Isaye Zairusore hodde, "No ḍorais, bolke biššaš gor, henot hiba aram oibo."
LUK 8:51 Bade Isa zehon Zairusor górot fõisse, Fitor, Yakub, Yuhanna edde he zerfuwar babma sara ar honokiyore Isaye góror butore golito no de.
LUK 8:52 Beggune hiballa handahaṛi edde bilag gorer kintu Isaye hodde, "No haindo! Hiba no more, gum zadde."
LUK 8:53 Hitara hen funi Isare ṭaṭṭa uraiye, kiyollahoile hiba mori giyegoide hiyan hitara zainto.
LUK 8:54 Kintu Isaye hibar hat dori ḍaki hodde, "Oh zi, uṭ!"
LUK 8:55 Henot hibar foran firi aišše edde hiba hehon uṛi tiyaiye. Ar Isaye hibare kissu haito dito hoiye.
LUK 8:56 Henot hibar babma ekkubare ammuwak oi giyegoi, kintu Isaye hitarare ei goṭonar hotagan honokiyore no hoibolla mana goijje.
LUK 9:1 Bade he barozon asabore ekottoro gori ḍaikke edde hibaye hitarare har bod ruhor uwore edde biyaram bala goribolla šokti edde kemota diye.
LUK 9:2 Ar Allar raijjor tobolig goribolla edde biyaram aram goribolla Isaye hitarare faṭai diye.
LUK 9:3 Toi Isaye hitarare hodde: "Tũwara fõtolla kissu no loiyo, laṛi otóba gaṭṭi, hána otóba ṭĩya kissu no loiyo. Findibar fušak o dui zura no loiyo.
LUK 9:4 Ar tũwara ze górot zo, he fara sari no zogoi foijjonto he górot taikko.
LUK 9:5 Zodi mainše tũwarare no gose, he šohor sari zaibar šomot tũwarar ṭengor tolar dul zari felaiyo, zene hine hitarar berudde goba oi tiya."
LUK 9:6 Toi sahabi okkol henttu giyegoi edde fara fara zai Allar raijjor kušir hóbor tobolig goijje edde biyaramma okkolore aram goijje.
LUK 9:7 Badša Herude Isaye zin zin gorer hin beggun fuinne kintu hite honnan biššaš goribo buzi uṛi no fajjil. Kiyollabulihoile kiye kiye hoito Yahya mora okkolor butottu uṛi giyegoi.
LUK 9:8 Ar kiye kiye hoito Eliyase deha diye, ar kiye kiye hoito, furan hailla nobi okkolor butottu ekzon zinda oi uiṭṭe.
LUK 9:9 Ar Herude hodde, "Ãi to Yahyar mata haṛi felailam, kintu iba honnuwa zar babute endilla hota funazar." Hetolla badša Herude Isare saibolla kušiš goijje.
LUK 9:10 Bade asab okkole zin zin goijje, firi aiyore hitara hinore kulasagori Isare zanaiye. Tarfore Isaye hitarare fũwati loi Betsaida farar ḍake ek nizam zagat giye.
LUK 9:11 Kintu mainše he hóbor zani fariyore hitara Isar fisa loiye. Toi Isaye hitarare rahamotor sãte goisse edde hitarar hãse Allar raijjor babute hota hoiye. Ar zara aram oibar dorhar aššil hitarare aram goijje.
LUK 9:12 Tarfore din šeš oi aišše, ar he barozon asabe Isar hãse zai hodde: "Õne ei manuš okkolore bidai do, zene itara sairo mikka farat, geramot zai rait haṛai fare edde hána fani tuwai loi fare, kiyollahoile ãra aside zagagan kissu naide zaga."
LUK 9:13 Kintu Isaye hitarare hodde: "Tũwara hitarare hána do!" Asab okkole hodde, "Fãswa ruṭi edde duwa mas sara ãrar hãse ar kissu nai. Ar ki ãra zai edun manušolla haiddo kini ani faijjum?"
LUK 9:14 (Heṛe onumanik fãs hazar furuš manuš aššil.) Hetunot Isaye sahabi okkolore hodde, "Itara beggunore fõnzašzon fõnzašzon grup gori buwai do."
LUK 9:15 Sahabi okkole hen goijje, beggunore buwai diye.
LUK 9:16 Tarfore Isaye he fãswa ruṭi edde duwa mas loi asmanor uzu suk tuli hinolla Allare šukuriya zanaiye edde hinore bangi sahabi okkolore diye, mainšore baṛi dibolla.
LUK 9:17 Toi beggune feṭbori hána háiye. Tarfore hitara zin hái bade guragara basi roiye hinore dola gori baro barang hána oiye.
LUK 9:18 Isaye ek bar ekela munazat goredde šomot sahabi okkol o hibar fũwati heṛe aššil. Isaye hitarare fusar goredde: "Ãi honnuwa, ei babute mainše ki ho?"
LUK 9:19 Hitara zuwab diye, "Torikotor gusol doya Yahya, kintu kiye kiye ho nobi Eliyas, ar kiye, beši agor nobi okkolor butottu ek nobi uṛigiyegoi."
LUK 9:20 Isaye hitarare fusar goredde: "Kintu tũwara ki ho, ãi honnuwa?" Fitore hodde, "Õne Allar he Mosi."
LUK 9:21 Hetunot Isaye hitarare ei hota honokiyore no hoibolla hũšiyari diye edde mana goijje.
LUK 9:22 Isaye hodde, "Adomor Futottu beši duk buggora foribo. Ar murobbi okkol, ḍõr imam edde alem okkole hibare batil goribo edde mari felaibo. Ar tin dinor din hibattu morattu uṛizagoi foribo."
LUK 9:23 Toi hibaye beggunore hodde: "Honokiye zodi ãr fise aito issa gore, hite nizore ošikar gorok edde hite fotti din nizor duk hoštore bordaš gori ãr fise fise aiyok.
LUK 9:24 Kiyollahoile ze honokiye hitar nizor foran basaito sa, hite hiyan haraibo. Kintu ze honokiye ãlla boli hitar nizor foran hara, hite hiyan basaibo.
LUK 9:25 Hitar ki lab oiye, zodi šara duniyai hama, kintu nizore harai fele otóba nošto gori fele?
LUK 9:26 Kiyollahoile ze honokiye ãre edde ãr kalamore mainšor munttu šorome ošikar gore. Adomor Fut zehon nizor, edde fobitro firista okkol edde Bafor tozolli loi aibo, hẽtte hibaye o he manuš okkolore ošikar goribo.
LUK 9:27 "Ãi tũwarare soiyi hoir, eṛe tũwarar butore en hozon ase zara Allar raijjo no deke foijjonto hitara hono mote moutor fiyala no fibo."
LUK 9:28 In okkol hoi ek hafta bade, Isaye munazat goribolla Fitor, Yuhanna, Yakub, itarare loi ek faharor uwore giye.
LUK 9:29 Munazat goribar šomot Isar mukor siyara bodoli giyegoi edde hibar fušak ujjol dola oi giyegoi.
LUK 9:30 Ar so, duizon manuš, Musa edde Eliyas, hitara Isa loi hota howa šuru goijje.
LUK 9:31 Hitara keramoti zak zomok loi deha diye edde Zeruzalemot Isaye ze moutor muamui oito zar, hitara he befare hotabatra hoiye.
LUK 9:32 He šomot Fitor edde hitar sãti okkol bári gumot aššil. Hitara seton oi Isar keramot edde oi duizon manuš zara Isar fũwati tiyai taikke hitarare deikke.
LUK 9:33 He duizon Isar hãsottu zargoide šomot Isare Fitore hodde: "Huzur, ãra eṛe aside bala oiye. Ãra tinnan bãša banai, ekkan õnolla, ekkan Musalla, ar ekkan Eliyasolla." (Kintu Fitore asole ki hor hin hite nize o no zane.)
LUK 9:34 Fitore hen hodde šomot ekkan miyula ai hitarar uwore saiya oiye. Hitara zẽtte miyular butore oiye, hẽtte hitara beši ḍoraiye.
LUK 9:35 Ar he miyular butottu endilla ek abaz funa giye, "Iba ãr fut, he basai gora, hibar hota fuinno."
LUK 9:36 Abaz oi mottor Isare ekela deha giye. Ar hitara suf gori taikke, zin zin sahabi okkole dekkil hin he šomot honokiyore no ho.
LUK 9:37 Tarfordin zehon hitara he faharottu lami aišše, bout mainše Isa loi deha goijje.
LUK 9:38 Ar so, zamor butottu ekzone guzori hodde, "Huzur, aroz gorir, ãr fuwawar uzu suk tuli so, kiyollahoile ite šude ãr lehar ek fut.
LUK 9:39 So, ek ruhuye itare hamela gorer, ar atikka kiskisai uṛe. He ruhuye itare musori dore, henot ite muk bai fena bair gore, ar ruhuye itare zal zal gori kub hošto di erizagoi.
LUK 9:40 Ãi õnor sahabi okkolore foriyad goijjilam, zene hitara ibare sarai de, kintu hitara no fare."
LUK 9:41 Toi Isaye zuwabe hodde: "Oh obiššaši edde bonḍor dol! Ar hotokal ãi tũwarar fũwati takiyum edde tũwarare bordaš goriyum? Tor futore loi eṛe ai!"
LUK 9:42 He fuwawa aiyerde hen šomot oi bod ruhuye hitare felai diye edde hora gori musori doijje. Kintu Isaye he napak ruhure dõk diyore fuwaware aram goijje. Toi hitare bafor hãse firai diye.
LUK 9:43 Henot beggune Allar he mohimar šokti deki tajjuf oiye. Toi hár manuš okkol Isaye goijjede hamot tajjuf oiyede šomot, Isaye sahabi okkolore hodde,
LUK 9:44 "Tũwara ei šob hota mon di funo! Kiyollahoile Adomor Futore manuš okkolor hatot tuli diya oibo."
LUK 9:45 Kintu hitara he hota buzi no fare, edde he hotar mani hitarattu gufon raka oiye, zenneki hitara buzi uṛi no fare, ar he babute Isattu fusar goitte o hitara ḍoraiye.
LUK 9:46 Sahabi okkol hone beggunottuwaro ḍõr hiyan loi hitarar butore hota haṛa haṛi oiye.
LUK 9:47 Isaye hitarar monor baf buzi fariyore ek gura fuware loi hibar ḍake tiyagoraiye.
LUK 9:48 Toi sahabi okkolore hodde, "Ze honokiye ãr name ei gura fuwaware gose, hite ãre gose. Ar ze honokiye ãre gose, hite hibare gose ze ãre defeṛaiye. Kiyollahoile ze tũwarar butore beggunottuwaro šoṛo, hite oilde dõr."
LUK 9:49 Bade Yuhannaye hodde, "Ustad, õnor name ekzon mainše but saradde dekkilam, hite ãrar dolot node hetolla buli ãra hitare mana goijjilam."
LUK 9:50 Kintu Isaye hodde, "Tũwara hitare mana no goijjo! Kiyollahoile ze tũwarar bifokke no hitede tũwarar fokke ase."
LUK 9:51 Ar zehon Isare uwore tuli loi zaibar ṭaim hãse aišše, hetunot Isa Zeruzalemor mikka zaibolla ek mone ereda gori felaiye.
LUK 9:52 Ar Isaye zaibar age hóborguwa okkolore defeṛaiye. Ar hitara zai Sameri okkolor farat góille, Isalla entezam gori farefan.
LUK 9:53 Isaye Zeruzalem zaibo ereda goijje buli heṛiyar manuš okkole Isare no gose.
LUK 9:54 Hendilla deki Isar sahabi Yakub edde Yuhannaye fusar goredde, "Malik, õne ki issa goro, Eliyase zendilla goijje hendilla ãra hoi, asmanottu oin lami ai itarare dongšo gori felok?"
LUK 9:55 Kintu Isaye hitarar mikka muk firai dõk diye edde hodde, tũwara no zano ne, tũwarare hon ruh loi banaiye? Adomor Futore manušor zibon dongšo goribolla faṭa oiyede no, kintu uddar goribolla.
LUK 9:56 Tarfore hitara oinno ekkan farat giyegoi.
LUK 9:57 Hitara fõt bai zadde hen šomot ekzon manuše Isare hodde, "Õne zeṛe zo ãi o õnor fũwati heṛe zaiyum."
LUK 9:58 Isaye hitare hodde, "Šiyal okkolottu gãt ase edde asmanor faikottu baha ase, kintu Adomor Fute mata rakibar hono zaga nai."
LUK 9:59 Isaye ar ekzonore hodde: "Ãr fisa lo." Kintu hite hodde: "Huzur, age ãr bafore dohon gorai aito do."
LUK 9:60 Isaye hitare hodde: "Mora okkole mora okkolore dohon gora ok, kintu tui zai Allar raijjor tobolig gor."
LUK 9:61 Ar ekzone Isare hodde, "Malik, ãi õnor fisa loiyum, kintu age ãre ãr góror manuš okkolottu bidai loi aito do."
LUK 9:62 Isaye hitare hodde, "Ze honokiye naholor kuṛi dori fis mikka firisa hite Allar raijjor laikka oi no fare."
LUK 10:1 Hiyar bade Malik Isaye aro oinno hoittor duizonor mainšore basona goijje. Ar Isa nize ze ze šohor ba fara okkolot zaibolla ereda goijje, he šomosto zaga edde šohorot hiba zaibar age duizon duizon gori hitarare defeṛaiye.
LUK 10:2 Isaye hitarare hodde, "Hãsa, dán beši foille kintu dán daoya manuš hom. Etolla danor malikor hãse foriyad goro zene malike hibar dán daibolla manuš faṭai de.
LUK 10:3 Tũwara zo! Ãi tũwarare sool hisabe genḍa bagor okkolor butore defeṛair.
LUK 10:4 Ṭiyar beg, hoilla ba ṭengor šendal fũwati no loiyo, edde fõtot honokiyor loi mulot oibolla no tiyaiyo.
LUK 10:5 "Kintu tũwara ze górot goliba, heṛe tũwara foila hoiba, 'Ei górot šanti aiyok.'
LUK 10:6 Zodi heṛe šantir manuš take henoile tũwarar šanti hitar uwore ziraibo. Ar zodi hendilla honokiye no take hentoile tũwarar šanti tũwarar hãse firi aibo.
LUK 10:7 Ar he górot taikko edde hitara zin há fiya gorito de hin haiyo, kiyollahoile ze ham gore hite beton faibar laikka. Ek gór sari ar ek górot no zaiyogoi.
LUK 10:8 "Zodi hono farat zo edde heṛeiyar manuš okkole tũwarare gose toile hitara tũwarare zin de hin haiyo!
LUK 10:9 He farar biyaraimma okkolore aram goijjo edde hoiba, 'Allar raijjo tũwarar hãse aišše.'
LUK 10:10 Kintu zodi hono farat zo edde heṛiyar mainše tũwarare no gose, he farar rasta rasta zai en hoiba,
LUK 10:11 'Tũwarar farar ze dul ãrar ṭengot boijje hin o ãra zari felailam, tarfore o tũwara zani rako ze Allar raijjo hãse aišše.'
LUK 10:12 Ãi tũwarare hoir, bisaror din he farattuwaro Súdum šohoror doša šowa zaibo.
LUK 10:13 "Korasin šohor tor bifod! Betsaida šohor tor bifod! Ze šob keramot tũwarar butore gora oiye, hin okkol zodi Tiros edde Sidon šohorot gora oito, toile hitara bout din age salar šoṭ findi saiyot boi gunattu mon firaito.
LUK 10:14 Kintu bisaror din tũwarar došattuwaro Tiros edde Sidon šohoror doša šowa zaibo.
LUK 10:15 Ar tui Kofornahum šohor, tũi bole ki asman uwore uṛibi? Honodin oi no fare, tore meṛir nise fatalfurot feli diya oibo!
LUK 10:16 "Zara tũwarar hota fune hitara ãr hota fune. Zara tũwarare hela gore, hitara ãre hela gore. Kintu zara ãre hela gore, hitara ãre ze defeṛaiye hibare hela gore."
LUK 10:17 He hoittor duizon ummote kušir sãte firi aišše edde hodde: "Malik, õnor nam dorile bod ruh okkole foijjonto ãrar hota fune!"
LUK 10:18 Toi Isaye hitarare hodde, "Ãi Šoitanore asmanottu bizoli somkefana gori nise foredde dekki.
LUK 10:19 So, ãi tũwarare haf edde bissure ṭenge fiši maribolla edde dušmon Šoitanor har šokti loi ziti faribolla šokti diyi. Hono kissuye tũwarare hoti gori no faribo.
LUK 10:20 Kintu bod ruhuye tũwarar hota fune boli kuši no goijjo bolke behostot tũwarar nam leka oiye boli kuši goro."
LUK 10:21 Hetunot Isaye Pak Ruhur kušiye ullaš oi hodde, "Ya Baf, tũi asman edde duniyair malik, ãi tũware šukuriya zanai, kiyollahoile ei hota okkol tũi giyani edde buddiman okkolottu lukairaki masum gura fuwaindor hãse forhaš goijjo. Oi, Baf, iyan tũwar bala issa.
LUK 10:22 "Ãr Bafe ãr hatot hár kissu diye. Baf sara ar honokiye no zane Fuwa honnuwade hiyan, ar Fuwa sara honokiye no zane Baf honnuwade hiyan. Ar Fuwaye zar hãse Bafore forhaš goitto sa šude hite zane."
LUK 10:23 Toi hitara zehon ekela oiye, hibaye hitarar mikka firiyore hodde, "Rahamot ok he suk okkolor uwore, tũwara dekodde hin zara deker.
LUK 10:24 Ãi tũwarare hoir: Tũwara dekorde hin bout nobi okkole edde badša okkole saito issa goijje kintu saibolla no fa, ar funito issa goijje kintu funito no fa."
LUK 10:25 Ar so, ekzon dórmiyo aleme Isare forikka gori saibolla hibar hãse aiyore hodde, "Huzur, akeri zibonor odihar faite ãttu ki gora foribo?"
LUK 10:26 Isaye hodde, "Ainot ki leka ase? Heṛe hondilla foijjo?"
LUK 10:27 He hite hodde: "'Tũi tũwar šomosto dil, šomosto mon, šomosto foran, šomosto šokti, diyore Allah Mabudore muhabbot goro. Ar tũwar ḍen gór bam gójjare nizor zani muhabbot goro.'"
LUK 10:28 Isaye hitare hodde: "Tũi ṭik zuwab diyo. Zodi tũi he mozin gorat tako, toi tũi o zibon faiba."
LUK 10:29 He aleme hitar nizor šorman basaibolla Isare abar hodde, "Bala, ãr ḍen gór bam gójja hontara?"
LUK 10:30 Zuwabe Isaye endilla hoiye: "Ekzon manuš Zeruzalemottu fõt bai lami Zeriku šohorot zar, hen šomot hite ḍahaitor hatot foijje. Ḍahait okkole hitar findonor hoorgun kuli loi felaiye edde hitare mari ada mora abostat raki giyegoi.
LUK 10:31 Goṭona sokkore ekzon imam o he fõt bai lami aišše. Hite he manušware deki rasta fašhaṛi gilgoi.
LUK 10:32 Bade hendilla ekzon dórmogór šasiyot goroya Levi o he zagat ai manušware deki, hite o fašhaṛi giyegoi.
LUK 10:33 Tarbade Sameriya elehar ekzon manuš, zarare šomazot niroš zat hisabe gona oito, he fõt bai zaite zaite oi manušwar hãsa hãsi aišše. Hitare deki tattu doya laigge,
LUK 10:34 edde hitar ḍake zai, hitar gá okkolot tel edde ãnguror roš ḍalidi hinore bandi diye. Tarfore hitar nizor zanuwaror uwore buwai ek šoraihanat loigiye edde hitare šeba zotton goijje.
LUK 10:35 Tarfordin he Sameriyar manušwaye duiyan dinar šoraihanar menezarore diyore hodde, 'Ei manušwar adorhatir goriba, beši za kissu horos o, hin ãi abar aile šud gori diyum.'
LUK 10:36 "Ehon tũwattu ki mone o? Ei tinzonor maze hone he ḍahaitor hatot fora manušwar ḍen gór bam gójja?"
LUK 10:37 He aleme zuwabe hodde, "Ze manušwaye hitare ador hatir goijje hite." Toi Isaye hitare hodde, "Toile tũi o zo he mozin gorogoi."
LUK 10:38 Ar hitara zadde šomot Isaye hono ek farat góille, heṛe Martá name ek maya fuwaye hibar górot Isare meheman hisabe goisse.
LUK 10:39 Moriyam name ekzon hibattu boin aššil. Hibaye Malik Isar ṭengor ḍake ai boi Isar hota funer.
LUK 10:40 Kintu Martá góror harz harbare beši duwadit aššil. Hibaye hitara dunizonor hãse aiyore hodde: "Malik õne ki kissu bafi no sor ne, ãr boine ãre beggun halika ga gora diyede? Õne hibare ãre modot gori dito ho!"
LUK 10:41 Kintu malik Isaye zuwabe hodde: "Martá! Tui bout hame duwadit edde sintat.
LUK 10:42 Kintu ekkan šude zoruri ham ase. Moriyame he hamman basi loiye, hetolla hiyan hibattu loi fela no zaibo."
LUK 11:1 Ek šome Isaye hono ek zagat duwa gorer. Duwa gora šeš oi bade Isar sahabi okkolor butottu ekzone Isare hodde: "Malik, Yahyaye zendilla hibar šagirit okkolore duwa gora šikaiye hendilla õne ãrare o duwa gora šikao."
LUK 11:2 Isaye hitarare hodde: "Tũwara duwa goribar šomot endilla ho: "'Ya, ãrar behosti Baf, Tũwar nam fobitro boli mana ok. Tũwar raijjo aiyok.
LUK 11:3 Fotti dinor haiddo tũi fotti din ãrare do.
LUK 11:4 Ãrar har gunare maf gori do, zendilla ãra o maf gori hitarare, zara ãrar berudde hosuri gore. ar ãrare forikkat foitto no diyo.'"
LUK 11:5 Tarfore Isaye hitarare hodde, "Mone goro! Tũwarar butore hono ekzonottu ekzon bondu ase. Ar hite zodi ada raitta hitar bondur hãse zai ho, 'Bondu, ãre tinnwa ruṭi udar do,
LUK 11:6 kiyollahoile ãr ek bondu musafer oi ãr heṛe aišše, hitar munttu ani dibolla ãttu kissu nai.'
LUK 11:7 Henoile ki he manušwaye butottu tai en zuwab dibo ne, 'Ãre hošto no diyo, ehon doroza banda, ar ãr fuwain ãr ḍake gum giye. Ãi uṛi tũware kissu di no farir.'
LUK 11:8 Ãi tũwarare hoir, hite zodi bondu hisabe uṛi no de, tarfore o hite bar bar foriyad goredde hiyanolla buli oile o hite uṛibo edde hitar zorulot mozin hitare hin dibo.
LUK 11:9 "Etolla ãi tũwarare hoir: Munazatot so, toi tũwarare diya oibo. Tuwo, toi tũwara tuwai faiba. Dorozat ṭulki maro, toi tũwaralla kula oibo.
LUK 11:10 Zara mage hitara to fottizonore diya o, ze tuwa, hite tuwai fa, ar ze dorozat ṭulki de, hitalla doroza kula o.
LUK 11:11 "Tũwarar butore endilla baf hone ase, fuwaye mas magile haf de,
LUK 11:12 otóba ãnḍa magile bissu de?
LUK 11:13 Tũwara zodi horaf oi bade o tũwarar fuwain okkolore uttom uttom ziniš di zano, toile ei hota hoto haṭi ze, zara mage hitarare behostiyo Bafe Pak Ruhure dibo!"
LUK 11:14 Ar ek bar Isaye ek buk but dafaiye. But zehon bair oigiyegoi, he buk manušwaye hota howa šuru goijje. Henot manuš okkol tajjuf oiye.
LUK 11:15 Kintu hitarar butore kiye kiye hodde, "Butor raza Belsebulor modote ite but bair gore."
LUK 11:16 Ar kiye kiye forikka gori saibolla Isare behostottu ekkan sinno dehaito hoiye.
LUK 11:17 Kintu Isaye hitarar monor baf buzi faijje edde hibaye hitarare hodde: "Ze raijjo bag o hiyan dongšo o, ar gór zodi góror bifokke o hiyan dongšo o.
LUK 11:18 Hendilla, Šoitane o zodi hitar nizor berudde ai tiya, toile ken gori hitar raijjo ṭikibo? Ar tũwara hor ãi Belsebulor modote but sarai.
LUK 11:19 Ašša! Ãi zodi Belsebulor modote but sarai, toile tũwarar nizor manuš okkole har modote but sara? Tũwara soiyi hor ne hiyan hitara bisar gori sok.
LUK 11:20 Kintu ãi zodi Allar kemota loi but sarai, henoile Allar raijjo tũwarar hãse aišše.
LUK 11:21 "Ekzon bolwala mainše zodi hár ḍoilla ostro loi nizor gór fahara de, toile hitar mal fottoro nirafodot take.
LUK 11:22 Kintu hitattuwaro bolwala honokiye zodi ai hitar loi zite, toile hite ze ostro okkolor uwore nirbor goijje hin oi manušwaye hari loi felaibo, ar luṛor mallun loi zai bag goribogoi.
LUK 11:23 "Ãi hoir: Zodi honokiye ãr fokke no take toile hitede ãr bifokke roiye, ze ãr fũwati no feṛa hitede šiṛe."
LUK 11:24 "Hono napak ruh zehon ekzon manušor butottu bair oi zagoi, hetunot hite aramor zaga tuwaibolla šuwana zagat zai gura fira gore. Bade zodi hite hendilla no fa, hite hode, 'Ãi ze górottu niyoli aiššyi he górot ãi abar firi zaiyumboi.'
LUK 11:25 Firi ai sadde, górgan foriškar edde hãzaiya.
LUK 11:26 Hetunot hite zai hitattuwaro aro hãt zon horaf napak ruhure fũwati loi ane edde heṛe goli bošobaš gore. Hiyanolla boli he manušwar doša foila barottuwaro šešor doša aro horaf o."
LUK 11:27 Isaye ei šob hota hodde šomot mainšor zamottu hono ek maya fuwaye guzori Isare hodde, "Mubarok he feṭ, ze õnore feṛot loiye edde bukor dud habaiye."
LUK 11:28 Kintu Isaye hodde: "Iyanottuwaro hitarare mubarak zara Allar kalam fune edde hindilla gore."
LUK 11:29 Toi aro manuš okkole Isare sairo ḍakottu berai doijje, hetunot Isaye hodde, "Ei halor manuš okkol horaf, hitara sinno tuwa, kintu Yunus nobir sinno bade ar hono sinno hitarare deha no oibo.
LUK 11:30 Nineveh šohoror manuš okkololla zendilla Yunus nobi nize sinno oil, ṭik hendilla ei halor manuš okkololla o Adomor Fut sinno oibo.
LUK 11:31 Bisaror din doin dešor raniye ei halor manuš okkolor fũwati uṛi itarare duši goribo, kiyollahoile hibaye badša Soloimanor giyanor hota funibolla duniyair šeš ḍakottu aiššil. Ar so, eṛe Soloimanottuwaro aro mohan ekzon ase.
LUK 11:32 Bisaror din Nineveh šohoror manuš okkole ei halor manuš okkolor fũwati uṛi itarare duši goribo, kiyollahoile Yunus nobir toboligor duwara Nineveh šohoror manuš okkole gunattu mon firail. Ar so, eṛe Yunusottuwaro aro mohan ekzon ase.
LUK 11:33 "Serag zalai honokiye ũjja góror tole ba laiyor nise no rake, bolke hiyan seragor tokor uwore rake, zene zara butore za hitara fohor deke.
LUK 11:34 Suk oilde gar serag, tũwar suk zodi taza o, hin hendilla oiyede haron oilde, gagan fohore furaiyade hetolla. Kintu suk zodi taza no o, hin hendilla oiyede haron oilde, gaganot andar ase.
LUK 11:35 Hetolla so, tũwar butore ze fohor ase hiyan hono andarot ne.
LUK 11:36 Tũwar šara ga zodi fohore furaiya o, edde ekkagori o andar no take, ṭik serag zendilla nizor teze tũware fohor de, hendilla tũwar hara ga furafuri bafe fohore furaiya oibo."
LUK 11:37 Isa hota howa šeš gori bade ekzon forošiye Isare hánar dawat diye. Hibaye butore zai hána haito boišše.
LUK 11:38 Isaye hána háibar age hat no duwede deki forošiwaye ammuwak oiye.
LUK 11:39 Kintu Malik Isaye hitare hodde: "Tũwara Foroši okkole fanir fiyala edde deššir bar ḍakottu foriškar goro kintu tũwarar butore lalos edde naformaniye boraiya.
LUK 11:40 Murokko manuš okkol! Ze baror ḍak banaiye, hibaye ki butoror ḍak o no bana ne?
LUK 11:41 Bolke deššir butore za za ase hin gorib okkolore dan goro, toi dekiba, beggun tũwaralla foriškar oibo.
LUK 11:42 "Bifod tũwara Foroši okkolore, kiyollahoile tũwara Allare fudina, tez fata edde hár ḍoilla hakor doš bagor ek bag di tako. Kintu niyai bisar edde Allar muhabbotor mikka diyan no do. Foilagan falon goribar fũware fũware dusoragan falon gora o tũwarar dorhari.
LUK 11:43 "Bifod tũwara Foroši okkolore, muzolišhanar mum mikkar zagat boite edde rasta gaṛot ijjot fare muhabbot goro.
LUK 11:44 "Bifod tũwara Foroši okkolore, tũwara en hobor okkolor ḍoilla zinor hono sinno no take, edde no zani mainše heṛe uwottu ãṛe, ar hitara napak o."
LUK 11:45 Hetunot dórmo šikoya alem okkolor butottu ekzone Isare hodde, "Huzur, õne ei hota hoi ãrare o ofoman goror."
LUK 11:46 Isaye hitarare hodde, "Bifod tũwara dórmo šikoya alem okkolore! Tũwara manušor uwore bor fũza tuli do, kintu hitara hin mani farefan modot gori hoi uggwa õl o no laro.
LUK 11:47 "Bifod tũwarare, tũwara nobi okkolor hoborore mazar banao, otoso tũwarar baf dada okkole hitarare kun goijje.
LUK 11:48 Iyan deki buza zar ze tũwara tũwarar baf dadar hamot ekmot oiyo, kiyollahoile hitara mari felaiye ar tũwara hitarar hoborore mazar banayo.
LUK 11:49 Etolla giyani Allaye Allar kalamot hodde, 'Ãi hitarar hãse nobi okkol edde asab okkolore defeṛaiyum. Hitarar butottu ho ekzonore hitara kun goribo edde ar kissur uwore ottisar goribo.'
LUK 11:50 Hetolla duniyair foilar šuru oite šuru gori zetozon nobire kun gora oiye, hitarar louwor dai oibo ei halor manuš okkol.
LUK 11:51 Habilor kun oiyede oite šuru gori Zakariya, zare pak zaga edde dórmogóror maza mazi zagat kun gora oiye. Oi, ãi tũwarare hoir, ei halor manuš okkol ei louwor dai oibo.
LUK 11:52 "Bifod tũwara dórmo šikoya alem okkololla! Tũwara giyanor sabi nizor hãse raki diyo. Giyanor butore tũwara o no golila, ar zara butore goilto saiye hitarare o tiya garai felaiyo."
LUK 11:53 Toi Isaye hentu niyoli zargoide šomot dórmiyo alem okkol edde Foroši okkole mezaz gorom gori bout ḍoilla suwal okkol loi Isar uwore zafai foijje.
LUK 11:54 Hitara Isare mukor hotat bul doribolla fand buwai raikke.
LUK 12:1 Hen šomot hazar hazar manuš en bafe dola oiye, hitara ṭelateli gori ekzone ar ekzonor uwore fora šuru goijje. Hetunot Isaye foila sahabi okkolor uzu firi hodde, "Tũwara Foroši okkolor šikkattu hũšiyar, hin tũwarar gat no farafan, kiyollahoile hin bonḍami.
LUK 12:2 Guijja kissu nai, zin forhaš no oibo, edde gufon kissu nai, zin zana no zaibo.
LUK 12:3 Otoso tũwara andarot za kissu hoiyo, hin fohorot funa zaibo, edde zin góror butore hane hane ho, hin sador uwottu guzori howa oibo.
LUK 12:4 "O ãr bondu okkol, ãi tũwarare hoir, zara ga dongšo gori bade ar kissu gori no fare, hitarare no ḍoraiyo.
LUK 12:5 Harare ḍoraiba ãi tũwarare hiyan hoir. Tũwarare mari felai bade jahannamot dibar kemota zattu ase hibare ḍoro. Oi ãi tũwarare hoir, hibare ḍoro.
LUK 12:6 Fãswa fiyajjare ki dui foišaye no bese ne? Tarfore o Allaye hinor uggware o forai no fele.
LUK 12:7 En ki tũwarar matar sullun o Allattu gona ase. No ḍoraiyo, tũwara beši fiyajja okkolottuwaro aro beši dami.
LUK 12:8 "Ãi tũwarare hoir, ze honokiye manušor šaikkat ãre šikar gore, Adomor Fute o Allar firistar šaikkat hitare šikar goribo.
LUK 12:9 Kintu ze honokiye ãre manušor šaikkat ošikar gore, Adomor Fute o Allar firistar šaikkat hitare ošikar goribo.
LUK 12:10 Adomor Futor berudde honokiye hota hoile, hite maf faibo. Kintu ze honokiye Pak Ruhure hingša gore, hitare maf gora no oibo.
LUK 12:11 "Ar mainše tũwarare zẽtte sinagogot edde šašon goroyar sarme loi za, hetunot ki zuwab diba ba ki hoiba he babute sinta no goijjo.
LUK 12:12 Kiyollahoile hetunot ki howa foribo tũwarare Pak Ruhuye šikai dibo."
LUK 12:13 Zamilar butottu ekzon manuše Isare hodde: "Huzur, ãr báiyore ãr loi miraz borat goitto ho!"
LUK 12:14 Kintu Isaye hodde, "Bondu, tũwarar uwore bisarhar ba miraz bag gori doya hoi ãre hone tuille?"
LUK 12:15 Bade Isaye manuš okkolore hodde, "Hũšiyar! Har ḍoilla lalsittu nizore basai rako, kiyollahoile ekzon mainšottu zafdi forefan dón šombotti oile o, hine zibon no de."
LUK 12:16 Ar Isaye hitarare ei mesal kahanigan hoiye, "Ekzon zomidaror zobinot kethõla beši oiye.
LUK 12:17 Henot hite mone mone sinta gori hodde, 'Ãi ehon ki goijjum? Ãttude hin rakibar zaga nai.'
LUK 12:18 "Bade hite hodde, 'Ãi endilla goijjum. Ãr gudam górgun bangi felai hinore ḍõr ḍõr gori banaiyum edde ãi ãr kuraffati edde ãr zinišfati okkolore heṛe zoma gori rakiyum.
LUK 12:19 Bade ãi nizor foranore hoiyum, foran, tolla bout bosorolla beša beši bala bala zinišfati dola goijja ase, há fiya gor, aram gor, asanot zibon haṛa.'
LUK 12:20 "Kintu Allaye hitare hodde, 'O bekub, aijja raitta tor foran hori loi zaiboi, toile tui in zinor bondobos goijjos, hin har oibo?'
LUK 12:21 "Ze nizolla dón zoma gore kintu Allar nozdikot dónban no hitalla hendilla oibo."
LUK 12:22 Bade Isaye sahabi okkolore hodde: "Etolla ãi tũwarare hoir: Ki háiyum hoi foranor babute, otóba ki findiyum hoi gar babute sinta no goijjo.
LUK 12:23 Kiyollahoile foran haiddottuwaro ar ga horottuwaro ḍõr ziniš.
LUK 12:24 Hawagunor uzu so, hine no laga, ar no da. Hinottu gudam ba hãijja o nai, to kintu Allaye hitarare o ahar de. Ar tũwara to faikottuwaro bout dami!
LUK 12:25 Ho sai, tũwarar butore bafa sinta gori hone šude ek gonḍa nizor aiyu barai fariba?
LUK 12:26 Zehon tũwara hen šoṛo ham o gori no faro, toile baki befare kiyolla sinta goriba?"
LUK 12:27 "Bafi so, full ken gori bare. Hine hono ham o no gore, hor banaibolla fũta o no haṛe. Kintu ãi tũwarare hoir: Badša Soloimane hibar šomosto zak zomokottu o inor ekkanor ḍoilla nizore hãzai no fare.
LUK 12:28 Maṛot ze ker ase, zin hailla sulat felai diya oibo, hin zodi Allaye endilla gori hãzai fare, toile oh olfo biššaši okkol! Allaye tũwarare hãzaibode hiyan aro hoto beši haṭi!
LUK 12:29 Ar ki há fiya goriba in loi tũwara no baiffo, sinta no goijjo.
LUK 12:30 In okkol to zara Allare biššaš no gore hitara tuwa, kintu tũwarar bafe zane ze tũwarattu in okkolor dorhar ase.
LUK 12:31 Hinottuwaro bolke Allar raijjor talaš goro, toi in beggun o tũwarare diya oibo."
LUK 12:32 "Oh šoṛo dol, no ḍorais! Kiyollahoile tũwarar Bafor bala issa oilde, he raijjore tũwarare diya.
LUK 12:33 Tũwarattu zin ase, hin besi horat hisabe dan goro. Ar behostot ofurani dón zoma goro, zeṛe sur o hãse nu aibo, fuk zuke o hoti gori no faribo.
LUK 12:34 Kiyollahoile zeṛe tũwarar dón, heṛe tũwarar dil o takibo."
LUK 12:35 "Tũwarar kiyail bandi tiyar tako edde serag zalai rako.
LUK 12:36 Ar tũwara en mainšor ḍoilla o, zitara hitarar malik biyar melattu firi aiyer ne sai take, zendilla neki malik ai dorozat ṭulki dile, hitara malikore toratori doroza kuli di fare.
LUK 12:37 Šuki he gulam okkol, zarare góror malike ai seton dekibo. Ãi tũwarare soiyi hoir, he malike kiyail bandi hitarare hánar ṭebilot buwaibo edde ḍake zai hitarare luid goribo.
LUK 12:38 Šuki hitara, zarare góror malike ada raitta ba dolfohor ode hetunot ai o seton dekibo.
LUK 12:39 Kintu iyan buzo: Sur hon šomoi loi aibo hiyan zodi góror malike zainto, toile seton takito, nizor górot šingar dito no dito.
LUK 12:40 Hetolla tũwara o tiyar tako, kiyollahoile ze šomot mone no goriba, he šomot Adomor Fut aibo."
LUK 12:41 Hetunot Fitore fusar goredde, "Malik, ei mesal ki õne ãrare hodde naki beggunore hodde?"
LUK 12:42 Malik Isaye hodde, "He biššaši, buddiwala menezar hiba honnuwa, zare hitar malike hibar gulam okkolor uwore buwaibo hitarare ṭãim motabek hána dibolla.
LUK 12:43 Šuki he gulam, zare malike ai hendilla goredde dekibo.
LUK 12:44 Ãi tũwarare soiyi hoir, hitare he góror malike hár kissur uwore zimma dibo.
LUK 12:45 Kintu mone goro! He gulame zodi mone mone ho, ãr malik aite aro deri ase hoi gulam edde bandi okkolore mara dora gore edde há fiya gori fól owa šuru gore.
LUK 12:46 Ze din Malik aibo hoi ofekka no gore edde ze šomoir hota hite no zane, he dinor he šomot he gulamor malik aibo edde hitare haṛi bag gori obiššaši okkolor fũwati hitar zaga ṭik goribo.
LUK 12:47 "He gulam ze hitar nizor malikor issa zane, tarfore o hite tiyar no o ba malikor issa mozin no gore hitare beši fiṛa diya zaibo.
LUK 12:48 Kintu ekzone hiyan no zane edde fiṛa faibar ham goijje, hitare hom šaza diya oibo. Zare beši diya oiye, hitattu beši dabi gora oibo, ar mainše zar hãse beši rake, hitattu beši uwafes lo.
LUK 12:49 "Ãi duniyait oin zalaito aiššyi. Ar ehon zodi ãi issa goijjilamde mozin he oin zolito!
LUK 12:50 Kintu ãttu dukkor torikotor gusol muwamui owa foribo, ar hiyan furon no o foijjionto ãi hoto sifor butore asi!
LUK 12:51 Tũwara ki mone goror, ãi ki duniyaire šanti dito aiššyi? Ãi tũwarare hoir, hen no, bolke hiyanor ulda.
LUK 12:52 Ehonottu loti ek góror fãszon aleda oibo, tinzon duizonor bifokke, duizon tinzonor bifokke lagibo.
LUK 12:53 Baf fuwar bifokke, ba fuwa bafor bifokke, ma ziyor bifokke, ba zi mar bifokke, hori bouwor bifokke ba bou horir bifokke lagibo."
LUK 12:54 Mainšor dolore Isaye hodde, "Tũwara zehon fosimottu miyula uṛede deko, hetunot onegane ho, 'Zór aibo', ar hendilla o.
LUK 12:55 Ar zẽtte doinottu bataš badde deho, hetunot ho, 'Beši roidor gorom oibo,' ar hendilla o.
LUK 12:56 Munafek okkol! Tũwara duniyai edde asmanor baf buzi faro, kintu ei ṭaim buzi no faror, iyan honḍoilla hota?
LUK 12:57 "Niyai oinnai tũwara nize bisar gori kiya no sor?
