LUK 12:58 Zẽtte tũwara bifokkor manušor fũwati bisarharor hãse zo, fõtot maze rehai faibolla kušiš goro, ar no oile hite tũwarare bisarharor hãse ṭani loizaibo. Ar bisarhare fulišor hatot gosai dibo edde fuliše tũware ziyol golai eribo.
LUK 12:59 Ãi tore hoir: Zetodin šeš foiša foijjonto fũzi no felos, hetodin tui hono mote hentu baire ai no faribi."
LUK 13:1 He šomot hozon manuš Isar heṛe hazir oil. Hitara Galilor kissu mainšor babute Isare howa šuru goijje. Hitara hoiye ze, Filate ei Galilor manuššunore haṛi hitarar kurbanir zanuwaror louwor fũwati itarar louwore mišai felaiye.
LUK 13:2 Zuwabe Isaye hodde, "He Galilor mainšor uwore endilla durgoti oiye boli ki hitara dusora Galilor manušottuwaro beši gunagar boli mone goro?
LUK 13:3 Ãi tũwarare hoir, hen no! Bolke tũwara zodi o mon no firo, tũwara beggune o hendilla dongšo oi zaibagoi.
LUK 13:4 Ar no oile he aṛarozon, zarar matar uwore Šilo guid bangi fori mori gilgoi. Tũwara ki mone goro, hitara ki ar baki Zeruzalemot bošobaš goredde hitarattuwaro beši gunagar aššil?
LUK 13:5 Ãi tũwarare hoir, hen no! Bolke tũwara zodi o mon no firo, tũwara beggune o hendilla dongšo oiba."
LUK 13:6 Tarfore Isaye ei mesal kahanigan hoiye: "Ekzon manuš, hitar ãngur ketit uggwa ḍuirgula gas aššil. Hite heṛe ai ḍuirgula tuwail, kintu no fa.
LUK 13:7 Henot hite keti sõloyare hodde, 'Ãi eṛe ei gasot tin bosor mula ailam edde ḍuirgula tuwailam, kintu hono gula fa no za. Iba haṛi felaide! Iba eṛe taiyore kiyolla zobin nošto oito!'
LUK 13:8 "Kintu keti sõloyaye hodde, 'Huzur, ibare ei bosor o raki do, ãi ibar šiyoror sairo ḍakottu kuri fãš diyum.
LUK 13:9 Zodi gula lage toile to bala, ar no oile hiba haṛi felaiyo.'"
LUK 13:10 Ek dórmor din Isaye hono ek sinagogot šikka dil.
LUK 13:11 Ar so, ekzon maya fuwa, zare aṛaro bosorfan ek bod ruhuye kuza gori raikke. Hiba en behã oi gilgoi hono mote uzu oi no farito.
LUK 13:12 Isaye zehon hibare deikke, toi hibare hãse ḍaikke, ar hodde: "Oh maya fuwa, tui ošukottu azad oiyos!"
LUK 13:13 Hen hoi bade Isaye hãttan hibar uwore raikke. Ar hehon hiba uzu oi tiyai faijje edde hibaye Allar tarif gora šuru goijje.
LUK 13:14 Kintu Isaye dórmor din aram goijje boli muzolišhanar netaye naraz oiye. Hite manuš okkolore hodde: "So din ase he šob ham goribar. Ar he šomosto din okkolot aiššo edde aram oiyo, dórmor din no!"
LUK 13:15 Kintu Malik Isaye hitare zuwab diye, "Munafek okkol! Tũwara fottizone ki dórmor din tũwarar goru sool okkolore urattu kuli fani habaito no loi zo?
LUK 13:16 Toile ei maya fuwa, Ibrahimor šontan, zare Šoitane, so, aijja aṛaro bosor dori bandi raikke, he bandottu dórmor din azad fa ki zoruri no ne?"
LUK 13:17 Isaye ei hotabattara zehon hoiye, hibar bifokkor beggune šorminda oiye. Kintu Isar duwara ze šomosto mohimar ham oiye, henot baki šomosto manuš okkol kuši oiye.
LUK 13:18 Tarfore Isaye hodde, "Allar raijjo kiyor ḍoilla? Ki loi ãi hiyanor tulona diyum?
LUK 13:19 Hiyan uggwa šoṛo danar ḍoilla, hono ekzone hiba loi zai nizor baganot lagaiye, bade hiba bari uiṭṭe edde uggwa gas oiye, ar faik okkole he gasor ḍeil okkolot baha bainde."
LUK 13:20 Isaye abar hodde, "Ãi ki loi Allar raijjor tulona diyum?
LUK 13:21 Hiyan išor ḍoil, zin mayafuwainde tin barang moidat maze mišaiye, šeše hin fuli uiṭṭe."
LUK 13:22 Ar Isaye šohore šohore edde fara fara guri guri šikka di di Zeruzalemor uzu giye.
LUK 13:23 Hetunot ekzone fusar goredde, "Malik, zara uddar far, hitara ki hom manuš?" Isaye hitare hodde,
LUK 13:24 "Haiṭṭa haṛiwala doroza bai golibolla har kušiš goro! Kiyollahoile ãi tũwarare hoir, bout kiye butore goilto kušiš goribo, kintu goli no faribo.
LUK 13:25 Góror malike uṛi zehon doroza bandi felaibo bade tũwara baire tiyai doroza baijjai howa šuru goriba, 'Malik, ãralla dorozagan kuli do!' "Kintu Malike zuwab di hoibo, 'Ãi no sini tũwara hoṛiyar manuš.'
LUK 13:26 "Toi tũwara howa šuru goriba, 'Ãra tũwar ekkui fũwati há fiya goijji, ãrare fõte fõte tũi šikka dila.'
LUK 13:27 "Kintu he malike hoibo, 'ãi tũwarare no sini, tũwara honttu aiššo. Horaf manuš okkol, ãr sarmottu dur oi zogoi!'
LUK 13:28 "He zagat tũwara handa haṛi goriba edde zala zontronaniye dat loi dat gošiba. Hetunot tũwara dekiba, Ibrahim, Isak edde Yakub edde nobi okkol Allar raijjor butore ase, ar tũwarare baire felai diya oiye.
LUK 13:29 Ar fuk edde fosimottu, uttor edde doinottu manuš okkol ai Allar raijjot boibo.
LUK 13:30 Ar so, šešor hataror hono hono manuš foila oibo. Ar foila hataror hono hono manuš šešor hatarot oibo."
LUK 13:31 He šomot hoekzon Foroši Isar hãse aišše edde hibare hodde, "Huzur! Õne entu ar oinno hono mikka zogoi, kiyollahoile badša Herude tũware mari felaito sar."
LUK 13:32 Isaye hodde: "Zo, tũwara zai he šiyalore hogoi, 'Aijja edde aiyerde hailla ãi bod ruh dafair edde biyaraimma okkolore aram gorir, ar tin dinor din ãr ham šeš goriyum.'
LUK 13:33 Zen oibo ok, aijja, aiyerde hailla edde forure šeš gora foribo. Kiyollahoile en to oi no faribo, Zeruzalemor baire hono nobi dongšo o!
LUK 13:34 "Zeruzalem! Zeruzalem! Tui nobi okkolore kun goros, tor hãse zarare defeṛa o, hitarare fattor mari takos! Faikor maye zendilla hibar so okkolore fakor nise ekkui fũwati gore, ãi hoto bar hendilla tor šontan okkolore ekkui fũwati goitto issa goijji. Kintu tũwara razi no oila.
LUK 13:35 Hetolla sa, tũwarar gór tũwarar muntu hali fori taibo. Ar ãi tũwarare hoir, tũwara ãre ar deha no faiba zetun foijjonto tũwara no ho, 'Šukuriya ze Mabudor name aišše.'"
LUK 14:1 Ek bar ekzon Foroši netaye Isare hitar górot hánar dawat diye. He din aššilde dórmor din, ar manušzone kub bala gori Isar uzu kiyal raikke.
LUK 14:2 Ar so, fula biyaram oiyede hendilla ekzon ošuikka manuš Isar sarme aišše.
LUK 14:3 Toi Isaye dórmiyo alem okkol edde Foroši okkolore fusar goredde, "Musar ain mozin dórmor din honokiyore aram goro ki ejazot ase, naki nai?"
LUK 14:4 Kintu hitara nizam oi taikke. Hetunot Isaye he manušware hate dori aram gori bidai diye.
LUK 14:5 Tarbade Isaye he dórmiyo neta okkolore hodde, "Tũwara honokiyor fũwa ba goru zodi kuwat fori zagoi, dórmor din oile o ki tũwara hitarare hehon hentu tuli no lo ne?"
LUK 14:6 Kintu hitara hiyanor zuwab o di no fare.
LUK 14:7 Ar dawatot aišše de manuš okkole ijjotor zaga ken gori basi lor deki, Isaye hitarare šikka dibolla ekkan kahani hoiye:
LUK 14:8 "Zehon honokiye tũware melat dawat de, hetunot tũi hánar ṭebilor uworor zagat zai no boiššogoi. Kiyollahoile oitfare tũwattuwaro aro ijjotdar honokiyore heṛe dawat diya oiye.
LUK 14:9 Ze tũware edde hibare dawat diye hiba ai zodi tũware ho, ei zaga iyan ubare do, hetunot to tũi šorom faiba. Ar tũwattu beggunottuwaro nisor zagat zai bowagoi foribo.
LUK 14:10 Tũware honokiye dawat dile, bolke beggunottuwaro nisor zagat zai boiyo. Hen oile dawat diyede góror malike aiyore tũware hoibo, 'Bondu aro bala zagat zai boyogoi.' Hetunot oinno meheman okkolor sarme tũi ijjotta oiba.
LUK 14:11 Kiyollahoile ze nizore usol gore hitare niso gora oibo, ar ze nizore niso gore hitare usol gora oibo."
LUK 14:12 Ar ze Isare dawat diye, hitare Isaye hodde, "Tũi zẽtte dũijjar otóba hazinnar hána goro, hẽtte tũwar bondu ba báiyaindore otóba egena gušṭire ba tuwangor ḍen gór bam góijjare dawat no diyo. Hen gorile oitofare hitara o tũware dawat dibo. Ar ei bafe tũwar dawat fũzi zaiboi.
LUK 14:13 Kintu tũi zẽtte hánar bebosta goro, hẽtte gorib, lula, anda edde ãtur, in okkolore ḍako.
LUK 14:14 Henot tũwar balai oibo, kiyollahoile tũware firai dibolla hitarattu kissu no takibo, forhesgar okkol morattu uwafes zinda oibar šomot hinor enam faiba."
LUK 14:15 Zara hána haito boišše hitarar butottu ekzone ei hota funi Isare hodde, "Hite hoto baggitta, ze Allar raijjot haito boibo."
LUK 14:16 Isaye hitare hodde, "Doro, hono ekzon mainše ekkan ḍõr mela goijje. He melat bout mainšore dawat diya oiye.
LUK 14:17 Mela zehon oiye, hite hitar gulamore di dawat diyede manuš okkolore hoito defeṛaiye, 'Aio, ehon hár kissu tiyar oiye.'"
LUK 14:18 "Kintu hitara ekzonor bade ekzone beggune bahana deha šuru goijje. Foila ekzone hodde, 'Ãi kissu zobin kinni, ãttu zaire hin sagoi forer. Ãi dawatot zai no faridde hiyanolla maf sai.'
LUK 14:19 "Ar ekzone hodde, 'Ãi fãs zura bolod goru kinni, hinore bala horaf forikka goitto zair. Ãi dawatot zai no faridde hiyanolla maf sai.'
LUK 14:20 "Oinno ar ekzone hodde, 'Ãi biya goijji, hetolla ãi zai no farir.'
LUK 14:21 "Toi he gulam firi zai hitar malikore ei šob hota zanaiyegoi. Henot góror malike hitar gulamore rag gori hodde, 'Tui toratori šohoror rasta rasta edde goliye goliye za, gorib lula, anda, ãtur okkolore eṛe loi ai.'
LUK 14:22 "Hite giye edde malike zen zen hoiye hen hen goijje. Toi hite górot firi ai hodde, 'Huzur, kintu ehono kissu hána háibar zaga hali ase.'
LUK 14:23 "Henot malike gulamore hodde, 'Šohoror baire rasta rasta edde fõte fõte za, eṛe aibolla mainšore zurgor, zene ãr gór bori zagoi.'
LUK 14:24 Ãi tũwarare hoir, zarare dawat diya oiye hitarar butottu honokiye ãr ei melat hána hái no faribo."
LUK 14:25 Bout manuš okkol Isar fũwati zat aššil. Isaye hitarar uzu muk firai hodde:
LUK 14:26 "Ze ãr hãse aiye hite zene nizor baf ma, bou fuwain edde bái boin, enki nizore foijjonto ãttuwaro hom adoijja boli mone gore. Hen no gorile hite ãr biššaši oi no fare.
LUK 14:27 Ze honokiye fotti din nizor duk hoštore bordaš gori ãr fise no aiye, hite ãr biššaši oi no fare.
LUK 14:28 "Tũwarar butore zodi honokiye ekkan usol gór banaito sa, toile hite age boi horosor hisab gori no saibo ne? Hite saibo hiyan bandi šeš gori farefan hitattu ṭĩya ase ne nai.
LUK 14:29 Kiyollahoile hite ṭuni gãri bade zodi bandi šeš gori no fare, toile ze mainše hiyan dekibo hitara beggune ṭaṭṭa uraibo.
LUK 14:30 Hitara hoibo, 'Manušwaye banda šuru goijje kintu šeš gori no fare.'
LUK 14:31 "Zodi ekzon razaye oinno ar ekzon raza loi zuddo gorito za, hite foila boi sinta goribo, kuri hazar šonnioye ãr loi zuddo goitto aiyer, šude doš hazar šoinno loi ki ãi hitarare tiya gorai fariyum?
LUK 14:32 Zodi hite hitar loi no fare toile hite oinno raza dure taite hitar loi šanti sukti goribolla manuš defeṛaibo.
LUK 14:33 "He bafe, tũwarar butore zodi honokiye bafi sinti hitar hár kissu sari no aiye, hen oile hite ãr biššaši oi no fare.
LUK 14:34 "Nun bala ziniš, kintu nunor moza zodi nošto oi zagoi, toile hin ken gori abar nun oibo?
LUK 14:35 Hetunot hin šude felai diya sara, zobinot fãš hisabe o ar bebar gora no zaibo. "Zattu funibar han ase hite funok!"
LUK 15:1 Ar hazna adaigoroya edde gunagar manuš okkol beggune Isar kalam funibolla Isar hãse aišše.
LUK 15:2 Henot Foroši okkole edde dórmiyo alem okkole monmonai endilla howa šuru goijje, "Ei manušwaye gunagar okkolore gose edde hitarar fũwati há fiya gore."
LUK 15:3 Isaye hetunot hitarare ei mesal kahanigan hoiye:
LUK 15:4 "Doro! Tũwarar butore hono ekzonottu ek šottuwa berasool ase. Zodi hinor butottu uggwa berasool hãzi zagoi. Toile ki aro nobboi noware maṛot raki, he uggware zetun tuwai no fa he foijjonto ki tuwaito no zaibo ne?
LUK 15:5 Ar hite zehon hiba tuwai faibo, hite kuši oi hibare handot tuli loibo.
LUK 15:6 Bade górot ai hitar fũwajja okkol edde ḍen gór ba gójjare ḍaki hoibo, 'Aiyo! Ãr fũwati kuši goro, kiyollahoile ãr hãzi gilgoide berasoolguwa tuwai faiyi.'
LUK 15:7 Ãi tũwarare hoir, ṭik hendilla, ekzon gunagar gunattu mon firaile behostot aro beši kuši oibo, zarattu monfira no fore, hendilla nobboi nozon forhesgaror babute heto beši kuši no oibo.
LUK 15:8 "Otóba hono ekzon mayafuwattu doššan rufar foiša ase, hibaye zodi ekkan hãzai fele, toile serag zalai gór kũsai zetun hiyan tuwai no fa, he foijjonto bala gori tuwai no saibo ne?
LUK 15:9 Toi hibaye zehon hiyan tuwai faibo, hibaye fũwajja okkolore, ḍen gór bam gójjare ḍaki hoibo, 'Aiyo! Ãr fũwati kuši goro, kiyollahoile hãzi gilgoide foišagan ãi abar tuwai faiyi.'
LUK 15:10 Ṭik hendilla, ãi tũwarare hoir, ekzon gunagar gunattu mon firaile Allar firista okkolor maze kuši aiye."
LUK 15:11 Isaye hodde: "Ekzonottu duizon morod fuwain aššil.
LUK 15:12 Šoṛo fuwawaye bafore hodde, 'Baba, šombottir ze borat ãr bagot fore, hiyan ãre difelo.' Henot hite hitar dui futor maze šombottigun borat gori diye.
LUK 15:13 Hotodin din bade he šoṛo fuwawaye hitar har šombotti besi ṭĩya loi ek duror dešot giyoi. Ar heṛe hite altifalti zibon haṛai hitar nizor ṭĩya foiša urai felaiye.
LUK 15:14 Hin horos goijja oiye, bade he dešot kub beši raṭ oiye. Henot hite obafot fora šuru goijje.
LUK 15:15 Toi hite zai he dešor ek girostorot sahara loiyegoi. He manušwaye hitare šuwor soraibolla hitar maṛot defeṛaiye.
LUK 15:16 Toi hite šuworor adar hái feṭ boraito saito, edde honokiye hitare hono kissu no dito.
LUK 15:17 "Hite zehon hitar nizor bul buzi faijje, hite hodde, 'Ãr bafor góror hoto muzur okkole beši beši hána far, kintu ãi eṛe bukke morir.
LUK 15:18 Ãi uṛi ãr Bafor heṛe zaiyum edde ãi hoiyumboi: O baf, ãi Allah edde tũwar berudde guna goijji.
LUK 15:19 Ãre tũi tũwar fuwa ho he zuiggota ãttu ar nai, kintu ãre tũi šude tũwar oinno muzur okkolor ḍoil gori ãre rako.'
LUK 15:20 Endilla hoi hite hitar bafor heṛe giye. "Hite dure taite bafe hitare deki hitalla doyaye dil bori uiṭṭe. Ar hite fuwar hãse dũri zai, gola sai berai dori galot suma diye.
LUK 15:21 "Fuwaye hodde, 'O baf, ãi Allah edde tũwar berudde guna goijji. Ãre tũi tũwar fuwa ho he zuiggota ãttu ar nai.'
LUK 15:22 "Kintu hitar bafe hitar gulam okkolore hodde, 'Toratori barik kurutawa ano edde itare gat diyai do, õlot õri, ṭengot šendal findai do.
LUK 15:23 Ar boli muṭa goruror sowa ano edde hiba zorgorao. Aiyo, mela gori edde hafiya gori.
LUK 15:24 Kiyollahoile ãr ei fuwa mori gilgoi edde ehon zinda oiye. Hite hãzigilgoi edde abar fa giye.' Toi hitara mela edde há fiya šuru goijje.
LUK 15:25 "Hetunot ḍõr fuwawa bare ketit aššil. Hite aite aite zehon góror hãsa hãsi fõisse, hetunot tal bazana nasor abaz fuinne.
LUK 15:26 Toi hite ekzonore ḍak mari fusar goredde: Eṛe ki oiyede?
LUK 15:27 Hite hodde: Tor šoṛo bái firi aišše, hitare šušondane firai faiyede hetolla tor bafe boli muṭa gorur soware zorgoraiye.
LUK 15:28 "Henot he ḍõr báiye gušša oiye edde górot no goilto saiye. Toi hitar bafe góror baire zai hitare górot golaibolla fot dori hoiye.
LUK 15:29 Kintu hite bafore hodde, 'So, hara bosorṭiya ãi tũwalla gulami gori aiyir, ar hono din tũwar hokumor baire no zai. Hen abostat maze o tũi ãre fũwajja okkol loi kuši aiyaši goribolla hoi uggwa soolor so foijjonto no do.
LUK 15:30 Kintu ze fuwaye tũi dilade ṭĩya foiša beggun beššiya okkolor fise hossa gori felaiye, bade górot firi aišše, hitalla boli tũi muṭa goruwa zorgoraiyo!'
LUK 15:31 "Bafe hodde, 'O fut, tui hamiša ãr fũwati asos, ar zin ãttu ase hin tor.
LUK 15:32 Kintu ãrattu mela gori kušiaši goron zorulot, kiyollahoile tor ei bái mori gilgoi, abar zinda oiye. Hite hãzigilgoi, abar hitare fa giye.'"
LUK 16:1 Isaye sahabi okkolore hodde: "Hono ek tuwangor mainšottu ekzon menezar aššil. He tuwangor manušwaye mainšottu funedde ei menezare hitar dón šombotti sarhar gori feler.
LUK 16:2 Hetunot hite menezarore ḍaki fusar goredde, 'Tor babute ãi in ki funir? Tor hamor hisab de, kiyollahoile tũi ar ãr menezar hisabe tai no faribi.'
LUK 16:3 "Hetunot he menezare mone mone hodde, 'Ãi ehon ki goijjum? Ãr malikede ãre hamottu niyolai der. Ãttu meṛi haṛibar o šokti nai, ar ãttu horat magite o šorom lage.
LUK 16:4 Zen oibo ok, malike hamottu niyolai dile, mainše zene ãre hitarar górot takito de he bebostalla ãttu ki gora foribo ãi zani.'
LUK 16:5 "En hoi, zitara hitar malikor hãsottu šud loiye hitarare ekzon ekzon fottikiyore ḍaikke edde foila ekzonore hodde, 'Tui ãr malikottu hozzo hodun loiyos?'
LUK 16:6 "Hite hodde: 'Ek šot mon tel.' "He menezare hitare hodde, 'Tor hozzor habosgan lo edde toratori boi, hiyanot fõnzaš mon lek.'
LUK 16:7 "He menezare ar ekzonore hodde, 'Tor hozzo hodun?' "Hite hodde, 'No šot mon gĩyu.' "Menezare hitare hodde: 'Tor habosot hãt šot mon lek.'
LUK 16:8 "He menezar ošot oile o hite aholor ham goijje boli hitar malike hitar bala nam goijje. Kiyollahoile ei duniyair manuš okkole nizor zatir babute fohoror fuwain okkolottuwaro beši buddiwala.
LUK 16:9 Ãi tũwarare hoir, ei horaf duniyair dónor duwara mainšolloi egenafoti zurao, zenneki he dón furai gilegoi bade hitara abadul abad takibar zagat tũwarare gose.
LUK 16:10 "Zare šoṛo befaror uwore biššaš gora za, hitare ḍõr befaror uwore o biššaš gora za, ar šoṛo befare zare biššaš gora no za, hitare ḍõr befare o biššaš gora no za.
LUK 16:11 Ei duniyair dón šombottir befare zodi tũwarare biššaš gora no za hen oile tũwarare biššaš gori asol dón hone dibo?
LUK 16:12 Oinnor šombottir uwore zodi tũi obiššaši o, tũware nizolla šombotti hone dibo?
LUK 16:13 "Hono gulame dui malikor šeba gori no fare, kiyollahoile hite ekzonore hingša goribo ar ekzonore ador goribo, otóba hite ekzonor uzu mon dibo, ar dusora zonore hela goribo. Allah edde dón šombotti ei duior šeba o tũwara ekku fũwati gori no fariba."
LUK 16:14 Toi Foroši okkol zara ṭĩya foišar lalsiwala, hitara Isar ei šob hota funni Isare loi ṭaṭṭai goijje.
LUK 16:15 Isaye hitarare hodde, "Tũwarattu to mainšor muntu forhesgar kuwalaito mon, kintu Allaye tũwarar monor abasta zane. Manuše ziyan šorman mone gore hiyan Allar sukot niroš."
LUK 16:16 "Torar ain edde nobi okkolor kitab mozin torikotor gusol doya Yahyar ṭaim foijjonto soille. Tarfore oite Allar raijjor kušir hóbor tobolig gora or, ar beggune heṛe golibolla ṭelaṭeli gorer.
LUK 16:17 Tarfore o Musar šoryotottu uggwa horof bad forattuwaro bolke asman zobin šeš oi za aro bout asan oibo.
LUK 16:18 "Ze honokiye nizor bouwore sari di ar ekzonore biya gore hite zena gore. Zamaiye sari diyede hendilla bouwore ze biya gore hite zena gore.
LUK 16:19 "Ekzon tuwangor manuš ze baiyonna rongor hor edde dami dami horsuwor findito. Hite fotti din kub zak zomok há fiya loi zibon haṛaito.
LUK 16:20 He tuwangor manušwar gaṛaṛ duwaror ḍake Lazarus name ekzon horat magoyare buwai dito. Hitar hara gat gá aššil.
LUK 16:21 He tuwangor manušwar hánar tebilottu ze hána fori zaitoi hin hái hite feṭ boraito issa gorito. Kũir okkole hitar gá lekito.
LUK 16:22 "Ek din he magoyawa mori gilgoi. Hetunot firista okkole hitare tuli loi zai Ibrahimor kulot buwai dilgoi. Tarfore ek din oi tuwangor manušwa o mori gilgoi, edde hitare hoborot garai fela oil.
LUK 16:23 Hite jahannamot kub zontrona loi uworor mikka sail, ar durottu tai dekedde Ibrahimor kulot Lazarus.
LUK 16:24 Hetunot oi tuwangor manušwaye ḍak mari hodde, 'Baf Ibrahim ãre rahamot goro. Lazarusore defeṛo, ãi zene hitar õlor matagan fanit bizai ãr zil ṭanḍa gori fari. Ei oinor zilhat ãi beši duk fair.'
LUK 16:25 "Kintu Ibrahime hodde, 'O fut, mone gori sa, tũi basi takite hoto šuk goijjili ar Lasare hoto duk toziya faiye. Kintu ehon hite eṛe šuk gorer ar tui duk for.
LUK 16:26 Hin bade o tũwara edde ãrar maze ekkan beši ḍõr fák ase, honokiye issa gorile o enttu farai tũwarar heṛe zai no fare edde henttu farai ãrar hãse ai no fare.'
LUK 16:27 "Hetunot he tuwangorwaye hodde, 'Toile baf, meherbani gori Lazarusore ãr bafor górot defeṛo,
LUK 16:28 zene ãr he fãs báiyore hite hũšiyar gori di fare. Ar no oilede hitara o ei zontronar zagat aibo.'
LUK 16:29 "Kintu Ibrahime hodde, 'Musa nobi edde nobi okkolor kitab to hitarar hãse ase. Hitara hinottu diyan di funok.'
LUK 16:30 "He tuwangor manušwaye hodde: 'No, no, baf Ibrahim, mora okkolor butottu honokiye zaile hitara gunattu mon firaibo.'
LUK 16:31 "Toi Ibrahime hodde, 'Musa nobi edde nobi okkolor hota zodi hitara no fune toile morar butottu honokiye uṛile o hitara biššaš no goribo.'"
LUK 17:1 Isaye hibar sahabi okkolore hodde: "Gunar fõtot loizaibar uskani sarme no aibo, hen to oi no fare, kintu bifod hitare, zar duwara hin aibo.
LUK 17:2 Ze ei šoṛo okkolor butottu ekzonore honokiye gunar fõtot ṭani loi zade o, henoile hitare golat ḍõr fattor bandi di doriyat felai diya hitalla aro beši bala oibo.
LUK 17:3 Hetolla tũwara nizor babute hũšiyar taikko. "Zodi tor báiye tor berudde hosuri gore, toile tui hitare hen no goribolla mana gor. Ar zodi hite mon fira toile tui hitare maf goride.
LUK 17:4 Zodi ek dinor butore hite hãt bar tor berudde hosuri gore edde hãtobar ai ho, 'Ãi ei oinnaittu firi aišši,' toile hitare tottu maf gori diya foribo."
LUK 17:5 Ar asab okkole malik Isare hodde: "Ãrar iman barai do."
LUK 17:6 Isaye zuwabe hodde, "Uggwa horoir dana borabor biššaš o zodi tũwarattu take edde ei gassware endilla ho, 'Ei gas, šiyõr udda šoho hãri zai doriyat fuṭgoi,' toile he gaswaye tũwarar hota manibo.
LUK 17:7 "Ar tũwarar butore endilla hone aso, zar gulame al so otóba sool sora, hite górot aile hoiba 'Tui ehon ai, hána haito bošgai?'
LUK 17:8 Bolke hitare ki no hoiba ne? 'Ãi ki háiyum hinor entezam gor! Ar zetun ãttu hána haiya no o, hetun kiyail bandi ãre šeba gor! Tarfore tui hána hái faribi!'
LUK 17:9 He gulame malikor hokum mainne buli ki hitar malike hitare šukuriya zanaibo?
LUK 17:10 He bafe har hokum mani bade o tũwara ho, 'Ãra niroš gulam, ziyan goribar zimma ãra šude hiyan goijji.'"
LUK 17:11 Ehon Isaye Zeruzalem zaibar šomot Sameriya edde Galilor mazottu di giye.
LUK 17:12 Hibaye hono ek farat góillede šomot došzon kurus biyaraimma manuš hibar sarme foijje. Hitara dure tiyaiye edde,
LUK 17:13 guzori hodde: "Isa, Malik, ãrare doya goro!"
LUK 17:14 Isaye hitarare deki hodde, "Zo, imam okkolor hãse zai nizore dehogoi." Zaite zaite hitara faksaf oi giyegoi.
LUK 17:15 Toi hitarar butottu ekzone aram oi giyegoide otfaiyore hite guzori Allar tarif gorat uwafes firi aišše,
LUK 17:16 edde Isar fõt uite fori Isare šukuriya zanaiye. He manušwa aššilde Sameriyar manuš.
LUK 17:17 Isaye hodde, "Došozon pak saf no o neki? Ar nozon hoṛe?
LUK 17:18 Ei ofor manušwa sara ki ar honokiye Allare tarif goribolla no ailo?"
LUK 17:19 Toi Isaye hitare hodde, "Uṭ edde zagoi! Tor biššaše tore bala goijje!"
LUK 17:20 Ek bar Foroši okkole Allar raijjo hõtte aibo Isare fusar goijje. Isaye zuwabe hodde, "Allar raijjor suke deha no za.
LUK 17:21 Ar manušore o no hoibo, so, Allar raijjo ei zagat ba o zagat, kiyollahoile so, Allar raijjo to tũwarar butore ase."
LUK 17:22 Toi Isaye sahabi okkolore hodde: "En šomoi aibo zẽtte tũwara Adomor Futor šomoir ekkan din dekibolla issa goriba, kintu deha no faiba.
LUK 17:23 Hẽtte manuš okkole tũwarare hoibo, 'So, Adomor Fut o zagat!' So, 'Adomor Fut ei zagat!' Kintu tũwara heṛe no zaiyo, ba hitarar fisa no loiyo.
LUK 17:24 Zendilla asmanor ek mikkattu bizoli somkile asmanor nise oinno mikka foijjonto fohor o, Adomor Futor dinot o hendilla oibo.
LUK 17:25 Kintu ei šob goṭibar age, Adomor Futottu beša beši duk bug gora foribo. Ar ei halor mainše hibare batil goribo.
LUK 17:26 "Ar Nuh nobir ṭaimot zendilla oiye, Adomor Futor ṭaimot o hindilla oibo.
LUK 17:27 Manuš okkole há fiya goijje, biya goijje, biyata oiye, ze foijjonto Nuh nobi kištit no gole. Toi bor tuwan aišše edde beggunore šeš gori felaiye.
LUK 17:28 "He bafe Lutor ṭaimot o hendilla oiye. Hẽtte mainše háiye edde fiye, beisse edde kinne, lagaiye edde banaiye.
LUK 17:29 Kintu ze din Lut Súdum šohorottu niyoli giyegoi, hedin asmanottu oin edde oini šilor zór fori hitara beggunore dongšo gori felaiye.
LUK 17:30 "Adomor Fut ze din nizore forhaš goribo, he din o hendilla oibo.
LUK 17:31 He dinor din zodi honokiye góror sãdor uwore take, ar hitar šomošto zinišfati góror butore take, henoile hite hin loibolla lami no ai ok. Hendilla ze maṛot take, hite górot uwafes firi no ai ok.
LUK 17:32 Lutor bouwor hota monot gori so!
LUK 17:33 Ze nizor foran basaito sa, hite hiyan haraibo. Kintu ze foran hara, hite hiyan uddar faibo.
LUK 17:34 Ãi tũwarare hoir: He raitta ek bisanat duizon takile ekzonore loi za oibo, ar oinno ekzon fori takibo.
LUK 17:35 Duizon mayafuwain ek ḍeit gĩyur dana dufe. Hentu ekzonore loi za oibo, ar oinno ekzon fori takibo.
LUK 17:36 (Zodi duizon manuš maṛot take, hentu ekzonore loi za oibo, ar oinno ekzon fori takibo.")
LUK 17:37 Toi sahabi okkole fusar goredde: "Malik, hoṛe goṭibode?" Isaye zuwabe hodde, "Mora ga zeṛe, heṛe hawa aiye."
LUK 18:1 Toi hibaye hitarare ekkan mesal kahanir babute hoiye zene hitara hamiša munazat gore edde niraš no o.
LUK 18:2 Hibaye hodde,"Ek šohorot maze ekzon bisarhar aššil. Hite no ḍoraito Allare, ar no manito manušore.
LUK 18:3 Ar he šohorot ek rari maya fuwa aššil. Hibaye he bisarharor hãse zai hoitode, 'Oinnair berudde tiyai ãr bifokkor hatottu ãre uddar goro!'
LUK 18:4 "Bisarhare hoto din foijjonto kissu no gore, kintu bade mone mone hite hodde, 'Zodi o ãi Allare no ḍorai, manušore no mani.
LUK 18:5 Tarfore o ei rari mayafuwawaye ãre zalar, hetolla oinnaittu ibare ãi uddar goriyum. Ar no oilede hibaye hamiša ãre zalat takibo.'"
LUK 18:6 Toi Malik Isaye hodde, "Ošot bisarhare ki hor funor ne!
LUK 18:7 Toile zara din rait Allar hãse handa haṛi gore, he Allar basai gora okkolore ki hitarar oinnair berudde tiyai soiyi bisar no goribo? Naki hin goitte Allaye deri goribo?
LUK 18:8 Ãi tũwarare hoir, hibaye toratori hitarar fokke niyai bisar gori dibo. Kintu Adomor Fut zẽtte aibo, hẽtte ki hibaye ei duniyait iman dekibo?"
LUK 18:9 Zara nizore nize forhesgarde biššaš goitto ar oinno mainšore hela gorito, hendilla hoekzon mainšore Isaye ei mesal kahanigan hoiye:
LUK 18:10 "Duizon manuše dórmogórot munazat goitto giye. Hitarar butore ekzon aššilde Foroši alem ar ekzon hazna adaigoroya.
LUK 18:11 Foroši alemwaye zai en zagat tiyayegoi zeṛe hitare deha za. Toi hite hitar nizor babute duwa gorer, hite hodde, 'Oh Allah, ãi tũware šukuriya zanai ze ãi oinno mainšor ḍoilla no, ṭok, ošot edde zena goroya no, enki oi hazna adai goroyar ḍoilla o no.
LUK 18:12 Ãi haftaye dui bar ruza raki, ãr šomosto hamanir doš bagor ek bag tũware di.'
LUK 18:13 "Kintu hazna adaigoroya manušwaye dure tiyaiye edde asmanor uzu suk tuli o sai no farer, bolke hite buk bajjai bajjai hodde, 'Oh Allah, ãi gunagar, ãre rahamot goro.'
LUK 18:14 "Ãi tũwarare hoir, he hazna adai goroyare Allaye forhesgar hoi mani loiye, hite arame górot firi giyegoi. Kintu he forošire no. Toile buzi so! Ze honokiye nizore usol gore hitare niso gora oibo, ar ze nizore niso gore hitare usol gora oibo."
LUK 18:15 Hitara gura gura dudor fuwain okkolore o Isar hãse ainne, Isaye zene hitarar uwore hat rake. Sahabi okkole hen deki hitarare gozgozaiye.
LUK 18:16 Kintu Isaye gura fuwaindore hãse ḍaikke edde hodde, "Gura fuwaindore ãr hãse aito do, hitarare band no diyo, kiyollahoile Allar raijjo itarar ḍoilla mainšor.
LUK 18:17 Ãi tũwarare soiyi hoir, ze honokiye ugguwa gura fuwar ḍoilla oi Allar raijjo no gose, hite hono mote heṛe goli no faribo."
LUK 18:18 Ek Ihudi netaye Isare fusar goredde: "Oh bala ustad, akéri zibonor miraz faite ãttu ki gora foribo?"
LUK 18:19 Kintu Isaye hitare hodde, "Ãre kiyolla bala hor? Allah ekzon sara ar honokiye bala no.
LUK 18:20 Tũi to hokumgun zano, 'Zena no goijjo, kun no goijjo, suri no goijjo, misa goba no diyo, tũwar baf mare ijjot goro.'"
LUK 18:21 Hite hodde, "Gura halottu loti ãi in okkol falon gori aiyir."
LUK 18:22 Isaye ei hota funiyore hitare hodde, "Ehon o tũwattu ekkan ham baki ase. Zo, tũwattu za kissu ase hin beggun besi felo, ar gorib okkolore baṛi do, henot behostot dón faiba. Tarfore ai ãr fisa lo."
LUK 18:23 Ei hota funi hite beši ferešan oiye, kiyollahoile hite aššilde ek ḍõr tuwangor manuš.
LUK 18:24 Toi Isaye hitar uzu saiyore hodde, "Tuwangor okkololla Allar raijjot gola ken duk!
LUK 18:25 Tuwangor okkol Allar raijjot golattuwaro fuišor fa bai uṭ gola aro asan."
LUK 18:26 Zara fuinne hitara hodde, "Henoile uddar hone oi faribo? Henoile Allar raijjot hone goli faribo?"
LUK 18:27 Isaye hodde, "Ziyan mainšolla ošombob, hiyan Allalla šombob."
LUK 18:28 Toi Fitore hodde: "Ãralla ken oibo? So, ãra nizor hár kissu felai aišši edde õnor fisa loiyi!"
LUK 18:29 Isaye hitarare hodde, "Ãi tũwarare soiyi hoir, ze honokiye Allar raijjolla buli nizor gór ba bou, bái boin, ma baf, ba fuwain eri diye,
LUK 18:30 hitara fottikiyor ei zugot o bout gun edde aiyedde zugot o akéri zibon faibo."
LUK 18:31 Bade Isaye hibar barozon sahabire ek ḍeikka loi zai hodde: "So, ãra Zeruzalem zair, Adomor Futor befare nobi okkole zin zin leikke, he mozin ãre di furon oibo.
LUK 18:32 He zonore Oihudi okkolor hatot tuli diya oibo. Hitara he zonore loi ṭaṭṭa edde ofoman goribo, ar hibar gat sep maribo,
LUK 18:33 beša beši souk maribo edde hibare mari felaibo. Ar tin dinor din abar zinda uṛi zaiboi."
LUK 18:34 Kintu sahabi okkole in kissu buzi no fare. Hitarattu Isaye hoiyede hotar mani gufon roigiyegoi. Hitara Isar hota buzi uṛi no fare.
LUK 18:35 Ar zẽtte Isa Zeriku šohoror hãsa hãsi aišše, he šomot ekzon anda manuše rastar kinare mager.
LUK 18:36 He anda manušwaye manuš okkolor ãṛar abaz funi fusar goredde: Ki oiyede?
LUK 18:37 Mainše hitare hodde: "Nasarator Isa ei fõt bai aiyer."
LUK 18:38 Hetunot hite guzori hodde: "Oh Nasarator Isa, Daudor šontan, ãre uwore doya goro."
LUK 18:39 Zara age age giye, hitara, suf tak, hoi he manušware dõk diye. Kintu hite aro beši sikkarai howa šuru goijje, "Oh Daudor šontan ãr uwore doya goro."
LUK 18:40 Toi Isa tiyaiye edde he manušware Isar hãse anibolla hokum goijje. Hite zehon Isar ḍake aišše Isaye hitare fusar goredde,
LUK 18:41 "Tui ki sos, ãi tolla ki gorium?" Hite hodde, "Malik, ãi suke deki farifan gori do."
LUK 18:42 Isaye hodde, "Dor, deki far! Tor imane tore aram goijje."
LUK 18:43 Henot hite hehon suke deki faijje edde Allar tarif gori gori Isar fisa loiye. Ar manušor dol, zara iyan deikke hitara o Allar tarif goijje.
LUK 19:1 Bade Isa Zeriku šohoror butottu di zar.
LUK 19:2 Ar so, heṛe ekzon Sakkeus name manuš aššil. Hite oilde ekzon hazna adaigoroya okkolor mazi, ek tuwangor manuš.
LUK 19:3 Ar hite Isare saito kušiš goijje, kintu hite baiṭṭa buli manušor zamot Isare sai no fare.
LUK 19:4 Toi hite Isare sai farefan, mum mikka dũri zai ek ḍũir gasor uwore uiṭṭe, kiyollahoile Isa he fõt bai gil.
LUK 19:5 Bade Isaye zẽtte he zagat fõisse, hetunot Isaye uwor mikka sai hitare hodde, "Sakkeus, toratori lami ai, kiyollahoile aijja ãttu tor górot taka foribo."
LUK 19:6 Henot Sakkeuse toratori lami aišše edde Isare kušir sãte mehemandari kobul goijje.
LUK 19:7 Kintu hen deki beggune monmonaiye, "Isaye ekzon gunagaror górot rait haṛaito zar."
LUK 19:8 Kintu heṛe Sakkeuse tiyai malik Isare hodde, "Malik so, ãr šombottir oddok ãi gorib okkolore dir. Ar zodi oinnai bafe honokiyor hono kissu ṭokai taki, toile hinor ãi sairgun firai diyum."
LUK 19:9 Hetunot Isaye hitare hodde: "Uddar aijja ei górot aišše, Sakkeus o ekzon Ibrahimor šontan.
LUK 19:10 Kiyollahoile zara hãzi giyegoi hitarare talaš edde basaibolla Adomor Fut aišše."
LUK 19:11 Ar zara Isar hota funnil hitarare Isaye šikka dibolla ekkan mesal kahani hoiye, kiyollahoile Isa zeṛe aššil hentu Zeruzalem beši dure nuwaššil. Ar mainše mone goijje Allar raijjo hara deha zaibo.
LUK 19:12 Isaye hodde: "Ek usol bongšor manuše razagiri firai anibo hoi ek duror dešot giye.
LUK 19:13 Ar hite hitar nizor došzon gulamore ḍaki fottizonore ekkan ekkan šunar mohor diyore hodde, 'Ãi zeto din foijjonto firi no aiyi, in diyore šodori goijjo.'
LUK 19:14 "Kintu hitar dešor mainše hitare hingša goitto, hitara hitar fise manuš defeṛaiye endilla hoibolla, 'Ãra no sai, ei manušwa ãrar raza ok!'
LUK 19:15 "Zen oibo ok, ei manušware raza banaiye edde hite górot uwafes firi aigiyegoi. Toi hite ze gulam okkolore ṭĩya dil, hitara šodorit hone hodun amodoni goijje hin saibolla he gulam okkolore hitar hãse ḍaikke.
LUK 19:16 "Toi foila ekzon ai hodde, 'Malik, tũwar ekkan šunar mohore aro doššan šunar mohor hamaiye.'
LUK 19:17 "Razaye hitare hodde, 'Bala goijjos tui ãr bala gulam! Kiyollahoile tui oti šoṛo hamot o biššaš dehaiyos etolla doššan šohoror uwore šašon goribar kemota dilam.'
LUK 19:18 "Toi dusora ekzon aišše edde hodde, 'Malik, tũwar šunar mohor loi aro fãssan mohor ãi hamaiyi.'
LUK 19:19 "Toi razaye hitare hodde, 'Tore o fãssan šohoror uwore šašon goribar kemota dilam.'
LUK 19:20 "Bade ar ekzone aiyore hodde, 'Malik, doro tũwar šunar mohorgan. Ãi iyan fakit nummalot bandi raki dilam.
LUK 19:21 Ãttu tũware ḍor laigge, kiyollahoile tui ekzon hora manuš, zin no rako hin tũi tuli lo, edde zin no lago hin haṛo.'
LUK 19:22 "Hite hitare hodde, 'O horaf gulam, ãi tor mukor hota loi tor bisar goriyum. Tui to ãi hora manuš de zaniti, zin no raki hin ãi tuli edde zin no lagai hin ãi dai.
LUK 19:23 Henoile ãr ṭĩya udar loyare kiya no dos, hen goriti buli ãi aile šudor fũwati hin uwafes adai gori faittam?'
LUK 19:24 "Toi heṛe aro zara tiyai aššil hitarare hite hodde: 'Itar hãsottu šunar mohorgan loifelo edde zattu doššan mohor ase hitare iyan o do.'
LUK 19:25 "Hitara hodde, 'Malik, hitattu de age loti doššan mohor ase!'
LUK 19:26 "Malike hodde, 'Ãi tũwarare hoir, zattu ase, hitare aro diya zaibo, kintu zattu nai, hitattu asede hin o loifela oibo.
LUK 19:27 Tũwara zo! He dušmon okkol zara ãi raza oi no sa, hitarare eṛe ano edde ãr šaikkat hitarar holla lo.'"
LUK 19:28 Ei šob hota hoi bade Isaye hitarar age age Zeruzalemor mikka uṛa šuru goijje.
LUK 19:29 Bade zẽtte Isa zaitun faharor ato hãse asede Betfage edde Betani farar hãsa hãsi oiye, hetunot hibaye duizon sahabire faṭai diye endilla hoi:
LUK 19:30 "Oi sarmor farat zo, heṛe goli mottor ek gadar so banda dekiba, zibar uwore hono manuš hono din no boiye. Hiba kuli ãlla loi anogoi.
LUK 19:31 Honokiye zodi hiba kiyolla kulor hoi fusar gore, toile endilla hoiba, 'Ibare malikottu dorhar oiye.'"
LUK 19:32 Toi zarare defeṛa oiye, hitara zai Isaye hoiyede mozin hár kissu deikke.
LUK 19:33 Hitara he gadar so zehon kuilto saiye, giros okkole hitarare fusar goijje, "Tũwara gada sowa kiyolla kulor?"
LUK 19:34 Hitara giros okkolore hodde, "Iba malikottu dorhar ase."
LUK 19:35 Tarfore sahabi okkole he gadar soware Isar hãse ainne. Toi hibar fiṛot hitarar hor bisai di, heṛe uwore Isare buwaiye.
LUK 19:36 Bade Isa zehon za šuru goijje, hẽtte manuš okkole hitarar nizor nizor hor okkolore rastat bisai diya šuru goijje.
LUK 19:37 Ar Isa zehon Zaitun faharottu lamibar zagar hãsa hãsi fõissegai, hen šomot biššaši okkole ze šob kuduruti ham deikke, hin okkololla kušir sãte guzori guzori hitara beggune Allar tarif goijje. Hitara howa šuru goijje:
LUK 19:38 "Rahamot he badšare, ze Malikor name aiyer!" "Behostot šanti ok ar Uwore Allar mohima ok!"
LUK 19:39 Manušor zamor butottu hoekzon forošiye Isare hodde, "Huzur, õnor sahabi okkolore mana goro."
LUK 19:40 Kintu Isaye hodde, "Ai tũwarare hoir, itara zodi suf take, toile fattorgune guzori uṛibo."
LUK 19:41 Isaye Zeruzalemor hãsa hãsi fõssi šohoror uzu saiye edde hiyanolla sukor fani felaiye.
LUK 19:42 Ar hodde, "Tui aijja o zodi šanti kiye de hiyan buziti, kintu tui no buzor, ehon he šob tor sukor arguwale oi taikke.
LUK 19:43 Endilla ṭaim aibo zẽtte tor dušmon okkole sairo mikkattu zonzal bandibo, tore giri doribo edde tore šomosto kunattu geruwa goribo.
LUK 19:44 Ar tore edde tor butoror šontan okkolore meṛi loi fišai felaibo, tor butore uggwa fattoror uwore fattor takito no dibo. Kiyollahoile Allaye tore basaito ze šuzug diye he šomoi tui sini no los."
LUK 19:45 Tarfore Isaye dórmogórot góille edde heṛe zara besa kina goijjil hitarare henttu baire lorai diye.
LUK 19:46 Isaye hitarare hodde, "Leka ase: 'Ãr gór munazator gór oibo.' Kintu tũwara iyanore ḍahaiṭor aḍḍahana banai felaiyo."
LUK 19:47 Isaye fotti din dórmogórot zai šikka dito. Ar ḍõr imam edde alem ar mainšor neta okkole Isare furai felaibolla kušiš goijje.
LUK 19:48 Kintu hitara ki bafe hen goribo he ufai tuwai no fa, kiyollahoile manuš beggune diyan di ekmone Isar hota fuinto.
LUK 20:1 Ek din Isaye dórmogórot manušzon okkolore šikka der edde bala hóbor tobolig gorer. Hen šomot ḍõr imam okkol, alem okkol edde bura murobbi okkol hitara beggune fũwati ai Isare hodde,
LUK 20:2 "Ãrare ho, tũi har kemota loi in goror? Tũware ei kemota diye de hiba honnuwa?"
LUK 20:3 Isaye hitarare hodde, "Ãi o tũwarare ekkan hota suwal goijjum. Ãre ho:
LUK 20:4 Yahyar torikotor gusol, hiyan ki behostottu naki mainšottu?"
LUK 20:5 Toi hitara ekzone ekzon loi mošora gori hodde, "Zodi hoi, 'Allaro torfottu,' hen oile hite hoibo, 'Toile tũwara Yahyare biššaš ka no goro?'
LUK 20:6 Ar zodi hoi, 'manušor torforttu,' toile mainše ãrare fattor maribo, kiyollahoile mainše Yahyare nobi mane."
LUK 20:7 Hetolla hitara endilla zuwab diye, "Ãra hoi no fari hontu."

LUK 20:10 Ãnguror ainda zehon aišše, hite hitar gular bag loi anibolla ekzon gulamore oi saša okkolor hãse defeṛaiye. Kintu hitara he gulamware mar doir goijje edde hitare hali hate dũrai diye.
LUK 20:11 Bade malike ar ekzon gulamore defeṛaiye, kintu hitara hitare o mar dor gori edde ofoman gori hali hate bidai diye.
LUK 20:12 Hendilla hite tisera ekzon gulamore o defeṛaiye, kintu hitara hitare o mari reza reza gori baire felai diye.
LUK 20:13 "Toi ãngur ketir giros hodde: 'Ãi ki goijjum? Ãi ãr adoijja fuware defeṛaiyum, oitofare hitara itare šorman goribo.'
LUK 20:14 "Kintu saša okkole hitare deki ekzone ekzonore howa hoi goredde: Ite oilde mirazdar, aiyo, ãra itare mari felai, toi mirazgun ãrar oi zaiboi.
LUK 20:15 Bade hitara hitare ãngur ketor baire loi zai mari felaiye. "Ãngur ketir girose hitarare loi ki goribo?
LUK 20:16 Hibaye zai ei saša okkolore furai felaibo edde ketigan oinno mainšor hatot dibo." Ei hota funi mainše hodde, "Endilla no ok!"
LUK 20:17 Kintu Isaye uzu hitarar mikka suk firaiyore hodde, "Toile endilla ze leka ase hiyanor mani ki? "'Ze fattor raz mistiri okkole batil goijje, hiba i beši dorhari fattor oi uiṭṭe!'
LUK 20:18 He fattoror uwore ze foribo, hite bangi ṭura ṭura oi zaiboi edde zar uwore he fattor foribo, hite guri oi zaiboi."
LUK 20:19 He šomot alem okkol edde ḍõr imam okkole Isare doitto saiye, kiyollahoile hitara buzi faijjil ze, oi kahanigan hitarar berudde hoiyede. Kintu hitara mainšore ḍoraiye.
LUK 20:20 Hetolla hitara Isare suke suke raikke. Ar hitara Isare šašon goroya bisar šoktir hatot tuli di farefan hoekzon spai defeṛaiye. He spai okkole bed dori Isar sarme forhesgar boinne, zene hitara Isar hotattu Isare gollot dori fare.
LUK 20:21 Toi hitara Isare fusar goredde, "Huzur! Ãra zani, õne zin ho edde šikka do hin ṭik, õne honokiyor uzu ṭan no goro, kintu soiyi bafe Allar rastar babute šikka do.
LUK 20:22 Ãrare hosai, Romor badšare hazna diya iyan ãralla ṭik ki no?"
LUK 20:23 Kintu Isaye hitarar salaki buzi fari hodde, "Ãre ekkan rufar foiša deho. Eṛe har foṭo edde nam ase?"
LUK 20:24 Hitara hodde, "Romor badšar"
LUK 20:25 Toi Isaye hitarare hodde: "Toile zin zin badšar hin badšare do, ar zin zin Allar hin Allare do."
LUK 20:26 Henot hitara manušor sarme Isar hotat hono šer tuwai no fa, bolke hitara Isar zuwab funi tajjuf oiye edde suf gori taikke.
LUK 20:27 Hodun Sadduki dolor manuše Isar hãse aišše, zara hono uwafes zinda nai hoito.
LUK 20:28 Hitara Isare hodde, "Huzur, Nobi Musaye ãralla leki giye, hono ekzonor bái zodi fuwain no owaite bouwore raki mori zagoi, toile hitar báiye he bouwore biya goribo, edde nizor báiyolla bongšo baraibo.
LUK 20:29 Ehon, hãt bái ase ek górot. He ḍõr báiye biya goijje, kintu fuwain no owaite mori giyegoi.
LUK 20:30 Hitar nisor ḍõr báiye hibare biya goijje,
LUK 20:31 tarfore tisera zone edde hendilla hãtozone biya goijje. Hitara beggune fuwain no owaite no owaite mori giyegoi.
LUK 20:32 Šeše he mayafuwawa o mori giyegoi.
LUK 20:33 Ehon, hitara zẽtte uwafes zinda oibo, hitarar butottu hiba har bou oibo? Hibarede hãtozone biya goijje."
LUK 20:34 Isaye zuwabe hodde, "Ei duniyair mainše biya gore edde biya difele.
LUK 20:35 Kintu zarare he duniyai edde mora okkolor butottu he uwafes zinda oibar laikka boli gona oiye, hitara biya o no gore ba biya o no de.
LUK 20:36 Kiyollahoile hitara ar mori no fare. Hitara firista okkolor ḍoilla. Hitara Allar góror fuwain, zarare morattu uwafes zinda gora oiye.
LUK 20:37 Kintu mora okkol uwafes uṛibode Musa nobir oin zoledde zongolor kahanit dehaiye, kiyollahoile Musa nobiye Mabudore, 'Ibrahimor Allah, Isakor Allah edde Yakubor Allah boli hoiye.'
LUK 20:38 Hiba mora okkololla Allah no kintu zinda okkololla, kiyollahoile Mabudor šaikkat hitara beggune zinda ase."
LUK 20:39 Hetunot hozon dórmiyo aleme hodde: "Huzur, õne bala zuwab diyo!"
LUK 20:40 He oite Sadduki dole ar hono hota suwal goitte šahoš no fa.

LUK 20:43 zetodin ãi tor dušmon okkolore tor ṭengor tolat no raki."'
LUK 20:44 Otoso Daude hibare 'Malik' ḍaker; toile hiba kengori hibar fut oi faribo?"
LUK 20:45 Manuš okkole funedde šomot, Isaye sahabi okkolore hodde,
LUK 20:46 "Alem okkolottu hũšiyar! Hitara lamba lamba hor findi beraito sa edde haṛot bazarot mainšor solam muzolišhanar usol zagat edde mela šobar barik zagat buware foson gore.
LUK 20:47 Hitara rari okkolor gór dokol gore ar mainšore dehaibolla lamba gori duwa gore. Hendilla mainše bisarot aro beši šasti faibo."
LUK 21:1 Bade Isaye suk tuli sadde, tuwangor manuš okkole dórmogóror dan bakšut hitarar nizor nizor sodka raker.
LUK 21:2 Ar o dekedde, ekzon gorib rari maya fuwaye o he bakšut duiyan foiša raikke.
LUK 21:3 Hetunot Isaye hodde, "Ãi tũwarare soiyi hoir, ei gorib rari mayafuwawaye beggunottuwaro beši raikke.
LUK 21:4 Kiyollahoile itara beggune nizor beši šombottittu kissu kissu dan bakšut raikke, kintu hiba obafi oi bade o, hibattu foran basaibolla zin aššil hin beggun di felaiye."
LUK 21:5 Heṛe biššaši okkolor butottu kiye kiye dórmogór babute hoil, hiyan ki šundor šundor fattore edde dan goijjede ziniš loi hãzaiya. Kintu Isaye hodde,
LUK 21:6 "Tũwara ei šob zin dehor, en din aiyer ekkan fattor ar ekkan fattoror uwore no takibo, beggun bangi fela oibo."
LUK 21:7 Toi hitara fusar goredde, "Huzur, in hõtte oibode edde in okkol šuru oibode hẽtte sinno ki?"
LUK 21:8 Isaye zuwab diye: "Saiyo, hono dúhat forizorgoi ne! Kiyollahoile boute ãr namor bed dori aibo, hoibo, 'Ãi Mosi' edde 'šomoi hãse aišše.' Kintu hitarar fise tũwara no zaiyo.
LUK 21:9 Ar zẽtte tũwara larai edde gonḍugulor hota funiba, hẽtte no ḍoraiyo! Kiyollahoile in okkol hameka foila goṭibo, kintu hehon ze šeš iyan o no."
LUK 21:10 Bade Isaye hitarare hodde: "Zatir bifokke zati edde raijjor bifokke raijjo tiyaibo.
LUK 21:11 Ḍõr ḍõr busal oibo edde bout zagat raṭ edde bor biyaram okkol oibo. Ajib goṭona okkol goṭibo edde asmanot ḍor lagede hanḍo edde ḍõr sinno okkol deha oibo.
LUK 21:12 "Kintu in goṭibar age manuš okkole tũwarare bondi goribo edde zulum goribo, sinagog edde ziyolot faṭaibo. Ar ãr namolla buli tũwarare raza edde šašon goroyar sarme ana oibo.
LUK 21:13 Hetunot tũwara ãr babute goba diya šuzug oibo.
LUK 21:14 Kintu tũwara ki zuwab diba hiyanolla agottu loti sinta no goribade hiyan ehon loti dilot yad rako.
LUK 21:15 Kiyollahoile ãi tũwarar mukot hota zuhai diyum edde giyan diyum, tũwarar bifokkor honokiye tũwarare baron otóba zuwab di no faribo.
LUK 21:16 Kintu en ki tũwarar bab ma, bái boin, egena fũwajja okkole tũwarare dušmonor hãtot tuli dibo. Ar tũwarar kiyore kiyore hitara mari felaibo.
LUK 21:17 Mainše ãlla buli tũwarare hingša goribo.
LUK 21:18 Kintu tũwarar matar ekkan sul o dongšo no oibo.
LUK 21:19 Tũwarar nizor sofore tũwarar nizor zibon furaiya faiba.
LUK 21:20 "Ar zẽtte tũwara Zeruzalemore armiye geruwa goijja dekiba, hẽtte hiyan donšo oibar ṭaim hãse aišše de zaniba.
LUK 21:21 Hetunot zara Ehudiyat take, hitara fahari elehat dai zoggoi, ar zara šohorot take hitara baire dai zoggoi. Ar zara gang zagat take hitara šohorot no aiyok.
LUK 21:22 Kiyollahoile ehon oilde šazar ṭaim, kitabot ze šob hota leka ase hin furon oibo.
LUK 21:23 Afsus! He šomot hamilwala mayafuwain edde dudor fuwawala mayafuwain okkololla, kiyollahoile dešot beši durgoti oibo edde ei zatir uwore Allar gozob lami aibo.
LUK 21:24 Manuš okkol toluwaror tole oi oi moribo edde bondi hisabe hár zatir heṛe loi za oibo. Zetodin Oihudi okkolor ṭaim šeš oi no zagoi hetodin foijjonto Zeruzalemore Oihudi okkole hitar ṭengor tole ḍolibo.
LUK 21:25 "Ar san surzo asmanor tara okkolot nanan ḍoilla sinno deha zaibo. Duniyait hár manuš okkole zontrona faibo. Doriyar goiror uzore hitara ḍore suhara oi zaiboi.
LUK 21:26 Duniyait zin goṭibo hinor ḍore manušor foran sulor agat zaiboi, kiyollahoile san, surzo, tara okkol oulzoul oi zaiboi.
LUK 21:27 Ar he šomot hitara Adomor Futore ḍõr šokti edde mohima loi miyular butottu aiyedde dekibo.
LUK 21:28 Ei hanḍo beggun šuru oile o tũwara uṛi tiyaiyo, matá tuillo, kiyollahoile tũwarar azadi hãse."
LUK 21:29 Ar Isaye hitarare ei mesal kahanigan hoiye: "Ei ḍũir gaswa edde ar har gasor uzu so!
LUK 21:30 Zehon hinottu noya fata fuṛe, hetunot tũwara hin sai hoi faro horan hal hãse aišše de.
LUK 21:31 He bafe tũwara o zẽtte ei šob oibode dekiba hẽtte zaniba Allar raijjo hãse aišše.
LUK 21:32 "Ãi tũwarare soiyi hoir, ze foijjonto in okkol furon no o, he foijjonto ei halor manuš okkolor mout no oibo.
LUK 21:33 Asman edde zobin šeš oibo, kintu ãr hota hono din šeš no oibo.
LUK 21:34 "Hũšiyar tako edde tũwarar kolobore beši niša fani hafiyar folai loi edde šongšari sinta loi kobza gori no raikko, zen atikka he din fandor ḍoilla oi tũwarar uwore no fore gai.
LUK 21:35 Kiyollahoile he dingan duniyair hár manuš beggunor uwore foribo.
LUK 21:36 Kintu tũwara hamiša seton taikko, munazat goijjo, zene he šob zin goṭibo hin okkolottu dai zaigoi faribolla edde Adomor Futor sarme tiyai faribolla šokti fo."
LUK 21:37 Isaye fotti din dórmogórot zai šikka dito edde fotti raitta hibaye hentu bair oi Zaitun faharot zai takitogoi.
LUK 21:38 Ar hár manuš okkol Isar hota funibolla kub binna sore dórmogórot zai Isar hãse hazir oito.
LUK 22:1 He šomot iš no diya ruṭir idor din hãse aišše, ze idore uddar id o howa za.
LUK 22:2 Ar dõr imam edde alem okkole ki bafe Isare mari felai fare hitara gufone he kušiš goijjil, kiyollahoile hitara manuš zonore ḍoraito.
LUK 22:3 Toi Ehudah Iskariyot, oi barozon sahabir ekzon, hitar butore Šoitan góille.
LUK 22:4 Toi hite ḍõr iman okkol edde dórmogór sõloya garḍ okkol loi dola oito giye edde kibafe Isare hitarar hatot tuli di faribo he babute mošora goijje.
LUK 22:5 Henot hitara kuši oiye edde hitare ṭĩya dibo wada diye.
LUK 22:6 Ar henot Ehudaye o razi oiye edde manuš okkolor nozor arguwale Isare hitarar hatot tuli dibolla šuzug tuwa šuru goijje.
LUK 22:7 Tarfore iš no diya ruṭir idor butore ze din uddar idor sool kurbani gora o, he din aišše.
LUK 22:8 Toi Isaye Fitor edde Yuhannare hoi defeṛadde, "Tũwara zo, uddar idor hána tiyar gorogoi, ãra uddar idor hána háiyum."
LUK 22:9 Hitara hodde, "Hoṛe tiyar goijjum? Tũwar issa ki?"
LUK 22:10 Isaye hitarare hodde, "Tũwara šohorot golile ekzon manuše ek gora fani boi loi zadde lot faiba. Tũwara hitar fise fise, hite ze górot golibo, heṛe zaiba.
LUK 22:11 Ar he góror malikore hoiba, 'Huzure fusar goijje, gorba gór hoṛe, zeṛe ãi ãr šahabi okkolore loi uddar idor hána hái fari?'
LUK 22:12 Henot hite tũwarare ekkan šaz guz goijja dui ṭalar uwore ekkan ḍõr kamera dehai dibo. Heṛe zai tũwara hána gorogoi."
LUK 22:13 Hitara baisa diye edde Isaye zendilla hoil, he mozin lot faiye, ar hitara uddar idor hána tiyar goijje.
LUK 22:14 Bade ṭaim mozin Isaye asab okkolore loi haito boišše.
LUK 22:15 Hetunot Isaye hitarare hodde, "Ãi duk šoibar age tũwarar fũwati ei uddar idor hána háiyum, ãi kub issa goijji.
LUK 22:16 Ãi tũwarare hoir, ze foijjonto Allar raijjo furon no o, ãi ar honokon ei idor hána na háiyum."
LUK 22:17 Bade Isaye fiyala loiye, šukuriya zanaiye edde hodde, "Lo in, tũwarar maze bag gori lo.
LUK 22:18 Kiyollahoile ãi tũwarare hoir, ze foijjonto Allar raijjo no aiye, ehon oite he foijjonto ãi ãnguror roš ar no fiyum."
LUK 22:19 Bade Isaye ruṭi loi šukuriya zanaiye edde hin bangi ṭura ṭura gori asab okkolore diyore hodde, "In ãr ga, ziyan tũwaralla diya oiye. Ãre monot goribolla endilla goijjo."
LUK 22:20 Ar ekkui bafe, Isaye hána šeš oi bade fiyalawa hãtot loi hodde, "Ei fiyala ãr louwor noya wadar sukti, ze lou tũwaralla ḍali diya oiye.
LUK 22:21 Kintu so, ze ãlloi beimani goribo, hite ãr fũwati hána hár.
LUK 22:22 Kiyollahoile zendilla faisala gori raikke, he bafe Adomor Fut zar. Kintu bifod hitar, ze Adomor Fut loi beimani gorer."
LUK 22:23 Hetunot asab okkole ekzone ekzon loi fusar gora šuru goijje ze hitarar butore endilla ham hone goribo.
LUK 22:24 Ar asab okkolor butore hone hokkolottuwaro ḍõr hin loi hitara hota haṛa haṛi goijje.
LUK 22:25 Hetunot Isaye hitarare hodde, "Oihudi dešor raza okkolena hitarar mainšor uwore munifgiri deha. Ar hitara zonogonor dusto boli o ho.
LUK 22:26 Kintu tũwara hendilla no oiyo. Bolke tũwarar butore ze beggunottuwaro ḍõr hite beggunottuwaro šoṛor ḍoilla ok. Ar ze neta hite šeba goroyar ḍoilla ok.
LUK 22:27 Kiyollahoile hone ḍõr? Ki ze hánar ṭebilot haito boiye, hite, naki ze gulame hána baride, hite? Ze hánar ṭebilot haito boiye, hite no ne! Kintu ãi tũwarar maze šeba goroyar ḍoilla oi roiyi.
LUK 22:28 Funo! Tũwara ãr har bola mosibot okkolot maze ãr fũwati roiyo.
LUK 22:29 Ar ãr Bafe zendilla ãre šašon kemota diye, hendilla ãi o tũwara ekkan raijjo diyi.
LUK 22:30 Zene tũwara ãr raijjot ãr mezot boi há fiya gori faro. Ar tũwara šingašonot boi Israilor baro bongšor bisar goriba.
LUK 22:31 "Simon, Simon, sa! Šoitane tũwara beggunore gĩyur dana salefan salibolla dabi gorer.
LUK 22:32 Kintu ãi tolla duwa gorir, zene tor iman komzur no o. Tui abar zẽtte ãr hãse firi aibi hẽtte tor báiyaindore tui tuwajjo dis."
LUK 22:33 Fitore Isare hodde, "Malik, õnor fũwati ãi ziyolot zaibolla edde moribolla o razi asi."
LUK 22:34 Isaye zuwabe hodde, "Fitor, ãi tore hoir, aijja rata kuraye bak no dite, tui ãre no sinos hoi tin bar ošikar goribi."
LUK 22:35 Tarfore Isaye sahabi okkolore fusar goredde: "Ãi zẽtte tũwarare ṭiyar toli, gaṭṭi edde zuta in hono kissu sara defeṛailam, tũwarattu ki hẽtte hono kissur obaf oil ne?" Hitara hodde, "Na, no o."
LUK 22:36 Hetunot Isaye hodde, "Kintu ehon zattu ṭiyar toli ase, te hin lok, ekkui bafe gaṭṭi o lok. Zattu toluwar nai hite hitar kuruta besi ekkan toluwar kinok.
LUK 22:37 Kiyollahoile ãi tũwarare hoir, pak kalamot ze leka ase: 'Adomor Futore naforman okkolor fũwati gona oiye,' hendilla ãr duwara furon oibo. Kiyollahoile ãr babute zin howa oiye, hin furon or."
LUK 22:38 Hetunot sahabi okkole hodde, "Malik, so, eṛe duiyan toluwar ase." Isaye hitarare hodde, "Oiye oiye!"
LUK 22:39 Bade Isaye niyoli zai nizor rosom mozin zaitun faharor mikka fõt bai za šuru goijje. Ar fũwati sahabi okkol o fise fise giye.
LUK 22:40 Isa heṛe fõsi bade sahabi okkolore hodde, "Tũwara duwa goro, zene tũwara forikkat no foro."
LUK 22:41 Bade Isaye hitarattuwaro hom beši ek dolar fõtot giye edde ãṛu feli munazat gora šuru goijje.
LUK 22:42 Munazatot hodde, "Ya, Baf, zodi tũi so, ãr hãsottu ei motor fiyala dur goro. Tarfore o ãr issaye no, tũwar issaye furon ok."
LUK 22:43 Hetunot behostottu ekzon firista aiyore Isare šokti diye.
LUK 22:44 Toi Isaye moron hoštoye mogno oi aro issa zuge munazat goijje. Ar Isar gar gám zen lour fuṛar ḍoilla oi meṛit fora šuru goijje.
LUK 22:45 Isaye munazat gori uṛi bade sahabi okkolor hãse aišše, ar dekedde hitarare, monor dukkor zoriya gumot fori giyoi.
LUK 22:46 Toi Isaye hitarare hodde, "Gum zor kiyolla? Uṛo, forikkat no forofan duwa goro."
LUK 22:47 Isaye hota howat roiye, hen šomot so, heṛe ek ḍõr mainšor dol aišše. Ehudah, ze barozon sahabir ekzon, hite o hitarar fũwati age age aišše. Ehudaye Isare suma diyore dehai dibolla Isar hãse giye.
LUK 22:48 Kintu Isaye Ehudare hodde: "Ehudah, sumar duwara ki Adomor Futore dori dor?"
LUK 22:49 Isar fũwati zara aššil hitara ki ki goṭibo hin buzi fariyore Isare fusar goredde: "Malik, ãra ki suri loi hamela goriyum?"
LUK 22:50 Ar hitarar butottu ekzone, ek ḍõr imamor gulamore hamela gori hitar ḍen han haṛi loi felaiye.
LUK 22:51 Kintu Isaye hodde, "Tam, ar hen no goris!" Bade Isaye hitar han suiyore hitare bala gori diye.
LUK 22:52 Isare doribolla ze ḍõr imam okkol, dórmogór sõloya garḍ okkol edde murubbi okkol aišše. Isaye hitarare hodde, "Ãi ki ḍahait ze tũwara laṛi sura, toluwar loi aiššo?
LUK 22:53 Ãi zẽtte fotti din dórmogórot tũwarar fũwati aššilam, hẽtte to ãr uwore tũwara hat o no tulo. Kintu ehon tũwarar šomoi, andaror razotto soler."
LUK 22:54 Toi hitara Isare dori loi giyegoi edde Isare ḍõr imamor górot ainne. Ar Fitor o dure taki hitarar fise fise giye.
LUK 22:55 Bade manuš okkol zara uṛanot oinor ṭal zali boišše hitarar fũwati Fitor o boišše.
LUK 22:56 Heṛe oinor ṭalor forot Fitor boiššede ek bandi maya fuwaye deki hitar mikka suk firai hodde, "Ei manušwa o utar fũwati aššil."
LUK 22:57 Kintu Fitore ošikar gori hodde, "He maya fuwa, ãi hitare no sini."
LUK 22:58 Ekkena gori bade ar ekzone Fitorore deki hodde, "Tui o to hitarar ekzon." Fitore hodde, "Na, ãi no."
LUK 22:59 Gonḍa anik bade ar ekzone zure hodde, "Soiyi, ei manušwa o hitar fũwati aššil, kiyollahoile ite o Galil elehar manuš."
LUK 22:60 Hetunot Fitore hodde, "No, tui ki hor ãi buzi no farir." Fitore hen hoiya šeš no oite uggwa rata kuraye bak di uiṭṭe.
LUK 22:61 Hetunot Malik Isaye Fitoror mikka muk firai saiye. Henot Isaye ze hota hoil: "Aijja ratakuraye bak no dite, tui ãre no sinos hoi tinbar ošikar goribi," hiyan Fitorottu monot foijje.
LUK 22:62 Hetunot Fitore baire zai kub hainde.
LUK 22:63 Ar Isare sõi roiyede manuš okkole Isare loi ṭaṭṭa goijje edde maijje.
LUK 22:64 Hitara Isar suk bandi Isattu fusar goredde, "Tui zodi nobi oi takos toile ho sai, tore hone maijje?"
LUK 22:65 Ar hitara ingša gori Isar berudde aro bout hota okkol hoiye.
LUK 22:66 Din zehon oiye, Ihudi dórmo komitir murubbi okkol, ḍõr imam okkol edde alem okkol beggune ekkui fũwati dola oiye. Toi Isare hitarar munttu ana oiye
LUK 22:67 edde hodde, "Tui zodi he Mosi, toile ãrare ho!" Isaye hitarare hodde, "Zodi ãi tũwarare hoi, tũwara biššaš no goriba.
LUK 22:68 Ar zodi tũwarare fusar gori, hono zuwab no diba.
LUK 22:69 Kintu ehonottu loti Adomor Fut šoktiwala Allar ḍen ḍakottu boiṛa takibo."
LUK 22:70 Hetunot hitara beggune fusar goredde, "Toile ki tui Allar Fut?" Isaye hitarare zuwab diye, "Tũwara hor ze, Ãi Hiba."
LUK 22:71 Toi hitara hodde, "Ãrattu ar gobar ki dorhar? Ãra beggune hitar nizor mukottu funilam."
LUK 23:1 Bade hitara dol šoho beggune uṛi Isare Rom šašok Filator hãse loigiye.
LUK 23:2 Ar hitara Isar berudde en hoi nališ goijje, "Ãra dekki ei manušwaye ãrar zatire kufõtot loi zargoi. Romor badšare hazna no dibolla mainšore mana gorer, ar nizore Mosi edde badša dabi gorer."
LUK 23:3 Toi Filate Isare fusar goredde, "Tui ki Ihudi okkolor badša?" Isaye Filatore zuwabe hodde, "Tũi ze hor."
LUK 23:4 Toi Filate ḍõr imam okkolore edde manušor dolore hodde, "Ãi ei manušwar hono hosuri no fair."
LUK 23:5 Kintu hitara zid gori howa šuru goijje, "Ehudiya elehar har zaga okkolot šikka di di ite manuš okkolore gonḍogul bazaider. Ite in Galilottu loti šuru goijje, ar ehon eṛe aišše."
LUK 23:6 Ei hota funi, Filate manušwa Galilor ne ki hoi fusar goijje.
LUK 23:7 Isa badša Herudor šašonor tole asede zani fari Filate Isare Herudor hãse faṭai diye. Ar he šomot Herud Zeruzalemot aššil.
LUK 23:8 Badša Herude Isare deki beša beši kuši oiye, kiyollahoile hite Isar babute bout hota funnil, ar bout din dori hite Isare saibolla issa gori aššil. Ar Herude aša goijje Isaye hono keramot gori dehaibo.
LUK 23:9 Herude Isattu bout suwal okkol fusar goijje, kintu Isaye hitare hono zuwab no de.
LUK 23:10 Ar ḍõr imam edde alem okkol tiyaiyore Isare beši hosuri diya šuru goijje.
LUK 23:11 Toi Herud edde hitar šena okkole o Isare ofoman goijje edde ṭaṭṭa goijje. Toi Herude Isare raz fušak findai abar Filator hãse faṭai diye.
LUK 23:12 Hedin Herud edde Filat hitara ekzon loi ekzon dusto oi giyegoi, hiyar age hitarar butore dušmonai baf aššil.
LUK 23:13 Tarfore Filate ḍõr iman okkol, neta okkol edde manuš okkolore ekkui fũwati ḍaki,
LUK 23:14 hitarare hodde, "Tũwara itare ãr hãse ainno edde hoiyo, ei manušwaye manuš okkolore kufõtot loizar. Ar so, ãi tũwarar šaikkat bisar gorile o, tũwara hitar uwore ze šob duš okkol dor, hinor butore ei manušwar hono hosuri no fair.
LUK 23:15 Ar Herude o no fa. Hetolla Herude itare ãr hãse uwafes faṭaiyede. Ar so, ei manušwaye moron šaza faibar laikka o kissu no gore.
LUK 23:16 Hetolla ãi hitare šasti diyore eri diyum."
LUK 23:17 (Filate ei šob hota hoiyede haron oilde he idor ṭaimot hitaralla ekzonore eridiya oito.)
LUK 23:18 Kintu hitara dol šoho beggune uzor diyore hodde, "Itare dur goro, ãralla Barabbasore sari do."
LUK 23:19 Ei Barabbas zare šohoror maze danga edde kunor harone ziyolot bondi gori raka oiye.
LUK 23:20 Deš šasiyot goroya Filate Isare eri dito saiye hetolla abar hite mainšor dolor hãse zanaiye.
LUK 23:21 Kintu manuš okkole guzori hodde, "Itare kurušot do! Kurušot do! Itare mari felo!"
LUK 23:22 Filate tin mottor barot hodde, "Kiyolla? Ite hosuri ki goijje? Ãi hitare šazaye mout dibar hono hosuri no dekir, hetolla ãi itare šasti di eri diyum."
LUK 23:23 Kintu Isare kurušot diya oibolla hitara zid gori beši uzor diya šuru goijje. Toi hitarar uzor kamiyaf oiye.
LUK 23:24 Filate hitarar issa mozin goribar hokum di felaiye.
LUK 23:25 Danga edde kungorar harone ze Barabbasore ziyolot raka oil, hitara hitare saiye. Toi Filate hitare hitaralla eri diye, kintu Isare mari felaibolla tuli diye. Hitarar issa furon oiye.
LUK 23:26 Tarfore hitara Isare loi zadde šomot Šimon name ekzon Kuronir manuš farar butottu di aiššil. Hitara Isar fise fise kuruš boi loi zaibolla he manušwar handot kuruš tuli diye.
LUK 23:27 Ar bout mainšor dol okkol fise fise giye. Hitarar butore bout mayafuwain okkol aššil, zara Isalla bilag gorer edde šuk tuli hander.
LUK 23:28 Kintu Isaye hitarar mikka firiyore hodde, "O Zeruzalemor hoinna okkol, ãlla no haindo, bolke nizolla edde nizor nizor fuwaindolla hando.
LUK 23:29 Kiyollahoile so en šomoi aiyer zẽtte tũwara hoiba, 'Šuki he bázá mayafuwain okkol, zarar udore hono fuwain no owa, zarar buke hono din dud no de!'
LUK 23:30 He šomot "'manuš okkole faharore hoibo, "Ãrar uwore for!" Ar mura okkolore hoibo, "Ãrare guri rak!"'
LUK 23:31 Kiyollahoile mainše hail gasor uwore zodi en gore, toile fuwana gasor uwore ki no goṭibo?"
LUK 23:32 Aro dusora duizon ašami manušore o Isar fũwati mari felaibolla loi za oiye.
LUK 23:33 Hitara Matakuli name ek zagat fõsi bade heṛe šena okkole Isa edde he duizon ašamire kurušot loṭkaiye, ekzonore Isar ḍen ḍake ar ekzonore bam ḍake gori.
LUK 23:34 Hetunot Isaye Allare hodde: "Ya Bab, itarare maf goro, kiyollahoile itara ki gorer hin itara no zane." Bade šena okkole Isar horgunore loṭari kelai bag goijje.
LUK 23:35 Manuš okkole tiyai sai taikke, kintu Ihudi neta okkole Isare loi ṭaṭṭa goijje edde hodde: "Ite oinno manuš okkolore basaito, zodi hite Allar he Mosi, Allar basai gora, toile ehon hite nizore basaok."
LUK 23:36 Ar šena okkole Isare horor roš dito saiye edde hitara ṭaṭṭa gori hodde,
LUK 23:37 "Tui zodi Ihudi okkolor badša os, toile nizore basa."
LUK 23:38 Ar Isar matar uwore ekkan sainboṛot mari diya aššil ziyanot leka ase: "Iba Ihudi okkolor badša."
LUK 23:39 Ar ze duizon hosurbonore kurušot ṭaikke, hitarar butore ekzone ṭiṭkari di Isare hodde, "Tui Mosi no ne? Tui nizore edde ãrare basasena!"
LUK 23:40 Kintu ar ekzon ze ase hite itare zejjeṛai hodde, "Tui šaza for, to ki Allare o boi no goros?
LUK 23:41 Ãra usit šaza fair, zin goijji hinor fól hisabe. Kintu Isayede hono kuham no gore."
LUK 23:42 Tarfore hite Isare hodde, "Huzur Isa, õne zẽtte nizor raijjot oiba hẽtte ãre monot raikko."
LUK 23:43 Isaye hitare hodde, "Ãi tore soiyi hoir, aijja tui ãr fũwati zonnotot oibi."
LUK 23:44 Hẽtte šomoi onumanik dũjja, beilore ganda doijje. Ar šara deš tin gonḍa mula andar oi taikke.
LUK 23:45 dórmogóror forodagan uwottu loti siri dui bag oi giyegoi.
LUK 23:46 Isaye guzori hodde: "Oh Baf, ãi tũwar hatot ãr ruh tuli dilam." Ei hota hoi bade Isaye hibar šeš niyaš felaiye.
LUK 23:47 Ei šob hanḍo deki ekzon Romor šenar boroye Allare tarif gori hodde, "Hãsa ei manušwa soiyi aššil."
LUK 23:48 Ar ze šomosto manuš okkole ei hanḍo saibolla zoma oiye, hitara zin zin goiṭṭe hin okkol deki buk bajjai bajjai henttu giyegoi.
LUK 23:49 Ar Isar sin foriso zara edde ze mayafuwain okkol Isar fũwati Galilottu aišše, hitara šoho beggune dure tiyai in okkol saiye.
LUK 23:50 Ar heṛe Yusuf name ekzon manuš aššil, dórmo komitir ekzon ze bala edde soiyi.
LUK 23:51 Komitir mainše hormo hanḍo, solla mošora zin Isar babute goijje hinot ei manušwaye razi oi no fare. hiba aššilde Ehudiyar Arimatiya farar manuš. Hibaye Allar raijjolla boi aššil.
LUK 23:52 Hiba Filator hãse zaiyore Isar lašwalla saiye.
LUK 23:53 Bade laš lamai kafonor hoor berai di fattorot kuinda, en ek hoborot raikkegoi, zeṛe honokiyore age heṛe raka no o.
LUK 23:54 He din dórmo dinor tiyarir din, dórmor din onumanik šuru oi giyegoi.
LUK 23:55 Isar fũwati ze mayafuwain okkol Galilottu aiššil hitara Yusufor kure kure zai he hobor edde ki bafe Isar laš raka oiye hin saiyegoi.
LUK 23:56 Bade hitara firi giye edde kušbo mollom edde tel banaiye. Tarfore dórmor din Musar ain mozin hitara ziraiye.
LUK 24:1 Haftar foila dinot, binna kub sore, mayafuwain okkole hoboror hãse aišše, ze mosolla hin loi
LUK 24:2 Heṛe hitara dekedde hoboror mukor fattorgan algaiya.
LUK 24:3 Ar hitara hoboror butore zai sadde Malik Isar laš heṛe nai.
LUK 24:4 Hitara ammuwak oi ei befare bafedde šomot, so, ujjol fušak finda duizon manuš hitarar ḍake ai tiyaiyegai.
LUK 24:5 Henot he mayafuwain okkole ḍore meṛir uzu matá nise gori taikke. He duizone hodde, "Tũwara morar butore zindare kiyolla tuwor?
LUK 24:6 Hiba eṛe nai, hiba uṛi giyoi. Galilot takite Isaye tũwarare ki hoil hin monot goro.
LUK 24:7 Hibaye endilla hoilde no ne, 'Adomor Futore gunagaror hatot tuli diya oibo edde kurušot diya oibo. Ar tin dinor din hiba abar uṛi zaiboi.'"
LUK 24:8 Hetunot Isar hota hitarattu monot foijje.
LUK 24:9 Toi hitara hoborottu firi giyegoi edde he egarozon asab edde aro oinno beggunore ei hota zanaiye.
LUK 24:10 He mayafuwain okkolor butore aššilde hitara oilde: Mogdaleni Moriyam, Joanna, edde Yakubor ma Moriyam. Ar hitarar fũwati oinno mayafuwain okkol edde aro zara aššil, hitara beggune asab okkolore ei šob hota hoiye.
LUK 24:11 Kintu zara ei šob hota fuinne hitarattu hin baze hota hoiye fan laigge. Hitara mayafuwaindor hotare biššaš no gore.
LUK 24:12 Tarfore o Fitore uṛi hoboror mikka dũr diye, ar heṛe zai holla niyuri sadde šude hor fori roiye. Ar zin goiṭṭe, hinot hite tajjuf oi he zagattu firi giyegoi.
LUK 24:13 Ar so, hedin duizon sahabi Zeruzalemottu hãt mail dure Emmaus name ek farat zadde šomot,
LUK 24:14 hitara oi šomosto goṭonar babute hotabattara hor.
LUK 24:15 Hitara hotabattara hor edde fusar asar goredde hen šomot maze Isaye nize ai hitarar fũwati ãṛa šuru goijje.
LUK 24:16 Kintu hitarar suk zen bon oi giyegoi, hetolla Isare hitara sini no fare.
LUK 24:17 Isaye hitarare hodde, "Tũwara ãṛat maze ekzonore ekzone ze šob hota howa hoi goror, hin ki?" Hitara nak muk hala gori tiyai roiye.
LUK 24:18 Bade zar nam Kleofas, hite hodde, "Tũi šude ekzon Zeruzalemot zoya oibo, ei hodinor butore heṛe ze goṭona okkol oiye hin no zanode."
LUK 24:19 Isaye hitarare hodde, "Ki goṭṭiyede?" Hitara hodde, "In Nasarator Isar babute goṭona, ze Allah edde har mainšor šaikkat hotaye edde hame ek ḍõr kemotawala nobi aššil.
LUK 24:20 Kintu ken gori ḍõr imam edde ãrar dórmo komiṭir neta okkole moron šaza dibolla tuli diye edde kurušot mari felaiye.
LUK 24:21 Ãra aša goijjilam iba hiba, zibaye Israil zatire azad goribo. Ar hin bade o, aijja tin din oiye in okkol goiṭṭede.
LUK 24:22 Ar ãrar hozon mayafuwainde o ãrare tajjuf goijje, hitara binna kub sore Isar hoborot giye.
LUK 24:23 Hitara Isar lašor deha no fa. Ar hitara henttu firi ai zaigoi bade ãrare hoiye, hitara ze firistar okkolor deha fail hitara Isa zinda ase buli hoiye.
LUK 24:24 Ar ãrar fũwajja okkolor butottu kiye kiye hoboror hãse zai, he mayafuwainde zen hoiye, hendilla zasai goijjegoi, kintu hitara o Isare no deke."
LUK 24:25 Hetunot Isaye hitarare hodde: "Tũwara hoto bekub! Ar nobi okkole ze šomosto hota hoiye, hin beggun biššaš goitte hoto durbol!
LUK 24:26 Mosiye ei šob duk bug gori nizor šanot golibolla hin gora ki zorulot no ne?"
LUK 24:27 Tarfore Isaye Musar ain edde šomosto nobi okkolor kitabottu šuru gori har kitabot hiba nizor babute ze šob leka ase, hin okkol hitarare buzai diye.
LUK 24:28 Tarfore hitara zeṛe zar he farar hãsa hãsi fõssiyegai. Toi Isaye aro dure zaibar alamot dehaiye.
LUK 24:29 Kintu hitara hoisali gori hodde, "Ehon din to giyegoi, hãz oi giyegoi, õne ãrar fũwati tako." Henot Isa hitarar fũwati takibolla górot góille.
LUK 24:30 Tarfore Isa zehon hitarar fũwati hána haito boišše, hetunot Isaye ruṭi loi duwa goijje edde hin bangi hitarare diya šuru goijje.
LUK 24:31 Hetunot hitarar suk kuli giyegoi, hitara Isare sini faijje. Kintu Isa hitarar hentu gayeb oi giyegoi.
LUK 24:32 Toi hitara ekzonore ekzone hodde, "Isaye ãra loi fõtot maze hota hoiyede he ṭaimot edde ãrar hãse Pak kitabor mani kuli diyede hẽtte ãrar dilor butore zoli zoli no uṛe ne?"
LUK 24:33 Ar hitara hehon uṛi Zeruzalem firi giye. Toi he egarozon asab edde hitarar fũwajja okkol beggune zomula oiya deha faiye,
LUK 24:34 ar hitara en hodde fuinne, "Malik hameka uṛi giyegoi, Simonore deha diye."
LUK 24:35 Bade itara duizone o fõtor goṭonar babute edde ruṭi bangibar šomot hitara ki bafe Isare sini faijje, he šob hota hitara beggunore funaiye.
LUK 24:36 Hitara ekzone ekzon loi howa hoi goredde šomot Isa nize ai hitarar maze tiyaiyegai. Hitarare hodde, "Tũwarar šanti ok."
LUK 24:37 Henot hitara ḍore somki uiṭṭe. Ar hitara but dekere buli mone goijje.
LUK 24:38 Isaye hitarare hodde, "Tũwara ḍoror kiyolla? Tũwarar dilot andaša ka anor?
LUK 24:39 Ãr hat ṭengor uzu so, so iba šoyong ãi. Ãre sui so, so ãre, butottu lou gusto no take zendilla ãttu asede dehor."
LUK 24:40 Ei hota hoi Isaye hitarare hat, ṭeng dehaiye.
LUK 24:41 Toi hitara eto kuši oiye, biššaš gori no fajjil ebbe ammuwak oi giyegoi. Toi Isaye hitarare hodde, "Tũwarar hãse eṛe hono kissu háibolla ase ne?"
LUK 24:42 Toi hitara Isare ekkan baijja mas diye.
LUK 24:43 Ar Isaye hiba loi hitarar šaikkat háiye.
LUK 24:44 Tarfore Isaye hitarare hodde, "Ãi tũwarar fũwati takite zin hoilam, he hota oilde endilla: Musar ain, nobi okkolor kitabot edde Zobur šorifot ãr babute ze hota leka ase hin hameka furon oibo."
LUK 24:45 Hetunot Isaye hitarar dil kuli diye zene hitara Pak kitabor kalam okkol buzi fare.
LUK 24:46 Toi Isaye hitarare hodde: "Endilla leka ase ze: Mosittu toziya fa foribo edde tin dinor din hiba morattu uṛibo.
LUK 24:47 Ar hibar name guna maf faibolla edde mon firaibar hóbor hokkol zatir hãse tobolig gora oibo. In Zeruzalemottu šuru oibo.
LUK 24:48 Tũwara in okkolor goba.
LUK 24:49 So, ãr Bafe ze wada goijje he wadare ãi tũwarar hãse defeṛaiyum. Ar behostottu šokti no fo foijjonto tũwara ei šohorot taikko."
LUK 24:50 Bade Isaye sahabi okkolore Betaniya foijjonto loigiye edde hitarare hat tuli duwa diye.
LUK 24:51 Toi endilla oiye, hibaye hitarare duwa gorat maze hitarattu alok oi giyegoi, edde hibare asmanot tuli loi za oiye.
LUK 24:52 Ar sahabi okkole hibare sojida goijje edde beši kuši oiyore Zeruzalem firi giyegoi.
LUK 24:53 Toi hitara hamiša dórmogórot taki Allare šukurana guzar gorat taikke.
JOH 1:1 Šurut Kalam aššil, Kalam Allar fũwati aššil edde Kalam nize Allah aššil.
JOH 1:2 Hiba šurut Allar fũwati aššil.
JOH 1:3 Hár kissu hibar duwara oiye, ar zin oiye, hinor ekkano hibare sara no o.
JOH 1:4 Hibattu zibon aššil, edde he zibon aššilde manušor nur.
JOH 1:5 Ar he nur andarot zoler, edde andare nurore loi ziti no fare.
JOH 1:6 Heṛe ekzon manuš hazir oil, hibare Allar torfottu defeṛa oil, hibar nam oilde Yahya.
JOH 1:7 Hibaye goba dito aiššil, zene hibaye Nuror babute goba de, toi zene hibar duwara beggune biššaš gore.
JOH 1:8 Hiba nize he nur nu aššil, kintu hibaye šude he nuror babute goba dito aiššil.
JOH 1:9 Hiba oilde asol nur, ze fotti manušore nur dan gore, hiba duniyait aišše.
JOH 1:10 Ei duniyait hiba aššil, edde duniyai hibar duwara oiye, to duniyair mainše hibare no sine.
JOH 1:11 Hiba nizor dešor aiššil, kintu hibar nizor mainše hibare no gose.
JOH 1:12 Tarfore o zeto zone hibare goisse, zara hibar namore biššaš goijje, hitara fottikiyore hibaye Allar fuwain oibar odihar diye.
JOH 1:13 Hitara louwottu no, gustottu no, manušor issaye o no o, kintu Allattu oiye.
JOH 1:14 He Kalam manušor ruf loiye edde ãrar fũwati bošobaš goijje. Bafor hãsottu aiššede šude lehar ek Fut, hibar ze mohima, he mohima ãra dekki, hiba doya edde soyiye furaiya.
JOH 1:15 (Yahyaye hibar babute goba diye, ar guzori hodde, "Iba hiba zar babute ãi hoilam, 'Hiba ze ãi bade aiyer hiba ãttuwaro mohan, kiyollahoile hiba ãr age loti ase.'")
JOH 1:16 Hibar he furaiyattu ãra beggune doyar uwore doya faiyi.
JOH 1:17 Kiyollahoile Musar duwara ain diya oil; Isa Mosir duwara doya edde soiyi aišše.
JOH 1:18 Allare honokiye hono din no deke, kintu lehar he Fut, ze nize Allah, edde ze bafor beša beši hãse ase, hibaye hibare forhaš goijje.
JOH 1:19 Ar iyan oilde Yahyar goba, zẽtte Ihudi neta okkole Zeruzalemottu hoekzon imam edde levire Yahyar hãse hiba honnuwa fusar goitto defeṛail.
JOH 1:20 Ar hibaye šikar goijje, ošikar no gore, bolke šikar goijje, "Ãi Messiyah no."
JOH 1:21 Hitara hibare fusar goijje, "Toile tũi honnuwa? Tũi ki Eliyas?" Hibaye hodde, "Ãi no." "Toile tũi ki he Nobi?" Hibaye zuwabe hodde, "No."
JOH 1:22 Hetunot hitara hibare hodde, "Toile tũi honnuwa? Ãrare ho, zara ãrare defeṛaiye, hitarare zene ãra zuwab di fari. Tũi tũwar nizor babute ki ho?"
JOH 1:23 Hibaye hodde, "Ãi, bošoti sara elehat ek abaze guzori zanai der, 'Mabudolla fõt ṭik goro.'" zendilla Esaiyah nobiye hoiye.
JOH 1:24 Toi defeṛa oiyede Foroši okkole,
JOH 1:25 hitara hibattu fusar goijje, "Tũi zodi Messiyah o no oile, Eliyas o no oile, otóba he Nobi o no oile, toile kiyolla tũi torikotor gusol dor?"
JOH 1:26 Yahyaye zuwabe hodde, "Ãi fani loi torikotor gusol dir, kintu tũwarar butore ekzon tiyai roiye, zare tũwara no sino.
JOH 1:27 Iba hiba ze ãi bade aiyer, hibar ṭengor zutar fita kuli dibar laikka o ãi no."
JOH 1:28 Zordanor oinno faror Betaniyat, zeṛe Yahya torikotor gusol dil, heṛe in okkol goiṭṭe.
JOH 1:29 Tarfordin Yahyaye Isare hibar mikka aiyedde dekiyore hodde, "So, Allar berasoolor so, ze duniyair guna boi loizargoi!
JOH 1:30 Iba oilde hiba zar babute ãi hoilam, 'Ãi bade en ekzon manuš aiyer ze ãttuwaro mohan, kiyollahoile hiba ãr age loti ase.'
JOH 1:31 Ãi nize hibare no sinitam, kintu hiba zene Israili okkolor hãse forhaš o, hiyanolla ãi aiyore fanit torikotor gusol dir."
JOH 1:32 Ar Yahyaye endilla goba diye, hodde: "Ãi dekki Ruh hoitoror ḍoilla oi asmanottu lami aiyedde, ar hiba hibar uwore roiye.
JOH 1:33 Ãi nize hibare no sinitam, kintu ze ãre fanit torikotor gusol dito defeṛaiye hibaye ãre hoiye, 'Zar uwore Pak Ruh lami aiyer edde hibar uwore roiyede dekibi, iba oilde hiba ze Pak Ruh loi torikotor gusol dibo.'
JOH 1:34 Ãi hen dekki edde goba dir ze, hiba oilde Allar Fut."
JOH 1:35 Tarfordin, abar Yahyaye hibar duizon šagiritore fũwati loi heṛe tiyai aššil.
JOH 1:36 Ar Isa aṛi zadde dekiyore hibaye hodde, "So, Allar berasoolor so!"
JOH 1:37 Ei hota hodde šagirit dunizone funiyore hitara Isar fise fise za šuru goijje.
JOH 1:38 Isaye fissa fijje edde dekedde hitara hibar fise fise aiyer. Toi fusar goredde, "Tũwara kiyor talaš gorodde?" Hitara hodde: "Rabbi! (zar mani ustad) Õne hoṛe tako?"
JOH 1:39 Isa hitarare hodde, "Aiyo edde sogai." Toi hitara giye edde hiba hoṛe take he zaga hiyan saiye. Ar he dingan hitara hibar fũwati haṛaiye. Hẽtte dinor sairguwa baijje.
JOH 1:40 Yahyar hota funi ze duizon Isar fise fise gil, hitara ekzonor nam aššil Andreas, hite Simon Fitoror bái.
JOH 1:41 Andreas foila hitar bái Simonore tuwai loiye edde hitare hodde, "Ãra Messiyar deha faiyi" (Messiyah zar mani he basona goijjawa).
JOH 1:42 Toi hite Simonore Isar hãse ainne. Isaye Simonor mikka saiyore hodde, "Tui Yohannar fut Simon, kintu tore Koifa hoi ḍaka oibo" (Koifa oilde Fitor zar mani fattor).
JOH 1:43 Tarfordin Isaye Galilot zaibo issa goijje. Ar hibaye Filipore faiyore hitare hodde, "Ãr fisa lo."
JOH 1:44 Filip o Andreas edde Fitoror ḍoil Betsaida ṭonor aššil.
JOH 1:45 Filipe Natanaelore lot faiye edde hitare hodde, "Musa nobiye zar babute Torah kitabot leikke edde zar babute nobi okkole o leikke, ãra hibar deha faiyi: Hiba oilde Nasarator Isa, Yusufor fut."
JOH 1:46 Toi Natanaelye hitare hodde, "Nasaratottu ki bala hono kissu ai faribo?" Filipe hitare hodde, "Ai edde sagai."
JOH 1:47 Isaye dekedde Natanael hibar mikka aiyer, toi hibaye hitar babute hodde, "Oto so, ekzon soiyi Israili, zar butore hono dúhabazi nai."
JOH 1:48 Natanaelye hibare hodde, "Õne ãre kengori sino?" Isaye zuwab diye edde hitare hodde, "Filipe tore ḍakibar age zẽtte tui ḍũir gasor tolat aššili, hẽtte ãi tore dekkilam."
JOH 1:49 Natanaelye zuwab diye edde hibare hodde, "Rabbi, õne Allar Fut, Israilor badša."
JOH 1:50 Isaye hodde, "Ãi tore ḍũir gasor tolat dekki boli hoiyi hetolla ki tui ãre biššaš goror? Tui hiyanottuwaro aro ḍõr kissu dekibi."
JOH 1:51 Bade Isaye aro hodde, "Soiyi, soiyi, ãi tũwarare hoir, tũwara dekiba, 'behosto kula, ar Allar firista okkol uṛa lama gorer' Adomor Futor uwore."
JOH 2:1 Ar tin dinor din Galilor Kana farat ekkan biya oiye. Isar ma heṛe aššil.
JOH 2:2 Ar he biyat Isa edde hibar sahabi okkolore o dawat diya oil.
JOH 2:3 Bade šoraf zehon furai giyegoi Isar maye Isare hodde, "Hitaratu šoraf furai giyegoi."
JOH 2:4 Isaye hodde, "He maya fuwa, ãre kiyolla ei babute šamil goror? Ãr ṭaim aizo nu aiye."
JOH 2:5 Hibar maye sakor okkolore hodde, "Hibaye tũwarare zen goitto ho, tũwara hendilla goro."
JOH 2:6 Heṛe Ihudi okkole pak saf oibolla bebar gorede sowa fattoror fanir siyũ buwagoraiya aššil, hin fotti ugguwat kuri tiriš gelom fani aṛito.
JOH 2:7 Isaye he soijja okkolore hodde, "Ei siugunot fani bori do." Toi hitara hinor hãra hãra ofan gori fani bori diye.
JOH 2:8 Hibaye hitarare hodde, "Ebar hentu olfo olfo furai loi hána baṛidoya okkolor mazir hãse loizo." Toi hitara hen goijje,
JOH 2:9 tarfore hána baṛidoya maziye ze fani šoraf oiye hin fi hái saiye, ar hite hin honttu aišše no zanito, kintu ze soijja okkole fani tuillil, hitara zanito. Toi hite dulare ek ḍaikka ḍaki loizai hodde,
JOH 2:10 "Mainše foila barik šoraf haito de, tarfore zehon meheman okkole beši fifele hetunot hosta šoraf diya o; kintu tui barik šoraf ehon o foijjonto rakidiyos."
JOH 2:11 Iyan aššilde sinno okkolor šuru, ziyan Isaye Galilor Kana farat goijje, edde hibar mohimare forhaš goijje; ar hibar sahabi okkole hibar uwore biššaš ainne.
JOH 2:12 Tarfore hiba, hibar ma, báiyain edde sahabi okkol Kofornahumot lami giye, ar heṛe beši din no take.
JOH 2:13 Hẽtte Ihudi okkolor uddar id hãse aišše, ar Isa uwore Zeruzalemot giye.
JOH 2:14 Heṛe dórmogóror uṛanot hibaye goru, sool, ar hoitor, besa kina goredde lotfaiye, ar heṛe fũnḍiola okkol boišše.
JOH 2:15 Toi hibaye dori loi ekkan souk banaiye, ar hiyan loi goru sool edde manuš beggunore dórmogórottu lorai diye; ar hibaye fũnḍiola okkolor foiša okkol šiṛidiye edde hitarar ṭebilgunore uldaidiye.
JOH 2:16 Toi hibaye he hoitor besoya okkolore hodde, "Ei zagattu in okkol šorai loi felo! Ãr Bafor górore bazaror zaga no banaiyo."
JOH 2:17 Hibar sahabi okkolottu monot foijje ze iyan leka ase: "Tũwar górolla zolonto issaye ãr dil zali tulibo."
JOH 2:18 Toi Ihudi okkole zuwab diye edde fusar goijje, "Tui ki sinno ãrare dehai faribi ze tottu in goribolla odihar ase?"
JOH 2:19 Isaye zuwab diye edde hitarare hodde, "Ei dórmogórgan bangifelo, ar ãi iyan abar tin dinor butore tuliyum."
JOH 2:20 Hitara hodde, "Ei dórmogór iyan bandite sališ so bosor laggil, ãr iyan tui tin dinor butore tulibi?"
JOH 2:21 Asole hibaye ḍórmogór hoite hibar nizor gar babute hoiyede.
JOH 2:22 Hetolla hiba zẽtte morattu uṛigiyegoi, hibar sahabi okkolottu monot foijje ze hibaye hitarare iyan hoilde, ar hitara Pak kitabor kalam edde Isaye hoilde hota biššaš goijje.
JOH 2:23 Uddar idor ṭaimot hiba zẽtte Zeruzalemot aššil, hẽtte ze sinno okkol hibaye gorat aššil, hin dekiyore boute hibar namot biššaš goijje.
JOH 2:24 Kintu Isa nize hitarar biššašor babute biššaš no gore, kiyollahoile hibaye hitara beggunore zane.
JOH 2:25 Ar manuš zatir babute honokiye goba dok, hibattu hiyanor hono dorhar nu aššil, kiyollahoile manušor butore ki aššilde hiyan hibaye nize zanito.
JOH 3:1 Heṛe Forošir ekzon manuš aššil, zar nam Nikoḍomas, Ihudi okkolor ek neta.
JOH 3:2 Ekdin raitta hibaye Isar hãse aiyore hodde, "Rabbi, ãra zani õne ekzon šikkadoya, ze Allar hãsottu aiššo. Kiyollahoile õne ze sinnor ham okkol zin goijjo, hin Allah fũwati no takile honokiye gori no fare."
JOH 3:3 Isaye zuwabe hodde, "Ãi tũware soiyi hoir, noya gori zormo no oile, honokiye Allar raijjo deki no faribo."
JOH 3:4 Nikoḍomase hibare hodde, "Manuš ekzon bura oile kengori zormo oi faribo? Hite ki dusora bar mar ferõt uwafes firizaiyore zormo oi faribo?"
JOH 3:5 Zuwabe Isaye hodde, "Ãi tũware soiyi hoir, zodi hono kiye fani edde Pak Ruhuttu zormo no o, hite Allar raijjot goli no fare.
