JOH 3:8 Boyar ze mikka baito sa he mikka ba. Tũwara hinor abas funo, kintu ei boyar hontu aiye edde hon mikka za hiyan tũwara hoi no faro. Pak Ruhor zormo owa o hendilla."
JOH 3:9 Nikoḍomase hodde, "En kengori oi faribo?"
JOH 3:10 Hetunot Isaye hodde, "Tũi Israilor šikkadoya oi bade ei ziniš okkol kissu no buzo kiya?
JOH 3:11 Ãi tũware soiyi hoir, ãra ziyan zani ãra hiyan hoi, ar zin deki hinor babute goba di, kintu tũwara ãrar goba no goso.
JOH 3:12 Ãi duniyaibi zinišor babute hoidde hin zodi biššaš no goror, henot behostor zinišor babute hoile ken gori biššaš goriba?
JOH 3:13 Ze behostottu lami aišše he Adomor Fut sara ar honokiye honodin behostot no uṛe.
JOH 3:14 Ar Musa nobiye zendilla bošoti sara elehat hafore uwore tullil, hendilla Adomor Futore o tuli lowa oibo,
JOH 3:15 zene fottikiye ze hibare biššaš gore hite akeri zibon fa."
JOH 3:16 Kiyollahoile Allaye duniyaire eto beši ador goijje ze, hibar he lehar ek Futore diye, zene, ze kiye hibar uwore biššaš ane hite dongšo no o, bolke akeri zibon fa.
JOH 3:17 Kiyollahoile Allaye hibar Futore defeṛaiyede duniyair bisar goribolla no, bolke duniyaiye zene hibar duwara uddar fa.
JOH 3:18 Hite ze hibare biššaš gorer, hitar bisar gora no oibo, kintu hite ze biššaš no gorer hitar bisar ehon loti oigiyegoi, kiyollahoile hite Allar šude lehar Futor namot biššaš no ane.
JOH 3:19 Ar iyan oilde bisar: Nur duniyait aišše, ar manuš okkole nurottuwaro andarore beši muhabbot goijje, kiyollahoile hitarar ham aššil horaf.
JOH 3:20 Kiyollahoile fottikiye ze horaf ham gorer, hitara nurore hingša gorer, ar nuror ḍake nu aiye, zene hitar horaf ham forhaš oi no zagoi
JOH 3:21 Kintu hite ze soyit soler, hite nuror hãse aiye, toi zene hitar hamgun Allar issa mozin gora oiyede hiyan foriškar deha za.
JOH 3:22 In okkol bade, Isa edde hibar sahabi okkol Ehudiya elehat aišše, ar hiba heṛe kissu din hitarar fũwati taikke, edde torikotor gusol diye.
JOH 3:23 Ehon, Yahyaye o Salimor hãsa hãsi Aenonot, torikotor gusol diyat aššil, kiyollahoile heṛe beši fani aššil, ar manuš okkol heṛe aiyore torikotor gusol lowat aššil.
JOH 3:24 (In aššilde Yahyare ziyolot dibar age.)
JOH 3:25 Hẽtte Ihudi rosomi pak safor babute Yahyar šagirit okkol loi edde ekzon Ihudi loi barabari uiṭṭe.
JOH 3:26 Bade hitara Yahyar hãse aiyore hodde, "Rabbi, ze Zordanor ofarot õnor fũwati aššil, edde zar babute õne goba dila, so, hibaye torikotor gusol der, ar beggune hibar hãse zar."
JOH 3:27 Yahyaye hodde, "Behostottu diya oiyede no oile ekzon mainše hono kissu fai no fare.
JOH 3:28 Tũwara nize ãr goba ze ãi hoiyi, 'Ãi Messiyah no, kintu ãre hibar age defeṛa oiye.'
JOH 3:29 Zar hãse hoinna, hiba oilde dula. Dular bondu, ze tiyaiyore hibar hota funer, hibaye dular abazot beši kušiye anondo gorer; aijja ãttu o hendilla furafuri kuši furon oiye.
JOH 3:30 Iyan zorulot ehonottu loti hibattu bara foribo, ãttu šoṛo owa foribo."
JOH 3:31 Ze uwottu aiye, hiba beggunor uwore; ze duniyaittu hite duniyair, ar duniyair ekzonor ḍoilla hota ho. Hiba ze behostottu aiye, hiba beggunor uwore.
JOH 3:32 Hibaye zin deikke edde fuinne hinor goba der, tarfore o honokiye hibar gobare no goser.
JOH 3:33 Hite ze hibar gobare goser, hiyane sil maijje ze Allah oilde soiyi.
JOH 3:34 Kiyollahoile hiba zare Allaye defeṛaiye, hibaye Allar kalam hor; kiyollahoile Allaye Ruhure mafiyore no de.
JOH 3:35 Bafe Futore ador gore edde hár kissure hibar hãtot šebi diye.
JOH 3:36 Hite ze Futore biššaš gore, hite akeri zibon faiye, kintu hite ze Futore batil gore, hite zibon no dekibo, bolke Allar gozob hitar uwore ase edde takibo.
JOH 4:1 Ehon, Malike zehon zani faijje ze Foroši okkole fuinnil, hibaye Yahyattuwaro beši sahabi banar edde torikotor gusol der,
JOH 4:2 (zodi o Isaye nize torikotor gusol no dito, kintu hibar sahabi okkole dito.)
JOH 4:3 Toi hiba Ehudiyattu giyegoi edde abar Galilot giye.
JOH 4:4 Zaite hibattu Sameriyar butottu di za foijje.
JOH 4:5 Toi hiba Sykar name Sameriyar ek šohorot, aiššiye; ziyan Yakube hibar fut Yusufore dilde zobinor hãse.
JOH 4:6 He zagat heṛe ugguwa Yakubor kuwa aššil. Fõtot zat maze Isa oran oiye, edde he kuwar ḍake boišše; ar hẽtte ṭaim onumanik dũijja.
JOH 4:7 Toi heṛe Sameriyattu ek mayafuwa fani tulito aišše, Isaye hibare hodde, "Ãre fani fito de"
JOH 4:8 (Hibar sahabi okkole šohorot hána kinto gil.)
JOH 4:9 He Sameriyo mayafuwawaye hibare hodde, "Õne, ekzon Ihudi oiyore, ãi ekzon Sameriyar mayafuwa oiyore, ãttu kengori fani sor?" (Kiyollahoile Ihudi okkole Sameriyo okkol loi suwa fiya no gorito.)
JOH 4:10 Isaye zuwabe hibare hodde, "Tui zodi zaniti Allar hadiya ki, edde hiba honnuwaye hor 'Ãre fani fito de', toile tui hibattu saiti, ar hibaye tore zinda fani dito."
JOH 4:11 Mayafuwawaye hodde, "Malik, õnottude fani tulibolla kissu nai ar kuwawa o mur. Toile he zinda fani hontu for?
JOH 4:12 Ãrar baf Yakubottuwaro ki õne mohan, edde ze ei kuwa ãrare diye, ar hibattu hiba nize edde hibar fuwain okkole, hibar zanuwaror záke fani fiye?"
JOH 4:13 Isaye zuwabe hibare hodde, "Fottikiye ze ei fani fiyer hite abar tiraši oibo,
JOH 4:14 kintu ze honokiye ãi diyumde he fanittu fibo, hite ar honodin tiraši no oibo; ãi diyumde fani hin hitar dilor butore ũtari uṛede zonnar fani ḍoilla oibo, edde akeri zibon dibo."
JOH 4:15 Mayafuwawaye hibare hodde, "Malik, toile ei fani ãre do, zene ãttu ar tiraš no lage, ar fani tulibolla eṛe aiya no fore."
JOH 4:16 Isaye hibare hodde, "Za, tor zamaire ḍaki loiagoi"
JOH 4:17 Mayafuwaye hodde, "Ãttu zamai nai." Isaye hibare hodde, "'Ãttu zamai nai' hoyosde hiyan tui ṭik hois.
JOH 4:18 Kiyollahoile ei foijjonto tottu fãszon zamai aššil, ar ehon tottu ze ase, hite tor zamai no; tui hodde hiyan soiyi."
JOH 4:19 Mayafuwaye hodde, "Malik, ãi buzi faijji ze õne ekzon nobi.
JOH 4:20 Ãrar fordada okkole ei faharor uwore ebadot gorito, kintu tũwara ho ze zagat ebadot gora foribo hiyan oilde Zeruzalemot."
JOH 4:21 Isaye hibare hodde: "Oh mayafuwa, ãrar hota biššaš gor, en ṭaim aiyer zẽtte tũwara, no ei faharot, no Zeruzalemot, Bafor ebadot goriba.
JOH 4:22 Tũwara ziyan no zano hiyanor ebadot goro; kintu ãra ziyan zani hiyanor ebadot gori, kiyollahoile uddar oilde Ihudi okkolor butottu.
JOH 4:23 Kintu en ṭaim aiyer, enki ehon he šomoi aigiyegoi zẽtte asol ebadot goroya okkole soiyit edde Ruhut Bafor ebadot goribo. Bafe o endilla ebadot goroya okkolore tuwa.
JOH 4:24 Allah oilde Ruh, ar hitara zara hibar ebadot gore, soiyit edde Ruhut ebadot gora foribo."
JOH 4:25 Mayafuwawaye hodde, "Ãi zani Messiyah aibo (zare Mosi ḍake). Hiba zẽtte aibo, hibaye ãrare hár kissu buzai dibo."
JOH 4:26 Toi Isaye hibare hodde, "Ãi, ze tor loi hota hoir, ãi hiba."
JOH 4:27 Hen šomot hibar sahabi okkol aišše, edde hibaye ekzon mayafuwa loi hota hodde dekiyore hitara ammuwak oiye. Tarfore o hitara honokiye no ho, "Õne ki sodde?" Ba "hibar loi kiyolla hota hor?"
JOH 4:28 Toi mayafuwawaye hibar gorawa felai raki šohoror butore giye, edde mainšore hodde,
JOH 4:29 "Aiyo, ekzon manušore sogai, ze ãi zaha kissu goijji, beggun ãre hoi diye; Iba ki hono Messiyah ne?"
JOH 4:30 Hitara šohorottu niyoli giye edde Isar hãse aišše.
JOH 4:31 Hen šomot hibar sahabi okkole hibare foriyad gori hodde, "Rabbi, kissu hó."
JOH 4:32 Isaye hitarare hodde: "Ãttu háibolla en hána ase, zinor babute tũwara no zano."
JOH 4:33 Sahabi okkol ekzone oinno zonore howa hoi goijje, "Honokiye ki hibare háibolla kissu ani diye oitfare?"
JOH 4:34 Isaye hitarare hodde, "Ze ãre defeṛaiye hibar issa falon gora edde hibar ham gori šeš gorifela oilde ãr hána.
JOH 4:35 Tũwara ki no ho ne, 'ehon o sair maš ase, tarfore gula daibar ainda aiyer'? Ãi tũwarare hoir, suk tuli maṭ okkolor mikka so, hin daibolla fagi dóla oiye.
JOH 4:36 Ze dar hite hitar beton far, ar akeri zibonolla gulagun dola gori raker, zene ze biz laga edde ze gula da, dunizone ekkui fũwati kuši gori fare.
JOH 4:37 Etolla ei bosongan soiyi, 'Ekzone laga ar ekzone da.'
JOH 4:38 Ãi tũwarare daito defeṛailam zinolla tũwara hono haṛoni no goro; haṛoni goijje oinno kiye, ar tũwara goillo hitarar haṛonir fošol daito."
JOH 4:39 'Ãi zaha kissu goijji, beggun ãre hoi diye' he mayafuwawar ei gobar hotar zoriya he šohoror bout Sameriyo okkole Isar uwore biššaš ainne.
JOH 4:40 Toi hitara hibar hãse aišše edde hibare hitarar fũwati takibolla foriyad goijje; ar hiba heṛe dui din taikke.
JOH 4:41 Hibar hotar zoriya aro bout beši mainše biššaši oiye.
JOH 4:42 Hitara mayafuwaware hodde: "Ãra šude tor hotar zoriya biššaš ainnide no; kiyollahoile ãra nize hibar hota fuinni edde zani ze iba oilde soiyi duniyair he Uddargoroya."
JOH 4:43 Dui din farai zaigoi bade Isaye hentu baisa diye edde Galilot giyegoi.
JOH 4:44 (Kiyollahoile hibaye nize goba dil ze ekzon nobi hibar nizor dešot ijjot no fa.)
JOH 4:45 Hiba zehon Galilot aišše, Galiliyo okkole hibare goisse, Zeruzalemot uddar idot hibaye goijjede hár kissu hitara dekiyore, kiyollahoile hitara o uddar idot gil.
JOH 4:46 Isa abar Galilor Kana farat giye, zeṛe hibaye fanire šoraf goijjil. Ar heṛe ek raz hormosari aššil, zar fute ošuk loi duk fat aššil.
JOH 4:47 Ehudiyattu Isa Galilot aišše funiyore hite hibar hãse aišše, edde foriyad goijje zene hiba hitar fũwati lamat za edde hitar futore aram gore, kiyollahoile hitarar foran zar zar oiye.
JOH 4:48 Toi Isaye hitare hodde: "Sinno edde keramoti ham no dekile, tũwara biššaš no goriba."
JOH 4:49 He raz hormosariye hodde: "Malik, meherbani gori ãr fuwawa no morite aiyo."
JOH 4:50 Isaye hitare hodde, "Za, tor fut basibo." Henot hite Isaye hoiyede hota biššaš goijje edde giyegoi.
JOH 4:51 Ar hite lamat zadde fõtot, hitar gulam okkole dola oiye edde hitar hãse hóbor diye ze hitar fuwawa baisse.
JOH 4:52 Hite hitarare hite hõtte bala oiye he babute zera goijje, ar hitara hitare hodde: "Gelde hailla ugguwa baze, hitattu zor sarigiyegoi."
JOH 4:53 Henot fuwawar bafe buzi faijje ze, ṭik he šomot Isaye hitare hoil, "Za, tũwar fut basibo." Toi hite edde hitar fura gór ṭiyaye biššaši oiye.
JOH 4:54 Ehudiyattu Galilot ai bade Isaye ei dusora bar keramoti ham goijjil.
JOH 5:1 Iyar bade Ihudi okkolor ek id oiye, ar Isa uwore Zeruzalem giye.
JOH 5:2 Ar heṛe Zeruzalemot Sool Geiṭor hãse ugguwa foir ase, zibare Ibroni bašat Betesda ho, ar hibat fãssan saniola gãṭ aššil.
JOH 5:3 In okkolot ek dõr biyaraimma mainšor dol foritakito, zara anda, lula, ãtur manuš okkol.
JOH 5:4 (Kiyollahoile ek firistaye šome šome oi foirot lami zaiyore fani hafaito, ei fani hafa bade ze foila fanit lamito, hitattu ze hono ḍoilla biyaram takibo takok, aram oi zaitogoi.)
JOH 5:5 Ar heṛe ekzon manuš aššil, ze tiriš ašṭo bosormula biyaraimma,
JOH 5:6 hite heṛe fori taikkede Isaye deikke, ar zani faijje ze hite bout din dori hite he abostat ase, toi hibaye hitare fusar goredde: "Tui aram oito sos ne?"
JOH 5:7 He biyaraimma manušwaye hodde, "Malik, fani hafi uṛede šomot ãre foirot lamai loizaoya ãttu hono kiye nai; ar ãi nize zaite zaite ar ekzon ãr agottu lamegoi."
JOH 5:8 Toi Isaye hitare hodde, "Uṭ, tor bisana tuli lo edde aṭ."
JOH 5:9 Hehon he manušwa aram oiye; ar hite hitar bisanagan tuli loiye edde ãiṭṭe. Ar he din aššilde Šabbat,
JOH 5:10 Ihudi neta okkole aram gora oiyede he manušware hodde, "Aijja, Šabbat, ain mozin bisana boi loi za mana."
JOH 5:11 Hite hitarare zuwab diye, "Hiba ze ãre aram goijje, hibaye ãre hoiye,'Tor bisana tuli lo edde aṭ.' "
JOH 5:12 Toi hitara hitattu fusar goijje, "Manuš hiba honnuwa ze tore bisana tuli lo edde aṭ hoiye?"
JOH 5:13 Ze manušwa aram oiye hite no zanito hiba honnuwa aššil, kiyollahoile Isaye šori gilgoi, heṛe beša beši manuš okkol aššil.
JOH 5:14 Fore zaiyore Isaye he manušware abar dórmogóror uṛanot lot faiye edde hitare hodde: "Sa, tui bala oiyos, guna ar no goris, toi zene tor uwore iyattuwaro aro horaf hono kissu no goṭe."
JOH 5:15 Hite zaiyore Ihudi netare hoiyegoi ze, hitare bala goijje hiba aššilde Isa.
JOH 5:16 Ar iyanolla boli Ihudi okkole hibare zala šuru goijje, kiyollahoile hibaye in okkol Šabbatot goijje.
JOH 5:17 Ar Isaye hitarare hodde, "Ãr Baf ehon foijjonto hamot, ar ãi o ham gorir."
JOH 5:18 Iyanor zoriya Ihudi okkole hibare marifelaibolla aro beši kušiš goijje; kiyollahoile hibaye šude Šabbator niyom no bange, kintu Allare hibaye nizor Baf o hoiye, hiba nizore Allar fuwainna goriyore.
JOH 5:19 Iyanot Isaye hitarare zuwab diye edde hodde: "Ãi tũwarare soiyi soiyi hoir, Fute nizottu hono kissu gori no fare; zodi hibar Bafe kissu gorede no deke; kiyollahoile zin hibaye gore Fute o gore.
JOH 5:20 Kiyollahoile Bafe Futore ador gore, ar hár kissu zin hibaye nize gore, beggun hibare deha; ar inottuwaro aro mohan ham okkol hibaye hibare dehaibo, zene tũwara ammuwak o.
JOH 5:21 Zendilla Bafe mora okkolore tule edde zibon de, hendilla Fute o hibattu zare issa hitare zibon de.
JOH 5:22 Aro, Bafe honokiyor bisar no gore, kintu bisaror fura bar hibar Futor uwore diye,
JOH 5:23 zene beggune Bafore šorman gorede mozin Futore šorman gore; hite ze Futore šorman no gore, hite Bafore šorman no gore, ze hibare defeṛaiye.
JOH 5:24 "Soiyi, soiyi, ãi tũwarare hoir, hite ze ãr kalam funer, ar ze ãre faṭaiye hibare biššaš gorer, hitattu akeri zibon ase; ar hitare bisarot tula no oibo, kintu morattu zibonot faraiyegoi.
JOH 5:25 Ãi tũwarare soiyi soiyi hoir, en ṭaim aiyer, bolke hiyan ehon aišše, zẽtte mora okkole Allar Futor abaz funibo, edde hitara zara funibo, hitara basibo.
JOH 5:26 Kiyollahoile Baf nizottu zendilla zibon ase, hendilla hibaye Fut nizottu o zibon taibolla diye.
JOH 5:27 Ar hibaye hibare bisar goribolla odihar diye, kiyollahoile hiba oilde Adomor Fut.
JOH 5:28 "Ei hota funi ammuwak no oiyo, kiyollahoile en ṭaim aiyer, zara hoborot ase hitara beggune hibar abaz funibo,
JOH 5:29 edde hitara niyoli aibo, hitara zara bala ham goijje hitara zibon faibolla, ar hitara zara horaf ham goijje, hitara šasti faibolla.
JOH 5:30 Ãi nizottu kissu gori no fari, zendilla funi hendilla bisar gori, ãr bisar niyaiwala, kiyollahoile ãi ãttu ziyan goitto mone hor, hen no sai, kintu hibaye zendilla sar, ze ãre defeṛaiye.
JOH 5:31 "Ãi nize zodi ãr babute goba di, ãr goba soiyi no.
JOH 5:32 Kintu ar ekzon ase ze ãr babute goba der, ar ãi zani ze hibaye ãr babute ze goba der hiyan soiyi.
JOH 5:33 "Tũwara Yahyar hãse manuš defeṛaila, ar hibaye soiyir foikka goba diye.
JOH 5:34 Manuše ãr gobar dok ãi hiyan saide no; kintu ãi iyan hoir zene tũwara uddar fo.
JOH 5:35 Yahya aššil he zoledde edde ujjol serag, ar tũwara hibar he fohorot hoto dinolla anondo goribolla issa goijjila.
JOH 5:36 "Kintu ãttu Yahyar gobattuwaro aro mohan goba ase, kiyollahoile Bafe ãre ze ham okkol gori šeš goribolla diye, ze ham okkol ãi gorir, in okkole ãr babute endilla goba der ze ãre Bafe defeṛaiye.
JOH 5:37 Ar Baf, ze ãre defeṛaiye, hibaye nize ãr babute goba diye. Tũwara honodin hibar abaz no funo, hibar rohom o no deko.
JOH 5:38 Ar tũwarar dilot hibar kalam o bošoti no gorer, kiyollahoile hibaye defeṛaiyede hibare tũwara biššaš no goro.
JOH 5:39 Tũwara pak kitabor kalam tuwo, kiyollahoile akeri zibon heṛe butore faiba boli mone goro. Kintu ei pak kitabor kalam okkol oilde hin zine ãr babute goba de,
JOH 5:40 tarfore o tũwara zibon faibolla ãr hase aito issa no goro.
JOH 5:41 "Ãi manušor hãsottu tarif no gosi,
JOH 5:42 kintu ãi tũwarare sini, tũwarar dilot Allar ador nai.
JOH 5:43 Ãi ãr Bafor namot aišši, ar tũwara ãre no gosor; kintu oinno kiye zodi hitar nizor name aiye, hitare tũwara gosiba.
JOH 5:44 Tũwara kengori biššaš gori faro? Tũwara ekzone ar ekzonottu tarif goso, kintu ze tarif šude Allar torfottu aiye hiyan no tuwo.
JOH 5:45 "Mone no goijjo ze, tũwarare ãi Bafor sarme duši banaiyum; kintu tũwarar duši goroya oilde Musa, zar uwore tũwarar aša raikko.
JOH 5:46 Kiyollahoile tũwara zodi Musare biššaš gorita, toile tũwara ãre biššaš gorita, kiyollahoile hibaye ãre babute leikke.
JOH 5:47 Kintu tũwara zodi hibar leka biššaš no goro, toile ãi hoidde hin kengori biššaš goriba?"
JOH 6:1 Iyar bade Isaye Galil doriyar dusora farot giye, (ziyanore Ṭaiberiya doriya o ho.)
JOH 6:2 Ar ek beši ḍõr mainšor dole hibar fise fise giye, kiyollahoile hibaye biyaraimma okkolore aram goijjilde he keramot okkol hitara dekkil.
JOH 6:3 Tarfore Isaye ek faharor uwore giye edde heṛe hibaye hibar sahabi okkolore loi boišše.
JOH 6:4 Hẽtte Ihudi uddar id hãse aššil.
JOH 6:5 Toi Isaye hibar suk tuille ek ḍõr mainšor dol hibar mikka aiyedde dekiyore, hibaye Filipore hodde, "Itara háibolla ãra ruṭi hontu kiniyum?"
JOH 6:6 Hibaye hitare ei hotagan šude forikka goribolla hoiye, kiyollahoile hibaye ki goribo hiyan hibaye agottu loti zanito.
JOH 6:7 Filipe hibare zuwabe hodde, "Hitarar fotti ekzone ek ṭukura gori faibolla dui šot dinaror ruṭiye o no kulaibo!"
JOH 6:8 Hibar sahabi okkol butore ekzon, Andreas, Simon Fitoror bái, hite hibare hodde,
JOH 6:9 "Eṛe ek gura fuwattu fãswa buṭkar aṭar ruṭi edde duwa mas ase, kintu edun mainšore hin diyore ki oibo?"
JOH 6:10 Isaye hodde, "Mainšore buwagorai do." He zagaganot beši ker aššil, manuš okkol heṛe uwore boišše. (Onumanik fãs hazar furuš manuš heṛe aššil.)
JOH 6:11 Tarfore Isaye he ruṭigun loi Allare šukuriya zanaiye edde zara boišše hitara ze zedun saiye hitare hedun hedun bag gori diye. Hibaye mas o hen gori bag gori diye.
JOH 6:12 Toi hitara beggune feṭ bori hái bade hibaye sahabi okkolore hodde, "Ze ṭuragun basi roiye hin beggun ekku fũwati dola goro, zene kissu nošto oi no zagoi."
JOH 6:13 Toi hitara hen goijje, hána hái bade ze he fãswa ruṭittu ṭura basi aššil hinore hitara dola gori baro barang oiye.
JOH 6:14 Isar ei keramoti ham deki mainše howahoi šuru goijje, "Iba oilde he nobi ze duniyait aiyer."
JOH 6:15 Isaye buzi faijje ze hitara aibo edde hitara hibare raza banaibolla zur goribo; hetolla hiba hentu šoṛi zaigoiyore ekela abar faharot giyegoi.
JOH 6:16 Toi hazinna zehon oiye, sahabi okkol lamat doriyar hãsat giye,
JOH 6:17 edde ekkan not uiṭṭe edde Kofornahumor mikka baisa diye. Ar hẽtte andar aiššil edde ehon o Isaye hitara loi ottor no o.
JOH 6:18 Heṛe beši zure bataš bonor zoriya fani beši utaltal oiye.
JOH 6:19 Hitara zẽtte tin sair mail no solai giye, bade dekedde Isaye fanir uwottu ãṛiyore hitarar mikka agguwai aiyer. Ar hitara beši ḍoraiye.
JOH 6:20 Kintu Isaye hitarare hodde, "Iba ãi, no ḍoraiyo."
JOH 6:21 Hitara hibare not tuli loito saiye, edde hehon nogan hitara zeṛe zat aššil he zagar kulot fõissegoi.
JOH 6:22 Tarfordin, ze manuš okkol doriyar oinno farot tiyai aššil, hitara deikke ze, heṛe ekkan bade ar hono no nu aššil, ar ze hibar sahabi okkol ziyanot uiṭṭe, Isaye hibar sahabi okkolor fũwati no hiyanot no uṛe, kintu hitara ekela gilgoi.
JOH 6:23 Ar Ṭaiberiyattu ho ekkan no, zeṛe Malike šukuriya zanai bade mainše ruṭi háil, he zagar ḍake aišše.
JOH 6:24 Mainšor dol okkole zehon dekilo ze Isa otóba hibar sahabi okkol kiye heṛe nai, hetunot hitara nogunot uiṭṭe edde Isare tuwaibolla Kofornahumot giye.
JOH 6:25 Ar hitara hibare doriyar ofarot faiyore, hitara hibare hodde, "Rabbi, õne eṛe hõtte aiššo?"
JOH 6:26 Isaye hitarare zuwab diye edde hodde, "Ãi tũwarare soiyi hoir, tũwara sinnor ham deikko boli tũwara ãre tuwodde no, bolke feṭ bori ruṭi hái faijjo boli.
JOH 6:27 Nošto oi zaiboide hánalla ham no goijjo, bolke hána zin akeri zibon foijjonto takibo, zin Adomor Fute tũwarare dibo, hinolla goro. Kiyollahoile he Baf Allah nize hibar uwore sil maijje."
JOH 6:28 Henot hitara hibare fusar goredde, "Henoile ãra Allar ham okkol goribolla ãrattu ki gora foribo?"
JOH 6:29 Isaye hitarare zuwabe hodde, "Allar ham oilde in: hibar uwore biššaš ano, zare Allaye defeṛaiye."
JOH 6:30 Toi hitara hibare hodde, "Õne ki en sinno goror, zin dekiyore ãra õnore biššaš gori faijjum? Õne en ki ham goriba de?
JOH 6:31 Ãrar bafdada okkole bošoti sara elehat manna háil, zendilla leka ase: 'Hibaye hitarare behostottu háibolla ruṭi diye.'"
JOH 6:32 Isaye hitarare hodde, "Ãi tũwarare soiyi soiyi hoir, tũwarare ruṭi behostottu Musaye diyede no, kintu ãr Bafe tũwarare behostottu he soiyi ruṭi de.
JOH 6:33 Kiyollahoile Allar ruṭi oilde hiba ze ruṭi behostottu nise lami aiye edde duniyaire zibon de."
JOH 6:34 Hitara hodde, "Malik, ei ruṭi ãrare hamiša do."
JOH 6:35 Isaye hitarare hodde, "Ãi oilamde he zibon ruṭi; hite ze ãr hãse aiye, hitattu buka no lagibo, ar hite ze ãre uwore biššaš ane, hite tiraši no oibo, hono dinolla.
JOH 6:36 Kintu ãi tũwarare hoiyi, tũwara ãre deikko, ar ehon o biššaš no goror.
JOH 6:37 Bafe zarare ãre diye, hitara beggun ãr hãse aibo, ar hite ze ãr hãse aiye, hitare ãi honodin baire felai no diyum.
JOH 6:38 Kiyollahoile ãi behostottu ãr issa mozin ham goribolla lami aiššide no, bolke hibar issa furon goribolla, ze ãre defeṛaiye.
JOH 6:39 Ar ze ãre defeṛaiye, hibar issa oilde iyan ze, hibaye beggun zarare ãre diye, hentu ekzon o zene ãi no harai, bolke šešor dinot hitarare uwafes tuli.
JOH 6:40 Ar ãr Bafor issa oilde iyan ze, fotti ekzon ze Futore sa edde hibar uwore biššaš ane, hite akeri zibon fa; ar ãi hitarare šešor dinot uwafes tuliyum."
JOH 6:41 Henot Ihudi okkole hibar berudde monmona šuru goijje, kiyollahoile hibaye hoil, "Ãi he ruṭi ze behostottu nise lami aišši."
JOH 6:42 Hitara hodde, "Iba ki Yusufor fut, Isa no ne? Zar baf mare ãra sini? Ite kengori endilla hoi fare, 'ãi behostottu nise lami aišši'?"
JOH 6:43 Isaye zuwabe hodde, "Tũwara ekzon loi ar ekzone monmonani bon goro;
JOH 6:44 Ãr Baf, ze ãre defeṛaiye, hibaye ṭani nu anile honokiye ãr hãse ai no fare, ar ãi hitare šešor dinot uwafes tuliyum.
JOH 6:45 Nobi okkolor kitabot leka ase: 'Hitara beggune Allar duwara šikka faibo.' Fottikiye ze Bafore funer edde hibattu šikka fa, hite ãr hãse aiyer.
JOH 6:46 Endilla no ze Bafore honokiye deke, hiba ze Allar hãsottu aišše, šude hibaye deikke Bafore.
JOH 6:47 Ãi tũwarare soiyi soiyi hoir, hite ze ãr uwore biššaš ane hitattu akeri zibon ase.
JOH 6:48 Ãi oilamde he zibonor ruṭi.
JOH 6:49 Tũwarar bafdada okkole bošoti sara elehat manna háil, ar hitara morigiyegoi.
JOH 6:50 Iba oilde he ruṭi ziba behostottu nise lami aišše, zene ze honokiye hibattu há, edde no morer.
JOH 6:51 Ãi oilamde he zinda ruṭi, ziba behostottu lami aišše. Hite ze ei ruṭi há, hite sirohalolla basibo. Ar ze ruṭi ãi diyum hiyan oilde ãr ga, ziyan ãi diyum duniyair zibonolla."
JOH 6:52 Ei hota funiyore Ihudi okkol ekzone ar ekzon loi doromoro barabari gori howa šuru goijje, "Ite kengori ãrare hitar ga haito di fare?"
JOH 6:53 Isaye hitarare hodde, "Ãi tũwarare soiyi soiyi hoir, Adomor Futor gusto zodi no ho, ar zodi no fiyo hibar lou, toile tũwarar butore zibon nai.
JOH 6:54 Hite ze ãr gusto edde lou há hitattu akeri zibon ase, ar ãi šeš dinot hitare uwafes tuliyum.
JOH 6:55 Ãr gusto oilde asol hána, ãr lou oilde asol fibar ziniš.
JOH 6:56 Hite ze ãr gusto edde lou há, hite ãr butore take ar ãi o hitar butore taki.
JOH 6:57 Zendilla zinda Bafe ãre defeṛaiye ar hibar duwara zinda asi, ṭik hendilla ze ãre há hite o ãr duwara zinda takibo.
JOH 6:58 Iba oilde he ruṭi ze behostottu nise lami aišše. Tũwarar bafdada okkole manna háil edde morigiyegoi, kintu ze honokiye ei ruṭi háibo hite sirohalolla basibo."
JOH 6:59 In okkol hibaye Kofornahumor sinagogot šikka dedde šomot hoil.
JOH 6:60 Hibar sahabi okkolor butore boute ei hota funiyore hodde, "In beši koṭin šikka. Hone inore gosi faribo?"
JOH 6:61 Hibar sahabi okkole ei babute monmonar, hiyan Isaye buzi fariyore hitarare hodde, "Iyanor zoriya ki tũwara forizorgoi?
JOH 6:62 Hetunot tũwara ki bafiba Adomor Fut age zeṛe aššil heṛe uṛi zargoide dekile?
JOH 6:63 Ruhuye zibon de; gustoye hono kissu faida no de, ze hota okkol ãi tũwarare hoilam, hin oilde Ruh edde zibon.
JOH 6:64 Tarfore o tũwarar butore en hozon ase, zara biššaš no gore." Kiyollahoile Isaye šuruttu loti zanito, hitara hontara zara hibare biššaš goribo, ar hite honnuwa ze hibar loi beimani goribo.
JOH 6:65 Ar hibaye hodde, "Etolla ãi tũwarare hoilam, zodi ãr Bafor torfottu kemota diya no o, toile honokiye ãr hãse ai no fare."
JOH 6:66 Iyar bade hibar bout sahabi okkol uwafes firi giyegoi edde hibar loi ar sola fira no gore.
JOH 6:67 Toi Isaye he barozonore fusar goijje, "Tũwara o ki uwafes firi zaibolla issa goror?"
JOH 6:68 Simon Fitore zuwabe hodde, "Malik, ãra har hãse zaiyum? Akeri zibonor kalam to õnor hãse ase.
JOH 6:69 Ãra biššaš goijji, ãra zani ze, õne Allar he Pakzon."
JOH 6:70 Toi Isaye hitarare hodde, "Ãi ki tũwara barozonore basi no loi ne? Zodi o tũwarar butore ekzon šoitan."
JOH 6:71 (Ei hota hibaye Iskariyoti Simonor fut Ehudar babute hoiyede, kiyollahoile hite, he barozonor butore ekzon oi bade o, hiba loi beimani goribo.)
JOH 7:1 In okkol bade, Isa Galilot gurafira gorer. Hiba Ehudiyat zaito no sa, kiyollahoile Ihudi neta okkole hibare marifelaibar kušišot aššil.
JOH 7:2 Ar hẽtte Ihudi bãša id (ziyanore Sukkut ho) hãsa hãsi aššil,
JOH 7:3 Isar báiyainde hibare hodde, "Enttu Ehudiyat zagoi, toi zene tui gorodde he ham okkol tor sahabi okkole deki fare.
JOH 7:4 Kiyollahoile ze nize mainšor muntu forhaš oito sa, hite gufone hono kissu no gore. Tui zehon in okkol goror, nizore duniyair sarme forhaš gor."
JOH 7:5 Kiyollahoile hibar nizor báiyainde o hibare biššaš no gorito.
JOH 7:6 Henot Isaye hitarare hodde, "Ãr ṭaim ehono nu aiye, kintu tũwarar ṭaim hamiša hazir.
JOH 7:7 Duniyaiye tũwarare hingša gori no fare, kintu hiyane ãre hingša gore, kiyollahoile ãi hiyanor babute goba di ze hiyanor ham horaf.
JOH 7:8 Idot tũwara zo; ãi ehon no zaiyum, kiyollahoile ãr ṭaim ehono furon no o."
JOH 7:9 Hibaye hitarare in okkol hoiyore hiba Galilot taigiyegoi.
JOH 7:10 Kintu hibar báiyain okkol uwore idot giyegoi, bade hiba nize o heṛe giye, tarfore o kulasa bafe no, gufone.
JOH 7:11 Idot Ihudi neta okkole Isare tuwail, ar hodde, "Hite hoṛe?"
JOH 7:12 Ar heṛe mainšor dolor butore hibar babute bout monmonani šuru oiye, kissuye hodde: "Hiba bala." Ar kiye hor, "No, hite mainšore bul fõtot loizargoi."
JOH 7:13 Kintu Ihudi neta okkolor ḍore honokiye hibar babute kulasa bafe kissu no ho.
JOH 7:14 Id ada adi oiyede ṭaimot Isa uwore dormogórot giye, edde šikka diya šuru goijje.
JOH 7:15 Henot Ihudi neta okkol tajjuf oiyore hodde, "Hono šikka no gori kengori ite endilla giyan zane?"
JOH 7:16 Isaye hitarare zuwabe hodde, "Ãr šikka ãr nizor no, kintu ze ãre defeṛaiye, hibar.
JOH 7:17 Ze honokiye hibar issa falon goribolla issa gore, hite ei šikkar babute zanibo, iyan Allattu or ne naki ãi nizottu hoi.
JOH 7:18 Hite ze nizottu ho hite hitar nizor tarif tuwa, kintu hite ze defeṛaiyede hibar tarif tuwa, toile hite soiyi, na soiyi hitar butore nai.
JOH 7:19 Musaye ki tũwarare ain no de ne? To tũwarar honokiye he ain falon no gore; tũwara ãre kiyolla marifelaito sor?"
JOH 7:20 Manuš okkole zuwabe hodde, "Tore bute faiye, tore marifelaito hone sar?"
JOH 7:21 Isaye zuwabe hitarare hodde, "Ãi ekkan ham goijji, ar tũwara beggune ammuwak oiyo.
JOH 7:22 Ar Musaye tũwarare azomi goraibar niyom dil, (zodi o ei niyom asole Musar hãsottu nu aiye, bafdada okkolottu aišše), ar tũwara Šabbator din o azomi goro.
JOH 7:23 Musar ain banga no ofan zodi Šabbator dinot ekzonore azomi gora za, toile Šabbatot ãi ekzon manušore furafuri aram goijjide hiyanolla kiyolla tũwara ãr uwore rag goror?
JOH 7:24 Tũwara dekodde mozin bisar no goijjo, bolke niyai bisar goro."
JOH 7:25 Hetunot hodun Zeruzalemor mainše hodde, "Manuš iba hiba no ne, zare hitara marifelaibolla tuwar?"
JOH 7:26 Kintu so, ite eṛe kulasa bafe hota hor, ar honokiye hitar berudde kissu no hor; toile šašon goroya okkole ki soiyi zani faijje ze iba Messiyah?"
JOH 7:27 Kintu ite hontu hiyan to ãra zani, ar Messiyah zẽtte aibo, hiba hontu honokiye no zanibo."
JOH 7:28 Tarfore Isaye dórmogóror uṛanot šikka dedde šomot guzori hodde,"Oi, tũwara ãre zano, ar ãi hontu iyano zano; ãi ãr nizottu nu aiyi, kintu ãre defeṛaiyede hiba soiyi, zare tũwara no zano,
JOH 7:29 ãi hibare zani, kiyollahoile ãi hibar hentu aišši, ar ãre hibaye defeṛaiye."
JOH 7:30 Henot hitara Isare doitto saiye, kintu honokiye hibar gat hat no de, kiyollahoile hibar ṭaim ehon o nu aiye.
JOH 7:31 Ehono, mainšor dolor butottu bout kiye hibar uwore biššaš ainne edde hodde, "Messiyah zẽtte aibo, hibaye ki ei manuššuwaye goijjede hinottuwaro beši sinno gori dehaibo?"
JOH 7:32 Foroši okkole hibar babute in okkol loi monmonadde fuinne; ar ḍõr imam okkole edde Foroši okkole hibare dori anibolla hoekzon dórmogóror faharadarore defeṛaiye.
JOH 7:33 Toi Isaye hodde, "Ehon o ãi olfo dinolla tũwarar fũwati asi, tarfore ze ãre defeṛaiye ãi hibar hãse zaiyumboi.
JOH 7:34 Tũwara ãre tuwaiba, kintu ãre no faiba; ar ãi zeṛe, heṛe tũwara ai no fariba."
JOH 7:35 Henot Ihudi okkole ekzonore ekzone hodde, "Iba hoṛe zaibo ze, ãra hibare tuwai no faiyum? Hiba hono ãrar Ihudi okkol zara Girikiyo okkolor fũwati šiṛašitta oi asede heṛe zaibo, edde Girikiyo okkolore šikka dibogoi?
JOH 7:36 Hibaye, 'Tũwara ãre tuwaiba, kintu tũwara ãre tuwai no faiba, ar ãi zeṛe, heṛe tũwara ai no fariba.' hoi ki hoito sadde?"
JOH 7:37 Idor šeše, ze din idor asol boro din, Isaye tiyaiyore guzori hodde, "Ze honokiye tiraši, hite ãr hãse aiyok edde fiyok.
JOH 7:38 Hite ze ãr uwore biššaš ane, kitabor leka mozin, hitar dilot zinda halor fani baibo."
JOH 7:39 Ei hota hibaye Pak Ruhur babute hoiye, hitara zara hibare biššaš goijje, hitara faibo, ze Pak Ruhure ehono diya no o, kiyollahoile hẽtte o Isare mohimaola gora no o.
JOH 7:40 Hibar hota okkol funiyore dolor butottu kiye kiye hodde, "Soiyi iba he nobi."
JOH 7:41 Ar kiye hodde, "Iba Messiyah" Kintu kiye kiye hodde, "Galilottu kengori Messiyah aibo?

JOH 7:43 Endilla gori hibare loi manuš okkolor butore bag oigiyegoi.
JOH 7:44 Ar hitarar butottu hodune hibare dorito saiye, kintu honokiye hibar gat hat no de.
JOH 7:45 Toi dormogór faharadar okkol uwafes ḍõr imam edde Foroši okkolor hãse aišše, toi hitara hitarare hodde, "Hitare tũwara nu ano kiyolla?"
JOH 7:46 Dormogór faharadar okkole zuwabe hodde, "Hibar ḍoilla endilla hota ar honokiye honodin no ho."
JOH 7:47 Henot Foroši okkole hodde, "Tũwarare o ki kufõtot loigiyegoi neki?
JOH 7:48 Šašon goroya okkol otóba Foroši okkolor butottu honokiye hitar uwore biššaš ainne ne, hono?
JOH 7:49 Kintu ei manušor dole Musar ain no zane, itarar uwore bodduwa ase."

JOH 7:53 Toi hitara beggune ze zar zar górot giyegoi,
JOH 8:1 kintu Isa zaitun faharot giyegoi.
JOH 8:2 Taforor din binna sore Isa abar dórmogóror uṛanot giye, zeṛe hár manuš okkol hibar sairo ḍakottu aišše. Ar hiba boiyore hitarare šikka diye.
JOH 8:3 Toi alem okkole edde Foroši okkole ekzon zenat dora háiyede mayafuware ainne edde hibare maze tiya goraiyore
JOH 8:4 edde hodde, "Ustad, ei mayafuware zenar hamot dora háiye.
JOH 8:5 Torar ainot Musaye endilla mayafuwaindore fattor maribolla ãrare hokum diye; kintu õne ki ho?"
JOH 8:6 Hitara hibare forikka goribolla iyan hoiye, zene hitara hibare hosuri dibolla ekkan muda tuwai fa. Kintu Isaye nise niyuriyore õl diyore meṛit leka šuru goijje.

JOH 8:8 Toi hiba abar nise niyuriyore meṛit leka doijje.
JOH 8:9 Toi hitara iyan funiyore ekzon ekzon, murubbi okkol loti šuru gori, giyegoi, šude Isa roigiyegoi, edde mayafuwawa hibar sarme tiyai aššil.
JOH 8:10 Isaye abar uzu oiyore he mayafuwaware hodde, "Mayafuwa, hitara hoṛe? Honokiye ki tore šasti no de?"
JOH 8:11 Hibaye hodde, "Malik, hono kiye nai." Toi Isaye hodde, "Henoile ãi o tore šasti no diyum; za ehon loti ar guna no goris."
JOH 8:12 Isaye abar mainšor loi hota hoiye, hibaye hodde, "Ãi duniyair nur; hite ze ãr fisa lo, hite andarot no ãṛibo, kintu hite zibonor nur faibo."
JOH 8:13 Foroši okkole hibare hodde, "Tui tor goba dor, tor goba soyi no."

JOH 8:15 Tũwara manušor ḍoilla bisar goro, kintu ãi honokiyor bisar no gori.
JOH 8:16 Ar zodi o ãi bisar gori, ãr bisar soiyi, kiyollahoile ãi ekela no, kintu ãi ãr Bafor fũwati asi, ze ãre defeṛaiye.

JOH 8:20 Ei hota okkol hibaye dórmogóror uṛanot šikka dibar šomot dan bakšur ḍake hoiye. Ar hibare honokiye no dore, kiyollahoile hehon o hibar ṭaim nu aiye.

JOH 8:22 Ihudi okkole hodde, "Hite ki nizor zan nize loibo, ar hetolla hor, 'Ãi zeṛe zaiyum tũwara heṛe ai no fariba.'?"

JOH 8:24 Ãi tũwarare hoilam ze tũwara tũwarar guna okkolot moriba; kiyollahoile tũwara zodi biššaš no goro ze ãi oi hiba, tũwara hameka tũwarar guna okkolot moriba."
JOH 8:25 Hitara hodde, "Tui honnuwa?" Hibaye hitarare hodde, "Hiyan ãi tũwarare šuruttu loti howat asi.
JOH 8:26 "Tũwarar babute hoibar edde bisar goribar ãttu beši kissu ase; kintu ze ãre defeṛaiye, hiba soiyi, ar ãi hibar hãsottu ziyan fuinni hiyan ãi duniyaire hoir."
JOH 8:27 Hibaye ze hibar nizor Bafor babute hor hiyan hitara buzi no fare.

JOH 8:29 Ãre defeṛoya ãr fũwati ase, ãre eka eri no zagoi, kiyollahoile ãi hamiša hibar razir ham gori."
JOH 8:30 Hibaye ei hota zehon hoiye, bout kiye hibar uwore biššaš ainne.
JOH 8:31 Isaye, Ihudi okkol zara hibar uwore biššaš ainne, hitarare hodde, "Tũwara zodi ãr hotar butore tako, toile soiyi tũwara ãr biššaši.
JOH 8:32 Toi tũwara soiyire zani fariba, ar he soiyiye tũwarare azadi dibo."

JOH 8:36 Hetolla Fute zodi tũwarare azadi de, toile tũwara soiyi azad oiba.

JOH 8:38 Ãi ãr Bafor hãse zin dekki he babute hoi, ar tũwara hin goro zin tũwara tũwarar bafottu fuinno."
JOH 8:39 Henot hitara zuwab diye, "Ãrar baf Ibrahim." Isaye hodde, "Tũwara zodi Ibrahimor fuwain oita, toile tũwara Ibrahimor ham gorita.
JOH 8:40 Kintu Allar hãsottu ze soiyi ãi funiyore tũwarare hoi boli tũwara ãre marifelaibolla kušiš goror. Ibrahime to endilla ham no gore.
JOH 8:41 Tũwara tũwarar bafor ham goror." Hitara hibare hodde, "Ãra zoura fuwain no; ãrar ek Baf ase: hiba oilde Allah."
JOH 8:42 Isaye hitarare hodde, "Allah zodi soiyi tũwarar Baf oito, toile tũwara ãre ador gorita, kiyollahoile ãi Allattu tũwarar eṛe aišši. Ãi nizottu nu aiyi; kintu hibaye ãre defeṛaiye.
JOH 8:43 Tũwara ãr hota kiyolla no buzo? Haron oilde iyan ze tũwara ãr hota bordaš gori no faro.
JOH 8:44 Tũwara tũwarar ek baf šoitanor, ar tũwara tũwarar bafor issa furon gora oilde tũwarar issa. Hite šuruttu loti ekzon kuni, soiyit no take, kiyollahoile hitar butore soiyi nai; hite zẽtte misa hota ho, hite hin hitar nizottu ho, kiyollahoile hite ek misa hoiya edde misa hota hoiyar baf.
JOH 8:45 Kintu ãi soiyi hoi, ar hetolla tũwara ãre biššaš no goror.
JOH 8:46 Tũwarar butottu ãre hone gunar hosurbon sabut gori fariba? Ar ãi zodi soiyi hoir, toile tũwara ãre biššaš kiya no goror?
JOH 8:47 Hite ze Allar, hite Allar kalam fune. Ar tũwara no funor, kiyollahoile tũwara Allar no."
JOH 8:48 He Ihudi okkole hibare zuwabe hodde, "Ãra ki ṭik no hoir ne ze tui ekzon Sameriyo, ar tore bute faiye?"
JOH 8:49 Isaye hodde, "Ãre bute no fa, kintu ãi ãr Bafore šorman gori, ar tũwara ãre ošormani goror.
JOH 8:50 Ãi ãr nizor tarif no tuwair, kintu ekzon ase ze tuwa, ar hiba oilde bisarhar.
JOH 8:51 Ãi tũwarare soiyi soiyi hoir, hite ze ãr kalam falon gore, hite honodin moron no dekibo."
JOH 8:52 Ihudi okkole zuwab diye, "Ehon, ãra zani farilam ze tore bute faiye; Ibrahim edde nobi okkol morigiyegoi; ar tui hor, hite ze ãr kalam falon gore hite honodin moron no dekibo.
JOH 8:53 Tui ki ãrar baf Ibrahim, ze morigiyegoi, hibattuwaro mohan? Ar nobi okkol o morigiyegoi. Tui nizore ki mone goros?"
JOH 8:54 Isaye zuwabe hodde, "Ãi zodi nizor tarif nize gori, toile ãr tarif kissu no; ãr Bafe ãr tarif gorer, hiba zar babute tũwara ho, hiba ãrar Allah.
JOH 8:55 Zodi o tũwarattu hibar zana nai, ar ãi zodi hoi ze ãi hibare no zani, toile tũwarar ḍoilla ãi o misa hoya oiyum; kintu ãi hibare zani edde hibar kalam falon gori.
JOH 8:56 Tũwarar baf Ibrahime ãr din saibolla aša loi kuši goijjil; ar hibaye hiyan deikke edde kuši goijje."

JOH 8:59 Henot hitara hibare mela maribolla fattor feṛai loiye, kintu Isa hitarattu lukaigiyegoi edde dórmogóror uṛanottu baire niyoli giyegoi.
JOH 9:1 Isa aṛi zat maze hibaye ek zormo anda manušore deikke.
JOH 9:2 Toi sahabi okkole hibare fusar goijje, hodde "Rabbi, guna hone goijjede, hite nize ne naki hitar ma bafe, ze hitattu anda zormo owa foijje?"
JOH 9:3 Isaye hodde, "Guna no ite goijje, otóba hitar ma bafe; kintu iyan oiye zene hitar butore Allar ham forhaš oi fare.
JOH 9:4 Din zetun ase hetun, ze ãre defeṛaiye, hibar ham ãra gora iyan zoruri. Rait aiyer, zẽtte honokiye ham gori no faribo.
JOH 9:5 Ãi zetodin duniyait asi, ãi oilamde duniyair nur."
JOH 9:6 Ei hota hoiyore, hibaye meṛit sep felaiyore hodun fũṭ goijje edde hin manušwar sukot lagai diye.
JOH 9:7 Tarfore hodde, "Za, Šiloam foirot zai dúifelagoi," (ziyanor mani gorile "defeṛa oiye" o). Toi hite zaiyore dúifelaiye, edde suke dekat maze firi aišše.
JOH 9:8 Ḍengór bam gójja okkol edde aro zara hite boiyore horat magitode dekkil, hitara hodde, "Ite no neki ze boiyore horat magitode?"
JOH 9:9 Kiye kiye, oi iba hite hoiye. Ar kiye hodde, "No, hitare saite hendilla lagedde" Kintu manušwaye nize hodde, "Oi, ãi hiba."
JOH 9:10 Hitara fusar goredde, "Kintu tor suk kengori kuli giyegoi?"
JOH 9:11 Hite zuwabe hodde, "Isa name manušwaye hodun fũṭ banaiye edde ãr sukor uwore lifidiye, ar ãre hodde, Šiloam foirot za, dúifelagoi; ãi zaiyore zehon dúifelaiyi, toi ãi deki faijji."
JOH 9:12 Hitara hodde, "hiba hoṛe?" Hite hodde, "Ãi no zani."
JOH 9:13 Toi hitara he anda aššilde manušware Foroši okkolor hãse loigiye.
JOH 9:14 Ze din Isaye fũṭ banaiyore manušwar suk kulidiye hedin aššilde Šabbat.
JOH 9:15 Hetolla Foroši okkole o hitattu fusar goijje, hite deki kengori faijje. Hite hitarare hodde: "Hibaye ãr sukgunor uwore fũṭ lifidiye, ar ãi duifelaiyi, toi ãi dekir."
JOH 9:16 Foroši hoekzone hodde, "Ei manušwa Allar hãsottu nu aiye, kiyollahoile hite Šabbat falon no gore." Ar kiye hodde, "Ekzon gunagar manuše kengori endilla sinnor ham gori fare?" Ei bafe hitarar butore baga bagi oiye.
JOH 9:17 Toi hitara he anda aššilde manušwattu abar fusar goijje, "Tui hitar babute ki hos, kiyollahoile hite to tor suk kuli diye" Manušwaye hodde, "Hiba ekzon nobi."
JOH 9:18 Ihudi okkole kintu manušwar baf mare ḍaki ani fusar no gore foijjonto hitara biššaš gori no faijjil ze hite age anda aššil, ar ehon deker.
JOH 9:19 Hitara manušwar baf mare fusar goijje, "Ite ki tũwarar he fut, ze anda zormo oiye boli tũwara ho? Ehon hite kengori deki farer?"
JOH 9:20 Hitar ma bafe zuwab diye, "Ãra zani iba ãrar fut, ar ite anda zormo oiye.
JOH 9:21 Kintu ehon hite kengori deki farer hiyan ãra no zani. Ar iyano no zani hiba honnuwa, ze hitar suk kuli diye. Hitattu boyoš oiye, hitattu fusar goro. Hite nizor babute nize hok."
JOH 9:22 Hitar baf maye Ihudi neta okkolor ḍore in okkol hoiye, kiyollahoile Ihudi neta okkol beggune razi aššil ze, ze kiye Isare Messiyah šikar gore, hitare sinagogottu niyolai diya oibo.
JOH 9:23 Iyanor zoriya hitar baf maye hoiye, "Hitar boyoš oiye, hitare fusar goro."
JOH 9:24 Anda aššilde manušware dusorabar ḍaikke edde hitare hodde, "Tui soiyi hoiyore Allare tarif de. Ãra to zani ze ei manušwa gunagar."
JOH 9:25 Hite hodde, "Hiba gunagar ne naki no ãi no zani, kintu ãi iyan zani ze, ãi age anda aššilam ar ehon ãi dekir!"
JOH 9:26 Toi hitara fusar goijje, "Hite tore ki goijje? Tor suk hite kengori kuli diye?"
JOH 9:27 Hite zuwab diye, "Ãi to tũwarare age hoiyi, kintu tũwara no funo. Toile tũwara abar kiyolla fuinto sor? Tũwara o ki hibar biššaši oito sor neki?"
JOH 9:28 Henot hitara hitare kub gozgozaiye edde hodde, "Tui hitar biššaši, kintu ãra Musar biššaši.
JOH 9:29 Ãra zani ze Allaye Musa loi hota hoiye, kintu ite hontu aišše hiyan ãra no zani."
JOH 9:30 Manušwaye hitarare zuwab diye, "Iyan ekkan ki tajjuiffa ze hiba hontu tũwara no zano, otoso hibaye ãr suk kuli diye.
JOH 9:31 Ãra zani ze Allaye gunagarore no fune, kintu hite zodi Allah bokto o, ar hibar issa falon gore, hibaye hitare fune.
JOH 9:32 Duniyai sirišti oiye loti iyan endilla honodin funa no za ze, honokiye zórmottu loti anda mainšor suk kuli diye.
JOH 9:33 Hiba zodi Allattu no aito, toile hibaye kissu gori no farito."
JOH 9:34 Hitara hodde, "Tor zormo ekkubare gunar butore oiyore, ar ãrare šikka dor!" Bade hitara hitare baire niyolai diye.
JOH 9:35 Isaye fuinne ze, hitara manušware bair gori diye, ar hibaye hitare tuwai faiyore hodde, "Tui ki Adomor Futore biššaš goros ne?"
JOH 9:36 Hite zuwab diye, "Malik, hiba honnuwa? Toi zene ãi hibare biššaš gori fari."
JOH 9:37 Toi Isaye hitare hodde, "Tui hibare dekor, ar hibaye tor loi hota hor."
JOH 9:38 Hetunot he manušwaye hodde, "Malik, ãi biššaš gori" ar hite hibare soida goijje.
JOH 9:39 Isaye hodde, "Bisarolla ãi ei duniyait aišši, zene zara anda hitara deke, ar zara deke hitara anda o."
JOH 9:40 Foroši okkolor butottu zara hibar fũwati aiššil hitara in okkol fuinne, toi hitara hibare hodde, "Ãra o ki anda neki?"
JOH 9:41 Isaye hodde, "Tũwara zodi anda oita, toile tũwarattu hono guna no takito; kintu ehon tũwara hor, 'Ãra dekir,' Hetolla tũwarar guna taki giyegoi."
JOH 10:1 "Ãi tũwarare soiyi soiyi hoir, hite ze soolor zãkot doroza bai no gole, kintu oinno ḍak bai zai faraiyore gole, hite ekzon sur edde ekzon ḍahait.
JOH 10:2 Kintu ze doroza bai gole, hite oilde soolgunor soroya.
JOH 10:3 Doroza fahara doyaye hiballa doroza kuli de, ar soolgune hibar abaz fune, ar hibar nizor soolgunore hibaye nam dori ḍake edde fõt dehai barkule loiza.
JOH 10:4 Ar zehon hibaye hibar nizor soolgunore barkule niyolaiye, hiba hitarar age age za, edde soolgune hibar fisa lo, kiyollahoile hitara hibar abaz sine.
JOH 10:5 Kintu hitara osina ekzonor fise no loibo; bolke hitar hãsottu dái zaiboi, kiyollahoile osina mainšor abazore hitara no sine."
JOH 10:6 Isaye ei mesal kahanigan hitarare hoiye, kintu hibaye hitarare ki ze hoiye, hiyan hitara no buze.
JOH 10:7 Hetolla Isaye abar hodde, "Ãi tũwarare soiyi soiyi hoir, soolgunolla ãi oilamde he doroza.
JOH 10:8 Beggun zara ãr age aišše, hitara sur okkol edde ḍahait okkol, kintu soolgune hitarare no fune.
JOH 10:9 Ãi doroza; ze ãr butottu di gole, hite uddar oibo edde butore aibo edde bare zaibo, ar sori háibolla zaga faibo.
JOH 10:10 Sur aiye šude zene hite suri, kun edde dongšo gori fare; ãi aiššyi, zene hitara zibon fa edde zaf di forefan gori fa.
JOH 10:11 "Ãi he bala soolsoroya. Bala soolsoroyaye soololla hitar nizor zibon šebi de.
JOH 10:12 Kintu betondari, ze sool soroya no, ar sool o zin hitar nizor no, ar so, hite zehon genḍa bag aiyedde deker, soolgun eri dái zargoi; toi bage hinore súlai loizagoi edde šiṛašiṭṭa goride,
JOH 10:13 kiyollahoile hite ekzon betondari, hitattu soolgunolla hono dorod nai.
JOH 10:14 "Ãi oilamde he bala soolsoroya; ãi ãrgunore sini ar ãrgune o ãre sine,
JOH 10:15 zendilla ãr Bafe ãre sine, ar ãi Bafore sini, soololla ãi ãr zibon šebi di.
JOH 10:16 Ãttu aro sool okkol ase, zin ei zãkor no, hitarare o ãttu ana foribo edde hitara o ãr abaz funibo, ar henot ugguwa zãk edde ekzon soolsoroya oibo.
JOH 10:17 Ãr Bafe ãre ador gore, kiyollahoile ãi ãr zibon šebi di, zene hiyan ãi abar uwafes firai loi fari.
JOH 10:18 Ãr foran honokiye no lor, bolke ãi nize hiyan šebi dir, ar hiyan šebi dibar kemota ãttu ase; edde hiyan abar loibar kemota o ãttu ase; ei hokum ãr Bafottu ãi faiyi."
JOH 10:19 Ei hota okkolor zoriya Ihudi okkolor butore abar baga bagi oiye.
JOH 10:20 Hitarar bout kiye hodde, "Hitar butore ek but ase, hite fool. Tũwara hitar hota kiyolla funor?"
JOH 10:21 Ar kiye hodde, "Ekzon bute faiya manuše endilla hota okkol no ho. Bute ki anda mainšor suk kuli di fare?"
JOH 10:22 Tarfore hannuka id aišše, ar hẽtte šit hal.
JOH 10:23 Isaye dórmogóror butore badša Soloimanor haissarat ãṛa ãṛi gorer.
JOH 10:24 Hẽtte Ihudi okkole hibar sairo ḍakottu zoma oiye edde hibaye hodde, "Tui ãrare ar hoto din šondot rakibi? Tui zodi Messiyah, toile ãrare ho."
JOH 10:25 Isaye zuwabe hodde, "Ãi to tũwarare hoiyi, kintu tũwara biššaš no goro. Ãr bafor name ze ham okkol ãi gori, hine ãr babute goba de,
JOH 10:26 kintu tũwara biššaš no goro, kiyollahoile tũwara ãr sool no.
JOH 10:27 Ãr sool okkole ãr abaz fune, ãi hitarare zani, edde hitara ãr fisa lo.
JOH 10:28 Ãi hitarare akeri zibon di, edde hitara honodin dongšo no oibo, ar honokiye ãr hatottu hitarare hari loi no faribo.
JOH 10:29 Ãr baf, ze hitarare ãre diye, hiba oilde hár kissuttuwaro mohan, ar honokiye ãr Bafor hatottu hari loi no faribo.
JOH 10:30 Ãi edde Baf ek."
JOH 10:31 Hetunot Ihudi okkole hibare maribolla abar fattor feṛailoiye,
JOH 10:32 kintu Isaye hitarare hodde, "Ãi ãr Bafor hentu tũwarare beši bala ham okkol gori dehaiyi. Hinor butore honnanolla tũwara ãre fattor mariba?"
JOH 10:33 Ihudi okkole zuwab diye, "Hono bala hamolla tore ãra fattor no marir, kintu kuferilla, haron tui ekzon manuš oiyore, nizore Allah dabi goror."
JOH 10:34 Isaye hodde, "Tũwarar ainot ki endilla leka nai ne, 'Ãi hoilam, tũwara allah okkol'?

JOH 10:36 Henoile, zare Bafe fobitro goijje edde duniyait defeṛaiye, tũwara ki hoiba, ze 'Tui kuferi goror' kiyollahoile ãi hoilam ze 'ãi Allar Fut'?
JOH 10:37 Ãr Bafor ham zodi ãi no gori, toile tũwara ãre biššaš no goijjo.
JOH 10:38 Kintu ãi zodi gori, tũwara ãre biššaš no gorile o, hamgunore oile biššaš goro, zene tũwara zani faro edde buzi faro ze, Baf ãr butore, ar ãi Bafor butore asi."
JOH 10:39 Abar hitara Isare doitto kušiš goijje, kintu hiba hitarar hatottu harigiyegoi.
JOH 10:40 Tarfore Isa abar Zordanor ofarot giye, zeṛe Yahyaye torikotor gusol dito. Hiba heṛe taikke.
JOH 10:41 Bout manuš okkol hibar hãse aišše, edde hodde, "Yahyaye hono keramoti ham no gore, tarfore o kintu hibaye ei manušwar babute zin zin hoiye hin beggun soiyi."
JOH 10:42 Ar heṛe bout manuš okkol Isar biššaši oiye.
JOH 11:1 Betaniyat ekzon ošuikka manuš aššil, nam Lazarus; ar hite Moriyam edde hibar boin Martár farar manuš.
JOH 11:2 (Iba he Moriyam, ze Malikore kušbo tel loi ḍoli dil, ar hibar nizor sul loi ṭeng fũsi dil, zar bái Lazarusottu ehon ošuk.)
JOH 11:3 Hetolla boinain okkole Isar hãse hóbor defeṛaiye, "Malik, zar loi õne kuši hitattu ehon ošuk."
JOH 11:4 Isaye ei hota funiyore hodde, "Ei ošuk moribolla no o, kintu Allar tarifolla, zene iyanor duwara Allar Fut mohimawala oi fare."
JOH 11:5 Isaye Martá, hibar boin edde Lazarusore ador gorito.
JOH 11:6 Hibaye zehon hitattu ošuk oiyede fuinne, hiba zeṛe aššil heṛe aro dui din taigiyegoi.
JOH 11:7 Tarfore hibaye sahabi okkolore hodde, "Aiyo, ãra abar Ehudiyat zai."
JOH 11:8 Sahabi okkole hibare hodde, "Rabbi, ei kissu din age no ne Ihudi okkole õnore fattor maitto saiye, ar õne abar heṛe zodde?"
JOH 11:9 Isaye zuwabe hodde, "Dinot ki baro gonḍa nai ne? Ar hite ze dinot solafira gore, hite ujaṭ no há, kiyollahoile hite ei duniyair fohor deke.
JOH 11:10 Ar hite ze raitta solafira gore, hite ujaṭ há, kiyollahoile hitar butore fohor nai."
JOH 11:11 Hibaye in okkol hoiye, in bade hibaye hitarare hodde, "Ãrar bondu Lazarus gumot foijje, kintu ãi hitare gumottu tulibolla heṛe zair."
JOH 11:12 Toi sahabi okkole hodde, "Malik, hite gum giyede oilede hite bala oi zaiboi."
JOH 11:13 Kintu Isaye hitar moronor babute hoilde, kintu hitara ṭaijje hibaye amfam gumor hota hor.
JOH 11:14 Toi Isaye foriškar gori hoiye, "Lazarus morigiyegoi,
JOH 11:15 ar tũwaralla hoi ãi kuši ze ãi heṛe nu aššilam, zene tũwara biššaš gori faro; hetolla aiyo, ãra Lazarusor hãse zai."
JOH 11:16 Hetunot Tomas, (zare Didymus ho) hibaye oinno fũwajja sahabi okkolore hodde, "Aiyo, ãra o zai, zene ãra o hitar fũwati mori fari."
JOH 11:17 Isa aiyore zani faijje ze, Lazarus hẽtte hoborot asede sair din oiye.
JOH 11:18 Betaniya aššilde Zeruzalemor hãsa hãsi, onumanik tin kilomiṭaror fõt.
JOH 11:19 Ihudi okkolor butottu boute Martá edde Moriyamor hãse aišše, zene hitarar báiyor babute šantona di fare.
JOH 11:20 Martáye zehon fuinne ze Isa aiyer, hiba zaiyore hibar loi deha goijje, ar Moriyam gorot boiṛa taigiyegoi.
JOH 11:21 Martáye Isare hodde, "Malik, õne zodi eṛe takita, toile ãr báiwa no morito.
JOH 11:22 Kintu ãi zani, õne Allar hãse ze kissu saiba, hin Allaye õnore dibo."
JOH 11:23 Isaye hibare hodde, "Tor bái abar uṛibo."
JOH 11:24 Martáye hodde, "Ãi zani šeš hale uwafes zindar šomot hite o uṛibo."
JOH 11:25 Isaye hodde, "Ãi oilamde he uwafes zinda edde he zibon. Hite ze ãr uwore biššaš ane hite morile o zinda takibo;
JOH 11:26 ar hite ze zinda edde ãre biššaš gore hite hono din no moribo, iyan ki biššaš goros?"
JOH 11:27 Hibaye hodde, "Oi, Malik, ãi biššaš gori õne he Messiyah, Allar Fut, ze duniyait aibar hota."
JOH 11:28 Ei hota hoi Martá zaiyore hibar boin Moriyamore gufone ḍakiyore hodde, "Malik eṛe ase, ar tore ḍaker."
JOH 11:29 Moriyame ei hota funiyore, toratori uiṭṭe edde hibar hãse giye.
JOH 11:30 Isa hetunot o farar butore no aiye, kintu ehono he zagat zeṛe Martáye hiba loi deha oil.
JOH 11:31 Ze Ihudi okkol Moriyamor górot aššil edde hibare šantona diyat aššil, hitara dekedde Moriyam toratori uṛi baire giye, ar hitara o hibar fise fise giye, ar mone goijje ze hibaye hoboror ḍake handito zar boli.
JOH 11:32 Toi Moriyam, Isa zeṛe aššil, hiba heṛe aišše edde hibare dekiyore hibar ṭengot foijje edde hodde, "Malik, õne zodi eṛe takita, toile ãr bái no morito."
JOH 11:33 Toi Isaye hibar handani edde hibar fũwati ze Ihudi okkol aššil, hitara handani dekiyore hibar dilor butore hoisali oiye, toi hibaye hodde,
JOH 11:34 "Tũwara hitare hoṛe raikko?" Hitara hodde, "Malik, aiyo sogai."
JOH 11:35 Isaye hainde.
JOH 11:36 Toi Ihudi okkole hodde, "So, hiba hitare loi hondilla kuši."
JOH 11:37 Kintu hitarar hodune hodde, "Iba hiba no ne, ze he anda manušwar suk ze kuli diye, hibaye ki ite no morefan gori no farito ne?"
JOH 11:38 Henot Isar dilot abar o hoisali oiye edde hoboror hãse aišše, ar hiba aššilde ugguwa guha, ar hiyanor uwore ugguwa šil aššil.
JOH 11:39 Isaye hodde, "Šilgan šoraifelo." morigiyegoide hitar boin Martáye hodde, "Malik, ehon hitattu baš uṛer, kiyollahoile hite heṛe sair dinna mora."
JOH 11:40 Isaye hibare hodde, "Ãi ki tore no hoi ne, ze tui zodi biššaš goros, toile tui Allar mohima dekibi?"
JOH 11:41 Tarfore hitara šilgan šoraifelaiye. Isaye hibar suk uwor mikka tuille edde hodde,"Baf, ãi tũware šukuriya gori, ze tũi ãre fuinno.
JOH 11:42 Ar ãi zani ze tũi ãre hamiša funo; kintu eṛe ze manuš okkol tiyaiye hitaralla ãi ei hota hoir, zene hitara ekin gore, ze tũi ãre defeṛaiyo."
JOH 11:43 In okkol hoi bade, hibaye ek zur abaz loi hodde, "Lazarus, niyoli ai."
JOH 11:44 Henot morawa niyoli aišše; hitar hat ṭeng aššil kafonor hor loi banda, ar hitar mukot aššil ekkan gamsa loi banda. Isaye hitarare hodde, "Hitare kuli do, hitare zaito do."
JOH 11:45 Bout Ihudi okkol zara Moriyamor hãse aiššil, edde Isaye ki goijje hin dekiyore, hitara hibar uwore biššaš ainne.
JOH 11:46 Kintu hitarar kiye kiye Foroši okkolor hãse giye, edde Isaye ki goijje hin hitarare hoiye.
JOH 11:47 Toi ḍõr imam edde Foroši okkole ḍõr šoba Sanhedrinore ekottro goriyore hodde, "Ãra ehon ki goriyum? Ei manušwaye bout sinnor ham okkol gorer.
JOH 11:48 Ãra zodi itare endilla solito di, toile beggune hitar uwore biššaš anibo; ar Romiyo okkol aiyore ãrar paki zaga edde ãrar zati dunigun hari loibo."
JOH 11:49 Ar hitarar butore ekzon, Kaifas name, he bosoror ḍõr imam, hibaye hitarare hodde, "Tũwara kissu no zano.
JOH 11:50 Ar bafi no sor ne ze, iyan ãralla bala oibo, mainšolla ekzon manuš more, edde guṛa zati dongšo no o."
JOH 11:51 Ei hota hite nizottu hoiye hen no, kintu hite he bosoror ḍõr imam hisabe hite nobi hisabe hota hoiye, ze Isa zatilla moribo,
JOH 11:52 šude he zatilla no, bolke he Allar fuwain okkololla o, zara šiṛašitta oi roiye, zene hibaye hitarare dola gore edde ek gore.
JOH 11:53 He dinottu loti hitara felain goijje ze hitara hibare marifelaibo.
JOH 11:54 Hetolla Isaye Ihudi okkol loi ar kulasa solafira no gore, kintu hentu zaigoiyore bošoti sara elehar ḍake Efraim name ekkan šohorot giye, zeṛe hiba hibar sahabi okkolore loi taikke.
JOH 11:55 Hẽtte Ihudi okkolor uddar id hãse aiššil, ar boute uddar idor age hitara nizore paksaf goribolla dešottu uwore Zeruzalem giye.
JOH 11:56 Hitara Isare tuwat aššil, edde dormogórot tiyaiyore ekzone oinnozonore hodde, "Tũwarattu ken lage? Hiba idot nu aibo ne ki?"
JOH 11:57 Ḍõr imam edde Foroši okkole hokum dilo ze, Isa hoṛe ase hiyan zodi honokiye zane hóborgan hitarare de, zene hitara Isare dori fare.
JOH 12:1 Uddar idor só din age Isa Betaniyat aišše, heṛe he Lazarus aššil, zare hibaye morattu tuille.
JOH 12:2 Heṛe hiballa ek hánar entezam gora oiye, ar Martáye hána bari dil, ar Lazarus o hibar fũwati hánar ṭebilot boiššilde hitarar maze.
JOH 12:3 Hen šomot Moriyame ada liṭar beši dami, haṭi ator aniyore Isar ṭengot ḍoli diye edde hibar sul loi hibar ṭeng fũsi diye. Ar he atoror kušboye gór bori giyegoi.
JOH 12:4 Iskariyoti Ehudah, hibar sahabi okkolor ekzon, ze hiba loi beimani goribo, hite endilla hodde,
JOH 12:5 "Ei ator in tin šot denar di besiyore kiyolla gorib okkolore diya no or?"
JOH 12:6 Hitattu goribolla dorod asede hiyan bafiyore hite ei hota hoiyede no, kintu hite aššilde ek sur, ar ṭiyar beg hitar hatot takitode hisabe, zin heṛe raka oito hite hentu loifelaito.
JOH 12:7 Isaye hodde,"Hiba loi hen no goijjo! Hibaye hin ãr hoboror dinolla raikkede.
JOH 12:8 Gorib okkol to hamiša tũwarar fũwati ase, kintu ãre hamiša tũwara no faiba."
JOH 12:9 Isa Betaniyat ase zani fariyore Ihudi okkolor ek ḍõr dol heṛe aišše, hitara šude Isare saito nu aiye, bolke Lazarus, zare hibaye morattu tuille, hitare o saito aišše.
JOH 12:10 Ar ḍõr imam okkole felain goijje zene hitara Lazarusore o marifelai fare,
JOH 12:11 kiyollahoile hitalla buli Ihudi okkolor boute heṛe zat aššil edde Isare biššaš gorat aššil.
JOH 12:12 Tarforor din idot falon goitto aiššede ek dõr mainšor dole Isa Zeruzalem aiyer funiyore,
JOH 12:13 hitara hazu fatar ḍeila okkol loiye edde dola oibolla niyoli giye, ar guzori hoiye, "Hosanna!" "Rahamoti hiba ze mabudor name aiyer, Israilor badša!"
JOH 12:14 Ar Isaye ugguwa gadar so faiye edde hibar uwore boišše, iyan zendilla leka ase:
JOH 12:15 "O Sion hoinna, no ḍorais, sa, tor badša aiyer, gadar sor fiṛot boiyore."
JOH 12:16 Hibar sahabi okkole in okkol foila buzi no fare, kintu Isa zehon mohimawala oiye, hẽtte hitarattu monot foijjil ze in okkol hibar babute leka aššil, edde manuš okkole hibare in okkol goijje.
JOH 12:17 Isa Lazarusore hoborottu aibolla ḍaikkede edde morattu tuillede šomot ze manuš okkol hibar fũwati aššil, hitara he babute goba diyat aššil.
JOH 12:18 Ar hetolla bout manuš okkole zaiyore hiba loi dola oiye, kiyollahoile hibaye ei sinnor ham goijjede hitara fuinnil.
JOH 12:19 Toi Foroši okkol ekzone ar ekzonore hodde, "Tũwara dekor, tũwarar hono kissu lab no or; so, duniyai udda hitar fisa loiye."
JOH 12:20 Idot ebadot goitto aiššede hitarar maze ho ekzon Girikiyo aššil.
JOH 12:21 Hitara Galilor Betsaidar Filipor hãse aišše, edde hibare foriyad goijje, "Ustad, ãra Isare saito sai."

JOH 12:25 Hite ze nizor foranore beši ador gore, hite hiyan haraibo; ar hite ze nizor zibonore ei duniyait hingša gore, hite hiyan akeri zibonolla basaibo.
JOH 12:26 Hite ze ãr šeba goribo, hite ãr fisa lok, ar ãi zeṛe, heṛe ãr šeba goroya o oibo; ar hite ze ãr šeba gore, ãr Bafe hitare šorman dibo.
JOH 12:27 "Ehon ãr dil ferešani oiye; iyanot ki ãi ki en hoiyum ne? 'Baf, ei ṭaimottu ãre basao'? no, bolke ai aiššilamde to ei ṭaimolla.
JOH 12:28 Baf, tũwar nam mohimawala goro!" Hetunot asmanottu ek abaz aišše, "Ãi hiyan mohimawala goijji, ar ãi abar hiyan mohimawala goriyum."

JOH 12:32 Ar ãi, ãre zẽtte zobinottu tula oibo, hár manušore ãi ãr mikka ṭaniyum."
JOH 12:33 Ar hibaye ei hotar duwara sin diye ze ki moron hibaye moribo.
JOH 12:34 Mainšor dole hodde, "Ãra Torar ainottu fuinni ze Messiyah sirohal takibo; toile tũi kene hoi faror, 'Adomor Futore uwore tula owa foribo'? Toile iba hon 'Adomor Fut'?"
JOH 12:35 Isaye hitarare hodde, "Aro olfo ṭaimolla šude he nur tũwarar fũwati ase; he nur tũwarar fũwati takite ãṛo, zene andar aiyore tũwarar uwore no fore; ar hite ze andarot sole, hoṛe zar hiyan hite no zane.
JOH 12:36 Nur tũwarar hãse takite nuror uwore biššaš ano, zene tũwara nuror fũwain oi faro." Ei hota hoiya oi bade Isaye hitarar hãsottu giyegoi edde hitarattu gufon oigiyegoi.
JOH 12:37 Zodi o Isaye hitarar sarme eduggun keramoti ham okkol goijje, tarfore o hitara hibar uwore biššaš no ane.
JOH 12:38 Iyan oiye zendilla Esaiya nobiye hoilde hota furon o: "Malik, ãrar diya hóbor hone biššaš goijje, Har hãse Malikor ḍũwa forhaš oiye?"
JOH 12:39 Etolla hitara biššaš no gore, kiyollahoile, zendilla Esaiyaye aro hor:
JOH 12:40 "Hibaye hitarar suk anda gori diye, ar hitarar dilore doro gori diye, zene hitara suk diyore no deke, ar hitarar dile o no buze, ar uwafes no fire, ar ãi hitarare aram goritam."
JOH 12:41 Esaiyaye in okkol hoiye, kiyollahoile hibaye Isar mohima dekkil edde hibar babute hoil.
JOH 12:42 Tarfore o neta okkolor butore boute hibar uwore biššaš ainne, kintu Foroši okkolor ḍore šikar no gore, ze hitarare sinagogottu niyolai dibo;

JOH 12:44 Bade Isaye guzori uiṭṭe, "Hite ze ãr uwore biššaš ane, hite ãr uwore no, kintu ze ãre defeṛaiye, hibar uwore biššaš ane.
JOH 12:45 Ze ãre deke, hite hibare deke, ze ãre defeṛaiye.

JOH 12:47 "Hite ze ãr kalam fune edde hin falon no gore, ãi nize hitar bisar no gori, kiyollahoile ãi duniyair bisar goribolla no, bolke duniyaire uddar goribolla, aišši.
JOH 12:48 Ze ãre hela gore edde ãr hota no gose, hitalla ek bisarhar ase; ãi ze kalam hoiyi, šeš dinot hiyane hitar bisar goribo.

JOH 12:50 Ar ãi zani ze, hibar hokum oilde akeri zibon; hetolla ãi zin hoi, Bafe ãre zendilla hoiye, hendilla hoi."

JOH 13:9 Simon Fitore hibare hodde, "Malik, toile šude ãr ṭeng no, kintu ãr hat edde mata o dui do."
JOH 13:10 Isaye hitare hodde,"Ze gusol goijje, ṭeng duwa sara hitattu ar hono kissur dorhar nai, hitar agagura foriškar, hite Pak fobitro. Ar tũwara Pak fobitro, kintu beggune no."

JOH 13:17 Ehon, tũwara in okkol zano, ar hin okkol zodi goro, toile tũwarar mubarok.
JOH 13:18 "Ãi tũwara beggunor hota no hoir; ãi hontarare ãlla basona goijji ãi zani. Kintu kitabor ei kalam furon owa forer: 'Ze ãr ruṭi hár, hite ãr berudde formuri tuille.'
JOH 13:19 "In goṭibar agottu ãi tũwarare hoi rakir, zene zẽtte in goṭibo hẽtte tũwara biššaš goro ze, ãi hiba.
JOH 13:20 Ãi tũwarare soiyi soiyi hoir, ãi zare defeṛai, hitare ze gose, hite ãre gose, ãre ze gose, hite hibare gose, ze ãre defeṛaiye."
JOH 13:21 Ei hota hoi bade Isar dilot hoisali oiye, ar goba diye, "Ãi tũwarare soiyi soiyi hoir, tũwarar butottu ekzone ãre dorai dibo."

JOH 13:23 Hetunot Isar sahabi okkolor butottu ekzon, zare Isaye muhabbot gorito, hite hibar kulot elan di boiššil.
JOH 13:24 Hetunot Simon Fitore išara goijjil edde hodde, "Hibaye zar babute hor, hiba honnuwa?"

JOH 13:26 Isaye zuwab diye, "Ei ruṭir ṭuragan buraiyore ãi zare diyum, iba oilde hite." Toi hibaye ruṭir ṭuragan buraiyore Iskariyoti Simonor fut Ehudare diye.

JOH 14:24 Hite ze ãre ador no gore, hite ãr kalam falon no gore; ar ze kalam okkol tũwara funor, hin ãr no, kintu Bafor, ze ãre defeṛaiye.

JOH 16:1 "In okkol ãi tũwarare hoilam, zene tũwara fori no zogoi.
JOH 16:2 Hitara tũwarare sinagogottu niyolai dibo; enki, en ṭaim aiyer, zẽtte tũwarare ze hono kiye marifelaibo, hite mone goribo, ze hiyan hitara Allare ek šeba der.
JOH 16:3 Hitara endilla goribo, kiyollahoile hitara no Bafore zane, ar no ãre zane.
JOH 16:4 Ãi tũwarare in okkol hoilam, zene hitarar ṭaim zẽtte aibo, tũwarar monot take ze ãi tũwarare hitarar babute hoiyi. Ãi tũwarare in age no hoi, kiyollahoile ãi tũwarar fũwati aššilam,
JOH 16:5 kintu ehon ãi zairgoi, ze ãre defeṛaiye hibar heṛe. Ar tũwarar honokiye ãre fusar o no goror, 'Tũi hoṛe zodde?'
JOH 16:6 Bolke ãi tũwarare in okkol hoi boli tũwarar dil dukke bori uiṭṭe.
JOH 16:7 Kintu ãi tũwarare soiyi hoir, ãi zairgoide hiyan tũwaralla bala, kiyollahoile ãi no zailegoi, he modot goroya tũwarar hãse no aibo; kintu ãi zodi zaigoi, toi hibare tũwarar hãse faṭai diyum.
JOH 16:8 Ar hiba aiyore gunar babute, soiyir babute edde forhesgarir babute, duniyaire golti dehai dibo:
JOH 16:9 gunar zoriya, hitara ãr uwore biššaš no ane.
JOH 16:10 edde forhesgarir babute, kiyollahoile ãi Bafor heṛe zair, ar tũwara ãre ar no dekiba;
JOH 16:11 ar Bisar babute, kiyollahoile ei duniyair šašon goroyar bisar oigiyegoi.
JOH 16:12 "Tũwarare ãttu bout kissu hoibar ase, kintu tũwara ehon hin bordaš gori no fariba.
JOH 16:13 Ar zẽtte hiba, he soiyir Ruh, aibo, hẽtte hibaye fõt dehaiyore tũwarare hár soyit loizaibo; kiyollahoile hibaye hiba nizottu hota no hoibo, kintu zin funibo hin hoibo, edde sarme goṭibode hin okkol tũwarare hoibo.
JOH 16:14 Hibaye ãre mohimawala goribo, kiyollahoile hibaye ãrgun loibo, edde tũwarare zanai dibo.
JOH 16:15 Ar Bafottu zin zin ase, beggun ãr; etolla ãi hoiyi, ze hibaye ãrgun loibo edde tũwarare zanai dibo."
JOH 16:16 "Olfo ṭaimor butore tũwara ãre ar no dekiba, toi tarfore abar olfo ṭaimor butore tũwara ãre dekiba."
JOH 16:17 Henot hibar sahabi okkol ho ekzone ekzonore ekzone hodde, "Ibaye ãrare in ki hor, 'Olfo ṭaimor butore tũwara ãre ar no dekiba, tarfore abar olfo ṭaimor butore tũwara ãre dekiba,' ar, 'Ãi Bafor hãse zair'?
JOH 16:18 Toi hitara hodde, "Hibaye 'olfo ṭaimor butore' hoi ki hodde? Hibaye ki hor ãra buzi no farir."
JOH 16:19 Isaye deikke ze hitara ei babute fusar goitto sar, toi hibaye hitarare hodde, "Tũwara ki ei babute howahoi goror ze ãi hoilam, 'Olfo ṭaimor butore tũwara ãre ar no dekiba, tarfore abar olfo ṭaimor butore tũwara ãre dekiba'?
JOH 16:20 Ãi tũwarare soiyi hoir, tũwara handiba edde bilag goriba, kintu duniyaiye anondo goribo; tũwara ferešan oiba, kintu tũwarar ferešani anondo oi zaibogoi.
JOH 16:21 Fuwa oibar šomot mayafuwaye duk fa, kiyollahoile hibar ṭaim aišše, kintu hibar fuwa zormo oi bade, ekzon noya manuš duniyait aišše, ei anondoye hibattu ar he bišor hota monot no take.
JOH 16:22 Hendilla tũwara o ehon duk for, kintu ãi tũwara loi abar deha oiyum, ar tũwarar dile anondo goribo, edde tũwarar he anondo honokiye no loi zaibo.
JOH 16:23 He din tũwara ãttu hono kissu suwal goribolla no takibo; soiyi soiyi, ãi tũwarare hoir, tũwara Bafor hãse zodi kissu so, hibaye ãr name tũwarare hin dibo.
JOH 16:24 Ehon foijjonto tũwara ãr name kissu no so. So, tũwara faiba, toi tũwarar anondo furafuri furon oibo.
JOH 16:25 "Zodi o ãi tũwarare in okkol mesalor duwara hoilam, kintu en ṭaim aiyer zẽtte ãi ar mesalor duwara hota no hoiyum, kintu kulasa gori Bafor babute hoiyum.
JOH 16:26 He din tũwara ãr name saiba, ar ãi tũwarare no hoir, ze ãi tũwaralla Bafor hãse foriyad goriyum.
JOH 16:27 Kiyollahoile Baf nize tũwarare ador gore, kiyollahoile tũwara ãre ador goror edde biššaš goijjo ze ãi Allar hentu aišši.
JOH 16:28 Ãi Bafor hentu ei duniyait aišši, ei duniyai ãi abar eri zairgoi edde Bafor heṛe zair."
JOH 16:29 Hetunot Isar sahabi okkole hodde, "So, õne ehon to kulasa gori hota hor, mesalor duwara no hor.
JOH 16:30 Ehon ãra buzi faijji ze õne beggun zano edde õnore honokiye suwal fusar gorok o dorhar nai. iyanot ãra biššaš goijji ze õne Allar hentu aiššo."
JOH 16:31 Isaye zuwabe hodde, "Henoile ki ehon biššaš goror?
JOH 16:32 En ṭaim aiyer, enki aigiyegoi, zẽtte tũwara šiṛašitta oi zaibagoi, ãre halikaga raki ze zar zar zagat hite zaibagoi, tarfore o ãi halikaga no, kiyollahoile Baf ãr fũwati ase.
JOH 16:33 "Ãi tũwarare in okkol hoilam zene tũwara ãr butore šanti fo. Ei duniyait tũwarattu mosibot takibo, kintu šahoš no haraiyo! Ãi duniyai loi zitti."
JOH 17:1 Isaye in okkol hoi bade, asmanor mikka hibar suk tuille, toi hodde: "Baf, šomoi aigiyegoi; tũwar Futore mohimawala goro, zene tũwar Fute tũware mohimawala gori fare.
JOH 17:2 Kiyollahoile tũi hibare hár manuš okkolor uwore kemota diyo, zene tũi zarare hibare diyo, hitara beggunore hibaye akeri zibon di fare.
JOH 17:3 Ar iyan oilde akeri zibon: zene hitara tũware, ek matro soiyi Allare, edde hiba zare tũi defeṛaiyo, he Isa Mosire, zane.
JOH 17:4 Tũi ãre ze ham goitto diyo hin ãi šeš goriyore ei duniyait tũware mohimawala goijji.
JOH 17:5 Ar ehon oh Baf, duniyair age tũwar loi ãr ze mohima aššil, tũi he mohima loi ãre tũwar sarme mohimawala goro.
JOH 17:6 "Duniyaittu zarare tũi ãrare diyo, ãi hitarar hãse tũwar nam forhaš goijji. Hitara tũwar aššil; tũi hitarare ãre diyo, ar hitara tũwar kalam falon goijje.
JOH 17:7 Hitara ehon zani faijje, ze tũi ãre zin diyo, hin tũwar hãsottu.
JOH 17:8 Kiyollahoile tũi ãre ze kalam okkol diyo, hin ãi hitarare diyi, ar hitara hinore goisse, ar soiyi gori zani faijje, ze ãi tũwar hãsottu aišši, ar hitara biššaš goijje ze, tũi ãre defeṛaiyo.
JOH 17:9 Ãi hitaralla foriyad gorir; Ãi duniyailla foriyad no gori, kintu hitaralla gori, zarare tũi ãre diyo; kiyollahoile hitara tũwar.
JOH 17:10 Ãr beggun tũwar, ar tũwattu beggun ãr; ar ãi hitarar duwara mohimawala oiyi.
JOH 17:11 Ãi ar ei duniyait no takiyum, kintu hitara ei duniyait ase, edde ãi tũwar hãse aiyir. Fobitro Baf, tũwar name hitarare hefazot goro, ze nam tũi ãre diyo, toi zene hitara ek oi fare, zendilla ãra ek.
JOH 17:12 Ãi hitarar fũwati taite, ãi hitarare tũwar name hefazotot raikki, ze nam tũi ãre diyo; ãi hitarare fahara di sõli raikki, hitarar butottu honokiye dongšo no o, dongšor fut bade, zene kitabor kalam furon o.
JOH 17:13 "Ar ehon ãi tũwar hãse aiyir, kintu in okkol ãi duniyait taite hoir, zene hitara ãr anondo hitara nizor butore furafuri bafe furon o.
JOH 17:14 Ãi hitarare tũwar kalam diyi, kintu duniyaiye hitarare hingša goijje, kiyollahoile hitara duniyair no, zendilla ãi duniyair no.
JOH 17:15 Ãr foriyad iyan no ze tũi hitarare duniyaittu loi zogoi, kintu tũi hitarare he horafottu rokka goro.
JOH 17:16 Hitara duniyair no, zendilla ãi duniyair no.
JOH 17:17 Hitarare soiyi loi fobitro goro; tũwar kalam soiyi.
JOH 17:18 Tũi zendilla ãre duniyait defeṛaiyo, hendilla ãi o hitarare duniyait defeṛaiyi.
JOH 17:19 Hitaralla ãi nizore fobitro goijji, zene hitarare o hitara nizore soyit fobitro oi fare.
JOH 17:20 "Ãi šude itaralla foriyad no gorir, kintu hitaralla o, zara itarar hotar duwara ãr uwore biššaš anibo,
JOH 17:21 zene hitara beggune ek o; Baf, zendilla tũi ãr butore, ar ãi tũwar butore, hitara o zene hendilla ãrar butore ek take; zene duniyaiye biššaš gore ze, tũi ãre defeṛaiyo.
JOH 17:22 Ar tũi ze mohima ãre diyo, hin ãi hitarare diyi, zene hitara o ãrar ḍoilla ek oi fare;
JOH 17:23 ãi hitarar butore, ar tũi ãr butore, toi zene hitara furafuri bafe ek o; zene duniyaiye zani fare ze, tũi ãre defeṛaiyo, edde tũi ãre zendilla ador goijjo, hendilla hitarare o ador goro.
JOH 17:24 "Baf, tũi ãre zarare diyo, ãi sai ze ãi zeṛe hitara o ãr fũwati taki fare, zene ze mohima tũi ãre diyo, hitara hiyan deki fare, kiyollahoile duniyai zuron dibar agottu tũi ãre ador goijjo.
JOH 17:25 "Niyaiwala Baf, duniyaiye zodi o tũware no zane, kintu ãi tũware zani, ar itara zainne ze tũi ãre defeṛaiyo.
JOH 17:26 Ar ãi itarare tũwar nam zanefan goijji edde zanefan goijjum, zene tũi ãre ze ador loi ador goijjo, he ador hitarar butore take, edde ãi hitarar butore taki."
JOH 18:1 In okkol hoi bade, Isaye hibar sahabi okkolore fũwati loi niyoliyore Kidron zúra farai giye; heṛe ugguwa bagan aššil, hibar butore hiba edde hibar sahabi okkol góille.
JOH 18:2 Ar Ehudah, ze hibare dorai dil, hitattu o he zagagan zana aššil, kiyollahoile Isaye bout bar hibar sahabi okkolore loi heṛe ekottro oito.
JOH 18:3 Hetolla Ehudaye ḍõr imam edde Foroši okkolor hentu ek šoinno dol edde hoekzon hitarar hormosari okkolore ainne, ar hitara uzal edde fanoš edde ostro loi heṛe aišše.
JOH 18:4 Isaye, hibar nizor uwore goṭedde hin okkol zaniyore, hibaye mummikka giye edde hitarare hodde, "Tũwara hare tuwor?"
JOH 18:5 Hitara hibare zuwabe hodde, "Nasarator Isare." Isaye hodde, "Ãi Oi." Ar Ehudah, ze hibare dorai der, hite o hitarar fũwati tiyat aššil.
JOH 18:6 Isaye zehon hitarare hoiye, "Ãi Oi" hetunot hitara fissa giye edde meṛit forigiyegoi.
JOH 18:7 Hibaye hitarare abar fusar goijje,"Tũwara hare tuwor?" Hitara hodde,"Nasarator Isare."
JOH 18:8 Isaye hodde, "Ãi to tũwarare hoilam ze, ãi oi. Tũwara zodi ãre tuwor, toile itarare zaito do."
JOH 18:9 Zene hibaye ze hoil hiyan furon o,"Tũi zarare ãre diyo, ãi hitarar ekzonore no harai."
JOH 18:10 Simon Fitor, zattu ekkan suri aššil, hibaye hiyan niyolaiye edde ek ḍõr imamor gulamore hamela gori hitar ḍen han haṛi felaiye. (Gulammuwar nam aššilde Malkos.)
JOH 18:11 Toi Isaye Fitorore hodde, "Tor suri ḍafor butore rak; ze fiyala Bafe ãre diye hiba ki ãi no fiyum ne?"
JOH 18:12 Hetunot he šoinno okkole edde hitarar komonḍar edde Ihudi neta okkolor hormosari okkole Isare gereftar goijje edde bainde,
JOH 18:13 edde foila Isare Annasor heṛe loigiye. Annas aššilde Kaifasor hour, ze he bosoror ḍõr imam aššil.
JOH 18:14 Ar ei Kaifas, ze Ihudi okkolore mošora dil, ekzon mora iyan mainšolla bala.
JOH 18:15 Simon Fitor edde ar ekzon sahabi Isar fise fise giye. He dusora sahabiwa ḍõr imamor sina aššil, edde Isar fũwati hite ḍõr imamor góror sarme uṛanot góille,
JOH 18:16 kintu Fitor bare dorozar hãse tiyai roiye. Toi ḍõr imamor sina dusora sahabiwaye bare giye edde doroza faharadar mayafuware hoiyore Fitorore butore loigiye.
JOH 18:17 He mayafuwawaye Fitorore hodde, "Tui o ki ei manušwar sahabi okkolor butottu ekzon?" Fitore hodde, "No, ãi no."
JOH 18:18 Hẽtte beši šit foijjil, hetolla gulam okkol edde faharadar okkole oinor ṭal zaillil edde tiyaiyore oin fuhail. Fitor o hitarar fũwati tiyaiyore oin fuhail.
JOH 18:19 He šomot ḍõr imame Isattu hibar sahabi okkolor babute edde hibar šikkar babute fusar goijje.
JOH 18:20 Kintu Isaye zuwabe hodde, "Ãi duniyair sarme kulasa gori hota howat asi. Ãi hamiša sinagog okkolot edde dórmogórot, zeṛe Ihudi okkol beggune ekottro o, heṛe šikka diyat asi. Ãi gufone kissu no hoi.
JOH 18:21 Ãre kiyolla fusar goror? Zara fuinne hitarare fusar goro, ãi hitarare ki hoiyi; so, ãi ki hoiyi hin hitara zane."
JOH 18:22 Isaye ei hota hodde ṭaimot, faharadar okkol butottu ekzon ze hibar ḍake tiyat aššil, hite hibare suwar mariyore hodde, "Endilla neki ḍõr imamore zuwab dodde?"
JOH 18:23 Isaye hitare hodde, "Zodi horaf kissu hoi taki, he horafir goba de, kintu zodi bala hoi taki, toile tui ãre kiyolla maror?"
JOH 18:24 Hetunot Annase banda abostat Isare ḍõr imam Kaifasor hãse defeṛaiye.
JOH 18:25 Simon Fitor tiyaiyore oin fuhadde šomot, hitara hibare hodde, "Tui o utar sahabi okkolor butottu ekzon no?" Hibaye ošikar goijje edde hodde, "No, ãi no."
JOH 18:26 Ḍõr imamor gulam okkolor ekzon, Fitore zar han haṛifelail, hitar ek egenaye hodde, "Ãi ki tore baganot hitar fũwati no deki ne?"
JOH 18:27 Fitore abar ošikar goijje, toi hetunot ugguwa rata kuraye bak diye.
JOH 18:28 Bade binna sore hitara Isare Kaifasor hentu Romiyo govarnaror mehelot loigiye. Ar hitara nafak no ofan, edde uddar idor hana hái farefan, hitara nize mehelor butore no gole.
JOH 18:29 Hetolla Filat baire hitarar ḍake aiyore hodde,"Ei manušwar berudde tũwara kiyor hošuri dodde?"
JOH 18:30 Hitara hodde, "Ite horaf ham no gorito boli ãra hitare õnor hãse no anitam."
JOH 18:31 Filate hitarare hodde, "Itare tũwara loizogoi edde tũwara nizor ain mozin bisar gorogoi." Henot hitara hodde, "Kintu honokiyore moron šaza dibar kemota to ãrar hatot nai."
JOH 18:32 Zene Isar kalam furon o, ziyan hoiyore hibaye dehai dil, hondilla moron hibaye moribo.
JOH 18:33 Toi Filat abar mehelot góille edde Isare ḍaki hodde, "Tui ki Ihudi okkolor badša?"
JOH 18:34 Isaye hodde, "Tũi ki nize ei hota hor, naki oinno kiye tũware ãr babute iyan hoiye?"
JOH 18:35 Filate zuwabe hodde, "Ãi ki Ihudi? Tor zati edde ḍõr imam okkole tore ãr hatot tuli diye. Tui ki goijjos?"
JOH 18:36 Isaye zuwabe hodde, "Ãr raijjo ei duniyair no; zodi ãr raijjo ei duniyair oito, toile ãre Ihudi neta okkolor hatot tuli diya no ofan, ãr mainše zuddo gorito, kintu ãr raijjo eṛe no."
JOH 18:37 Filate Isare hodde, "Toile ki tui badša?" Isaye hodde, "Tũi ṭik hoiyo ze, ãi badša. Soiyir foikka goba dibolla ãi zormo oiyi, ar hetolla ãi duniyait aišši. Fottikiye ze soiyir foikka hite ãr hota fune."
JOH 18:38 Filate hibare hodde, "Soiyi ki?" Ei hota hoi hite abar bare Ihudi neta okkolor hãse zaiyore hodde, "Ãi ei manušwar hono hosuri no fair.
JOH 18:39 Kintu tũwarar ekkan niyom ase ze, uddar idor ṭaimot ãi tũwarar ekzon hodire tũwaralla eridi. Tũwara ki so ze ãi Ihudi okkolor badšare eridi?"
JOH 18:40 Hitara beggune abar guzori hodde, "No, hitare no! Ãra Barabbasore sai." He Barabbas aššilde ekzon ḍahait.
JOH 19:1 Filate Isare loigiye edde beša beši souk maraiye.
JOH 19:2 Šoinno okkole keṛa lota diyore ekkan taz banaiye edde hibar matat buwai diye. Ar hitara hibare ugguwa baiyonna rongor zubba o findai diye.
JOH 19:3 Tarfore hitara hibar hãse zai zai hodde, "Oh Ihudi okkolor badšar hayat lamba ok!" Ar hitara hibare suwar maijje.
JOH 19:4 Filat abar mainšor dolor heṛe niyoli aišše edde Ihudi okkolore hodde, "So, ãi hitare tũwarar hãse niyolai anir zene tũwara buzi faro ze, ãi hitar hono hosuri no fair."
JOH 19:5 Isaye he keṛar taz edde baiyonna rongor hor finda abostat maze baire aišše. Hetunot Filate mainšore hodde, "Oto so ei manušwa!"
JOH 19:6 Kintu Isare dekiyore ḍõr imam edde faharadar okkole guzoriyore hodde, "Kurušot do, itare kurušot do!" Filate hodde, "Tũwara itare loizaiyore kurušot dogoi! Ãi hitar hono hosuri no fair."
JOH 19:7 Ihudi okkole hodde, "Ãrattu ek ain ase, he ain mozin hitattu mora foribo, kiyollahoile hite nizore Allar Fut hoiye."
JOH 19:8 Filate zehon ei hota fuinne hetunot hite aro ḍoraiye;
JOH 19:9 edde hite abar mehelor butore giye edde Isare hodde, "Tui honttu aiššos?" Kintu Isaye hitare hono zuwab no de.
JOH 19:10 Filate hodde, "Tui ki ãr loi hota no hoibi? Tui ki no zanos ze, tore eridibar edde kurušot dibar kemota ãttu asede?"
JOH 19:11 Isaye hodde, "Uwottu tũware kemota diya no oito buli ãr uwore tũwar hono kemota no takito; etolla hite ze ãre tũwar hatot tuli diye, hitar guna beši ḍõr."
JOH 19:12 Ei hota funi Filate Isare eridibolla kušiš goijje, kintu Ihudi okkole guzori hoiye, "Õne zodi itare erido, toile õne Kaisaror bondu no; ze honokiye nizore badša dabi gore hite to Kaisaror bifokke hota ho."
JOH 19:13 Filate ei hota zehon fuinne, hite Isare baire ainne edde ek šil bisaiya zagat bisaror siyarot boišše, (ze zagaganore Ibroni zubanot Gabbata howa oito).
JOH 19:14 He dinnan aššil uddar id entezamor din; hẽtte ṭaim oilde dũijja. Filate Ihudi okkolore hodde, "Ei so, tũwarar badša"
JOH 19:15 Henot hitara guzori hodde, "Dur goro! Dur goro! hitare kurušot do." Filate hitarare hodde, "Tũwarar badšare ki ãi kurušot diyum?" Ḍõr imam okkole zuwab diye, "Kaisar bade ãrattu ar hono badša nai."
JOH 19:16 Toi hite Isare hitarar hatot tuli diye, zene hibare kurušot diya o. Toi hitara hibare hentu loi giyegoi;
JOH 19:17 ar hiba nizor kuruš boi loizaiyore Matakuli name ek zagat giye (ziyanore Ibroni zubanot Golgotá ho.)
JOH 19:18 Heṛe hitara Isare kurušot diye, edde hibar fũwati aro duizonore diye, ekzonore ek ḍakottu ek ḍakottu, ar maze Isare.
JOH 19:19 Filate ekkan dušnama lekiyore Isar kurušor uwore lagai diye, ar leka aššil: "NASARATOR ISA, IHUDI OKKOLOR BADŠA."
JOH 19:20 Ihudi okkolor boute he dušnamagan foijje, kiyollahoile Isare kurušot diya oiyede zagagan aššilde šohoror ḍake, ar hiyan leka aššil Ibroni, Romiyo edde Girik bašat.
JOH 19:21 Ihudi okkolor ḍõr imam okkole Filatore hodde, "'Ihudi okkolor badša no leikko,' kintu leko ze, ite hoito, 'ãi Ihudi okkolor badša.'"
JOH 19:22 Filate hodde, "Ãi ziyan lekki, hiyan ãi lekki."
JOH 19:23 Šoinno okkole Isare kurušot di bade, hitara hibar horgunore sair bag goriyore ekzone ek bag gori loiye, ar zubba o loiye; kintu hiba silaiya nu aššil, uwottu nise foijjonto banaiya.
JOH 19:24 Toi hitara ekzonore ekzone hodde, "Iyan no faṛiyum, bolke iyanolla loṭari mari, sai iba har o." Zene ei kalam furon oi fare, "Hitara ãr horgunore hitarar maze bag goijje, ar ãr zubbawalla loṭari maijje" Ar hendilla in okkol ei šoinno okkole goijje.
JOH 19:25 Ar Isar kurušor ḍake hibar ma, hibar mar boin, Klofasor bou Moriyam, edde Mogdaleni Moriyam, itara tiyat aššil.
JOH 19:26 Isaye, mare edde sahabi zare hibaye ador gorito, hitara tiyai taikkede dekiyore, hibaye mare hodde, "Mayafuwa, sa, iba tor fut."
JOH 19:27 Tarfore he sahabire hodde, "Sa, iba tor ma." He oite, he sahabiye hibare hitar nizor górot loigiyegoi.
JOH 19:28 Tarfore, Isaye buzi farer ze beggun šeš oiye, kitabor kalam zene furon o, hibaye hodde,"Ãi tiraši oiyi."
JOH 19:29 Heṛe horor roš furaiya ugguwa dešši aššil, toi hitara ekkan hanire he horor rošot bizaiye edde esup gasor ḍeila loi hin Isar mukor hãse doijje.
JOH 19:30 Isaye he horor roš haiyore hodde,"Šeš oiye." Tarfore hibaye mata niso gori hibar šeš niyaš felaiye.
JOH 19:31 He dinnan aššilde entezamor din, ar Šabbator din zene lašgun kurušor uwore no take, kiyollahoile he Šabbat aššilde ek moha din, etolla Ihudi okkole Filatore foriyad goijje zene hitarar ṭenggun bangi diyore hitarare kurušottu lamaifela o.
JOH 19:32 Toi šoinno okkol aiyore foila ekzonore, edde hibar fũwati kurušot diya oiyede dusora ekzonore, ṭenggun bangi diye.
JOH 19:33 Kintu hitara zẽtte Isar hãse aiyore dekilo ze, hiba mori giyegoi, toi hibar ṭeng no bange.
JOH 19:34 Kintu soinno okkolor ekzone hibar ḍak sai sel loiyore hana goijje; henot toratori lou edde fani niyoli aišše.
JOH 19:35 Ze nizor suke deikke, hite goba diye, ar hitar goba soiyi. Ar hite zane ze hite soiyi hor, zene tũwara o biššaš goro.
JOH 19:36 Haron in okkol goiṭṭe, zene kitabor ei kalam furon o, "Hibar ekkan ãḍḍi o banga no oibo."
JOH 19:37 Abar kitabor ar ek kalam endilla hor, "Hitara zare hana goijje hibare hitara saibo."
JOH 19:38 Ar in okkol bade, Arimatiyar Yusuf, ze aššil Isar sahabi, kintu Ihudi okkolor ḍore gufone aššil, hibaye Filatore foriyad goijje, zene hibaye Isar gagan loizai fare; Filate loizaibolla ezajot diye. Toi hibaye aiyore hibar gagan loigiyegoi.
JOH 19:39 Ar Nikoḍomas, hiba ze foilabar raitta Isar hãse aiššil, hibaye o heṛe aššil, myrrah edde aloi miyaiya onumanik ek šot fond mosolla loiyore.
JOH 19:40 Hitara Isar ga loizaiyore Ihudi okkolore dohon gorade niyom mozin he kušbo mosolla kafon horot diyore berai diye.
JOH 19:41 Isare zeṛe kurušot diya oiye, heṛe ek bagan aššil, ar he baganot ugguwa noya hobor aššil, zibat honokiyore ehono raka no o.
JOH 19:42 He din aššilde Ihudi okkolor entezamor din, hitara Isare he hoborot raikke, kiyollahoile he hoborguwa ḍake aššil.
JOH 20:1 Haftar foila din binna sore, andar taite Mogdaleni Moriyame hoboror hãse giye, ar hibaye dekedde hoboror mukottu fattorgan algaifela oiye.
JOH 20:2 Hibaye dũri Simon Fitoror hãse edde dusora sahabi zare Isaye ador gorito hibar hãse aišše, ar hitarare hodde, "Hitara Malikore hoborottu loigiyegoi; ar hitara hibare hoṛe raikke ãra no zani."
JOH 20:3 Toi Fitor edde he dusora sahabiwa hetunot niyoli giye edde hoboror mikka zat aššil.

JOH 20:6 Simon Fitor o hibar fise fise aišše, edde hoboror butore giye edde dekedde kafonor horgun heṛe fori roiye,
