JOH 20:11 Toi Moriyam hoboror baire tiyai handat roiye, hibaye handat maze niyuriyore hoboror butore saiye,
JOH 20:12 ar dekedde, dola hor finda duizon firista Isar ga ze zagat neṛai diya oil, ekzon hibar matar hentu, ar ekzon ṭengor hentu, boi taikke.
JOH 20:13 Hitara hibare hodde, "He mayafuwa, handor kiyolla?" Hibaye hitarare hodde, "Hitara ãr Malikore loigiyegoi, edde hibare hoṛe raikke ãi no zani."
JOH 20:14 In okkol hoiyore hiba fissa firi sadde Isa tiyai roiye, kintu hiba Isade hiyan hibaye buzi no fare.
JOH 20:15 Isaye hibare hodde, "He mayafuwa, handor kiyolla? Hare tuwor?" Isare baganor mali boli ṭariyore, hibaye hodde, "So, õne zodi hibare loi giyogoide o, toile ãre ho hoṛe raikko, ãi hibare loi ainnumboi."
JOH 20:16 Isaye hibare hodde, "Moriyam." Henot Moriyame hibar mikka firiyore Ibroni zubanot Isare hodde, "Rabbuni" zar mani "ustad."
JOH 20:17 Isaye Moriyamore hodde, "Ãre no suis, kiyollahoile ãi ehono uwore Bafor hãse no zai. Tui bolke ãr báiyaindor hãse zaiyore hogoi, ze ãr edde tũwarar Baf, ze ãr edde tũwarar Allah, ãi uwore hibar hãse zair."
JOH 20:18 Toi Mogdaleni Moriyam hentu giyegoi edde sahabi okkolore hodde, "Ãi Malikore dekki!" Ar Isaye hibare ki hoil hin okkol o hibaye hitarare hoiye.
JOH 20:19 He ekkui dinor hazinna, haftar foila din, Ihudi okkolor ḍore, sahabi okkol ziyot dola oiya aššil he góror doroza okkol bon gori dil. Isa nize ai hitarar maze tiyaiyore hodde, "Tũwarar šanti ok."
JOH 20:20 Ei hota hoi bade hibaye hitarare hat edde ḍak dehaiye. Sahabi okkole Malikore dekiyore beši kuši oiye.
JOH 20:21 Toi Isaye abar hodde, "Tũwarar šanti ok; zendilla ãre he Bafe defeṛaiye, ãi o tũwarare defeṛair."
JOH 20:22 Ei hota hoiyore hibaye hitarar uwore fu diye edde hodde, "Pak Ruhure goso.
JOH 20:23 Tũwara zodi honokiyor guna maf gori do, toile hitarar guna maf oibo, ar zodi honokiyor guna maf gori no do, toile hitarar guna maf gora no oibo."
JOH 20:24 Isa zẽtte aššil, hẽtte Ṭomas, he barozonor ekzon, (zare Didymus ḍaka oito,) hiba oinno sahabi okkolor fũwati nu aiššil.
JOH 20:25 Toi oinno sahabi okkole hibare hodde, "Ãra Malikore dekki." Kintu hibaye hitarare hodde, "Ãi zodi hibar dui hatot ferakor sinno no deki, edde he ferakor sinnot ãr õl diyore, edde hibar ḍakot ãr hat diyore ãi sai no fari, toile hono mote ãi biššaš no goriyum."
JOH 20:26 Ar ašṭo din bade, hibar sahabi okkole abar he górot dola oiye, edde Ṭomas o hitarar fũwati aššil, ar hẽtte dorozagun banda taki bade o Isa aišše, edde hiba hitarar maze tiyaiye, ar hodde, "Tũwarar šanti ok."
JOH 20:27 Tarfore hibaye Ṭomasore hodde, "Tor õl eṛe an, ar ãr dui hat sa. Ar tor hat barai de, edde ãr ḍakot rak. Obiššaši no ois, kintu biššaši o."
JOH 20:28 Hetunot Ṭomase zuwab diye edde hibare hodde, "Ãr Malik, ãr Allah."
JOH 20:29 Isaye hibare hodde, "Ṭomas, tui ki ãre deikkos boli biššaš ainnos? Mubarok hitara, zara no dekiyore biššaš gore."

JOH 21:1 In okkol bade, Isaye Ṭaiberia doriyar farot abar nizore sahabi okkolore deha diye. Ar hibaye nizore endilla gori forhaš goijje.

JOH 21:24 Iba oilde he sahabi ze in beggunor babute goba der, edde in okkol hibaye leikke; ar ãra zani ze, hibar goba soiyi.
JOH 21:25 Isaye aro bout kissu goijjil; hin okkol zodi ek ekkan gori leka oito, toile edun kitab ze oito, ãi mone gorir he kitab okkol hin duniyait nu ãṛito.
ACT 1:1 Adoijja Teofilos, ãr foila siyarat ãi beggun hin okkolor babute leikki, zin Isaye goijje edde šikka diye, hibaye šuru goijjede hiya loti
ACT 1:2 hedin foijjonto zẽtte hibare behostot tuli loiza oiye. Hẽtte hibaye hibar basai goijja asab okkolore Pak Ruhur duwara hokum dil.
ACT 1:3 Hibaye toziya bordaš gori bade ei manuš okkolore deha diye edde hiba ze zinda ase hiyanor beša besi biššaš lagede saf forman okkol diye. Sališ din dori hitarare deha diye edde Allar raijjor babute bout hota okkol hoiye.
ACT 1:4 Ek bar hibaye hitarar fũwati hána háil, hen šomot hitarare endilla hokum diye: "Tũwara Zeruzalem sari no zaiyogoi, kintu Bafor wada gora ze hadiyar hota tũwara ãttu fuinno hiyanolla entezar goijjo.
ACT 1:5 Kiyollahoile Yahyaye fani loi torikotor gusol diye, kintu ho ek dinor butore tũwara he Pak Ruhur torikotor gusol faiba."
ACT 1:6 Sahabi okkole ekku fũwati dola oiyore Isare fusar goredde: "Malik, õne ki ei šomot Israili okkolor hatot raijjo firai diba?"
ACT 1:7 Isaye zuwabe hodde: "Ze din otóba ṭaim zin Bafe nizor odiharor butore raikke, hin tũwarare zanito diya no o.
ACT 1:8 Kintu he Pak Ruh tũwarar uwore aile tũwara šokti faiba. Ar Zeruzalem, Ehudiya beggulla, Sameriya edde duniyair šeš mata foijjonto tũwara ãr goba oiba."
ACT 1:9 Ei hota hoi bade, Isare tuli loi za odde hitara sai taikke. Ar ekkan miyulaye hibare hitarar sukor arguwale gori felaiye.
ACT 1:10 Hitara asmanor mikka ek diyane sai roiye hen šomot, dóla hoor finda duizon manuš hitarar hãse ai tiyaiyegai.
ACT 1:11 Ar hitarare hodde: "Oh Galilor manuš okkol! Tuwara eṛe tiyai asmanor uzu kiyolla sai roiyo? Ei Isa zare tũwarar hãsottu behostot tuli loi za oiyede deikko, ode ode hendilla gori hiba abar uwafes firi aibo."
ACT 1:12 Tarfore Sahabi okkol Zaitun faharottu uwafes Zeruzalem firi giyegoi. He faharguwa Zeruzalemottu onumanik ada mailor fõt.
ACT 1:13 Šohoror butore hitara zeṛe takito, he góror uworor ṭalat giye. Hitara aššilde Fitor, Yahya, Yakub, Andreas, Filip, Ṭomas, Bartolomeus, Moti, Alfeyusor fuwa Yakub, Bahadur Simon Zelot, edde Yakubor fuwa Ehudah.
ACT 1:14 Itara hoekzon mayafuwain edde Isar ma Moriyam ar Isar báiyain okkolor fũwati hamiša beggune ekmone duwa gorat roiye.
ACT 1:15 Hẽtte ek bar onumanik ekšo kuri zon torikotor bái bondu okkolor maze tiyai,
ACT 1:16 Fitore hodde: "Oh ãr báiboinain okkol, Ehudar babute Pak Ruhuye nobi Daudor muke zendilla hoil, Pak kalamor he hota hameka furon owa foijje. Isare zara doijje hitarare ei Ehudaye fõt dehaiye.
ACT 1:17 Hite ãrar butoror ekzon aššil edde ei ekkui šeba hamor bag fail."
ACT 1:18 (Hite kuham gori ze beton faiye hin loi ekkan zobin kinne. Kintu hite mata hemmika abostat meṛit foijje, hitar feṭ faṛi ãti zula niyoli giyegoi.
ACT 1:19 Zeruzalemor hár mainše ei hota zani faijjil. Hetolla hitarar zubanot he zobinganore Hokkoldama mani Louwor Zobin name foriso.)
ACT 1:20 "Kiyollahoile Zobur Šorifot leka ase: "'Hitar bošot bari hali takok, heṛe honokiye bošoti no gorok,' Edde, "'Hitar hamor bar oinno honokiye lok.'
ACT 1:21 Malik Isa ãrar fũwati solafira goijjilde hiya ãrar fũwati hamiša hozon manuš aššil,
ACT 1:22 Ebbe šuruttu loti, zẽtte Isaye Yahyattu torikotor gusol loil hiya loti šuru gori hibare ãrar hãsottu behostot tuli loiza oiye foijjonto. Ehon, ei manuš okkolor butottu ekzon ãrar fũwati Isar uwafes zindar babute goba doya owa foribo."
ACT 1:23 Toi hitara dui zonore tiya goraiye, Yusuf zare Barsabbas ba Yustus hoi ḍakito edde Motottiyas.
ACT 1:24 Tarfore hitara duwa goijje: "Oh, Malik, tũi har zonor dilore zano. Ãrare dehai do ei dui zonor butottu zare basona goijjo,
ACT 1:25 šeba edde asabor tokka loibolla, ziyan Ehudaye eri di ze ze laikka heṛe giyegoi."
ACT 1:26 Tarfore hitara loṭari maijje edde Motottiyasor name loṭari uiṭṭe. Henot hite o he egarozon asabor fũwati zug diye.
ACT 2:1 Fõnzaš dinna idor din sahabi okkol beggune ek zagat dola oiye.
ACT 2:2 Hetunot atikka asmanottu bári boyaror abazor ḍoilla ek abaz aišše edde ze górot hitara boiššil hiyanor hár mikka he abaze furaigiyegoi.
ACT 2:3 Toi hitara dekedde, hinore saite oinor zil okkolor ḍoil, zin šiṛiyore hitara fottizonor uwore boišše.
ACT 2:4 Henot hitara beggune Pak Ruhuye furaiya oiye edde Ruhuye zare zendilla hota hoibar šokti diye he mozin hitara oinno oinno zuban okkolot hota howa šuru goijje.
ACT 2:5 Hẽtte Allar ḍorwala Ihudi okkol duniyair har zatittu ai Zeruzalemot bošobaš goijjil.
ACT 2:6 Ar hitara ei abaz funiyore ek dol manuš zoma oiye edde hitara beggune giyan hara oigiyoi, kiyollahoile hitara fotti ekzonor nizor zubanot hota howa odde fuinne.
ACT 2:7 Hitara kub beši ammuwak edde tajjuf oiyore fusar goredde: "So, hota hodde itara beggun ki Galilor manuš no neki?
ACT 2:8 To ãra kene fottikiyor nizor nizor madinna zuban hodde funir?
ACT 2:9 Fartiyo, Madiyo edde Elamiyo, edde Mesofotamiyar bašinda okkol, Ehudiya edde Kafnadkiya, Pontus edde Ešia,
ACT 2:10 Forugiya edde Famfuliya, Mišor edde Leviya deš šoho Kuronir ate hãsor elehar bašinda okkol edde boidešitta Romiyo,
ACT 2:11 Ihudi edde Ihudi dórmo manoya manuš okkol edde Kreṭiyo edde Arabiyo manuš okkol ze ãra, ãra ze zar zar zubanot hitara Allar ḍõr ḍõr hamor hota hodde funir!"
ACT 2:12 Endilla gori hitara beggune tajjuf oiye. Ar hitara suhara oiyore ekzonore ekzone fusar gora šuru goijje, "Iyanor mani ki?"
ACT 2:13 Abar hodune hitarare loi ṭaṭṭa urar edde hodde, "Hitara taza šoraf beši fifelaiyore fool oiyede."
ACT 2:14 Kintu Fitore he egarozon sahabir fũwati tiyaiyore he manušor dolore guzori hodde: "Oh Ihudi manuš okkol edde Zeruzalemor bašinda okkol! Tũwara beggune ei hota zani rako edde ãr hota funo!
ACT 2:15 Tũwara ziyan mone goror hiyan no, itara šoraf hái fool oiyede no, kiyollahoile aizo binna nowa baijjede!
ACT 2:16 Kintu iyan oilde he goṭona ze hota Zuel nobir duwara howa oiye:
ACT 2:17 "'Šeš hale endilla oibo, Allaye hor, har mainšor uwore ãi ãr Ruhure ḍali diyum. Tũwarar futziyainde nobi hisabe agam hota hoibo, He zuwan okkole deha faibo, ar he burá okkole šoppon dekibo.
ACT 2:18 En ki, ãr gulam edde bandi okkolor uwore, he din okkolot ãi ãr Ruh ḍali diyum, ar hitara nobi hisabe agam hota hoibo.
ACT 2:19 Ãi uwore asmanot nanan keramotor alamot ar nise duniyait nanan ḍoilla sinno, lou, oin ar dũwa dehaiyum.
ACT 2:20 Malikor he moha mohimar din aibar age, beil andar oi zaiboi, san louwor ḍoilla oi zaiboi,
ACT 2:21 Ar ze honokiye Malikor nam ḍake, hite uddar faibo.'
ACT 2:22 "Oh Israili manuš okkol, ei hotagun funo: Nasarator Isaye kuduruti ham, keramot, ar sinno okkolor duwara tũwarar hãse hiba ekzon Allar torfottu formanwala manuš. Isar duwara Allaye tũwarar maze ei ham okkol goijje, zin tũwara nize nize zano.
ACT 2:23 Allah, ze age loti zane edde faisala gori rakkil, he mozin hibare tũwarar hatot šebi diya oiye. Ar tũwara hibare bedormiyo okkolor hatot tuli di kurušot di mari felaiyo.
ACT 2:24 Kintu Allaye hibare moron zontronar hatottu uddar gori tuli loi giyegoi, kiyollahoile hibare moute dori rakibolla šaiddo no aššil.
ACT 2:25 Badša Daude hibar babute hor: "'Ãi Malikore hamiša ãr sarme deki, kiyollahoile hiba ãr ḍen ḍakottu ase, zene ãi bifodot no fori.
ACT 2:26 Hetolla ãr dil kuši o, edde ãr zile kušir hota ho, ar ãr gagan o aša loi basibo.
ACT 2:27 Kiyollahoile tũi ãr foranore fatalfurot raki no zaibagoi, No diba tũi, tũwar Paki zonor gare fõsito.
ACT 2:28 Tũi ãre sinaiyo, zibon fõtore, tũwar hazirir duwara ãre kušiye furon gore.'
ACT 2:29 "Báiyain okkol, he raz bongšor baf Daudor babute ãi tũwarare kula zubane hoi fariyum, ze hiba morigiyegoi edde hibare dohon gora oiye, ar hibar hobor aizo foijjonto ãrar hãse ase.
ACT 2:30 Bala, hiba ekzon nobi aššil ar hibaye zanito ze Allaye hosom hái son goijje, Daudor ekzon bongšodorore hibar šingašonot buwaibo.
ACT 2:31 Hetolla Daude agottu loti dekkil buli Isa Mosir uwafes zinda uṛar babute hoiye ze hibare fatalfurot feli raka no o, hibar ga o no fõse.
ACT 2:32 Ehon! Ei Isare Allaye morattu uwafes tuille, ar ãra beggun iyanor goba.
ACT 2:33 Allar ḍen ḍakottu boibar ijjot hibare diya oiye edde hibaye wada gora Pak Ruhure hibar Bafottu faiye, ar ehon tũwara zin dekor edde funor hin oilde he Pak Ruh zin Isaye ḍali diye.
ACT 2:34 Daud hono behostot no za, kintu hibaye nize ei hota hoiye, "'Mabude ãr malikore hodde: "Tui ãr ḍen ḍakottu boi,
ACT 2:35 zetodin ãi tor dušmon okkolore tor fottole no raki."'
ACT 2:36 "Etolla Israilor hár mainše haṭi gori zanok: Zare tũwara kurušot marifelaila, Allaye he Isare Malik edde Mosi duni ḍoilla goijje."
ACT 2:37 Ei hota funone hitarar dilot tir góillefan oiye. Ar hitara Fitorore edde oinno asab okkolore hodde, "Báiyain okkol, ãrattu ki gora foribo?"
ACT 2:38 Fitore zuwabe hodde, "Tũwara fotti ekzone gunattu mon firao edde Isa Mosir name torikotor gusol lo, toi tũwara guna maf faiba, ar hadiya hisabe tũwara Pak Ruhure faiba.
ACT 2:39 Kiyollahoile tũwaralla edde tũwarar futziyain okkololla edde zara dure ase hitara beggunolla, zar mani zedun manušore ãrar Allah Malike ḍaki anibo hitara beggunolla ei wada gora oiye."
ACT 2:40 Hin bade o aro bout hota hoi Fitore goba diye, edde hitarare endilla nosiyot goijje: "Ei zobanar naforman, horaf manuš okkolottu tũwara nizore dure raikko."
ACT 2:41 Henot hitara zara Fitoror hota mani loiye, hitara torikotor gusol loiye edde henot hedin hom beši tin hazar manušore Allaye hitarar ekku fũwati zug goijje.
ACT 2:42 Ar hitara sahabi okkolor šikka lowat, edde hitarar fũwati šongo diyat, ruṭi bangat edde munazat gorat fori taito.
ACT 2:43 Toi beggunor dilot Allar ḍor góille, kiyollahoile sahabi okkole bout tajjuiffa alamot edde sinnor ham okkol goitto.
ACT 2:44 Ar biššaši okkol beggune ekku fũwati takito edde hár kissu ek taillatt rakito.
ACT 2:45 Ar hitarar zaga zobin edde šombotti za kissu aššil hin besi zar zendilla zorulot oito he mozin beggunore baṛi diya oito.
ACT 2:46 Hitara fotti din dórmogóror uṛanot ekku fũwati dola oito, ar gór okkolot hitara hãši kušiye edde šorol mone há fiya gorito.
ACT 2:47 Hitara Allar tarif gorat taito edde hár mainše hitarare ijjot goitto. Ar zara din din uddar faito, Malike hitarare o ani itarar dolot zug gorito.
ACT 3:1 Ekdin dinor tinnwa baze munazator ṭaimot Fitor edde Yuhanna dórmogórot gil.
ACT 3:2 Heṛe mar feṛottu loti ãtur ekzon manušore hodun manuše bar gori ani dórmogóror šundor name dorozar hãse fotti din buwai dito, zene zara dórmogórot gole hitarattu hite horat sai fare.
ACT 3:3 Fitor edde Yuhanna dórmogórot goledde dekiyore he manušwaye hitarattu horat saiye.
ACT 3:4 Henot Fitore edde Yuhannaye šuza hitar mikka saiye. Bade Fitore hodde: "Ãrar mikka sa!"
ACT 3:5 Toi manušwaye hitarar hãsottu kissu faibar aša loi hitarar mikka sai roiye.
ACT 3:6 Toi Fitore hodde, "Rufa ba šuna ãttu nai, kintu za ase hin tore diyum: Nasarator Isa Mosir name uṛi tiya edde aṭ."
ACT 3:7 Bade Fitore hitar ḍen hat sai dori hitare tuille, henot hehon hitar ṭeng edde formuri sokto oiye.
ACT 3:8 Hite faldi uṛi ṭengor fatar uwore tiyaiye edde aṛa šuru goijje. Toi hite faldi faldi ãṛat maze Allare šukuriya guzar gori gori hitarar fũwati dórmogóror uṛanot giye.
ACT 3:9 Har mainše zehon hite aṛi faredde edde Allar tarif goredde deikke,
ACT 3:10 hẽtte hitara hitare sini faijje ze hite he manuš, ze dórmogóror šundor name dorozat boi horat magito. Ar hitar uwore ze hanḍo goiṭṭe hin deki hitara beša beši tajjuf edde ammuwak oiye.
ACT 3:11 He horat magoyawaye kintu Fitor edde Yuhannar fisa no sare. Fitoror he hamot hár manuš okkol tajjuf oiyore Soloimanor haissarar tole hitarare giri doijje.
ACT 3:12 Hetunot Fitore hodde: "Israili okkol! Tũwara iyanot tajjuf kiyolla or? Ãrar nizor šoktiye otóba Allare ḍorai de he gunor zoriya itare ãṛi faribolla šokti diyi mone gori kiyolla tũwara ãrar uzu sai taikko?
ACT 3:13 No, Ibrahim edde Isak edde Yakubor Allah, ãrar baf dadar Allaye ei hamor duwara hibar nizor gulam Isar mohima forhaš goijje. Tũwara to Isare mari felaibolla dori dila. Filate hibare eri dito sail, kintu tũwara Filator muntu hibare ošikar goijjo.
ACT 3:14 Tũwara he Fobitro edde Niyaiwalare ošikar gori ekzon kuni manušore tũwaralla eri dito hoiyo.
ACT 3:15 Ze zibon doya hibare tũwara mari felaila, kintu Allaye hibare zinda gori tuille, hiyanor goba ãra.
ACT 3:16 Ei manuš iba zare tũwara dekor edde zare tũwara sino, hite Isar namor gune he šokti hamaiye. Isar butottu di ze biššaš ãra fai hiyane ei manušware furafuri bafe aram goijje, zendilla tũwara beggune dekor.
ACT 3:17 "Ehon báiyain okkol, ãi zani tũwara tũwarar neta okkolor ḍoil no buziyore Isare kurušor uwore mari felaiyo.
ACT 3:18 Kintu Allaye hibar Mosiye ze duk šoibo he hota ei bafe furon goijje, ziyan hibaye bout age har nobi okkolor duwara howabail.
ACT 3:19 Hetolla, tũwara mon firo, toi tũwarar guna fũsi fela oibo.
ACT 3:20 Ar he Mosi zare tũwaralla basona gora oiye mani Isa, hibare defeṛaiyore tũwarare tottaza gori tuli fare.
ACT 3:21 Allaye hár kissure abar agor ḍoilla uwafes firai anibode hibar he ṭaim nuwaiye foijjonto hibattu behostot taka foribo, zendilla hibaye bout age hibar nobi okkolor muke hoil.
ACT 3:22 Musaye to hoiye, 'Mabud Allaye tũwaralla ãr ḍoilla ekzon nobi tũwarar nizor zatir butottu tulibo. Har kissu zin tũwarare hibaye ho hin beggun funa foribo.
ACT 3:23 Ze hibar hota no funibo hitare hibar mainšor butottu furafuri bafe fũsi fela oibo.'
ACT 3:24 "Hin bade o, nobi Samuelottu loti šuru gori har nobi okkol zara kalam hoi giye hitara o ei din okkolot zin goṭer hinor babute hoi giye.
ACT 3:25 Ar tũwara to he nobi okkolor bongšor manuš edde he wadar suktir šiyardar, ziyan Allaye tũwarar bafdada okkol loi goijjil, hẽtte Allaye Ibrahimore hoil, 'Tor bongšor butottu di duniyair har zatiye rahamot faibo.'
ACT 3:26 Allaye hibar gulam Isare tũwarar sarme tiya goraiye foila, hibare defeṛaiye, ze kufõtottu firi aiye hitare rahamot goribolla."
ACT 4:1 Hitara ehono mainšor loi hota howat ase, hen šomot imam okkol edde dórmogór sõloya okkolor boro edde Sadduki okkol aišše.
ACT 4:2 Fitor edde Yuhannaye manuš okkolore šikka dedde edde Isar duwara mora okkol abar uwafes uṛar babute tobolig goredde deki hitara beši gušša oiye.
ACT 4:3 Hitara Fitor edde Yuhannare doijje. He din hãzinna oi giyegoi buli tarforor din foijjonto hitarare ziyolot bon gori raikke.
ACT 4:4 Kintu hitara zara Fitoror boyan fuinne hitara boute biššaš ainne, henot biššaši furuš manuš okkolor dol barizaiyore hom beši fãs hazar oiye.
ACT 4:5 Ihudi okkolor neta okkol, murubbi okkol, edde alem okkol ekku fũwati Zeruzalem dola oiye.
ACT 4:6 He ḍõr imam Annas o heṛe hazir aššil, ar Kaifas, Yuhanna edde Alekzendar, edde he ḍõr imamor góror oinno manuš okkol o heṛe aššil.
ACT 4:7 Hitara Fitor edde Yuhannare hitarar sarmottu tiya goraiyore fusar goijje: "Tũwara kiyor šokti loi otóba har nam loi ei ham goijjo?"
ACT 4:8 Hetunot Fitore Pak Ruhuye furaiya oiyore hitarare hodde: "Ãrar neta okkol, murubbi okkol!
ACT 4:9 Ekzon ãtur manušore balai goijji buli zehon aijja ãrare zera gora or edde ei manušwa kengori bala oiye, he babute fusar gora or.
ACT 4:10 Henoile tũwara beggune edde har Israil zatiye, ei hota zani rako: Iyan Nasarator Isa Mosi loi, zare tũwara kurušor uwore mari felaila edde zare Allaye mora okkolor butottu tuille, hibar šokti loi ei manušwa furafuri bafe aram oiyore õnorar sarme tiyai roiye.
ACT 4:11 Hiba oilde "'he fattor, zibare tũwara raz mistiri okkole bad diyo, kintu hiba i har beggunottuwaro dorhari fattor oiye.'
ACT 4:12 Uddar ar honokiyor hãse fa no za, kiyollahoile asmanor nise manušor butore en ar hono nam diya no o, ze namor zoriya ãra uddar oi fari."
ACT 4:13 Hitara Fitor edde Yuhannar himmot deikke, ar itara ze anfora edde awam manuš hiyan dekiyore hitara tajjuf oiye, ar itara ze Isar fũwati aššil hiyan buzi faijje.
ACT 4:14 Aram oiyede manušwa, Fitor edde Yuhannar fũwati tiyat ase, dekiyore hitara itarar berudde hoibar ar kissu no aššil.
ACT 4:15 Etolla hitarare bisar šobattu bare zaibolla hokum diye edde hitara ekku fũwati biyasanat boišše.
ACT 4:16 Hitara hodde: "Ãra ei manuš okkolore loi ken goriyum? Zeruzalemot asede har kiye zane ze itara ekkan ḍõr keramoti ham goijje, ar hiyan ãra ošikar gori no fariyum.
ACT 4:17 Kintu iyan aro mainšor hãse sorai zai no farefan ei manuš okkolore domki diya foribo, toi zene itara ar honokiyore ei namor babute hono hota no ho."
ACT 4:18 Tarfore hitara Fitor edde Yuhannare abar butore ḍaki aniyore hokum diye, zene hitara Isar name hono hota no ho otóba šikka ebbere no de.
ACT 4:19 Fitor edde Yuhannaye zuwabe hodde: "Tũwarar hokum falon goijjum ne naki Allar hokum falon goijjum? Allar nozorot honnan ṭik, tũwara hiyan bisar gori so!
ACT 4:20 Kiyollahoile ãra zin dekki edde fuinni hinor babute no hoi tai no faijjum."
ACT 4:21 Toi hitarare aro sokto gori domki diyore eri diye. Kiyollahoile hitara itarare šaza dibolla hono ufai tuwai no fa, haron zin goṭṭil hinolla hár manuš okkole Allare tarif goijjil.
ACT 4:22 Ze manušware keramotir duwara aram gora oiye hitar umor sališ bosorottuwaro beši.
ACT 4:23 Hitara hentu sara fai bade, hitarar nizor manuš okkolor hãse giye, ar ḍõr imam edde murubbi okkole zin zin hoil har kissu hitarare zanaiye.
ACT 4:24 Ei hota funiyore hitara beggune mili ek diyane Allar mutallek munazat gori hodde: "Oh Malik, tũi asman zobin, doriya, hinor butore ze kissu ase beggun sirišti goijjo.
ACT 4:25 Tũi Pak Ruhur duwara tũwar gulam ãrar fordada Daudor muk diyore howaila: "'Har zatir manuš okkole kiyolla suhara oi sesamesi gorer? Kiyolla manuš okkole hannak misa misi Allar berudde zar?
ACT 4:26 Duniyair badša okkole Mabud edde hibar Mosir berudde tiyaiye, ar šašon goroya okkole ekkui fũwati oiye.'
ACT 4:27 Hendilla ode ode oiye, tũwar Paki gulam Isa, zare tũi Mosi hisabe basona goijjila, badša Herud edde Pontus Filate, ei šohorot hibar berudde Oihudi okkolor fũwati edde Israili okkolor fũwati hat milail.
ACT 4:28 Tũwar kuduruti edde issa mozin zin zin goṭibode tũi age loti ṭik gori rakkila, hitara hendilla goijje.
ACT 4:29 Ar ehon Mabud, itara ãrare ki bafe ḍor lagar tũi kiyal goror. Tũwar gulam okkolore endilla šokti do zene kub himmot loi hitara tũwar kalam hoi fare.
ACT 4:30 Tũwar hat barai do, zene tũwar Paki gulam Isar name hitara manuš okkolore aram gori fare edde keramot edde sinnor ham okkol gori fare."
ACT 4:31 Ze zagat hitara dola oiye, munazat gori bade he zagagan hafi uiṭṭe. Ar hitara beggune Pak Ruhuye furaiya oi fũwati šahoš loi Allar kalam howa šuru goijje.
ACT 4:32 Har biššaši okkol beggunor mon dil ek aššil. Hitarar nizor dón šombottire nizor hoi dabi no gorito, kintu hitarattu zin aššil hinore beggun loi borat gorito.
ACT 4:33 Asab okkole ḍõr šokti loi goba diya šuru goijje ze Isa morattu zinda uṛi giyegoi, ar hitara beggunor uwore Allar ofurani rahamot aššil.
ACT 4:34 Hitarattu hono obafi manuš nuaššil, kiyollahoile zarattu zobin otóba gór aššil hitara hin okkol besi ṭĩya foiša anito,
ACT 4:35 edde asab okkolor ṭengor ḍake rakito. Bade zattu zendilla zorulot he bafe hitare diya oito.
ACT 4:36 Yusuf, Kiprus ḍiyar ekzon Levi. Hitare asab okkole Barnabas hoito, zar mani tuwajjo doyar fut.
ACT 4:37 Hitattu ekkan zobin aššil, hite hiyan besi ṭĩya ani asab okkolor ṭengor ḍake rakkil.
ACT 5:1 Ehon, Ananiyas name ekzon manuš edde hitar bou Safiraye ekkan zobin šombotti beisse.
ACT 5:2 Hite ṭiyattu hodun nizolla raki diyore baki ṭiyagun asab okkolor ṭengor ḍake raikkegoi, ar hite hen goijjede hitar bouwe o furafuri zanito.
ACT 5:3 Hetunot Fitore hodde, "Ananiyas, Šoitane tor mon kengori dokol goijje, ziyanor zoriya tui Pak Ruhur hãse misa hota hoiyos edde zobin besa ṭiyattu hodun nizolla raki diyos?
ACT 5:4 Besibar age ki zobingan tor nu aššil ne? Ar besi bade o ki ṭiyagun tor hatot nu aššil ne? To kiyolla tui endilla ham goribi ṭik goijjos? Tui šude mainšor loi misa no hos, kintu Allar loi misa hoiyos."
ACT 5:5 Ei hota funi mottor Ananiyas meṛit fori mori giyegoi. Ei goṭonar hota zara fuinne hitara beggune beša beši ḍoraiye.
ACT 5:6 Bade hozon zuwan manuš aišše edde hitar gat kafonor hor berai diye edde bare loi zai hitare dohon gorai felaiye.
ACT 5:7 Iyar tin gonḍa bade Ananiyasor bou heṛe aišše, kintu ki oiye hin hibaye no zanito.
ACT 5:8 Fitore hibare fusar goredde, "Sai ho sai, tũwara zobin besiyore beggun failade in ne ki?" Hibaye hodde, "Oi hin beggun in."
ACT 5:9 Hetunot Fitore hodde, "Tũwara kengori Mabudor Ruhure entehan goribolla razi oila? Sa, ze mainše tor zamaire dohon goraito aišše hitara dorozar hãsat aišše, ar hitara tore o baire loizaibo."
ACT 5:10 Safira hetunot Fitoror ṭengor ḍake mori giyegoi. Ar he zuwan manuš okkole butore aiyore dekedde hiba mora, toi hibare baire loizai hibar zamair ḍakottu dohon goraiye.
ACT 5:11 Hetunot zomator manuš edde oinno zara he hota fuinne hitara beggune beši ḍoraiye.
ACT 5:12 Asab okkolor duwara bout ḍoilla keramot edde sinnor ham okkol mainšor maze gora oiye. Ar biššaši okkol beggune dórmogóror Soloimanor haissarat ekku fũwati dola oito.
ACT 5:13 Oinno hono mainše hitarar loi dola oibolla himmot no gorito, zodi o hitarare manuš okkole kub beši ijjot gorito.
ACT 5:14 Ar din din bout furuš edde mayafuwain okkol Malikor uwore biššaš ainne edde Malikor dolor fũwati zug goijje.
ACT 5:15 Ar manuš okkole biyaraimma okkolore rastar uwore bar gori ani haṭor uwore edde faṛir uwore neṛai rakito, zene rasta bai zaibar šomot ebbe no oile Fitoror sabagan oile hitarar hono hono kiyor uwore fore.
ACT 5:16 Zeruzalemor atehasor fara okkolottu bout manuš okkole hitarar biyaraimma okkolore edde horaf zine faiyede manuš okkolore bar gori anito edde hitara beggune aram oito.
ACT 5:17 Hetunot ḍõr imam edde hitar har sãti okkol, zara Sadduki dolor manuš, hitara riše zoli uiṭṭe.
ACT 5:18 Hitara asab okkolore dori šorkari ziyolot diye.
ACT 5:19 Kintu raitta Mabudor ekzon firistaye ziyolor dorozagun kuli hitarare hentu baire niyalai ani hodde,
ACT 5:20 "Zo, tũwara dórmogóror uṛanot tiyaiore manuš okkolore ei noya zibonor babute har hóbor hogoi."
ACT 5:21 Ei hota funiyore tarfore binna kub sore hitara dórmogórot giye edde šikka diya šuru goijje. Toi heṛe maze, ḍõr imam edde hitar fũwajja okkol, zara Sadduki dol, mani Israili okkolor murubbi neta beggunore loi ek ḍõr bisar muzoliš ḍaikke edde asab okkolore anibolla hoekzon manušore ziyolot defeṛaiye.
ACT 5:22 Kintu zehon faharadar okkol heṛe aišše, heṛe hitarare no fa. Hitara uwafes firi zaiyore ei hóbor hoiyegoi,
ACT 5:23 "Ãra ziyolor doroza mojbut gori ṭala lagaiya asede edde doroza doroza faharadar okkol tiyai roiyede lot faiyi, kintu doroza kuli honokiyore butore no dekilam."
ACT 5:24 Ei hota funi dórmogór sõloya garḍ okkolor boro edde ḍõr imam okkol suhara oi bafa šuru goijje, iyanor anzam ki oibo,hoi.
ACT 5:25 Hetunot ekzon manuš aiyore hodde, "So, ze manuš okkolore tũwara ziyolot dila hitara dórmogóror uṛanot tiyaiyore mainšore šikka der."
ACT 5:26 Hetunot faharadar okkolor boroye hitar manuš okkol loi zaiyore hitarare dori ainne. Kintu mainše fattor maribo ḍore hitara asab okkolor uwore hono zobodusti no gore.
ACT 5:27 Hitara asab okkolore aniyore bisar šobar sarme tiya goraiye. Hetunot ḍõr imame asab okkolore hodde:
ACT 5:28 "Ãra tũwarare hora bafe hokum dilam he namor babute šikka no dibolla, kintu tũwara tũwarar šikkare Zeruzalemor aga gura borai felaiyo, edde he manušwar louwor dai ãrare goitto sor."
ACT 5:29 Hetunot Fitor edde oinno asab okkole zuwab dedde: "Manušor hokum falon goribattuwaro bolke Allar hokum ãra falon goronnan zoruri!
ACT 5:30 Zare õnora ek gasor uwore ṭaikko edde mari felaiyo, ãrar baf dadar Allaye he Isare morattu uwafes tuille.
ACT 5:31 Allaye hibare badša edde Basailoya hisabe hibar ḍen ḍakottu boibar ijjot diye, zene hibaye Israili okkolore gunattu mon firat ani fare edde gunar maf di fare.
ACT 5:32 Ãra in beggunor babute goba, ar zara Allar baiddo o, hitarare Allaye he Pak Ruhure diye, he Pak Ruh o hibar goba."
ACT 5:33 Ei hota funi hitara guššaye oin oiye edde hitarare furai felaibolla ereda loiye.
ACT 5:34 Kintu he bisar šobattu Gamaliel name ekzon Foroši alem, zare hár mainše ijjot goitto, hiba tiyai giyegoi edde ei manuššunore hotun baire loizai raka oibolla hokum diye.
ACT 5:35 Tarfore hibaye ḍõr šobare hodde: "Israili okkol! Tũwara ei manuššunore kissu goribar age bala gori bafi so.
ACT 5:36 Oto! kissu din age Tevdas name ekzon manuš muntu aišše, hitare hite ekzon ḍõr manuš dabi goijjil, ar hom beši sair šot mainše hitar fũwati zug dil. Hitare mari fela oiye edde hitar har sãti okkol šiṛašitta oi giyegoi edde hãzi giyegoi.
ACT 5:37 Hite bade, manuš gona oibar šomot endilla oilo, Galilot Ehudaye ek dol manušore failo, kintu hite o mori giyegoi, ar hitar sãti okkol beggun šiṛašiṭṭa oi giyegoi.
ACT 5:38 Hetolla ãi tũwarare hoir: Ei manuš okkolore kissu no goijjo. Itarare sari do, kiyollahoile itarar moksud edde haz harbar zodi manušor torfottu oi take, toile hin dongšo oi zaiboi.
ACT 5:39 Kintu zodi Allar torfottu o, toile tũwara itarare tamai no fariba. Hetolla hũšiyar! Ar no oile šude dekiba, tũwara Allar berudde larai goror."
ACT 5:40 Toi hitara hibar mošowarat razi oiye. Hitara asab okkolore abar butore ḍaki ainne edde hitarare bet marabaiye. Tarfore hitarare Isar nam loi tobolig no goribolla hokum diyore bade eri diye.
ACT 5:41 Henot Isar namolla buli asab okkole ze ohomani oibar laikka oiye, hiyanolla kuši gori gori hitara he bisar šobattu giyegoi.
ACT 5:42 Hitara fotti din dórmogórot edde góre góre zai šikka diye, hitara hinore tiya gorai no fele, Isa ze Mosi he kušir hóbor tobolig gorat aššil.
ACT 6:1 Ar he ṭaimot, zehon biššaši okkol bari uṛa šuru goijje, hitarar butore Girik baša hoiya okkole Ibroni baša hoiya okkolore endilla hoi hosuri diya šuru goijje, ze fotti din hána dibar šomot hitarar rari mayafuwain okkole kissu no fa.
ACT 6:2 Henot maze he barozon asabe har biššaši okkolore ek zagat ḍakiyore hodde: "Ãra Allar kalam tobolig gora bad gori hána diyar befar loi fori taka, iyan ãralla ṭik no.
ACT 6:3 Kintu oh báiyain okkol tũwara tũwarar butore zarar bala nam ase edde zara Pak Ruhuye furaiya edde giyani manuš hendilla hãt zonore basi lo. Hitarare ãra ei hamor bar diyum.
ACT 6:4 Kintu ãra munazat edde kalam toboligot diyan diyum."
ACT 6:5 Ei mošowarare dolor beggune bala gori goisse edde hitara biššaš edde Pak Ruhuye boron botti Stifanore, bade Filip, Frokorus, Nikanor, Timon, Farmenas, edde Anṭiyok šohoror Ihudi dórmot zat diya Nikolas, itarare basi loiye.
ACT 6:6 Bade asab okkolor sarme hitarare tiya goraiye, zara duwa goijje edde hitarar uwore hat raikke.
ACT 6:7 Toi Allar kalam ei bafe sorai giyegoi edde Zeruzalemot biššaši okkol beša beši bari uṛi gilgoi. Ar ek dol ḍor imam okkolor dole o biššašor baiddota oiye.
ACT 6:8 Stifane Allar rahamot edde šokti furaiya oiyore manuš okkolor butore bout keramot edde sinnor ham okkol goijje.
ACT 6:9 Ze muzolišhanare azad gora manuš okkolor sinagog hoito, hiyanor hoekzon manuše Stifanor fisali laigge. Hitara aššilde Kuroni edde Alekzanderiya šohor ar Kilikiya edde Ešiar hoekzon Ihudi okkol, hitara Stifan loi hotat bara bari diya šuru goijje.
ACT 6:10 Kintu Stifane Pak Ruhur duwara kub giyan loi hota hoiye. Hetolla hitara hibar berudde tiyai no fare.
ACT 6:11 Hetunot he Ihudi okkole gufone hoekzon Ihudire endilla hoibolla uskani diye, "Ãra Stifanore nobi Musa edde Allar berudde kuferi goredde funni."
ACT 6:12 Endilla gori hitara mainšore, murubbi okkolore edde Alem okkolore hafai tuille. Ar hitara Stifanore dori he ḍõr bisar šobar sarme ainne.
ACT 6:13 Hitara ho ekzon misa goba tiyagoraiye, hitara hodde, "Ei manušwaye hamiša dórmogóror edde Musar ainor berudde hota ho.
ACT 6:14 Ãra ite endilla hodde funni ze, he Nasarator Isaye bole ei dórmogór bangi felaibo edde Musaye ze ain okkol ãrare di giye hinore bole bodoli felaibo."
ACT 6:15 He ḍõr bisar šobat boiššilde hitara beggune Stifanor uzu sadde Stifanor siyaragan ek firistar siyarar ḍoil oi giyegoi.
ACT 7:1 Toi ḍõr imame Stifanore fusar goijje, "Ei hota ki soiyi ne?"
ACT 7:2 Zuwabe Stifane hodde: "Oh ãr báiyain edde baf okkol ãr hota funo! Ãrar fordada Ibrahim Harran šohorot bošoti loibar age zẽtte Mesofotemiya dešot aššil, hẽtte fohoraiwala Allaye hibare deha diyore hoil,
ACT 7:3 'Tui tor nizor deš edde tor egena gušti feli ãi tore ze deš dehaiyum heṛe zagoi.'
ACT 7:4 "Toi hiba Kalaḍiya okkolor deš felai Harran šohorot gil edde heṛe bošoti loil. Ar hibar baf mori bade, Allaye Ibrahimore ei dešot defeṛail, zeṛe tũwara ehon bošoti goror.
ACT 7:5 Allaye hibare nizolla hono zobin no de, enki ekkan ṭeng raki farefan zaga o no, kintu hibaye wada goijjil ze hibare edde hibar bade hibar bongšor manuš okkolore hitarar miraz hisabe he dešore dibo, zodi o he šomot Ibrahimottu hono fuwain no aššil.
ACT 7:6 Allaye hibare endilla hoil: 'Tor bongšodor okkol bidešot bošobaš goribo. Manuš okkole hitarare gulam banai rakibo edde sair šot bosor dori hitarar uwore zulum salaibo.'
ACT 7:7 Allaye aro hodde, 'Kintu ze zatiye hitarare gulam banaibo ãi hitarare šasti diyum. Bade hitara he dešottu niyoli aiyore ei zagat ãr ebadot goribo.'
ACT 7:8 Tarfore Allaye Ibrahimore wadar suktir sinno hisabe azomi goraibar niyom dil, bade hiba Isakor baf oiye edde ašṭo dinor din hibare azomi gora oiye. Hendilla Isake Yakubore edde Yakube he baro gušṭir baf okkolore azomi goraiye.
ACT 7:9 "He baro bongšor baf okkole riš gori Yusufore gulam hisabe Mišor dešot besifelail. Kintu Allah hibar fũwati aššil,
ACT 7:10 edde har duk hošṭottu hibare uddar goijje. Allaye hibare giyan dan goijjil edde Mišor dešot razar bala nozorot felabail. Hetolla he razaye hibare Mišor dešor šašon goroya edde razar nizor gór dehafuna goriballa buwail.
ACT 7:11 "Tarfore Mišor agagura edde Kenanot raṭ deha dilo, edde beši ḍõr hošṭo hazir oiye hetunot ãrar bafdada okkole haiddo lot no fail.
ACT 7:12 Kintu Mišorot gĩyu ase funi Yakube ãrar bafdada okkolore foila bar heṛe defeṛaiye.
ACT 7:13 Dusora bar zẽtte hitara aišše Yusufe hibar báiyaindore sin diye edde razaye Yusufor górwala okkolor babute zani faijje.
ACT 7:14 Iyar bade, Yusufe hibar baf Yakub edde góror gušṭi ṭiya, muṭ hoittor fãszon, beggunore ḍaki anibolla hóbor defeṛaiye.
ACT 7:15 Tarfore Yakub lami Mišor dešot gil, zeṛe hiba edde ãrar bafdada okkol entehal goijje.
ACT 7:16 Hitarare Šekimot ana oiye edde ze hoboror gãt Ibrahime Šekim šohoror Hamoror fũwain okkolottu rufa diyore kini loil, hibat dohon gora oil.
ACT 7:17 "Ibrahimor hãse Allaye ze wada goijje hin furon oibar ṭaim zehon hãse aišše, hetunot deha zadde ãrar manušzon okkol kub beši bari giyegoi.
ACT 7:18 Tarfore Mišor dešot en 'ekzon noya badša oiye, ze Yusufor babute kissu no zanito.'
ACT 7:19 He badšaye ãrar manuš okkolore ṭokaito edde ãrar bafdada okkolor uwore zulum goitto, enki hitarattu ze futziyain okkol zormo oito hitara mori zagoifan he gura fuwain okkolore baire felai rakibolla zur gorito.
ACT 7:20 "He šomot Musa zormo oil. Musa Allar šanot ekzon beši šundojja fuwa aššil. Hibare tin maš foijjonto baf mar górot lalon falon gora oil.
ACT 7:21 Bade zẽtte hibare baire felai raka oiye, hẽtte razar ziye tuli loizaiyore hibare nizor fuwa hisabe lalon falon goijje.
ACT 7:22 Mišoriyo okkolor har giyane en bafe šikkita oiye, hiba hotaye edde hame šoktišali aššil.
ACT 7:23 "Musar umor sališ bosor oiyede šomot hibaye Israili báiyain okkol loi deha goitto zaibo faisela loil.
ACT 7:24 Ar heṛe Mišoriyo ekzone hitarar ekzonore horaf bebohar goredde Musaye deikke, toi hibaye ei Israili manušwar foikka oibolla giye edde he Mišoriyo manušware marifelaiyore hiyanor daiya loiye.
ACT 7:25 Musaye mone gojjil hibar nizor manuš okkole buzibo ze Allaye hibar duwara hitarare uddar goribo, kintu hitara hiyan buzi no fare.
ACT 7:26 Tarforor din Musaye duizon Israilire mara mari goredde deikke. Hetunot hitarare milai dibolla hodde, 'Oh báiyain, tũwara to bái bái, to kiyolla ekzone ekzon loi endilla horaf bebohar goror?'
ACT 7:27 "Kintu ze manušwaye horaf bebohar goijjil hite Musare ḍeikka mari lorai diyore hodde, 'Ãrar uwore tore šašon goroya edde bisarhar hone tuille?
ACT 7:28 Gelde hailla zendilla gori he Mišoriyo manušware mari felaiyos, ãre o ki hendilla gori mari felaito sos?'
ACT 7:29 Ei hota funi Musa dai zaigoi Midiyan dešot musafer hisabe bošobaš gora šuru goijje. Heṛe hibattu duizon morod fuwain zormo oil.
ACT 7:30 "Sališ bosor farai zaigoi bade, Sinai faharor ḍake bošoti sara elehat maze ek firistaye ek zolonto zaḍḍowar oinor butottu Musare deha diye.
ACT 7:31 Musaye dekiyore tajjuf oil. Hibaye aro hãse zai saibolla zehon giye, hetunot Mabudor abaz fuinne:
ACT 7:32 'Ãi tor fordada okkolor Allah, Ibrahim, Isak edde Yakubor Allah.' Kintu Musaye ḍore hafa šuru goijje, hikka saibolla o himmot no gore.
ACT 7:33 "Hetunot Mabude hibare hodde, 'Tor ṭengor zuta kulifela, kiyollahoile ze zagat tui tiyaiyos hiyan Paki zaga.
ACT 7:34 Mišor dešot ãr bonda okkolor uwore ze zulum or hin ãi dekki. Ãi hitarar hatoranir ḍak funni edde hitarare uddar goribolla ãi nise lami aišši. Ehon ãi tore Mišor dešot uwafes defeṛaiyum.'
ACT 7:35 "Iba oilde he Musa zare Israili okkole en hoi batil goijjil, 'Tore šašon goroya edde bisarhar hone banaiye.' Ze firistaye he zaḍḍowar butottu Musare deha dil, he firistar duwara Allah nize ei Musare Israili okkolor šašon goroya edde uddar goroya hisabe Mišorot defeṛail.
ACT 7:36 Ei Musaye Mišor dešottu Israili okkolore niyolai loi ainnil edde Mišor dešot, louwor doriyar ḍake edde sališ bosorfan bošoti sara elehat bout keramot edde sinnor ham okkol goijjil.
ACT 7:37 "Iba oilde he Musa ze Israili okkolore hoil, 'Allaye tũwarar nizor báiyain okkolor butottu tũwaralla ãr ḍoil ekzon nobi tiya goraibo.'
ACT 7:38 Ei Musa bošoti sara elehat maze Israili okkolor dolor butore, ãrar fordada okkolor fũwati aššil. Ze firistaye Sinai faharottu hota hoil ei Musaye he firistar fũwati heṛe aššil. Ãrare dibolla hibaye zinda kalam fail.
ACT 7:39 "Kintu ãrar fordada okkole Musare mainto no sa. Hiyanor bodole hitara hibare batil goijjil edde hitarar dil Mišoror uzu oigilgoi.
ACT 7:40 Hitara Harunore hodde, 'Ãrare fõt dehai loi zai farefan dev devi banao, kiyollahoile ze Musaye Mišor dešottu ãrare niyolai loi ainne hibar ki oiye ãra hoi no fari.
ACT 7:41 He ṭaimot maze hitara gorur so ḍoil gori uggwa mutti tiyar goijje. Hitara he muttir mutallek zanuwar kurbani goijje edde nizor hate banaiyede hiyanor uwore hitara kušir mela goijje.
ACT 7:42 Kintu Allaye hitarattu muk firai felaiye edde asmanor san šurzo edde tara fũzat maze hitarare felai raikke, zendilla nobi okkolor kitabot leka ase: "'Oh, Israil zati, bošoti sara elehat he sališ bosorfan tũwara ki ãr mutallek hono zandar kurbani ba hadiya dila ne?
ACT 7:43 No, no do, bolke tũwara to Mulok devotar mutti, ar Rifon devotar tara, tũwara bar gori boi loi gila, fũza goribar niyote he mutti okkol banaila. Kintu ãi tũwarare Babilonor okule felai diyum.'
ACT 7:44 "Bošoti sara elehat ãrar fordada okkolottu uggwa ṭambu aššil zibaye Allah hitarar fũwati aššilde forman diye. Allaye Musare zendilla gori hokum dil edde Musare ze nomuna dehail he mozin ei ṭambu tiyar gora oil.
ACT 7:45 Ãrar fordada okkol he ṭambu faiyore hitarar neta Yosbar anḍare hiyan hitarar fũware ei dešot loi aššil. Allaye hitarar sarmottu oinno zatire lorai dil edde hitara ei deššan adai goijjil. Daudor ṭaim foijjonto he ṭambu ei dešot aššil.
ACT 7:46 Hibaye Allattu rahamot fail edde ejazot dibolla foriyad goijjil zene Yakubor bongšolla ekkan dórmogór hibaye tiyar gori fare.
ACT 7:47 Kintu Soloimane hiballa ekkan dórmogór tiyar goijjil.
ACT 7:48 "Zen oibo ok, šorbo šoktiwala Allah manušor tiyari górot no take, zendilla nobiye hor:
ACT 7:49 "'Behosto oilde ãr šingašon, ar duniyai ãr ṭeng rakibar zaga. Ãlla tui hondilla gór tiyar goribi, Mabude hor. Zaga hiyan hoṛe, zeṛe ãi zirai faijjum?
ACT 7:50 Ei šob ziniš beggun ki ãi nizor hate foida no gori ne?'
ACT 7:51 "Oh ek gũwaijja zati! Tũwarar han edde dil Oihudi okkolor ḍoil, ar tũwara o tũwarar fordada okkolor ḍoil. Tũwara šob šome Pak Ruhure bad di tako.
ACT 7:52 En hono ki nobi ase, zare tũwarar fordada okkole zulum no gore? Hitara hitarare mari felail, zara agottu loti he niyaiwala aibar babute tobolig goijjil. Ar ehon tũwara hibar loi dúha bazi goijjo edde mari felaiyo.
ACT 7:53 Firista okkolor duwara tũwarar hãse to ain diya oil, kintu tũwara hin falon no goro."
ACT 7:54 Ei hota okkol funi hitara guššaye oin oi giyegoi edde Stifanor berudde dat loi dat kirkiraiye.
ACT 7:55 Kintu Stifane, Pak Ruhuye furaiya oi behostor mikka sai taikke edde heṛe Allar mohimar deha faiye. Hibaye Isare Allar den ḍakottu tiyai taikkede dekiyore,
ACT 7:56 Stifane hodde, "So, ãi behosto kula asede dekir edde Adomor Fut Allar ḍen ḍakottu tiyai roiye."
ACT 7:57 Henot hitara hanot õl diye edde zure guzoriyore beggune Stifanor uwore zafai foijje.
ACT 7:58 Bade hitara Stifanore fattor maribolla ṭani šohoror bar kule loigiye, ar goba okkole hitarar zubba okkol gattu kuli Šaulus name ek zuwan fuwar ṭengor ḍake eijje.
ACT 7:59 Hitara Stifanore fattor maredde šomot, hibaye munazat goijje edde hodde, "Malik Isa, ãr ruhure gosi lo."
ACT 7:60 Tarfore hibaye ãṛu felaiye edde ḍõr gori guzojje, "Malik, itarar berudde ei gunare monot no raikko," ei hota hoi hiba zurai giyegoi.
ACT 8:1 Saul o Stifanore kun gorat razi aššil. He din Zeruzalemot Isayi zomator manuš okkolor uwore beša beši zulum owa šuru oiye. Henot asab okkolgun bade ar har biššaši okkol Ehudiya edde Sameriyar hár zagat šiṛa šitta oi giyegoi.
ACT 8:2 Hoekzon allawala manuše Stifanore dohon goraiye edde hiballa kub beši bilag goijje.
ACT 8:3 Kintu Saule he zomatore dongšo gori felaibar kušišot góre góre zai zomator mayafuwain edde morod fuwain okkolore ṭani ani ani ziyolot diya šuru goijje.
ACT 8:4 Ze biššaši okkol šiṛa šiṭṭa oigilgoi, hitara sairo mikka giye edde kalam tobolig goijje.
ACT 8:5 He šomot Filipe Sameriyar ek šohorot zai Mosir babute tobolig goijje.
ACT 8:6 Ar beggune zara hibar hota fuinne edde ze keramoti ham okkol hibaye goijje, hin saiyore hitara hibar hota mon di fuinne.
ACT 8:7 Bout kiyor butottu napak ruh okkol sikkar mari niyoli gilgoi edde bout leng biyaraimma edde ãtur okkol aram oiye.
ACT 8:8 Henot heṛe šohorot ek ḍõr kuši oiye.
ACT 8:9 He šohorot Simon name ekzon manuš aššil, ze bout din dori heṛe zadu dehaito, henot Sameriyar manuš okkol ebbere tajjuf oi zaitogoi. Hite hitare ek ḍõr manuš fukarito.
ACT 8:10 Ar šoṛo ḍõr beggune hitar hotare dam dito edde hoito: "Allar ze kudurutire ḍõr kuduruti howa o, ite he ḍõr kuduruti."
ACT 8:11 Mainše hitar hota mozin solito, kiyollahoile bout din dori hite hitar zadu dehaiyore hitarare tajjuf gorat aššil.
ACT 8:12 Kintu Filipe zehon Allar raijjor babute edde Isa Mosir namor kušir hóbor tobolig goijje hetunot manuš okkole hibar hotat biššaš ainne, Hitara mayafuwain edde morod fuwain beggune torikotor gusol loiye.
ACT 8:13 He Simon nize o biššaš ainne, toi hite torikotor gusol loi bade Filipor fũwati fũwati gil, ar sinno edde ḍõr ḍõr keramoti ham okkol deki hite ammuwak oil.
ACT 8:14 Zeruzalemor asab okkole zehon fuinne, ze Sameriyar manuš okkole Allar kalamor uwore biššaš ainne, hetunot hitara Fitor edde Yuhannare hitarar hãse defeṛaiye.
ACT 8:15 Hitara heṛe fõsi bade, hitara Pak Ruhure faibolla duwa goijje.
ACT 8:16 Kiyollahoile hẽtte o hitarar uwore Pak Ruh no aiye. Bolke hitarare šude Isar name torikotor gusol diya oil.
ACT 8:17 Ehon hitarar uwore hat raikke, ar hitara Pak Ruhure faiye.
ACT 8:18 Kintu Simone zehon deikke ze asab okkole hat rakiyore hitarare Pak Ruhure diye, hetunot hite hitarar hãse ṭĩya ainne
ACT 8:19 edde hodde: "Ãre o ei šokti do, zene ãi o honokiyor uwore hat rakile hite he Pak Ruhure fa."
ACT 8:20 Hetunot Fitore hitare hodde: "Tor ṭĩya tor fũwati donšo ok, kiyollahoile tui mone goijjos Allar hadiya ṭĩya di kina fa.
ACT 8:21 Tottu ei hamot hono miraz otóba bag nai, kiyollahoile tor dil Allar mikka soiyi no.
ACT 8:22 Ei horafittu tui mon fira edde Mabudor hãse munazat gor. Hen oile Allaye tor dilor ei horaf sinta oitfare maf goribo.
ACT 8:23 Kiyollahoile ãi dekir, tor dil lalsiye boraiya edde tui gunar hãse kobza oi taikkos."
ACT 8:24 Hetunot Simone hodde: "Tũwara Mabudor hãse ãlla duwa goro zene tũwara zen hoiyo hendilla ãr uwore no goṭe."
ACT 8:25 Hitara Malikor babute kalam tobolig edde goba diye bade Zeruzalem firi giyegoi. Zargoide fõtot hitara Sameri okkolor bout fara okkolot kušir hóbor tobolig goijje.
ACT 8:26 Ekdin Mabudor ek firistaye Filipore hodde, "Uṭ, doin mikkar rastat za, ze rasta Zeruzalemottu Gaza šohoror mikka giye." He rastawa aššilde bošoti sara elehat.
ACT 8:27 Toi Filipe hikka giye edde fõtot Etupia dešor ekzon has raz hormosari loi deha oiye. Etupiar Kandaki ranir dón mal dehafuna goribar bar ei manušwar uwore aššil. Allar ebadot goribolla ei raz hormosariwa Zeruzalem gil,
ACT 8:28 ar ehon górot uwafes firi zargoide fõtot, hite hitar gũra garit boi nobi Esaiyar kitab telewat gorer.
ACT 8:29 Pak Ruhuye Filipore hodde, "Oi gũra garir hãse za edde hiyanor hãse takis."
ACT 8:30 Toi Filipe dũri he gũra garir hãse giye edde funedde manušwaye nobi Esaiyar kitabwa telewat gorer. Filipe fusar goredde, "Tũi telewat gorodde hin buzo ne?"
ACT 8:31 He hormosariye hodde, "Honokiye buzai no dile ãi ken gori buzi fariyum." Hite Filipore gũra garit uiṭṭo edde hitar ḍake boibolla foriyad goijje.
ACT 8:32 He raz hormosariwaye zin telewat goijje hin oilde in: "Zorgoraibar soolore loizafan gori hibare loigiye, soolor kẽš ãsoyar munttu zendilla sool suf take, hendilla hibaye o muk no kuler.
ACT 8:33 Hiba ohomani oiye, hibar uwore niyai bisar gora no o. Hone hoi faribo hibar bongšor hota? zehon hibar foran ei duniyaittu loifela oiye."
ACT 8:34 He raz hormosariwaye Filipore hodde, "Meherbani gori ekkena hona, nobiye ei hota har babute hodde, nizor babute ne naki ar oinno honokiyor babute?"
ACT 8:35 Toi Filipe Pak kitabor he aiyatottu loti šuru goijje edde Isar kušir hóbor hitar hãse zanaiye.
ACT 8:36 Hitara fõt bai zaite zaite en ek zagat fõissegoi, zeṛe fani ase. Hetunot he raz hormosariwaye hodde, "So, eṛe fani ase, ãi torikotor gusol loite ãttu banda hoṛe?"
ACT 8:37 (Filipe hodde, "Tũi zodi zane dile biššaš goro toile tũi loi fariba." Hetunot he hormosariwaye hodde, "Ãi biššaš gori ze Isa Mosi oilde Allar Fut.")
ACT 8:38 Toi he hormosariwaye gũra gari tiya goraito hokum diye. Ar Filip edde raz hormosari, hitara dunizone fanit maze laimme. Toi Filipe hitare torikotor gusol diye.
ACT 8:39 Hitara fanittu uṛi aiššede šomot, Mabudor Ruhuye Filipore loigiyegoi, raz hormosariwaye hibare ar no deke. Toi hite kuši oiyore hitar nizor baisar uzu giyegoi.
ACT 8:40 Filipore kintu Ašdud šohorot deha giye. Ar hibaye har šohor okkolot kušir hóbor tobolig gori gori Sizeriya foijjonto giye.
ACT 9:1 Saule hehono Malikor sahabi okkolor uwore zafai forat roiye edde hitarare zane mari felaibo domki diyat roiye. Saule ḍõr imamor heṛe giye,
ACT 9:2 edde hitattu Damaskus šohoror sinagog okkololla šeṛi saiye, zene Saule he fõtot giyede hendilla nari furuš zarare faibo, hitarare bandi Zeruzalem loi ani fare.
ACT 9:3 Hite baisa di Damaskusor hãsa hãsi fõissegoide šomot, asmanottu atikka ek fohoror šoṛak hitar sairo mikka foijje.
ACT 9:4 Hite meṛit fori giyegoi edde ek abaz fuinne, hodde, "Saul, Saul, kiyolla tui ãr uwore zulum goror?"
ACT 9:5 Saule hodde, "Malik, tũi honnuwa?" Malike hodde, "Ãi he Isa, zar uwore tui zulum goror.
ACT 9:6 Tui ehon uṛi šohoror butore za, tottu ki gora foribo hin tore heṛe howa oibo."
ACT 9:7 Ze manuš okkol Saulor fũwati giye hitara ammuwak oi tiyai roiye, hitara abaz fuinne kintu honokiyore no deke.
ACT 9:8 Bade Saul uṛi tiyaiye edde suk kuille, kintu hite suke deki no faijjil. Hetunot hitar fũwajja okkole hate dori dori hitare Damaskus šohorot loigiye.
ACT 9:9 Tin din foijjonto Saul anda oi aššil edde hána fani kissu no há.
ACT 9:10 Damaskusot Ananiyas name ekzon sahabi aššil. Malike hibare deha diyore hodde, "Ananiyas!" Hibaye hodde, "Malik, so ãi eṛe."
ACT 9:11 Toi Malike hibare hodde, "Uzu name ze rasta ase tui he rastat za, heṛe Ehudar górot Saul hoi ekzon Tarsus šohoror manušore talaš gorgoi, kiyollahoile hite duwa gorer.
ACT 9:12 Ar hite ek deha faiyede heṛe dekedde, Ananiyas name ekzon manuš aiyore hitar uwore hat rakibo, toi hite abar suke dekibo."
ACT 9:13 Kintu Ananiyase hodde, "Malik, ãi bout kiyor mukottu ei manušwar babute fuinni, Zeruzalemot tũwar Paki manuš okkolor uwore ite hondilla zulum okkol goijje.
ACT 9:14 Ar ehon, hite ḍõr imamottu kemota loi õnor name ḍakede har mainšore bandi loizaibolla eṛe o aiššiye."
ACT 9:15 Kintu Ananiyasore Malike hodde,"Tui za! Kiyollahoile Oihudi edde hitarar badša okkol edde Israili okkolor hãse ãr babute tobolig goribolla ite ãr basona goijja zontro.
ACT 9:16 Ãi hitare dehaiyum ãr namolla buli hitattu hoto duk šowa foribo."
ACT 9:17 Toi Ananiyas giye edde he górot góille, ar Saulor uwore hat rakiyore hodde, "Bái Saul, eṛe aibar fõtot tore ze deha dil he Isaye ãre defeṛaiye, zene tui suke dekibar šokti firai fos edde Pak Ruhuye furaiya os."
ACT 9:18 Hetunot Saulor sukottu õišor ḍoilla ekkan ki fori giyegoi, toi hite abar suke deki faijje. Tarfore hite uiṭṭe edde torikotor gusol loiye,
ACT 9:19 tarfore hite hána haiyore doromoro oiye. Saule hoto din Damaskus šohoror biššaši okkolor fũwati heṛe taikke.
ACT 9:20 Ar deri no gori hibaye sinagog okkolot tobolig gora šuru goijje, ze Isa oilde Allar Fut.
ACT 9:21 Beggune zara hibar hota funito, hitara tajjuf oi fusar gorito, Zeruzalemot zara Isar nam dori ḍakito hitarare zulum goittode, ite no ne ki? Ar eṛe o zara Isar nam dori ḍake hitarare bandi ḍõr imamor hãse loi zaibolla aiššede, ite no ne ki?
ACT 9:22 Saule kintu lagatar ḍõr ḍõr šokti faiye. Damaskusor Ihudi okkole zuwab dibolla fõt udda tui no fa, zẽtte hibaye Isa Moside forman diye.
ACT 9:23 Iyar bout din bade Ihudi okkole hibare mari felaibolla felain goijje.
ACT 9:24 Kintu Saule hitarar felainor hota zani faijje. Hibare mari felaibolla hitara šohoror geiṭ okkolot dine raite fahara diye.
ACT 9:25 Kintu ek raitta hibar šagirit okkole hibare ek ḍular butore gori loizai ḍebal far gorai diye.
ACT 9:26 Saul Zeruzalem ai bade sahabi okkol loi zug dito saiye, kintu beggune hibare ḍoraiye. Saul ze ekzon hãsa biššaši hiyan hitara biššaš gori no faijjil.
ACT 9:27 Kintu Barnabase hibare fũwati asab okkolor hãse loigiye edde Saule fõtot ki bafe Malikor deha fail edde ki bafe Malike Saul loi hota hoil, ar ki bafe Saule Damaskusot šahoš loi Isar nam tobolig goijje hin okkol hibaye hitarare zanaiye.
ACT 9:28 Tarfore oite Saul hitarar fũwati Zeruzalemot takito edde butore baire aša zawa goitto, ar kulasa bafe edde šahoš loi Malikor namot tobolig gorito.
ACT 9:29 Hibaye Girik baša hoiya Ihudi okkol loi hotabattara edde barabari goitto, kintu hitara hibare mari felaibolla kušiš goijje.
ACT 9:30 Torikotor báiyain okkole zehon ei hota fuinne, hibare Sizeriya šohorot loi giyegoi, toi hentu Tarsus šohorot faṭai diye.
ACT 9:31 He šomot Ehudiya, Galil edde Sameriya eleha okkolor zomat okkolot šanti aššil. He zomatgun gori uṭṭil, hiyanor zoriya Malikor mutallek ḍor edde Pak Ruhur tuwajjo loi solat zomator manuš okkol bari uṭṭil.
ACT 9:32 Fitore hár zagat gurite gurite Ludda šohorot ze Allar bonda okkol aššil hitarar hãse aišše.
ACT 9:33 Heṛe Aneas name ekzon manušore dekkil, hite aššilde ãtur, ze ašṭo bosor mula bisanat fori roiye.
ACT 9:34 Fitore hitare dekiyore hodde: "Aneas, Isa Mosiye tore bala gorer. Uṭ, tor bisana tuli lo." Hite hehon uṛi tiyaiye.
ACT 9:35 Henot Ludda šohorot edde Šarun ḍeilot takitode hár manuš okkole Aneasore deki Malikor mikka fijje.
ACT 9:36 Zaffa šohorot Tabita name ek mayafuwa biššaši aššil, Girik bašat Dorka (mani Horini). Hibaye beši bala ham okkol edde gorib okkolore modot okkol gorito.
ACT 9:37 Kintu hẽtte hibattu beši ošuk oiyore bade mori giyegoi, ar manuš okkole hibare duwaiyore uworor uggwa kamerat rakkil.
ACT 9:38 Ludda aššilde Zaffa šohoror hãsa hãsi, toi sahabi okkole fuinne ze Fitor Luddat ase. Hitara duizon manušore hibar hãse defeṛaiye, hibare hitarar heṛe toratori aito foriyad goribolla hoi.
ACT 9:39 Toi Fitor hitarar fũwati giye. Hiba heṛe fõsi bade hibare uworor kamerat loigiye. Heṛe rari okkol beggune Fitorore berai doijje. Dorka basi taite hibaye ze kuruta edde oinno horsuwor silail hin okkolore hitara Fitorore deha šuru goijje edde handa šuru goijje.
ACT 9:40 Toi Fitore beggunore hentu niyolai diye edde ãṛu felai duwa goijje. Tarfore he mora maya fuwawar uzu firiyore hodde: "Tabita, uṭ! Henot hibaye suk kuille, ar Fitorore deki uṛi boišše."
ACT 9:41 Toi Fitore hat diyore hibare tuille. Tarfore biššaši edde rari okkolore ḍaikke edde hibare zinda dehaiye.
ACT 9:42 Ei hota Zaffa šohoror beggune zani faijje edde boute Malikor uwore biššaš ainne.
ACT 9:43 Fitor bout din mula Zaffa šohorot Simon name ekzon samorar ham goroyar górot taigilgoi.
ACT 10:1 Sizeriya šohorot Kornelius name ekzon manuš aššil. Hite aššilde Iṭalittu Romiyo šoinno dolor ofisar.
ACT 10:2 Hite ekzon allawala manuš, hitar góror beggune o Allare ḍoraito. Hite Ihudi gorib okkolore šome šome modot okkol dito, ar Allar hãse hamiša munazat gorito.
ACT 10:3 Ek din, dinor tinnwa baijjede ṭaimot maze hite ekkan deha faiye. Hite foriškar gori deikke ze Allar ekzon firista aiyore hitare ḍaker: "Kornelius!"
ACT 10:4 Korneliuse ḍoraiye edde he firistar mikka saiyore hodde, "Ki hodde, malik?" Firistaye hodde, "Tor munazat edde gorib okkolore modotor hota Allar hãse fõisse edde Allaye hin monot raikke.
ACT 10:5 Ehon tui Zaffa šohorot manuš defeṛai Simon, zare Fitor o ho, hitare ḍaki an.
ACT 10:6 Hite Simon name ek samora biyarir górot ase, ze górgan doriyar hãsat."
ACT 10:7 Ze firistaye Kornelius loi hota hoil hiba hentu giyegoi, bade Korneliuse duizon gulam edde ekzon nizor faharadari šoinnore ḍaikke.
ACT 10:8 Hite har hota buzaiye edde hitarare Zaffa šohorot defeṛaiye.
ACT 10:9 Tarforor din he manuš okkol fõt bai zaite zaite zẽtte Zaffa šohoror hãsa hãsi fõissegai, hẽtte ṭaim onumanik dũijja, Fitore sador uwore munazat goribolla uṭṭil.
ACT 10:10 Hibattu bug laigge edde kissu haito saiye, kintu hitara hehono hána tiyar gorat aššil, hetunot Fitor zurainna mikka abostat aššil.
ACT 10:11 He abostat maze Fitore dekedde asman kuli giyegoi edde hono kissu ekkan lami aiyer, hiyanore saite ekkan ḍõr saddor sair kuna loi duniyait lamai diya or.
ACT 10:12 He saddoror uwore hár ḍoilla sair ṭenga zanuwar edde buke aṛede zandar okkol edde faik okkol ase.
ACT 10:13 Tarfore ek abaze hibare hodde, "Fitor, uṭ, zora edde há!"
ACT 10:14 Fitore hodde: "No, no, Malik, hono mote no, kiyollahoile ãi hono din hono napak, oforiškar no hái."
ACT 10:15 Hetunot hibaye dusora bar ei abaz fuinne, "Allaye zinore Pak goijje, hinore tui napak no hois."
ACT 10:16 Endilla tin bar oiye, toi bade he saddorgan abar asmanot tuli loi za oiye.
ACT 10:17 Fitore ze deha faiye hiyanor mani ki oitfare, ei babute hibaye ehono bafer, hen šomot Korneliuse defeṛaiyede manuššune Simonor gór tuwaiyore ehon dorozar sarme ai tiyaiyegai.
ACT 10:18 Tarfore hitara góror butore ḍak maijje edde fusar goijje, Simon, zare Fitor ḍaka o, hiba ki heṛe ase ne, hoi.
ACT 10:19 Fitore ehono o deha failde he babute bafat ase, toi Pak Ruhuye hibare hodde, "Sa, tinzon manuše tor talaš gorer.
ACT 10:20 Toratori gor, lamat za. Hono andeša no ani hitarar fũwati za, kiyollahoile hitarare ãi defeṛaiyide."
ACT 10:21 Toi Fitore lamiyore oi manuššunor hãse giye edde hodde: "So, tũwara zare talaš goror hiba ãi. Tũwara eṛe kiyolla aiššode?"
ACT 10:22 Hitara zuwabe hodde, "Ãrare šenafoti ofisar, Korneliuse defeṛaiyede. Hiba ekzon dormiyo manuš, ze Allare ḍora. Ar har Ihudi okkole hibar šunam gore. Hibaye ek Paki firistattu hokum faiye ze õnore hibar gõrot ḍaki loi zaiyore hibaye õnor hota fune."
ACT 10:23 Toi Fitore he manuš okkolore góror butore ḍaki ainne edde hitarare mehemandari goijje. Tarforor din uṛi hitarar fũwati giye. Ar Zaffa šohorottu ho ekzon torikotor báiyain hibar fisa fise giye.
ACT 10:24 Tarforor din hitara Sizeriyat fõissegoi. He šomot Korneliuse hitar nizor afonzon, egena, dusto okkolore ek zagat gori hitaralla entezar goijjil.
ACT 10:25 Bade Fitor zehon górot góille hetunot Korneliuse hibar loi deha oiye edde hibar ṭengot uitefori hibare soida goijje.
ACT 10:26 Kintu Fitore hitare tuli loiye, edde hodde: "Uṛi zagoi, ãi nize o bolke ekzon manuš."
ACT 10:27 Kornelius loi hota hoite hoite, Fitore butore zai sadde heṛe beša beši manuš okkol zoma oi taikke.
ACT 10:28 Hetunot Fitore hitarare hodde: "Õnora to zanode hota ze oinno hono zatir manuš loi aza gora ba hitarar loi dola owa ekzon Ihudilla iyan niyomor baire. Kintu ãre Allaye dehaiye ze honokiyore napak ba oforiškar howa bala no.
ACT 10:29 Hetolla tũwara zẽtte ãre ḍakito defeṛaila hẽtte hono bázá no raki ãi aišši. Kintu ãi ehon tũwarare fusar gori, tũwara ãre kiyolla ḍakito defeṛailade?"
ACT 10:30 Hetunot Kornileuse hodde: "Sair din age ṭik ei šomot, ãi ãr górot munazat goijjilam. Hen šomot atikka ekzon ujjol dola hor finda manuš ãr sarme aiyore tiyaiye.
ACT 10:31 Edde hodde, 'Kornelius, tor munazat edde gorib okkolore modotor hota Allar hãse fõisse edde Allaye hin monot raikke.
ACT 10:32 Ehon tui Zaffa šohorot manuš defeṛai Simon, zare Fitor o ḍaka o.hitare ḍaki ana. Hite Simon name ek samora biyarir górot ase, ze górgan doriyar hãsat.'
ACT 10:33 Hetolla ãi hehon õnore ḍaki anibolla manuš defeṛailam. Õne aiššode bala oiye. Ar ãra ehon beggune Allar sarme asi, Malike õnore ãrar hãse ziyan hoibolla hokum diye ãra hiyan funiyum."
ACT 10:34 Tarfore Fitore muk kuille edde hitarare hodde: "Soiyi ãi buzi faijji ze Allaye hono manušore forok no gore.
ACT 10:35 Kintu hár zatir butottu zara hibare ḍora edde ziyan hibar sukot ṭik hiyan ze gore, hitarare hibaye gose.
ACT 10:36 Tũwara zanode hota, Allaye ei kušir hóbor Israili okkolor hãse defeṛail, Isa Mosir duwara he šantir kušir hóbor, Isa Mosi, hiba ziba beggunor uwore Malik.
ACT 10:37 Tũwara beggune ei goṭona zano ze Yahyar duwara torikotor gusol tobolig gora oi bade Galilottu loti šuru gori šara Ehudiya agagura ei hóbor sorai gilgoi.
ACT 10:38 Ar Allaye kibafe Nasarator Isare Pak Ruh edde šokti diye, kibafe hibaye hár mikka giye edde bala ham okkol goijje, ar zara Šoitanor kobzar butore duk bug goitto, hitara beggunore aram gorito. Kiyollahoile hibar fũwati Allah aššil.
ACT 10:39 "Hibaye Ihudi okkolor dešot edde Zeruzalemot zin zin goijje hin beggunor goba oilamde ãra, hitara zara hibare kurušot loṭkaiyore mari felaiye.
ACT 10:40 Kintu Allaye hibare tin dinor din uwafes tuille, ar endilla goijje zene mainše hibare deke.
ACT 10:41 Hibare beggune no deke, kintu ze goba okkolore agottu loti Allaye basona goijjil hitarare deha diye. Hiba morattu uwafes uṛi zaigoi bade ãra hibar fũwati hafiya goijjilam.
ACT 10:42 Hibaye ãrare hokum diye, ãra zene tobolig gori edde goba di, ze Iba oilde he zon zibare Allaye zinda edde mora okkololla bisarhar hisabe buwaiye.
ACT 10:43 Hibar babute har nobi okkole goba der, ze honokiye hibar uwore biššaš ane, hite hibar namor duwara guna maf faibo."
ACT 10:44 Fitore ehono hota howat ase, hen šomot hitara zara he kalam funnil, hitara beggunor uwore Pak Ruh aiššiye.
ACT 10:45 Ze Ihudi biššaši okkol Fitoror fũwati aiššil hitara Oihudi okkolor uwore o Pak Ruhure hadiya hisabe ḍali diya oiyede deki tajjuf oiye.
ACT 10:46 Kiyollahoile zilor baša hodde edde Allar tarif goredde hitara fuinne. Toi Fitore hodde:
ACT 10:47 "Itara o ãrar ḍoilla Pak Ruhure faiye. Honokiye ki itarare torikotor gusol dite banda di faribo?"
ACT 10:48 Toi Fitore he manuš okkolore Isar name torikotor gusol dibolla hokum diye. Bade hitara Fitorore ho ek din hitarar hãse takibolla foriyad goijje.
ACT 11:1 Oihudi okkole o Allar kalam goissede he hota asab okkole edde Ehudiyar har biššaši báiyain okkole fuinne.
ACT 11:2 Ar zẽtte Fitor Zeruzalemot aišše, he azomi goraiya biššaši okkole Fitorore hosuri diyore hodde,
ACT 11:3 "Tũi azomi agoraiya manuš okkolor górot zai hitarar loi kiyolla hafiya goijjo?"
ACT 11:4 Fitore foilattu loti šuru gori zin zin goiṭṭe ekkan ekkan buzaiyore hoiye.
ACT 11:5 Hodde: "Ãi Zaffa šohorot munazat goijjilam, hẽtte zurainna mikka oi ãi ek deha failam. Ãi dekidde ekkan ḍõr saddoror ḍoil ziniš sair kuna loi asmanottu lamai diya or, ar hiyan ãr hãse aišše.
ACT 11:6 Ãi hiyanore kiyal gori sailam, ar dekidde sair ṭenga zanuwar edde fahari zanuwar okkol, buke aṛede zandar edde faik okkol ase.
ACT 11:7 Toi ãre hodde ek abaz fuinni: 'Fitor, Fitor, uṭ, zora edde há'
ACT 11:8 "Ãi hoilam: 'No, No, Malik, ãi hono mote hái no faijjum, kiyollahoile ãi hono din hono napak, oforiškar no hái.'
ACT 11:9 "Kintu dusora bar asmanottu howa oiye: 'Allaye zinore paksaf goijje hinore tui napak no hois.'
ACT 11:10 Endilla tin bar oiye, toi bade hin beggun abar asmanot tuli loi za oiye.
ACT 11:11 "Ar hin deki mottor dekidde tinzon manuš, ãra ze górot aiššilam heṛe ai tiyaiyegai. Hitarare Sizeriya šohorottu defeṛa oil.
ACT 11:12 Hetunot Pak Ruhuye ãre hono andeša no ani hitarar fũwati zaito hoiye. Ei sozon báiyain itara o ãr fũwati gil. Bade ãrare ze ḍakito defeṛail he manušwar gõrot goillilam.
ACT 11:13 Hite ekzon firistare ki bafe hitar górot deha fail hin hite ãrare hoiye. He firistaye hitare hoil, 'Zaffa šohorot manuš defeṛai Simon, zare Fitor o ḍaka o, hitare ḍaki an.
ACT 11:14 Hite tor hãse kalam hoibode he kalamor duwara tui edde tor góror gušṭi ṭiyaye uddar faibo.'
ACT 11:15 "Bade ãi hota howa šuru goijjibar, Pak Ruh hitarar uwore aišše, zendilla foilar šurut ãrar uwore aiššil.
ACT 11:16 Hetunot ãttu Malikor hota monot foijje, zendilla hibaye hoil: 'Yahyaye fani loi torikotor gusol dito, kintu tũwarare he Pak Ruh loi torikotor gusol diya oibo.'
ACT 11:17 Allaye zehon hitarare o he hadiya diye ziyan ãra Malik Isa Mosir uwore biššaš ainnide hiya failam, henot ãi honnuwa ze Allare banda di fari?"
ACT 11:18 Hitara in okkol zehon fuinne, toi nizam oiye edde Allare tarif goriyore hodde: "Henoile to Allaye Oihudi okkolore o gunattu mon firaiyore zibonot aibolla šuzug diye."
ACT 11:19 Ehon Stifanore loi šuru oilde he zulumor zoriya biššaši okkol zara Fonikiya, Kiprus, edde Anṭiyok foijjonto sorai gilgoi, hitara šude Ihudi okkolore sara ar honokiyore kalam tobolig no gore.
ACT 11:20 Kintu hitarar butore Kiprus edde Kuronir hoekzon manuše Anṭiyokot zaiyore Oihudi okkolor hãse Isar babute kušir hóbor tobolig gora šuru goijje.
ACT 11:21 Ar Malikor hat hitarar uwore aššil edde bout manuš okkole biššaš ani Malikor mikka fijje.
ACT 11:22 Ei hóbor zehon Zeruzalemor zomator manuš okkolor hanot giye, hitara Barnabasore Anṭiyokot defeṛaiye.
ACT 11:23 Barnabas heṛe aiyore zehon Allar rahamote ki goijje hin deikke, hiba kuši oiye, edde hitarare tuwajjo diye zene hitara hitarar furafuri dil diyore Malikore dori take.
ACT 11:24 Barnabas ekzon bala manuš aššil edde hiba Pak Ruhuye edde biššaše furaiya aššil. Ar bout manuš okkolore Malikolla zitaiye.
ACT 11:25 Tarfore Barnabase Saulore tuwaibolla Toršišot giye.
ACT 11:26 Toi hibare tuwai faiyore Anṭiyokot ainne. Barnabas edde Saule ek bosor foijjonto zomator manuš okkol loi mille edde beši manuš okkolore šikka diye. Ei foilabar Anṭiyokor biššaši okkolore Kiristan hoi nam diye.
ACT 11:27 He ṭaimot hoekzon nobi okkol Zeruzalemottu Anṭiyokot aišše.
ACT 11:28 Hitarar butore Agab name ekzon uṛi tiyaiore Pak Ruhur duwara hodde, Rom raijjo agagurat ek ḍõr raṭ oibo. (Badša Klaudius šašonor ṭaimot he hota furon oil.)
ACT 11:29 Hetunot biššaši okkole bebosta goijje ze Ehudiya elehar biššaši báiboinain okkololla hitarar nizor šaiddo mozin modot faṭaibo.
ACT 11:30 Ar hitara he mozin goijje, Barnabas edde Saulor hatot Ehudiyar zomat okkolor murubbi okkolor hãse modot faṭaiye.
ACT 12:1 He šomot badša Herude zulum goribolla zomator hoekzon manušore dori annil.
ACT 12:2 Hite Yuhannar bái Yakubore toluwar loi kun gori felaiye.
ACT 12:3 Henot Ihudi okkole kuši oiyede deki hite abar giye edde Fitorore o doijje. In goiṭṭede iš adiya ruṭir idor šomot.
ACT 12:4 Hite Fitorore dori ziyol golai raikke. Ar Fitorore fahara dibolla sairzon sairzon gori šoinno okkolor uwore bar diya oiye. Herude ṭik goijjede uddar idor bade bisar goribolla Fitorore mainšor hãse niyolai anibo.
ACT 12:5 Hetolla Fitorore ziyolot bondi raka oil. Zomator manuš okkole kintu hiballa Allar hãse ekmone duwa goijje.
ACT 12:6 Ze din Herude bisar goribolla Fitorore niyolai anibo, hiyar agor raitta duizon šoinnor maze Fitor gum zai aššil. Hibare duiyan siyol loi bandi raka oil, ar faharadar okkole dorozat fahara dil.
ACT 12:7 So, hen šomot atikka Allar ek firista heṛe aiyore tiyaiyegai. Henot ziyolhanagan fohore ujjol oigiyegoi. Firistaye Fitoror gat zure ṭela diyore gumottu tuli diye edde hodde: "Toratori uṭ!" Henot Fitoror dui hatottu siyol kuli fori giyegoi.
ACT 12:8 Hetunot firistaye hodde: "Tor kĩyailot kiyail bandoni band edde šendal find," Fitore hen goijje. Bade firistaye hodde: "Tor saddor gat diyore ãr fise fise ai."
ACT 12:9 Henot Fitore niyoliyore firistar fise fise za šuru goijje. Kintu firistar duwara zin gora oiye, hin ze hãsa hin hibaye buzi no faijjil, bolke hibaye šoppon deker buli mone goijje.
ACT 12:10 Bade hitara foila edde dusora faharadar okkolor dolore ḍiyai zaiyore šohorot golede luwar dorozar hãse aišše. Dorozagan hitaralla onegane kuli giyegoi, ar hitara heṛe butottu di niyoli giyegoi. Hitara ekkan rasta bai, rasta hiyan furafan foijjonto giye. Ar hetunot firistawa atikka hibar hãsottu gayeb oigiyegoi.
ACT 12:11 Hetunot Fitore buzi fariyore hodde, "Ehon ãi buzilam, Malik nize firista defeṛaiye edde Herudor hatottu edde Ihudi okkolor har monor issattu ãre uddar goijje."
ACT 12:12 Ei babute buzi fariyore hibaye Yuhannar ma Moriyamor górot giye. Ei Yuhannare Mark hoi o ḍaka oito. He górot boute ekku fũwati dola oi munazat goijje.
ACT 12:13 Fitore battu tai doroza bajjaiye toi Ruda name ekzon goroni maya fuwaye doroza kuli dibolla aišše.
ACT 12:14 Fitoror abaz sini fariyore hibaye eto kuši oiye, doroza no kulite, dũri butore giye edde hoiye, ze Fitor dorozar hãse tiyai roiye!
ACT 12:15 Hetunot biššaši okkole he mayafuwaware hodde, "Tor mata horaf oiyede oibo." Kintu hibaye bar bar zurgori zehon hoiye hitara hodde, "Toile iba Fitoror firista."
ACT 12:16 Eṛe Fitore doroza baijjat roiye. Hetunot biššaši okkole doroza kuli Fitorore deki ammuwak oiye.
ACT 12:17 Fitore hitarare nizam oibolla hate išara goijje edde ziyolottu Malike hibare kengori niyolai ainne hiyan zanaiye. Toi Fitore hodde, "Tũwara ei hóbor Yakubore edde aro báiyain okkolore hoiyo," hen hoi hiba hentu niyoli oinno zagat giyegoi.
ACT 12:18 Binna sore šoinno okkolor maze uruskul oiye, Fitor hoṛe giyegoi hoi.
ACT 12:19 Herude Fitorore talaš goijje, kintu hibare tuwai zehon no fa, faharadar okkolore zera goijje edde hite hitarare mari felaibolla hokum diye. Tarfore Herude Ehudiyattu Sizeriya giye edde heṛe hoto din taikke.
ACT 12:20 Hešomot Herud Tiros edde Sidon šohoror manuš okkolor uwore guššaye oin oil. Ehon, heṛiyar manuš okkole ekkui fũwati miliyore Herud loi deha gorito gil. Blastos name ekzon badšar góror has hormosari loi hat goriyore hitara badšattu šanti saiye, kiyollahoile hitarar hánar zinišfati okkol he badšar dešottu itarar dešot aito.
ACT 12:21 Hẽtte ekdin Herude ekkan din ṭik goijje, hite hedin raz fušak findi šingašonot boiyore hitarare bašon diye.
ACT 12:22 Hitar hota funi manuš okkole guzoriyore hodde: "In oilde devotar abaz, manušor no!"
ACT 12:23 Hetunot atikka Mabudor ekzon firistaye hitare maijje, kiyollahoile hite Allare tarif no de. Hitar ga loge háiye edde morigiyegoi.
ACT 12:24 Kintu Allar kalam mummikka giye edde sairo mikka sorai gilgoi.
ACT 12:25 Ar Barnabas edde Saule Zeruzalemot hitarar šebar ham šeš gori bade, Yuhanna, zare Mark ho hibare fũwati loi hitara uwafes firi giyegoi.
ACT 13:1 Anṭiyok šohoror zomatot hoekzon nobi edde ustat aššil. Hitarar nam Barnabas, Simeon zare Niger o ḍaka oito, Kuroni šohoror Lukiyus, šašon goroya Herudor falok bái Manaen, edde Saul.
ACT 13:2 Hitara ruza rakiyore Mabudor ebadot goredde hetunot Pak Ruhuye hitarare hodde: "Barnabas edde Saulore ãi ze hamolla ḍaikki he hamolla hitarare aleda gori lo!"
ACT 13:3 Toi hitara ruza edde munazat gori bade he duizonor uwore hat raikke edde hitarare faṭaiye.
ACT 13:4 Ei dunizonore endilla gori Pak Ruhur duwara defeṛa oil, hitara dunizon Selebkiyat giye, hentu zahazot gori Kiprus ḍiyat aišše.
ACT 13:5 Hitara Salamit hazir oiyore Ihudi okkolor sinagogot Allar kalam tobolig goijje. Yuhanna o modot goroya hisabe hitarar fũwati aššil.
ACT 13:6 Hitara ḍiya gũṛa farai zaiyore šeše Pafosot hazir oiye. Heṛe hitara ekzon Ihudi zadugor edde bonḍo nobire lot faiye, zar nam Bar-Isa.
ACT 13:7 Hite aššilde šašon goroya Sergius Paulosor ekzon bondu, ar he šašon goroya manušwa aššil ekzon bala manuš. Sergius Paulose Allar kalam funibolla Barnabas edde Saulore ḍaikke.
ACT 13:8 Kintu Elymas, ze namor mani zadugor, hite Barnabas edde Saulore mana goijje ar hite sailde šašon goroyaye biššašottu muk firai felok.
ACT 13:9 Kintu Saul zare Paulos ho, hibaye Pak Ruhuye furaiya oiyore hitar mikka šuza saiyore
ACT 13:10 hodde: "Tui Šoitanor fuwa, zin bala hinor dušmon edde hár ḍoilla dúha edde sokkore furaiya, tui ki Malikor uzu fõtore behã gora no tamaibi ne ki?
ACT 13:11 Sa, tor uwore Allar gozob foijje. Tui anda oibi edde hoto din foijjonto beilor fohor no dekibi." Hetunot kuwa edde andare hitare guri felaiye, edde honokiye hitare hate dori loizai farefan hite ata šuru goijje.
ACT 13:12 In okkol deki he šašon goroyaye biššaš ainne. Kiyollahoile Malikor babute ze šikka hibaye faiye henot hiba tajjuf oiye.
ACT 13:13 Bade Paulos edde hibar fũwajja okkol Pafos sari zahazot gori Famfuliya elehar Forga šohorot giye. Heṛe Yuhannaye hitarare eri Zeruzalem firi giyegoi.
ACT 13:14 Bade hitara Forgattu Pisidiya elehar Anṭiyok šohorot giye edde dórmo din sinagogot goli zai boiššegoi.
ACT 13:15 Torah edde nobi okkolor kitabottu telewat goijja šeš oi bade muzolišhanar neta okkole hitarar hãse hoi defeṛaiyede: "Báiyain okkol! Manuš okkolore tuwajjo dibolla zodi hono hota take toile ho."
ACT 13:16 Hetunot Paulose uṛi tiyaiye edde hate išara gori hodde: "Israili okkol edde aro zara Allare ḍorode Oihudi manuš okkol, tũwara ãr hota funo!
ACT 13:17 Israil zatir Allaye ãrar bafdada okkolore basiloil. Hitara zẽtte Mišor dešot aššil hẽtte hitarare ek ḍõr zati goijjil. Bade Allaye ḍõr kudurutir duwara he dešottu hitarare niyolai ainnil.
ACT 13:18 Onumanik sališ bosorfan bošoti sara elehat hitarar oinnai bebar bordaš goriyore hitarar fũwati aššil.
ACT 13:19 Bade hibaye Kenanot hãt zatire furai felaiye. Ar Israil zatire he šomosto zatir dešore diye.
ACT 13:20 Endilla owat sair šo fõnzaš bosorfan haṛi giyegoi. Tarfore nobi Samuelor ṭaim foijjonto Allaye hoekzon bisarhar okkolore dil.
ACT 13:21 Tarfore manuš okkole ekzon badša sail hetolla Allaye Benjaminor bongšor ekzon manuš, Kišor fuwa Saulore hitaralla badša hisabe diye, ze sališ bosorfan raza aššil.
ACT 13:22 Tarfore Allaye hibare lari hitarar raza oibolla Daudore tuille, zar babute Allaye hoil, hiba oilde he Daud: 'Ãi Yasiror fuwa Daudore faiyi, hite ãr monor moto manuš, hite ãr šomosto issa falon goribo.'
ACT 13:23 "Allaye hibar wada hisabe ei manušwar bongšo okkolor butottu basailoya Isare Israili okkolor hãse hazir goijjil.
ACT 13:24 Isa aibar age har Israili okkolor hãse Yahyaye gunattu mon fira edde torikotor gusol tobolig goijje.
ACT 13:25 Ham šeš goribar šomot Yahyaye hodde: 'Ãi hiba no, tũwara ziba ãi oi boli mone goror. Kintu ãi bade en ekzon ze aiyer, ãi hibar zutar fita kuli dibar laikka o no.'
ACT 13:26 "Báiyain okkol, Ibrahimor bongšor manuš okkol edde allawala Oihudi manuš okkol, uddaror ei hóbor hiyan ãrar hãse faṭa oiye.
ACT 13:27 Zeruzalemor manuš okkole otóba hitarar neta okkole hiba honnuwa sini no fare, hitara hibare hosurbon goriyore, ze kalam okkol hitara fotti dórmo din telewat gorito he šob kalam furon goijje.
ACT 13:28 Ar moron šaza dibolla hono hosuri no fa, tarfore o kintu hitara Filator hãse dabi goijje, zene hibare mari fela o.
ACT 13:29 Ar hibar babute zin leka aššil hitara hin beggun furon goijje. Bade hitara hibare gasottu lamaiye edde ek hoborot rakkilgoi.
ACT 13:30 Kintu Allaye he mora okkolor butottu hibare zinda tuille.
ACT 13:31 Galilottu zara hibar fũwati Zeruzalemot aiššil hitarare hibaye bout din foijjonto deha diye. Ehon hitara manušor hãse hibar goba.
ACT 13:32 "Hetolla ãra tũwarar hãse he kušir hóbor tobolig gorir. Ãrar bafdada okkolore Allaye ze wada goijjil,
ACT 13:33 hiyan Allaye Isare uwafes zinda gori tuli, ãra zara hitarar bongšo okkol, hitarar hãse wada furon goijje, zendilla dui lombor zoburot o leka ase: "'Tui ãr fut, aziya, ãi tor baf oilam'
ACT 13:34 Allaye ze hibare morattu zinda goijje edde hibar ga ze ar hono din nošto no oibo, ei babute Allaye hor, "'Ãi Daudor hãse ze Paki edde haṭi duwar wada goijji, hin ãi tũwarare dium.'
ACT 13:35 Ar ek zagat hibaye hodde: "'Tui tor Paki zonore fõsito no dibi.'
ACT 13:36 "Daude hibar amolot, hiba ek zon Allar gulam aššil. Tarfore hiba mori giyoi edde hibar bafdada okkolor fũwati hibare hobor diya oil, ar hibar ga fõsi giyegoi.
ACT 13:37 Kintu Allaye zare morattu zinda tuille hibar ga no fõse.
ACT 13:38 "Hetolla oh ãr báiyain okkol! Tũwarattu iyan zana zoruri, ze Isar duwara gunattu maf faibar babute tũwarar hãse tobolig gora or.
ACT 13:39 Tũwara Musar ainor duwara gunar šazattu rehai fai no faro, kintu ze hono kiye Isar uwore biššaš ane hite gunar šazattu rehai fa.
ACT 13:40 Etolla tũwara hũšiyar o! Zene nobi okkole hoi giyede hen tũwarar uwore no goṭe:
ACT 13:41 "'Tũwara zara omainno goroya okkol, so edde ammuwak o edde dongšo o. Kiyollahoile tũwarar din okkolot ãi ekkan en ham goijjum. Zodi o he hamor hota honokiye tũwarare ho, hiyan biššaš no goriba.'"
ACT 13:42 Paulos edde Barnabas sinagog sari zargoide šomot, manuš okkole hitarare foriyad goijje, zene hitara sarmor baror dórmor din ei babute aro kissu ho.
ACT 13:43 Muzolišhanar šoba šeš oi bade bout Ihudi okkol edde Allar ḍorola Ihudi zat diyede manuš okkole hitarar fisa loiye. Paulos edde Barnabase hitarar loi hota hoiye edde hitarare tuwajjo diye zene hitara Allar rahamotor butore mojbut take.
ACT 13:44 Tarforor haftat dórmor din šohoror hár manuš okkol Allar kalam funibolla dola oiye.
ACT 13:45 Eto manušor zam oiyede dekiyore Ihudi okkole hingšaye zoli uiṭṭe. Ar Paulose zin tobolig goijjil hitara hinor berudde nanan ḍoilla hota okkol hoi hibare ninda gora šuru goijje.
ACT 13:46 Hetunot Paulos edde Barnabase šahoš loi hodde: "Allar kalam age ãrattu tũwarar hãse tobolig goron dorhar aššil. Kintu tũwara zehon hiyanore hela goror edde nizore akeri zibon faibar belaikka gori tulor, toile ãra Oihudi okkolor hãse zaiyum.
ACT 13:47 Kiyollahoile Mabude ãrare endilla hokum diye: "'Ãi oinno zati okkolor hãse tore fohoror ḍoil goijji, zene tui uddarore duniyair šeš šima foijjonto loizos.'"
ACT 13:48 Oihudi okkole ei hota okkol zẽtte fuinne hẽtte hitara kuši oiye edde Mabudor kalamor tarif goijje. Ar zarare akeri zibonolla basi lowa oil, hitara beggune biššaš goijje.
ACT 13:49 Mabudor kalam he elehar hár mikka sorai foijje.
ACT 13:50 Kintu Ihudi okkole Allar ḍorwala tuwangor mayafuwain okkol edde šohoror ḍai ḍõr manuš okkolore uskani diye. Endilla gori hitara Paulos edde Barnabasor uwore zulum goriyore he elehattu hitarare niyolai diye.
ACT 13:51 Hẽtte Paulos edde Barnabase he manuš okkolor berudde hitarar ṭengor dul zari felai Ikuniya šohorot giyegoi.
ACT 13:52 Kintu heṛiyar biššaši okkole kuši edde Pak Ruhuye furon oiye.
ACT 14:1 Tarfore Paulos edde Barnabas Ikuniya šohorot hitarar niyom mozin Ihudi sinagogot góille edde heṛe hitara endilla gori hota hoiye ze, ek dõr Ihudi edde Oihudi okkolor dole biššaš ainne.
ACT 14:2 Kintu ze Ihudi okkole biššaš nu ane hitara Oihudi okkolore Paulos edde Barnabasor berudde uskani diyore hitarar dilore tita gori tuille.
ACT 14:3 Tarfore o Paulos edde Barnabas bout din heṛe tai zaigoiyore šahoš edde Malikor uwore boroša raki tobolig goijje. Ar Malik nize hitarar duwara he keramot edde sinno okkol goṭabaiyore hibar rahamotor hotar goba diye.
ACT 14:4 Hiyanor zoriya šohoror manuš okkol dui bag oi giyegoi, ek dol Ihudi okkolor foikka, ar ek dol asab okkolor foikka loiye.
ACT 14:5 Oihudi edde Ihudi okkol, dui dole hitarar neta okkol loi mili Paulos edde Barnabasore ottisar goribolla edde fattor maribolla felain goijjede buzi faijje,
ACT 14:6 hitara Lukainiyar Lystra edde Dorbi šohorot edde heṛiyar ate hãsor zaga okkolot dai dai roiye.
ACT 14:7 Ar heṛe o hitara kušir hóbor tobolig goijje.
ACT 14:8 Lystra šohorot ekzon manuš boi takito, hitattu tiyaibar hono šokti nuwaššil, hite fodaši ãtur ze hono din nu ãṛe.
ACT 14:9 Hite Paulosor hota funnil, Paulose šuza hitar mikka saiye, ar dekedde hite aram oibolla hitattu biššaš ase.
ACT 14:10 Toi hitare zure ḍak maijje: "Tor ṭengor uwore bor di uzu oi tiya." Toi hite fal mari tiyaiye edde aṛa šuru goijje.
ACT 14:11 Paulose zin goijje hin manuš okkole Lukaniyo zubanot guzoriyore hodde, "Devota okkol manuš ruf loiyore ãrar hãse lami aišše."
ACT 14:12 Ar mainše Barnabasore Zaius nam diye, ar Paulos asol hota hoiya aššil buli hibar nam diye Harmes.
ACT 14:13 Zaius devotar mondir aššilde he šohoror baire. Šohor geiṛot dorozar sarme Zaius devotar mondiror imame hougguwa bolod goru edde fulor mala loi aiššiye, kiyollahoile he imam edde hár mainše Paulos edde Barnabasolla kurbani dito saiye.
ACT 14:14 Kintu asab Barnabas edde Paulose he hota zehon fuinne, hitara nizor hor faṛi dũri mainšor butore giye edde guzori hodde,
ACT 14:15 "Bondu okkol! Tũwara in kiyolla gorodde? Ãra o tũwarar ḍoilla insan. Ãra tũwarare ei kušir hóbor tobolig gorir zene tũwara ei šob abi zabi hamottu zinda Allar hãse firi aiyo, ze asman, zobin, duniyai, doriya edde hin butore za kissu ase beggunore sirišti goijje.
ACT 14:16 Agor din okkolot har zatire hibaye hitarar issa mozin solito diye.
ACT 14:17 Tarfore o kintu hibaye hamiša hiba nizor babute goba diye, asmanottu zór edde ainda mozin haiddo diyaiyore hibaye hibar doyare tũwarare dehaiye. Hibaye beša beši haiddo zuhai diyore tũwarar dilore kušiye borai tuille."
ACT 14:18 Ei hota okkol honor bade o, Paulos edde Barnabasolla zanuwar kurbani gorattu manuš okkolore tamaite beši hošto oiye.
ACT 14:19 Bade Anṭiyok edde Ikuniyattu hoekzon Ihudi ai Paulos edde Barnabas berudde manuš okkolore uskani diye. Henot mainše Paulosore fattor maijje edde hibare šohoror baire ṭani loigiye, kiyollahoile hitara mone goijje, hiba mori giyegoi.
ACT 14:20 Kintu biššaši okkol hibar sairo mikkattu dola oiye, bade hentu uṛi šohoror butore firi giye. Tarforor din hiba edde Barnabas Dorbi šohorot giyegoi.
ACT 14:21 Dorbi šohorot kušir hóbor tobolig goijje edde bout manuš okkolore biššaši goijje. Tarfore hitara uwafes Lystra, bade Ikuniya, bade hentu Anṭiyokot firi giyegoi.
ACT 14:22 Heṛe hitara biššaši okkolore dilot šokti edde boroša diye, biššaše mojbut takibolla, ar hodde: "Ãrattu bout duk hošṭor mazottu di Allar raijjot gola foribo."
ACT 14:23 Paulos edde Barnabase hitara fotti muzolišolla murubbi okkol tuille. Ar ruza edde duwa goijje, ar zara Malikore biššaš goijjil hitarare Mabudor hatot gosai diye.
ACT 14:24 Tarfore hitara Pisidiyar butottu di Famfuliya aišše.
ACT 14:25 Tarfore hitara Forgat maze Allar kalam tobolig gori bade hentu Attaliya giyegoi.
ACT 14:26 Bade Attaliyattu zahazot gori Anṭiyokot firi aišše, zeṛe hitarare ei hamolla Allar rahamotor hãse šebi diya oil, ziyan ehon gori šeš oiye.
ACT 14:27 Hitara zehon firi aišše, toi zomator beggunore ekottro goijje edde hitarare beggun hoiye, Allaye hitarar duwara ze ham okkol goijje edde kibafe Oihudi okkololla biššašor doroza kuli diye, he hota okkol hitarare kulasa gori zanaiye.
ACT 14:28 Bade hitara biššaši okkolor heṛe lamba ṭaim taikke.
ACT 15:1 Ho ekzon manuš Ehudiya elehattu lami nise Anṭiyok šohorot aiyore torikotor báiyain okkolore endilla hoi šikka diya šuru goijje: "Musar ain mozin tũwara azomi goraiya no oile, tũwara uddar oi no fariba."
ACT 15:2 Iyan loi hoijja oiye, Paulos edde Barnabasor loi ei manuš okkolor maze beša beši hota haṛa haṛi oiye. Toi hitara iyan ṭik goijje ze Paulos edde Barnabas, aro hoekzon šoho beggune uwore Zeruzalem zaibo edde heṛe asab okkol edde he murubbi okkol loi ei suwalor babute biyasana goribo.
ACT 15:3 Anṭiyokor zomate hitarare zaibolla bebosta gori diye. Toi hitara Fonikiya edde Sameriya bai zaibar šomot Paulos edde Barnabase Oihudi okkol ki bafe mon firaiye ei hóbor heṛe torikotor biššaši okkolore hoiye. Ar hitara hen funiyore beši kuši oiye.
ACT 15:4 Zehon hitara Zeruzalem fõisse, zomator mainše, murubbi okkole edde asab okkole hitarare kuši mone goisse. Hitarar duwara Allaye zin zin goijje hin beggun hitara beggunore zanaiye.
ACT 15:5 Kintu Foroši dolottu biššaši oilde hendilla hoekzon mainše tiyaiyore hodde: "Oihudi okkolottu hameka azomi gora foribo, ar Musar ain manefan hitarare hokum diya zok."
ACT 15:6 Toi asab okkol edde murubbi okkole ei babute biyasana goribolla ek zagat ottor oiye.
ACT 15:7 Bout hota haṛa haṛi gori bade Fitore uṛiyore hitarare hodde: "Báiyain okkol, tũwara to zano ze, bout din age tũwarar butottu Allaye ãre basi loiye, zene Oihudi okkole ãr mukottu kušir hóbor fune edde biššaš ane.
ACT 15:8 Ar Allaye har mainšor dilore zane, hibaye hitarar foikka goba diye ze ãra zendilla, hitarare o hendilla Pak Ruhure diya oiye.
