ACT 15:9 Hibaye ãra edde hitarar maze hono beš hom no rake, kiyollahoile hitara biššaš ainne boli hibaye hitarar dil o foriškar goijje.
ACT 15:10 Hen abostat maze, ãrar bafdada otóba ãra ze fũza boi no fari, he fũza Oihudi biššaši okkolor handor uwore tuli diyore kiyolla tũwara Allare forikka goribolla kušiš goror?
ACT 15:11 Ãra biššaš gori hitara zendilla hendilla ãra o ekkui bafe Malik Isar rahamotor duwara uddar faiyum."
ACT 15:12 Hetunot šobar beggune nizam oiye. Ar Paulos edde Barnabasor duwara Allaye Oihudi okkolor maze ze keramoti ham okkol goijje hin okkol hitarar mukottu fuinne.
ACT 15:13 Hitarar hota hoiya šeš oi bade Yakube hota hoiye, hodde, "Báiyain okkol funo!
ACT 15:14 Allaye hibar nizor bonda oibolla Oihudi okkolor butottu ek dol mainšore kengori basi loiye he babute Simeone ãrare buzail.
ACT 15:15 Ar ei hota nobi okkolor agam hóbor loi mil ase, zendilla kitabot leka ase:
ACT 15:16 "'Iyar bade ãi abar firi aiššum, Daudor fori taikkede gór uwafes tuliyum. Ziyan dongšo oigiyegoi, hiyan abar banaiyum, hiyan abar noya gori tuliyum.
ACT 15:17 Zene bad baki manuš okkole Mabudore tuwa, ar zeto Oihudi okkole ãr nam boi loizar, Mabud, zibaye ei šob ham gore hibaye ei hota hor,'
ACT 15:18 zin hibattu bout age loti zana.
ACT 15:19 "Hetolla ãr howa oilde Oihudi okkol zara Allar mikka fijje hitarare ãra iyan duk ofan gori no di.
ACT 15:20 Kintu ãra hitarar hãse endilla leki faṭaiyum, zene hitara mutti fũzar har hamottu edde zenar hamottu, ar gola sibi dori marifelai zandaror gusto edde lou hattu dure take.
ACT 15:21 Ei hokumgun diya bala oibo, kiyollahoile Musaye zin hoiye hin bout age loti fotti šohore šohore tobolig gora oiye. Ar zin zin hibaye leki giye hin fotti dórmo din sinagog okkolot telewat gora o."
ACT 15:22 Hetunot asab okkole, zomator murubbi okkole edde aro oinno manuš okkole endilla faisala loiye ze, hitara hoekzon manušore basi loi Paulos edde Barnabasor fũwati Anṭiyok šohorot defeṛaibo. Ehudah, zare Barsabbas hoito edde Silas, zara báiyain okkolor butore ijjotdar manuš, hitarare basona goijje.
ACT 15:23 Toi hitarar fũwati ei šeṛigan defeṛa oiye: Anṭiyok, Siriya edde Kilikiyar Oihudi biššaši báiyain okkol, tũwarare ãr Šalom.
ACT 15:24 Ãra fuinni ze ãrar butottu ho ekzone zaiyore, hitara bout ḍoilla hota hoiyore tũwarare bekub banaiye edde tũwara alabula oiyo. Kintu ãra hitarare hendilla hoibolla no defeṛai.
ACT 15:25 Hetolla ãra beggune ek oiyore ho ekzonore basi loi ãrar adoijja fũwajja Barnabas edde Paulusor fũwati tũwarar hãse hitarare defeṛair.
ACT 15:26 Ei dunizone ãrar Malik Isalla buli hitarar nizor zibonore morar fõtot lagai diye.
ACT 15:27 Ãra Ehudah edde Silasore o defeṛair zene ãra zin lekki hin tũwarare hitarar muke hoi fare.
ACT 15:28 Pak Ruhuye edde ãra iyan bala mone gorilam ze, ei ho ekkan beši dorhari ziniš sara ar hono oinno fũza tũwarar uwore tulidiya no o.
ACT 15:29 He dorhari zinišgun oilde: Tũwara devotar name kurbani goijjode hána no haiyo, lou, gola sibi dori mari felaiya zanuwaror gusto hattu edde beššagirittu dure tako. In okkolottu tũwarare dure rakile tũwarar balai oibo. Tũwarar šanti ok.
ACT 15:30 Toi hitarare defeṛaiye, hitara lamat Anṭiyokot aišše. Heṛe hitara zomator manuš okkolore ekottro goriyore he šeṛigan hitarare diye.
ACT 15:31 Hitara hiyan foijje edde hiyane ze tuwajjo diye hin loi beggune kuši oiye.
ACT 15:32 Ar Ehudah edde Silas, hitara nize o nobi hisabe, hitara o bout hota okkol hoiyore heṛiyar báiyain okkolore tuwajjo edde šokti diye.
ACT 15:33 Hitara kissu din heṛe taki bade, zara hitarare defeṛail, hitarar hãse firi zaiboilla báiyain okkolottu šanti gori bidai loiye.
ACT 15:35 Kintu Paulus edde Barnabas Anṭiyokot taigilgoi, zeṛe hitara edde aro bout manuš okkolore fũwati šikka dito edde kušir hóbor tobolig gorito.
ACT 15:36 Kissu din bade Paulose Barnabasore hodde: "Aiyo, ãra Malikor kalam tobolig goijjilamde he šohor okkolot torikotor báiboinain okkolor heṛe beraito zai, ar hitara ken ase saigoi."
ACT 15:37 Hetunot Barnabase Yuhanna, zare Mark ho, hibare fũwati loi zaito saiye.
ACT 15:38 Paulose kintu hibare fũwati loizare bala mone no gore, kiyollahoile Marke hitarare Famfuliyat eri hentu gilgoi. He oite hitarar fũwati ar ham no gore.
ACT 15:39 Hetunot hitarar butore mot omil oiye, hetolla hitara ekzone ekzon loi aleda oigilgoi. Barnabase Markore loi zahazot gori Kiprus ḍiyat giye,
ACT 15:40 kintu Paulose Silasore basi loiye. Ar báiyain okkole Paulus edde Silasore Mabudor rahamotor hatot tuli di bade hitara rowana diye.
ACT 15:41 Paulose Siriya edde Kilikiya di baisa diye, ar zomat okkolore aro mojbut goijje.
ACT 16:1 Bade Paulos Dorbi šohorot aišše, hentu Lystra šohorot giye. Ar so, heṛe Timoti name ekzon biššaši aššil. Hite aššilde ekzon biššaši Ihudi mayafuwar fuwa, ar baf aššilde Girik zat.
ACT 16:2 Lystra edde Ikuniyar biššaši báiboinain okkole Timotir babute bala nam gorito.
ACT 16:3 Paulose Timotire fũwati loi zaito sail buli hitare azomi goraiye, kiyollahoile heṛe ze Ihudi okkol takito hitara zanito Timotir baf ekzon Girik zatide hiyan.
ACT 16:4 Bade hitara šohore šohore giye edde Zeruzalemor asab okkol edde he murubbi okkole ze hokum okkol dil hitara hin manuš okkolore zanaiye. Ar he niyom okkol falon goitto hoiye.
ACT 16:5 Ei bafe zomator manuš okkol biššaše mojbut oiye edde hitarar dol din din bari za šuru goijje.
ACT 16:6 Pak Ruhuye hitarare Ešia dešot kalam tobolig gorito no de, hetolla hitara Forugiya edde Galatiya deš bai giye.
ACT 16:7 Hitara Mysiyar hãsa hãsi fõsi, hentu Bitúniya zaito kušiš goijje, kintu Isar Ruhuye hitarare zaito no de.
ACT 16:8 Toi hitara Mysiya bai lamat Troasot aišše.
ACT 16:9 Raitta Paulose ek deha fail, hibaye dekedde, ekzon Makeḍuniyar manuš aiyore tiyaiye edde foriyad gori ḍaki hodde: "Makeḍuniyat aiyore ãrare modot goro!"
ACT 16:10 Paulose ei deha fai bade ãra Makeḍuniyat zaibolla hehon tiyar oilam, kiyollahoile ãra buzi faijjilam ze Allaye ãrare heṛe kušir hóbor tobolig goribolla ḍaker.
ACT 16:11 Bade ãra doriyar fõte Troasottu uzu siri Samotrak, tarforor din Neofolisot fõsilam.
ACT 16:12 Henttu Filifit maze gilam, hiyan Makeḍuniyar he elehar mein šohor edde Romiyo okkolor koloni, he šohorot ãra hoddin takilam.
ACT 16:13 Ar dórmor din ãra šohoror baire doriyar farot gilam, ar ãra mone goijjilam heṛe munazator zaga ase. Ãra heṛe boilam edde heṛe ek dol mayafuwain dola oiyede hitara loi hota hoilam.
ACT 16:14 Ar hitarar butore Tuwatira šohoror Ludiya name ek allawala maya fuwa aššil. Hibaye baiyonna rongor horor beboša gorito. Hibaye ãrar hota funnil. Malike hibar dil kuli dil zene hibaye Paulosor hotat diyan de.
ACT 16:15 Hiba edde hibar góror manuš okkol beggune torikotor gusol loiye. Bade hibaye ãrare foriyad gori hodde: "Õnora zodi ãre Malikor name biššaši boli mone goro, toile ãr górot ai takogai." Ei hota hoiyore hibaye ãrare ata ati gori dori ṭani hibar gorot loigiye.
ACT 16:16 Ek din ãra he munazator zagat zaidde šomot, ekzon bandir loi deha oilam zattu ek ruh aššil, ziyan loi hibaye goni farito. Hibaye gonafora loi hibar malik okkololla beši ṭiya hamaiye.
ACT 16:17 Hibaye Paulos edde ãrar fise fise aiššil edde guzori hoil: "Ei manuš itara Šorbo šoktiwala Allar gulam okkol, itara tũwarare nazator fõt zanai dedde."
ACT 16:18 Hibaye bout din foijjonto endilla gorat takil. Kintu Paulose ar bordaš gori no fari muk firai he ruhure hodde: "Ãi Isa Mosir name hokum dir, hibar butottu niyoli zagoi." Henot hehon hiba hibattu niyoli giyegoi.
ACT 16:19 Kintu hibar malik okkole, lafor aša ar nai deki Paulos edde Silasore dori bazarot šorharor hãse ṭani loigiye.
ACT 16:20 Hitara itarare Romiyo bisarhar okkolor munttu loizaiyore hodde: "Ei manuš okkole ãrar šohorot beši gonḍogul sirišti gorer.
ACT 16:21 Itara Ihudi, ar ãra Romiyo. Ãrar riti niti mozin zin falon gora mana, itara hin tobolig gorer."
ACT 16:22 Henot oinno manuš okkole o hitarar berudde giye. Ar bisarhar okkole hitarar gar hoor siri felaito edde bet maribolla hokum diye.
ACT 16:23 Toi hitarare beša beši mar dor gori bade ziyolot golai eijje. Ar hitarare bala gori fahara dibolla ziyolarore hokum diye.
ACT 16:24 Endilla hokum faiyore ziyolare hitarare beši butoror kamerat loigiye edde kundat maze ṭeng ãṭkai eijje.
ACT 16:25 Kintu ada raitta Paulos edde Silas Allar hãse munazat edde šukuriya gan goijjil edde hodi okkole hin õl gori funnil.
ACT 16:26 Hetunot atikka ḍõr busal oil, en ki ziyolhanar meṛi udda hafi uṭṭil, ar hannasun šomosto doroza okkol kuligilgoi edde har hodi okkolor band kuligilgoi.
ACT 16:27 Henot ziyolar gumottu seton oil edde ziyolor dorozagun kula deki, toluwar loi hite hitar nizor zan nize loibolla bebosta loiye. Kiyollahoile hite hodi okkol dai giyegoi boli mone goijje.
ACT 16:28 Kintu Paulose guzori ḍak mari hodde, "Oh, nizor hoti no goris, kiyollahoile ãra beggun eṛe asi."
ACT 16:29 Hetunot he ziyolare serag ani hoi hite dũri butore giye, edde beša beši ḍore hafite hafite Paulos edde Silasor ṭengor sarme foijje.
ACT 16:30 Toi hite hitarare hentu baire niyolai ainne edde fusar goredde, "Sahab okkol, uddar faibolla ãttu ki gora foribo?"
ACT 16:31 Hitara zuwabe hodde, "Tũi Malik Isare biššaš goro, toi tũi edde tũwar gór ṭiyaye uddar faiba."
ACT 16:32 Bade hitara hitare edde hitar góror manuš beggunore Malikor kalam hoiye.
ACT 16:33 Ar he raitta ziyolare hitarare hitar fũwati loigiye edde hitarar haṛa sira gá okkolore duiye. Ar hite edde hitar góror manuš beggune hehon torikotor gusol loiye.
ACT 16:34 Tarfore ziyolare hitarare góror butore loigiye edde hitarar sarme hána fani ani diye. Hite edde góror manuš beggune Allare biššaš gori faijjede hiyanor uwore hitara beggune beši kuši oiye.
ACT 16:35 Bade din zehon oiye, bisarhar okkole ziyolaror hãse endilla hokum loi ofisar okkolore defeṛaiye: "Ei manuš okkolore erido."
ACT 16:36 Toi ziyolare ei hóbor Paulosore diyegoi edde hodde: "Bisarhar okkole õnorare eri dito hokum diye. Õnora ehon niyoli aiyo, aramor sãte zogoi."
ACT 16:37 Hetunot Paulose hodde: "Ãra Romor nagorik oi bade ãrar bisar no gori, beainna mainšor šaikkat ãrare bet mara oiye edde ziyolot diya oiye. Ar ehon ãrare gufone bair gori dito sadde neki? Hen oi no fare. Hitara nize aiyok edde ãrare bair gori loi zok."
ACT 16:38 Toi ofisar okkole ei hóbor bisarhar okkolore zanaiyegoi. Itara Romor nagorikde zani fariyore ḍoraiye.
ACT 16:39 Toi bisarhar okkole aiyore Paulos edde Silasottu maf saiye edde hitarare ziyolottu baire niyolai loigiye, ar šohor sari zaibolla foriyad goijje.
ACT 16:40 Hitara ziyolhanattu niyoli ai bade Ludiyar górot giye. Heṛe torikotor báiboinain okkol loi deha goijje edde hitarare tuwajjo di bade henttu giyegoi.
ACT 17:1 Bade hitara Amfipuli edde Apolloniyar mazottu faṛi zai Tessalonika šohorot aiššil, zeṛe ek Ihudi okkolor sinagog aššil.
ACT 17:2 Ar Paulose hibar niyom mozin sinagogot giye. Hendilla tin dórmor din fan hitarare kitabottu buzaiye.
ACT 17:3 Hibaye kitabottu mainšore forman diye ze Mosir moron edde mora okkolor butottu uwafes uṛa iyan hameka zorulot aššil. Hibaye hitarare hodde: "Ze Isar hota ãi tũwarar hãse tobolig gorir, hiba oilde he Mosi."
ACT 17:4 Henot ho ekzone hitarar hotat biššaš ainne edde Paulos edde Silasor fũwati zug oiye. Ar ek ḍõr Allar ḍorwala Girik manušor dole edde beš hoekzon zimmadar mayafuwainde o zug dil.
ACT 17:5 Kintu Ihudi okkole rag gori, bazarguwa hoekzon horaf manuš zomula goijjil edde šohorot gonḍogul bazai dil. Tarfore hitara Paulos edde Silasore tuwai bair gori manuš okkolor munttu anibolla Jaisonor górot hamela goijje.
ACT 17:6 Kintu hitarare tuwai no faiyore Jaison edde ho ek báiyore hitara šohor šasiyot goroyar hãse ṭani loi zaiyore guzori hodde: "Ei manuš okkole fura duniyaire utaltal goijje, ehon hitara eṛe hazir oiye,
ACT 17:7 ar Jaisone hitarare mehemandari gorer. Itara beggune Romor badša hokumor beruddota gorer edde Isa name ar ekzon badša ase boli hor."
ACT 17:8 Zehon ei šob hota okkol fuinne, manušor dol okkol edde šohoror šasiyot goroya okkol ũtari uiṭṭe.
ACT 17:9 Ar hitara Jaison edde oinno beggunottu zomanot loi zabine eri diye.
ACT 17:10 Bade raitta torikotor báiyain okkole Paulosore edde Silasore Beriyat faṭai dil. Hitara heṛe fõsi bade, Ihudi okkolor sinagogot giye.
ACT 17:11 Tessalonikar Ihudi okkolottuwaro Beriya šohoror Ihudi okkolor dil kula mela aššil. Hitara beši ajju loi Allar kalam fuinne edde hinore kobul goijje. Ar Paulose zin hoiye hin soiyi ne naki no saibolla fotti din hitara kitabot maze tuwai saito.
ACT 17:12 Hitarar butottu bout Ihudi okkole biššaš ainne, hendilla bout tuwangor Girik mayafuwain okkol edde manuš okkole o biššaš ainne.
ACT 17:13 Kintu Tessalonikar Ihudi okkole zehon zani faijje ze, Beriyat o Paulose Allar kalam tobolig gorer hetunot hitara heṛe aišše edde manuš okkolore uskani diyore gulmal bazai diye.
ACT 17:14 Henot torikotor báiyain okkole hehon Paulosore doriyar soror hãsat zaibolla faṭai diye. Kintu Silas edde Timoti Beriyat taki giyegoi.
ACT 17:15 Zara Paulosore fũwati loigiye hitara hibare Aten foijjonto ainne. Tarfore hitara uwafes aigiyegoi Silas edde Timotilla endilla hokum loi, tũwara zeto toratori šombob ãr hãse aizogoi.
ACT 17:16 Paulose Aten šohorot Silas edde Timotilla entezar goredde šomot dekedde he šohorgan mutti okkole boraiya, hen dekiyore hibar mon hošoṛi uiṭṭe.
ACT 17:17 Hibaye Muzolišhanat Ihudi okkol loi, Allar ḍorwala Girik okkol loi edde fotti din bazarot zai zara loi deha oito hitara loi hota hoito.
ACT 17:18 Toi Efikurian edde Sṭoiki dolor hoekzon fonḍite Paulos loi hotat baza bazi diye. Hitarar butottu ho ekzone hodde: "Ei hotabaze ki hoito sadde?" Kintu kiye kiye hodde: "Hite hono oinno devota okkolor hota zanaito sar oibo!" Kiyollahoile Paulose Isa edde uwafes zindar babute kušir hóbor tobolig goijjil.
ACT 17:19 Toi hitara hibare hitarar fũwati loigiye edde Eripagas šobar sarme hazir goijje. Hitara Paulosore fusar goijje, "Tũi ze noya šikka tobolig goror hin hon ḍoilla, ãra zani faijjum ne?
ACT 17:20 Kiyollahoile tũi ze en hodun hota hor zin ãra funi toddo oir. Ar hetolla ei šob hotar mani ki ãra zainto sai."
ACT 17:21 (Hitara ei hota hoiyede kiyollabuli hoile, Atenor bašinda okkol otóba bideši okkol zara heṛe takito hitara šude noya noya hota howa ba funa sara oinno hono kissut ṭaim borbat no goitto.)
ACT 17:22 Hetunot Paulose Eripagas šobat maze uṛi tiyaiye edde hodde: "Oh Atenor manuš okkol! Ãi dekir, tũwara har mikkattu beši dórmidar.
ACT 17:23 Kiyollahoile ãi guitto giyide šomot tũwarar fũzagór dekkilam. Ar en ugguwa devota zibar uwore leka ase, OZANA DEVOTAR MUTALLEK. Tũwara no zani zar fũza goror, hibar babute ãi tũwarar hãse tobolig gorirde.
ACT 17:24 Allah ze duniyai edde hiyanor butoror hár kissure tiyar goijje, hiba oilde asman zobinor Malik, hiba manušor hate banaiya fũza górot no take.
ACT 17:25 Hibattu hono obaf nai, hetolla manušor hatottu o šeba lowa hibattu dorhar nai, kiyollahoile hibaye hár manuš okkolore zibon edde foran ar oinno hár kissu diye.
ACT 17:26 Hibaye ekzon manušor duwara har zatire banaiye. Hibaye hitarare duniyair agagura bošobaš goitto diye. Hitara hõtte hoṛe bošobaš goribo hin o faisala gori diye.
ACT 17:27 Allaye iyan goijje zene manuš okkole hibare tuwa, zodi hitara tuwaite tuwaite hitara hibare tuwai fa. Asole hiba ãra honokiyor hãsottu dure no.
ACT 17:28 Kiyollahoile ãra hibar butore zinda asi edde solafira gorir, ar basi asi. Zendilla tũwarar hoekzon šaire o hoiye, 'Kiyollahoile ãra o hibar bongšodor.'
ACT 17:29 "Henoile ãra zehon Allar fuwain toile Allare manušor hat edde sinta šokti diyore tiyar goijja šuna rufa ba fattoror mutti ãrattu mone no gora foribo.
ACT 17:30 Agor mainše no zanito boli Allaye in okkol dekiyore hinore hosuri mone no gorito. Kintu ehon hibaye hár zagat mon firaibolla manuš okkolore hokum diye.
ACT 17:31 Kiyollahoile hibaye en ekkan din ṭik goijje ze din hiba nizor basona goijja he zonore diyore duniyair bisar goraibo. Ar he zonore morattu zinda tuliyore hár manuš okkolor hãse forman diye."
ACT 17:32 Morattu abar zinda uiṭṭe he hota funiyore hitara kiye kiye hãša hãši goijje, kintu ar oinnogune hodde, "Ei babute tũwar hota ãra abar hono šomot funium."
ACT 17:33 Hetunot Paulos he šoba sari giyegoi.
ACT 17:34 Kintu hoekzon manuše Paulos loi zug diye edde biššaš ainne. He biššaši okkolor butore Dionysios name Eripagas šobar ekzon, Damariš name ekzon maya fuwa, ar fũwati aro hoekzon.
ACT 18:1 Iyar bade Paulose Aten šohor sari Korontiyo šohorot giye.
ACT 18:2 Heṛe Akila name ekzon Ihudi manuš loi deha oiye. Pontus destrikot Akila zormo oil. Badša Klaudiuse har Ihudi okkolore Rom šohorottu zaitogoi hokum dil, hetolla kissu din age Akilaye hitar bou Priskillare loi Itali dešottu Korontiyo šohorot aigilgoi. Paulose hitarar heṛe giye.
ACT 18:3 Kiyollahoile Paulos o hitarar ḍoilla ṭambu banaoya aššil. Hibaye hitarar fũwati taki ham gora doijje.
ACT 18:4 Fotti dórmor din Paulose sinagogot Isar babute Ihudi okkolore edde Girik okkolore hota buzaito edde hitarare Isar uwore biššaš anibolla tagid gorito.
ACT 18:5 Silas edde Timoti zehon Makeḍoniyattu aišše, Paulose šude Allar kalam tobolig goitto, ar Isa Moside hiyan Ihudi okkolor hãse goba dito.
ACT 18:6 Kintu Ihudi okkole zehon Paulosor berudde hota hoi hibare ofoman gora šuru goijje, hetunot hitarar berudde Paulose hor zarifelai hodde, "Tũwarar louwor dai tũwara nizor matar uwore forok. Ei babute ãr hono dai nai. Ehonottu loti ãi Oihudi okkolor hãse zaiyum."
ACT 18:7 Toi Paulose sinagog sari Titius Zoštus name ekzon allawala manušor górot giye, zar górgan he sinagog loi bazaiya aššil.
ACT 18:8 Krispus name sinagog šasiyot goroya edde hitar fura góror gušṭi ṭiya beggune Malikor uwore biššaš ainne edde aro bout Korontiyo okkol, zara hibar hota fuinne hitara o biššaš ainne edde torikotor gusol loiye.
ACT 18:9 Ek raitta Malike Paulosore sopponot deha diyore hodde: "No ḍorais, bolke hota ho, suf no takis.
ACT 18:10 Ãi tor fũwati fũwati asi, honokiye tore sui no faribo otóba tor hoti gori no faribo, kiyollahoile ei šohorot ãr bout manuš ase."
ACT 18:11 Henot Paulos der bosor he šohorot takiyore manuš okkolore Allar kalam šikka diye.
ACT 18:12 Galliyo ze šomot Akaia destrikor šašon goroya oiye hẽtte Ihudi okkol beggune mili Paulosor berudde uiṭṭe edde hibare dori adalotot loigiye.
ACT 18:13 Hitara hodde, "Ei manušwaye endilla gori Allar ebadot goribolla uskani der ziyan ainor ulda."
ACT 18:14 Kintu Paulose muk kulibar agottu Gallioye Ihudi okkolore hodde: "Oh Ihudi okkol, iyan zodi hono oinnai ba beši ḍõr hosuri oito toile ãi tũwarar hota funa ãlla ṭik ham oito.
ACT 18:15 Kintu iyan zehon nam ba hota otóba tũwarar nizor ainor babute suwal, toile tũwara tũwara iyanor faisala gorogoi. Ãi endilla befarot ãi bisar goroya oito no sai."
ACT 18:16 Bade hite hitarare adalotottu lorai diye.
ACT 18:17 Tarfore manuš beggune miliyore sinagog šasiyot goroya Sostinesore dori loizai adalotor sarme mardor goijje. Gallioye kintu hin dekiyore o no dekefan gori taikke.
ACT 18:18 Bout hoto din Korontiyo šohorot haṛai bade Paulose torikotor báiyain okkolottu bidai loiye edde Akila edde Priskillar fũwati doriyar fõte Siriya dešot giye. Paulose manoš goijjil buli zahazot uṛibar age hibaye Kinšeriyat bondorot matar sul haṛi felail.
ACT 18:19 Tarfore hitara Efisus šohorot fõisse, zeṛe Paulose Akila edde Priskillare raikke. Kintu hiba nize sinagogot giye edde Ihudi okkolore loi Isar babute buzaiye.
ACT 18:20 Ar hitarar hãse aro hoto din zehon hibare takito hoiye, hibaye takibolla razi no o.
ACT 18:21 Kintu hitarar hãsottu bidai loiye edde hodde, "Iyan zodi Allar issa o toile ãi abar aiššum." Tarfore hibaye doriyar fõte Efisusottu giyegoi.
ACT 18:22 Paulose Sesariya šohorot fõsi zahazottu lamiyore Zeruzalem giye. Heṛe zomator manuš okkol loi mulahat oiye, bade Anṭiyok šohorot giyegoi.
ACT 18:23 Anṭiyok šohorot hoto din haṛai bade Paulose hentu baisa di Galatiya edde Forugiya destrikor ek zagattu ar ek zagat zai zai biššaši okkolore tuwajjo di di hitarare mojbut goijje.
ACT 18:24 Heṛe butore Apollo name ekzon Alekzanderiya šohoror Ihudi Efisusot aišše. Hiba ekzon bala wazi aššil, ar hibaye pak kitabore o bala gori buzito.
ACT 18:25 Hibaye Malikor fõtor babute šikka faiye, ar hibaye beši nizor ajju loi hota hoito edde Isar babute soiyi mote šikka dito. Kintu hibaye Yahyar torikotor gusol sara ar hono torikotor gusolor hota no zainto.
ACT 18:26 Hibaye beši šahoš loi sinagogot hota howa šuru goijje. Hetunot Priskilla edde Akilaye Apollor hota funi hibare hitarar górot dawat diye edde Allar rastar babute hibare aro bala gori buzai diye.
ACT 18:27 Bade Apollo zehon Akaia destrikot zaito saiye, torikotor báiyain okkole hibare tuwajjo diye edde heṛiyar torikotor báiyain okkole hibare gosefan ekkan šeṛi leikke. Ar Allar rahamote zara heṛe biššaši oil Apollo heṛe fõsiyore hitaralla hiba ek ḍõr modot oil,
ACT 18:28 kiyollahoile Isa ze Mosi hiyan pak kitabottu harot mozin lowa zade hendilla forman dehaiyore Apolloye himmot gori manuš okkolor sarme Ihudi okkolore ekkubare la zuwab gori felail.
ACT 19:1 Apollo Korontiyo šohorot aššilde šomot, Paulose he elehar butottu di zaiyore Efisusot aišše. Heṛe hibaye hoekzon biššaši loi dola oiye,
ACT 19:2 edde hitarare fusar goijje, "Tũwara biššaš ainnode hẽtte ki Pak Ruhure faila ne?" Hitara zuwab diye, "No, Pak Ruh asede hiyan udda ãra no funi."
ACT 19:3 Hibaye hodde, "Toile tũwara ki torikotor gusol loiyode?" Hitara zuwab diye, "Yahyar torikotor gusol."
ACT 19:4 Paulose hodde, "Yahyar torikotor gusol oilde gunattu mon firaibar torikotor gusol. Yahyaye mainšore hoil, ze hibar bade aibode hibare biššaš goribolla, hiba oilde Isa."
ACT 19:5 Ei hota funi he biššaši okkole Isar name torikotor gusol loiye.
ACT 19:6 Toi Paulose hitarar uwore hat raikke, toi Pak Ruh hitarar uwore aišše, ar hitara zilor baša hoiye edde nobi hisabe hota hoiye.
ACT 19:7 Hitara beggune onumanik barozon furuš manuš aššil.
ACT 19:8 Tarfore Paulose sinagogot giye edde tin maš foijjonto kub beši šahoš loi hota hoiye. Allar raijjor babute hibaye manuš okkolore buzaiye zene hitara biššaš ane, he kušiš gora šuru goijje.
ACT 19:9 Kintu hitarar butore ho ekzonor dil hora oigilgoi buli hitara biššaš nuane edde beggunor sarme Malikor rastar babute beši hingša gora doijje. Toi Paulose hentu giyegoi edde biššaši okkolore hitarattu aleda gori hibar fũwati loigiye, ar fotti din Tyrannuse šikka ditode he holl górot šikka diye.
ACT 19:10 Endilla dui bosor guzori zaigoi bade Ešia dešot bošobaš goroya Ihudi edde Girik okkol beggune Malikor kalam fuinne.
ACT 19:11 Allaye Paulosor duwara beši tajjuiffa keramoti ham okkol goijje,
ACT 19:12 enki Paulosor bebar goijja gamsa edde gar hor biyaraimma okkolor hãse loigile hitarar ošuk aram oi zaitogoi edde bod ruh niyoli zaitogoi.
ACT 19:13 Ar hozon sair goroya Ihudi boiddo okkole o bod ruhuye faiya manuš okkolor uwore Malik Isar nam bebar gori bod ruh dafaito kušiš goijje. Hitara hoito, "Paulose ze name tobolig gorer, he Isar name niyoli aibolla ãi tore hokum dir."
ACT 19:14 In okkol goittode Šikva name ekzon Ihudi okkolor ḍõr imamor hãt fute.
ACT 19:15 Ekdin he bod ruhuye zuwabe hodde, "Isare ãi sini, Paulosor babute ãi zani, kintu tũwara hontara?"
ACT 19:16 Hetunot ze manušware bute fail hite he hãtozonor uwore zafai foijje edde hitara beggunore endilla gori hamela goijje, hitara louwe touwe oi lenḍa abostat he górottu dai giyegoi.
ACT 19:17 Ei hóbor zehon Efisusor bašinda Ihudi edde Girik okkole zani faijje, hẽtte hitara beggunor butore ḍor góille, edde Malik Isar namore tarif goijje.
ACT 19:18 Zara Isar uwore biššaš ainne hitara boute aiyore kulasa bafe hitarar horaf hamor babute šikar goijje.
ACT 19:19 Ar zara zadu ṭuna gorito hitarar butottu boute aiyore nizor nizor kitab okkol ani ekku fũwati dola gori mainšor sarme hin furai difelaiye. Kitabgunor dam hisab gori deha giye ze beggune fõnzaš hazar rufar foiša.
ACT 19:20 Endilla gori Malikor kalam hár mikka sorai foijje edde hibar šokti mainšor dilot ham goijje.
ACT 19:21 Ei šob ham šeš oi bade Paulose ereda loiye ze hiba Makeḍoniya edde Akaia zaibo, toi hentu Zeruzalem zaibo. Hibaye hodde, "Heṛe zai bade ãttu Rom šohorot o zai sa foribo."
ACT 19:22 Bade hibaye Timoti edde Erastos name duizon hibar modot goroyare Makeḍoniyat defeṛaiye. Ar nize aro hoto din Ešia dešot roigilgoi.
ACT 19:23 Ar he šomot Isar rastar babute loi hotornak gonḍogul šuru oiye.
ACT 19:24 Dimitiri name ekzon bainnaye Artemis devir mondiror forma loi rufa di šoṛo šoṛo mondir okkol banaito, ar henot mistiri okkolottu o beši lab oito.
ACT 19:25 Dimitiriye he mistiri okkol edde hitarar ḍoilla harigor okkolor beggunore ek zagat ḍaikke edde hodde: "Báiyain okkol! Tũwara to zano ze ei bebošat ãrattu lab beši bala o.
ACT 19:26 Kintu tũwara dekor edde funor ze Paulos name ei manušwaye šude ãrar Efisus bašinda okkolore no, bolke Ešia dešor onumanik hár manuš okkolore buzaiyore ekin goraiye edde hitarare bul fõtot loizargoi. Hite ho ze manušor hator tiyar goijja dev devi okkol bole devota no.
ACT 19:27 Hetolla ehon šude iyan ḍor no o ze ãrar bebošar horaf nam oibo, kintu ãrar ḍõr devi Artemisor mondiror kimot o no takibo. Ar Ešia dešor hár manuš, enki duniyair har kiye ze ei devire fũza gore he devi o ar ḍõr no takibo."
ACT 19:28 Ei hota funiyore he manuš okkol guššaye oin oiye edde guzori howa šuru goijje: "Efisusor Artemis devi ḍõr."
ACT 19:29 Fũwati fura šohorot gonḍogul bazi giyegoi. Makeḍoniyar Gaiyus edde Aristarkos name duizon Paulosor fũwati gilde fũwajja manušore mainše doijje edde beggune fũwati dol bandiyore hitarare šobar maṛot loigiye.
ACT 19:30 Hetunot Paulos nize o mainšor dolor hãse zaibolla monša goijje, kintu biššaši okkole hibare zaito no de.
ACT 19:31 He dešor hoekzon raz hormosari loi Paulosor bondutai aššil. Hitara o hóbor defeṛaiye ze hibaye bifod matar uwore loi he šobar zagat no za.
ACT 19:32 Šobar butore manuš okkole kub uzora uzori ar genzam lagaiye. Bešir bag mainše no udda zanito kiyolla hitara heṛe dola oiye.
ACT 19:33 Ihudi okkole Alekzendarore mummikka ṭeli diye, bade dolor ho ekzone ki howa foribo hitare buzai diye. Hetunot hite hate išara goijje zene manuš nizam o edde hitar bottita fune.
ACT 19:34 Kintu mainše zehon zani faijje ze Alekzendar ekzon Ihudi, hetunot beggune ek abaze onumanik dui gonḍa foijjonto en hoi guzojje: "Efisusi okkolor Artemis devota beši ḍõr."
ACT 19:35 Šešottu, ekzon ḍõr šorkari šohor keraniye manuš okkolore nizam maraiyore hodde: "Efisusor manuš okkol, hosai, hon manuše no zane ze, ḍõr Artemisor mondirore edde asmanottu hiyanor mutti lami foijjede hibare sõloya oilde Efisus šohor de?
ACT 19:36 Ar ei soiyi hotare honokiye ošikar gori no faribo he hota zaniyore tũwara nizam taka dorhar edde bekufor ḍoil ham no gora zorulot.
ACT 19:37 Ei manuš dunizone ãrar mondire o luṭ no gore, ar ãrar ḍõr devir hono bod nam o no gore, tarfore o tũwara itarare dori eṛe ainno.
ACT 19:38 Hetolla funo, Dimitiri edde hitar bainna okkole zodi honokiyor berudde nališ goitto sa, toile adalot to kula ase, ãrattu heṛe šašon goroya okkol ase. Hitara heṛe zai moddima gori faribo.
ACT 19:39 Kintu tũwarattu zodi aro beši hono dabi dawa take, hin niyom mozin boiṛok boiyore faisala gora oibo.
ACT 19:40 Asole aijja genzam baijjede hiyanor babute ãrar uwore hosuri forit fare, ei gonḍugulor hono haron dehai no faijjum."
ACT 19:41 Ei hota hoi hite he šobagan bangi diye.
ACT 20:1 Gulmal tamizaigoi bade Paulose biššaši okkolore ḍakito defeṛaiye. Tarfore hitarare tuwajjo diye edde hitarattu bidai loi hiba Makeḍoniyar mikka baisa diye.
ACT 20:2 Makeḍoniya bai zaibar šomot Paulose bout hota okkol hoi manuš okkolore tuwajjo diye. Bade hiba Girik dešot aišše,
ACT 20:3 zeṛe hiba tin maš taikke. Tarfore hibaye hentu zahazot gori Siriya dešot zaito sar funi Ihudi okkole hibar berudde sail solaye, hetolla hibaye ṭik goijjil ze hiba Makeḍoniya bai uwafes firizaibogoi.
ACT 20:4 Modot goroya hisabe Beriya šohorottu Firosor fuwa Sopatros, Tessalonikattu Aristarkos edde Sekundus, Dorbittu Gaius, Timoti, edde Ešiyattu Tikiyos edde Trofimos hibar fũwati aššil.
ACT 20:5 Ei manuš okkole age Troas šohorot zai ãralla entezar goijjil.
ACT 20:6 Iš adiya ruṭir id bade ãra doriyar fõte Filifittu baisa šuru gorilam, ar fãs din bade Troasot hitarar loi dola oilam edde heṛe ãra hãt din takilam.
ACT 20:7 Haftar foila din ãra ekkui fũwati Isar ruṭi bangibolla dola oilam. Hẽtte Paulose hitara loi hota hoiye. Tarforor din hitara zaibar hota aššil buli Paulose ada raitta foijjonto hota howat aššil.
ACT 20:8 Ãra uworor ṭalat ze górot dola oilam heṛe bout beši serag okkol aššil.
ACT 20:9 Utuk name ekzon zuwan fuwaye he góror kirkirir uwore boi aššil. Paulose bout hotun dori hota hoil boli hite aste aste gumot fori gilgoi. Gum bári oiyede šomot hite tin ṭalar uwottu lamat fori giyegoi, hitare tuli loiyede šomot hite mora.
ACT 20:10 Hetunot Paulose nise lami giye edde he fuwawar uwore niyuriyore hitare sibi doijje edde hodde: "Tũwara no ḍoraiyo, hite basi ase!"
ACT 20:11 Tarfore Paulose abar uworor ṭalat zai Isar ruṭi bangi háiye edde raitta loti binna ofan foijjonto hota hoiye edde hiba henttu giyegoi.
ACT 20:12 Zuwan fuwaware hitara zinda górot loigiye edde beši šantona faiye.
ACT 20:13 Ãra agottu zai zahazot uṛi Assosor mikka baisa dilam, zentu Paulosore tuli loibar hota aššil. Hibare tuli loibolla ãra loi age hota ṭik aššil, kiyollahoile hiba aṛar fõte heṛe zat aššil.
ACT 20:14 Assosot ãrar loi hibaye deha oiye, bade ãra hibare zahazot tuli loilam edde Mitulanit ailam.
ACT 20:15 Tarfor din ãra hentu baisa di Kios ḍiyar ḍakaḍaikka fõsilam. Tarforor din ãra doriya farai Samos ḍiyat gilam. Iyar bado din ãra Miletusot fõsilam.
ACT 20:16 Ešiyat zene deri no o hiyanolla Paulose faisela loiye ze hiba Efisusot no oziyore zaiboi. Hibaye Zeruzalem fõsibolla zolti goijjil, zene šombob oile fõnzaš dinna idor dinot hiba heṛe hazir oi fare.
ACT 20:17 Paulose Miletusottu Efisusot manuš defeṛaiye heṛiyar zomator murubbi okkolore ḍakibolla.
ACT 20:18 Hitara heṛe zehon aišše Paulose hitarare hodde: "Ešia dešot ai bade foila din loti šob šome ãi tũwarar fũwati kene ṭaim haṛaiyi tũwara zano.
ACT 20:19 Ihudi okkolor bout ḍoilla dukor duwara ãttu entehanot fora foijje, tarfore o ãi kub šorol mone edde sukor fani loi Malikor šeba gorat roiyi.
ACT 20:20 Tũwarar modot ode hendilla hono kissu tũwarare no hoi ãi nizam no taki, bolke barkule kulasa bafe edde tũwarar góre góre šikka diyi edde tobolig goijji.
ACT 20:21 Ãi Ihudi edde Girik okkolor hãse goba diyi gunattu mon firai Allar mikka hitarattu fira foribo. Ar ãrar Malik Isar uwore biššaš ana foribo.
ACT 20:22 Ar so, ehon ãi Pak Ruhur hokume Zeruzalem zair. Heṛe ãr uwore ki goṭibo hin ãi no zani.
ACT 20:23 Ãi šude iyan zani, Pak Ruhuye fotti šohorot ãre ei hota zanaiye ze ãttu ziyol haṛa edde hošto fa foribo.
ACT 20:24 Kintu ãr foranor hono foruwa no gori, zodi ãi ei dũra šeš gori fari, mani Isaye ze hamor bar ãre diye hiyan šeš gori fari. He ham oilde Allar rahamotor kušir hóboror babute goba diya.
ACT 20:25 "Ehon ãi ei hota zani ze eto din tũwara zarar hãse ãi Allar raijjor babute tobolig goijji, hitarar honokiye ãre ar no dekiba.
ACT 20:26 Hetolla aijja, ãi tũwarare foriškar gori hoir, hono kiyor louwor daiyottu ãi halas.
ACT 20:27 Kiyollahoile Allah ki sar hiyan tũwarare zanaite ãi hono din fis fa no gori.
ACT 20:28 Tũwara nize edde he fura zakor babute hũšiyar taikko, ze zakor uwore Pak Ruhuye tũwarare dehafuna goroya goijje. Allar zomator soolsoroya o, ze zomatore hibaye hibar nizor lou diyore zitte.
ACT 20:29 Ãi zani ãi zailegoi bade bukalo genḍa bag okkol tũwarar butore aibo edde soolor zakor hoti goribo.
ACT 20:30 Enki, tũwarar nizor butottu manuš okkol uṛi Allar soyire misa banaibolla kušiš goribo, zene biššaši okkolore nizor dolor mikka ṭani loizai fare.
ACT 20:31 Etolla tũwara seton taikko. Monot raikko, tin bosor dori dine raite sukor fani loi ãi tũwara fottikiyore hũšiyar goijjilam, hono din suf gori no taki.
ACT 20:32 "Ar ehon ãi tũwarare Allah edde hibar rahamotor kalamor hãse šebi dilam, zine tũwarare gori tulibo edde Allar Paki bonda okkolor fũwati tũwarare miraz dibo.
ACT 20:33 Honokiyor šuna, rufa, otóba hor suworor uwore ãi lalsi no gori.
ACT 20:34 Tũwara nize zanode hota ze ãr ei dui hate ãr edde ar fũwajja okkolor obaf miṭaiye.
ACT 20:35 Ãi zin goijji hin hár kissu tũwarare dehaiyi, ze endilla dukkor mehennot goriyore ošohai okkolore modot gora dorhar. Ar ãrar Malik Isar ei hota ãrattu monot raka dorhar ze, 'Fattuwaro diyat maze aro beši rahamot ase.'"
ACT 20:36 Ei hota hoi bade Paulos beggunor fũwati ãṛu felai munazat goijje.
ACT 20:37 Bade beggune Paulosore gola sai berai dori hainde edde hibare suma diye.
ACT 20:38 Paulosor muk hitara ar no dekibo, has gori ei hotagan loi hitara beši šuk goijje. Bade hitara hibar fũwati fũwati zahazor heṛe foijjonto giye.
ACT 21:1 Efisus zomator murubbi okkolottu bidai loi ãra zahazot gori uzu Kus ḍiyat gilam. Tarfore Rudos ḍiyat ailam. Tarfore hentu Patara fõsilam.
ACT 21:2 Ar heṛe en ekkan zahaz failam, ziyan Fonikiya zaibo. Ãra he zahazot gori baisa dilam.
ACT 21:3 Bade Kiprus ḍiya dekilam, he ḍiyar doin ḍakottu felai Siriya dešot gilam. Toi ãra Tiros šohorot lamilam, zeṛe ãrar zahaze hiyanor malfottro lamaibar hota aššil.
ACT 21:4 Heṛe biššaši okkol lot faiyore ãra heṛe hãt din takkilam. Hitara Pak Ruhur duwara Paulosore foriyad goijje hiba zene Zeruzalem no za.
ACT 21:5 Ãra ei hãt din taki bade ãra baisa dilam. Hetunot hitara beggune, bou fut ziyain loi ãrare šohoror baire barai dito aišše. Heṛe ãra ãṛu felai duwa gori ekzone ekzonore bidai zanailam.
ACT 21:6 Ekzone ar ekzonor hãsottu bidai loi bade ãra uṛilam, ar hitara górot firi giyegoi.
ACT 21:7 Tiros šohorottu baisa di ãra Ptolemit fõsilam. Heṛe biššaši báiyain okkolore solam zanai bade hitarar fũwati heṛe ekdin takilam.
ACT 21:8 Tarforor din ãra baisa di Siriyat fõsilam edde kušir hóbor tobolig goroya Filipor górot takilam. Iba aššilde Zeruzalem zomator he hãt zoinna kušir hóbor tobolig goroyar butottu ekzon.
ACT 21:9 Hibattu sairzon abiyata mayafuwain aššil. Hitara manuš okkolor hãse nobi hisabe Allar kalam hoito.
ACT 21:10 Ãra heṛe bout hoto din taki bade Agab name ekzon nobi Ehudiyattu nise lami aišše.
ACT 21:11 Hibaye ãrar hãse aiyore Paulosor kiyailor zali kuli loiye, hiyan loi nizor hat ṭeng bandiyore hodde, "Pak Ruhuye hor, 'Zeruzalemor Ihudi okkole ei kiyailor zali iyan zar, he manušware endilla gori bandibo edde Oihudi okkolor hãse gosai dibo.'"
ACT 21:12 Ei hota funi ãra edde heṛiyar manuš okkole Paulosore Zeruzalemot no zaibolla foriyad goijji.
ACT 21:13 Hetunot Paulose zuwabe hodde, "Tũwara handiyore ãr monot kiyolla duk dor? Malik Isalla ãi šude Zeruzalemor hodi boinni de no, bolke moribolla o tiyar asi."
ACT 21:14 Hibare tamai no fari ãra šabbiš dilam edde hoilam: "Malikor issa furon ok."
ACT 21:15 Tarfore ãra ziniš fati gusai loi Zeruzalem gilam.
ACT 21:16 Ar Sesariyattu hoekzon biššaši okkol ãrar fũwati aiššil edde Mnason name ekzon Kiprus ḍiyar manušor górot ãra takibar hota aššil. Ite aššilde foila biššaši okkolor butottu ekzon.
ACT 21:17 Zeruzalem fõsi bade torikotor báiyain okkole ãrare kušir sãte goisse.
ACT 21:18 Tarforor din Paulose ãrar fũwati Yakubore saito gil. Heṛe zomator har murubbi okkol hazir aiššil.
ACT 21:19 Paulose hitarare solam diye edde hibar toboligor duwara Allaye ki bafe Oihudi okkolor butore ham goijje hin ekkan ekkan gori hitarare buzaiye.
ACT 21:20 Ei hota funi hitara beggune Allar tarif goijje edde Paulosore hodde: "Bái, tui to dehor, hoto hazar hazar Ihudi okkole biššaš ainne, ar hitara beggunottu Musar ain o falon goribolla kub beši ajju ase.
ACT 21:21 Hitara tor ei babute hóbor faiye, ze tui Oihudi okkolor butore ze forbaši Ihudi okkol take, hitarare Musar ain bad difelaibolla šikka dos. Tui hitarar morod fuwaindore azomi gora edde Ihudi okkolor soledde rosom falon no goribolla mana goros.
ACT 21:22 Hitara to hameka funibo ze tui eṛe aiššos. Ehon ãra ki goriyum?
ACT 21:23 Hetolla ehon tore ãra zen hoi tui hen gor. Ãrattu eṛe en sair zon manuš ase, zara manoš goijje.
ACT 21:24 Tui itarar fũwati zaiyore nizore pak saf gorgoi. Ar hitarar matar sul hamaibar horos dis. Toi henot beggune zanibo ze, tor babute hitara ze hóbor fail hin misa oi zaibogoi edde tui Musar ain manos.
ACT 21:25 Kintu Oihudi biššaši okkolor babute zendilla faisela goijji he babute ãra hitarar hãse lekilam ze, mutti okkololla kurbani diya gusto, lou, ar gola sibi marifelaiya hono zanuwaror gusto, beššagiri, in okkolottu hitara dure take."
ACT 21:26 Toi Paulose he manuš okkolore fũwati loi zai hitarar fũwati nizore o pak saf goijje. Tarforor din hiba dórmogórot giye. Ar hitarar pak saf oibar ham hõtte šeš oibo edde fotti zonolla hõtte kurbani diya oibo hin funai diye.
ACT 21:27 Ar he hãt din onumanik šeš oi giyegoide šomot Ešia dešottu hoekzon Ihudiye Paulosore Dórmogórot deikke. Hitara heṛiyar hár manuš okkolore uskani diye edde Paulosore doijje.
ACT 21:28 Bade hitara guzori howa šuru goijje, "Israili okkol, uzai aiyo! Har zagar manuš okkolor hãse, ãrar zati edde ãrar ain edde dórmogóror berudde ze šikka di guri bera, hite oilde ite. Hin bade o dórmogórot Girik okkolore ani ei pak zagare napak gorifeler."
ACT 21:29 (Hitara ei hota hoi fajjilde haron oilde, iyar age Efisusor Trofimusore Paulosor fũwati ei šohoror butore dekkil. Hetolla hitara ṭajjil ze Paulose Trofimusore dórmogórot o ainne.)
ACT 21:30 Hetunot gũṛa šohor utal tal oi uiṭṭe. Manuš okkol beggune ekku fũwati dũri aiyore Paulosore dori dórmogórottu ṭani bair gori ainne, edde hehon dórmogóror dorozagun bon gori diye.
ACT 21:31 Mainše Paulosore marifelaito saiye. En šomot Rom šoinno okkolor komonḍaror hãse hóbor giye, ze šara Zeruzalem šohorot gonḍogul šuru oiye.
ACT 21:32 He šoinno okkolor boroye hetunot hoekzon šoinno loi dũri zamor butore giye. Mainše šoinno okkolor boro edde šoinno okkolore deki Paulosore fiṛa bondo goijje.
ACT 21:33 Toi šoinno okkolor boro aiyore Paulosore bondi goijje, ar duiyan siyol loiyore hibare bandibolla hokum diye. Tarfore hite hiba honnuwa edde hibaye ki goijjede fusar goijje.
ACT 21:34 Hetunot dolor butottu hodune guzori endilla hor abar ar hodune oinno ḍoilla hor. Henot šoinno okkolor boroye gulmalor zoriya asol befargan zani no fare. Toi Paulosore berekot loi zaibolla hokum diye.
ACT 21:35 Paulos šeri foijjonto fõsi bade mainšor hatottu rehai faibolla šoinno okkolottu hibare bar gori boi loiza foijje.
ACT 21:36 Manuš okkol hibar fise fise guzori howa šuru goijje: "Itare marifelo!"
ACT 21:37 Šoinno okkole Paulosore berekot golaibo hen šomot Paulose šoinno okkolor borore hodde, "Ãi tũware ki kissu hoi fariyum ne?" Šoinno okkolor boroye hodde, "Tui dekir Girik baša zanos!
ACT 21:38 Toile ki tui he Mišor dešor hite no neki, ze iyar age larai goriyore sair hazar kunire fũwati loi bošoti sara elehat gilgoide?"
ACT 21:39 Hetunot Paulose hodde, "Ãi ekzon Ihudi, ãi Kilikiyar Tarsus šohoror bašinda, hiyan za ta šohor no. Meherbani gori foriyad gorir, õne ãre manuš okkol loi hota hoito ejazot do."
ACT 21:40 Paulose hiyan ejazot faiye, edde hibaye šerir uwore tiyaiyore hat tuli mainšore nizam oibolla išara goijje. Manuš okkol zehon nizam oiye, toi hibaye Ibroni zubanot hitarare hodde:
ACT 22:1 "Báiyain okkol, baf okkol, ehon ãi ãr nizor fokke hota hoi, funo"
ACT 22:2 Manuš okkole hibare Ibroni bašat hota hodde funi ekkubare nizam oi giyegoi. Hetunot Paulose hodde:
ACT 22:3 "Ãi ekzon Ihudi, Kilikiyar Tarsus šohorot ãr zormo, kintu ãi ei šohorot ḍõr oiyi. Ãi Gamlielor ṭengor ḍake boiyore ãrar bafdadar dinna ainor babute furafuri šikka faiyi. Tũwara zendilla Allar babute issawala hendilla ãi o issawala aššilam.
ACT 22:4 Isar ei fõtot zara solito hitarar uwore ãi beši mot foijjonto zulum goritam. Ar furuš fuwain edde mayafuwain okkolore dori ziyolot ditam.
ACT 22:5 Ei hota soiyide hiyanor goba oilde ḍõr imam edde dórmo komiṭir beggun, enki ãi itarar hãsottu Damaskusor dormiyo neta okkolore dibolla seṛi failam edde ei manuš okkolore dori ani Zeruzalemot šaza dibolla ãi heṛe gilam.
ACT 22:6 "Ṭaim onumanik dũijja, zẽtte ãi Damaskusor hãsa hãsi aišši, toi atikka ãr sairo ḍakottu asmanottu ekkan ujjol fohoror šoṛak foijjil.
ACT 22:7 Ãi meṛit fori gilamboi edde ar ãre hodde ek abaz fuinni, 'Saul, Saul, tui ãr uwore kiyolla zulum goror?'
ACT 22:8 "Ãi fusar gorilam, 'Malik õne honnuwa?' "Hibaye hodde, 'Ãi Nasarator Isa, zar uwore tui zulum goror.'
ACT 22:9 Zara ãr fũwati aššil hitara o he fohoror šoṛakore deikke, kintu ze ãr loi hota hoiye hibar hota hitara buzi no fare.
ACT 22:10 "'Malik, ãi ki goritam?'" hoi ãi fusar goijjilam. "Malike hoil,'Tui uṛi Damaskusot za. Tolla ziyan ṭik gori raka oiye hiyan heṛe tore howa oibo.'
ACT 22:11 Toi ãr fũwajja okkole ãre hate dori dori loigiye, kiyollahoile he ujjol fohoror šoṛake ãi anda oigilamboi.
ACT 22:12 "Toi heṛe Ananiyas name ekzon allawala edde Musar ain biššaši manuše ãre saito aiššil. Heṛiyar har Ihudi okkole hibare beši ijjot gorito.
ACT 22:13 Hibaye ãr ḍake aiyore tiyaiye edde hodde, 'Bái Saul, dor, tor sukor rošni firi aiyok' Ar hehon ãi hibare suke deki farilam.
ACT 22:14 "Toi hibaye hodde: 'Ãrar bafdadar Allaye tore basi loiye zene tui hibar issa zani faros, ar he niyaiwalare, mani Isa Mosir deha fos edde hibar mukottu hota funi faros.
ACT 22:15 Kiyollahoile tui zin deikkos edde fuinnos he babute har mainšor hãse hibar goba oibi.
ACT 22:16 Ehon tui kiyolla deri goror? Uṭ, torikotor gusol lo edde Isar name ḍakiyore tor gunare duifela.'
ACT 22:17 "Bade ãi Zeruzalem firi aiyore zehon ekdin dormogórot munazat goijjilam, hetunot ãi ek deha failam.
ACT 22:18 Ar dekidde Malike ãr loi hota hor. Hibaye ãre hodde: 'Toratori gor! Ehon tui Zeruzalem sari zagoi, kiyollahoile eṛiyar mainše ãr babute tor goba diya no funibo.'
ACT 22:19 "Ãi hoiyi, 'Malik, ei manuš okkole zane, zara tũwar uwore biššaš anito hitarare mardor gori ziyolot dibolla ãi ek muzolišhanattu ar ek sinagog okkolot zaitam.
ACT 22:20 Zẽtte tũwar goba doya Stifanore kun gora oil hẽtte ãi heṛe aššilam. Zara hibare kun goijjil ãi hitarar foikka aššilam edde hitarar hor sõllilam.'
ACT 22:21 "Toi Malike ãre hodde, 'Tui za, ãi tore dure Oihudi okkolor hãse defeṛair.' "
ACT 22:22 Manuš okkol etun foijjonto Paulosor hota funi aššil, kintu ehon hitara uzor di howa šuru goijje, "Itare duniyaittu dur goro! Ite zinda takibar laikka no!"
ACT 22:23 Hitara guzojje edde hitarar gar hor kuli mela maijje edde asmanor mikka dul ura šuru goijje.
ACT 22:24 Hetunot šoinno okkolor boroye Paulosore šoinno okkolor berekot loi zaibolla hokum diye. Hite Paulosore souk maribolla edde kiyolla manuš okkole Paulosor berudde guzora guzori gorer hiyan zera goribolla hokum diye.
ACT 22:25 Paulosore zehon souk maribolla bainde, hetunot heṛe ekzon ofisar tiyai aššil. Paulose hitare hodde, "Hosurbon ṭorai no faro de hendilla ekzon Romiyo mainšore souk mara iyan ki ain mozin or?"
ACT 22:26 Ei hota ofisare funiyore hite šoinno okkolor borore hodde, "Ei manušwa ekzon Romiyo nagorik."
ACT 22:27 Toi he šoinno okkolor boroye Paulosor hãse zaiyore hodde, "Sai hosai, tui ki Romiyo nagorik?" Paulose hodde, "Oi, ãi oi."
ACT 22:28 Šoinno okkolor boroye hodde, "Ãi nagorik oibolla ãttu beši ṭĩya diya foijje." Paulose hodde, "Kintu ãi zormo oiyi loti ekzon nagorik."
ACT 22:29 Ei hota funi zara hibare zera goijjil hitara hehon hentu šori giyegoi. Ar hiba ze Romiyo ei hota šoinno okkolor boroye buzi fariyore hite ḍoraiye.
ACT 22:30 Ihudi okkole Paulosore kiyolla hosurbon goijjil hiyan soiyi gori zanibolla saiye. Tarforor din šoinno okkolor boroye Paulosor ban kuli diye edde ḍõr imam okkol edde dórmo komiṭir manuš okkolore ekku fũwati dola oibolla hokum diye. Tarfore hite Paulosore loi ani hitarar sarme tiya goraiye.
ACT 23:1 Ar Paulos ḍõr šobar mikka šuza saiyore hodde, "Oh báiyain okkol, aijja foijjonto ãi har Allar hamot ãr zimmare hono suwal sara falon goijji."
ACT 23:2 Ei hota funiyore ḍõr imam Ananiyase Paulosor ḍake zara tiyai aššil hitarare Paulosor galot suwar maribolla hokum diye.
ACT 23:3 Hetunot Paulose Ananiyasore hodde, "Munafek, Allaye tũware o šasti dibo. Ain mozin bisar goribolla tũi o heṛe boiššo, kintu ãre maribolla hokum diyore to tũi nize ain bangor!"
ACT 23:4 Zara Paulosor ḍake tiyai aššil hitara Paulosore hodde, "Tui Allar ekzon ḍõr imamore ofoman goror!"
ACT 23:5 Hetunot Paulose hodde, "Báiyain okkol hiba ḍõr imamde hiyan to ãi no zanitam. Zodi zanitam toile ki ãi ei hota hoitam ne, kiyollahoile pak kitabot endilla leka ase: 'Tũwar zatir netar berudde bura hota no hoiyo.'"
ACT 23:6 Tarfore Paulose he ḍõr šobar ek dol ze Sadduki ar ek dol Foroši, ei hota zaniyore Paulose ḍõr šobat maze guzori hodde, "Ãr báiyain okkol, ãi ekzon Foroši edde forošir fuwa. Mora okkol uwafes zinda oibode hiyanore aša goijji boli ãttu bisarot tiya foijje."
ACT 23:7 Paulosor ei hotar zoriya Foroši edde Sadduki okkolor maze ek hoijja šuru oiye. Ar henot šobar manuš okkol dui bag oigiyegoi.
ACT 23:8 Kiyollahoile Sadduki okkole hodde, heṛe hono uwafes zinda nai, hono firista nai, heṛe hono ruh nai, kintu Foroši okkole in okkolore biššaš gore.
ACT 23:9 Henot heṛe beši gulmal šuru oiye. Foroši dolor hoekzon alem uṛi beši hora gori bara bari suru gori diye. Hitara hodde, "Ãra ei manušwar hono hosuri no fair. Oitfare hono ruh otóba hono firistaye itar loi hota hoiye."
ACT 23:10 He hoijja endilla doro oiye, šena okkolor komonḍare ḍoraiye ze hitara Paulosore siri ṭura ṭura gori felaibo, hetolla hite šena okkolore hokum diye zene hitara zai manuš okkolor hatottu Paulosore surai loi fuliš berekot loi ane.
ACT 23:11 Tarforor din raitta Malik Isa Paulosor ḍake tiyaiyore hodde, "Himmotwala o! Zeruzalemot zendilla tui ãr babute goba diyos, hendilla Rom šohorot o tottu ãr babute goba diya foribo."
ACT 23:12 Tarforor din binna sore Ihudi okkole ekkan sail goijje edde Paulosore hitara marifelai no fare foijjonto kissu no háibo hoi hosom háiye.
ACT 23:13 Sališzonottuwaro beši manuše ei sail goijje.
ACT 23:14 Hitara ḍõr imam edde murubbi okkolor hãse zai hodde, "Paulosore marifela no o foijjonto kissu no háiyum hoi ãra doro hosom háiyi.
ACT 23:15 Ehon tũwara edde ḍõr šobar manuš okkole aro bala gori zera goribolla hoi bahana dehai Paulosore tũwarar sarme anibolla šena okkolor komonḍaror hãse hóbor defeṛo. Hite eṛe fõsibar age ãra hitare furai felaibolla tiyar oi roiyi."
ACT 23:16 Kintu Paulosor boinor fuwaye ei sailor hóbor funiyore fuliš berekot giye edde Paulosore he hóbor hoiye.
ACT 23:17 Hetunot Paulose ekzon šenare ḍakiyore hodde, "Ei fuwaware komonḍaror hãse loi zo. Itattu hibar hãse kissu hoibar ase."
ACT 23:18 Toi hite hitare komonḍaror hãse loigiye.
ACT 23:19 Hetunot šena komonḍare he zuwan fuwawar hat sai dori ek ḍaikka loizai fusar goredde, "Tui ãre ki hoito sodde?"
ACT 23:20 He zuwan fuwawaye hodde: "Kissu Ihudiye Paulosor babute aro bala gori zera goribolla hoi bahana gori hibare aiyedde hailla ḍõr šobar sarme loi zaibolla õnor hãse foriyad goribo.
ACT 23:21 Õne hitarar hotat razi no oiyo, kiyollahoile sališzonottuwaro besi manuše Paulosor entezarot ase. Paulosore marifelai no fare foijjonto ei manuš okkole kissu no háibo hoi hosom háiye. Hitara ehon tiyar oi roiye, šude õne hitarar foriyadot razi oiba he entezarot ase."
ACT 23:22 Šena komonḍare he zuwan fuwaware zaito ejazot diye kintu endilla hũšiyari diye, "Ei hota ze tui ãr hãse zanaiyos hiyan honokiyore no hois!"
ACT 23:23 Šena komonḍare hitar duizon šenare ḍaki hodde, "Dui šot šoinno, hoittorzon gũrar suwari edde dui šot songinwala šoinno raitor nowa baze Sesariya zaibolla tiyar goro.
ACT 23:24 Ar Paulosolla o gũrar bebosta goro zene hitare o nirafodor sãte govarnar Feliksor hãse loiza za."
ACT 23:25 Bade komonḍare endilla ekkan šeṛi leikke:
ACT 23:26 Ãi, Klaudius Lysiyas, ḍõr ijjotwala govarnar Feliksor hãse. Ãr solam goisso.
ACT 23:27 Ihudi okkole ei manušware dori onumanik marifelaito sailde šomot ãi ãr soinno okkol loi zai hitare hentu uddar gori ainni, kiyollahoile ãi zani faijjilam ze hite ekzon Romiyo nagorik.
ACT 23:28 Bade ãi zainto sailam kiyolla hitara itare hosurbon gorer, hetolla hitarar ḍõr šobar hãse ãi itare loi gilam.
ACT 23:29 Ãi buzi faijjilam ze hitarar ainor hotabattara loi hitara itare hosurbon goijje, kintu moribar otóba ziyolot zaibar laikka hen hono hosuri ite no gore.
ACT 23:30 Ãi zehon zani farilam ze mainše ei manušwar berudde sail goijje, hiyanor zoriya hitare ãi õnor hãse defeṛailam. Zara hitare duši gorer hitarare o ãi hokum diyi zene hitara itar hosurir babute õnor hãse ho.
ACT 23:31 Toi soinno okkole šena komonḍaror hokum mozin Paulosore raitta hitarar fũwati Antipatris šohor foijjonto loigiye.
ACT 23:32 Tarfordin hitara gũrar suwari soinno okkolor fũwati Paulosore faṭai diyore hitara berekot firi aigiyegoi.
ACT 23:33 Gũrar suwari okkol Sesariyat fõsi bade šeṛigan edde Paulosore Govarnoror hatot diye.
ACT 23:34 Governore šeṛigan fori bade Paulos hon elehar manuš fusar goijje. Paulos ze Kilikiya elehar manuš hiyan zani fariyore
ACT 23:35 hite hodde, "Tore zara hosurbon goijje hitara eṛe fõsilegai ãi tor hota funiyum." Bade hite badša Herudor górot Paulosore fahara diyore sõi goribolla hokum diye.
ACT 24:1 Fãs din bade ḍõr imam Ananiyase hozon Ihudi murubbi edde Tertullus name ekzon ukilore loi Sesariyat giye. Ar Paulosor berudde govarnoror hãse nališ goijje.
ACT 24:2 Paulosore zehon ḍaki ana oiye, Tertulluse endilla hoi Paulosor keisore Feliksor sarme ainne: "Ijjotdar Feliks, õnor anḍare ãra bout din dori kub šantit asi. Õne õnor giyanor zoriya ei zatir bout unnoti goijjo.
ACT 24:3 Etolla ãra har šomot hár zagat õnore ãrar dilor butottu šukurana guzar gori.
ACT 24:4 Kintu beši hota hoi õnor šomoi nošto goitto no sai, ar hetolla foriyad gorir, õne meherbani gori hotun ãrar hotagun baiṭṭat funiba.
ACT 24:5 "Ãra dekir ei manušwa ek afod, šob šomoi hite gulmal gorat take. Šara duniyair Ihudi okkolor maze ite gulmal bazai de. Ite Nasaratiyo dolor neta.
ACT 24:6 Ar ite dórmogór foijjonto napak gorito kušiš goijje, hetolla ãra hitare doijji.
ACT 24:8 Ãra hitare ze šob hosuri dir, hin õne nize hitare zera gorile hár kissu zani fariba."
ACT 24:9 Ihudi okkole o fũwati hosuri diye edde hin soiyi boli hoiye.
ACT 24:10 Hetunot Governore Paulosore išara goijje hota hoibolla, toi Paulose hota howa šuru goijje: "Ãi zani, õne bout bosor dori ei Ihudi zatir bisar gori aiyor, hetolla ãi kuši oiyore nizor fokke hota hoir.
ACT 24:11 Aijja baro dinottuwaro beši no o, ãi ebadot goribolla Zeruzalem gilamde, zasai gorile õne hiyan asanir sãte zani fariba.
ACT 24:12 Ãre zara hosuri der hitara dórmogórot ãre honokiyore loi bosa bosi goridde no deke otóba sinagogot ba šohorot, oinno hono mikka manušore uskani diyide o no deke.
ACT 24:13 Ar ehon itara ze ãr berudde hosuri dehar hinor forman o hitara õnor hãse di no faribo.
ACT 24:14 Zen oibo ok, ei hota ãi šikar gorir, ze Isa Mosir fõt, ziyanore itara dórmo berudi fõt ho, ãi he fõtot ãr bafdada okkolor Allar ebadot gori. Kiyollahoile Torah edde Nobi okkolor kitabot za kissu leka ase ãi hin beggunore biššaš gori,
ACT 24:15 ar hitara zendilla aša gore ãttu o hendilla Allar uwore ei aša ase ze, soiyi otóba na soiyi beggunore morattu abar uwafes zinda gora oibo.
ACT 24:16 Hetolla ãi Allah edde manušor hãse hár šomot ãr biyasanare foriškar rakibolla kušiš gori.
ACT 24:17 "Bout bosor bade ãi Zeruzalem gilam zene ãi ãr zatir gorib manušore kissu ṭĩya foiša di fari edde zanuwar kurbani di fari.
ACT 24:18 Hitara ãre dórmogóror uṛanot lot failde he šomot, ãi nizore pak saf goijji, ar heṛe ãre loi mainšor hono genzam, gulmal hono kissu no o.
ACT 24:19 Kintu heṛe Ešia dešor hoekzon Ihudi aššil, hitarattu õnor hãse aiyon aššil. Ar ãr hono hosuri dibar takile, hitarattu diya forito.
ACT 24:20 Ar no oile eṛe zara hazir ase hitara hok, ãi zẽtte ḍõr šobar sarme tiya aššilam hẽtte ki hitara ãr hono hosuri fail.
ACT 24:21 Bolke ei ekkan hotar babute hitara ãre hosuri di fare, ze ãi hitarar sarme tiyaiyore guzori hoilam, 'Mora okkol abar zinda oi uṛibar babute loi aijja tũwarar sarme ãr bisar or.'"
ACT 24:22 Isar fõtor babute Felikse kub bala gori zanito. Hite bisar gora bon gori diyore hodde, "Šena komonḍar Lysiyas aile bade ãi tũwarar bisar šeš goriyum."
ACT 24:23 Hite Paulosore fahara dibolla ofisarore hokum diye, kintu hibare kissu azadi edde hibar hono nizor bondu bando okkole hibar šeba zotton gori farefan ezajot diye.
ACT 24:24 Ho ekdin bade Felikse hitar Ihudi bou Drusillare fũwati gori aišše. Hite Paulosore ḍakito defeṛaiye edde Paulosottu Mosir uwore biššašor hota okkol fuinne.
ACT 24:25 Paulose zehon soiyi bafe sola edde nizore sõli raka edde hãšoror bisaror dinor hota hoiye, hetunot Felikse ḍoraiye, edde hodde, "Tui ehon za, ṭaim mozin ãi tore abar ḍakium"
ACT 24:26 Hite aša goijjil Paulose hitare guš dibo. Hetolla bar bar Paulosore ḍakai ani hite hiba loi hota hoito de.
ACT 24:27 Dui bosor farai zaigoi bade Feliksor zagat Porkius Festus aišše. Feliks Ihudi okkolore kuši goribolla Paulosore ziyolhanat raki gilgoi.
ACT 25:1 Festus he elehat ai tin din bade Sesariyattu Zeruzalem giye.
ACT 25:2 Hetunot ḍõr imam okkol edde Ihudi leiḍar okkol hitar hãse zai Paulosor berudde nališ goijje.
ACT 25:3 Hitara Festusore foriyad goijje zene hite hitarar uwore doya gori Paulosore Zeruzalem fõsai de. Iyanor motolob oilde, hitara fõtot maze lukai takiyore Paulosore marifelaibar sail solail.
ACT 25:4 Kintu Festuse zuwabe hodde, "Paulosore Sesariyat bondi gori raka oiye, ar ãi o heṛe hara uwafes firi zaiumboi.
ACT 25:5 Tũwarar butottu zara leiḍar, hitara ãr fũwati aiyo, hite zodi hono hosuri gori take toile hiyanor berudde bisar do."
ACT 25:6 Festus hitarar heṛe ašṭo doš din taki bade hite Sesariyat uwafes firi giyegoi. Tarforor din hite adalotor siyarot boišše edde Paulosore hitar sarme anibolla hokum diye.
ACT 25:7 Paulos zehon hazir oiye, ze Ihudi okkol Zeruzalemottu aišše hitara sairo ḍakottu tiyai Paulosor berudde bout beši ḍoilla hosuri okkol diye, kintu hinor hono forman hitara di no fare.
ACT 25:8 Hetunot Paulose hibar nizor foikka ei hotagan hoiye: "Ãi Ihudi okkolor ain, dórmogór otóba Romor badšar berudde hono bul no gori."
ACT 25:9 Festuse Ihudi okkolore kuši goitto saiye, hite Paulosore hodde: "Ei mamelar bisar ãi Zeruzalemot goitto sair, tui heṛe zaito razi asos ne?"
ACT 25:10 Paulose zuwabe hodde: "Ãi ehon Romiyo adalotor sarme tiyat, ãr bisar eṛe gora ok. Ãi Ihudi okkolor hono oinnai no goride hiyan to õne bala gori zano.
ACT 25:11 To zodi ãi hono kissu goijjide hiyanolla hosurbon oi taki edde šazaye mout fai, toile ãi morite ošikar no gori. Kintu itara ãr uwore ze hosurigun diye hinot ei Ihudi okkol soiyi no, hetolla hitarar hatot ãre tuli dibolla honokiyor hok nai, ãi Romor badšar hãse afil gorir!"
ACT 25:12 Hetunot Festuse hitar mošora doya okkol loi mošora gori bade, hite hodde: "Tui badšar heṛe zehon afil goror, toile badša heṛe zaibi!"
ACT 25:13 Hoekdin bade badša Agrippa edde hitar boin Berenik, hitara Festusore solam zanaibolla Sesariyat aišše.
ACT 25:14 Hitara heṛe bout din takkil buli Festuse Paulosor babute badšar sarme boyan goijje. Hite hodde: "Filikse ekzon manuš ziyolot raki giyegoi.
ACT 25:15 Ãi zẽtte Zeruzalem gilam hẽtte ḍõr imam edde Ihudi leiḍar okkole endilla hoi ei manušwar berudde beši nališ zanail edde hitar šasti saiye.
ACT 25:16 "Ãi hitarare hoilam, hono manušor berudde zodi hono nališ gora o, toile zara nališ goijje hitarar sarme nizore hosuri sara forman goribar šuzug diya no o foijjonto hitare šasti diya hiyan Romiyo okkolor niyomot nai.
ACT 25:17 He Ihudi okkol ãr fũwati eṛe aišše bade ãi deri no gori tarforor din bisarot boiššilam edde he manušware ḍakai anibolla hokum dilam.
ACT 25:18 Ze manuš okkole hitare hosuri dil hitara zehon hota hoibolla uṛi tiyaiye hẽtte ãi zendilla baffilam hendilla hono nališ hitara no gore.
ACT 25:19 Bolke hitarar dórmo mozin edde Isa hoi ekzon mora manušor babute loi adalotot nališ goijje. Paulos name he manušwaye dabi goijje, ze he Isa zinda ase.
ACT 25:20 Ei mamelar zasai basai kengori goriyum hin buzi no fari ãi fusar goijjilam, ei šob mamelar bisar gora ofan hite Zeruzalem zaibolla razi ase ne nai.
ACT 25:21 Kintu hite zehon Romor badšar raiolla entezar gori ãr hãse afil goijje, hetunot Romor badšar hãse no defeṛai foijjonto hitare fahar di rakibolla ãi hokum diyi."
ACT 25:22 Toi Agrippaye Festusore hodde, "Ãi nize ei manušwar hota funibolla sai." Festuse hodde, "Hitar hota tũi hailla funi fariba."
ACT 25:23 Tarforor din badša Agrippa edde Berenik, šoinno okkolor ḍõr ofisar edde šohoror mein mein manuš okkolore loi beši zakzomok loi šoba góror butore góille. Festusor hokume Paulosore heṛe ana oiye.
ACT 25:24 Hetunot Festuse hodde: "Badša Agrippa edde aro zara eṛe hazir aso, tũwara ei manušware dekor, har Ihudi okkole Zeruzalemot edde Sesariyat ãr hãse afil goijje edde guzori hoiye, ze ei manušwa ar basi takon no sa.
ACT 25:25 Kintu ãi dekilam, ze moron šasti faibar laikka hono hosuri hite no gore. Tarfore o zehon hite Romor badšar hãse afil goijje hetunot ãi o hitare Romor badšar hãse defeṛaiyum ṭik gorilam.
ACT 25:26 Kintu badšar hãse lekifarifan en hono soiyi hosuri kissu no failam. Hetolla ãi tũwara beggunor sarme, has gori badša Agrippa, tũwar sarme hitare ainni zene hitare zera gori homse hom kissu ãi leki fari.
ACT 25:27 Kiyollahoile ãr mote hono bondire salan dibar šomot hitar hosurigun o zana dorhar."
ACT 26:1 Agrippaye Paulosore hodde, "Tor nizor fokke hota hoibolla tore ejazot diya giye." Hetunot Paulose hat barai diyore nizor fokke ei hota hoiye,
ACT 26:2 "Oh badša Agrippa, Ihudi okkole ãre ze hosuri diye hinor berudde õnor sarme aijja ãi nizor fokke hota hoibar šuzug faiyore ãi nizore baggitta mone gorir,
ACT 26:3 has gori zehon Ihudi okkolor soledde niyom edde hitarar barabarir babute õnottu bala gori zana ase. Hetolla doijjo dori ãr hotagun funibolla ãi õnore meherbani gori foriyad gorir.
ACT 26:4 "Ihudi manuš okkol beggune zane, šoṛo hale loti ãr nizor dešor manuš okkol edde bade Zeruzalemor manuš okkole zane ãi ki bafe zibon haṛaiyi.
ACT 26:5 Hitara ãre bout din dori sine. Ar hitara issa gorile goba o di faribo, ze ãrar dórmiyo Foroši name ze hora dol ase, ãi he Foroši zibon haṛaiyi.
ACT 26:6 Ar ehon Allaye ãrar bafdada okkolor hãse ze wada goijjil hinor uwore aša goijji buli ãr bisar or.
ACT 26:7 Ãrar baro bongšor manuš okkole dine raite zan foran diyore Allar ebadot goijjede hisabe he wada furon oiya dekibolla he ašat ase. Badša sahab, ei ašar zoriya Ihudi okkole ãre hosurbon gorer.
ACT 26:8 Allaye morare zinda tuillede ei hota kiyolla tũwara honokiye iyanore biššaš lagede hendilla mone no goror?
ACT 26:9 "Ãi nize o mone goritam ze Nasarator Isar namor berudde zen zen gora za hin beggun ãttu o gora dorhar buli.
ACT 26:10 Ar ṭik hen ãi Zeruzalemot goijjilam. Ḍõr imamottu kemota faiyore ãi bout Isar uwore biššaši okkolore ziyolot ditam edde hitarare marifelaibar šomot hitarar berudde boṭ ditam.
ACT 26:11 Hitarare šasti dibolla ãi har sinagog okkolot zaitam ar Isar berudde hoibolla ãi hitarare zur goritam. Hitarar uwore ãttu eto rag aššil ze hitarare zulum goribolla ãi bidešor šohor okkolot foijjonto zaitam.
ACT 26:12 "Endilla ek bar ḍõr imamor hãsottu kemota edde hokum loi ãi Damaskus zair.
ACT 26:13 Badša sahab, hẽtte ṭaim onumanik dũijja, fõtot maze beilottuwaro ujjol ekkan fohor asmanottu ãi edde ãr fũwajja okkolor sairo ḍakottu zola šuru goijje.
ACT 26:14 Ãra beggune meṛit fori gilamboi. Ar Ibroni bašat ãre hodde ek abaz funni, 'Saul, Saul, tui ãr uwore kiyolla zulum goror? Keṛa buwaiya laṛir mukot lati mariyore ki tui tor nizor hoti no goror ne?'
ACT 26:15 "Hetunot ãi fusar goridde, "Malik, õne honnuwa?"
ACT 26:16 "Malike hodde, 'Ãi Isa, zar uwore tui zulum goror. Ehon uṭ, tor ṭengot bor diyore tiya. Šeba goroya edde goba doya hisabe tore loibolla ãi deha diyi, zin tui ãttu deikkos edde zin ãi tore dehaiyum he babute goba dibi.
ACT 26:17 Tor nizor manuš okkol edde Oihudi okkolor hatottu ãi tore uddar goriyum. Ãi tore hitarar heṛe defeṛair,
ACT 26:18 hitarar suk kuli dibolla edde andarottu fohorot, edde Šoitanor dokolottu Allar hãse firai anibolla, zene ãr uwore biššaš anonor zoriya hitara guna maf fa edde zarare Paki gora oiye hitarar butore itarar zaga o.'
ACT 26:19 "Etolla badša Agrippa, behostottu ze deha diye ãi hiyanor obaiddo no oi.
ACT 26:20 Zara Damaskusot ase foila hitarar hãse, tarfore zara Zeruzalemot edde fura Ehudiya elehat ase, hitarar hãse edde tarfore Oihudi okkolor hãse ãi tobolig goijji, ze hitarattu gunattu mon firai Allar mikka firon sa, edde hitarar haz harbare forman fa za ze hitara gunattu mon firaiye.
ACT 26:21 Etolla Ihudi okkole ãre dórmogóror butore dori marifelaito kušiš goijje.
ACT 26:22 Kintu Allaye ãre aijja foijjonto modot gori aiyer. Ar hetolla ãi eṛe tiyaiyore šoṛo ḍõr beggunor hãse goba dir. Nobi okkol edde Musaye zin goṭibo hoi giye hinor baire ãi hono kissu no hoir.
ACT 26:23 He hota oilde endilla, Mosittu duk šowa foribo edde hiba he foila zon ze morattu zinda uṛi zaiboi, hibar nizor zatir manuš okkolor hãse edde Oihudi okkolor hãse nuror hóbor gušona goribo."
ACT 26:24 Paulose endilla gori nizor foikka hota hodde ṭaimot Festuse hoito no diyore guzori hodde, "Paulos, tui fol oi giyosgoi. Tui beši fonna foijjosde hine tore fol banai felaiye."
ACT 26:25 Hetunot Paulose hodde: "Ijjotdar Festus, ãi fol no, ãi zin hoir hin soiyi edde lowazade hota.
ACT 26:26 Badšaye to ei babute zane. Ãi hibar loi kulasa gori har hota hoi fariyum. Ar ãi iyano zani, ze in okkolor hono kissu hibar sukor arguwale no fore, kiyollahoile ei goṭona okkol to gufone no o.
ACT 26:27 Badša Agrippa, õne ki nobi okkolor hota biššaš goro? Ãi zani õne goro."
ACT 26:28 Hetunot Agrippaye Paulosore hodde, "Tui ki eto baiṭṭa ṭaimot maze ãre Isayi banaibolla kušiš goror?"
ACT 26:29 Paulose hodde, "Ṭaim baṛi otóba lamba, ãi šude tũwalla duwa no gorir bolke beggunolla, zara aijja ãr hota fuinne hitara beggune zen ãr ḍoilla o, ei siyolgan sara."
ACT 26:30 Hetunot badša uiṭṭiye, hitar fũwati govarnar Festus edde Berenik, edde zara hitarar fũwati boiššil hitara beggun uṛi tiyaiye.
ACT 26:31 Tarfore hitara he górottu giyegoi edde ekzone ekzonore howa hoi šuru goijje,"Ei manušwaye moron šaza ba ziyol haṛibar laikka hono kissu no gore."
ACT 26:32 Agrippaye Festusore hodde, "Ei manušwaye zodi Romor badšar hãse afil no gorito, toile hitare eridiya zaito."
ACT 27:1 Zahazot gori ãrare Itali loi za oibo hiyan zehon faisela gora oiye, Paulos edde aro hoekzon ziyolor hodire Julius name ek ofisaror hatot diya oiye. Julius aššilde Romor badšar nizor soinno dolor ekzon ofisar.
ACT 27:2 Ãra Adramuttiumottu aiyedde ekkan zahazot uṛi baisa šuru gorilam, ze zahazsan Ešiar bout bondor okkolot zaibo. Ãrar fũwati Makeḍoniya elehar Tessalonika šohoror Arištak o aššil.
ACT 27:3 Ãrar zahaz tarforor din Sidonot taimme. Juliuse Paulosore beši bondutai dehaiye edde hibare hibar bondu okkolor hãse zaibolla ejazot diye zene Paulosor bondu okkole hibare dorhari zinišfati di fare.
ACT 27:4 Bade hentu abar ãra zahaz sarilam. Bataš ãrar ulda mikkattu baiye boli ãra Kiprus ḍiyar bataš nu aššilde he mikkattu gilam.
ACT 27:5 Tarfore ãra Kilikiya edde Famfuliyar sarmottu ze doriya ase, hiyan faraiyore Lukiya elehar Mura šohorot fõsilamboi.
ACT 27:6 Heṛe ofisarguwaye ekkan zahaz Alekzanderiyattu Itali zadde deha faiyore ãrare he zahazot tuli diye.
ACT 27:7 Ãrar zahazsan bout din dori aste aste soille, ar beši hošṭo bišṭo gori Knidos šohoror hãsa hãsi fõssi, kintu bataše ãrare ar mummikka zaito no de. Hetunot ãra Kreta ḍiyar ze ḍakottu bataš nu aššil he ḍaikkar Salomona bai sola šuru gorilam.
ACT 27:8 Doriyar kinaror hãsa hãsa beši hošṭo bišṭo gori solaiyore ãra en ek zagat aišši ziyanore Šundor Bondor boli ho, hiyan oiyede Lasea šohoror ḍake.
ACT 27:9 Endilla bout din haṛi giyegoi. Hẽtte ruzar din šeš oi zaiyore šithal onumanik aigiyegoi. Hetolla zahazot gori za ekkan ḍõr moškil ham oiye. Hiyanolla buli Paulose zahazor manuš okkolore hũšiyari di hoiye,
ACT 27:10 "So, ãi dekir ãrar ei baisat kub beši hoti oibo. Ei hoti ze šude zahaz edde mal fottror oibo hen to no, bolke ãrar zanor uwore o hoti oibo."
ACT 27:11 Kintu ofisare Paulosor hota no funiyore zahazor kepṭin edde zahazor malikor hota fuinne.
ACT 27:12 Ar bondorgan šit hal haṛaibar laikka zaga no boli, beši bag mainše faisela goijje ze, hentu baisa diyore šombob oile Foniksot zai šit hal haṛa oibo. Foniks aššilde Kreta ḍiyar zahaz tamede zaga. Ei zagagan doin fosim edde uttor fosim ḍakor muk kula aššil.
ACT 27:13 Bade zehon doinali bataš halka halka ba šuru goijje, hetunot hitara mone goijje, hitara zen saiye hen faiye, hetolla hitara zahazor nogol tuli loi Kreta ḍiyar hãsa hãsa sola šuru goijje.
ACT 27:14 Kintu ekka gori bade he ḍiyattu Urakul name ek beši ḍõr tuwan šuru oiye.
ACT 27:15 Bade zahazsan he tuwanot foijje edde batašolla boli ar ãra mummikka zai no farilam. Toi ãra mummikka zaibar kušiš saridiyore zahazganore bataše baši zaito dilam.
ACT 27:16 Bade Kaudo name ugguwa šoṛo ḍiya, hibar ze ḍakottu bataš nu aššil he ḍakottu ãra za šuru gorilam. Ar zahazot foran basaibar ze gura no take, hiyan beši duk gori ãra dongšor hatottu basailam.
ACT 27:17 Manuš okkole nogan zahazor uwore ṭani tuille. Bade dori loi zahazor kúl sai bainde zene hiyanor tottagun aleda oi no zagoi. Syrtis name doriyar sorot zahaz bazi zaiboi ḍore šor nise lamai felaiyore zahazganore bataše solito diye.
ACT 27:18 Tuwan beši zur onor zoriya ãrar zahazsan endilla ḍula šuru goijje, tarforor din mainše zahazor malfottro okkol felai diya šuru goijje.
ACT 27:19 Tin dinor din hitara nizor hate zahazor sai samana hãtiyar okkol felai diye.
ACT 27:20 Bout din dori beil otóba tara kissu deha no za edde beša beši tuwan bat roiye. Šeše ãra foran basai faribar har aša sari dilam.
ACT 27:21 Manuš okkole bout din dori hono kissu no há boli Paulose hitarar munttu tiyaiyore hodde: "So, ãr hota funiyore Kreta ḍiyattu zahazgan no saron aššil. Hen goitta boli ei mosibot edde dongšor hatottu uddar faita.
ACT 27:22 Kintu ehon ãi tũwarare foriyad gorir, tũwarar dilot himmot rako, kiyollahoile tũwara honokiye no moriba kintu ei zahazgan dongšo oibo.
ACT 27:23 Ãi zar manuš edde zar šeba gori, hibar ek firista ãr hãse ai tiyaiyore hoiye,
ACT 27:24 'Paulos, no ḍorais, tottu Romor badšar munttu tiya foribo. Ei zahazot zara tor fũwati zar, hitara beggunor zibonore Allaye doya goriyore tore diye.'
ACT 27:25 Etolla tũwarar monot šahoš rako, Allar uwore ãttu ei biššaš ase ze hibaye ãre zen hoiye hen oibo.
ACT 27:26 Kintu ãrattu hono ugguwa ḍiyat ouzagoi foribo."
ACT 27:27 Ãra Adriya doriya bai en bafe zat takilam, tuwanor soiddo dinor din ada raitta zahazor serainga okkole kulor mikka fõissegai boli ṭaijje.
ACT 27:28 Ar hitara mafi sadde fani aši hat mur. Ar hotun bade hitara abar mafi sadde heṛe fani haiṭ hat.
ACT 27:29 Fattoror loi dakka háibo ḍore zahazor fis ḍakottu hitara sairguwa nogol felaiye. Ar hitara dinor fohor oibolla duwa gora šuru goijje.
ACT 27:30 Bade zahazor serainga okkol dai zaiboilla kušišot zahazor sarmor mikkattu nogol felerfan gori hitara foran basaibar nogan doriyat lamai diye.
ACT 27:31 Hetunot Paulose ofisar edde šoinno okkolore hodde, "Ei zahazor serainga okkol no takile tũwara rehai no faiba."
ACT 27:32 Hetunot šoinno okkole noganor dori haṛi diye, zene hiyan fanit fori zagoi.
ACT 27:33 Binna oibar age Paulose beggunore kissu háibolla foriyad goijje. "Aijja soiddo din oiye, ki oibo no oibo sinta loi tũwara no hái taikko, hono hána no hó.
ACT 27:34 Ehon ãi tũwarare kissu háibolla foriyad gorir. Forane basi taibolla tũwarattu kissu há zorulot. Saiyo, tũwarar ekkan matar sul foijjonto luksan no oibo."
ACT 27:35 Ei hota hoi Paulose ruṭi loi hitara beggunor sarme Allare šukuriya zanaiye edde hinore bangiyore há šuru goijje.
ACT 27:36 Hetunot hitara beggune o šahoš faiyore há šuru goijje.
ACT 27:37 Ãra zahazot moṭ dui šo hoittor sozon aššilam.
ACT 27:38 Beggune feṭ bori hái bade zahazor uzon homaibolla buli gĩyu okkol doriyat felai diya oiye.
ACT 27:39 Binna zehon oiye hitara he zagagan sini no fare, kintu en ekkan hári deikke ziyanor ḍake balur sor ase, toi hitara faisela goijje, šombob oile zahazgan he kinare tuli dibo.
ACT 27:40 Hitara zahazor nogolgunor dori haṛi diyore doriyat felai diye edde suwanir dori o kuli diye. Tarfore hitara boyaror mukor muntu šor ṭakidiye edde kinaror mikka ozi zaiyore sorot bazi giyegoi.
ACT 27:41 Mummikkar ḍak toratori boizagoinor zoriya zahazsan usol oigiyegoi. Ar fis ḍakottu goiror ḍakkaye ṭura ṭura oi bangi za šuru oiye.
ACT 27:42 Hetunot šoinno okkole hodi okkolore mari felaibo ereda loiye, zene hitarar butottu honokiye hãsuriyore dai zaigoi no fare.
ACT 27:43 Kintu ofisare Paulosor foran basaito sail boli šoinno okkolor ereda mozin goitto no de. Hite hokum diye, zara hãsuri fare hitara age zahazottu falmari zai kul suwok.
ACT 27:44 Ar baki beggune zahazor totta ba oinno hono kissu doriyore heṛe zok. Ebafe beggune šušondane kulot fõisse.
ACT 28:1 Ãra aramor sãte kul sui fari bade zani farilamde, he ḍiyawar nam Malṭa.
ACT 28:2 Ar heṛiyar mainše ãrar uwore beša beši doya dehaiye. Hitara ãra beggunore ḍaki loigiye edde oinor ṭal zali diye kiyollahoile hẽtte zór diya šuru goijjil edde ṭanḍa aššil.
ACT 28:3 Paulose ek ãza fuwana darguwa dola gori oinot furai dibar šomot ugguwa bišwala haf, oinor gorom faiyore he darguwar ṭalor butottu niyoliyore hibar hat sai hõri doijje.
ACT 28:4 Hafwa Paulosor hatot ḍuli taikkede dekiyore he ḍiyar manuš okkole howahoi gora šuru goijje, "Ei manušwa hameka kuni oibo, kiyollahoile doriyattu rehai oi farile o niyai deviye hitare basito no de."
ACT 28:5 Kintu Paulose hat zara mariyore hafware oinot felai diye edde hibar hono hoti no o.
ACT 28:6 Manuš okkole baffil hibar ga fuli zaiboi, otóba hiba atikka fori mori zaiboi, kintu bout hotun entezar gori bade o zehon hono kissu no o, hen deki hitarar ereda bodolai felaiye edde hodde, iba ek devota.
ACT 28:7 Heṛe ḍake ekzon Publiyus name he ḍiyar neta aššil. Hite ãrare hitar górot loizaiyore tin din mula beši adoror sãte ãrare mehemandari goijje.
ACT 28:8 Ar hẽtte Publiyusor bafe zor edde amoša biyaram loi bisanat fori aššil. Ar Paulose butore hitar ḍake zaiyore duwar fũwati hitar uwore hat raikke edde hitare aram goijje.
ACT 28:9 Ei goṭona bade he ḍiyar baki har biyaraimma okkol o aišše edde aram oiye.
ACT 28:10 Hitara nanan ḍoilla gori ãrare ijjot dehaiye. Toi zẽtte ãra zahazsan saribolla reḍi oilam, hitara ãrattu zoruloti ziniš fottoro okkol zahazot ani diye.
ACT 28:11 Tin maš haṛi zaigoi bade ãra ekkan zahazot gori za šuru gorilam ziyane heṛe šit hal haṛail. Ar ei zahazsan aššilde Alekzandriyar, hiyanor matat zoikka devota, Kastor edde Polluxor sinno aššil.
ACT 28:12 Ãra Sirakušot ailam edde heṛe tin din takilam.
ACT 28:13 Henttu baisa di ãra Régiumot fõsilam. Tarforor din doinali bataš uiṭṭe ar dusora din ãra Futeoli fõsilam.
ACT 28:14 Heṛe hoekzon biššaši failam, zitara ãrare hitarar fũwati haftanik takibolla dawat diye. Ei bafe ãra Rom šohorot ailam.
ACT 28:15 Heṛe torikotor báiboinain okkole ãra aibar hóbor funiyore ãrar loi dola oibolla hoi hitarar kiye kiye Appius bazar edde Tin Šoraihana fara foijjonto aiššil. Ei manuš okkolore dekiyore Paulose Allare šukuriya zanaiye, ar hiba nize o tuwajjo faiye.
ACT 28:16 Rom šohorot ãra fõsi bade Paulosore faharadari šoinno okkolor fũwati hibar bote hiba azadi bafe taki faribolla ezajot faiye.
ACT 28:17 Tin din bade Paulose heṛiyar Ihudi neta okkol beggunore ḍaki ekkui fũwati dola goijje. Hitara zehon dola oiye Paulose hodde: "Báiyain okkol! Zodi o ãi ãrar zatir berudde kissu no gori, otóba bafdadar dinna solti niyomor ulda kissu no gori, tarfore o ãre ãṭok gora oiye edde Romiyo okkolor hatot diya oiye.
ACT 28:18 Romiyo okkole ãre zera goriyore bade eridito sail, kiyollahoile moron šazar laikka hono hosuri ãi no gori.
ACT 28:19 Kintu Ihudi okkole hiyanot baza diye buli ãi Romor badšar hãse afil goijji. Ar iyan o haṭi ze ãi ãr nizor zatir hosuri dehaito aššide no.
ACT 28:20 Etolla ãi tũwara loi deha goitto edde hota hoito sair. Israili okkolor ekkui ašalla boli ãi siyolor bondi."
ACT 28:21 Hitara Paulosore zuwabe hodde, "Ãra tũwar babute Ehudiyattu hono šeṛi no fai, ar ãrar manuš hentu eṛe aiyore o hono hóbor no de otóba tũwar babute hono kissur bura no ho.
ACT 28:22 Tarfore o ãra tũwar motamot fuinto sai, kiyollahoile ãra beggune zani ze beggune he dolor berudde hota ho."
ACT 28:23 Paulos loi dola oibolla hitara ekkan din ṭik goijje edde hitara aro manuš okkol šoho Paulos zeṛe takito heṛe aišše. Hetunot Paulose binnattu loti hazinna ofan foijjonto hitarar hãse goba diye, Allar raijjor babute zanaiye edde buzaiye. Musar Torah edde Nobi okkolor kitab okkolor butottu Isar babute hitarare buzaibolla kušiš goijje.
ACT 28:24 Paulose hoiyede hin hodune biššaš goijje, ar hodune biššaš no gore.
ACT 28:25 Paulosor hotat hitara hitara naraz oiye edde hitara hentu giyegoi. Hitara zaibar agottu Paulose hodde, "Pak Ruhuye nobi Esaiyar duwara tũwarar bafdada okkolore hãsa soiyi hoil:
ACT 28:26 "'Manuš okkolor hãse zai ho, tũwara funat takiba kintu hono bote no buziba, sat takiba kintu hono bote no zaniba.
ACT 28:27 Kiyollahoile ei mainšor dil ošar oigiyegoi, ar itarar han o bondo oi giyegoi. Ar hitara hitarar suk o bandi raikke. Ar no oile hitara hitarar suke dekito, hitarar hane funito, hitarar dile buzito edde firi aito. Ar ãi hitarare aram goritam.'
ACT 28:28 "Etolla tũwara zani rako ze Allar uddar Oihudi okkolor hãse defeṛa oiye, ar hitara funibo!"
ACT 28:29 (Paulose zehon hendilla hoiye, Ihudi okkole tara tara doro biyasana gori gori hentu giyegoi.)
ACT 28:30 Fura dui bosormula Paulos heṛe hibar nizor bara górot taikke edde zara hibar loi deha goitto aito, hitara beggunore hibaye gosito.
ACT 28:31 Hibaye beši šahoš loi hono baza sara Allar raijjor babute šikka dito edde Isa Mosir babute šikka dito.
GAL 1:1 Ãi Paulos Isa Mosir ekzon asab, manuš okkol otóba hono manušor duwara no, kintu Isa Mosi edde Allah Baf, ze hibare mora okkolor butottu tuille.
GAL 1:2 Ãi edde ãr fũwati asede hár torikotor báiboinain okkolor torfottu Galatiyat šomaz okkolor hãse:
GAL 1:3 Allah baf edde ãrar Malik Isa Mosir torfottu tũwarar uwore rahamot edde šanti ok,
GAL 1:4 ze ãrar gunalla boli nizor zibon diye, zene hibaye ãrar Baf Allar issa mozin ãrare ehonor horaf zobanattu uddar gori fare,
GAL 1:5 hamišalla Allar šanor tarif ok! Amen.
GAL 1:6 Ãi ammuwak oir ze Mosir doyat ze Allaye tũwarare ḍaikke, eto toratori hibare felaizaigoiyore ar oinno ekkan kušir hóborot zor,
GAL 1:7 asole hiyan kušir hóbor no. En hodun manuš ase zine tũwarare uldafaldat felar edde Mosir babute kušir hóborore bodoli felaito sar.
GAL 1:8 Kintu ze kušir hóbor ãra tũwarar hãse tobolig goijji, hinottuwaro aleda hono šikka ãra ba behostor firistaye tũwarare de, toile hitar uwore gozob forok.
GAL 1:9 Ãra in age o hoilam, ar ãi tũwarare abar o hoir: Ze kušir hóbor tũwara goisso, hin bade ar oinno šikka zodi honokiye tũwarare de, hitar uwore gozob forok.
GAL 1:10 Ãi ki ehon manušor nam faibolla ne Allar nam faibolla saidde? Ãi ki manušore razi goribolla kušiš gorir? No! Zodi ãi ehono manušore razi gorat takitam, henoile ãi ekzon Mosir gulam no oitam.
GAL 1:11 Báiboinain okkol, ãi tũwarare zanai dir, ze kušir hóbor ãi tobolig goijji, hiyan mainšottu no.
GAL 1:12 Iyan ãi hono mainšottu faiyi de no, ar hono mainšottu šikkide o no, iyan ãlla Isa Mosiye forhaš goijje.
GAL 1:13 Ihudi dórmot age ãr ze solafira aššil, hiyanor babute tũwara fuinno, ãi Allar zomatore hoto beši zulum goritam edde hiyanore dongšo gorifelaibolla kušiš goritam.
GAL 1:14 Ar ãi Ihudi dórmot ãr zatit, ãr boyošša beši manušor butore ãi barik aššilam, hiyan bade o ãr bafdada okkolor rosonolla ãttu beši ṭan aššil.
GAL 1:15 Kintu Allah, ze ãre ãr mar feṛottu loti basi loiye edde hibar doyar butore ḍaikke, hiba beši razi oiye,
GAL 1:16 ãr butore hibar Futore forhaš goribolla, zene ãi oihudi okkolor hãse hibar babute tobolig gori fari. Hetunot ãi hiyan hono manuš zati loi biyasana no gori.
GAL 1:17 Ar Zeruzalemot hitara zara ãr age asab oil hitarar heṛe o no zai, kintu Arob dešot gilamboi. Toi abar Damaskusot uwafes firi aišši.
GAL 1:18 Toi tin bosor bade ãi Zeruzalemot Fitor loi dola oito gilam, ar hibar fũwati heṛe fundro din takkilam.
GAL 1:19 Ãi šude Malikor bái Yakubore sara ar hono asab okkolore no deki.
GAL 1:20 Allare sarme raki hoir, ãi tũwarar hãse zin lekir, hin misa no!
GAL 1:21 Tarfore ãi Siriya edde Kilikiya eleha okkolot gilam.
GAL 1:22 Ar hẽtte o Ehudiya elehar Mosir zomat okkole ãr siyara no deke.
GAL 1:23 Hitara šude ei hota howa oiyede fuinnil, "Ze ãrare age zulum goitto, ehon hite nize he biššašganor tobolig gorer, ziyan hite ek hale dongšo gorifelaibolla kušiš goijje."
GAL 1:24 Tarfore ãlla hitara Allar tarif goijje.
GAL 2:1 Soiddo bosor bade ãi Barnabasor fũwati abar uwore Zeruzalem giyi, ar Titusore o fũwati loigiyi.
GAL 2:2 Ãi ohi fonor zoriya heṛe giyilam edde Oihudi okkolor hãse ze kušir hóbor tobolig gori ãi hin okkol goinno mainno zimmadar okkolor hase gufone hoi funaiyi, kiyollahoile ãi hono hannasun behazor dũra dũrir ne hiyanor ḍore.
GAL 2:3 En ki, bái Titus, ze Girik zati ãr fũwati aššil, hitare udda azomi gora foribo hoi zur no gore.
GAL 2:4 Asole ei goṭona uiṭṭilde haron oilde hoekzon misa biššašiye Mosi Isar butore ze azadi ãrattu ase hiyanore hitara gufone spaigiri goribolla góillegai, toi zene hitara ãrare gulam banaifelai fare.
GAL 2:5 Ãra hitarare ekka gorilla udda šuzug no di, kiyollahoile ãra saiyi ze kušir hóboror soyi tũwarar fũwati mojbut take.
GAL 2:6 Ar zarare beši goinno mainno zimmadar dora oito, hitara zettor ḍõr oibo ok, hiyanot ãttu kissu aiye no za, kiyollahoile Allaye manušore forok no gore. Ar he goinno mainno zimmadar okkole ãi hoi funaiyide hinot noya hono kissu zug no gore.
GAL 2:7 Bolke aro uzan dekilo ze Fitorore zendilla azomi goraiya okkolor hãse kušir hóbor tobolig goribolla, hendila ãre o Oihudi okkolor hãse kušir hóbor tobolig goribolla bár diya oil.
GAL 2:8 Kiyollahoile, ze Allaye azomi goraiya okkololla Fitorore asab goijje, hibaye ãre o oinno zati okkololla asab goijje.
GAL 2:9 Ar Yakub, Fitor edde Yuhanna, hitara zarare asol faiya hisabe gona o, ãi hon doya faiyi hiyan buzi fariyore hitara ãi edde Barnabas loi hitarar šiyardar hisabe den hat milaiye ze ãra oinno zati okkolor hãse, ar hitara azomi goraiya okkolor hãse za.
GAL 2:10 Hitara šude hoil ze ãra zene gorib okkolore monot raki, ziyan ãi goribolla o ãttu issa aššil.
GAL 2:11 Ar zẽtte Fitor Anṭiyokot aišše, ãi sarma sarmi hibar berudde tiyaiyi, kiyollahoile hibaye oinnai goijjil.
GAL 2:12 Kiyollahoile Yakubor hentu kissu manuš aibar age, hibaye oinno zati okkolor fũwati hána haito, hitara zẽtte aišše, hibaye he azomi goraiya okkolore ḍoraiyore hiba fissa hõiṭṭe edde ga alok gora šuru goijje.
GAL 2:13 Ar hibar fũwati oinno Ihudi okkole endilla bonḍami gora šuru goijje, enki Barnabasore o hitarar bonḍamiye ṭainne.
GAL 2:14 Kintu ãi zehon dekilam ze hitara kušir hóboror soiyi mozin no soler, ãi beggunor sarme Fitorore hoidde, "Tũi ekzon Ihudi oiyore zodi ekzon Ihudir ḍoilla no soliyore oinno zatir ḍoilla hassa goro, toile tũi kengori oinno zati okkolore Ihudi okkolor ḍoilla oi solibolla zur gorifariba?
GAL 2:15 "Ãra foidaši Ihudi, ar oinno gunagar zati no.
GAL 2:16 Tarfore o, ãra iyan zani ze ekzon manušore Torar ainor ham goronor zoriya forhesgar gona no o, šude Isa Mosir uwore biššašor zoriya o. Hetolla ãra o Mosir uwore biššaš ainni, toi zene ãrare forhesgar gone, Mosi Isar uwore biššašor zoriya, ar ainor ham goronor zoriya no, kiyollahoile ainor ham goriyore honokiye forhesgar oi no fare.
GAL 2:17 "Ar zodi Mosir uwore biššašor zoriya forhesgar oito zaiyore ãra gunagar oi, Mosi ki toile gunar šeba goroya? Ebbere o no!
GAL 2:18 Kiyollahoile ãi zinottu niyoli giyigoi, hin zodi ãi abar bandi tuli, toile ãre ãi ekzon ain bangoya oiyum.
GAL 2:19 "Kiyollahoile ãi ainor duwara ainot morigiyigoi, toi zene ãi Allalla zibon haṛai fari.
GAL 2:20 Ãre Mosir fũwati kurušot diya oiye, ãi ar zinda nai, kintu ãr butore Mosi zinda ase. Ar ze zibon ãi manuš hisabe haṛair hiyan ãi Allar Futor uwore biššaš raki haṛair, zibaye ãre muhabbot goijje edde hiba nize kurbani hisabe ãlla kurban oiye.
GAL 2:21 Ãi Allar doyare batil no gori, kiyollahoile zodi forhesgari Torar ainor duwara o, toile Mosi behazor moijje!"
GAL 3:1 O bekub Galatiyo okkol! Tũwarare zadu hone goijje? Isa Mosire kurušot diyore marifela oilde hiyan ki tũwarar sukor sarme kulasa gori howa no o ne?
GAL 3:2 Ãi tũwarattu iyan zainto sair: Tũwara Pak Ruhure ki ainor ham goronor duwara faiyode ne naki ze kušir hóbor fuinno edde biššaš goijjo hinor duwara?
GAL 3:3 Tũwara eto bekub ka? Tũwara Ruh loi noya zibon šuru goriyore, ehon gar issa mozin šeš goitto sodde neki?
